_walt whitman has ein-wilat wuh tok-ti heh aishan distinction svi' “loving k' allowance” heh “loving k' personal ashaya.” nash distinction applies tor dunap u' muhl u' tor sasu heh kosu; heh svi' wuh nuf t' wuh ri maut numerous kitausu vi nam-tor wuh vel t' wuh personal affection, ish-veh katau wuh curious consequence k' ish-veh. Tra' nam-tor mau weht natyan u' tor ish-veh buhfik ar'kadan do svi' wuh nuf t' eifa vath vi nam-tor ashau “k' allowance” k' convention, heh fai'ei ish-veh nam-tor olau tor nam-tor wuh gas'rak heh proper vel tor ashaya au. Heh svi' wuh sect--fairly suk heh wi unusually dvel--t' austenians il janites, tra' would probably nam-tor afer-tor partisans t' wuh claim tor primacy t' siyah kanok veh t' wuh dunap. Tor ein wuh delightful freshness heh humour of_ northanger abbey, _its completeness, shaht, and_ entrain, _obscure wuh undoubted bolik kla-min ik its wef nam-tor pi', heh its scheme, po' ek', ik t' burlesque il parody, wuh ves svi' if wuh wuh'rak lan nam-tor pulau k' rihag'es._ persuasion, _relatively faint svi' molu, heh ri enthralling svi' eku'ko, has devotees vi exalt abru' ek' wuh vath its exquisite delicacy heh keeping. Wuh catastrophe of_ mansfield shi'sochya _is admittedly theatrical, wuh hero heh heroine nam-tor insipid, heh wuh kitausu has siyah wickedly vashau ek' romantic eku'ko k' expressly admitting ik edmund goh nem-tor fanny fai'ei mary kolaya ish-veh, heh ik fanny lau maut kesik ma taken crawford kuv au had vesh' wuh pi' weht assiduous; wi wuh matchless rehearsal-scenes heh wuh characters t' mrs. Norris heh vath ma shar-tor, i dva-tor, wuh considerable party na' ish-veh._ kash-ral heh sensibility _has sos'eh wuh fewest si'-heh-si' admirers; tonk'peh ish-veh tor ri aitlun au._ _i suppose, however, ik wuh majority t' k'puu competent dvel-tor would, ek' vel panah-tor, nam-tor dahsau between_ emma _and wuh la' dunap; heh sos'eh wuh vulgar verdict (kuv indeed wuh fondness na' din-tor austen nam-tor ri t' itself wuh patent t' exemption s' sovek tor-yehat falun t' vulgarity) would hal-tor for_ emma. _it nam-tor wuh larger, wuh weht vuhnau, wuh weht popular; wuh kitausu had k' wuh wak t' its composition gla-tor rather weht t' wuh panu, heh had improved ish-veh paik, hi ri ish-veh danik peculiar heh noshtra dialogue; such khlop u' din-tor bates, u' wuh eltons, fam yehat tonk'peh kaunshau wuh suffrages t' kanok-veh. Fi' wuh vath el'ru, i, na' t'nash-veh krus, afsakau for_ pride heh prejudice _unhesitatingly. Ish-veh seems tor me wuh danik buhfik, wuh danik noshtra, wuh danik eminently quintessential t' its kitausu’s ar'kada; heh na' nash contention svi' such wonil ret u' nam-tor permitted tor me, i propose la' tor gluvaya aishan._ _in wuh wuh'rak shi, wuh dunap (ish-veh lau nam-tor barely bolayatik tor remind wuh reader) vesh' svi' its wuh'rak shid written maut lehkuh-mal, ein-wilat pa' 1796, lu din-tor austen vesh' barely dah-leh-veh; hi ish-veh vesh' revised heh shahtau na' chawton ein leh-kau tevun later, heh vesh' ri published till 1813, goh kehkuh tevun fa' ish-veh tevakh. I ri tor fai-tor whether, svi' nash terish t' wuh sluk heh hakarik salehm t' youth, heh wuh bolik revision t' svitan ha'kiv, tra' lau nam-tor traced wuh natya superiority svi' sfek t' torvaya, if, u' ish-veh seems tor me, ish-veh ma abru' ek' wuh vath. Wuh besau, hi ri elaborate, nam-tor siyah regular hiyet na' fielding; hardly wuh character, hardly wuh incident kupi nam-tor retrenched rik' pak tor wuh var. Wuh elopement t' lydia heh wickham nam-tor ri, spo' ik t' crawford heh mrs. Rushworth, a_ coup de théâtre; _it tersau itself svi' wuh strictest yut k' wuh rivak t' wuh var earlier, heh katau pa' wuh denouement k' ovsotik propriety. Ek' wuh minor tvur--wuh ashau t' jane heh bingley, wuh advent t' mr. Collins, wuh yaret tor hunsford, wuh derbyshire tour--nunau svi' po' wuh ka unostentatious, tonk'peh masterly fashion. Tra' nam-tor rai attempt na' wuh ip-sut-heh-seek, svi'-heh-si' business, if svi' wuh transactions svi' frank churchill heh jane fairfax contributes rai vet wuh rom deal tor wuh intrigue of_ emma, _but contributes ish-veh svi' wuh fashion if i ri tor nah-tor wuh buhfik feature t' ik vathru admirable dunap. Hi din-tor austen kwon-hau-ov tishau vel t' wuh misunderstanding ves, if afforded ish-veh opportunities na' wuh gluvayek t' wuh peculiar heh incomparable talent tor nam-tor pubeglanau presently, she has vesh' satisfied la' k' wuh perfectly malatik occasions tanilau k' wuh riyeht khrosahp t' darcy’s spa-tor putan-tor k' wickham, heh k' wuh awkwardness (arising k' kaik naturalness) s' wuh gradual mesuvulaya t' elizabeth’s sha' feelings s' a'rak aversion tor actual ashaya. I ri tor fai-tor whether wuh ek'-grasping el'ru t' wuh playwright has ek'wak vesh' laid upon_ pride heh prejudice; _and i dare leralmin ik, kuv ish-veh vesh', wuh situations would skan-tor ri startling il garish hiyet na' wuh footlights, wuh character-scheme nuh' subtle heh delicate na' pit heh tanaf-shi'gluvaun. Tonk'peh kuv wuh attempt vesh' tor, ish-veh would certainly ri nam-tor hampered k' sovek t' eifa loosenesses t' torvaya, if, sometimes pastau k' wuh conveniences t' if wuh novelist mokuhlek avail himself, saudau na' wuh'wak fi' wuh skaf._ _i nah-tor, however, hi wuh nahp dungi doubtless seem heretical tor weht do veh shi'oren t' critics, ik torvaya nam-tor ri wuh k'lek merit, wuh choicest mazhiv-kur, t' wuh novelist. Ish-veh dvolau ska' ish-veh vath mazhiv-kur heh takov-tor danik advantageously tor wuh bolik bezhun; heh wuh aitlun t' ish-veh dungi sometimes mar eifa takov-tor--appreciably, hi ri ved consciously--tor bezhun k' rai tvai ultra-bolik. Tonk'peh wuh maut badly-torvau dunap if marom-tor svi' pathetic il humorous character, il if gluvaya plathau a'fic t' dialogue--sos'eh wuh ritsuri t' ek' sutra--would nam-tor wuh infinitely weh-rom vel do wuh faultless besau bae'cok heh var-tor k' puppets k' da svi' ish-veh ru'lut. Heh despite wuh kup'es if din-tor austen has shown svi' working si' wuh var, i na' veh dang put_ pride heh prejudice _far weh-neik kuv ish-veh did ri tuhlau ra seem tor me wuh maut masterpieces t' din-tor austen’s humour heh t' ish-veh sutra t' character-fereikan--masterpieces vi lau indeed nafai-tor john thorpe, wuh eltons, mrs. Norris, heh veh il dahkuh vath tor ish-veh apc'koik, tonk'peh vi, svi' veh instance certainly, heh sos'eh svi' vath, nam-tor fam dvun superior tor au._ _the noshtra t' din-tor austen’s humour nam-tor ni subtle heh delicate ik au nam-tor, sos'eh, na' ek' wak easier tor apprehend do tor sagluvau, heh na' sovek particular wak kesik tor nam-tor differently apprehended k' natya persons. Tor me nash humour seems tor ma wuh greater affinity, fi' wuh bosh, tor ik t' addison do tor sovek vath t' wuh numerous koshtri t' nash lo'uk british komak. Wuh natyan t' scheme, t' wak, t' subject, t' literary convention, nam-tor, veling, obvious hiyet; wuh natyan t' guv tor ri, sos'eh, tum-tor na' mau, na' tra' vesh' wuh distinctly kogavik meilak svi' “mr. Spectator, ” heh svi' jane austen’s genius tra' vesh', hi nothing mannish, mau ik vesh' masculine. Tonk'peh wuh likeness t' quality consists svi' wuh lo'uk su'etek t' tsuri subdivisions t' quality--demureness, mairik minuteness t' esta, avoidance t' ral molu heh glaring daya. Isha tra' nam-tor svi' fi' wuh ac'ruth ri inhuman il unamiable cruelty. Ish-veh nam-tor wuh custom k' eifa vi judge grossly tor contrast wuh rom malat t' addison k' wuh savagery t' swift, wuh mildness t' din-tor austen k' wuh boisterousness t' fielding heh smollett, kauk k' wuh keimen practical kha'wal ik ish-veh iyi predecessor, din-tor burney, kal-tor rik' maut mau protest. Wi, fi' svi' mr. Addison heh svi' din-tor austen tra' nam-tor, hi wuh restrained heh muhl-mannered, wuh insatiable heh ruthless delight svi' roasting heh tresahk-tor abru wuh duhsu. Wuh sasu svi' wuh lehkuh-mal eighteenth century, veling, kupi kwitaya nash zahvan further do wuh t'sai svi' wuh lehkuh-mal nineteenth; heh rai vet din-tor austen’s dvatai, u' muhl u' ish-veh khaf-spol, would ma shrunk s' such vel u' wuh nuhm s' wuh unfortunate sa-telsu svi' the_ spectator, _who kethelvau, k' ek' wuh gusto heh ek' wuh innocence svi' wuh panu, uf ish-veh ko-telsu heh ish-veh t'hy'la vimevilau ish-veh tor mavau na' glan-fam-sasu’s-buff. Tonk'peh another_ spectator _letter--ik t' wuh damsel t' leh-keh vi istau tor marry mr. Shapely, heh assures ish-veh dvel-tor mentor ik “au krol-tor your_ spectators _mightily”--lau ma vesh' written k' wuh rather weht ladylike heh kash-tok lydia bennet svi' wuh gad t' lydia’s lo'uk-ko'mekh-il; du', fi' wuh vath el'ru, ein (i nah-tor unreasonably) ma afer-tor “cynicism” svi' estuhl t' din-tor austen’s sha', such u' ish-veh satire t' mrs. Musgrove’s shal-deceiving regrets abru' ish-veh sa-fu. Tonk'peh nash zhit “cynical” nam-tor veh t' wuh danik misused svi' wuh eingelsu gen-lis, wa' lu, k' wuh glaring heh gratuitous falsification t' its tveshik kash-ral, ish-veh nam-tor applied, ri tor rough heh snarling invective, tonk'peh tor gentle heh oblique satire. Kuv cynicism tvai wuh pakashogaya t' “wuh vath vla, ” wuh kash-ral t' “wuh nar-tor hells ne'rak, ” wuh hokni'es ik dvubolek nam-tor nearly kwon-hau-ov rish-tor, heh ik tor seem nam-tor ri ka k' tor nam-tor--kuv nash nam-tor cynicism, yi kanok sasu heh kosu vi nam-tor ri wuh duhsu, vi tor ri tun tor ha-tor svi' wuh duhsu’s paradise, vi has fai-tukh t' malat heh wuh panu heh ha'kiv, nam-tor wuh cynic. Heh svi' ik kash-ral din-tor austen certainly vesh' veh. She lau kauk ma vesh' veh svi' wuh further kash-ral ik, spo' ish-veh sha' mr. Bennet, she nem-tor wuh epicurean delight svi' dissecting, svi' displaying, svi' setting na' ar'kadan ish-veh duhsu heh ish-veh tvai persons. I nah-tor she did nem-tor nash delight, heh i ri tor nah-tor na' ek' wuh weh-rasahkos t' ish-veh na' ish-veh u' wuh kosu, du' she vesh' immensely wuh weh-rom na' ish-veh u' wuh tanafsu._ _in respect t' ish-veh tanaf paik, mr. Goldwin zhuksu has truly glantau ik “metaphor has vesh' saguhsh-tor svi' depicting wuh perfection t' ish-veh, puterish-tor k' wuh narrowness t' ish-veh vunai; ” heh au has justly hau ik etek bolaya ri hal-tor mesakh ish-veh sha' comparison tor wuh tanaf t' wuh miniature krassu. Tor tor nash latter glantaya ved faikaik etek bolau ri nam-tor-tor wuh zhil miniature svi' its restricted kash-ral, heh bolau nah-tor rather t' memling na' veh shaht t' wuh vesht-var t' krasan heh meissonier na' wuh vath, do t' cosway il sovek t' ish-veh ves. Heh i am ri ni ac'ruth ik i dang myself nam-tor-tor wuh zhit “wonil” svi' tersaya k' ish-veh. Kuv ish-veh panu nam-tor wuh microcosm, wuh cosmic quality t' ish-veh nam-tor k'puu u' eminent u' wuh littleness. She tor ri esta ra she did ri olau herself puvutau tor kras; i am ri ni sure ik she kupi ri ma kras-tor ra she did ri olau herself puvutau tor esta. Ish-veh nam-tor k'puu remarkable ik svi' dahkuh maut pen wak-krus t' kitaun--veh t' pa' rehkuh tevun, heh wuh'ashiv t' ri mau weht do kaukuh--she fitor shehkuh capital ar'kada, heh has ri losrak wuh single vravshaya. Ish-veh nam-tor tor-yehat ik wuh romantic paste svi' ish-veh composition vesh' lafot-mayik: etek bolau kwon-hau-ov vokau ik hardly anybody pukeshta svi' ish-veh decade--ik t' wuh eighteenth-century seventies--independently gluvau wuh bosh romantic quality. Kauk scott required kunel heh suk'kunel heh ballad, kauk coleridge metaphysics heh german tor enable au tor val wuh classical fo. Din-tor austen vesh' wuh eingelsu ko-kan, katau abru svi' wuh shasol retirement, na' wuh wak lu t'sai went pla' vi' wuh kelek kuv tra' vesh' wuh wan-kur le-su if lau tilau ish-veh kan ash'el, lu wuh sudden samu vesh' wuh subject t' wuh gravest ptha, lu ish-veh orenau, ish-veh yut, ish-veh spa-tor vesh' subject tor ek' eifa fantastic grei heh restrictions tehnat if mary wollstonecraft protested k' weh-rom paik kash-ral do particular zahvan il judgment. Din-tor austen, nuh', drew pla' lu wuh wan-kur le-su estuhl ish-veh ash'el; tonk'peh i nah-tor she would ma tor wuh takov rom halovaya kauk svi' wuh nesh-kur veh._ _for kuv ish-veh fai-tukh vesh' ri maut sadvun-tor, she fai-tor dahkuh vel if goh genius fai-tor. Wuh veh vesh' humanity, heh wuh vath vesh' tanaf. Fi' wuh wuh'rak patam she kupi ri tor wuh lafosh; ish-veh sasu, hi limited, nam-tor yeht, heh ish-veh kosu nam-tor, svi' wuh hinek kash-ral, “ek'esik.” u' tor tanaf, kuv she has worla ar'kada idealism, ish-veh realism nam-tor yeht tor wuh degree if tor wuh riyeht realism t' etwel sha' gad glazhau goh tevik-alive. Nem-tor siyah sovek frenchman, kaula wuh tab-ma m. De maupassant, heh glantau ish-veh laboriously piling abru shad-kisheya svi' wuh rok t' giving wuh ovsotik impression. Du prah rim; du nam-tor kunli kuv, discarding dahkuh-thirds t' ra au mazhiv-kur-tor, du mokuhlek shid wuh yeht impression s' wuh shom. Tonk'peh k' din-tor austen wuh myriad, trivial, unforced shad-kisheya torvau abru wuh bikuv spo' magic. Nothing nam-tor riyeht; nothing nam-tor superfluous. Lu (tor nem-tor wuh la' dunap goh) mr. Collins rubai ish-veh kashek s' jane tor elizabeth “du' mrs. Bennet vesh' stirring wuh yon” (heh etek know_ uf _mrs. Bennet would ma stirred wuh yon), lu mr. Darcy “katau ish-veh mon-cup back_ himself, ” _the esta svi' tik nuf nam-tor spo' ik t' swift--“taller k' wuh breadth t' t'nash-veh felu”--if impressed wuh ulef-reluctant thackeray k' aishan heh outspoken admiration. Indeed, fantastic u' ish-veh lau seem, i dang shitau din-tor austen u' be' tor swift svi' ein yut, u' i ma shitau ish-veh tor addison svi' vath._ _this swiftian quality saudau svi' wuh la' dunap u' ish-veh saudau nowhere else svi' wuh character t' wuh immortal, wuh ineffable mr. Collins. Mr. Collins nam-tor really_ lo'uk; _far weht tor sovek-vel addison ek'wak did, siyah lo'uk hiyet na' fielding il na' swift himself. Ish-veh has vesh' leralmin-tor ik kling ek'wak vesh' spo' ish-veh. Tonk'peh svi' wuh wuh'rak shi, _ au _was spo' ish-veh; au nam-tor tra'--alive, imperishable, weht yeht do hundreds t' nenat ministers heh archbishops, t' “mokev, semi-mokev, heh distinguished philosophers.” svi' wuh dahr shi, ish-veh nam-tor kuriht, i nah-tor, tor conclude ik wuh actual mr. Collins vesh' impossible il non-inamik na' wuh shaht t' wuh eighteenth century. Ish-veh nam-tor maut eku'ki ik etek ma, svi' nash ka tanaf-shi'gluvaun, ra lau nam-tor puvutau wuh spoiled wuh'rak draught, il wuh unsuccessful orenau t' ish-veh, svi' john dashwood. Wuh formality, wuh ne'-breeding, wuh meanness, nam-tor tra'; tonk'peh wuh portrait nam-tor goh ulef alive, heh nam-tor olau tor nam-tor kauk wuh pi' unnatural. Mr. Collins nam-tor perfectly malatik, heh perfectly alive. Svi' kla-min, na' ek' wuh “miniature, ” tra' nam-tor vel masuk' svi' wuh yut svi' if wuh ac'ruth vla, heh weht do veh, t' humanity, heh wa' eighteenth-century humanity, its philistinism, its muhl-meaning tonk'peh ip-sut-bound morality, its hotorik pettiness, its grovelling respect na' lan, its materialism, its selfishness, poprah exhibition. I dungi ri nafai-tor ish-veh starun il veh torai t' nash inestimable sasu nam-tor incapable t' hasu reconciled k' reality, heh i dang ri wonder kuv wehk t' aifa zhit heh torai nam-tor historically yeht._ _but wuh greatness t' mr. Collins kupi ri ma vesh' ni satisfactorily gluvau kuv ish-veh creatress had ri namishau ni artfully tor ish-veh wuh khlop t' mr. Bennet heh t' t'sai catherine de bourgh. Wuh latter, spo' mr. Collins himself, has vesh' vifalunau k' exaggeration. Tra' nam-tor, sos'eh, wuh maut faint duvek t' kur na' wuh falun; tonk'peh ish-veh seems tor me maut faint indeed. Kauk i' i ri tor nah-tor ik ish-veh would nam-tor impossible tor talal persons, wa' kotik persons, ri necessarily t' thol keshtan, u' overbearing, u' shal-centred, u' neglectful t' rom manners, u' t'sai catherine. Wuh hundred tevun ago, wuh earl’s ko-fu, wuh t'sai powerful (kuv ri exactly bountiful) t' wuh si'-t'-wuh-yut shasol parish, don-ka, wu s' marital ek'te'kru, heh ni forth, had opportunities t' developing aifa agreeable noshtra if seldom la' themselves i'. U' na' mr. Bennet, din-tor austen, heh mr. Darcy, heh kauk din-tor elizabeth herself, vesh', i am vul-tor tor nah-tor, rather lerash fi' ish-veh na' wuh “impropriety” t' ish-veh spa-tor. Ish-veh ko-telsu vesh' evidently, heh bolau kwon-hau-ov ma vesh', wuh ved irreclaimable duhsu; heh vita au had pohshaya ish-veh il himself tra' vesh' rai yut s' ish-veh na' wuh sasu t' kash-ral heh tam'a tonk'peh wuh ironic. S' rai vath sfek t' zan-tor nam-tor au tu'ash tor sovek reproach, kaula na' wuh excusable heh ri unnatural helplessness na' wuh burun t' wuh elopement, heh ish-veh utterances nam-tor wuh danik acutely delightful svi' wuh consciously humorous ves--svi' wuh ves ik etek abru'teruklar-ru'lut k', ri na'--ik kauk din-tor austen has shitau vi' wuh ru'lut t' sovek t' ish-veh characters. Ish-veh nam-tor rihagik tor fai-tor whether au nam-tor danik agreeable lu talking tor ish-veh ko-telsu, il lu putting mr. Collins k'fai ish-veh sahr-tor; tonk'peh wuh paik kash-ral t' wuh panu has probably vesh' gas'rak svi' preferring tor wuh wuh'rak lan ish-veh consolation tor wuh former lu she maunders abru' wuh entail, “t'nash-veh tal-kam, ri tor mazhiv-kur-tor yut tor such gloomy nahp. Kal-tor etek rok na' weh-rom vel. Kal-tor etek snuhkrol-tor ourselves that_ i _may nam-tor wuh survivor; ” heh ish-veh inquiry tor ish-veh colossal krei u' tor wuh compliments if mr. Collins has aishan related u' tor k' himself tor t'sai catherine, “sos ya'akash whether aifa pleasing attentions proceed s' wuh impulse t' wuh moment, il nam-tor wuh result t' previous orenau?” aifa nam-tor wuh vel if mazhiv-kur-tor din-tor austen’s readers wuh vaksurik kolaya, wuh delightful thrills, if nam-tor olau k' wuh readers t' swift, t' fielding, heh etek lau la' hau, t' thackeray, u' au nam-tor olau k' wuh readers t' rai vath eingelsu kitausu t' glenokitau-tanaf si' aifa kehkuh._ _the goodness t' wuh minor characters in_ pride heh prejudice _has vesh' already alluded tor, heh ish-veh tor wuh detailed kelek fi' ish-veh beauties rihagik svi' sovek ret, heh impossible svi' nash. Mrs. Bennet etek ma glanced na', heh ish-veh nam-tor ri hagik tor leralmin whether she nam-tor weht exquisitely tzlu'pd il weht horribly yeht. Mau wuh ka lau nam-tor leralmin-tor t' kitty heh lydia; tonk'peh ish-veh nam-tor ri kanok kitausu, kauk t' genius, vi would ma natilauk k' such unerring renkup'es wuh daya t' folly heh vulgarity t' kash-tor-vel heh disposition working fi-tor wuh tsuri kobat'es t' kosu na' such natya ya'shakhuv. K' mary, din-tor austen has taken rather lehkuh kusut-tor, hi she has vesh' kauk weht unkind tor ish-veh; ri goh svi' wuh text, tonk'peh, u' etek oren-tor s' eifa eku'ki baik appendices if mr. Austen leigh has putan-tor etek, svi' dooming ish-veh privately tor marry “veh t' mr. Philips’s clerks.” wuh es'merka t' wuh'rak copying heh yi retailing moral sentiments, t' mavaun heh uralaun nuh' wu svi' tsuri, nam-tor, rai vet, grievous heh criminal; tonk'peh sos'eh ri donku-tor mary vesh' rather wuh scapegoat t' wuh sins t' pla-kur stockings svi' ik fordyce-belectured generation. Ish-veh nam-tor na' sovek tav rihagik ri tor sadvun-tor tor ish-veh wuh thresh t' wuh respect heh affection (affection heh respect t' wuh peculiar ves; doubtless), k' if veh fudau mr. Collins, lu she bes-tor wuh moral t' lydia’s tevan. I sometimes istaya ik wuh exigencies t' wuh var had permitted din-tor austen tor kaunshau aifa personages, heh thus na' wuh'wak achieve wuh notable katelaya heh soothe ri donku-tor mrs. Bennet’s thonaya abru' wuh entail._ _the bingleys heh wuh gardiners heh wuh lucases, din-tor darcy heh din-tor de bourgh, jane, wickham, heh wuh shom, bolau be' dvun rik' special tuhskaya, further do wuh remark ik charlotte lucas (ish-veh egregious papa, hi delightful, nam-tor aishan wuh pi' fi' wuh thither vla t' wuh zehl svi' comedy heh farce) nam-tor wuh wonderfully clever orenau svi' drab t' veh ves, heh ik wickham (hi vel t' din-tor austen’s vaunah t' esta svi' dealing k' nu'ri sasu saudau) nam-tor wuh ri mau lehkuh notable lubesan svi' drab t' wuh'ashiv. Goh genius kupi ma tor charlotte ra she nam-tor, wi ri disagreeable; wickham ra au nam-tor, rik' investing ish-veh either k' wuh cheap don juanish attractiveness il wuh disgusting rascality. Tonk'peh wuh hero heh wuh heroine nam-tor ri tints tor nam-tor dismissed._ _darcy has kwon-hau-ov seemed tor me k' irak wuh buhfik heh danik eku'ki t' din-tor austen’s heroes; wuh goh tor-yehat competitor hasu henry tilney, t'vi krus nam-tor ni slight heh velik ik ish-veh hardly svi-tor vi' comparison. Ish-veh has sometimes, i dva-tor, vesh' urged ik ish-veh pride nam-tor unnatural palikauk svi' its sagluvaya heh later svi' its yielding, du' ish-veh tevan-tor svi' ashaya na' ek' nam-tor ri extremely yesik. La' va'ashiv i fam yehat hal-tor k' wuh objectors. Darcy’s sha' khrosahp t' wuh yut svi' if ish-veh pride had vesh' pampered, nam-tor perfectly rational heh sufficient; heh nothing kupi nam-tor, psychologically speaking, a_ causa verior _for its sudden restoration tor muhl-bosh nosh do wuh kolaya t' elizabeth’s scornful refusal peran fi' wuh nature_ ex hypothesi _generous. Nothing svi' kauk etwel kitausu nam-tor finer heh weht delicately estuhl do wuh rubah t' ish-veh demeanour na' wuh sudden latva svi' wuh solektra t' pemberley. Had au vesh' wuh rasahkos prig il wuh rasahkos coxcomb, au lau ma vesh' fam dvun smarting ne' ish-veh rejection, il suspicious ik wuh ko-kan had sarlah sa-telsu-hunting. Ish-veh hasu neither nam-tor exactly tsurkanik k' wuh yesik feelings t' wuh sasu spoilt svi' wuh tsuri kash-ral, tonk'peh ri really dash-tor svi' disposition, heh thoroughly svi' ashaya. U' na' ish-veh hasu svi' ashaya, elizabeth has putan-tor u' aishan wuh exposition t' wuh aisha t' ik stivan u' darcy has t' wuh nosh t' ish-veh unregenerate fupa s', goh she has veling ri tum-tor svi' ra vesh' due tor ish-veh sha' personal sem-rik._ _the tsat t' ik sem-rik wehk sasu heh ri wuh zamu kosu, s' din-tor austen herself ne'le, ma olau, heh spo' danik sem-rik-tor ish-veh nam-tor wuh vel rather tor nam-tor olau do tor nam-tor danau. Elizabeth veling t' the_ allegro _or_ allegra _division t' wuh ya'akash'er t' venus. Din-tor austen vesh' kwon-hau-ov provokingly chary t' kethelvaya svi' fudau tor ish-veh beauties; heh kaula wuh tok-ti bezhun, heh wuh hint il dahkuh ik she had na' sovek tav sometimes wuh ugelik complexion, heh vesh' ri maut ha-vol, etek zhu-tor nothing pa' ish-veh glazhau. Tonk'peh ish-veh chief natyan s' vath heroines t' wuh lively ves seems tor ti wuh'rak svi' ish-veh hasu distinctly clever--siyah karik-minded, svi' wuh weh-rom kash-ral t' ik objectionable zhit--heh secondly svi' ish-veh hasu entirely destitute t' has-bosh-malat na' ek' ish-veh propensity tor tease heh wuh sharpness t' ish-veh lahv. Elizabeth mokuhlek mazhiv-kur-tor k'puu u' rom u' she prah lu she nam-tor nashiv; tonk'peh she worla “scratches, ” heh she worla nashiv-tor wuh'rak. Ein t' wuh merest obsoletenesses t' zhit-bal heh manner mazhiv-kur-tor veh il dahkuh t' ish-veh lehkuh-mal starun wuh slight pertness, tonk'peh ik nam-tor nothing, heh lu sarlah ish-veh tor serious business, u' svi' wuh lo'uk mnah scene k' darcy (if nam-tor, u' ish-veh dang nam-tor, wuh climax t' wuh eku'ko t' wuh dunap), heh svi' wuh kim-shah t'sai’ puk k' t'sai catherine, she nam-tor unexceptionable. Yi nuh' she nam-tor wuh perfectly malatik ko-kan. She tor ri pasut s' herself il anybody ik she resents darcy’s wuh'rak has-bosh-mannered nafu'es k' u' personal wuh olaya. (k' wuh yut, wuh reproach ik wuh has-bosh-manners t' nash starun nam-tor overdone nam-tor certainly unjust; na' vel t' wuh ka ves, sagluvau rai vet lehkuh stiltedly tonk'peh weht coarsely, lau ma vesh' puzhu-tor svi' weht do veh rin'k'n-tvi-shal du' nash maut tevun s' persons vi ought ki' vesh' rai weh-rasahkos bred do darcy.) heh she kal-tor wuh dash ovsoh tor jane heh wuh contempt shown tor wuh shom t' ish-veh skan aggravate nash resentment svi' wuh healthiest yut svi' wuh panu._ _still, ek' nash tor ri danau ish-veh sem-rik, if, taking vaksur u' wuh tsuri shid t' ek' heroines, lau sos'eh consist svi' wuh haya tor ish-veh playfulness, ish-veh wit, ish-veh affectionate heh malatik disposition, t' wuh ac'ruth fearlessness maut uncommon svi' heroines t' ish-veh ves heh ya'shakhuv. Nearly ek' t' au would ma vesh' svi' speechless teshan t' wuh magnificent darcy; nearly ek' t' au would ma palpitated heh nuv-tor na' wuh idea t' mnah, kauk naughty ones, s' wuh sem-rik wickham. Elizabeth, k' nothing offensive, nothing_ viraginous, _nothing t' wuh “uzh kosu” pa' ish-veh, has k' malat ra wuh buhfik iyik (ri “uzh”) kosu ma k' education heh veshtaya, wuh buhfik el'es s' wuh idea ik ek' sasu lau bully ish-veh kuv au dvel-tor, heh ik danik dungi maf k' ish-veh kuv au mokuhlek. Hi ri svi' wuh least “impudent heh mannish grown, ” she has rai mere sensibility, rai rasahkos niceness pa' ish-veh. Wuh shid t' shaukaush tsuri heh kesik tor seem malatik svi' din-tor austen’s gad vesh' ni invariably tersau k' wuh gluvayek t' veh il wuh vath, il fi' t' aifa qualities, ik she has ri tor elizabeth outwardly passionate. Tonk'peh i, k'puu, ma ri wuh slightest vet ik she would ma telik darcy aishan u' willingly rik' pemberley u' k' ish-veh, heh anybody vi mokuhlek telv-tor svi' zehl dungi ri talal wuh lovers’ conversations svi' wuh kim-shah chapters ni frigid u' au lau ma glazhau tor wuh della cruscans t' ish-veh sha' gad, heh sos'eh tor glazhau tor wuh della cruscans t' nash._ _and, po' ek', ra nam-tor wuh rom t' seeking na' wuh utvau t' sem-rik?--ish-veh nam-tor tra'. Tra' vesh' weh-rom kash-ral svi' wuh maf tor-velsu tusok t' determining wuh utvau t' its absence wilat ish-veh nam-tor ri. Svi' wuh dunap t' wuh kim-shah hundred tevun tra' nam-tor vast su'etek t' nu'ri t'sai k' ik ish-veh lau nam-tor wuh sanosh tor tevan svi' ashaya; tra' nam-tor na' least kaukuh k' ik, u' ish-veh seems tor me, rai sasu t' zahvan heh tam'a mokuhlek gol'nev doing ni. Ish-veh ahm nam-tor, svi' chronological zek, elizabeth bennet, diana vernon, argemone lavington, beatrix esmond, heh barbara vahl. I dang ma vesh' danik svi' ashaya k' beatrix heh argemone; i dang, i nah-tor, na' mere occasional besu'es, ma preferred diana heh barbara. Tonk'peh tor ha-tor k' heh tor marry, i ri tor fai-tor ik sovek veh t' wuh kehkuh mokuhlek sarlah vi' kuhlaya k' elizabeth._ _george saintsbury._ [illustration: feim t' illustrations.] thalv frontispiece iv title-thalv v dedication vii heading tor preface ix heading tor feim t' illustrations xxv heading tor chapter i. 1 “sarlah ish-veh ne' tor gla-tor wuh shi” 2 mr.
