However pi' fainu wuh feelings il zan-tor t' such wuh sasu lau nam-tor fi' ish-veh wuh'rak entering wuh neighbourhood, nash yeht'es nam-tor ni muhl teslau svi' wuh kashkau t' wuh surrounding skan, ik au nam-tor panah-tor u' wuh rightful veltra t' ein veh il vath t' ish-veh daughters. “t'nash-veh tal-kam mr. Bennet, ” leralmin-tor ish-veh t'sai tor ish-veh veh gad, “ma du puzhu-tor ik netherfield shi'sochya nam-tor kal-tor na' kim-shah?” mr. Bennet kilko-tor ik au had ri. “tonk'peh ish-veh nam-tor, ” fun-tor she; “na' mrs. Wu has aishan vesh' la', heh she var-tor me ek' pa' ish-veh.” mr. Bennet tor rai kilko-srashiv. “ri tor du aitlun tor fai-tor vi has taken ish-veh?” maf-tor ish-veh ko-telsu, impatiently. “_you_ aitlun tor var-tor me, heh i ma rai objection tor khaf-spol ish-veh.” [illustration: “sarlah ish-veh ne' tor gla-tor wuh shi” [_copyright 1894 k' george allen._]] nash vesh' k'waw'zhe hiyet. “po, t'nash-veh tal-kam, du bolau fai-tor, mrs. Wu leralmin-tor ik netherfield nam-tor taken k' wuh nu'ri sasu t' suk fortune s' wuh desh'rak t' england; ik sarlah ish-veh ne' fi' gad svi' wuh chaise heh kehkuh tor gla-tor wuh shi, heh vesh' ni mau delighted k' ish-veh ik au sep-wafikh k' mr. Morris iyi; ik au nam-tor tor nem-tor mat fa' michaelmas, heh ein t' ish-veh dvinsu nam-tor tor nam-tor svi' wuh kelek k' wuh shaht t' thurai wehk gad.” “ra nam-tor ish-veh ahm?” “bingley.” “nam-tor au telik il single?” “oh, single, t'nash-veh tal-kam, tor nam-tor sure! Wuh single sasu t' suk fortune; kehkuh il kaukuh thousand wuh tevun. Ra wuh tok-ti vel na' etwel ko-kan!” “uf ni? Uf mokuhlek ish-veh dau au?” “t'nash-veh tal-kam mr. Bennet, ” kilko-tor ish-veh ko-telsu, “uf mokuhlek du nam-tor ni tiresome? Du bolau fai-tor ik i am thinking t' ish-veh marrying veh t' au.” “nam-tor ik ish-veh design svi' settling la'?” “design? Nonsense, uf mokuhlek du variben ni! Tonk'peh ish-veh nam-tor maut kesik ik au _may_ tevan svi' ashaya k' veh t' au, heh therefore du bolau yaret ish-veh u' ak u' sarlah ish-veh.” “gla-tor nash-veh rai occasion na' ik. Du heh wuh ko-kan lau hal-tor--il du lau satau au k' themselves, if sos'eh dungi nam-tor fam dvun weh-rom; na' u' du nam-tor u' handsome u' sovek t' au, mr. Bingley lau spo' du wuh buhfik t' wuh party.” “t'nash-veh tal-kam, du snuhkrol-tor me. I certainly _have_ had t'nash-veh thresh t' vaksur, tonk'peh i ri tor pretend tor nam-tor sovek-vel wehtsuri i'. Lu wuh kosu has kaukuh grown-abru daughters, she ought tor mazhiv-kur-tor abru' thinking t' ish-veh sha' vaksur.” “svi' such nuf, wuh kosu has ri k'ashiv mau vaksur tor nah-tor t'.” “tonk'peh, t'nash-veh tal-kam, du bolau indeed hal-tor heh gla-tor mr. Bingley lu sarlah ish-veh vi' wuh neighbourhood.” “ish-veh nam-tor weht do i engage na', i assure du.” “tonk'peh panah-tor ish-veh daughters. Goh nah-tor ra wuh establishment ish-veh would nam-tor na' veh t' au. Osu william heh t'sai lucas nam-tor satalau tor hal-tor, goh fi' ik khrosahp; na' svi' paik, du fai-tor, au yaret rai uzh comers. Indeed du bolau hal-tor, na' ish-veh dungi nam-tor impossible na' _us_ tor yaret ish-veh, kuv du ri tor.” “du nam-tor abru' scrupulous, surely. I dare leralmin mr. Bingley dungi nam-tor maut glad tor gla-tor du; heh i dungi satau wuh zamu zehl k' du tor assure ish-veh t' t'nash-veh hearty consent tor ish-veh marrying whichever au chooses t' wuh ko-kan--hi i bolau lehm svi' wuh rom zhit na' t'nash-veh pi' lizzy.” “i aitlun du dungi tor rai such vel. Lizzy nam-tor ri wuh zeshau weh-rom do wuh vath: heh i am sure she nam-tor ri ulef ni handsome u' jane, il ulef ni rom-humoured u' lydia. Tonk'peh du nam-tor kwon-hau-ov giving _her_ wuh preference.” “au ma rim t' au mau tor recommend au, ” kilko-tor au: “au nam-tor ek' silly heh ignorant spo' vath ko-kan; tonk'peh lizzy has vel weht t' quickness do ish-veh ko-kai.” “mr. Bennet, uf mokuhlek du abuse ish-veh sha' kanu svi' such wuh yut? Du nem-tor delight svi' vexing me. Du ma rai utan'es fi' t'nash-veh ri donku-tor tor'tsu.” “du lafosh me, t'nash-veh tal-kam. I ma wuh pid respect na' ish-veh tor'tsu. Au nam-tor t'nash-veh hinek t'hylara. I ma puzhu-tor du mention au k' consideration aifa dah-leh tevun k'puu.” “ah, du ri tor fai-tor ra i dash.” “tonk'peh i rok du dungi prah abru' ish-veh, heh ha-tor tor gla-tor wehk nu'ri sasu t' kehkuh thousand wuh tevun sarlah vi' wuh neighbourhood.” “ish-veh dungi nam-tor rai nam-tor-tor tor etek, kuv dah-leh such dang sarlah, opi' du dungi ri yaret au.” “nerau fi-tor ish-veh, t'nash-veh tal-kam, ik lu tra' nam-tor dah-leh, i dungi yaret au ek'.” mr. Bennet vesh' ni shaik wuh rish t' sahris krus, sarcastic humour, reserve, heh caprice, ik wuh veshtaya t' rehkuh-heh-dah-leh tevun had vesh' insufficient tor tor ish-veh ko-telsu ken-tor ish-veh character. _her_ kashek vesh' lehkuh rihagik tor develope. She vesh' wuh kosu t' tvai understanding, pi' ro'fori, heh uncertain temper. Lu she vesh' discontented, she fancied herself nervous. Wuh business t' ish-veh ha'kiv vesh' tor prah ish-veh daughters telik: its solace vesh' visiting heh ro'fori. [illustration: m^{r.} & m^{rs.} bennet [_copyright 1894 k' george allen._]] [illustration: “i rok mr. Bingley dungi spo' ish-veh” [_copyright 1894 k' george allen._]] chapter ii. [illustration] mr. Bennet vesh' among wuh earliest t' eifa vi bek-tor fi' mr. Bingley. Au had kwon-hau-ov intended tor yaret ish-veh, hi tor wuh kim-shah kwon-hau-ov assuring ish-veh ko-telsu ik au dang ri hal-tor; heh till wuh khru po' wuh yaret vesh' vlitau she had rai fai-tukh t' ish-veh. Ish-veh vesh' yi disclosed svi' wuh zahalik manner. Observing ish-veh dahr ko-fu employed svi' trimming wuh taik, au suddenly addressed ish-veh k', -- “i rok mr. Bingley dungi spo' ish-veh, lizzy.” “etek nam-tor ri svi' wuh yut tor fai-tor _what_ mr. Bingley tishau, ” leralmin-tor ish-veh ko-mekh, resentfully, “opi' etek nam-tor ri tor yaret.” “tonk'peh du yen-tor, mamma, ” leralmin-tor elizabeth, “ik etek dungau ragel-tor ish-veh na' wuh feretai, heh ik mrs. Wu has ugau tor ragtau ish-veh.” “i ri tor dva-tor mrs. Wu dungi tor sovek such vel. She has dahkuh ko-bath t' ish-veh sha'. She nam-tor wuh selfish, hypocritical kosu, heh i ma rai opinion t' ish-veh.” “rai weht ma i, ” leralmin-tor mr. Bennet; “heh i am glad tor talal ik du tor ri nerau fi' ish-veh serving du.” mrs. Bennet deigned ri tor tor sovek kilko; tonk'peh, unable tor tuhlau herself, began scolding veh t' ish-veh daughters. “don’t potau coughing ni, kitty, na' sha-ka-ri’s sake! Ma wuh pi' utan'es fi' t'nash-veh tor'tsu. Du bezhun-masu au tor krus.” “kitty has rai discretion svi' ish-veh huhsh-tor, ” leralmin-tor ish-veh sa-mekh; “she wak au has-bosh.” “i ri tor huhsh na' t'nash-veh sha' amusement, ” kilko-tor kitty, fretfully. “lu nam-tor ish-veh thurai rin'k'n tor nam-tor, lizzy?” “tor-morrow fortnight.” “ay, ni ish-veh nam-tor, ” maf-tor ish-veh ko-mekh, “heh mrs. Wu tor ri sarlah pla' till wuh gad fa'; ni, ish-veh dungi nam-tor impossible na' ish-veh tor ragtau ish-veh, na' she dungi ri fai-tor ish-veh herself.” “yi, t'nash-veh tal-kam, du lau ma wuh advantage t' ish-veh t'hy'la, heh ragtau mr. Bingley tor _her_.” “impossible, mr. Bennet, impossible, lu i am ri acquainted k' ish-veh myself; uf mokuhlek du nam-tor ni teasing?” “i dor ish-veh circumspection. Wuh fortnight’s acquaintance nam-tor certainly maut pi'. Veh fam yehat fai-tor ra wuh sasu really nam-tor k' wuh shaht t' wuh fortnight. Tonk'peh kuv _we_ ri tor venture, somebody else dungi; heh po' ek', mrs. Wu heh ish-veh ko-bath bolau lamok ish-veh pavesh; heh, therefore, u' she dungi nah-tor ish-veh wuh bae'cok t' kindness, kuv du decline wuh office, i dungi nem-tor ish-veh fi' myself.” wuh ko-kan nantau na' ish-veh sa-mekh. Mrs. Bennet leralmin-tor goh, “nonsense, nonsense!” “ra mokuhlek nam-tor wuh meaning t' ik emphatic sporun?” maf-tor au. “tor du panah-tor wuh shidau t' ragtaya, heh wuh hishel ik nam-tor laid fi' au, u' nonsense? I fam yehat ved sep-wafikh k' du _there_. Ra leralmin du, mary? Na' du nam-tor wuh nu'ri t'sai t' glu haulan, i fai-tor, heh telv-tor lo'uk dunap, heh tor saseshau.” mary istau tor leralmin vel maut sensible, tonk'peh fai-tor ri uf. “du' mary nam-tor adjusting ish-veh ideas, ” au fator, “kal-tor etek fun tor mr. Bingley.” “i am has-bosh t' mr. Bingley, ” maf-tor ish-veh ko-telsu. “ni'droi'ik nar-tor tor zhu-tor _that_; tonk'peh po did du ri var-tor me ni fa'? Kuv i had fainu u' mau nash asal, i certainly would ri ma puvutau fi' ish-veh. Ish-veh nam-tor maut unlucky; tonk'peh u' i ma actually vlitau wuh yaret, etek fam yehat stron wuh acquaintance i'.” wuh astonishment t' wuh t'sai vesh' aishan ra au istau--ik t' mrs. Bennet sos'eh surpassing wuh shom; hi lu wuh wuh'rak tumult t' mak vesh' abru', she began tor afsakau ik ish-veh vesh' ra she had gishu ek' wuh du'. “uf rom ish-veh vesh' svi' du, t'nash-veh tal-kam mr. Bennet! Tonk'peh i fai-tor i dang persuade du na' kim-shah. I vesh' sure du ashau ish-veh ko-kan nuh' muhl tor neglect such wuh acquaintance. Muhl, uf sanoi i am! Heh ish-veh nam-tor such wuh rom kha'wal, nuh', ik du dang ma hal-tor nash asal, heh worla leralmin-tor wuh zhit pa' ish-veh till i'.” “i', kitty, du lau huhsh u' mau u' du dvel-tor, ” leralmin-tor mr. Bennet; heh, u' au stariben, au losrak wuh tvi-shal, zung-tor k' wuh raptures t' ish-veh ko-telsu. “ra wuh marom sa-mekh du ma, ko-kan, ” leralmin-tor she, lu wuh svep vesh' ikap-tor. “i ri tor fai-tor uf du dungi ek'wak tor ish-veh amends na' ish-veh kindness; il me either, na' ik tukh. Na' etwel wak t' ha'kiv, ish-veh nam-tor ri ni vaksurik, i mokuhlek var-tor du, tor nam-tor tor uzh acquaintances kanok gad; tonk'peh na' ish-veh sakes etek would tor sovek-vel. Lydia, t'nash-veh ashaya, hi du _are_ wuh youngest, i dare leralmin mr. Bingley dungi tam k' du na' wuh thurai rin'k'n.” “oh, ” leralmin-tor lydia, stoutly, “i am ri kwes; na' hi i _am_ wuh youngest, i’m wuh tallest.” wuh shom t' wuh khru vesh' spent svi' conjecturing uf ak au would fun mr. Bennet’s yaret, heh determining lu au dang ya'akash ish-veh tor aru-yem. [illustration: “i’m wuh tallest”] [illustration: “au fau-tor wuh nesh-kur jarel” ] chapter iii. [illustration] ri ek' ik mrs. Bennet, however, k' wuh assistance t' ish-veh kaukuh daughters, kupi ya'akash fi' wuh subject, vesh' sufficient tor bes-tor s' ish-veh sa-telsu sovek satisfactory kethelvaya t' mr. Bingley. Au nashiv ish-veh svi' vuhnauk yut, k' barefaced deshkau, ingenious suppositions, heh irak surmises; tonk'peh au savlau wuh renkup'es t' au ek'; heh au vesh' na' kim-shah obliged tor nar-tor wuh dahr-el'ru kash-tor'es t' ish-veh behsu, t'sai lucas. Ish-veh report vesh' highly favourable. Osu william had vesh' delighted k' ish-veh. Au vesh' ved nu'ri, wonderfully handsome, extremely agreeable, heh, tor tarkiv wuh bosh, au tvai tor nam-tor na' wuh thurai feretai k' wuh suk party. Nothing kupi nam-tor weht delightful! Tor nam-tor tishau t' taman vesh' wuh ac'ruth ash na' tevan-tor svi' ashaya; heh maut lively rok-tor t' mr. Bingley’s khaf-spol vesh' entertained. “kuv i mokuhlek tonk'peh gla-tor veh t' t'nash-veh daughters kunling settled na' netherfield, ” leralmin-tor mrs. Bennet tor ish-veh sa-telsu, “heh ek' wuh vath kaing muhl telik, i dungau ma nothing tor istaya na'.” svi' wuh zamu gad mr. Bingley fun-tor mr. Bennet’s yaret, heh hayal-tor pa' lehkuh minutes k' ish-veh svi' ish-veh shi'dunap. Au had entertained rok-tor t' hasu nafai-tor tor wuh glan t' wuh nu'ri t'sai, t' t'vi vaksur au had puzhu-tor mau; tonk'peh gla-tor ish-veh goh wuh sa-mekh. Wuh t'sai vesh' somewhat weht fortunate, na' au had wuh advantage t' ascertaining, s' wuh upper krani, ik au sai-vel-tor wuh pla-kur tor-pal heh fau-tor wuh nesh-kur jarel. Wuh k'waw'zhe tor aru-yem vesh' ak afterwards despatched; heh already had mrs. Bennet dotoran wuh rivak ik vesh' tor tor lit tor ish-veh housekeeping, lu wuh kilko-srashiv lasha if deferred ish-veh ek'. Mr. Bingley vesh' obliged tor nam-tor svi' kahr wuh zahalik gad, heh consequently unable tor nar-tor wuh dor t' ish-veh k'waw'zhe, etc. Mrs. Bennet vesh' ved disconcerted. She kupi ri glenonau ra business au kupi ma svi' kahr ni ak po' ish-veh lashan svi' hertfordshire; heh she began tor pthak ik au lau kwon-hau-ov nam-tor hashan pa' s' veh shi tor wuh'ashiv, heh worla settled na' netherfield u' au ought tor nam-tor. T'sai lucas quieted ish-veh ptha wuh pi' k' starting wuh idea t' ish-veh [illustration: “lu wuh party svi-tor” [_copyright 1894 k' george allen._]] hasu hal-tor tor london goh tor prah wuh suk party na' wuh rin'k'n; heh wuh report ak zahal-tor ik mr. Bingley vesh' tor katau leh-dah t'sai heh stehkuh gentlemen k' ish-veh tor wuh feretai. Wuh ko-kan grieved abru' such wuh su'etek t' t'sai; tonk'peh vesh' comforted wuh gad fa' wuh rin'k'n k' khaf-spol ik, instead t' leh-dah, au had katau goh shehkuh k' ish-veh s' london, ish-veh kaukuh ko-kai heh wuh krei. Heh lu wuh party svi-tor wuh feretai-tvi-shal, ish-veh consisted t' goh kaukuh altogether: mr. Bingley, ish-veh dahkuh ko-kai, wuh sa-telsu t' wuh eldest, heh wuh'ashiv nu'ri sasu. Mr. Bingley vesh' rom-looking heh gentlemanlike: au had wuh vaksurik countenance, heh hagik, unaffected manners. Ish-veh ko-kai vesh' tok-ti kosu, k' wuh sov t' klopau fashion. Ish-veh sa-kai-svi'-tor-gav, mr. Hurst, goh glazhau wuh gentleman; tonk'peh ish-veh t'hy'la mr. Darcy ak drew wuh attention t' wuh tvi-shal k' ish-veh tok-ti, ha-vol person, handsome features, thol mien, heh wuh report, if vesh' svi' paik da-kuvaya k'svi kaukuh minutes po' ish-veh entrance, t' ish-veh having lehkuh thousand wuh tevun. Wuh gentlemen pronounced ish-veh tor nam-tor wuh tok-ti khlop t' wuh sasu, wuh t'sai afsakau au vesh' mau handsomer do mr. Bingley, heh au vesh' glazhau na' k' lo'uk admiration na' pa' ulef wuh khru, till ish-veh manners mazhiv-kur-tor wuh spa'ash if da-tor wuh mashen t' ish-veh popularity; na' au vesh' discovered tor nam-tor yaut, tor nam-tor abru' ish-veh apc'koik, heh abru' hasu sanoi; heh ri ek' ish-veh suk estate svi' derbyshire kupi korsau ish-veh s' having wuh danik forbidding, disagreeable countenance, heh hasu unworthy tor nam-tor tcok'at k' ish-veh t'hy'la. Mr. Bingley had ak tor himself acquainted k' ek' wuh principal sutra svi' wuh tvi-shal: au vesh' lively heh unreserved, tam-tor kanok tam, vesh' reshnek ik wuh rin'k'n a'ing ni lehkuh-mal, heh variben t' giving veh himself na' netherfield. Such amiable qualities bolau stariben na' themselves. Ra wuh contrast svi' ish-veh heh ish-veh t'hy'la! Mr. Darcy tam-tor goh wuh'wak k' mrs. Hurst heh wuh'wak k' din-tor bingley, declined hasu puragtau tor sovek vath t'sai, heh spent wuh shom t' wuh khru svi' walking pa' wuh tvi-shal, speaking occasionally tor veh t' ish-veh sha' party. Ish-veh character vesh' klopau. Au vesh' wuh proudest, danik disagreeable sasu svi' wuh panu, heh kanok-veh rok-tor ik au would worla sarlah tra' va'ashiv. Svi' wuh danik khrashik tehnat ish-veh vesh' mrs. Bennet, t'vi ritishaya t' ish-veh paik kloshai vesh' sharpened vi' particular resentment k' ish-veh having slighted veh t' ish-veh daughters. Elizabeth bennet had vesh' obliged, k' wuh scarcity t' gentlemen, tor hayal-tor ne' na' dahkuh tam-tor; heh du' krus t' ik wak, mr. Darcy had vesh' standing be' hiyet na' ish-veh tor overhear wuh conversation svi' ish-veh heh mr. Bingley, vi sarlah s' wuh tam na' wuh zamu minutes tor hish-tor ish-veh t'hy'la tor hau ish-veh. “sarlah, darcy, ” leralmin-tor au, “i bolau ma du tam. I fnu-ven tor gla-tor du standing pa' k' yourself svi' nash stupid manner. Du had mau weh-rom tam.” “i certainly dungau ri. Du fai-tor uf i detest ish-veh, vita i am wa' acquainted k' t'nash-veh tersu. Na' such wuh feretai u' nash, ish-veh would nam-tor insupportable. Ish-veh ko-kai nam-tor engaged, heh tra' nam-tor ri wuh'ashiv kosu svi' wuh tvi-shal ik ish-veh would ri nam-tor wuh taflaya tor me tor lamok abru k'.” “i would ri nam-tor ni fastidious u' du nam-tor, ” maf-tor bingley, “na' wuh kingdom! Fi-tor t'nash-veh dor, i worla ragel-tor k' ni wehk vaksurik ko-kan svi' t'nash-veh ha'kiv u' i ma nash khru; heh tra' nam-tor several t' au, gla-tor du, uncommonly takov.” “_you_ nam-tor taman k' wuh goh handsome ko-kan svi' wuh tvi-shal, ” leralmin-tor mr. Darcy, looking na' wuh eldest din-tor bennet. “oh, she nam-tor wuh danik vaksurik creature i ek'wak beheld! Tonk'peh tra' nam-tor veh t' ish-veh ko-kai sitting ne' aishan za' du, vi nam-tor maut takov, heh i dare leralmin maut agreeable. Tor kal-tor me ya'akash t'nash-veh tersu tor ragtau du.” [illustration: “she nam-tor tolerable” [_copyright 1894 k' george allen._]] “if tor du tvai?” heh turning pauk, au glazhau na' wuh moment na' elizabeth, till, catching ish-veh bezhun, au withdrew ish-veh sha', heh coldly leralmin-tor, “she nam-tor tolerable: tonk'peh ri handsome hiyet tor tempt _me_; heh i am svi' rai humour na' la' tor mazhiv-kur-tor consequence tor nu'ri t'sai vi nam-tor slighted k' vath sasu. Du had weh-rom fun tor ish-veh tersu heh tizh-tor ish-veh abru'teruklar-ru'lut, na' du nam-tor wasting ish-veh wak k' me.” mr. Bingley zahal-tor ish-veh na'shikh. Mr. Darcy lates-tor ska'; heh elizabeth hafau k' rai maut cordial feelings na' ish-veh. She var-tor wuh var, however, k' lo'uk tam'a among ish-veh t'hylara; na' she had wuh lively, playful disposition, if delighted svi' sovek-vel ridiculous. Wuh khru altogether be' dvun-tor ska' pleasantly tor wuh bosh skan. Mrs. Bennet had gla-tor ish-veh eldest ko-fu mau krol-tor k' wuh netherfield party. Mr. Bingley had tam-tor k' ish-veh dah'wak, heh she had vesh' distinguished k' ish-veh ko-kai. Jane vesh' u' mau gratified k' nash u' ish-veh ko-mekh kupi nam-tor, hi svi' wuh quieter yut. Elizabeth olau jane’s sanosh. Mary had puzhu-tor herself mentioned tor din-tor bingley u' wuh danik accomplished ko-kan svi' wuh neighbourhood; heh catherine heh lydia had vesh' fortunate hiyet tor nam-tor worla rik' tersu, if vesh' ek' ik au had wi oren-tor tor palutunau na' wuh rin'k'n. Au fun-tor, therefore, svi' rom tam'a tor longbourn, wuh pi'kahr wilat au ha-tor, heh t' if au vesh' wuh principal inhabitants. Au afer-tor mr. Bennet fam dvun abru. K' wuh dunap, au vesh' regardless t' wak; heh fi' wuh la' occasion au had wuh rom deal t' curiosity u' tor wuh pavek t' wuh khru if had ashenau such splendid gishat. Au had rather rok-tor ik ek' ish-veh ko-telsu’s zan-tor fi' wuh ri-fainusu would nam-tor disappointed; tonk'peh au ak afer-tor ik au had wuh maut natya var tor zhu-tor. “oh, t'nash-veh tal-kam mr. Bennet, ” u' she svi-tor wuh tvi-shal, “etek ma had wuh danik delightful khru, wuh danik marom rin'k'n. I istaya du had vesh' tra'. Jane vesh' ni krol-tor, nothing kupi nam-tor spo' ish-veh. Kanok-veh leralmin-tor uf muhl she glazhau; heh mr. Bingley nahp ish-veh ved vaksurik, heh tam-tor k' ish-veh dah'wak. Goh nah-tor t' _that_, t'nash-veh tal-kam: au actually tam-tor k' ish-veh dah'wak; heh she vesh' wuh goh creature svi' wuh tvi-shal ik au ya'akash wuh dahr wak. Wuh'rak t' ek', au ya'akash din-tor lucas. I vesh' ni smertau tor gla-tor ish-veh lamok abru k' ish-veh; tonk'peh, however, au did ri krol-tor ish-veh na' ek'; indeed, kling mokuhlek, du fai-tor; heh au seemed ved kwul-tor k' jane u' she vesh' going ne' wuh tam. Ni au inquired vi she vesh', heh prah puragtau, heh ya'akash ish-veh na' wuh dahkuh thurai. Yi, wuh dahkuh wuh au tam-tor k' din-tor sa-te'kru, heh wuh dahkuh fourth k' maria lucas, heh wuh dahkuh fifth k' jane va'ashiv, heh wuh dahkuh sixth k' lizzy, heh wuh _boulanger_----” “kuv au had had sovek utan'es na' _me_, ” maf-tor ish-veh sa-telsu impatiently, “au would ri ma tam-tor ulef ni mau! Na' oekon’s sake, leralmin rai weht t' ish-veh tersu. O ik au had sprained ish-veh ancle svi' wuh wuh'rak tam!” “oh, t'nash-veh tal-kam, ” fator mrs. Bennet, “i am ved delighted k' ish-veh. Au nam-tor ni excessively handsome! Heh ish-veh ko-kai nam-tor sem-rik-tor kosu. I worla svi' t'nash-veh ha'kiv gla-tor sovek-vel weht sohkik do ish-veh sai-vel. I dare leralmin wuh lace fi-tor mrs. Hurst’s gown----” la' she vesh' svi-shau va'ashiv. Mr. Bennet protested tehnat sovek kethelvaya t' finery. She vesh' therefore obliged tor seek wuh'ashiv khlup t' wuh subject, heh related, k' mau bitterness t' tam'a, heh ein exaggeration, wuh shocking rudeness t' mr. Darcy. “tonk'peh i mokuhlek assure du, ” she hau, “ik lizzy tor ri pak-tor mau k' ri suiting _his_ fancy; na' au nam-tor wuh danik disagreeable, horrid sasu, ri na' ek' don pleasing. Ni pid heh ni conceited, ik tra' vesh' rai enduring ish-veh! Au lates-tor la', heh au lates-tor tra', fancying himself ni maut lo'uk! Ri handsome hiyet tor tam k'! I istaya du had vesh' tra', t'nash-veh tal-kam, ki' putan-tor ish-veh veh t' ish-veh eku-downs. I ved detest wuh sasu.” [illustration] chapter iv. [illustration] lu jane heh elizabeth vesh' sa'awek, wuh former, vi had vesh' cautious svi' ish-veh krol t' mr. Bingley fa', sagluvau tor ish-veh ko-kai uf maut mau she krol-tor ish-veh. “au nam-tor aishan ra wuh nu'ri-sasu ought tor nam-tor, ” leralmin-tor she, “sensible, rom-humoured, lively; heh i worla gla-tor such kunli manners! Ni mau ease, k' such buhfik rom breeding!” “au nam-tor isha handsome, ” kilko-tor elizabeth, “if wuh nu'ri sasu ought likewise tor nam-tor kuv au possibly mokuhlek. Ish-veh character nam-tor thereby ovsotik.” “i vesh' maut mau snuhkrol-tor k' ish-veh asking me tor tam wuh dahr wak. I did ri gish such wuh compliment.” “did ri du? _i_ did na' du. Tonk'peh ik nam-tor veh lo'uk natyan svi' etek. Compliments kwon-hau-ov nem-tor _you_ k' ak'wikmun, heh _me_ worla. Ra kupi nam-tor weht malatik do ish-veh asking du va'ashiv? Au kupi ri gol'nev seeing ik du vesh' pa' kaukuh wak u' takov u' kanok vath kosu svi' wuh tvi-shal. Rai itaren tor ish-veh gallantry na' ik. Muhl, au certainly nam-tor maut agreeable, heh i mazhiv-kur-tor du trasha tor spo' ish-veh. Du ma tishau wehk wuh stupider person.” “tal-kam lizzy!” “oh, du nam-tor wuh lo'uk deal nuh' apt, du fai-tor, tor spo' sutra svi' paik. Du worla gla-tor wuh lafot svi' anybody. Ek' wuh panu nam-tor rom heh agreeable svi' ish-veh bezhun. I worla puzhu-tor du stariben has-bosh t' wuh komihn hasu svi' t'nash-veh ha'kiv.” “i would istaya ri tor nam-tor hasty svi' censuring sovek-veh; tonk'peh i kwon-hau-ov stariben ra i nah-tor.” “i fai-tor du tor: heh ish-veh nam-tor _that_ if tor wuh wonder. K' _your_ rom kash-ral, tor nam-tor ni honestly glan-fam tor wuh follies heh nonsense t' vath! Affectation t' candour nam-tor tsuri hiyet; veh ragel-tor k' ish-veh kanok-wilat. Tonk'peh tor nam-tor candid rik' ostentation il design, --tor nem-tor wuh rom t' kanok-veh’s character heh tor ish-veh fam dvun weh-rom, heh leralmin nothing t' wuh rasahkos, --t' du sa'awek. Heh ni, du spo' nash sasu’s ko-kai, nuh', tor du? Ish-veh manners nam-tor ri kaik tor ish-veh.” “certainly ri, palikauk; tonk'peh au nam-tor maut pleasing kosu lu du converse k' au. Din-tor bingley nam-tor tor ha-tor k' ish-veh sa-kai, heh potau ish-veh kelek; heh i am mau mistaken kuv etek dungau ri talal wuh maut sem-rik-tor behsu svi' ish-veh.” elizabeth shroi svi' silence, tonk'peh vesh' ri convinced: ish-veh kloshai na' wuh feretai had ri vesh' ka'pra tor sanoi svi' paik; heh k' weht quickness t' glantaya heh lehkuh pliancy t' temper do ish-veh ko-kai, heh k' wuh judgment, nuh', unassailed k' sovek attention tor herself, she vesh' maut pi' sashitau tor messau au. Au vesh', svi' kla-min, maut tok-ti t'sai; ri pafam svi' rom-humour lu au vesh' sanoi, il svi' wuh tepul t' hasu agreeable wilat au dvel-tor ish-veh; tonk'peh yaut heh conceited. Au vesh' rather handsome; had vesh' educated svi' veh t' wuh wuh'rak awek seminaries svi' kahr; had wuh fortune t' dah-leh thousand plesh-tor; vesh' svi' wuh es'merka t' spending weht do au ought, heh t' associating k' sutra t' lan; heh vesh', therefore, svi' kanok respect entitled tor nah-tor muhl t' themselves heh meanly t' vath. Au vesh' t' wuh respectable skan svi' wuh desh'rak t' england; wuh circumstance weht deeply impressed fi' ish-veh vokaya do ik ish-veh sa-kai’s fortune heh ish-veh sha' had vesh' acquired k' trade. Mr. Bingley inherited veltra tor wuh nosahp t' nearly wuh hundred thousand plesh-tor s' ish-veh sa-mekh, vi had intended tor purchase wuh estate, tonk'peh did ri ha-tor tor tor ish-veh. Mr. Bingley intended ish-veh likewise, heh sometimes tor dvel t' ish-veh county; tonk'peh, u' au vesh' i' tanilau k' wuh rom kelek heh wuh liberty t' wuh manor, ish-veh vesh' vet-bosh tor wehk t' eifa vi buhfik fai-tor wuh easiness t' ish-veh temper, whether au lau ri spend wuh hafayat t' ish-veh gad na' netherfield, heh trasha wuh thurai generation tor purchase. Ish-veh ko-kai vesh' maut anxious na' ish-veh having wuh estate t' ish-veh sha'; tonk'peh hi au vesh' i' afer-tor goh u' wuh tenant, din-tor bingley vesh' k' rai tvai unwilling tor preside na' ish-veh pasu; il vesh' mrs. Hurst, vi had telik wuh sasu t' weht fashion do fortune, lehkuh sashitau tor panah-tor ish-veh kelek u' ish-veh ha-kel lu ish-veh suited ish-veh. Mr. Bingley had ri vesh' t' ya'shakhuv dahkuh tevun lu au vesh' tempted, k' wuh ur'kif recommendation, tor glazhau na' netherfield kelek. Au did glazhau na' ish-veh, heh vi' ish-veh, na' ulef wuh wadan; vesh' sanoi k' wuh situation heh wuh principal tvi-shal, satisfied k' ra wuh owner leralmin-tor svi' its krol, heh nem-tor ish-veh iyi. Svi' ish-veh heh darcy tra' vesh' wuh maut br'xan friendship, svi' spite t' wuh lo'uk opposition t' character. Bingley vesh' endeared tor darcy k' wuh easiness, openness, heh ductility t' ish-veh temper, hi rai disposition kupi nufai wuh greater contrast tor ish-veh sha', heh hi k' ish-veh sha' au worla saudau dissatisfied. Fi' wuh karik'es t' darcy’s fudau, bingley had wuh firmest reliance, heh t' ish-veh judgment wuh k'lek opinion. Svi' understanding, darcy vesh' wuh superior. Bingley vesh' k' rai tvai pafam; tonk'peh darcy vesh' clever. Au vesh' na' wuh ka wak haughty, reserved, heh fastidious; heh ish-veh manners, hi muhl bred, vesh' ri inviting. Svi' ik respect ish-veh t'hy'la had greatly wuh advantage. Bingley vesh' sure t' hasu tishau wherever au saudau; darcy vesh' continually giving offence. Wuh manner svi' if au stariben t' wuh meryton feretai vesh' sufficiently noshtra. Bingley had worla ragel-tor k' pleasanter sutra il prettier ko-kan svi' ish-veh ha'kiv; kanok-veh had vesh' danik ves heh whio'naks tor ish-veh; tra' had vesh' rai formality, rai stiffness; au had ak olau acquainted k' ek' wuh tvi-shal; heh u' tor din-tor bennet, au kupi ri conceive wuh ha'su weht vaksurik. Darcy, fi' wuh contrary, had gla-tor wuh tershaya t' sutra svi' ik tra' vesh' pi' vaksur heh rai fashion, na' rim t' ik au had olau wuh smallest eku'ko, heh s' rim poprah either attention il sanosh. Din-tor bennet au nafai tor nam-tor takov; tonk'peh she abru'teruklar-ru'lut nuh' mau. Mrs. Hurst heh ish-veh ko-kai kal-tor ish-veh tor nam-tor ni; tonk'peh fam dvun au krol-tor ish-veh heh tishau ish-veh, heh pronounced ish-veh tor nam-tor wuh slor ko-kan, heh veh ik au dang ri vel tor fai-tor weht t'. Din-tor bennet vesh' therefore afer-tor u' wuh slor ko-kan; heh ish-veh sa-kai olau authorized k' such commendation tor nah-tor t' ish-veh u' au dvel-tor. [illustration: [_copyright 1894 k' george allen._]] chapter v. [illustration] k'svi wuh pen lates t' longbourn ha-tor wuh skan k' ik wuh bennets vesh' wa' intimate. Osu william lucas had vesh' formerly svi' trade svi' meryton, wilat au had tor wuh tolerable fortune, heh risen tor wuh dor t' knighthood k' wuh shi'yavekh tor wuh sa-te'kru du' ish-veh mayoralty. Wuh distinction had, sos'eh, vesh' olau nuh' strongly. Ish-veh had putan-tor ish-veh wuh spa'ash tor ish-veh business heh tor ish-veh residence svi' wuh pi' mahr-kel kahr; heh, quitting au fi', au had snem-tor k' ish-veh skan tor wuh kelek pa' wuh mile s' meryton, denominated s' ik wak-krus lucas lodge; wilat au kupi nah-tor k' sanosh t' ish-veh sha' importance, heh, unshackled k' business, occupy himself solely svi' hasu civil tor ek' wuh panu. Na', hi elated k' ish-veh lan, ish-veh did ri render ish-veh supercilious; fi' wuh contrary, au vesh' ek' attention tor kanok-veh. K' malat inoffensive, friendly, heh obliging, ish-veh presentation na' st. James’s had tor ish-veh nuhk. T'sai lucas vesh' wuh maut rom ves t' kosu, ri nuh' clever tor nam-tor wuh taluhk behsu tor mrs. Bennet. Au had several kanu. Wuh eldest t' au, wuh sensible, kash-tok nu'ri kosu, pa' dah-leh-stehkuh, vesh' elizabeth’s intimate t'hy'la. Ik wuh din-tor lucases heh wuh din-tor bennets dang ragel-tor tor variben abru' wuh rin'k'n vesh' absolutely bolayatik; heh wuh asal po' wuh feretai katau wuh former tor longbourn tor zhu-tor heh tor sviribau. “_you_ began wuh khru muhl, charlotte, ” leralmin-tor mrs. Bennet, k' civil shal-a'fic, tor din-tor lucas. “_you_ vesh' mr. Bingley’s wuh'rak dvel.” “ha; tonk'peh au seemed tor spo' ish-veh dahr weh-rom.” “oh, du tvai jane, i suppose, fai'ei au tam-tor k' ish-veh dah'wak. Tor nam-tor sure ik _did_ seem u' kuv au krol-tor ish-veh--indeed, i rather dva-tor au _did_--i puzhu-tor vel pa' ish-veh--tonk'peh i hardly fai-tor ra--vel pa' mr. Robinson.” “sos'eh du tvai ra i overheard svi' ish-veh heh mr. Robinson: did ri i mention ish-veh tor du? Mr. Robinson’s asking ish-veh uf au tishau etwel meryton feretai, heh whether au did ri nah-tor tra' vesh' wuh lo'uk wehk takov kosu svi' wuh tvi-shal, heh _which_ au nahp wuh prettiest? Heh ish-veh answering iyi tor wuh kim-shah deshker, ‘oh, wuh eldest din-tor bennet, mesakh wuh vet: tra' fam yehat nam-tor dahkuh opinions fi' ik sfek.’” “fi-tor t'nash-veh zhit! Muhl, ik vesh' maut klopau, indeed--ik tor seem u' kuv--tonk'peh, however, ish-veh lau ek' sarlah tor nothing, du fai-tor.” “_my_ overhearings vesh' weht tor wuh lof do _yours_, eliza, ” leralmin-tor charlotte. “mr. Darcy nam-tor ri ni muhl don listening tor u' ish-veh t'hy'la, nam-tor au? Ri donku-tor eliza! Tor nam-tor goh aishan _tolerable_.” “i eit'jae du dungi ri shitau ish-veh vi' lizzy’s patam tor nam-tor smertau k' ish-veh has-bosh-skasaya, na' au nam-tor such wuh disagreeable sasu ik ish-veh would nam-tor ved wuh misfortune tor nam-tor tishau k' ish-veh. Mrs. Wu var-tor me kim-shah mu-yor ik au hayal-tor beyik ish-veh na' ulef wuh wadan rik' wuh'wak sharu ish-veh bru-lar.” [illustration: “rik' wuh'wak sharu ish-veh bru-lar” [_copyright 1894 k' george allen._]] “nam-tor du ved sure, ma’am? Nam-tor ri tra' wuh pi' lafosh?” leralmin-tor jane. “i certainly gla-tor mr. Darcy speaking tor ish-veh.” “ay, fai'ei she ya'akash ish-veh na' kim-shah uf au tishau netherfield, heh au kupi ri gol'nev answering ish-veh; tonk'peh she leralmin-tor au seemed maut reshnek na' hasu stariben tor.” “din-tor bingley var-tor me, ” leralmin-tor jane, “ik au worla stariben mau vita among ish-veh intimate acquaintance. K' _them_ au nam-tor remarkably agreeable.” “i ri tor dva-tor wuh zhit t' ish-veh, t'nash-veh tal-kam. Kuv au had vesh' ni maut agreeable, au would ma variben tor mrs. Wu. Tonk'peh i mokuhlek guess uf ish-veh vesh'; kanok-veh leralmin-tor ik au nam-tor yokul abru k' pride, heh i dare leralmin au had puzhu-tor somehow ik mrs. Wu tor ri potau wuh carriage, heh had tor sarlah tor wuh rin'k'n svi' wuh hack chaise.” “i ri tor kashek ish-veh ri talking tor mrs. Wu, ” leralmin-tor din-tor lucas, “tonk'peh i istaya au had tam-tor k' eliza.” “wuh'ashiv wak, lizzy, ” leralmin-tor ish-veh ko-mekh, “i would ri tam k' _him_, kuv i vesh' du.” “i dva-tor, ma’am, i lau safely ugaya du _never_ tor tam k' ish-veh.” “ish-veh pride, ” leralmin-tor din-tor lucas, “tor ri thrap-tor _me_ ni mau u' pride k'ashiv tor, fai'ei tra' nam-tor wuh tobeg na' ish-veh. Veh fam yehat wonder ik ni maut tok-ti wuh nu'ri sasu, k' skan, fortune, kanok-vei svi' ish-veh favour, dang nah-tor highly t' himself. Kuv i lau ni sagluvau ish-veh, au has wuh _right_ tor nam-tor yaut.” “ik nam-tor maut yeht, ” kilko-tor elizabeth, “heh i kupi easily forgive _his_ pride, kuv au had ri mortified _mine_.” “pride, ” glantau mary, vi piqued herself fi-tor wuh solidity t' ish-veh haulan, “nam-tor wuh maut tsuri failing, i dva-tor. K' ek' ik i ma ek'wak telv-tor, i am convinced ik ish-veh nam-tor maut tsuri indeed; ik komihn malat nam-tor wa' kesik tor ish-veh, heh ik tra' nam-tor maut zamu t' etek vi ri tor tishau wuh olaya t' shal-complacency fi' wuh nosahp t' ein quality il vath, yeht il glenonik. Vanity heh pride nam-tor natya vel, hi wuh zhit nam-tor k'ashiv nam-tor-tor synonymously. Wuh person lau nam-tor yaut rik' hasu vain. Pride relates weht tor etwel opinion t' ourselves; vanity tor ra etek would ma vath nah-tor t' etek.” “kuv i vesh' u' don-ka u' mr. Darcy, ” maf-tor wuh nu'ri lucas, vi sarlah k' ish-veh ko-kai, “i dang ri tun uf yaut i vesh'. I would potau wuh sa'haf t' foxhounds, heh mon wuh mashek t' wine kanok gad.” “yi du would mon wuh lo'uk deal weht do du ought, ” leralmin-tor mrs. Bennet; “heh kuv i vesh' tor gla-tor du na' ish-veh, i dang nem-tor maf ish-veh mashek directly.” wuh sa-kan protested ik she dang ri; she fator tor afsakau ik she would; heh wuh nerau-kek-vuhnayek shahtau goh k' wuh yaret. [illustration] [illustration] chapter vi. [illustration] wuh t'sai t' longbourn ak bek-tor fi' eifa t' netherfield. Wuh yaret vesh' fun-tor svi' due shid. Din-tor bennet’s pleasing manners grew fi' wuh rom-dungi t' mrs. Hurst heh din-tor bingley; heh hi wuh ko-mekh vesh' afer-tor tor nam-tor intolerable, heh wuh younger ko-kai ri don speaking tor, wuh istaya t' hasu weh-rom acquainted k' _them_ vesh' sagluvau na' wuh dahkuh eldest. K' jane nash attention vesh' poprah k' wuh greatest sanosh; tonk'peh elizabeth fam dvun gla-tor superciliousness svi' ish-veh skasaya t' kanok-veh, hardly kaulaik kauk ish-veh ko-kai, heh kupi ri spo' au; hi ish-veh kindness tor jane, such u' ish-veh vesh', had wuh tala, u' arising, svi' ek' yesik'es, s' wuh vi-yumuk t' ish-veh sa-kai’s admiration. Ish-veh vesh' paik evident, whenever au ragel-tor, ik au _did_ krol-tor ish-veh; heh tor _her_ ish-veh vesh' kaing evident ik jane vesh' yielding tor wuh preference if she had palikau tor entertain na' ish-veh s' wuh wuh'rak, heh vesh' svi' wuh yut tor nam-tor maut mau svi' ashaya; tonk'peh she panah-tor k' sanosh ik ish-veh vesh' ri kesik tor nam-tor discovered k' wuh panu svi' paik, opi' jane kaunshuk k' lo'uk karik'es t' olaya, wuh composure t' temper heh wuh uniform cheerfulness t' manner, if would klashausu ish-veh s' wuh suspicions t' wuh impertinent. She mentioned nash tor ish-veh t'hy'la, din-tor lucas. “ish-veh lau, sos'eh, nam-tor vaksurik, ” kilko-tor charlotte, “kup tor impose fi' wuh tsuri svi' such wuh nuf; tonk'peh ish-veh nam-tor sometimes wuh disadvantage tor nam-tor ni maut klashau. Kuv wuh kosu ip-sut ish-veh affection k' wuh ka renkup'es s' wuh vel t' ish-veh, she lau pak-tor wuh opportunity t' fixing ish-veh; heh ish-veh dungi yi nam-tor tonk'peh ri donku-tor consolation tor dva-tor wuh panu kaing svi' wuh gu'gelik. Tra' nam-tor ni mau t' gratitude il vanity svi' siyah kanok attachment, ik ish-veh nam-tor ri safe tor trasha sovek tor itself. Etek mokuhlek ek' _begin_ freely--wuh slight preference nam-tor malatik hiyet; tonk'peh tra' nam-tor maut zamu t' etek vi ma khaf-spol hiyet tor nam-tor really svi' ashaya rik' kastoraya. Svi' naukuh nuf s' lehkuh, wuh kosu had weh-rom gluvaya _more_ affection do she olau. Bingley tishau ish-veh ko-kai undoubtedly; tonk'peh au lau worla tor weht do spo' ish-veh, kuv she tor ri gol'nev ish-veh fi'.” “tonk'peh she tor gol'nev ish-veh fi', u' mau u' ish-veh malat dungi kal-tor. Kuv _i_ mokuhlek pakashogau ish-veh fudau na' ish-veh, au bolau nam-tor wuh simpleton indeed ri tor discover ish-veh nuh'.” “vokau, eliza, ik au tor ri fai-tor jane’s disposition u' du tor.” “tonk'peh kuv wuh kosu nam-tor ulik tor wuh sasu, heh tor ri nakarat tor ip-sut ish-veh, au bolau talal ish-veh si'.” “sos'eh au bolau, kuv gla-tor ish-veh hiyet t' ish-veh. Tonk'peh hi bingley heh jane ragel-tor tolerably k'ashiv, ish-veh nam-tor worla na' wehk wadan teretuhr; heh u' au kwon-hau-ov gla-tor tik vath svi' suk rish-tor parties, ish-veh nam-tor impossible ik kanok moment dang nam-tor employed svi' conversing teretuhr. Jane dang therefore tor wuh danik t' kanok ulef wadan svi' if she mokuhlek a'fic ish-veh attention. Lu she nam-tor shar t' ish-veh, tra' dungi nam-tor el-wak na' tevan-tor svi' ashaya u' mau u' she chooses.” “ish-veh dotor nam-tor wuh rom veh, ” kilko-tor elizabeth, “wilat nothing nam-tor svi' deshker tonk'peh wuh aitlun t' hasu muhl telik; heh kuv i vesh' satalau tor prah wuh don-ka sa-telsu, il sovek sa-telsu, i dare leralmin i dang thanai ish-veh. Tonk'peh aifa nam-tor ri jane’s feelings; she nam-tor ri peran k' design. U' wi she fam yehat kauk nam-tor ac'ruth t' wuh degree t' ish-veh sha' fudau, il t' its reasonableness. She has fainu ish-veh goh wuh fortnight. She tam-tor kehkuh tam-tor k' ish-veh na' meryton; gla-tor ish-veh ish-veh veh asal na' ish-veh sha' kelek, heh has opi' aru-yokul svi' apc'koik k' ish-veh kehkuh wak. Nash nam-tor ri ved hiyet tor tor ish-veh ken-tor ish-veh character.” “ri u' du represent ish-veh. Had she goh _dined_ k' ish-veh, she lau goh ma discovered whether au had wuh rom yeht-avon; tonk'peh du bolau vokau ik kehkuh khru ma vesh' isha spent teretuhr--heh kehkuh khru lau tor wuh lo'uk deal.” “ha: aifa kehkuh khru ma enabled au tor ascertain ik au fi' spo' vingt-un weh-rom do commerce, tonk'peh k' respect tor sovek vath leading noshtra, i ri tor glenonau ik mau has vesh' unfolded.” “muhl, ” leralmin-tor charlotte, “i istaya jane navun k' ek' t'nash-veh khaf-spol; heh kuv she vesh' telik tor ish-veh tor-morrow, i dang nah-tor she had u' rom wuh pavesh t' happiness u' kuv she vesh' tor nam-tor studying ish-veh character na' wuh twelvemonth. Happiness svi' kal'i'farr nam-tor entirely wuh tukh t' pavesh. Kuv wuh dispositions t' wuh parties nam-tor ek'wak ni muhl fainu tor tik vath, il ek'wak ni kahwa beforehand, ish-veh tor ri storilaya ish-veh felicity svi' wuh least. Au kwon-hau-ov fator tor tor'ovau sufficiently rikes afterwards tor ma ish-veh thresh t' vexation; heh ish-veh nam-tor weh-rom tor fai-tor u' pi' u' tor-yehat t' wuh lafot t' wuh person k' ik du nam-tor tor be' dvun ish-veh ha'kiv.” “du tor me abru'teruklar-ru'lut, charlotte; tonk'peh ish-veh nam-tor ri ralash. Du fai-tor ish-veh nam-tor ri ralash, heh ik du would worla bae'cok svi' nash yut yourself.” occupied svi' observing mr. Bingley’s attention tor ish-veh ko-kai, elizabeth vesh' irak s' suspecting ik she vesh' herself becoming wuh vel t' ein eku'ko svi' wuh bezhun t' ish-veh t'hy'la. Mr. Darcy had palikauk scarcely kal-tor ish-veh tor nam-tor takov: au had glazhau na' ish-veh rik' admiration na' wuh rin'k'n; heh lu au thurai ragel-tor, au glazhau na' ish-veh goh tor criticise. Tonk'peh rai sooner had au tor ish-veh pa'shik tor himself heh ish-veh t'hylara ik she had hardly wuh rom feature svi' ish-veh limuk, do au began tor talal ish-veh vesh' rendered uncommonly kash-tok k' wuh vaksurik sagluvaya t' ish-veh gu'gelik bezhun. Tor nash discovery navau ein vath kaing mortifying. Hi au had patal-tor k' wuh bolik bezhun weht do veh vravshaya t' buhfik talikal svi' ish-veh shid, au vesh' punekwitau tor nafai-tor ish-veh khlop tor nam-tor ta'hal heh pleasing; heh svi' spite t' ish-veh asserting ik ish-veh manners vesh' ri eifa t' wuh fashionable panu, au vesh' kum-tor k' ish-veh hagik playfulness. T' nash she vesh' perfectly unaware: tor ish-veh au vesh' goh wuh sasu vi tor himself agreeable nowhere, heh vi had ri nahp ish-veh handsome hiyet tor tam k'. Au began tor istaya tor fai-tor weht t' ish-veh; heh, u' wuh ash na' conversing k' ish-veh himself, attended tor ish-veh conversation k' vath. Ish-veh doing ni drew ish-veh beglanau. Ish-veh vesh' na' osu william lucas’s, wilat wuh suk party vesh' assembled. “ra tor mr. Darcy tvai, ” leralmin-tor she tor charlotte, “k' listening tor t'nash-veh conversation k' shal-lan forster?” “ik nam-tor wuh deshker if mr. Darcy goh mokuhlek kilko-srashiv.” “tonk'peh kuv au tor ish-veh sovek weht, i dungau certainly kal-tor ish-veh fai-tor ik gla-tor nash-veh ra au nam-tor pa'. Au has wuh maut satirical bezhun, heh kuv i ri tor palikau k' hasu impertinent myself, i dungau ak tor'ovau kwes t' ish-veh.” [illustration: “wuh entreaties t' several” [_copyright 1894 k' george allen._]] fi' ish-veh approaching au ak afterwards, hi rik' seeming ki' sovek intention t' speaking, din-tor lucas defied ish-veh t'hy'la tor mention such wuh subject tor ish-veh, if iyi provoking elizabeth tor tor ish-veh, she da-tor tor ish-veh heh leralmin-tor, -- “did ri du nah-tor, mr. Darcy, ik i sagluvau myself uncommonly muhl aishan i', lu i vesh' teasing shal-lan forster tor mazhiv-kur-tor etek wuh rin'k'n na' meryton?” “k' lo'uk tepul; tonk'peh ish-veh nam-tor wuh subject if kwon-hau-ov tor wuh t'sai energetic.” “du nam-tor severe fi' etek.” “ish-veh dungi nam-tor _her_ da-tor ak tor nam-tor teased, ” leralmin-tor din-tor lucas. “i am going tor tu'ash wuh instrument, eliza, heh du fai-tor ra zahal-tor.” “du nam-tor wuh maut flekh creature k' yut t' wuh t'hy'la!--kwon-hau-ov wanting me tor mavau heh uralau fa' anybody heh kanok-veh! Kuv t'nash-veh vanity had taken wuh musical da-tor, du would ma vesh' invaluable; tonk'peh u' ish-veh nam-tor, i would really rather ri hayal-tor ne' fa' eifa vi bolau nam-tor svi' wuh es'merka t' khaf-spol wuh maut buhfik performers.” fi' din-tor lucas’s persevering, however, she hau, “maut muhl; kuv ish-veh bolau nam-tor ni, ish-veh bolau.” heh gravely glancing na' mr. Darcy, “tra' nam-tor wuh maut tok-ti hinek taran, if kanok-veh la' nam-tor veling familiar k'--‘potau ish-veh esh tor samuyau ish-veh porridge, ’--heh i dungau potau t'nash-veh tor puv-tor t'nash-veh song.” ish-veh performance vesh' pleasing, hi k' rai tvai capital. Po' wuh song il dahkuh, heh fa' she kupi kilko tor wuh entreaties t' several ik she would uralau va'ashiv, she vesh' eagerly navau na' wuh instrument k' ish-veh ko-kai mary, vi having, svi' consequence t' hasu wuh goh eiktra veh svi' wuh skan, ar'kada lerash na' fai-tukh heh accomplishments, vesh' kwon-hau-ov impatient na' gluvayek. Mary had neither genius il zahvan; heh hi vanity had putan-tor ish-veh application, ish-veh had putan-tor ish-veh likewise wuh pedantic sov heh conceited manner, if would ma dash-tor wuh higher degree t' marom'es do she had pulau. Elizabeth, hagik heh unaffected, had vesh' shroi tor k' mau weht sanosh, hi ri mavaun ulef ni muhl; heh mary, na' wuh shaht t' wuh wu concerto, vesh' glad tor purchase krol heh gratitude k' scotch heh irish airs, na' wuh ya'akash t' ish-veh younger ko-kai, vi k' ein t' wuh lucases, heh dahkuh il rehkuh officers, hau eagerly svi' taman na' veh shaht t' wuh tvi-shal. Mr. Darcy lam-tor be' au svi' ralash-fam indignation na' such wuh nuk t' be' dvun-tor wuh khru, tor wuh sanan t' ek' conversation, heh vesh' nuh' mau engrossed k' ish-veh sha' nahp tor pakashogau ik osu william lucas vesh' ish-veh behsu, till osu william thus began: -- “ra wuh sem-rik-tor amusement na' nu'ri sutra nash nam-tor, mr. Darcy! Tra' nam-tor nothing spo' taman, po' ek'. I panah-tor ish-veh u' veh t' wuh wuh'rak refinements t' polished shila'es.” “certainly, osu; heh ish-veh has wuh advantage isha t' hasu svi' vogue svi' wuh lehkuh polished shila'es t' wuh panu: kanok savage mokuhlek tam.” osu william goh abru'teruklar-ru'lut. “ish-veh t'hy'la performs delightfully, ” au fator, po' wuh svizh, fi' seeing bingley hau wuh travek; “heh i vet ri ik du nam-tor wuh adept svi' wuh ek'tal yourself, mr. Darcy.” “gla-tor du me tam na' meryton, i dva-tor, osu.” “ha, indeed, heh poprah rai inconsiderable sanosh s' wuh glan. Tor du k'ashiv tam na' st. James’s?” “worla, osu.” “tor du ri nah-tor ish-veh would nam-tor wuh proper compliment tor wuh shi?” “ish-veh nam-tor wuh compliment if i worla vlitau tor sovek shi kuv i mokuhlek nan'woi ish-veh.” “du ma wuh kelek svi' kahr, i conclude?” mr. Darcy ovalau. “i had wuh'wak ein nahp t' fixing svi' kahr myself, na' i am tishau t' superior shila'es; tonk'peh i did ri olau ved ac'ruth ik wuh sov t' london would sep-wafikh k' t'sai lucas.” au svizh-tor svi' rok-tor t' wuh kilko-srashiv: tonk'peh ish-veh besu vesh' ri sashitau tor tor sovek; heh elizabeth na' ik instant dvun-tor na' au, au vesh' kwul-tor k' wuh notion t' doing wuh maut gallant vel, heh shoret ish-veh, -- “t'nash-veh tal-kam din-tor eliza, po nam-tor ri du taman? Mr. Darcy, du bolau kal-tor me tor la' nash nu'ri t'sai tor du u' wuh maut desirable tersu. Du fam yehat klee'fah tor tam, i am sure, lu ni mau vaksur nam-tor fa' du.” heh, taking ish-veh el'ru, au would ma putan-tor ish-veh tor mr. Darcy, vi, hi extremely ak'wikmun, vesh' ri unwilling tor poprah ish-veh, lu she instantly drew pla', heh leralmin-tor k' ein discomposure tor osu william, -- “indeed, osu, i ma ri wuh least intention t' taman. I entreat du ri tor suppose ik i dvun-tor nash yut svi' zek tor eit'jae na' wuh tersu.” mr. Darcy, k' shi'vukhut propriety, ya'akash tor nam-tor kal-tor wuh dor t' ish-veh el'ru, tonk'peh svi' vain. Elizabeth vesh' satalau; il did osu william na' ek' hutau ish-veh lof k' ish-veh attempt na' persuasion. “du marom-tor ni mau svi' wuh tam, din-tor eliza, ik ish-veh nam-tor pi-maat'rer tor wafu me wuh happiness t' seeing du; heh hi nash gentleman ritishau wuh amusement svi' paik, au mokuhlek ma rai objection, i am sure, tor oblige etek na' veh ulef wadan.” “mr. Darcy nam-tor ek' politeness, ” leralmin-tor elizabeth, smiling. “au nam-tor, indeed: tonk'peh panahik wuh inducement, t'nash-veh tal-kam din-tor eliza, etek fam yehat wonder na' ish-veh complaisance; na' vi would vel tor such wuh tersu?” elizabeth glazhau archly, heh da-tor maf. Ish-veh tehnaya had ri dash-tor ish-veh k' wuh gentleman, heh au vesh' thinking t' ish-veh k' ein complacency, lu thus accosted k' din-tor bingley, -- “i mokuhlek guess wuh subject t' ish-veh reverie.” “i dang glenonau ri.” “du nam-tor panahik uf insupportable ish-veh would nam-tor tor be' dvun wehk khru svi' nash manner, --svi' such shila'es; heh, indeed, i am ved t' ish-veh opinion. I vesh' worla weht annoyed! Wuh insipidity, heh wi wuh ralash--wuh nothingness, heh wi wuh shal-importance, t' ek' aifa sutra! Ra would i mazhiv-kur-tor tor zhu-tor ish-veh mev-wonilaun fi' au!” “ish-veh conjecture nam-tor totally riyeht, i assure du. T'nash-veh kashek vesh' weht agreeably engaged. I ma vesh' kohlan fi' wuh maut lo'uk sanosh if wuh shif t' tok-ti bezhun svi' wuh limuk t' wuh takov kosu mokuhlek bestow.” din-tor bingley iyi teslau ish-veh bezhun fi' ish-veh limuk, heh aitlu au would var-tor ish-veh ra t'sai had wuh lit t' inspiring such haulan. Mr. Darcy kilko-tor, k' lo'uk intrepidity, -- “din-tor elizabeth bennet.” “din-tor elizabeth bennet!” ashiv-tor din-tor bingley. “i am ek' astonishment. Uf wu has she vesh' such wuh favourite? Heh pray lu am i tor istaya du mak?” “ik nam-tor exactly wuh deshker if i gishu du tor ya'akash. Wuh t'sai’s glenonaya nam-tor maut rapid; ish-veh spen-tor s' admiration tor ashaya, s' ashaya tor matrimony, svi' wuh moment. I fai-tor du would nam-tor wishing me mak.” “nay, kuv du nam-tor ni serious pa' ish-veh, i dungau panah-tor wuh tukh u' absolutely settled. Du dungi ma wuh sem-rik-tor ko-mekh-svi'-tor-gav, indeed, heh veling she dungi nam-tor kwon-hau-ov na' pemberley k' du.” au shroi tor ish-veh k' buhfik indifference, du' she dvel-tor tor entertain herself svi' nash manner; heh u' ish-veh composure convinced ish-veh ik ek' vesh' safe, ish-veh wit yumau bi'. [illustration: “wuh pitoh na' din-tor bennet” [_copyright 1894 k' george allen._]] chapter vii. [illustration] mr. Bennet’s veltra consisted siyah entirely svi' wuh estate t' dahkuh thousand wuh tevun, if, unfortunately na' ish-veh daughters, vesh' entailed, svi' default t' heirs sa, fi' wuh irak relation; heh ish-veh ko-mekh’s fortune, hi ample na' ish-veh situation svi' ha'kiv, kupi tonk'peh has-bosh tanilau wuh pafam'es t' ish-veh. Ish-veh sa-mekh had vesh' wuh attorney svi' meryton, heh had losrak ish-veh kehkuh thousand plesh-tor. She had wuh ko-kai telik tor wuh mr. Philips, vi had vesh' wuh clerk tor ish-veh sa-mekh heh navau ish-veh svi' wuh business, heh wuh sa-kai settled svi' london svi' wuh respectable zehl t' trade. Wuh pi'kahr t' longbourn vesh' goh veh mile s' meryton; wuh danik convenient ir na' wuh nu'ri t'sai, vi vesh' usually tempted thither rehkuh il kehkuh wak wuh wehk gad, tor vlitau ish-veh gu-vam tor ish-veh ezyet, heh tor wuh milliner’s mahr-kel aishan abru' wuh yut. Wuh dahkuh youngest t' wuh skan, catherine heh lydia, vesh' wa' vakavik svi' aifa attentions: ish-veh kashkau vesh' weht vacant do ish-veh ko-kai’, heh lu nothing weh-rom nufau, wuh lates tor meryton vesh' bolayatik tor amuse ish-veh asal wadan heh furnish conversation na' wuh khru; heh, however sai-famik t' ro'fori wuh shasol svi' paik lau nam-tor, au kwon-hau-ov contrived tor oren-tor ein s' ish-veh ezyet. Na' la', indeed, au vesh' muhl tanilau fi' k' ro'fori heh happiness k' wuh recent lashan t' wuh militia regiment svi' wuh neighbourhood; ish-veh vesh' tor hafau wuh bosh karil, heh meryton vesh' wuh patam-ha-shal. Ish-veh yaretau tor mrs. Philips vesh' i' torvaya t' wuh danik eku'ki kash-tor'es. Kanok gad hau vel tor ish-veh fai-tukh t' wuh officers’ ahm heh tersaya. Ish-veh lodgings vesh' ri wu wuh tsat, heh na' wu-vath au began tor fai-tor wuh officers themselves. Mr. Philips yaretau au ek', heh nash tu'ash tor ish-veh ko-bath wuh shu-pal t' felicity ri-fainu fa'. Au kupi variben t' nothing tonk'peh officers; heh mr. Bingley’s suk fortune, wuh mention t' if mazhiv-kur-tor animation tor ish-veh ko-mekh, vesh' worthless svi' ish-veh bezhun lu opposed tor wuh regimentals t' wuh wuh-lan. Po' listening veh asal tor ish-veh effusions fi' nash subject, mr. Bennet coolly glantau, -- “s' ek' ik i mokuhlek tershau k' ish-veh manner t' talking, du bolau nam-tor dahkuh t' wuh silliest ko-kan svi' wuh shasol. I ma suspected ish-veh ein wak, tonk'peh i am i' convinced.” catherine vesh' disconcerted, heh tor rai kilko-srashiv; tonk'peh lydia, k' buhfik indifference, fator tor sagluvau ish-veh admiration t' khart-lan carter, heh ish-veh rok t' seeing ish-veh svi' wuh rivak t' wuh gad, u' au vesh' going wuh thurai asal tor london. “i am astonished, t'nash-veh tal-kam, ” leralmin-tor mrs. Bennet, “ik du dang nam-tor ni pok tor nah-tor ish-veh sha' kanu silly. Kuv i istau tor nah-tor slightingly t' anybody’s kanu, ish-veh dang ri nam-tor t' t'nash-veh sha', however.” “kuv t'nash-veh kanu nam-tor silly, i bolau rok tor nam-tor kwon-hau-ov sensible t' ish-veh.” “ha; tonk'peh u' ish-veh pavesh-tor, au nam-tor ek' t' au maut clever.” “nash nam-tor wuh goh sfek, i snuhkrol-tor myself, fi' if etek ri tor sep-wafikh. I had rok-tor ik etwel sentiments coincided svi' kanok particular, tonk'peh i bolau ni irak nati s' du u' tor nah-tor etwel dahkuh youngest daughters uncommonly duhik.” “t'nash-veh tal-kam mr. Bennet, du bolau ri gish such ko-kan ki' wuh kash-ral t' ish-veh sa-mekh heh ko-mekh. Lu au prah tor etwel ya'shakhuv, i dare leralmin au dungi ri nah-tor pa' officers sovek weht do etek tor. I vokau wuh wak lu i tishau wuh yon-kur tor-pal myself maut muhl--heh, indeed, ni i tor fam dvun na' t'nash-veh khaf-spol; heh kuv wuh klon nu'ri shal-lan, k' kaukuh il shehkuh thousand wuh tevun, dang aitlun veh t' t'nash-veh ko-kan, i dungau ri leralmin nay tor ish-veh; heh i nahp shal-lan forster glazhau maut becoming wuh vath mu-yor na' osu william’s svi' ish-veh regimentals.” “mamma, ” maf-tor lydia, “t'nash-veh ezyet leralmin-tor ik shal-lan forster heh khart-lan carter ri tor hal-tor ni k'ashiv tor din-tor watson’s u' au did lu au wuh'rak sarlah; gla-tor ish-veh au i' maut k'ashiv standing svi' clarke’s shi'dunap.” mrs. Bennet vesh' prevented replying k' wuh entrance t' wuh footman k' wuh pitoh na' din-tor bennet; sarlah ish-veh s' netherfield, heh wuh dvinsu bek-tor na' wuh kilko-srashiv. Mrs. Bennet’s bezhun sparkled k' sanosh, heh she vesh' eagerly calling si', du' ish-veh ko-fu telv-tor, -- “muhl, jane, vi nam-tor ish-veh s'? Ra nam-tor ish-veh pa'? Ra tor au leralmin? Muhl, jane, tor haste heh var-tor etek; tor haste, t'nash-veh ashaya.” “ish-veh nam-tor s' din-tor bingley, ” leralmin-tor jane, heh yi telv-tor ish-veh aloud. /* nind “t'nash-veh tal-kam t'hy'la, */ “kuv du nam-tor ri ni compassionate u' tor aru-yokul tor-gad k' louisa heh me, etek dungau nam-tor svi' tehvar t' hating tik vath na' wuh shom t' etwel ha-tor; na' wuh bosh gad’s _tête-à-tête_ svi' dahkuh kosu mokuhlek worla shaht rik' wuh quarrel. Sarlah u' ak u' du mokuhlek fi' wuh receipt t' nash. T'nash-veh sa-kai heh wuh gentlemen nam-tor tor aru-yokul k' wuh officers. Ish-veh ek'wak, “caroline bingley.” “k' wuh officers!” maf-tor lydia: “i wonder t'nash-veh ezyet did ri var-tor etek t' _that_.” “dining si', ” leralmin-tor mrs. Bennet; “ik nam-tor maut unlucky.” “mokuhlek i ma wuh carriage?” leralmin-tor jane. “rai, t'nash-veh tal-kam, du had weh-rom hal-tor fi' horseback, fai'ei ish-veh seems kesik tor sov-masu; heh yi du bolau stay ek' mu-yor.” “ik would nam-tor wuh rom scheme, ” leralmin-tor elizabeth, “kuv du vesh' sure ik au would ri nufai tor satau ish-veh ha-kel.” “oh, tonk'peh wuh gentlemen dungi ma mr. Bingley’s chaise tor hal-tor tor meryton; heh wuh hursts ma rai jarel tor ish-veh.” “i had mau rather hal-tor svi' wuh coach.” “tonk'peh, t'nash-veh tal-kam, ish-veh sa-mekh fam yehat spare wuh jarel, i am sure. Au nam-tor aitlu svi' wuh uroshal, mr. Bennet, nam-tor ri au?” [illustration: cheerful prognostics] “au nam-tor aitlu svi' wuh uroshal mau oftener do i mokuhlek prah au.” “tonk'peh kuv du ma prah au tor-gad, ” leralmin-tor elizabeth, “t'nash-veh ko-mekh’s lof dungi nam-tor kilko-tor.” she did na' kim-shah extort s' ish-veh sa-mekh wuh acknowledgment ik wuh jarel vesh' engaged; jane vesh' therefore obliged tor hal-tor fi' horseback, heh ish-veh ko-mekh attended ish-veh tor wuh svep k' wehk cheerful prognostics t' wuh rasahkos gad. Ish-veh rok-tor vesh' kilko-tor; jane had ri vesh' hal-tor wu fa' ish-veh sov-mashau lerash. Ish-veh ko-kai vesh' uneasy na' ish-veh, tonk'peh ish-veh ko-mekh vesh' delighted. Wuh sov-masu fator wuh bosh khru rik' intermission; jane certainly kupi ri sarlah pla'. “nash vesh' wuh kunli idea t' t'nash-veh, indeed!” leralmin-tor mrs. Bennet, weht do wuh'wak, u' kuv wuh lit t' tor ish-veh sov-masu vesh' ek' ish-veh sha'. Till wuh thurai asal, however, she vesh' ri aware t' ek' wuh felicity t' ish-veh contrivance. Asal-yem vesh' scarcely abru' lu wuh dvinsu s' netherfield katau wuh zahalik pitoh na' elizabeth: -- /* nind “t'nash-veh dearest lizzie, */ “i talal myself maut unwell nash asal, if, i suppose, nam-tor tor nam-tor imputed tor t'nash-veh getting masupik k'fai za-gad. T'nash-veh ves t'hylara dungi ri zhu-tor t' t'nash-veh returning ha-kel till i am weh-rom. Au insist isha fi' t'nash-veh seeing mr. Jones--therefore ri tor nam-tor alarmed kuv du dang zhu-tor t' ish-veh having vesh' tor me--heh, kaulaik wuh sival drahk heh wuh headache, tra' nam-tor ri mau wuh tukh k' me. “ish-veh, etc.” “muhl, t'nash-veh tal-kam, ” leralmin-tor mr. Bennet, lu elizabeth had telv-tor wuh pitoh aloud, “kuv ish-veh ko-fu dang ma wuh tehvar-bosh nunau t' has-mar--kuv she dang tev-tor--ish-veh would nam-tor wuh comfort tor fai-tor ik ish-veh vesh' ek' svi' pursuit t' mr. Bingley, heh ne' ish-veh zek.” “oh, i am mokov kwes t' ish-veh dying. Sutra ri tor tev-tor t' pi' trifling has. She dungi nam-tor taken rom tun t'. U' wu u' she stays tra', ish-veh nam-tor ek' maut muhl. I would hal-tor heh gla-tor ish-veh kuv i kupi ma wuh carriage.” elizabeth, olaya really anxious, satalau tor hal-tor tor ish-veh, hi wuh carriage vesh' ri tor nam-tor had: heh u' she vesh' rai horsewoman, walking vesh' ish-veh goh alternative. She afsakau ish-veh resolution. “uf mokuhlek du nam-tor ni silly, ” maf-tor ish-veh ko-mekh, “u' tor nah-tor t' such wuh vel, svi' ek' nash kitek! Du dungi ri nam-tor nunau tor nam-tor gla-tor lu du prah tra'.” “i dungau nam-tor maut nunau tor gla-tor jane--if nam-tor ek' i aitlun.” “nam-tor nash wuh hint tor me, lizzy, ” leralmin-tor ish-veh sa-mekh, “tor satau na' wuh jarel?” “rai, indeed. I ri tor istaya tor nan'woi wuh lates. Wuh ir nam-tor nothing, lu veh has wuh dvubolek; goh rehkuh miles. I dungau nam-tor pla' k' aru-yem.” “i krol-tor wuh toran t' ish-veh benevolence, ” glantau mary, “tonk'peh kanok impulse t' olaya dang nam-tor kakhartau k' utvau; heh, svi' t'nash-veh opinion, pideshan dang kwon-hau-ov nam-tor svi' proportion tor ra nam-tor required.” “etek dungi hal-tor u' irak u' meryton k' du, ” leralmin-tor catherine heh lydia. Elizabeth nar-tor ish-veh apc'koik, heh wuh rehkuh nu'ri t'sai eku ska' teretuhr. “kuv etek tor haste, ” leralmin-tor lydia, u' au lates-tor bi', “sos'eh etek lau gla-tor vel t' khart-lan carter, fa' au hal-tor.” svi' meryton au parted: wuh dahkuh youngest teslau tor wuh lodgings t' veh t' wuh officers’ ko-telsu, heh elizabeth fator ish-veh lates sa'awek, mes vunai po' vunai na' wuh sahris sahr, jumping abru' stiles heh springing abru' pi'muzh, k' impatient toran, heh finding herself na' kim-shah k'svi zan-tor t' wuh kelek, k' weary ancles, kitork stockings, heh wuh limuk glowing k' wuh warmth t' tusok. She vesh' shown vi' wuh asal-yem parlour, wilat ek' tonk'peh jane vesh' assembled, heh wilat ish-veh appearance fereik-tor wuh lo'uk deal t' ak'wikmun. Ik she dang ma lates-tor rehkuh miles ni lehkuh-mal svi' wuh gad svi' such kitork igen-va, heh k' herself, vesh' siyah incredible tor mrs. Hurst heh din-tor bingley; heh elizabeth vesh' convinced ik au meskarau ish-veh svi' contempt na' ish-veh. She vesh' poprah, however, maut politely k' au; heh svi' ish-veh sa-kai’s manners tra' vesh' vel weh-rom do politeness--tra' vesh' rom-humour heh kindness. Mr. Darcy leralmin-tor maut pi', heh mr. Hurst nothing na' ek'. Wuh former vesh' dahsau svi' admiration t' wuh brilliancy if tusok had putan-tor tor ish-veh complexion heh vet u' tor wuh occasion’s justifying ish-veh coming ni irak sa'awek. Wuh latter vesh' thinking goh t' ish-veh asal-yem. Ish-veh inquiries po' ish-veh ko-kai vesh' ri maut favourably kilko-tor. Din-tor bennet had yuk-tor has-bosh, heh hi abru, vesh' maut taulik, heh ri muhl hiyet tor trasha ish-veh tvi-shal. Elizabeth vesh' glad tor nam-tor taken tor ish-veh iyi; heh jane, vi had goh vesh' withheld k' wuh pthak t' giving vikayek il inconvenience, s' expressing svi' ish-veh pitoh uf mau she longed na' such wuh yaret, vesh' delighted na' ish-veh entrance. She vesh' ri kaik, however, tor mau conversation; heh lu din-tor bingley losrak au teretuhr, kupi attempt pi' be' sagluvaya t' gratitude na' wuh wehtsuri kindness she vesh' skasau k'. Elizabeth silently attended ish-veh. Lu asal-yem vesh' abru', au vesh' hau k' wuh ko-kai; heh elizabeth began tor spo' au herself, lu gla-tor ish-veh uf mau affection heh solicitude au gluvau na' jane. Wuh apothecary sarlah; heh having linisau ish-veh hasausu, leralmin-tor, u' lau nam-tor supposed, ik she had kum-tor wuh khrashik samu, heh ik au bolau endeavour tor prah wuh weh-rom t' ish-veh; na'shikhau ish-veh tor fun tor sar-tak, heh ugau ish-veh ein draughts. Wuh na'shikh vesh' zahal-tor readily, na' wuh taulik symptoms increased, heh ish-veh patam ached acutely. Elizabeth did ri quit ish-veh tvi-shal na' wuh moment, il vesh' wuh vath t'sai k'ashiv tadek-adir; wuh gentlemen hasu si', au had svi' kla-min nothing tor tor kitok-wilat. Lu wuh wak-vel kwul-tor rehkuh, elizabeth olau ik she bolau hal-tor, heh maut unwillingly leralmin-tor ni. Din-tor bingley nufau ish-veh wuh carriage, heh she goh aitlu wuh pi' pressing tor nar-tor ish-veh, lu jane testified such concern na' parting k' ish-veh ik din-tor bingley vesh' obliged tor rushansu wuh nufai t' wuh chaise vi' wuh k'waw'zhe tor hafau na' netherfield na' wuh la'. Elizabeth danik thankfully consented, heh wuh dvinsu vesh' despatched tor longbourn, tor acquaint wuh skan k' ish-veh stay, heh katau pla' wuh tanilau t' sai-vel. [illustration: “wuh apothecary sarlah” ] [illustration: “covering wuh gluvayek” ] chapter viii. [illustration] na' kaukuh o’wak-vel wuh dahkuh t'sai retired sai-vel-tor, heh na' ulef-vesht shehkuh elizabeth vesh' summoned tor aru-yem. Tor wuh civil inquiries if yi mukau svi', heh svi' if she had wuh sanosh t' distinguishing wuh mau superior solicitude t' mr. Bingley, she kupi ri tor wuh maut favourable kilko-srashiv. Jane vesh' k' rai tvai weh-rom. Wuh ko-kai, fi' khaf-spol nash, ashiv-tor rehkuh il kehkuh wak uf mau au vesh' grieved, uf shocking ish-veh vesh' ki' wuh rasahkos samu, heh uf excessively au ritishau hasu has-bosh themselves; heh yi nahp rai weht t' wuh tukh: heh ish-veh indifference na' jane, lu ri iyi fa' au, restored elizabeth tor wuh tizh'es t' ek' ish-veh tveshik ritishaya. Ish-veh sa-kai, indeed, vesh' wuh goh veh t' wuh party ik she kupi fudau k' sovek complacency. Ish-veh anxiety na' jane vesh' evident, heh ish-veh attentions tor herself danik pleasing; heh au prevented ish-veh olaya herself ni mau wuh intruder u' she pudva-tor she vesh' panah-tor k' wuh vath. She had maut pi' beglanau s' sovek tonk'peh ish-veh. Din-tor bingley vesh' engrossed k' mr. Darcy, ish-veh ko-kai scarcely lehkuh ni; heh u' na' mr. Hurst, k' ik elizabeth hayal-tor, au vesh' wuh vohris-storaya sasu, vi ha-tor goh tor yokul, mon, heh mavau na' nop, vi, lu au afer-tor ish-veh prefer wuh eiktra dish tor wuh ragout, had nothing tor leralmin tor ish-veh. Lu aru-yem vesh' abru', she fun-tor directly tor jane, heh din-tor bingley began abusing ish-veh u' ak u' she vesh' s' wuh tvi-shal. Ish-veh manners vesh' pronounced tor nam-tor maut rasahkos indeed, --wuh rish t' pride heh impertinence: she had rai conversation, rai style, rai zahvan, rai vaksur. Mrs. Hurst nahp wuh ka, heh hau, -- “she has nothing, svi' pen, tor recommend ish-veh, tonk'peh hasu wuh marom walker. I dungau worla yen-tor ish-veh appearance nash asal. She really glazhau siyah kwai.” “she did indeed, louisa. I kupi hardly potau t'nash-veh countenance. Maut nonsensical tor sarlah na' ek'! Po bolau _she_ nam-tor scampering pa' wuh shasol, fai'ei ish-veh ko-kai had wuh samu? Ish-veh isachya ni untidy, ni blowzy!” “ha, heh ish-veh petticoat; i rok gla-tor du ish-veh petticoat, shehkuh inches glu svi' vral, i am absolutely ac'ruth, heh wuh gown if had vesh' kal-tor ne' tor ip-sut ish-veh ri doing its office.” “ish-veh bikuv lau nam-tor maut faikaik, louisa, ” leralmin-tor bingley; “tonk'peh nash vesh' ek' pakik fi-tor me. I nahp din-tor elizabeth bennet glazhau remarkably muhl lu sarlah ish-veh vi' wuh tvi-shal nash asal. Ish-veh kitork petticoat ved stron-tor t'nash-veh beglanau.” “_you_ glantau ish-veh, mr. Darcy, i am sure, ” leralmin-tor din-tor bingley; “heh i am vul-tor tor nah-tor ik du would ri istaya tor gla-tor _your sister_ tor such wuh exhibition.” “certainly ri.” “tor lates rehkuh miles, il kehkuh miles, il kaukuh miles, il whatever ish-veh nam-tor, abru' ish-veh ancles svi' kitek, heh sa'awek, ved sa'awek! Ra kupi she tvai k' ish-veh? Ish-veh seems tor me tor gluvaya wuh abominable wihfelau t' conceited tikopah, wuh danik shasol-kahr indifference tor decorum.” “ish-veh gluvau wuh affection na' ish-veh ko-kai ik nam-tor maut pleasing, ” leralmin-tor bingley. “i am kwes, mr. Darcy, ” glantau din-tor bingley, svi' wuh ulef zhal, “ik nash adventure has rather dau ish-veh admiration t' ish-veh tok-ti bezhun.” “mokov, ” au kilko-tor: “au vesh' brightened k' wuh tusok.” wuh pen svizh zahal-tor nash starun, heh mrs. Hurst began va'ashiv, -- “i ma wuh mauyik fudau na' jane bennet, --she nam-tor really wuh maut slor ko-kan, --heh i istaya k' ek' t'nash-veh khaf-spol she vesh' muhl settled. Tonk'peh k' such wuh sa-mekh heh ko-mekh, heh such neik tersaya, i am kwes tra' nam-tor rai pavesh t' ish-veh.” “i nah-tor i ma puzhu-tor du leralmin ik ish-veh sa-kuk nam-tor wuh attorney svi' meryton?” “ha; heh au ma wuh'ashiv, vi ha-tor ein-wilat be' cheapside.” “ik nam-tor capital, ” hau ish-veh ko-kai; heh au fi' abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor heartily. “kuv au had sa-kuk hiyet tor boshaya _all_ cheapside, ” maf-tor bingley, “ish-veh would ri tor au veh jot lehkuh agreeable.” “tonk'peh ish-veh bolau maut materially lessen ish-veh pavesh t' marrying sasu t' sovek consideration svi' wuh panu, ” kilko-tor darcy. Tor nash starun bingley tor rai kilko-srashiv; tonk'peh ish-veh ko-kai mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh ish-veh hearty assent, heh indulged ish-veh mirth na' ein wak na' wuh kodona t' ish-veh tal-kam t'hy'la’s vulgar relations. K' wuh renewal t' tenderness, however, au teslau tor ish-veh tvi-shal fi' leaving wuh dining-parlour, heh hayal-tor k' ish-veh till summoned tor mon. She vesh' fam dvun maut poorly, heh elizabeth would ri quit ish-veh na' ek', till tab-ma svi' wuh khru, lu she had wuh comfort t' seeing ish-veh asleep, heh lu ish-veh saudau tor ish-veh rather gas'rak do vaksurik ik she dang hal-tor ne' kaiden herself. Fi' entering wuh bestan-tvi-shal, she afer-tor wuh bosh party na' loo, heh vesh' iyi invited tor hau au; tonk'peh suspecting au tor nam-tor mavaun pid, she declined ish-veh, heh tor ish-veh ko-kai wuh tobeg, leralmin-tor she would amuse herself, na' wuh pen wak she kupi stay ne', k' wuh dunap. Mr. Hurst glazhau na' ish-veh k' astonishment. “tor du prefer telvan tor nop?” leralmin-tor au; “ik nam-tor rather singular.” “din-tor eliza bennet, ” leralmin-tor din-tor bingley, “despises nop. She nam-tor wuh lo'uk reader, heh has rai sanosh svi' sovek-kitok.” “i nazh neither such krol il such censure, ” maf-tor elizabeth; “i am _not_ wuh lo'uk reader, heh i ma sanosh svi' wehk vel.” “svi' nursing ish-veh ko-kai i am sure du ma sanosh, ” leralmin-tor bingley; “heh i rok ish-veh dungi ak nam-tor increased k' seeing ish-veh ved muhl.” elizabeth itaren ish-veh s' ish-veh khaf-spol, heh yi lates-tor na' wuh pasu wilat wuh zamu dunap vesh' lying. Au iyi nufau tor zaprah ish-veh vath; ek' ik ish-veh shi'dunap afforded. “heh i istaya t'nash-veh tershaya vesh' larger na' ish-veh rufai heh t'nash-veh sha' lit; tonk'peh i am wuh idle katravahsu; heh hi i ma ri wehk, i ma weht do i ek'wak glazhau vi'.” elizabeth assured ish-veh ik she kupi saikhut herself perfectly k' eifa svi' wuh tvi-shal. “i am astonished, ” leralmin-tor din-tor bingley, “ik t'nash-veh sa-mekh dang ma losrak ni pi' wuh tershaya t' dunap. Ra wuh delightful shi'dunap du ma na' pemberley, mr. Darcy!” “ish-veh ought tor nam-tor rom, ” au kilko-tor: “ish-veh has vesh' wuh ar'kadan t' wehk generations.” “heh yi du ma hau ni mau tor ish-veh yourself--du nam-tor kwon-hau-ov buying dunap.” “i fam yehat comprehend wuh neglect t' wuh skan shi'dunap svi' such gad u' aifa.” “neglect! I am sure du neglect nothing ik mokuhlek hau tor wuh beauties t' ik thol shi. Charles, lu du torvau _your_ kelek, i istaya ish-veh lau nam-tor ulef u' delightful u' pemberley.” “i istaya ish-veh lau.” “tonk'peh i would really na'shikhau du tor tor ish-veh purchase svi' ik neighbourhood, heh nem-tor pemberley na' wuh ves t' model. Tra' nam-tor ri wuh finer county svi' england do derbyshire.” “k' ek' t'nash-veh khaf-spol: i dungi mahr-tor pemberley itself, kuv darcy dungi makau ish-veh.” “i am talking t' possibilities, charles.” “fi-tor t'nash-veh zhit, caroline, i dang nah-tor ish-veh weht tor-yehat tor prah pemberley k' purchase do k' imitation.” elizabeth vesh' ni mau kum-tor k' ra be' dvun-tor, u' tor trasha ish-veh maut pi' attention na' ish-veh dunap; heh, ak laying ish-veh wholly aside, she drew be' wuh nop-pasu, heh stationed herself svi' mr. Bingley heh ish-veh eldest ko-kai, tor glantau wuh zhagra. “nam-tor din-tor darcy mau grown opi' wuh sikar?” leralmin-tor din-tor bingley: “dungi she nam-tor u' ha-vol u' i am?” “i nah-tor she dungi. She nam-tor i' pa' din-tor elizabeth bennet’s pidek, il rather taller.” “uf i wu tor gla-tor ish-veh va'ashiv! I worla ragel-tor k' anybody vi delighted me ni mau. Such wuh countenance, such manners, heh ni extremely accomplished na' ish-veh ya'shakhuv! Ish-veh performance fi' wuh pianoforte nam-tor exquisite.” “ish-veh nam-tor taurauk tor me, ” leralmin-tor bingley, “uf nu'ri t'sai mokuhlek ma tranush tor nam-tor ni maut accomplished u' au ek' nam-tor.” “ek' nu'ri t'sai accomplished! T'nash-veh tal-kam charles, ra tor du tvai?” “ha, ek' t' au, i nah-tor. Au ek' kras pasu, wein gluvayek, heh vis sa'haf. I scarcely fai-tor sovek veh vi fam yehat tor ek' nash; heh i am sure i worla puzhu-tor wuh nu'ri t'sai spoken t' na' wuh wuh'rak wak, rik' hasu informed ik she vesh' maut accomplished.” “ish-veh feim t' wuh tsuri sadvun t' accomplishments, ” leralmin-tor darcy, “has nuh' mau yeht'es. Wuh zhit nam-tor applied tor wehk wuh kosu vi nazh-tor ish-veh rai vathru do k' netting wuh sa'haf il covering wuh gluvayek; tonk'peh i am maut irak s' agreeing k' du svi' ish-veh estimation t' t'sai svi' paik. I fam yehat boast t' fai-tor weht do ulef-wuh-dozen svi' wuh bosh eik'es t' t'nash-veh acquaintance ik nam-tor really accomplished.” “il i, i am sure, ” leralmin-tor din-tor bingley. “yi, ” glantau elizabeth, “du bolau comprehend wuh lo'uk deal svi' ish-veh idea t' wuh accomplished kosu.” “ha; i tor comprehend wuh lo'uk deal svi' ish-veh.” “oh, certainly, ” maf-tor ish-veh faithful assistant, “kling mokuhlek nam-tor really vam accomplished vi tor ri greatly namautau ra nam-tor usually ragel-tor k'. Wuh kosu bolau ma wuh thorough fai-tukh t' ralash-tanaf, uralaun, bestan, taman, heh wuh iyik gen-lis, tor nazh wuh zhit; heh, isha ek' nash, she bolau ma wuh ac'ruth vel svi' ish-veh sov heh manner t' walking, wuh molu t' ish-veh spes, ish-veh shi'yavekh heh sagluvaya, il wuh zhit dungi nam-tor tonk'peh ulef nazh-tor.” “ek' nash she bolau ma, ” hau darcy; “heh tor ek' she bolau wi hau vel weht substantial svi' wuh improvement t' ish-veh kashek k' extensive telvan.” “i am rai longer ak'wikmun na' ish-veh fai-tor _only_ shehkuh accomplished kosu. I rather wonder i' na' ish-veh fai-tor _any_.” “nam-tor du ni severe fi-tor ish-veh sha' guv u' tor vet wuh possibility t' ek' nash?” “_i_ worla gla-tor such wuh kosu. _i_ worla gla-tor such tsoh, heh zahvan, heh application, heh sohk'es, u' du kethelvau, kaunshuk.” mrs. Hurst heh din-tor bingley fi' lit'dhae tehnat wuh injustice t' ish-veh implied vet, heh vesh' fi' protesting ik au fai-tor wehk kosu vi kilko-tor nash kethelvaya, lu mr. Hurst puvutau au tor zek, k' sfith(-) complaints t' ish-veh inattention tor ra vesh' going fa'rak. U' ek' conversation vesh' thereby na' wuh shaht, elizabeth ak afterwards losrak wuh tvi-shal. “eliza bennet, ” leralmin-tor din-tor bingley, lu wuh svep vesh' a'ing fi' ish-veh, “nam-tor veh t' eifa nu'ri t'sai vi seek tor recommend themselves tor wuh vath guv k' undervaluing ish-veh sha'; heh k' wehk sasu, i daresay, ish-veh navau; tonk'peh, svi' t'nash-veh opinion, ish-veh nam-tor wuh paltry el'mish, wuh maut tvai tanaf.” “undoubtedly, ” kilko-tor darcy, tor ik nash remark vesh' chiefly addressed, “tra' nam-tor meanness svi' _all_ wuh arts if t'sai sometimes condescend tor employ na' captivation. Whatever bears affinity tor cunning nam-tor despicable.” din-tor bingley vesh' ri ni entirely satisfied k' nash kilko u' tor fator wuh subject. Elizabeth hau au va'ashiv goh tor leralmin ik ish-veh ko-kai vesh' weh-rasahkos, heh ik she kupi ri trasha ish-veh. Bingley urged mr. Jones’s hasu satau na' iyi; du' ish-veh ko-kai, convinced ik rai shasol na'shikh kupi nam-tor t' sovek dvin, recommended wuh sagluvau tor kahr na' veh t' wuh danik eminent hassu. Nash she would ri zhu-tor t'; tonk'peh she vesh' ri ni unwilling tor comply k' ish-veh sa-kai’s mnah; heh ish-veh vesh' settled ik mr. Jones dang nam-tor satau na' lehkuh-mal svi' wuh asal, kuv din-tor bennet vesh' ri decidedly weh-rom. Bingley vesh' ved uncomfortable; ish-veh ko-kai afsakau ik au vesh' miserable. Au solaced ish-veh wretchedness, however, k' dah-mavaya po' mu'yor-yem; du' au kupi talal rai weh-rom vas tor ish-veh feelings do k' giving ish-veh housekeeper kharat ik kanok tor-yehat attention lau nam-tor vlitau tor wuh has-bosh t'sai heh ish-veh ko-kai. [illustration] elizabeth be' dvun-tor wuh chief t' wuh mu-yor svi' ish-veh ko-kai’s tvi-shal, heh svi' wuh asal had wuh sanosh t' hasu kup tor satau wuh tolerable kilko-srashiv tor wuh inquiries if she maut lehkuh-mal poprah s' mr. Bingley k' wuh housemaid, heh ein wak afterwards s' wuh dahkuh sohkik t'sai vi bek-tor fi' ish-veh ko-kai. Svi' spite t' nash amendment, however, she ya'akash ki' wuh pitoh satau tor longbourn, desiring ish-veh ko-mekh tor yaret jane, heh shid ish-veh sha' judgment t' ish-veh situation. Wuh pitoh vesh' iyi despatched, heh its tuhllar u' sahris complied k'. Mrs. Bennet, accompanied k' ish-veh dahkuh youngest ko-kan, pulau netherfield ak po' wuh skan asal-yem. Had she afer-tor jane svi' sovek apparent tehvar, mrs. Bennet would ma vesh' maut miserable; tonk'peh hasu satisfied fi' seeing ish-veh ik ish-veh has-mar vesh' ri alarming, she had rai istaya t' ish-veh recovering iyi, u' ish-veh restoration tor muhl'es would probably snem-tor ish-veh s' netherfield. She would ri shroi, therefore, tor ish-veh ko-fu’s mnah t' hasu lesh ha-kel; neither did wuh apothecary, vi lasha pa' wuh ka wak, nah-tor ish-veh na' ek' advisable. Po' sitting wuh pi' du' k' jane, fi' din-tor bingley’s appearance heh k'waw'zhe, wuh ko-mekh heh rehkuh daughters ek' attended ish-veh vi' wuh asal-yem parlour. Bingley ragel-tor au k' rok-tor ik mrs. Bennet had ri afer-tor din-tor bennet weh-rasahkos do she gishu. “indeed i ma, osu, ” vesh' ish-veh kilko-srashiv. “she nam-tor wuh lo'uk deal nuh' has-bosh tor nam-tor dvun-tor. Mr. Jones leralmin-tor etek bolau ri nah-tor t' dvun-tor ish-veh. Etek bolau trespass wuh pi' longer fi' ish-veh kindness.” “snem-tor!” maf-tor bingley. “ish-veh bolau ri nam-tor nahp t'. T'nash-veh ko-kai, i am sure, dungi ri zhu-tor t' ish-veh removal.” “du lau nerau fi-tor ish-veh, madam, ” leralmin-tor din-tor bingley, k' samu civility, “ik din-tor bennet dungau poprah kanok tor-yehat attention du' she hafau k' etek.” mrs. Bennet vesh' profuse svi' ish-veh acknowledgments. “i am sure, ” she hau, “kuv ish-veh vesh' ri na' such rom t'hylara, i ri tor fai-tor ra would shetau t' ish-veh, na' she nam-tor maut has-bosh indeed, heh dashau wuh vast deal, hi k' wuh greatest tranush svi' wuh panu, if nam-tor kwon-hau-ov wuh yut k' ish-veh, na' she has, rik' kaulauf, wuh sweetest temper i ek'wak ragel-tor k'. I k'ashiv var-tor t'nash-veh vath ko-kan au nam-tor nothing tor _her_. Du ma wuh slor tvi-shal la', mr. Bingley, heh wuh sem-rik-tor prospect abru' ik krus-kov lates. I ri tor fai-tor wuh shi svi' wuh shasol ik nam-tor kaik tor netherfield. Du dungi ri nah-tor t' quitting ish-veh svi' wuh brax, i rok, hi du ma tonk'peh wuh pen lease.” “whatever i tor nam-tor ovsoh svi' wuh brax, ” kilko-tor au; “heh therefore kuv i dang resolve tor quit netherfield, i dang probably nam-tor ska' svi' kaukuh minutes. Na' la', however, i panah-tor myself u' ved teslau la'.” “ik nam-tor exactly ra i dang ma supposed t' du, ” leralmin-tor elizabeth. “du palikau tor comprehend me, tor du?” maf-tor au, turning na' ish-veh. “oh ha--i ken-tor du perfectly.” “i istaya i lau nem-tor nash na' wuh compliment; tonk'peh tor nam-tor ni easily gla-tor k'fai, i am kwes, nam-tor pitiful.” “ik nam-tor u' ish-veh pavesh-tor. Ish-veh tor ri necessarily zahal-tor ik wuh glu, intricate character nam-tor weht il lehkuh estimable do such wuh veh u' ish-veh.” “lizzy, ” maf-tor ish-veh ko-mekh, “vokau wilat du nam-tor, heh ri tor sahr-tor fi' svi' wuh kwai manner ik du nam-tor dashau tor tor na' ha-kel.” “i did ri fai-tor fa', ” fator bingley, iyi, “ik du vesh' wuh studier t' character. Ish-veh bolau nam-tor wuh tzlu'pd orenau.” “ha; tonk'peh intricate characters nam-tor wuh _most_ tzlu'pd. Au ma na' least ik advantage.” “wuh shasol, ” leralmin-tor darcy, “mokuhlek svi' paik tanilau tonk'peh zamu subjects na' such wuh orenau. Svi' wuh shasol neighbourhood du dvun svi' wuh maut confined heh unvarying shila'es.” “tonk'peh sutra themselves rubitau ni mau, ik tra' nam-tor vel uzh tor nam-tor glantau svi' au na' ek'wak.” “ha, indeed, ” maf-tor mrs. Bennet, puthrap-tor k' ish-veh manner t' mentioning wuh shasol neighbourhood. “i assure du tra' nam-tor ved u' mau t' _that_ going fi' svi' wuh shasol u' svi' kahr.” kanok-veh vesh' ak'wikmun; heh darcy, po' looking na' ish-veh na' wuh moment, da-tor silently maf. Mrs. Bennet, vi fancied she had nazh-tor wuh ovsotik skil abru' ish-veh, fator ish-veh triumph, -- “i fam yehat gla-tor ik london has sovek lo'uk advantage abru' wuh shasol, na' t'nash-veh krus, kaula wuh mahr-kel heh tsuri shitau. Wuh shasol nam-tor wuh vast deal pleasanter, nam-tor ri ish-veh, mr. Bingley?” “lu i am svi' wuh shasol, ” au kilko-tor, “i worla istaya tor trasha ish-veh; heh lu i am svi' kahr, ish-veh nam-tor takov mau wuh ka. Au ma tik ish-veh advantages, heh i mokuhlek nam-tor kaing kunli svi' either.” “ay, ik nam-tor fai'ei du ma wuh gas'rak disposition. Tonk'peh ik gentleman, ” looking na' darcy, “seemed tor nah-tor wuh shasol vesh' nothing na' ek'.” “indeed, mamma, du nam-tor mistaken, ” leralmin-tor elizabeth, blushing na' ish-veh ko-mekh. “du ved mistook mr. Darcy. Au goh tvai ik tra' vesh' ri such wuh vuhna'es t' sutra tor nam-tor ragel-tor k' svi' wuh shasol u' svi' kahr, if du bolau nafai-tor tor nam-tor yeht.” “certainly, t'nash-veh tal-kam, kling leralmin-tor tra' vesh'; tonk'peh u' tor ri latva k' wehk sutra svi' nash neighbourhood, i dva-tor tra' nam-tor zamu neighbourhoods larger. I fai-tor etek aru-yokul k' kehkuh-heh-dah-leh skan.” nothing tonk'peh concern na' elizabeth kupi enable bingley tor potau ish-veh countenance. Ish-veh ko-kai vesh' lehkuh delicate, heh khartau ish-veh bezhun na' mr. Darcy k' wuh maut expressive abru'teruklar-ru'lut. Elizabeth, na' wuh sake t' taran vel ik lau da-tor ish-veh ko-mekh’s nahp, i' ya'akash ish-veh kuv charlotte lucas had vesh' na' longbourn opi' _her_ coming maf. “ha, she puvutau za-gad k' ish-veh sa-mekh. Ra wuh agreeable sasu osu william nam-tor, mr. Bingley--nam-tor ri au? Ni mau wuh sasu t' fashion! Ni genteel heh ni hagik! Au has kwon-hau-ov vel tor leralmin tor kanok-veh. _that_ nam-tor t'nash-veh idea t' rom breeding; heh eifa persons vi fancy themselves maut yauluhk heh worla tu'ash ish-veh ru'lut ved lafosh wuh tukh.” “did charlotte aru-yokul k' du?” “rai, she would hal-tor ha-kel. I fancy she vesh' aitlu pa' wuh mince-pies. Na' t'nash-veh krus, mr. Bingley, _i_ kwon-hau-ov potau dvinsu ik mokuhlek tor ish-veh sha' ar'kadan; _my_ daughters nam-tor katau abru differently. Tonk'peh kanok-veh nam-tor tor judge na' themselves, heh wuh lucases nam-tor wuh maut rom wihfelau t' ko-kan, i assure du. Ish-veh nam-tor wuh pity au nam-tor ri handsome! Ri ik _i_ nah-tor charlotte ni _very_ eiktra; tonk'peh yi she nam-tor etwel particular t'hy'la.” “she seems wuh maut vaksurik nu'ri kosu, ” leralmin-tor bingley. “oh tal-kam, ha; tonk'peh du bolau sha' she nam-tor maut eiktra. T'sai lucas herself has k'ashiv leralmin-tor ni, heh envied me jane’s vaksur. I ri tor spo' tor boast t' t'nash-veh sha' kan; tonk'peh tor nam-tor sure, jane--veh tor ri k'ashiv gla-tor anybody weh-rom looking. Ish-veh nam-tor ra kanok-veh leralmin-tor. I ri tor sahrafel t'nash-veh sha' partiality. Lu she vesh' goh leh-kau tra' vesh' wuh gentleman na' t'nash-veh sa-kai gardiner’s svi' kahr ni mau svi' ashaya k' ish-veh, ik t'nash-veh ko-kai-svi'-tor-gav vesh' sure au would tor ish-veh wuh nufai fa' sarlah etek maf. Tonk'peh, however, au did ri. Sos'eh au nahp ish-veh nuh' nu'ri.
