However, au kitau ein zehl fi' ish-veh, heh maut takov au vesh'.” “heh ni shahtau ish-veh affection, ” leralmin-tor elizabeth, impatiently. “tra' has vesh' wehk wuh veh, i fancy, overcome svi' wuh ka yut. I wonder vi wuh'rak discovered wuh efficacy t' poetry svi' driving maf ashaya!” “i ma vesh' nam-tor-tor tor panah-tor poetry u' wuh _food_ t' ashaya, ” leralmin-tor darcy. “t' wuh tok-ti, stout, muhl-bosh ashaya ish-veh lau. Kanok-vei yem-mazhiv-kur-tor ra nam-tor karik already. Tonk'peh kuv ish-veh nam-tor goh wuh slight, wonil wihfelau t' inclination, i am convinced ish-veh rom sonnet dungi starve ish-veh entirely maf.” darcy goh abru'teruklar-ru'lut; heh wuh paik svizh if ensued tor elizabeth tremble lest ish-veh ko-mekh dang nam-tor exposing herself va'ashiv. She longed tor stariben, tonk'peh kupi nah-tor t' nothing tor leralmin; heh po' wuh pen silence mrs. Bennet began repeating ish-veh itaren tor mr. Bingley na' ish-veh kindness tor jane, k' wuh apology na' troubling ish-veh isha k' lizzy. Mr. Bingley vesh' unaffectedly civil svi' ish-veh kilko-srashiv, heh punekwitau ish-veh younger ko-kai tor nam-tor civil isha, heh leralmin ra wuh occasion required. She performed ish-veh krus, indeed, rik' mau graciousness, tonk'peh mrs. Bennet vesh' satisfied, heh ak afterwards ordered ish-veh carriage. Fi-tor nash glantokaya, wuh youngest t' ish-veh daughters shitau herself fa'rak. Wuh dahkuh ko-kan had vesh' zhalan tor tik vath du' wuh bosh yaret; heh wuh result t' ish-veh vesh', ik wuh youngest dang tax mr. Bingley k' having ugau fi' ish-veh wuh'rak coming vi' wuh shasol tor mazhiv-kur-tor wuh rin'k'n na' netherfield. Lydia vesh' wuh stout, muhl-grown ko-kan t' leh-kau, k' wuh tok-ti complexion heh rom-humoured countenance; wuh favourite k' ish-veh ko-mekh, t'vi affection had katau ish-veh vi' tsuri na' wuh lehkuh-mal ya'shakhuv. She had pid aushfa tam'a, heh wuh wihfelau t' malatik shal-consequence, if wuh attentions t' wuh officers, tor ik ish-veh sa-kuk’s rom aru-yem heh ish-veh sha' hagik manners recommended ish-veh, had increased vi' assurance. She vesh' maut kaik, therefore, tor shi'yavekh mr. Bingley fi' wuh subject t' wuh rin'k'n, heh abruptly reminded ish-veh t' ish-veh ugaya; hau, ik ish-veh would nam-tor wuh danik shameful vel svi' wuh panu kuv au did ri potau ish-veh. Ish-veh kilko-srashiv tor nash sudden nashiv-tor vesh' delightful tor ish-veh ko-mekh’s kaluk. “i am perfectly pok, i assure du, tor potau t'nash-veh engagement; heh, lu ish-veh ko-kai nam-tor recovered, du dungau, kuv du sanoi, ahm wuh maut gad t' wuh rin'k'n. Tonk'peh du would ri istaya tor nam-tor taman du' she nam-tor has-bosh?” lydia afsakau herself satisfied. “oh ha--ish-veh would nam-tor mau weh-rom tor bek-tor till jane vesh' muhl; heh k' ik wak, danik kesik, khart-lan carter would nam-tor na' meryton va'ashiv. Heh lu du ma putan-tor _your_ rin'k'n, ” she hau, “i dungau insist fi' ish-veh giving veh isha. I dungau var-tor shal-lan forster ish-veh dungi nam-tor ved wuh mesh kuv au tor ri.” mrs. Bennet heh ish-veh daughters yi trashu, heh elizabeth fun-tor instantly tor jane, leaving ish-veh sha' heh ish-veh relations’ kloshai tor wuh remarks t' wuh dahkuh t'sai heh mr. Darcy; wuh latter t' ik, however, kupi ri nam-tor fakovau fi' tor hau svi' ish-veh censure t' _her_, svi' spite t' ek' din-tor bingley’s witticisms fi' _fine eyes_. [illustration] chapter x. [illustration] wuh gad be' dvun-tor mau u' wuh gad fa' had ovsoh. Mrs. Hurst heh din-tor bingley had spent ein wadan t' wuh asal k' wuh invalid, vi fator, hi slowly, tor nodolau; heh, svi' wuh khru, elizabeth hau ish-veh party svi' wuh bestan-tvi-shal. Wuh loo pasu, however, did ri saudau. Mr. Darcy vesh' kitaun, heh din-tor bingley, hayal-tor be' ish-veh, vesh' watching wuh progress t' ish-veh nuhm, heh repeatedly calling ska' ish-veh attention k' skladan tor ish-veh ko-kai. Mr. Hurst heh mr. Bingley vesh' na' piquet, heh mrs. Hurst vesh' observing ish-veh zhagra. Elizabeth nem-tor abru ein needlework, heh vesh' sufficiently amused svi' attending tor ra be' dvun-tor svi' darcy heh ish-veh besu. Wuh perpetual commendations t' wuh t'sai either fi' ish-veh el'ru-kitaun, il fi' wuh evenness t' ish-veh zehl, il fi' wuh wu-vath t' ish-veh nuhm, k' wuh buhfik unconcern k' if ish-veh krol-tor vesh' poprah, shidau wuh curious dialogue, heh vesh' exactly svi' unison k' ish-veh opinion t' tik. “uf delighted din-tor darcy dungi nam-tor tor poprah such wuh nuhm!” au tor rai kilko-srashiv. “du kitau uncommonly sahris.” “du nam-tor mistaken. I kitau rather slowly.” “uf wehk nuhm du bolau ma occasion tor kitau svi' wuh rivak t' wuh tevun! Nuhm t' business, nuh'! Uf odious i dang nah-tor au!” “ish-veh nam-tor fortunate, yi, ik au tevan tor t'nash-veh lot instead t' tor ish-veh.” “pray var-tor ish-veh ko-kai ik i wu tor gla-tor ish-veh.” “i ma already var-tor ish-veh ni wuh'wak, k' ish-veh aitlun.” “i am kwes du ri tor spo' ish-veh pen. Kal-tor me nodolau ish-veh na' du. I nodolau pens remarkably muhl.” “nemaiyo--tonk'peh i kwon-hau-ov nodolau t'nash-veh sha'.” “uf mokuhlek du contrive tor kitau ni kauk?” au vesh' ralash-fam. “var-tor ish-veh ko-kai i am delighted tor zhu-tor t' ish-veh improvement fi' wuh harp, heh pray kal-tor ish-veh fai-tor ik i am ved svi' raptures k' ish-veh vaksurik pi' design na' wuh pasu, heh i nah-tor ish-veh infinitely superior tor din-tor grantley’s.” “dungi du mazhiv-kur-tor me trasha tor defer ish-veh raptures till i kitau va'ashiv? Na' la' i ma ri tvi-shal tor tor au yeht-gav.” “oh, ish-veh nam-tor t' rai consequence. Dungau gla-tor nash-veh ish-veh svi' january. Tonk'peh tor du kwon-hau-ov kitau such sem-rik-tor wu nuhm tor ish-veh, mr. Darcy?” “au nam-tor paik wu; tonk'peh whether kwon-hau-ov sem-rik-tor, ish-veh nam-tor ri na' me tor satalau.” “ish-veh nam-tor wuh tor-go k' me, ik wuh person vi mokuhlek kitau wuh wu nuhm k' ease fam yehat kitau has-bosh.” “ik dungi ri tor na' wuh compliment tor darcy, caroline, ” maf-tor ish-veh sa-kai, “fai'ei au tor _not_ kitau k' ease. Au orenau nuh' mau na' zhit t' kehkuh zhit-shaya. Ri tor du, darcy?” “t'nash-veh style t' kitaun nam-tor maut natya s' ish-veh.” “oh, ” maf-tor din-tor bingley, “charles kitau svi' wuh danik careless yut imaginable. Au mor si' ulef ish-veh zhit, heh blots wuh shom.” “t'nash-veh ideas yumaya ni rapidly ik i ma ri wak tor sagluvau au; k' if tvai t'nash-veh nuhm sometimes zhelesh rai ideas na' ek' tor t'nash-veh correspondents.” “ish-veh humility, mr. Bingley, ” leralmin-tor elizabeth, “bolau disarm reproof.” “nothing nam-tor weht deceitful, ” leralmin-tor darcy, “do wuh appearance t' humility. Ish-veh nam-tor k'ashiv goh carelessness t' opinion, heh sometimes wuh indirect boast.” “heh if t' wuh dahkuh tor du vutau _my_ pi' recent krus t' modesty?” “wuh indirect boast; na' du nam-tor really yaut t' ish-veh lafot svi' kitaun, fai'ei du panah-tor au u' proceeding s' wuh rapidity t' nahp heh carelessness t' execution, if, kuv ri estimable, du nah-tor k'puu highly eku'ki. Wuh tepul t' doing sovek-vel k' quickness nam-tor kwon-hau-ov mau prized k' wuh possessor, heh k'ashiv rik' sovek attention tor wuh imperfection t' wuh performance. Lu du var-tor mrs. Bennet nash asal, ik kuv du ek'wak resolved fi' quitting netherfield du dang nam-tor hal-tor svi' kaukuh minutes, du tvai ish-veh tor nam-tor wuh wihfelau t' panegyric, t' compliment tor yourself; heh wi ra nam-tor tra' ni maut laudable svi' wuh precipitance if bolau trasha maut bolayatik business undone, heh mokuhlek nam-tor t' rai yeht advantage tor yourself il sovek-veh else?” “nay, ” maf-tor bingley, “nash nam-tor nuh' mau, tor vokau na' mu-yor ek' wuh duhik vel ik vesh' leralmin-tor svi' wuh asal. Heh wi, fi-tor t'nash-veh dor, i pudva-tor ra i leralmin-tor t' myself tor nam-tor yeht, heh i dva-tor ish-veh na' nash moment. K'puu, therefore, i did ri ngiq'e wuh character t' needless precipitance goh tor gluvaya ska' fa' wuh t'sai.” “i daresay du pudva-tor ish-veh; tonk'peh i am k' rai tvai convinced ik du would nam-tor hal-tor k' such celerity. Ish-veh spa-tor would nam-tor ved u' nerik fi' pavesh u' ik t' sovek sasu i fai-tor; heh kuv, u' du vesh' mounting ish-veh jarel, wuh t'hy'la vesh' tor leralmin, ‘bingley, du had weh-rom stay till thurai wehk gad, ’ du would probably tor ish-veh--du would probably ri hal-tor--heh, na' wuh'ashiv zhit, lau stay wuh tevun-krus.” “du ma goh skan-tor k' nash, ” maf-tor elizabeth, “ik mr. Bingley did ri tor yeht-gav tor ish-veh sha' disposition. Du ma shown ish-veh ska' i' mau weht do au did himself.” “i am exceedingly gratified, ” leralmin-tor bingley, “k' ish-veh converting ra t'nash-veh t'hy'la leralmin-tor vi' wuh compliment fi' wuh sweetness t' t'nash-veh temper. Tonk'peh i am kwes du nam-tor giving ish-veh wuh da-tor if ik gentleman did k' rai tvai intend; na' au would certainly nah-tor wuh weh-rom t' me kuv, ne' such wuh circumstance, i vesh' tor mazhiv-kur-tor wuh pa'ash wafaya, heh fau ska' u' sahris u' i kupi.” “would mr. Darcy yi panah-tor wuh rashness t' ish-veh tveshik intention u' atoned na' k' ish-veh obstinacy svi' adhering tor ish-veh?” “fi-tor t'nash-veh zhit, i fam yehat exactly danau wuh tukh--darcy bolau stariben na' himself.” “du gish me tor khrosahp na' opinions if du dvel-tor tor vutau t'nash-veh, tonk'peh if i ma worla nafai. Allowing wuh nuf, however, tor lamok fupa s' ish-veh representation, du bolau vokau, din-tor bennet, ik wuh t'hy'la vi nam-tor supposed tor aitlun ish-veh fun tor wuh kelek, heh wuh vohtaya t' ish-veh dotor, has goh aitlu ish-veh, ya'akash ish-veh rik' nufaya veh nerau-kek-vuhnayek svi' favour t' its propriety.” “tor yield readily--easily--tor wuh _persuasion_ t' wuh t'hy'la nam-tor rai merit k' du.” “tor yield rik' conviction nam-tor rai compliment tor wuh understanding t' either.” “du saudau tor me, mr. Darcy, tor kal-tor nothing na' wuh vi-yumuk t' friendship heh affection. Wuh fudau na' wuh requester would k'ashiv tor veh readily yield tor wuh ya'akash, rik' waiting na' nerau-kek-vuhnayek tor utvau veh vi' ish-veh. I am ri wa' speaking t' such wuh nuf u' du ma supposed pa' mr. Bingley. Etek lau u' muhl bek-tor, sos'eh, till wuh circumstance paresh-tor, fa' etek discuss wuh discretion t' ish-veh kloshai thereupon. Tonk'peh svi' paik heh ordinary nuf, svi' t'hy'la heh t'hy'la, wilat veh t' au nam-tor aitlu k' wuh vath tor rubah wuh resolution t' rai maut lo'uk moment, dang du nah-tor has-bosh t' ik person na' complying k' wuh aitlun, rik' waiting tor nam-tor gyirm'i vi' ish-veh?” “dungi ish-veh ri nam-tor advisable, fa' etek proceed fi' nash subject, tor arrange k' rather weht precision wuh degree t' importance if nam-tor tor appertain tor nash ya'akash, u' muhl u' wuh degree t' intimacy subsisting svi' wuh parties?” “k' ek' tvai, ” maf-tor bingley; “kal-tor etek zhu-tor ek' wuh particulars, ri forgetting ish-veh comparative pidek heh suk'es, na' ik dungi ma weht rasath svi' wuh nerau-kek-vuhnayek, din-tor bennet, do du lau nam-tor aware t'. I assure du ik kuv darcy vesh' ri such wuh lo'uk ha-vol katravahsu, svi' comparison k' myself, i dang ri vlitau ish-veh ulef ni mau deference. I afsakau i ri tor fai-tor wuh weht awful vel do darcy fi' particular occasions, heh svi' particular shitau; na' ish-veh sha' kelek wa', heh t' wuh gad khru, lu au has nothing tor tor.” mr. Darcy abru'teruklar-ru'lut; tonk'peh elizabeth nahp she kupi pakashogau ik au vesh' rather puthrap-tor, heh therefore rihamau ish-veh abru'teruklar-ru'lut. Din-tor bingley warmly resented wuh indignity au had poprah, svi' wuh expostulation k' ish-veh sa-kai na' talking such nonsense. “gla-tor nash-veh ish-veh design, bingley, ” leralmin-tor ish-veh t'hy'la. “du ritishaya wuh nerau-kek-vuhnayek, heh aitlun tor silence nash.” “sos'eh i tor. Nerau-kek-vuhnayek nam-tor nuh' mau spo' disputes. Kuv du heh din-tor bennet dungi defer ish-veh till i am s' wuh tvi-shal, i dungau nam-tor maut itar-bosh; heh yi du lau leralmin whatever du spo' t' me.” “ra du ya'akash, ” leralmin-tor elizabeth, “nam-tor rai sacrifice fi' t'nash-veh vla; heh mr. Darcy had mau weh-rom shaht ish-veh nuhm.” mr. Darcy nem-tor ish-veh na'shikh, heh did shaht ish-veh nuhm. Lu ik business vesh' abru', au applied tor din-tor bingley heh elizabeth na' wuh indulgence t' ein ralash-tanaf. Din-tor bingley dvun-tor k' alacrity tor wuh pianoforte, heh po' wuh polite ya'akash ik elizabeth would ras-tukh wuh yut, if wuh vath u' politely heh weht earnestly negatived, she hayal-tor herself. Mrs. Hurst sang k' ish-veh ko-kai; heh du' au vesh' thus employed, elizabeth kupi ri gol'nev observing, u' she da-tor abru' ein ralash-tanaf-dunap ik ti fi' wuh instrument, uf frequently mr. Darcy’s bezhun vesh' teslau fi' ish-veh. She hardly fai-tor uf tor suppose ik she kupi nam-tor wuh vel t' admiration tor ni lo'uk wuh sasu, heh wi ik au dang glazhau na' ish-veh fai'ei au ritishau ish-veh vesh' fam dvun weht flekh. She kupi goh glenonau, however, na' kim-shah, ik she drew ish-veh beglanau fai'ei tra' vesh' vel pa' ish-veh weht riyeht heh reprehensible, fupa s' ish-veh ideas t' gas'rak, do svi' sovek vath person la'. Wuh supposition did ri kusut ish-veh. She tishau ish-veh nuh' pi' tor palutunau ish-veh approbation. Po' mavaun ein italian songs, din-tor bingley vuhnau wuh sem-rik k' wuh lively scotch sov; heh ak afterwards mr. Darcy, bestan be' elizabeth, leralmin-tor tor ish-veh, -- “tor du ri olau wuh lo'uk inclination, din-tor bennet, tor seize such wuh opportunity t' taman wuh magu?” she abru'teruklar-ru'lut, tonk'peh tor rai kilko-srashiv. Au ashiv-tor wuh deshker, k' ein ak'wikmun na' ish-veh silence. “oh, ” leralmin-tor she, “i puzhu-tor du fa'; tonk'peh i kupi ri iyi satalau ra tor leralmin svi' kilko. Du aitlu me, i fai-tor, tor leralmin ‘ha, ’ ik du lau ma wuh sanosh t' despising t'nash-veh zahvan; tonk'peh i kwon-hau-ov delight svi' overthrowing eifa ves t' schemes, heh cheating wuh person t' ish-veh premeditated contempt. I ma, therefore, tor abru t'nash-veh kashek tor var-tor du ik i ri tor aitlun tor tam wuh magu na' ek'; heh i' despise me kuv du dare.” “indeed i ri tor dare.” elizabeth, having rather gishu tor affront ish-veh, vesh' putaurau na' ish-veh gallantry; tonk'peh tra' vesh' wuh rish t' sweetness heh archness svi' ish-veh manner if tor ish-veh rihagik na' ish-veh tor affront anybody, heh darcy had worla vesh' ni bewitched k' sovek kosu u' au vesh' k' ish-veh. Au really pudva-tor ik, vesh' ish-veh ri na' wuh inferiority t' ish-veh tersaya, au dang nam-tor svi' ein tehvar. Din-tor bingley gla-tor, il suspected, hiyet tor nam-tor kis-ka; heh ish-veh lo'uk anxiety na' wuh recovery t' ish-veh tal-kam t'hy'la jane poprah ein assistance s' ish-veh aitlun t' getting rid t' elizabeth. She k'ashiv ar'kada tor provoke darcy vi' disliking ish-veh be'hai'la, k' talking t' ish-veh supposed kal'i'farr, heh planning ish-veh happiness svi' such wuh alliance. “i rok, ” leralmin-tor she, u' au vesh' walking teretuhr svi' wuh tuula wuh thurai gad, “du dungi mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh ko-mekh-svi'-tor-gav wuh zamu hints, lu nash desirable pavek nem-tor shi, u' tor wuh advantage t' holding ish-veh lahv; heh kuv du mokuhlek seshan-kharat-thonek ish-veh, tor bohrau wuh younger ko-kan t' sahran po' wuh officers. Heh, kuv i lau mention ni delicate wuh subject, endeavour tor rihamau ik pi' vel, bordering fi' conceit heh impertinence, if ish-veh t'sai ma.” [illustration: “rai, rai; stay wilat du nam-tor” [_copyright 1894 k' george allen._]] “ma du sovek-kitok tor propose na' t'nash-veh ka'kelik felicity?” “oh ha. Tor kal-tor wuh portraits t' ish-veh sa-kuk heh ezyet philips nam-tor shitau svi' wuh tanaf-shi'gluvaun na' pemberley. Shitau au nam-tor' ish-veh lo'uk-sa-kuk wuh judge. Au nam-tor svi' wuh ka ha'yigal, du fai-tor, goh svi' natya zehl. U' na' ish-veh elizabeth’s bikuv, du bolau ri attempt ki' ish-veh taken, na' ra krassu kupi tor yeht-gav tor eifa vaksurik bezhun?” “ish-veh would ri nam-tor hagik, indeed, tor kum ish-veh sagluvaya; tonk'peh ish-veh kur heh shid, heh wuh bezhun-isach, ni remarkably tok-ti, lau nam-tor va'asau.” na' ik moment au vesh' ragel-tor s' wuh'ashiv lates k' mrs. Hurst heh elizabeth herself. “i did ri fai-tor ik du intended tor lates, ” leralmin-tor din-tor bingley, svi' ein confusion, lest au had vesh' overheard. “du nam-tor-tor etek abominably has-bosh, ” kilko-tor mrs. Hurst, “sahran maf rik' telling etek ik du vesh' coming si'.” yi taking wuh dahl-tor kar t' mr. Darcy, she losrak elizabeth tor lates k' herself. Wuh yut aishan nafai-tor rehkuh. Mr. Darcy olau ish-veh rudeness, heh iyi leralmin-tor, -- “nash lates nam-tor ri eik hiyet na' etwel party. Etek had weh-rom hal-tor vi' wuh avenue.” tonk'peh elizabeth, vi had ri wuh least inclination tor hafau k' au, laughingly kilko-tor, -- “rai, rai; stay wilat du nam-tor. Du nam-tor charmingly grouped, heh saudau tor uncommon advantage. Wuh picturesque would nam-tor spoilt k' admitting wuh fourth. Rom-bye.” she yi sahr-tor gaily ska', rejoicing, u' she rambled pa', svi' wuh rok t' hasu na' ha-kel va'ashiv svi' wuh gad il dahkuh. Jane vesh' already ni mau recovered u' tor intend leaving ish-veh tvi-shal na' wuh couple t' wadan ik khru. [illustration: “piling abru wuh yon” [_copyright 1894 k' george allen._]] chapter xi. [illustration] lu wuh t'sai snem-tor po' aru-yem elizabeth sahr-tor abru tor ish-veh ko-kai, heh seeing ish-veh muhl klashau s' samu, attended ish-veh vi' wuh bestan-tvi-shal, wilat she vesh' welcomed k' ish-veh dahkuh t'hylara k' wehk ha'yigal t' sanosh; heh elizabeth had worla gla-tor au ni agreeable u' au vesh' du' wuh wadan if be' dvun-tor fa' wuh gentlemen saudau. Ish-veh tepul t' conversation vesh' considerable. Au kupi kethelvau wuh entertainment k' accuracy, relate wuh anecdote k' humour, heh abru'teruklar-ru'lut na' ish-veh acquaintance k' tam'a. Tonk'peh lu wuh gentlemen svi-tor, jane vesh' rai longer wuh wuh'rak vel; din-tor bingley’s bezhun vesh' instantly da-tor na' darcy, heh she had vel tor leralmin tor ish-veh fa' au had storilau wehk ash-tor. Au addressed himself directly tor din-tor bennet k' wuh polite congratulation; mr. Hurst isha tor ish-veh wuh slight kes-wun, heh leralmin-tor au vesh' “maut glad; ” tonk'peh diffuseness heh warmth hafau na' bingley’s salutation. Au vesh' bosh t' mak heh attention. Wuh wuh'rak ulef wadan vesh' spent svi' piling abru wuh yon, lest she dang dash s' wuh rubah t' tvi-shal; heh she snem-tor, na' ish-veh aitlun, tor wuh vath vla t' wuh yon-sha'ti, ik she lau nam-tor weh-irak s' wuh svep. Au yi hayal-tor ne' k' ish-veh, heh variben scarcely tor sovek-veh else. Elizabeth, na' ar'kadan svi' wuh mesyutik teruk, gla-tor ish-veh ek' k' lo'uk delight. Lu theris-masu vesh' abru' mr. Hurst reminded ish-veh ko-kai-svi'-tor-gav t' wuh nop-pasu--tonk'peh svi' vain. She had prah awek kash-tor'es ik mr. Darcy did ri istaya na' nop, heh mr. Hurst ak afer-tor kauk ish-veh tu'ash petition rejected. She assured ish-veh ik kling intended tor mavau, heh wuh silence t' wuh bosh party fi' wuh subject seemed tor justify ish-veh. Mr. Hurst had, therefore, nothing tor tor tonk'peh tor sakadaya himself fi' veh t' wuh ku-san heh hal-tor tor yuk. Darcy nem-tor abru wuh dunap. Din-tor bingley did wuh ka; heh mrs. Hurst, principally occupied svi' mavaun k' ish-veh kar-nik-zhel heh mokov, hau i' heh yi svi' ish-veh sa-kai’s conversation k' din-tor bennet. Din-tor bingley’s attention vesh' ved u' mau engaged svi' watching mr. Darcy’s progress k'fai _his_ dunap, u' svi' telvan ish-veh sha'; heh she vesh' perpetually either tor ein inquiry, il looking na' ish-veh thalv. She kupi ri skil ish-veh, however, tor sovek conversation; au goh kilko-tor ish-veh deshker heh telv-tor fi'. Na' wu-vath, ved saguhsh-tor k' wuh attempt tor nam-tor amused k' ish-veh sha' dunap, if she had goh pudvel-tor fai'ei ish-veh vesh' wuh dahr ral'es t' ish-veh, she mazhiv-kur-tor wuh lo'uk luvaya heh leralmin-tor, “uf vaksurik ish-veh nam-tor tor spend wuh khru svi' nash yut! I afsakau, po' ek', tra' nam-tor rai tizh'es spo' telvan! Uf mau sooner veh tires t' sovek-vel do t' wuh dunap! Lu i ma wuh kelek t' t'nash-veh sha', i dungau nam-tor miserable kuv i ma ri wuh marom shi'dunap.” kling tor sovek kilko. She yi luvau va'ashiv, threw aside ish-veh dunap, heh vishizhau ish-veh bezhun pauk wuh tvi-shal svi' psthan t' ein amusement; lu, khaf-spol ish-veh sa-kai mentioning wuh rin'k'n tor din-tor bennet, she da-tor suddenly na' ish-veh heh leralmin-tor, -- “k' wuh bye charles, nam-tor du really serious svi' kohlan wuh tam na' netherfield? I would na'shikhau du, fa' du satalau fi' ish-veh, tor consult wuh istau t' wuh la' party; i am mau mistaken kuv tra' nam-tor ri ein akhlami tor ik wuh rin'k'n would nam-tor rather wuh taflaya do wuh sanosh.” “kuv du tvai darcy, ” maf-tor ish-veh sa-kai, “au lau hal-tor tor sar-tak, kuv au chooses, fa' ish-veh palikau; tonk'peh u' na' wuh rin'k'n, ish-veh nam-tor ved wuh settled vel, heh u' ak u' nicholls has tor wan-kur shur hiyet i dungau satau pauk t'nash-veh nop.” “i dang spo' rin'k'n infinitely weh-rom, ” she kilko-tor, “kuv au vesh' lesh fi' svi' wuh natya manner; tonk'peh tra' nam-tor vel insufferably tedious svi' wuh tsuri torek t' such wuh latva. Ish-veh would surely nam-tor mau weht rational kuv conversation instead t' taman tor wuh zek t' wuh gad.” “mau weht rational, t'nash-veh tal-kam caroline, i dare leralmin; tonk'peh ish-veh would ri nam-tor be' ni mau spo' wuh rin'k'n.” din-tor bingley tor rai kilko-srashiv, heh ak afterwards prah abru heh lates-tor pa' wuh tvi-shal. Ish-veh khlop vesh' sohkik, heh she lates-tor muhl; tonk'peh darcy, na' ik ish-veh vesh' ek' mokh-tor, vesh' fam dvun inflexibly studious. Svi' wuh desperation t' ish-veh feelings, she resolved fi' veh urgam weht; heh, turning tor elizabeth, leralmin-tor, -- “din-tor eliza bennet, kal-tor me persuade du tor zahal-tor t'nash-veh li-fal, heh nem-tor wuh da-tor pa' wuh tvi-shal. I assure du ish-veh nam-tor maut refreshing po' sitting ni wu svi' veh attitude.” elizabeth vesh' ak'wikmun, tonk'peh sep-wafikh tor ish-veh iyi. Din-tor bingley navau rai lehkuh svi' wuh yeht vel t' ish-veh civility: mr. Darcy glazhau abru. Au vesh' u' mau kum'i tor wuh novelty t' attention svi' ik yonuk u' elizabeth herself kupi nam-tor, heh unconsciously a'ing ish-veh dunap. Au vesh' directly invited tor hau ish-veh party, tonk'peh au declined ish-veh, observing ik au kupi glenonau tonk'peh dahkuh dvubolek na' ish-veh choosing tor lates abru heh ne' wuh tvi-shal teretuhr, k' either t' if dvubolek ish-veh hau au would snertau. Ra kupi au tvai? She vesh' dying tor fai-tor ra kupi nam-tor ish-veh meaning--heh ya'akash elizabeth whether she kupi na' ek' ken-tor ish-veh. “mokov, ” vesh' ish-veh kilko-srashiv; “tonk'peh, nerau fi-tor ish-veh, au tvai tor nam-tor severe fi' etek, heh etwel surest yut t' disappointing ish-veh dungi nam-tor tor ya'akash nothing pa' ish-veh.” din-tor bingley, however, vesh' incapable t' disappointing mr. Darcy svi' sovek-vel, heh persevered, therefore, svi' requiring wuh danaya t' ish-veh dahkuh dvubolek. “i ma ri wuh smallest objection tor explaining au, ” leralmin-tor au, u' ak u' she kal-tor ish-veh tor stariben. “du either dvel-tor nash method t' be' dvun-tor wuh khru fai'ei du nam-tor svi' tik vath’s guhl'es, heh ma tsat tek'ik tor discuss, il fai'ei du nam-tor d'wonil ik ish-veh khlop saudau tor wuh greatest advantage svi' walking: kuv wuh wuh'rak, i dang nam-tor completely svi' ish-veh yut; heh kuv wuh dahr, i mokuhlek krol-tor du mau weh-rom u' i hayal-tor k' wuh yon.” “oh, shocking!” maf-tor din-tor bingley. “i worla puzhu-tor sovek-vel ni abominable. Uf dungau etek taflau ish-veh na' such wuh starun?” “nothing ni hagik, kuv du ma tonk'peh wuh inclination, ” leralmin-tor elizabeth. “etek mokuhlek ek' plague heh taflau veh wuh'ashiv. Tease ish-veh--abru'teruklar-ru'lut na' ish-veh. Intimate u' du nam-tor, du bolau fai-tor uf ish-veh nam-tor tor nam-tor ovsoh.” “tonk'peh fi-tor t'nash-veh dor i tor _not_. I tor assure du ik t'nash-veh intimacy has ri wi saven-tor me _that_. Tease calmness t' temper heh la'es t' kashek! Rai, rai; i olau au lau defy etek tra'. Heh u' tor laughter, etek dungi ri sashavau ourselves, kuv du sanoi, k' attempting tor abru'teruklar-ru'lut rik' wuh subject. Mr. Darcy lau teraya-martaya himself.” “mr. Darcy nam-tor ri tor nam-tor abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor na'!” maf-tor elizabeth. “ik nam-tor wuh uncommon advantage, heh uncommon i rok ish-veh dungi fator, na' ish-veh would nam-tor wuh lo'uk pak tor _me_ ki' wehk such acquaintance. I dearly ashaya wuh abru'teruklar-ru'lut.” “din-tor bingley, ” leralmin-tor au, “has putan-tor me lit na' weht do mokuhlek nam-tor. Wuh wisest heh buhfik t' sasu, --nay, wuh wisest heh buhfik t' ish-veh torai, --lau nam-tor rendered ridiculous k' wuh person t'vi wuh'rak vel svi' ha'kiv nam-tor wuh kha'wal.” “certainly, ” kilko-tor elizabeth, “tra' nam-tor such sutra, tonk'peh i rok i am ri veh t' _them_. I rok i worla ridicule ra nam-tor kau-bosh il rom. Follies heh nonsense, whims heh inconsistencies, _do_ matau me, i sha', heh i abru'teruklar-ru'lut na' au whenever i mokuhlek. Tonk'peh aifa, i suppose, nam-tor precisely ra du nam-tor rik'.” “sos'eh ik nam-tor ri tor-yehat na' sovek-veh. Tonk'peh ish-veh has vesh' wuh orenau t' t'nash-veh ha'kiv tor nan'woi eifa kobat'es if k'ashiv sashavau wuh karik understanding tor ridicule.” “such u' vanity heh pride.” “ha, vanity nam-tor wuh kobat'es indeed. Tonk'peh pride--wilat tra' nam-tor wuh yeht superiority t' kashek--pride dungi nam-tor kwon-hau-ov ne' rom regulation.” elizabeth da-tor maf tor ip-sut wuh abru'teruklar-ru'lut. “ish-veh linisaya t' mr. Darcy nam-tor abru', i presume, ” leralmin-tor din-tor bingley; “heh pray ra nam-tor wuh result?” “i am perfectly convinced k' ish-veh ik mr. Darcy has rai lafot. Au ma ish-veh himself rik' pasut.” “rai, ” leralmin-tor darcy, “i ma tor rai such pretension. I ma lafot hiyet, tonk'peh au nam-tor ri, i rok, t' understanding. T'nash-veh temper i dare ri vouch na'. Ish-veh nam-tor, i dva-tor, nuh' pi' yielding; certainly nuh' pi' na' wuh convenience t' wuh panu. I fam yehat yen-tor wuh follies heh vices t' vath ni ak u' i ought, il ish-veh offences tehnat myself. T'nash-veh feelings nam-tor ri puffed pa' k' kanok attempt tor dvun au. T'nash-veh temper would sos'eh nam-tor puvutau resentful. T'nash-veh rom opinion wuh'wak pakik nam-tor pakik na' ek'wak.” “_that_ nam-tor wuh failing, indeed!” maf-tor elizabeth. “implacable resentment _is_ wuh duvek svi' wuh character. Tonk'peh du ma pudvel-tor ish-veh lafot muhl. I really fam yehat _laugh_ na' ish-veh. Du nam-tor safe s' me.” “tra' nam-tor, i dva-tor, svi' kanok disposition wuh tendency tor ein particular ek'rasah, wuh malatik lafot, if ri kauk wuh buhfik education mokuhlek overcome.” “heh _your_ lafot nam-tor wuh propensity tor fnu-ven kanok-veh.” “heh ish-veh, ” au kilko-tor, k' wuh abru'teruklar-ru'lut, “nam-tor wilfully tor misunderstand au.” “tor kal-tor etek ma wuh pi' ralash-tanaf, ” maf-tor din-tor bingley, zungor t' wuh conversation svi' if she had rai thresh. “louisa, du dungi ri kashek t'nash-veh waking mr. Hurst.” ish-veh ko-kai tor ri wuh smallest objection, heh wuh pianoforte vesh' tu'ash; heh darcy, po' wuh zamu moments’ recollection, vesh' ri sorry na' ish-veh. Au began tor olau wuh tehvar t' paying elizabeth nuh' mau attention. [illustration] chapter xii. [illustration] svi' consequence t' wuh agreement svi' wuh ko-kai, elizabeth kitau wuh thurai asal tor ish-veh ko-mekh, tor eit'jae ik wuh carriage lau nam-tor satau na' au svi' wuh rivak t' wuh gad. Tonk'peh mrs. Bennet, vi had ka'pra fi' ish-veh daughters remaining na' netherfield till wuh zahalik gad, if would exactly shaht jane’s wehk gad, kupi ri katau herself tor poprah au k' sanosh fa'. Ish-veh kilko-srashiv, therefore, vesh' ri propitious, na' least ri tor elizabeth’s istau, na' she vesh' impatient tor prah ha-kel. Mrs. Bennet satau au zhit ik au kupi ri possibly ma wuh carriage fa' gad; heh svi' ish-veh postscript ish-veh vesh' hau, ik kuv mr. Bingley heh ish-veh ko-kai hish-tor au tor stay longer, she kupi spare au maut muhl. Tehnat staying longer, however, elizabeth vesh' positively resolved--il did she mau gish ish-veh would nam-tor ya'akash; heh pthak-bosh, fi' wuh contrary, t' hasu panah-tor u' intruding themselves needlessly wu, she urged jane tor yahv-tor mr. Bingley’s carriage iyi, heh na' wu-vath ish-veh vesh' settled ik ish-veh tveshik design t' leaving netherfield ik asal dang nam-tor mentioned, heh wuh ya'akash tor. Wuh sviribaya teporilau wehk ha'yigal t' concern; heh hiyet vesh' leralmin-tor t' wishing au tor stay k'puu till wuh zahalik gad tor ar'kadan fi' jane; heh till wuh morrow ish-veh going vesh' deferred. Din-tor bingley vesh' yi sorry ik she had proposed wuh vohtaya; na' ish-veh jealousy heh ritishaya t' veh ko-kai mau namautau ish-veh affection na' wuh vath. Wuh trensu t' wuh kelek puzhu-tor k' yeht sorrow ik au vesh' tor hal-tor ni ak, heh repeatedly ar'kada tor persuade din-tor bennet ik ish-veh would ri nam-tor safe na' ish-veh--ik she vesh' ri hiyet recovered; tonk'peh jane vesh' pesik wilat she olau herself tor nam-tor gas'rak. Tor mr. Darcy ish-veh vesh' welcome kash-tor'es: elizabeth had vesh' na' netherfield wu hiyet. She skamau ish-veh weht do au tishau; heh din-tor bingley vesh' uncivil tor _her_ heh weht teasing do tsuri tor himself. Au wisely resolved tor nam-tor wa' tun-bosh ik rai glat t' admiration dang _now_ stron ish-veh--nothing ik kupi ashenau ish-veh k' wuh rok t' influencing ish-veh felicity; sensible ik, kuv such wuh idea had vesh' suggested, ish-veh kloshai du' wuh kim-shah gad bolau ma tukh rasath svi' confirming il crushing ish-veh. Br'xan tor ish-veh lof, au scarcely stariben lehkuh zhit tor ish-veh k'fai wuh bosh t' gad: heh hi au vesh' na' veh wak losrak k' themselves na' ulef wuh wadan, au adhered danik conscientiously tor ish-veh dunap, heh would ri kauk glazhau na' ish-veh. Fi' gad, po' asal dvin, wuh dahshaya, ni agreeable tor siyah ek', nem-tor shi. Din-tor bingley’s civility tor elizabeth increased na' kim-shah maut rapidly, u' muhl u' ish-veh affection na' jane; heh lu au parted, po' assuring wuh latter t' wuh sanosh ish-veh would kwon-hau-ov mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh tor gla-tor ish-veh either na' longbourn il netherfield, heh embracing ish-veh danik tenderly, she kauk hutau el'ru k' wuh former. Elizabeth nem-tor trasha t' wuh bosh party svi' wuh liveliest tam'a. Au vesh' ri welcomed ha-kel maut cordially k' ish-veh ko-mekh. Mrs. Bennet wondered na' ish-veh coming, heh nahp au maut riyeht tor mazhiv-kur-tor ni mau trouble, heh vesh' sure jane would ma kum-tor samu va'ashiv. Tonk'peh ish-veh sa-mekh, hi maut laconic svi' ish-veh sagluvaya t' sanosh, vesh' really glad tor gla-tor au; au had olau ish-veh importance svi' wuh skan da-kuv. Wuh khru conversation, lu au vesh' ek' assembled, had pakik mau t' its animation, heh siyah ek' its kash-ral, k' wuh k'torr jane heh elizabeth. Au afer-tor mary, u' tsuri, glu svi' wuh orenau t' thorough neralash heh komihn malat; heh had ein uzh saseshau tor krol-tor heh ein uzh glantaya t' threadbare morality tor shroi tor. Catherine heh lydia had ro'fori na' au t' wuh natya wihfelau. Mau had vesh' ovsoh, heh mau had vesh' leralmin-tor svi' wuh regiment opi' wuh preceding gad; several t' wuh officers had aru-yokul lately k' ish-veh sa-kuk; wuh awek had vesh' flogged; heh ish-veh had actually vesh' hinted ik shal-lan forster vesh' going tor nam-tor telik. [illustration] chapter xiii [illustration] “i rok, t'nash-veh tal-kam, ” leralmin-tor mr. Bennet tor ish-veh ko-telsu, u' au vesh' na' asal-yem wuh thurai asal, “ik du ma ordered wuh rom aru-yem tor-gad, fai'ei i ma utvau tor gish wuh haya tor etwel skan party.” “vi tor du tvai, t'nash-veh tal-kam? I fai-tor t' kling ik nam-tor coming, i am sure, vita charlotte lucas dang pavesh-tor tor vutau svi'; heh i rok _my_ aru-yem nam-tor rom hiyet na' ish-veh. I ri tor dva-tor she k'ashiv gla-tor such na' ha-kel.” “wuh person t' ik i stariben nam-tor wuh gentleman heh wuh ri-fainusu.” mrs. Bennet’s bezhun sparkled. “wuh gentleman heh wuh ri-fainusu! Ish-veh nam-tor mr. Bingley, i am sure. Po, jane--du worla eku-tor wuh zhit t' nash--du sly vel! Muhl, i am sure i dungau nam-tor extremely glad tor gla-tor mr. Bingley. Tonk'peh--rom s'haile! Uf unlucky! Tra' nam-tor ri wuh zeshau t' aluk tor nam-tor prah tor-gad. Lydia, t'nash-veh ashaya, mokov wuh kus-vakh. I bolau stariben tor kunel nash moment.” “ish-veh nam-tor _not_ mr. Bingley, ” leralmin-tor ish-veh sa-telsu; “ish-veh nam-tor wuh person ik i worla gla-tor svi' wuh bosh rivak t' t'nash-veh ha'kiv.” nash kastorilau wuh paik astonishment; heh au had wuh sanosh t' hasu eagerly deshkau k' ish-veh ko-telsu heh kaukuh daughters na' wuh'wak. Po' tzlu'pd himself ein wak k' ish-veh curiosity, au thus danau: --“pa' wuh tevun-krus ago i poprah nash nuhm, heh pa' wuh fortnight ago i kilko-tor ish-veh; na' i nahp ish-veh wuh nuf t' ein delicacy, heh requiring lehkuh-mal attention. Ish-veh nam-tor s' t'nash-veh krei, mr. Collins, vi, lu i am tevik, lau da-tor du ek' s' nash kelek u' ak u' au sanoi.” “oh, t'nash-veh tal-kam, ” maf-tor ish-veh ko-telsu, “i fam yehat lesh tor zhu-tor ik mentioned. Pray ri tor variben t' ik odious sasu. I tor nah-tor ish-veh nam-tor wuh hardest vel svi' wuh panu, ik ish-veh estate dang nam-tor entailed maf s' ish-veh sha' kanu; heh i am sure, kuv i had vesh' du, i dang ma ar'kada wu ago tor tor vel il vath pa' ish-veh.” jane heh elizabeth attempted tor danau tor ish-veh wuh malat t' wuh entail. Au had k'ashiv attempted ish-veh fa': tonk'peh ish-veh vesh' wuh subject fi' if mrs. Bennet vesh' mesakh wuh pulau t' utvau; heh she fator tor rail bitterly tehnat wuh cruelty t' settling wuh estate maf s' wuh skan t' kaukuh daughters, svi' favour t' wuh sasu ik kling tun-tor sovek-vel pa'. “ish-veh certainly nam-tor wuh danik iniquitous tek'ik, ” leralmin-tor mr. Bennet; “heh nothing mokuhlek pa'shik mr. Collins s' wuh guilt t' inheriting longbourn. Tonk'peh kuv du dungi shroi tor ish-veh nuhm, du lau, sos'eh, nam-tor wuh pi' softened k' ish-veh manner t' expressing himself.” “rai, ik i am sure i dungau ri: heh i nah-tor ish-veh vesh' maut impertinent t' ish-veh tor kitau tor du na' ek', heh maut hypocritical. I fnu-ven such riyeht t'hylara. Po kupi ri au potau fi' quarrelling k' du, u' ish-veh sa-mekh did fa' ish-veh?” “po, indeed, au tor seem ki' had ein filial scruples fi' ik patam, u' du dungi zhu-tor.” /* gas'rak “hunsford, be' westerham, kent, _15th october_. */ “tal-kam osu, “wuh disagreement subsisting svi' yourself heh t'nash-veh tab-ma pudor-tor sa-mekh kwon-hau-ov mazhiv-kur-tor me mau uneasiness; heh, opi' i ma had wuh misfortune tor pak-tor ish-veh, i ma frequently istau tor hakau wuh breach: tonk'peh, na' ein wak, i vesh' potau pla' k' t'nash-veh sha' vet-tor, fearing lest ish-veh lau seem disrespectful tor ish-veh vokaya na' me tor nam-tor fi' rom zhil k' sovek-veh k' ik ish-veh had kwon-hau-ov sanoi ish-veh tor nam-tor na' variance.”--‘tra', mrs. Bennet.’--“t'nash-veh kashek, however, nam-tor i' tor abru fi' wuh subject; na', having poprah ordination na' easter, i ma vesh' ni fortunate u' tor nam-tor distinguished k' wuh patronage t' wuh gas'rak dorli t'sai catherine de bourgh, kir'an t' osu lewis de bourgh, t'vi bounty heh beneficence has preferred me tor wuh taluhk rectory t' nash parish, wilat ish-veh dungau nam-tor t'nash-veh earnest endeavour tor demean myself k' grateful respect na' ish-veh ladyship, heh nam-tor ek'wak pok tor perform eifa rites heh hali-kal if nam-tor instituted k' wuh church t' england. U' wuh clergyman, moreover, i olau ish-veh t'nash-veh gu-vam tor promote heh afer-tor wuh kudaya t' sochya svi' ek' skan k'svi wuh pulau t' t'nash-veh vi-yumuk; heh fi' aifa solektra i snuhkrol-tor myself ik t'nash-veh la' overtures t' rom-dungi nam-tor highly commendable, heh ik wuh circumstance t' t'nash-veh hasu thurai svi' wuh entail t' longbourn estate dungi nam-tor kindly overlooked fi' ish-veh vla, heh ri ras-tukh du tor reject wuh nufau olive khlup. I fam yehat nam-tor vathru do concerned na' hasu wuh tvai t' injuring ish-veh amiable daughters, heh eit'jae trasha tor apologize na' ish-veh, u' muhl u' tor assure du t' t'nash-veh readiness tor tor au kanok tor-yehat amends; tonk'peh t' nash hereafter. Kuv du dang ma rai objection tor poprah me vi' ish-veh kelek, i propose myself wuh satisfaction t' waiting fi' du heh ish-veh skan, gad, november 18th, k' kehkuh o’wak-vel, heh dungau probably trespass fi' ish-veh hospitality till wuh gad se’nnight zahalik, if i mokuhlek tor rik' sovek inconvenience, u' t'sai catherine nam-tor irak s' objecting tor t'nash-veh occasional absence fi' wuh gad, tanilau ik ein vath clergyman nam-tor engaged tor tor wuh gu-vam t' wuh gad. I hafau, tal-kam osu, k' respectful compliments tor ish-veh t'sai heh daughters, ish-veh muhl-wisher heh t'hy'la, “william collins.” “na' kehkuh o’wak-vel, therefore, etek lau gish nash sochya-tor gentleman, ” leralmin-tor mr. Bennet, u' au hesha abru wuh nuhm. “au seems tor nam-tor wuh danik conscientious heh polite nu'ri sasu, fi-tor t'nash-veh zhit; heh, i vet ri, dungi skan-tor wuh taluhk acquaintance, wa' kuv t'sai catherine dang nam-tor ni indulgent u' tor kal-tor ish-veh sarlah tor etek va'ashiv.” “tra' nam-tor ein kash-ral svi' ra au leralmin-tor pa' wuh ko-kan, however; heh, kuv au nam-tor sashitau tor tor au sovek amends, i dungau ri nam-tor wuh person tor discourage ish-veh.” “hi ish-veh nam-tor rihagik, ” leralmin-tor jane, “tor guess svi' ra yut au mokuhlek tvai tor tor etek wuh atonement au nah-tor etwel due, wuh istaya nam-tor certainly tor ish-veh lit.” elizabeth vesh' chiefly kwul-tor k' ish-veh wehtsuri deference na' t'sai catherine, heh ish-veh ves intention t' christening, marrying, heh burying ish-veh parishioners whenever ish-veh vesh' required. “au bolau nam-tor wuh oddity, i nah-tor, ” leralmin-tor she. “i fam yehat tor ish-veh si'. Tra' nam-tor vel maut pompous svi' ish-veh style. Heh ra mokuhlek au tvai k' apologizing na' hasu thurai svi' wuh entail? Etek fam yehat suppose au would gol'nev ish-veh, kuv au kupi. Mokuhlek au nam-tor wuh sensible sasu, osu?” “rai, t'nash-veh tal-kam; i nah-tor ri. I ma lo'uk rok-tor t' finding ish-veh ved wuh reverse. Tra' nam-tor wuh rish t' servility heh shal-importance svi' ish-veh nuhm if ugau muhl. I am impatient tor gla-tor ish-veh.” “svi' sfek t' composition, ” leralmin-tor mary, “ish-veh nuhm tor ri seem lafot-mayik. Wuh idea t' wuh olive khlup sos'eh nam-tor ri wholly uzh, wi i nah-tor ish-veh nam-tor muhl sagluvau.” tor catherine heh lydia neither wuh nuhm il its kitausu vesh' svi' sovek degree eku'ki. Ish-veh vesh' nam-tor' impossible ik ish-veh krei dang sarlah svi' wuh ug'yon-kur tor-pal, heh ish-veh vesh' i' ein wehk gad opi' au had poprah sanosh s' wuh shila'es t' wuh sasu svi' sovek vath kur. U' na' ish-veh ko-mekh, mr. Collins’s nuhm had ovsoh maf mau t' ish-veh has-bosh-dungi, heh she vesh' preparing tor gla-tor ish-veh k' wuh degree t' composure if astonished ish-veh sa-telsu heh daughters. Mr. Collins vesh' punctual tor ish-veh wak, heh vesh' poprah k' lo'uk politeness k' wuh bosh skan. Mr. Bennet indeed leralmin-tor pi'; tonk'peh wuh t'sai vesh' pok hiyet tor variben, heh mr. Collins seemed neither svi' bolaya t' kastoraya, il vul-tor tor nam'uh ralash-fam himself. Au vesh' wuh ha-vol, ras-looking nu'ri sasu t' kaukuh-heh-dah-leh. Ish-veh sov vesh' shi'vukhut heh stately, heh ish-veh manners vesh' maut hotorik. Au had ri vesh' wu hayal-tor fa' au complimented mrs. Bennet fi' having ni tok-ti wuh skan t' daughters, leralmin-tor au had puzhu-tor mau t' ish-veh vaksur, tonk'peh ik, svi' nash instance, khin had tevan-tor pen t' wuh yeht'es; heh hau, ik au did ri vet ish-veh seeing au ek' svi' due wak muhl sashitau t' svi' kal'i'farr. Nash gallantry vesh' ri mau tor wuh zahvan t' ein t' ish-veh hearers; tonk'peh mrs. Bennet, vi quarrelled k' rai compliments, kilko-tor danik readily, -- “du nam-tor maut ves, osu, i am sure; heh i istaya k' ek' t'nash-veh khaf-spol ish-veh lau skan-tor ni; na' else au dungi nam-tor destitute hiyet. Vel nam-tor settled ni oddly.” “du allude, sos'eh, tor wuh entail t' nash estate.” “ah, osu, i tor indeed. Ish-veh nam-tor wuh grievous tek'ik tor t'nash-veh ri donku-tor ko-kan, du bolau confess. Ri ik i tvai tor talal lafot k' _you_, na' such vel, i fai-tor, nam-tor ek' pavesh svi' nash panu. Tra' nam-tor rai fai-tor uf estates dungi hal-tor lu wuh'wak sarlah au tor nam-tor entailed.” “i am maut sensible, madam, t' wuh hardship tor t'nash-veh rom krei, heh kupi leralmin mau fi' wuh subject, tonk'peh ik i am cautious t' appearing fa'rak heh precipitate. Tonk'peh i mokuhlek assure wuh nu'ri t'sai ik sarlah nash-veh dator tor krol-tor au. Na' la' i dungi ri leralmin weht, tonk'peh, sos'eh, lu etek nam-tor weh-rom acquainted----” au vesh' svi-shau k' wuh summons tor aru-yem; heh wuh ko-kan abru'teruklar-ru'lut fi' tik vath. Au vesh' ri wuh goh vel t' mr. Collins’s admiration. Wuh tvur, wuh dining-tvi-shal, heh ek' its furniture, vesh' linisau heh krol-tor; heh ish-veh commendation t' kanok-vei would ma estuhl mrs. Bennet’s khaf-spol, tonk'peh na' wuh mortifying supposition t' ish-veh viewing ish-veh ek' u' ish-veh sha' fa-wak veltra. Wuh aru-yem, nuh', svi' its da-tor, vesh' highly krol-tor; heh au eit'jae tor fai-tor tor if t' ish-veh rom krei wuh marom'es t' its cookery vesh' owing. Tonk'peh la' au vesh' eku gas'rak k' mrs. Bennet, vi assured ish-veh, k' ein asperity, ik au vesh' maut muhl kup tor potau wuh rom fas-tor, heh ik ish-veh daughters had nothing tor tor svi' wuh af'tum. Au eit'jae pardon na' having displeased ish-veh. Svi' wuh softened molu she afsakau herself mokov puthrap-tor; tonk'peh au fator tor apologize na' pa' wuh yonuk t' wuh wadan. [illustration] chapter xiv [illustration] du' aru-yem, mr. Bennet scarcely stariben na' ek'; tonk'peh lu wuh dvinsu vesh' saseshau, au nahp ish-veh wak ki' ein conversation k' ish-veh be'hai'la, heh therefore palikau wuh subject svi' if au gishu ish-veh tor min-tor, k' observing ik au seemed maut fortunate svi' ish-veh patroness. T'sai catherine de bourgh’s attention tor ish-veh istau, heh consideration na' ish-veh comfort, saudau maut remarkable. Mr. Bennet kupi ri ma pudvel-tor weh-rom. Mr. Collins vesh' eloquent svi' ish-veh krol. Wuh subject ashenau ish-veh tor weht do tsuri solemnity t' manner; heh k' wuh danik yauluhk pulva au protested ik au had worla svi' ish-veh ha'kiv toglantau such kloshai svi' wuh person t' lan--such affability heh condescension, u' au had himself veshtau s' t'sai catherine. She had vesh' graciously sanoi tor messau t' fi' wuh discourses if au had already had wuh dor t' preaching fa' ish-veh. She had isha ya'akash ish-veh dah'wak tor aru-yokul na' rosings, heh had satau na' ish-veh goh wuh gad fa', tor tor abru ish-veh patra t' quadrille svi' wuh khru. T'sai catherine vesh' reckoned yaut k' wehk sutra, au fai-tor, tonk'peh _he_ had worla gla-tor sovek-vel tonk'peh affability svi' ish-veh. She had kwon-hau-ov spoken tor ish-veh u' she would tor sovek vath gentleman; she tor ri wuh smallest objection tor ish-veh hau svi' wuh shila'es t' wuh neighbourhood, il tor ish-veh leaving ish-veh parish occasionally na' wuh wehk gad il dahkuh tor yaret ish-veh relations. She had kauk condescended tor na'shikhau ish-veh tor marry u' ak u' au kupi, tanilau au dvel-tor k' discretion; heh had wuh'wak vlitau ish-veh wuh yaret svi' ish-veh humble parsonage, wilat she had perfectly messau ek' wuh alterations au had vesh' tor, heh had kauk vouchsafed tor suggest ein herself, --ein nef svi' wuh tsorayek upstairs. “ik nam-tor ek' maut proper heh civil, i am sure, ” leralmin-tor mrs. Bennet, “heh i dare leralmin she nam-tor wuh maut agreeable kosu. Ish-veh nam-tor wuh pity ik lo'uk t'sai svi' paik nam-tor ri weht spo' ish-veh. Tor she ha-tor be' du, osu?” “wuh bah-ker svi' if lam-tor t'nash-veh humble abode nam-tor dahshau goh k' wuh lane s' rosings shi'sochya, ish-veh ladyship’s residence.” “i nah-tor du leralmin-tor she vesh' wuh kir'an, osu? Has she sovek skan?” “she has veh goh ko-fu, wuh heiress t' rosings, heh t' maut extensive veltra.” “ah, ” maf-tor mrs. Bennet, shaking ish-veh patam, “yi she nam-tor weh-rom ska' do wehk ko-kan. Heh ra wihfelau t' nu'ri t'sai nam-tor she? Nam-tor she handsome?” “she nam-tor wuh danik sem-rik-tor nu'ri t'sai, indeed. T'sai catherine herself leralmin-tor ik, svi' sfek t' yeht vaksur, din-tor de bourgh nam-tor irak superior tor wuh handsomest t' ish-veh guv; fai'ei tra' nam-tor ik svi' ish-veh features if ulidar wuh nu'ri kosu t' distinguished keshtan. She nam-tor unfortunately t' wuh sickly constitution, if has prevented ish-veh tor ik progress svi' wehk accomplishments if she kupi ri vathru ma vravshau t', u' i am informed k' wuh t'sai vi superintended ish-veh education, heh vi fam dvun resides k' au. Tonk'peh she nam-tor perfectly amiable, heh k'ashiv condescends tor yetur k' t'nash-veh humble abode svi' ish-veh pi' phaeton heh ponies.” “has she vesh' presented? I ri tor vokau ish-veh ahm among wuh t'sai na' kelek.” “ish-veh indifferent fupa s' t' muhl'es unhappily prevents ish-veh hasu svi' kahr; heh k' ik tvai, u' i var-tor t'sai catherine myself veh gad, has deprived wuh british kelek t' its brightest fanet. Ish-veh ladyship seemed sanoi k' wuh idea; heh du lau glenonau ik i am kunli fi' kanok occasion tor nufai eifa pi' delicate compliments if nam-tor kwon-hau-ov acceptable tor t'sai. I ma weht do wuh'wak glantau tor t'sai catherine, ik ish-veh sem-rik-tor ko-fu seemed pukeshta tor nam-tor wuh duchess; heh ik wuh danik ashenau lan, instead t' giving ish-veh consequence, would nam-tor tong'av k' ish-veh. Aifa nam-tor wuh ves t' pi' vel if sanoi ish-veh ladyship, heh ish-veh nam-tor wuh wihfelau t' attention if i conceive myself peculiarly bound tor vlitau.” “du judge maut properly, ” leralmin-tor mr. Bennet; “heh ish-veh nam-tor kunli na' du ik du ma wuh talent t' flattering k' delicacy. Sos ya'akash whether aifa pleasing attentions proceed s' wuh impulse t' wuh moment, il nam-tor wuh result t' previous orenau?” “au arise chiefly s' ra nam-tor be' dvun-tor na' wuh wak; heh hi i sometimes amuse myself k' suggesting heh arranging such pi' sohkik compliments u' lau nam-tor rubilau tor ordinary occasions, i kwon-hau-ov istaya tor mazhiv-kur-tor au u' unstudied wuh sov u' tor-yehat.” mr. Bennet’s gishat vesh' fully kilko-tor. Ish-veh krei vesh' u' absurd u' au had rok-tor; heh au shroi tor ish-veh k' wuh keenest tizh'es, maintaining na' wuh ka wak wuh danik resolute composure t' countenance, heh, kaula svi' wuh occasional glance na' elizabeth, requiring rai tersu svi' ish-veh sanosh. K' theris-masu-wak, however, wuh fim had vesh' hiyet, heh mr. Bennet vesh' glad tor nem-tor ish-veh be'hai'la vi' wuh bestan-tvi-shal va'ashiv, heh lu theris-masu vesh' abru', glad tor invite ish-veh [illustration: “protested ik au worla telv-tor dunap” h.t feb 94 ] tor telv-tor aloud tor wuh t'sai. Mr. Collins readily assented, heh wuh dunap vesh' torvau; tonk'peh fi' beholding ish-veh (na' kanok-vei tor'pra ish-veh tor nam-tor s' wuh circulating shi'dunap) au palikau pla', heh, begging pardon, protested ik au worla telv-tor dunap. Kitty nantau na' ish-veh, heh lydia sporiben. Vath dunap vesh' torvau, heh po' ein deliberation au dvel-tor “fordyce’s sermons.” lydia gaped u' au tu'ash wuh ral'es; heh fa' au had, k' maut monotonous solemnity, telv-tor rehkuh thalv, she svi-shau ish-veh k', -- “tor du fai-tor, mamma, ik t'nash-veh sa-kuk philips variben t' turning maf richard? Heh kuv au tor, shal-lan forster dungi hire ish-veh. T'nash-veh ezyet var-tor me ni herself fi' gad. I dungau lates tor meryton tor-morrow tor zhu-tor weht pa' ish-veh, heh tor ya'akash lu mr. Denny sarlah pla' s' kahr.” lydia vesh' nufai k' ish-veh dahkuh eldest ko-kai tor meskaraya ish-veh lahv; tonk'peh mr. Collins, mau puthrap-tor, laid aside ish-veh dunap, heh leralmin-tor, -- “i ma k'ashiv glantau uf pi' nu'ri t'sai nam-tor interested k' dunap t' wuh serious stamp, hi written solely na' ish-veh rufai. Ish-veh taurau me, i confess; na' certainly tra' mokuhlek nam-tor nothing ni advantageous tor au u' instruction. Tonk'peh i dungi rai longer importune t'nash-veh nu'ri krei.” yi, turning tor mr. Bennet, au nufau himself u' ish-veh antagonist na' nesh-kur heh yon-kur. Mr. Bennet nar-tor wuh kali-fi, observing ik au bae'cok maut wisely svi' leaving wuh ko-kan tor ish-veh sha' trifling amusements. Mrs. Bennet heh ish-veh daughters apologized danik civilly na' lydia’s svi-shaya, heh ugau ik ish-veh dang ri paresh-tor va'ashiv, kuv au would resume ish-veh dunap; tonk'peh mr. Collins, po' assuring au ik au spitau ish-veh nu'ri krei rai has-bosh-dungi, heh dang worla resent ish-veh kloshai u' sovek affront, hayal-tor himself na' wuh'ashiv pasu k' mr. Bennet, heh dator na' nesh-kur heh yon-kur. [illustration] chapter xv. [illustration] mr. Collins vesh' ri wuh sensible sasu, heh wuh pafam'es t' malat had vesh' tonk'peh pi' gol-tor k' education il shila'es; wuh greatest krus t' ish-veh ha'kiv having vesh' spent ne' wuh guidance t' wuh illiterate heh miserly sa-mekh; heh hi au belonged tor veh t' wuh universities, au had goh potau wuh bolayatik zhil rik' forming na' ish-veh sovek useful acquaintance. Wuh subjection svi' if ish-veh sa-mekh had katau ish-veh abru had putan-tor ish-veh originally lo'uk humility t' manner; tonk'peh ish-veh vesh' i' wuh rom deal counteracted k' wuh shal-conceit t' wuh kobat patam, living svi' retirement, heh wuh consequential feelings t' lehkuh-mal heh ri-gishu smusma'es. Wuh fortunate pavesh had recommended ish-veh tor t'sai catherine de bourgh lu wuh living t' hunsford vesh' vacant; heh wuh respect if au olau na' ish-veh pid lan, heh ish-veh veneration na' ish-veh u' ish-veh patroness, mingling k' wuh maut rom opinion t' himself, t' ish-veh ek'te'kru u' wuh clergyman, heh ish-veh gas'rak u' wuh rector, tor ish-veh altogether wuh rish t' pride heh obsequiousness, shal-importance heh humility. Having i' wuh rom kelek heh wuh maut sufficient income, au intended tor marry; heh svi' seeking wuh reconciliation k' wuh longbourn skan au had wuh ko-telsu svi' zan-tor, u' au tvai tor dvel-tor veh t' wuh daughters, kuv au afer-tor au u' handsome heh amiable u' au vesh' represented k' tsuri report. Nash vesh' ish-veh dotor t' amends--t' atonement--na' inheriting ish-veh sa-mekh’s estate; heh au nahp ish-veh wuh marom veh, bosh t' eligibility heh suitableness, heh excessively generous heh disinterested fi' ish-veh sha' krus. Ish-veh dotor did ri vuhnau fi' seeing au. Din-tor bennet’s lovely limuk wugau ish-veh zan-tor, heh afer-tor ek' ish-veh strictest notions t' ra vesh' due tor seniority; heh na' wuh wuh'rak khru _she_ vesh' ish-veh settled dvel. Wuh thurai asal, however, tor wuh alteration; na' svi' wuh yonuk t' wuh wadan’s _tête-à-tête_ k' mrs. Bennet fa' asal-yem, wuh conversation palikaya k' ish-veh parsonage-kelek, heh leading naturally tor wuh avowal t' ish-veh rok-tor, ik wuh mistress na' ish-veh lau nam-tor afer-tor na' longbourn, torvau s' ish-veh, svi' maut complaisant abru'teruklar-ru'lut heh paik kastoraya, wuh yuzhat tehnat wuh maut jane au had teslau fi'. “u' tor ish-veh _younger_ daughters, she kupi ri nem-tor fi-tor ish-veh tor leralmin--she kupi ri positively kilko-srashiv--tonk'peh she did ri _know_ t' sovek prepossession; --ish-veh _eldest_ ko-fu she bolau aishan mention--she olau ish-veh incumbent fi' ish-veh tor hint, vesh' kesik tor nam-tor maut ak engaged.” mr. Collins had goh tor rubah s' jane tor elizabeth--heh ish-veh vesh' ak ovsoh--ovsoh du' mrs. Bennet vesh' stirring wuh yon. Elizabeth, kaing nam-tor' jane svi' keshtan heh vaksur, navau ish-veh veling. Mrs. Bennet treasured abru wuh hint, heh trusted ik she lau ak ma dahkuh daughters telik; heh wuh sasu ik she kupi ri lesh tor stariben t' wuh gad fa', vesh' i' pid svi' ish-veh rom takov-tor. Lydia’s intention t' walking tor meryton vesh' ri yen-tor: kanok ko-kai kaula mary sep-wafikh tor hal-tor k' ish-veh; heh mr. Collins vesh' tor attend au, na' wuh ya'akash t' mr. Bennet, vi vesh' danik anxious tor prah rid t' ish-veh, heh ma ish-veh shi'dunap tor himself; na' thither mr. Collins had zahal-tor ish-veh po' asal-yem, heh tra' au would fator, nominally engaged k' veh t' wuh largest folios svi' wuh tershaya, tonk'peh really talking tor mr. Bennet, k' pi' cessation, t' ish-veh kelek heh bah-ker na' hunsford. Such doings discomposed mr. Bennet exceedingly. Svi' ish-veh shi'dunap au had vesh' kwon-hau-ov sure t' el-wak heh tranquillity; heh hi dator, u' au var-tor elizabeth, tor ragel-tor k' folly heh conceit svi' kanok vath tvi-shal svi' wuh kelek, au vesh' nam-tor-tor tor nam-tor elik s' au tra': ish-veh civility, therefore, vesh' danik prompt svi' inviting mr. Collins tor hau ish-veh daughters svi' ish-veh lates; heh mr. Collins, hasu svi' kla-min mau weh-rom fitted na' wuh walker do wuh reader, vesh' extremely muhl sanoi tor ikap-tor ish-veh suk dunap, heh hal-tor. Svi' pompous nothings fi' ish-veh vla, heh civil assents fi' ik t' ish-veh krei, ish-veh wak be' dvun-tor till au svi-tor meryton. Wuh attention t' wuh younger ones vesh' yi rai longer tor nam-tor nazh-tor k' _him_. Ish-veh bezhun vesh' iyi wandering abru wuh yut svi' psthan t' wuh officers, heh nothing lehkuh tor wuh maut klon bonnet, indeed, il wuh really uzh muslin svi' wuh mahr-kel krani, kupi recall au. Tonk'peh wuh attention t' kanok t'sai vesh' ak kum-tor k' wuh nu'ri sasu, ik au had worla gla-tor fa', t' danik gentlemanlike appearance, walking k' wuh officer fi' wuh vath vla t' wuh yut. Wuh officer vesh' wuh maut mr. Denny fundik t'vi fun s' london lydia sarlah tor inquire, heh au ovalau u' au be' dvun-tor. Ek' vesh' kwul-tor k' wuh ri-fainusu’s sov, ek' wondered vi au kupi nam-tor; heh kitty heh lydia, satalau kuv tor-yehat tor talal si', pufulag-tor wuh yut mes' wuh yut, ne' pretence t' wanting vel svi' wuh mesyutik mahr-kel, heh fortunately had aishan nazh-tor wuh pavement, lu wuh dahkuh gentlemen, turning pla', had pulau wuh ka gla-tor. Mr. Denny addressed au directly, heh entreated permission tor ragtau ish-veh t'hy'la, mr. Wickham, vi had fun-tor k' ish-veh wuh gad fa' s' kahr, heh, au vesh' kunli tor leralmin, had nar-tor wuh kadvin svi' ish-veh corps. Nash vesh' exactly u' ish-veh dang nam-tor; na' wuh nu'ri sasu aitlu goh regimentals tor tor ish-veh completely sem-rik-tor. Ish-veh appearance vesh' greatly svi' ish-veh favour: au had ek' wuh buhfik krus t' vaksur, wuh tok-ti countenance, wuh rom khlop, heh maut pleasing shi'yavekh. Wuh ragtaya vesh' zahal-tor abru fi' ish-veh vla k' wuh kunli readiness t' conversation--wuh readiness na' wuh ka wak perfectly yeht heh unassuming; heh wuh bosh party vesh' fam dvun standing heh talking teretuhr maut agreeably, lu wuh ralash t' jarel drew ish-veh beglanau, heh darcy heh bingley vesh' gla-tor riding ne' wuh yut. Fi' distinguishing wuh t'sai t' wuh travek wuh dahkuh gentlemen sarlah directly na' au, heh began wuh tsuri civilities. Bingley vesh' wuh principal spokesman, heh din-tor bennet wuh principal vel. Au vesh' yi, au leralmin-tor, fi' ish-veh yut tor longbourn fi' lof tor inquire po' ish-veh. Mr. Darcy corroborated ish-veh k' wuh kes-wun, heh vesh' palikaya tor satalau ri tor teslau ish-veh bezhun fi' elizabeth, lu au vesh' suddenly pehkau k' wuh glan t' wuh ri-fainusu; heh elizabeth aisha tor gla-tor wuh countenance t' fi' u' au glazhau na' tik vath, vesh' ek' astonishment na' wuh daya t' wuh latva. Fi' rubai kur, veh glazhau wan-kur, wuh vath yon-kur. Mr. Wickham, po' wuh zamu moments, estuhl ish-veh taik--wuh salutation if mr. Darcy aishan deigned tor fun. Ra kupi nam-tor wuh meaning t' ish-veh? Ish-veh vesh' impossible tor glenonau; ish-veh vesh' impossible ri tor wu tor fai-tor. Svi' wuh'ashiv minute mr. Bingley, tonk'peh rik' seeming ki' pubeglanau ra be' dvun-tor, nem-tor trasha heh fau-tor fi' k' ish-veh t'hy'la. Mr. Denny heh mr. Wickham lates-tor k' wuh nu'ri t'sai tor wuh svep t' mr. Philips’s kelek, heh yi tor ish-veh ovalau, svi' spite t' din-tor lydia’s pressing entreaties ik au would sarlah svi', heh kauk svi' spite t' mrs. Philips’s throwing abru wuh parlour krani, heh loudly seconding wuh k'waw'zhe. Mrs. Philips vesh' kwon-hau-ov glad tor gla-tor ish-veh ko-bath; heh wuh dahkuh eldest, s' ish-veh recent absence, vesh' wa' welcome; heh she vesh' eagerly expressing ish-veh ak'wikmun na' ish-veh sudden fun ha-kel, if, u' ish-veh sha' carriage had ri zaprah au, she dang ma fainu nothing pa', kuv she had ri pavesh-tor tor gla-tor mr. Jones’s shopboy svi' wuh yut, vi had var-tor ish-veh ik au vesh' ri tor satau sovek weht draughts tor netherfield, fai'ei wuh din-tor bennets vesh' sarlah maf, lu ish-veh civility vesh' claimed na' mr. Collins k' jane’s ragtaya t' ish-veh. She poprah ish-veh k' ish-veh maut buhfik politeness, if au fun-tor k' u' mau weht, apologizing na' ish-veh vi-kwitaya, rik' sovek previous acquaintance k' ish-veh, if au kupi ri gol'nev flattering himself, however, lau nam-tor justified k' ish-veh relationship tor wuh nu'ri t'sai vi puragtau ish-veh tor ish-veh beglanau. Mrs. Philips vesh' ved putesha k' such wuh mau-mazhiv-kur t' rom breeding; tonk'peh ish-veh contemplation t' veh ri-fainusu vesh' ak shitau wuh shaht tor k' sporun heh inquiries pa' wuh vath, t' ik, however, she kupi goh var-tor ish-veh ko-bath ra au already fai-tor, ik mr. Denny had katau ish-veh s' london, heh ik au vesh' ki' wuh ot-lan’s kadvin svi' wuh ----shire. She had vesh' watching ish-veh wuh kim-shah wadan, she leralmin-tor, u' au lates-tor abru heh ne' wuh yut, --heh had mr. Wickham saudau, kitty heh lydia would certainly ma fator wuh occupation; tonk'peh unluckily kling be' dvun-tor wuh krani i' kaula wuh zamu t' wuh officers, vi, svi' comparison k' wuh ri-fainusu, vesh' shetau “stupid, disagreeable katravahsu.” ein t' au vesh' tor aru-yokul k' wuh philipses wuh thurai gad, heh ish-veh ezyet ugau tor tor ish-veh sa-telsu vutau fi' mr. Wickham, heh mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh wuh k'waw'zhe isha, kuv wuh skan s' longbourn would sarlah svi' wuh khru. Nash vesh' sep-wafikh tor; heh mrs. Philips protested ik au would ma wuh nice kel'o noisy zhagra t' lottery tickets, heh wuh pi' zeshau t' fal mu'yor-yem afterwards. Wuh prospect t' such delights vesh' maut cheering, heh au parted svi' mutual rom tam'a. Mr. Collins ashiv-tor ish-veh apologies svi' quitting wuh tvi-shal, heh vesh' assured, k' unwearying civility, ik au vesh' perfectly needless. U' au lates-tor ha-kel, elizabeth related tor jane ra she had gla-tor be' dvun svi' wuh dahkuh gentlemen; tonk'peh hi jane would ma fosh-tor either il fi', had au saudau tor nam-tor riyeht, she kupi rai weht danau such kloshai do ish-veh ko-kai. Mr. Collins fi' ish-veh fun highly gratified mrs. Bennet k' krol-tor mrs. Philips’s manners heh politeness. Au protested ik, kaula t'sai catherine heh ish-veh ko-fu, au had worla gla-tor wuh weht sohkik kosu; na' she had ri goh poprah ish-veh k' wuh utmost civility, tonk'peh had kauk pointedly vinan-tor ish-veh svi' ish-veh k'waw'zhe na' wuh thurai khru, hi utterly ri-fainu tor ish-veh fa'. Vel, au supposed, lau nam-tor attributed tor ish-veh tersaya k' au, tonk'peh wi au had worla ragel-tor k' ni mau attention svi' wuh bosh rivak t' ish-veh ha'kiv. [illustration] chapter xvi. [illustration] u' rai objection vesh' tor tor wuh nu'ri sutra’s engagement k' ish-veh ezyet, heh ek' mr. Collins’s scruples t' leaving mr. Heh mrs. Bennet na' wuh single khru du' ish-veh yaret vesh' danik steadily tehnau, wuh coach zhelesh ish-veh heh ish-veh kaukuh krei na' wuh suitable wadan tor meryton; heh wuh ko-kan had wuh sanosh t' khaf-spol, u' au svi-tor wuh bestan-tvi-shal, ik mr. Wickham had nar-tor ish-veh sa-kuk’s k'waw'zhe, heh vesh' yi svi' wuh kelek. Lu nash ro'fori vesh' putan-tor, heh au had ek' taken ish-veh ku-san, mr. Collins vesh' na' el-wak tor glazhau pa' ish-veh heh krol-tor, heh au vesh' ni mau kwul-tor k' wuh suk'es heh furniture t' wuh ha-shal, ik au afsakau au lau siyah ma supposed himself svi' wuh pi' belaar asal-yem parlour na' rosings; wuh comparison ik did ri palikauk zhelesh mau gratification; tonk'peh lu mrs. Philips ken-tor s' ish-veh ra rosings vesh', heh vi vesh' its proprietor, lu she had shroi tor wuh kethelvaya t' goh veh t' t'sai catherine’s bestan-tvi-shal, heh afer-tor ik wuh vuzh-mev-krus sa'awek had kodona ohkuh hundred plesh-tor, she olau ek' wuh nekwitaya t' wuh compliment, heh would hardly ma resented wuh comparison k' wuh housekeeper’s tvi-shal. Svi' describing tor ish-veh ek' wuh grandeur t' t'sai catherine heh ish-veh mansion, k' occasional savarun svi' krol t' ish-veh sha' humble abode, heh wuh improvements ish-veh vesh' receiving, au vesh' kunling employed abi' wuh gentlemen hau au; heh au afer-tor svi' mrs. Philips wuh maut whio'naks listener, t'vi opinion t' ish-veh consequence increased k' ra she puzhu-tor, heh vi vesh' resolving tor retail ish-veh ek' among ish-veh behsu u' ak u' she kupi. Tor wuh ko-kan, vi kupi ri shroi tor ish-veh krei, heh vi had nothing tor tor tonk'peh tor istaya na' wuh instrument, heh linisau ish-veh sha' indifferent imitations t' china fi' wuh mantel-krus, wuh tvi-wak t' waiting saudau maut wu. Ish-veh vesh' abru' na' kim-shah, however. Wuh gentlemen did betaya: heh lu mr. Wickham lates-tor vi' wuh tvi-shal, elizabeth olau ik she had neither vesh' seeing ish-veh fa', il thinking t' ish-veh opi', k' wuh smallest degree t' unreasonable admiration. Wuh officers t' wuh ----shire vesh' svi' paik wuh maut creditable, gentlemanlike eku heh wuh buhfik t' au vesh' t' wuh la' party; tonk'peh mr, wickham vesh' u' irak mesakh au ek' svi' person, countenance, sov, heh lates, u' _they_ vesh' superior tor wuh sax'ksei-limuk-tor stuffy sa-kuk philips, eshan kif wine, vi zahal-tor au vi' wuh tvi-shal. [illustration: “wuh officers t' wuh ----shire” [_copyright 1894 k' george allen._]] mr. Wickham vesh' wuh kunli sasu na' ik siyah kanok kotik bezhun vesh' da-tor, heh elizabeth vesh' wuh kunli kosu k' ik au t'forti hayal-tor himself; heh wuh agreeable manner svi' if au iyi tevan-tor vi' conversation, hi ish-veh vesh' goh fi' its hasu wuh masupik mu-yor, heh fi' wuh yesik'es t' wuh sov-masuyanik tevun-yonuk, tor ish-veh olau ik wuh commonest, dullest, danik threadbare ong lau nam-tor rendered eku'ki k' wuh renkup'es t' wuh saralashek. K' such rivals na' wuh beglanau t' wuh rom u' mr. Wickham heh wuh officers, mr. Collins seemed tor ne'hal-tor vi' insignificance; tor wuh nu'ri t'sai au certainly vesh' nothing; tonk'peh au had fam dvun na' tvi-wak wuh ves listener svi' mrs. Philips, heh vesh', k' ish-veh watchfulness, danik abundantly tanilau k' mon heh muffin. Lu wuh nop pasu vesh' shitau, au had wuh opportunity t' obliging ish-veh, svi' fun, k' sitting ne' tor whist. “i fai-tor pi' t' wuh zhagra na' la', ” leralmin-tor au, “tonk'peh i dungau nam-tor glad tor improve myself; na' svi' t'nash-veh situation t' ha'kiv----” mrs. Philips vesh' maut itar-bosh na' ish-veh compliance, tonk'peh kupi ri bek-tor na' ish-veh utvau. Mr. Wickham did ri mavau na' whist, heh k' pok delight vesh' au poprah na' wuh vath pasu svi' elizabeth heh lydia. Palikauk tra' seemed tehvar t' lydia’s engrossing ish-veh entirely, na' she vesh' wuh danik satalau talker; tonk'peh hasu likewise extremely tishau t' lottery tickets, she ak grew nuh' mau interested svi' wuh zhagra, nuh' nayik svi' tor sihau heh exclaiming po' prizes, ki' attention na' sovek-veh svi' particular. Allowing na' wuh tsuri halishau t' wuh zhagra, mr. Wickham vesh' therefore na' el-wak tor variben tor elizabeth, heh she vesh' maut willing tor zhu-tor ish-veh, hi ra she chiefly istau tor zhu-tor she kupi ri rok tor nam-tor var-tor, wuh vesht-var t' ish-veh acquaintance k' mr. Darcy. She dared ri kauk mention ik gentleman. Ish-veh curiosity, however, vesh' unexpectedly vas-tor. Mr. Wickham began wuh subject himself. Au inquired uf irak netherfield vesh' s' meryton; heh, po' receiving ish-veh kilko-srashiv, ya'akash svi' wuh hesitating manner uf wu mr. Darcy had vesh' staying tra'. “pa' wuh tevun-krus, ” leralmin-tor elizabeth; heh yi, unwilling tor kal-tor wuh subject eku, hau, “au nam-tor wuh sasu t' maut suk veltra svi' derbyshire, i ken-tor.” “ha, ” kilko-tor wickham; “ish-veh estate tra' nam-tor wuh thol veh. Wuh pa'shik lehkuh thousand fundauik annum. Du kupi ri ma ragel-tor k' wuh person weht capable t' giving du ac'ruth ro'fori fi' ik patam do myself--na' i ma vesh' tersau k' ish-veh skan, svi' wuh particular manner, s' t'nash-veh infancy.” elizabeth kupi ri tonk'peh glazhau ak'wikmun. “du lau muhl nam-tor ak'wikmun, din-tor bennet, na' such wuh assertion, po' seeing, u' du probably lau, wuh maut samu manner t' etwel latva za-gad. Nam-tor du mau acquainted k' mr. Darcy?” “u' mau u' i ek'wak istaya tor nam-tor, ” maf-tor elizabeth, warmly. “i ma spent kehkuh gad svi' wuh ka kelek k' ish-veh, heh i nah-tor ish-veh maut disagreeable.” “i ma rai gas'rak tor mazhiv-kur-tor _my_ opinion, ” leralmin-tor wickham, “u' tor ish-veh hasu agreeable il vathru. I am ri qualified tor shid veh. I ma fainu ish-veh nuh' wu heh nuh' muhl tor nam-tor wuh rom judge. Ish-veh nam-tor impossible na' _me_ tor nam-tor impartial. Tonk'peh i dva-tor ish-veh opinion t' ish-veh would svi' paik astonish--heh, sos'eh, du would ri sagluvau ish-veh ved ni strongly sovek-wilat else. La' du nam-tor svi' ish-veh sha' skan.” “fi-tor t'nash-veh zhit i leralmin rai weht _here_ do i lau leralmin svi' sovek kelek svi' wuh neighbourhood, kaula netherfield. Au nam-tor mokov tishau svi' hertfordshire. Kanok-veh nam-tor spa'ash k' ish-veh pride. Du dungi ri talal ish-veh weht favourably spoken t' k' sovek-veh.” “i fam yehat pretend tor nam-tor sorry, ” leralmin-tor wickham, po' wuh pen svi-shaya, “ik au il ik sovek sasu dang ri nam-tor talupau mesakh ish-veh eshikh; tonk'peh k' _him_ i dva-tor ish-veh tor ri k'ashiv pavesh-tor. Wuh panu nam-tor blinded k' ish-veh fortune heh consequence, il koltha k' ish-veh pid heh imposing manners, heh gla-tor ish-veh goh u' au chooses tor nam-tor gla-tor.” “i dang nem-tor ish-veh, kauk fi' _my_ slight acquaintance, tor nam-tor wuh has-bosh-tempered sasu.” wickham goh hutau ish-veh patam. “i wonder, ” leralmin-tor au, na' wuh thurai opportunity t' speaking, “whether au nam-tor kesik tor nam-tor svi' nash shasol mau longer.” “i tor mokov fai-tor; tonk'peh i _heard_ nothing t' ish-veh going maf lu i vesh' na' netherfield. I rok ish-veh dotoran svi' favour t' wuh ----shire dungi ri nam-tor dau k' ish-veh hasu svi' wuh neighbourhood.” “oh rai--ish-veh nam-tor ri na' _me_ tor nam-tor driven maf k' mr. Darcy. Kuv _he_ istau tor nan'woi seeing _me_ au bolau hal-tor. Etek nam-tor ri fi' friendly zhil, heh ish-veh kwon-hau-ov mazhiv-kur-tor me kusut tor ragel-tor ish-veh, tonk'peh i ma rai utvau na' avoiding _him_ tonk'peh ra i lau afsakau tor ek' wuh panu--wuh kash-ral t' maut lo'uk has-bosh-nam-tor, heh danik kusut-tor regrets na' ish-veh hasu ra au nam-tor. Ish-veh sa-mekh, din-tor bennet, wuh tab-ma mr. Darcy, vesh' veh t' wuh buhfik sasu ik ek'wak breathed, heh wuh truest t'hy'la i ek'wak had; heh i mokuhlek worla nam-tor svi' apc'koik k' nash mr. Darcy rik' hasu grieved tor wuh soul k' wuh thousand sival recollections. Ish-veh kloshai tor myself has vesh' scandalous; tonk'peh i verily dva-tor i kupi forgive ish-veh sovek-vel heh kanok-vei, rather do ish-veh disappointing wuh rok-tor heh disgracing wuh vokaya t' ish-veh sa-mekh.” elizabeth afer-tor wuh eku'ko t' wuh subject increase, heh shroi k' ek' ish-veh khaf-spol; tonk'peh wuh delicacy t' ish-veh prevented further inquiry. Mr. Wickham began tor stariben fi' weht paik ong, meryton, wuh neighbourhood, wuh shila'es, appearing highly sanoi k' ek' ik au had wi gla-tor, heh speaking t' wuh latter, wa', k' gentle tonk'peh maut intelligible gallantry. “ish-veh vesh' wuh prospect t' ek'kayik shila'es, heh rom shila'es, ” au hau, “if vesh' t'nash-veh chief inducement tor svi-tor wuh ----shire. I fai-tor ish-veh tor nam-tor wuh danik respectable, agreeable corps; heh t'nash-veh t'hy'la denny tempted me further k' ish-veh khrosahp t' ish-veh la' ha-shal, heh wuh maut lo'uk attentions heh marom acquaintance meryton had procured au. Shila'es, i sha', nam-tor bolayatik tor me. I ma vesh' wuh disappointed sasu, heh t'nash-veh tam'a dungi ri lesh awek'es. I _must_ ma employment heh shila'es. Wuh askital ha'kiv nam-tor ri ra i vesh' intended na', tonk'peh circumstances ma i' tor ish-veh eligible. Wuh church _ought_ ki' vesh' t'nash-veh ha'yigal--i vesh' katau abru na' wuh church; heh i dang na' nash wak ma vesh' svi' mat t' wuh danik taluhk living, had ish-veh sanoi wuh gentleman etek vesh' speaking t' aishan i'.” “indeed!” “ha--wuh tab-ma mr. Darcy bequeathed me wuh thurai presentation t' wuh buhfik living svi' ish-veh mazhiv-kur. Au vesh' t'nash-veh godfather, heh excessively attached tor me. I fam yehat tor yeht-gav tor ish-veh kindness. Au tvai tor tanilau na' me amply, heh nahp au had ovsoh ish-veh; tonk'peh lu wuh living tevan-tor, ish-veh vesh' putan-tor kitok-wilat.” “rom heavens!” maf-tor elizabeth; “tonk'peh uf kupi _that_ nam-tor? Uf kupi ish-veh dungi nam-tor bau-tor? Po did ri du seek legal redress?” “tra' vesh' aishan such wuh informality svi' wuh zhil t' wuh bequest u' tor mazhiv-kur-tor me rai rok s' tor-gav. Wuh sasu t' dor kupi ri ma vet-tor wuh intention, tonk'peh mr. Darcy dvel-tor tor vet ish-veh--il tor skasau ish-veh u' wuh goh conditional recommendation, heh tor seo'a ik i had forfeited ek' claim tor ish-veh k' madon'es, imprudence, svi' pen, sovek-vel il nothing. Ac'ruth ish-veh nam-tor ik wuh living became vacant dahkuh tevun ago, exactly u' i vesh' t' wuh ya'shakhuv tor meskaraya ish-veh, heh ik ish-veh vesh' putan-tor tor wuh'ashiv sasu; heh rai lehkuh ac'ruth nam-tor ish-veh, ik i fam yehat accuse myself t' having really ovsoh sovek-vel tor nazh tor pak-tor ish-veh. I ma wuh lamekh unguarded temper, heh i lau sos'eh ma sometimes spoken t'nash-veh opinion _of_ ish-veh, heh _to_ ish-veh, nuh' freely. I mokuhlek recall nothing weh-rasahkos. Tonk'peh wuh kla-min nam-tor, ik etek nam-tor maut natya wihfelau t' sasu, heh ik au fnu-ven me.” “nash nam-tor ved shocking! Au nazh-tor tor nam-tor publicly disgraced.” “ein wak il vath au _will_ nam-tor--tonk'peh ish-veh dungau ri nam-tor k' _me_. Till i mokuhlek yen-tor ish-veh sa-mekh, i mokuhlek worla defy il sashavau _him_.” elizabeth pudor-tor ish-veh na' such feelings, heh nahp ish-veh handsomer do ek'wak u' au sagluvau au. “tonk'peh ra, ” leralmin-tor she, po' wuh svizh, “mokuhlek ma vesh' ish-veh dvubolek? Ra mokuhlek ma vimevilau ish-veh tor kloshah ni cruelly?” “wuh thorough, satalau ritishaya t' me--wuh ritishaya if i fam yehat tonk'peh attribute svi' ein thon-tor tor jealousy. Had wuh tab-ma mr. Darcy tishau me lehkuh, ish-veh sa-fu lau ma borne k' me weh-rom; tonk'peh ish-veh sa-mekh’s uncommon attachment tor me ornaiga ish-veh, i dva-tor, maut lehkuh-mal svi' ha'kiv. Au had ri wuh temper tor lesh wuh wihfelau t' kuhlaya svi' if etek lam-tor--wuh wihfelau t' preference if vesh' k'ashiv putan-tor me.” “i had ri nahp mr. Darcy ni rasahkos u' nash--hi i ma worla tishau ish-veh, i had ri nahp ni maut has-bosh t' ish-veh--i had supposed ish-veh tor nam-tor despising ish-veh katravahsu-creatures svi' paik, tonk'peh did ri suspect ish-veh t' descending tor such malicious revenge, such injustice, such inhumanity u' nash!” po' wuh zamu minutes’ haulan, however, she fator, “i _do_ vokau ish-veh boasting veh gad, na' netherfield, t' wuh implacability t' ish-veh resentments, t' ish-veh having wuh unforgiving temper. Ish-veh disposition bolau nam-tor dreadful.” “i dungi ri sahrafel myself fi' wuh subject, ” kilko-tor wickham; “_i_ mokuhlek hardly nam-tor aishan tor ish-veh.” elizabeth vesh' va'ashiv glu svi' nahp, heh po' wuh wak sporiben, “tor skasau svi' such wuh manner wuh godson, wuh t'hy'la, wuh favourite t' ish-veh sa-mekh!” she kupi ma hau, “wuh nu'ri sasu, nuh', spo' _you_, t'vi maut countenance lau vouch na' ish-veh hasu amiable.” tonk'peh she contented herself k'--“heh veh, nuh', vi had probably vesh' ish-veh sha' besu s' kan-wak, tersau teretuhr, u' i nah-tor du leralmin-tor, svi' wuh closest manner.” “etek vesh' pukeshta svi' wuh ka parish, k'svi wuh ka shi'sochya; wuh greatest krus t' etwel youth vesh' be' dvun-tor teretuhr: inmates t' wuh ka kelek, thresh-tor wuh ka amusements, vel t' wuh ka parental tun. _my_ sa-mekh began ha'kiv svi' wuh ha'yigal if ish-veh sa-kuk, mr. Philips, saudau tor tor ni mau lit tor; tonk'peh au mazhiv-kur-tor abru kanok-vei tor nam-tor t' nam-tor-tor tor wuh tab-ma mr. Darcy, heh vaikau ek' ish-veh wak tor wuh tun t' wuh pemberley veltra. Au vesh' danik highly vam k' mr. Darcy, wuh danik intimate, confidential t'hy'la. Mr. Darcy k'ashiv nafai himself tor nam-tor ne' wuh greatest obligations tor t'nash-veh sa-mekh’s torupik superintendence; heh lu, iyi fa' t'nash-veh sa-mekh’s tevakh, mr. Darcy mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh wuh toripik ugaya t' providing na' me, i am convinced ik au olau ish-veh tor nam-tor u' mau wuh sa'akh t' gratitude tor _him_ u' t' affection tor myself.” “uf flekh!” maf-tor elizabeth. “uf abominable! I wonder ik wuh maut pride t' nash mr. Darcy has ri tor ish-veh aishan tor du. Kuv s' rai weh-rom dvubolek, ik au dang ri ma vesh' nuh' yaut tor nam-tor ritrau, --na' dishonesty i bolau vutau ish-veh.” “ish-veh _is_ wonderful, ” kilko-tor wickham; “na' siyah ek' ish-veh torai lau nam-tor traced tor pride; heh pride has k'ashiv vesh' ish-veh buhfik t'hy'la. Ish-veh has tersau ish-veh nearer k' virtue do sovek vath olaya. Tonk'peh etek nam-tor rim t' etek tsurkanik; heh svi' ish-veh kloshai tor me tra' vesh' stronger impulses kauk do pride.” “mokuhlek such abominable pride u' ish-veh ma ek'wak ovsoh ish-veh rom?” “ha; ish-veh has k'ashiv pufulag-tor ish-veh tor nam-tor liberal heh generous; tor mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh donku freely, tor gluvayek hospitality, tor gol-tor ish-veh tenants, heh vas-tor wuh ri donku-tor. Skan pride, heh _filial_ pride, na' au nam-tor maut yaut t' ra ish-veh sa-mekh vesh', ma ovsoh nash. Ri tor saudau tor disgrace ish-veh skan, tor degenerate s' wuh popular qualities, il pak-tor wuh vi-yumuk t' wuh pemberley kelek, nam-tor wuh powerful dvubolek. Au has isha _brotherly_ pride, if, k' _some_ brotherly affection, tor ish-veh wuh maut ves heh tun-bosh guardian t' ish-veh ko-kai; heh du dungi zhu-tor ish-veh paik maf-tor abru u' wuh danik whio'naks heh buhfik t' sa-kai.” “ra wihfelau t' wuh ko-kan nam-tor din-tor darcy?” au hutau ish-veh patam. “i istaya i kupi vutau ish-veh amiable. Ish-veh mazhiv-kur-tor me kusut tor stariben has-bosh t' wuh darcy; tonk'peh she nam-tor nuh' mau spo' ish-veh sa-kai, --maut, maut yaut. U' wuh kan, she vesh' affectionate heh pleasing, heh extremely tishau t' me; heh i ma vaikau wadan heh wadan tor ish-veh amusement. Tonk'peh she nam-tor nothing tor me i'. She nam-tor wuh handsome ko-kan, pa' leh-kau il leh-sheh, heh, i ken-tor, highly accomplished. Opi' ish-veh sa-mekh’s tevakh ish-veh ha-kel has vesh' london, wilat wuh t'sai ha-tor k' ish-veh, heh superintends ish-veh education.” po' wehk svizh-tor heh wehk trials t' vath subjects, elizabeth kupi ri gol'nev reverting wuh'wak weht tor wuh wuh'rak, heh taran, -- “i am astonished na' ish-veh intimacy k' mr. Bingley. Uf mokuhlek mr. Bingley, vi seems rom-humour itself, heh nam-tor, i really dva-tor, truly amiable, nam-tor svi' friendship k' such wuh sasu? Uf mokuhlek au saikhut tik vath? Tor du fai-tor mr. Bingley?” “mokov.” “au nam-tor wuh slor-tempered, amiable, sem-rik-tor sasu. Au fam yehat fai-tor ra mr. Darcy nam-tor.” “probably ri; tonk'peh mr. Darcy mokuhlek sanoi wilat au chooses. Au tor ri aitlun kup'es. Au mokuhlek nam-tor wuh conversible besu kuv au nah-tor ish-veh don ish-veh du'. Among eifa vi nam-tor na' ek' ish-veh kaik svi' consequence, au nam-tor wuh maut natya sasu s' ra au nam-tor tor wuh lehkuh prosperous. Ish-veh pride worla eshikh ish-veh; tonk'peh k' wuh don-ka au nam-tor liberal-minded, aishan, sincere, rational, dorli, heh, sos'eh, agreeable, --allowing vel na' fortune heh khlop.” wuh whist party ak afterwards breaking abru, wuh hahf hoknau pauk wuh vath pasu, heh mr. Collins nem-tor ish-veh wurzel svi' ish-veh krei elizabeth heh mrs. Philips. Wuh tsuri inquiries u' tor ish-veh navun vesh' tor k' wuh latter. Ish-veh had ri vesh' maut lo'uk; au had pakik kanok sfek; tonk'peh lu mrs. Philips began tor sagluvau ish-veh concern thereupon, au assured ish-veh, k' mau earnest ne-seshan, ik ish-veh vesh' ri t' wuh least importance; ik au panah-tor wuh donku u' wuh mere trifle, heh eit'jae she would ri tor herself uneasy. “i fai-tor maut muhl, madam, ” leralmin-tor au, “ik lu persons hayal-tor ne' tor wuh nop pasu au bolau nem-tor ish-veh pavesh t' aifa vel, --heh kunling i am ri svi' such circumstances u' tor tor kaukuh shillings sovek vel. Tra' nam-tor, undoubtedly, wehk vi kupi ri leralmin wuh ka; tonk'peh, itaren tor t'sai catherine de bourgh, i am snem-tor irak mesakh wuh bolayek t' fundauik pi' tukh.” mr. Wickham’s attention vesh' kum-tor; heh po' observing mr. Collins na' wuh zamu moments, au ya'akash elizabeth svi' wuh neik spes whether ish-veh relations vesh' maut intimately acquainted k' wuh skan t' de bourgh. “t'sai catherine de bourgh, ” she kilko-tor, “has maut lately putan-tor ish-veh wuh living. I hardly fai-tor uf mr. Collins vesh' wuh'rak puragtau tor ish-veh beglanau, tonk'peh au certainly has ri fainu ish-veh wu.” “du fai-tor veling ik t'sai catherine de bourgh heh t'sai anne darcy vesh' ko-kai; consequently ik she nam-tor ezyet tor wuh la' mr. Darcy.” “rai, indeed, i did ri. I fai-tor nothing na' ek' t' t'sai catherine’s tersaya. I worla puzhu-tor t' ish-veh nam till wuh gad fa' za-gad.” “ish-veh ko-fu, din-tor de bourgh, dungi ma wuh maut suk fortune, heh ish-veh nam-tor pudva-tor ik she heh ish-veh krei dungi kaunshau wuh dahkuh estates.” nash ro'fori tor elizabeth abru'teruklar-ru'lut, u' she nahp t' ri donku-tor din-tor bingley. Vain indeed bolau nam-tor ek' ish-veh attentions, vain heh nam-tor-fam ish-veh affection na' ish-veh ko-kai heh ish-veh krol t' himself, kuv au vesh' already shal-destined tor wuh'ashiv. “mr. Collins, ” leralmin-tor she, “stariben highly fi' t' t'sai catherine heh ish-veh ko-fu; tonk'peh, s' ein particulars ik au has related t' ish-veh ladyship, i suspect ish-veh gratitude misleads ish-veh; heh ik, svi' spite t' ish-veh hasu ish-veh patroness, she nam-tor wuh arrogant, conceited kosu.” “i dva-tor ish-veh tor nam-tor fi' svi' wuh lo'uk degree, ” kilko-tor wickham; “i ma ri gla-tor ish-veh na' wehk tevun; tonk'peh i maut muhl vokau ik i worla tishau ish-veh, heh ik ish-veh manners vesh' dictatorial heh insolent. She has wuh reputation t' hasu remarkably sensible heh clever; tonk'peh i rather dva-tor she derives krus t' ish-veh kup'es s' ish-veh lan heh fortune, krus s' ish-veh authoritative manner, heh wuh shom s' wuh pride t' ish-veh sa-bath, vi chooses ik kanok-veh tersau k' ish-veh dang ma wuh understanding t' wuh wuh'rak mohrn.” elizabeth kal-tor ik au had putan-tor wuh maut rational khrosahp t' ish-veh, heh au fator talking teretuhr k' mutual satisfaction till mu'yor-yem shitau wuh shaht tor nop, heh mazhiv-kur-tor wuh shom t' wuh t'sai ish-veh thresh t' mr. Wickham’s attentions. Tra' kupi nam-tor rai conversation svi' wuh ralash t' mrs. Philips’s mu'yor-yem party, tonk'peh ish-veh manners recommended ish-veh tor kanok-veh. Whatever au leralmin-tor, vesh' leralmin-tor muhl; heh whatever au did, ovsoh gracefully. Elizabeth went maf k' ish-veh patam bosh t' ish-veh. She kupi nah-tor t' nothing tonk'peh t' mr.
