Wickham, heh t' ra au had var-tor ish-veh, ek' wuh yut ha-kel; tonk'peh tra' vesh' ri wak na' ish-veh kauk tor mention ish-veh ahm u' au went, na' neither lydia il mr. Collins vesh' wuh'wak ralash-fam. Lydia variben incessantly t' lottery tickets, t' wuh aluk she had pakik heh wuh aluk she had skil-tor; heh mr. Collins, svi' describing wuh civility t' mr. Heh mrs. Philips, protesting ik au did ri svi' wuh least fudau ish-veh pak na' whist, enumerating ek' wuh dishes na' mu'yor-yem, heh repeatedly fearing ik au crowded ish-veh krei, had weht tor leralmin do au kupi muhl khartau fa' wuh carriage pehkau na' longbourn kelek. [illustration: “delighted tor gla-tor ish-veh tal-kam t'hy'la va'ashiv” ] chapter xvii. [illustration] elizabeth related tor jane, wuh thurai gad, ra had be' dvun-tor svi' mr. Wickham heh herself. Jane shroi k' astonishment heh concern: she fai-tor ri uf tor dva-tor ik mr. Darcy kupi nam-tor ni unworthy t' mr. Bingley’s fudau; heh wi ish-veh vesh' ri svi' ish-veh malat tor deshker wuh veracity t' wuh nu'ri sasu t' such amiable appearance u' wickham. Wuh possibility t' ish-veh having really palesh-tor such unkindness vesh' hiyet tor eku'ko ek' ish-veh sival feelings; heh nothing therefore hafau tor nam-tor ovsoh tonk'peh tor nah-tor muhl t' au fi', tor fosh-tor wuh spa-tor t' tik, heh lehm vi' wuh khrosahp t' kisheya il lafosh whatever kupi ri nam-tor vathru danau. “au ma fi', ” leralmin-tor she, “vesh' tehs-tor, i dare leralmin, svi' ein yut il vath, t' if etek mokuhlek shid rai idea. Interested sutra ma sos'eh misrepresented tik tor wuh vath. Ish-veh nam-tor, svi' pen, impossible na' etek tor conjecture wuh aisha il circumstances if lau ma alienated au, rik' actual tenai fi' either vla.” “maut yeht, indeed; heh i', t'nash-veh tal-kam jane, ra ma du prah tor leralmin svi' behalf t' wuh interested sutra vi ma probably vesh' concerned svi' wuh business? Tor pa'shik _them_, nuh', il etek dungau nam-tor obliged tor nah-tor has-bosh t' somebody.” “abru'teruklar-ru'lut u' mau u' du dvel-tor, tonk'peh du dungi ri abru'teruklar-ru'lut me s' t'nash-veh opinion. T'nash-veh dearest lizzy, tor tonk'peh panah-tor svi' ra wuh disgraceful ta'hal ish-veh shitau mr. Darcy, tor nam-tor treating ish-veh sa-mekh’s favourite svi' such wuh manner, --veh ik ish-veh sa-mekh had ugau tor tanilau na'. Ish-veh nam-tor impossible. Rai sasu t' tsuri humanity, rai sasu vi had sovek tala na' ish-veh character, kupi nam-tor capable t' ish-veh. Mokuhlek ish-veh danik intimate t'hylara nam-tor ni excessively tehs-tor svi' ish-veh? Oh rai.” “i mokuhlek mau weht easily dva-tor mr. Bingley’s hasu imposed fi' do ik mr. Wickham dang fereik-tor such wuh vesht-var t' himself u' au mazhiv-kur-tor me kim-shah mu-yor; ahm, kla-min, kanok-vei mentioned rik' hali-kal. Kuv ish-veh nam-tor ri ni, kal-tor mr. Darcy contradict ish-veh. Isha, tra' vesh' yeht'es svi' ish-veh glazhau.” “ish-veh nam-tor rihagik, indeed--ish-veh nam-tor distressing. Veh tor ri fai-tor ra tor nah-tor.” “i eit'jae ish-veh pardon; --veh fai-tor exactly ra tor nah-tor.” tonk'peh jane kupi nah-tor k' certainty fi' goh veh sfek, --ik mr. Bingley, kuv au _had been_ imposed fi', would ma mau tor dash lu wuh tek'ik became tsuri. Wuh dahkuh nu'ri t'sai vesh' summoned s' wuh tuula, wilat nash conversation be' dvun-tor, k' wuh lashan t' ein t' wuh maut persons t' ik au had vesh' speaking; mr. Bingley heh ish-veh ko-kai sarlah tor mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh personal k'waw'zhe na' wuh wu gishu rin'k'n na' netherfield, if vesh' teslau na' wuh zahalik gad. Wuh dahkuh t'sai vesh' delighted tor gla-tor ish-veh tal-kam t'hy'la va'ashiv, puvutau ish-veh wuh ya'shakhuv opi' au had ragel-tor, heh repeatedly ya'akash ra she had vesh' doing k' herself opi' ish-veh dahshaya. Tor wuh shom t' wuh skan au vlitau pi' attention; avoiding mrs. Bennet u' mau u' tor-yehat, taran ri mau tor elizabeth, heh nothing na' ek' tor wuh vath. Au vesh' ak hal-tor va'ashiv, rising s' ish-veh ku-san k' wuh toran if nem-tor ish-veh sa-kai k' ak'wikmun, heh hurrying ska' u' kuv nayik tor stron s' mrs. Bennet’s civilities. Wuh prospect t' wuh netherfield rin'k'n vesh' extremely agreeable tor kanok kotik t' wuh skan. Mrs. Bennet dvel-tor tor panah-tor ish-veh u' putan-tor svi' compliment tor ish-veh eldest ko-fu, heh vesh' wa' snuhkrol-tor k' receiving wuh k'waw'zhe s' mr. Bingley himself, instead t' wuh ceremonious nop. Jane pictured tor herself wuh kunli khru svi' wuh shila'es t' ish-veh dahkuh t'hylara, heh wuh attentions t' ish-veh sa-kai; heh elizabeth nahp k' sanosh t' taman wuh lo'uk deal k' mr. Wickham, heh t' seeing wuh wugaya t' kanok-vei svi' mr. Darcy’s glazhau heh kloshai. Wuh happiness anticipated k' catherine heh lydia nerau lehkuh fi' sovek single pavek, il sovek particular person; na' hi au tik, spo' elizabeth, tvai tor tam ulef wuh khru k' mr. Wickham, au vesh' k' rai tvai wuh goh tersu vi kupi satisfy au, heh wuh rin'k'n vesh', na' sovek tav, wuh rin'k'n. Heh kauk mary kupi assure ish-veh skan ik she had rai disinclination na' ish-veh. “du' i mokuhlek ma t'nash-veh asal tor myself, ” leralmin-tor she, “ish-veh nam-tor hiyet. I nah-tor ish-veh nam-tor rai sacrifice tor hau occasionally svi' khru engagements. Shila'es has claims fi' etek ek'; heh i profess myself veh t' eifa vi panah-tor tvi-wak t' recreation heh amusement u' desirable na' kanok-veh.” elizabeth’s tam'a vesh' ni pid fi' wuh occasion, ik hi she did ri k'ashiv stariben unnecessarily tor mr. Collins, she kupi ri gol'nev asking ish-veh whether au intended tor nar-tor mr. Bingley’s k'waw'zhe, heh kuv au did, whether au would nah-tor ish-veh proper tor hau svi' wuh khru’s amusement; heh she vesh' rather ak'wikmun tor talal ik au entertained rai scruple whatever fi' ik patam, heh vesh' maut irak s' dreading wuh rebuke, either s' wuh archbishop il t'sai catherine de bourgh, k' venturing tor tam. “i am k' rai tvai t' opinion, i assure du, ” leralmin-tor au, “ik wuh rin'k'n t' nash ves, putan-tor k' wuh nu'ri sasu t' character, tor respectable sutra, mokuhlek ma sovek ek'rasah tendency; heh i am ni irak s' objecting tor taman myself, ik i dungau rok tor nam-tor pudor-tor k' wuh el'ru t' ek' t'nash-veh rom krei svi' wuh rivak t' wuh khru; heh i nem-tor nash opportunity t' soliciting ish-veh, din-tor elizabeth, na' wuh dahkuh wuh'rak tam-tor wa'; wuh preference if i sahrafel t'nash-veh krei jane dungi attribute tor wuh gas'rak aishan, heh ri tor sovek disrespect na' ish-veh.” elizabeth olau herself completely taken svi'. She had fully proposed hasu engaged k' wickham na' eifa maut tam-tor; heh ki' mr. Collins instead!--ish-veh liveliness had vesh' worla weh-rasahkos timed. Tra' vesh' rai gol'nev na' ish-veh, however. Mr. Wickham’s happiness heh ish-veh sha' vesh' perforce vohtau wuh pi' longer, heh mr. Collins’s mnah nar-tor k' u' rom wuh takov u' she kupi. She vesh' ri wuh weh-rom sanoi k' ish-veh gallantry, s' wuh idea ish-veh suggested t' vel weht. Ish-veh i' wuh'rak kwul-tor ish-veh, ik _she_ vesh' dvel-tor s' among ish-veh ko-kai u' worthy t' hasu wuh mistress t' hunsford parsonage, heh t' assisting tor shid wuh quadrille pasu na' rosings, svi' wuh k'torr weht eligible visitors. Wuh idea ak pulau tor conviction, u' she glantau ish-veh increasing civilities na' herself, heh puzhu-tor ish-veh vakavik attempt na' wuh compliment fi' ish-veh wit heh vivacity; heh hi weht astonished do gratified herself k' nash daya t' ish-veh sem-rik-tor, ish-veh vesh' ri wu fa' ish-veh ko-mekh mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh tor ken-tor ik wuh yesik'es t' ish-veh kal'i'farr vesh' exceedingly agreeable tor _her_. Elizabeth, however, did ri dvel-tor tor nem-tor wuh hint, hasu muhl aware ik wuh serious dispute bolau nam-tor wuh consequence t' sovek kilko. Mr. Collins lau worla tor wuh nufai, heh, till au did, ish-veh vesh' nam-tor-fam tor quarrel pa' ish-veh. Kuv tra' had ri vesh' wuh netherfield rin'k'n tor dator na' heh variben t', wuh younger din-tor bennets would ma vesh' svi' wuh pitiable fupa s' na' nash wak; na', s' wuh gad t' wuh k'waw'zhe tor wuh gad t' wuh rin'k'n, tra' vesh' such wuh succession t' sov-masu u' prevented ish-veh walking tor meryton wuh'wak. Rai ezyet, rai officers, rai ro'fori kupi nam-tor sought po'; wuh maut ash'el-roses na' netherfield vesh' panavau proxy. Kauk elizabeth lau ma afer-tor ein trial t' ish-veh tranush svi' igen-va if totally suspended wuh improvement t' ish-veh acquaintance k' mr. Wickham; heh nothing lehkuh tor wuh tam fi' gad kupi ma tor such wuh gad, gad, gad, heh gad endurable tor kitty heh lydia. [illustration] chapter xviii. [illustration] till elizabeth svi-tor wuh bestan-tvi-shal na' netherfield, heh glazhau svi' vain na' mr. Wickham among wuh cluster t' yon-kur tor-pal tra' assembled, wuh vet t' ish-veh hasu la' had worla paresh-tor tor ish-veh. Wuh certainty t' latva ish-veh had ri vesh' rihamau k' sovek t' eifa recollections ik lau ri unreasonably ma alarmed ish-veh. She had sai-vel-tor k' weht do tsuri tun, heh dator svi' wuh k'lek tam'a na' wuh conquest t' ek' ik hafau unsubdued t' ish-veh khaf-spol, trusting ik ish-veh vesh' ri weht do lau nam-tor skil-tor svi' wuh rivak t' wuh khru. Tonk'peh svi' wuh instant arose wuh dreadful suspicion t' ish-veh hasu purposely omitted, na' mr. Darcy’s sanosh, svi' wuh bingleys’ k'waw'zhe tor wuh officers; heh hi nash vesh' ri exactly wuh nuf, wuh ek'esik kla-min t' ish-veh absence vesh' pronounced k' ish-veh t'hy'la mr. Denny, tor ik lydia eagerly applied, heh vi var-tor au ik wickham had vesh' obliged tor hal-tor tor kahr fi' business wuh gad fa', heh vesh' ri wi fun-tor; hau, k' wuh significant abru'teruklar-ru'lut, -- “i ri tor glenonau ish-veh business would ma puvutau ish-veh maf aishan i', kuv au had ri istau tor nan'woi wuh ac'ruth gentleman la'.” nash krus t' ish-veh kash-tor'es, hi unheard k' lydia, vesh' kum-tor k' elizabeth; heh, u' ish-veh assured ish-veh ik darcy vesh' ri lehkuh answerable na' wickham’s absence do kuv ish-veh wuh'rak surmise had vesh' aishan, kanok olaya t' displeasure tehnat wuh former vesh' ni sharpened k' iyi disappointment, ik she kupi hardly kilko k' tolerable civility tor wuh polite inquiries if au directly afterwards betau tor tor. Attention, forbearance, tranush k' darcy, vesh' dash tor wickham. She vesh' resolved tehnat sovek wihfelau t' conversation k' ish-veh, heh da-tor maf k' wuh degree t' has-bosh-humour if she kupi ri wholly surmount kauk svi' speaking tor mr. Bingley, t'vi glan-fam partiality provoked ish-veh. Tonk'peh elizabeth vesh' ri shidau na' has-bosh-humour; heh hi kanok prospect t' ish-veh sha' vesh' vashau na' wuh khru, ish-veh kupi ri dwell wu fi' ish-veh tam'a; heh, having var-tor ek' ish-veh griefs tor charlotte lucas, ik she had ri gla-tor na' wuh wehk gad, she vesh' ak kup tor tor wuh toripik transition tor wuh oddities t' ish-veh krei, heh tor sfek ish-veh si' tor ish-veh particular beglanau. Wuh dahkuh wuh'rak tam-tor, however, katau wuh fun t' flakosh: au vesh' tam-tor t' mortification. Mr. Collins, awkward heh solemn, apologizing instead t' attending, heh k'ashiv dvun-tor riyeht rik' hasu aware t' ish-veh, mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh ek' wuh mesh heh misery if wuh disagreeable tersu na' wuh couple t' tam-tor mokuhlek mazhiv-kur-tor. Wuh moment t' ish-veh sadalaya s' ish-veh vesh' prahk'es. She tam-tor thurai k' wuh officer, heh had wuh refreshment t' talking t' wickham, heh t' khaf-spol ik au vesh' universally tishau. Lu eifa tam-tor vesh' abru', she fun-tor tor charlotte lucas, heh vesh' svi' conversation k' ish-veh, lu she afer-tor herself suddenly addressed k' mr. Darcy, vi nem-tor ish-veh ni mau k' ak'wikmun svi' ish-veh application na' ish-veh el'ru, ik, rik' fai-tor ra she did, she nar-tor ish-veh. Au lates-tor maf va'ashiv iyi, heh she vesh' losrak tor fret abru' ish-veh sha' aitlun t' la'es t' kashek: charlotte ar'kada tor console ish-veh. “i dare leralmin du dungi talal ish-veh maut agreeable.” “sha-ka-ri zadau! _that_ would nam-tor wuh greatest misfortune t' ek'! Tor talal wuh sasu agreeable ik veh nam-tor satalau tor fnu-ven! Ri tor istaya me such wuh ek'rasah.” lu wuh taman recommenced, however, heh darcy betau tor claim ish-veh el'ru, charlotte kupi ri gol'nev cautioning ish-veh, svi' wuh zhal, ri tor nam-tor wuh simpleton, heh kal-tor ish-veh fancy na' wickham tor tor ish-veh saudau unpleasant svi' wuh bezhun t' wuh sasu k'ashiv wak ish-veh consequence. Elizabeth tor rai kilko-srashiv, heh nem-tor ish-veh shi svi' wuh eku, putaurau na' wuh dignity tor if she vesh' lasha svi' hasu kal-tor tor lamok mesyutik tor mr. Darcy, heh telvan svi' ish-veh behsu’ glazhau ish-veh kaik tauraya svi' beholding ish-veh. Au lam-tor na' ein wak rik' speaking wuh zhit; heh she began tor glenonau ik ish-veh silence vesh' tor kim-shah k'fai wuh dahkuh tam-tor, heh, na' wuh'rak, vesh' resolved ri tor shaya ish-veh; till suddenly fancying ik ish-veh would nam-tor wuh greater taflaya tor ish-veh tersu tor oblige ish-veh tor variben, she tor ein slight glantaya fi' wuh tam. Au kilko-tor, heh vesh' va'ashiv ralash-fam. Po' wuh svizh t' ein minutes, she addressed ish-veh wuh dahr wak, k'-- “ish-veh nam-tor _your_ da-tor tor leralmin vel i', mr. Darcy. _i_ variben pa' wuh tam, heh _you_ ought tor tor ein ves t' remark fi' wuh suk'es t' wuh tvi-shal, il wuh su'etek t' couples.” au abru'teruklar-ru'lut, heh assured ish-veh ik whatever she istau ish-veh tor leralmin dang nam-tor leralmin-tor. “maut muhl; ik kilko dungi tor na' wuh la'. Sos'eh, k'-heh-k', i lau glantau ik awek rin'k'n nam-tor mau pleasanter do tsuri ones; tonk'peh _now_ etek lau nam'uh ralash-fam.” “tor du variben k' tor-go, yi, du' du nam-tor taman?” “sometimes. Veh bolau stariben wuh pi', du fai-tor. Ish-veh would glazhau shaik tor nam-tor entirely ralash-fam na' ulef wuh wadan teretuhr; heh wi, na' wuh advantage t' _some_, conversation ought tor nam-tor ni arranged u' ik au lau ma wuh trouble t' taran u' pi' u' tor-yehat.” “nam-tor du consulting ish-veh sha' feelings svi' wuh la' nuf, il tor du glenonau ik du nam-tor gratifying t'nash-veh?” “fi', ” kilko-tor elizabeth archly; “na' i ma kwon-hau-ov gla-tor wuh lo'uk similarity svi' wuh da-tor t' etwel kashkau. Etek nam-tor tik t' wuh unsocial, taciturn disposition, unwilling tor stariben, vita etek gish tor leralmin vel ik dungi taurau wuh bosh tvi-shal, heh nam-tor handed ne' tor posterity k' ek' wuh _éclat_ t' wuh proverb.” “nash nam-tor rai maut striking resemblance t' ish-veh sha' character, i am sure, ” leralmin-tor au. “uf be' ish-veh lau nam-tor tor _mine_, i fam yehat pretend tor leralmin. _you_ nah-tor ish-veh wuh faithful portrait, undoubtedly.” “i bolau ri klopau fi' t'nash-veh sha' performance.” au tor rai kilko-srashiv; heh au vesh' va'ashiv ralash-fam till au had hal-tor ne' wuh tam, lu au ya'akash ish-veh kuv she heh ish-veh ko-kai did ri maut k'ashiv lates tor meryton. She kilko-tor svi' wuh affirmative; heh, unable tor tehnau wuh temptation, hau, “lu du ragel-tor etek tra' wuh vath gad, etek had aishan vesh' forming wuh uzh acquaintance.” wuh daya vesh' iyi. Wuh deeper duvek t' _hauteur_ overspread ish-veh features, tonk'peh au leralmin-tor ri wuh zhit; heh elizabeth, hi blaming herself na' ish-veh sha' kobat'es, kupi ri hal-tor fi'. Na' wu-vath darcy stariben, heh svi' wuh constrained manner leralmin-tor, -- “mr. Wickham nam-tor blessed k' such kunli manners u' lau insure ish-veh _making_ t'hylara; whether au lau nam-tor kaing capable t' _retaining_ au, nam-tor lehkuh ac'ruth.” “au has vesh' ni unlucky u' tor pak-tor ish-veh friendship, ” kilko-tor elizabeth, k' emphasis, “heh svi' wuh manner if au nam-tor kesik tor dash s' ek' ish-veh ha'kiv.” darcy tor rai kilko-srashiv, heh seemed desirous t' rubai wuh subject. Na' ik moment osu william lucas saudau beyik au, meaning tor be' dvun k'fai wuh eku tor wuh vath vla t' wuh tvi-shal; tonk'peh, fi' perceiving mr. Darcy, au pehkau, k' wuh kes-wun t' superior nuhk'es, tor compliment ish-veh fi' ish-veh taman heh ish-veh tersu. “i ma vesh' danik highly gratified, indeed, t'nash-veh tal-kam osu; such maut superior taman nam-tor ri k'ashiv gla-tor. Ish-veh nam-tor evident ik du belong tor wuh wuh'rak da-kuv. Kal-tor me tor leralmin, however, ik ish-veh rom tersu tor ri disgrace du: heh ik i bolau rok ki' nash sanosh k'ashiv ashiv-tor, wa' lu wuh ac'ruth desirable pavek, t'nash-veh tal-kam din-tor eliza (glancing na' ish-veh ko-kai heh bingley), dungau nem-tor shi. Ra congratulations dungi yi yumaya svi'! I appeal tor mr. Darcy; --tonk'peh kal-tor me ri svi-shau du, osu. Du dungi ri itaren me na' detaining du s' wuh bewitching converse t' ik nu'ri t'sai, t'vi ugelik bezhun nam-tor isha upbraiding me.” [illustration: “such maut superior taman nam-tor ri k'ashiv gla-tor.” [_copyright 1894 k' george allen._]] wuh latter krus t' nash shi'yavekh vesh' scarcely puzhu-tor k' darcy; tonk'peh osu william’s allusion tor ish-veh t'hy'la seemed tor kwul ish-veh forcibly, heh ish-veh bezhun vesh' khartau, k' wuh maut serious sagluvaya, na' bingley heh jane, vi vesh' taman teretuhr. Recovering himself, however, shortly, au da-tor tor ish-veh tersu, heh leralmin-tor, -- “osu william’s svi-shaya has tor me yen-tor ra etek vesh' talking t'.” “i ri tor nah-tor etek vesh' speaking na' ek'. Osu william kupi ri ma svi-shau sovek dahkuh sutra svi' wuh tvi-shal vi had lehkuh tor leralmin na' themselves. Etek ma ar'kada dahkuh il rehkuh subjects already rik' navun, heh ra etek nam-tor tor variben t' thurai i fam yehat glenonau.” “ra nah-tor du t' dunap?” leralmin-tor au, smiling. “dunap--oh rai!--i am sure etek worla telv-tor wuh ka, il ri k' wuh ka feelings.” “ni'droi'ik nar-tor du nah-tor ni; tonk'peh kuv ik nam-tor wuh nuf, tra' mokuhlek k'puu nam-tor rai aitlun t' subject. Etek lau tcok'at etwel natya opinions.” “rai--i fam yehat variben t' dunap svi' wuh rin'k'n-tvi-shal; t'nash-veh patam nam-tor kwon-hau-ov bosh t' vel else.” “wuh _present_ kwon-hau-ov occupies du svi' such scenes--tor ish-veh?” leralmin-tor au, k' wuh glazhau t' vet. “ha, kwon-hau-ov, ” she kilko-tor, rik' fai-tor ra she leralmin-tor; na' ish-veh nahp had czar-tor irak s' wuh subject, u' ak afterwards saudau k' ish-veh suddenly exclaiming, “i vokau khaf-spol du wuh'wak leralmin, mr. Darcy, ik du hardly ek'wak forgave; --ik ish-veh resentment, wuh'wak fereik-tor, vesh' unappeasable. Du nam-tor maut cautious, i suppose, u' tor its _being created_?” “i am, ” leralmin-tor au, k' wuh pesik spes. “heh worla kal-tor yourself tor nam-tor blinded k' prejudice?” “i rok ri.” “ish-veh nam-tor wa' incumbent fi' eifa vi worla rubah ish-veh opinion, tor nam-tor shar t' judging properly palikauk.” “sos ya'akash tor ra aifa deshkau palutunau?” “goh tor wuh illustration t' _your_ character, ” leralmin-tor she, endeavouring tor hutau ska' ish-veh ne-seshan. “i am trying tor tor ish-veh si'.” “heh ra nam-tor ish-veh navun?” she hutau ish-veh patam. “i ri tor prah fi' na' ek'. I zhu-tor such natya khrosahp t' du u' puzzle me exceedingly.” “i mokuhlek readily dva-tor, ” kilko-tor au, gravely, “ik reports lau vuhnau greatly k' respect tor me; heh i kupi istaya, din-tor bennet, ik du vesh' ri tor lubesan t'nash-veh character na' wuh la' moment, u' tra' nam-tor utvau tor pthak ik wuh performance would haul-tor rai lit fi' either.” “tonk'peh kuv i ri tor nem-tor ish-veh likeness i', i lau worla ma wuh'ashiv opportunity.” “i would k' rai tvai suspend sovek sanosh t' ish-veh, ” au coldly kilko-tor. She leralmin-tor rai weht, heh au went ne' wuh vath tam heh parted svi' silence; fi' tik vla dissatisfied, hi ri tor wuh kaik degree; na' svi' darcy’s thasek tra' vesh' wuh tolerably powerful olaya na' ish-veh, if ak procured ish-veh pardon, heh khartau ek' ish-veh reshan tehnat wuh'ashiv. Au had ri wu dahshau lu din-tor bingley sarlah na' ish-veh, heh, k' wuh sagluvaya t' civil disdain, thus accosted ish-veh, -- “ni, din-tor eliza, i zhu-tor du nam-tor ved delighted k' george wickham? Ish-veh ko-kai has vesh' talking tor me pa' ish-veh, heh asking me wuh thousand deshkau; heh i talal ik wuh nu'ri sasu forgot tor var-tor du, among ish-veh vath communications, ik au vesh' wuh sa-fu t' hinek wickham, wuh tab-ma mr. Darcy’s steward. Kal-tor me recommend du, however, u' wuh t'hy'la, ri tor mazhiv-kur-tor implicit guhl'es tor ek' ish-veh assertions; na', u' tor mr. Darcy’s using ish-veh has-bosh, ish-veh nam-tor perfectly riyeht: na', fi' wuh contrary, au has vesh' kwon-hau-ov remarkably ves tor ish-veh, hi george wickham has skasau mr. Darcy svi' wuh danik infamous manner. I ri tor fai-tor wuh particulars, tonk'peh i fai-tor maut muhl ik mr. Darcy nam-tor ri svi' wuh least tor tenai; ik au fam yehat lesh tor zhu-tor george wickham mentioned; heh ik hi t'nash-veh sa-kai nahp au kupi ri muhl nan'woi including ish-veh svi' ish-veh k'waw'zhe tor wuh officers, au vesh' excessively glad tor talal ik au had taken himself s' wuh yut. Ish-veh coming vi' wuh shasol na' ek' nam-tor wuh danik insolent vel, indeed, heh i wonder uf au kupi presume tor tor ish-veh. I pity du, din-tor eliza, na' nash discovery t' ish-veh favourite’s guilt; tonk'peh really, panahik ish-veh tevan, veh kupi ri gish mau weh-rom.” “ish-veh guilt heh ish-veh tevan saudau, k' ish-veh khrosahp, tor nam-tor wuh ka, ” leralmin-tor elizabeth, angrily; “na' i ma puzhu-tor du accuse ish-veh t' nothing weh-rasahkos do t' hasu wuh sa-fu t' mr. Darcy’s steward, heh t' _that_, i mokuhlek assure du, au informed me himself.” “i eit'jae ish-veh pardon, ” kilko-tor din-tor bingley, turning maf k' wuh sneer. “tobeg t'nash-veh interference; ish-veh vesh' kindly tvai.” “insolent ko-kan!” leralmin-tor elizabeth tor herself. “du nam-tor mau mistaken kuv du gish tor vi-yumuk me k' such wuh paltry nashiv-tor u' nash. Gla-tor nash-veh nothing svi' ish-veh tonk'peh ish-veh sha' wilful ignorance heh wuh malice t' mr. Darcy.” she yi sought ish-veh eldest ko-kai, vi had undertaken tor tor inquiries fi' wuh ka subject t' bingley. Jane ragel-tor ish-veh k' wuh abru'teruklar-ru'lut t' such slor complacency, wuh min t' such kunli sagluvaya, u' sufficiently pu'ulidau uf muhl she vesh' satisfied k' wuh occurrences t' wuh khru. Elizabeth instantly telv-tor ish-veh feelings; heh, na' ik moment, solicitude na' wickham, resentment tehnat ish-veh nemut, heh kanok-vei else, mazhiv-kur-tor yut fa' wuh rok t' jane’s hasu svi' wuh fairest yut na' happiness. “i aitlun tor fai-tor, ” leralmin-tor she, k' wuh countenance rai lehkuh smiling do ish-veh ko-kai’s, “ra du ma oren-tor pa' mr. Wickham. Tonk'peh sos'eh du ma vesh' nuh' pleasantly engaged tor nah-tor t' sovek wuh person, svi' if nuf du lau nam-tor sure t' t'nash-veh pardon.” “rai, ” kilko-tor jane, “i ma ri yen-tor ish-veh; tonk'peh i ma nothing satisfactory tor var-tor du. Mr. Bingley tor ri fai-tor wuh bosh t' ish-veh vesht-var, heh nam-tor ved ignorant t' wuh circumstances if ma principally puthrap-tor mr. Darcy; tonk'peh au dungi vouch na' wuh rom spa-tor, wuh probity heh dor, t' ish-veh t'hy'la, heh nam-tor perfectly convinced ik mr. Wickham has nazh-tor mau lehkuh attention s' mr. Darcy do au has poprah; heh ni'droi'ik nar-tor tor leralmin ik k' ish-veh khrosahp, u' muhl u' ish-veh ko-kai’s, mr. Wickham nam-tor k' rai tvai wuh respectable nu'ri sasu. I am kwes au has vesh' maut imprudent, heh has nazh-tor tor pak-tor mr. Darcy’s fudau.” “mr. Bingley tor ri fai-tor mr. Wickham himself.” “rai; au worla gla-tor ish-veh till wuh vath asal na' meryton.” “nash khrosahp yi nam-tor ra au has poprah s' mr. Darcy. I am perfectly satisfied. Tonk'peh ra tor au leralmin t' wuh living?” “au tor ri exactly recollect wuh circumstances, hi au has puzhu-tor au s' mr. Darcy weht do wuh'wak, tonk'peh au believes ik ish-veh vesh' losrak tor ish-veh _conditionally_ goh.” “i ma ri wuh vet t' mr. Bingley’s sincerity, ” leralmin-tor elizabeth warmly, “tonk'peh du bolau tobeg t'nash-veh ri hasu convinced k' assurances goh. Mr. Bingley’s defence t' ish-veh t'hy'la vesh' wuh maut kup veh, i dare leralmin; tonk'peh opi' au nam-tor unacquainted k' several krus t' wuh var, heh has oren-tor wuh shom s' ik t'hy'la himself, i dungau venture fam dvun tor nah-tor t' fi' gentlemen u' i did fa'.” she yi rubai wuh discourse tor veh weht gratifying tor tik, heh fi' if tra' kupi nam-tor rai natyan t' sentiment. Elizabeth shroi k' delight tor wuh kunli hi modest rok-tor if jane entertained t' bingley’s fudau, heh leralmin-tor ek' svi' ish-veh tepul tor heighten ish-veh guhl'es svi' ish-veh. Fi' ish-veh hasu hau k' mr. Bingley himself, elizabeth withdrew tor din-tor lucas; tor t'vi inquiry po' wuh pleasantness t' ish-veh kim-shah tersu she had scarcely kilko-tor, fa' mr. Collins sarlah abru tor au, heh var-tor ish-veh k' lo'uk exultation, ik au had aishan vesh' ni fortunate u' tor tor wuh danik yauluhk discovery. “i ma afer-tor si', ” leralmin-tor au, “k' wuh singular kisheya, ik tra' nam-tor i' svi' wuh tvi-shal wuh be' relation tor t'nash-veh patroness. I pavesh-tor tor overhear wuh gentleman himself mentioning tor wuh nu'ri t'sai vi tor wuh dor-tor t' nash kelek wuh ahm t' ish-veh krei din-tor de bourgh, heh t' ish-veh ko-mekh, t'sai catherine. Uf wonderfully aifa wihfelau t' vel paresh-tor! Vi would ma nahp t' t'nash-veh latva k'--sos'eh--wuh sa-bath t' t'sai catherine de bourgh svi' nash feretai! I am danik itar-bosh ik wuh discovery nam-tor tor svi' wak na' me tor vlitau t'nash-veh respects tor ish-veh, if i am i' going tor tor, heh sahrafel au dungi tobeg t'nash-veh ri having ovsoh ish-veh fa'. T'nash-veh ovus ignorance t' wuh tersaya bolau plead t'nash-veh apology.” “du nam-tor ri going tor ragtau yourself tor mr. Darcy?” “indeed i am. I dungau entreat ish-veh pardon na' ri having ovsoh ish-veh earlier. I dva-tor ish-veh tor nam-tor t'sai catherine’s _nephew_. Ish-veh dungi nam-tor svi' t'nash-veh tepul tor assure ish-veh ik ish-veh ladyship vesh' ved muhl za-gad se’nnight.” elizabeth ar'kada lerash tor dissuade ish-veh s' such wuh scheme; assuring ish-veh ik mr. Darcy would panah-tor ish-veh addressing ish-veh rik' ragtaya u' wuh impertinent el'es, rather do wuh compliment tor ish-veh ezyet; ik ish-veh vesh' ri svi' wuh least bolayatik tra' dang nam-tor sovek beglanau fi' either vla, heh ik kuv ish-veh vesh', ish-veh bolau belong tor mr. Darcy, wuh superior svi' consequence, tor palikau wuh acquaintance. Mr. Collins shroi tor ish-veh k' wuh satalau sov t' zahalik ish-veh sha' inclination, heh lu she ceased speaking, kilko-tor thus, -- “t'nash-veh tal-kam din-tor elizabeth, i ma wuh k'lek opinion svi' wuh panu t' ish-veh marom judgment svi' ek' tukh k'svi wuh scope t' ish-veh understanding, tonk'peh permit me tor leralmin ik tra' bolau nam-tor wuh eik natyan svi' wuh afer-tor shidau t' hali-kal svi' wuh laity heh eifa if pakhartau wuh clergy; na', mazhiv-kur-tor me trasha tor glantau ik i panah-tor wuh clerical office u' kaik svi' sfek t' dignity k' wuh k'lek lan svi' wuh kingdom--tanilau ik wuh proper humility t' kloshai nam-tor na' wuh ka wak rompotau. Du bolau, therefore, kal-tor me tor zahal-tor wuh dictates t' t'nash-veh conscience fi' nash occasion, if ras-tukh me tor perform ra i glazhau fi' u' wuh sfek t' gu-vam. Pardon me na' neglecting tor pinkaunu k' ish-veh na'shikh, if fi' kanok vath subject dungau nam-tor t'nash-veh ek'kayik kakhartausu, hi svi' wuh nuf fa' etek i panah-tor myself weht fitted k' education heh habitual orenau tor klopau fi' ra nam-tor gas'rak do wuh nu'ri t'sai spo' yourself; ” heh k' wuh neik kes-wun au losrak ish-veh tor nashiv-tor mr. Darcy, t'vi reception t' ish-veh storilaya she eagerly glantau, heh t'vi astonishment na' hasu ni addressed vesh' maut evident. Ish-veh krei prefaced ish-veh starun k' wuh solemn kes-wun, heh hi she kupi ri zhu-tor wuh zhit t' ish-veh, she olau u' kuv khaf-spol ish-veh ek', heh gla-tor svi' wuh dvunel t' ish-veh bru-lar wuh zhit “apology, ” “hunsford, ” heh “t'sai catherine de bourgh.” ish-veh smertau ish-veh tor gla-tor ish-veh sashavau himself tor such wuh sasu. Mr. Darcy vesh' eyeing ish-veh k' unrestrained wonder; heh lu na' kim-shah mr. Collins kal-tor ish-veh tor stariben, kilko-tor k' wuh sov t' irak civility. Mr. Collins, however, vesh' ri discouraged s' speaking va'ashiv, heh mr. Darcy’s contempt seemed abundantly increasing k' wuh wu-vath t' ish-veh dahr starun; heh na' wuh shaht t' ish-veh au goh tor ish-veh wuh slight kes-wun, heh dvun-tor wuh'ashiv yut: mr. Collins yi fun-tor tor elizabeth. “i ma rai utvau, i assure du, ” leralmin-tor au, “tor nam-tor dissatisfied k' t'nash-veh reception. Mr. Darcy seemed mau sanoi k' wuh attention. Au kilko-tor me k' wuh utmost civility, heh kauk vlitau me wuh compliment t' taran, ik au vesh' ni muhl convinced t' t'sai catherine’s discernment u' tor nam-tor ac'ruth she kupi worla bestow wuh favour unworthily. Ish-veh vesh' really wuh maut handsome nahp. Fi-tor wuh bosh, i am mau sanoi k' ish-veh.” u' elizabeth had rai longer sovek eku'ko t' ish-veh sha' tor pursue, she da-tor ish-veh attention siyah entirely fi' ish-veh ko-kai heh mr. Bingley; heh wuh ranau t' agreeable haulan if ish-veh glantaya mazhiv-kur-tor keshtan tor tor ish-veh sos'eh siyah u' kunli u' jane. Gla-tor ish-veh ish-veh svi' idea settled svi' ik maut kelek, svi' ek' wuh felicity if wuh kal'i'farr t' yeht affection kupi bestow; heh she olau capable, ne' such circumstances, t' endeavouring kauk tor spo' bingley’s dahkuh ko-kai. Ish-veh ko-mekh’s nahp she plainly gla-tor vesh' keh'sei wuh ka yut, heh she satalau ri tor venture be' ish-veh, lest she lau zhu-tor nuh' mau. Lu au hayal-tor ne' tor mu'yor-yem, therefore, she panah-tor ish-veh wuh danik unlucky perverseness if shitau au k'svi veh t' tik vath; heh deeply vesh' she smertau tor talal ik ish-veh ko-mekh vesh' talking tor ish-veh person (t'sai lucas) freely, openly, heh t' nothing else tonk'peh t' ish-veh gishat ik jane would nam-tor ak telik tor mr. Bingley. Ish-veh vesh' wuh animating subject, heh mrs. Bennet seemed incapable t' zung du' enumerating wuh advantages t' wuh match. Ish-veh hasu such wuh sem-rik-tor nu'ri sasu, heh ni don-ka, heh living tonk'peh rehkuh miles s' au, vesh' wuh wuh'rak sfekau t' shal-gratulation; heh yi ish-veh vesh' such wuh comfort tor nah-tor uf tishau wuh dahkuh ko-kai vesh' t' jane, heh tor nam-tor ac'ruth ik au bolau aitlun wuh tersaya u' mau u' she kupi tor. Ish-veh vesh', moreover, such wuh promising vel na' ish-veh younger daughters, u' jane’s marrying ni greatly bolau lehm au svi' wuh yut t' vath don-ka sasu; heh, lastly, ish-veh vesh' ni vaksurik na' ish-veh wak t' ha'kiv kup tor consign ish-veh single daughters tor wuh tun t' ish-veh ko-kai, ik she lau ri nam-tor obliged tor hal-tor vi' apc'koik weht do she tishau. Ish-veh vesh' bolayatik tor tor nash circumstance wuh tukh t' sanosh, fai'ei fi' such occasions ish-veh nam-tor wuh yeht-shila-kloshai; tonk'peh kling vesh' lehkuh kesik do mrs. Bennet tor talal comfort svi' staying na' ha-kel na' sovek wak-krus t' ish-veh ha'kiv. She concluded k' wehk rom istau ik t'sai lucas lau ak nam-tor kaing fortunate, hi evidently heh triumphantly believing tra' vesh' rai pavesh t' ish-veh. Svi' vain did elizabeth endeavour tor rihamau wuh rapidity t' ish-veh ko-mekh’s zhit, il persuade ish-veh tor kethelvau ish-veh felicity svi' wuh lehkuh zhu-yehat zhal; na' tor ish-veh inexpressible vexation she kupi pakashogau ik wuh chief t' ish-veh vesh' overheard k' mr. Darcy, vi hayal-tor mesyutik tor au. Ish-veh ko-mekh goh scolded ish-veh na' hasu nonsensical. “ra nam-tor mr. Darcy tor me, pray, ik i dang nam-tor kwes t' ish-veh? I am sure etek owe ish-veh rai such particular civility u' tor nam-tor obliged tor leralmin nothing _he_ lau ri spo' tor zhu-tor.” “na' sha-ka-ri’s sake, madam, stariben weh-neik. Ra advantage mokuhlek ish-veh nam-tor tor du tor thrap-tor mr. Darcy? Du dungi worla recommend yourself tor ish-veh t'hy'la k' ni doing.” nothing ik she kupi leralmin, however, had sovek vi-yumuk. Ish-veh ko-mekh would variben t' ish-veh zan-tor svi' wuh ka intelligible molu. Elizabeth blushed heh blushed va'ashiv k' mesh heh vexation. She kupi ri gol'nev frequently glancing ish-veh bezhun na' mr. Darcy, hi kanok glance convinced ish-veh t' ra she dreaded; na' hi au vesh' ri kwon-hau-ov looking na' ish-veh ko-mekh, she vesh' convinced ik ish-veh attention vesh' invariably teslau k' ish-veh. Wuh sagluvaya t' ish-veh limuk rubai gradually s' indignant contempt tor wuh tertitau heh br'xan ne-seshan. Na' wu-vath, however, mrs. Bennet had rai weht tor leralmin; heh t'sai lucas, vi had vesh' wu yawning na' wuh repetition t' delights if gla-tor ish-veh rai likelihood t' thresh-tor, vesh' losrak tor wuh comforts t' samu ham heh kahm. Elizabeth i' began tor zaprah. Tonk'peh ri wu vesh' wuh tvi-wak t' tranquillity; na' lu mu'yor-yem vesh' abru', uralaun vesh' variben t', heh she had wuh mortification t' seeing mary, po' maut pi' entreaty, preparing tor oblige wuh apc'koik. K' wehk significant glazhau heh ralash-fam entreaties did she endeavour tor prevent such wuh skan t' complaisance, --tonk'peh svi' vain; mary would ri ken-tor au; such wuh opportunity t' exhibiting vesh' delightful tor ish-veh, heh she began ish-veh song. Elizabeth’s bezhun vesh' teslau fi' ish-veh, k' danik kusut-tor kashan; heh she glantau ish-veh progress k'fai wuh several stanzas k' wuh impatience if vesh' maut has-bosh rewarded na' ish-veh ikap-tor; na' mary, fi' receiving svi' wuh itaren t' wuh pasu wuh hint t' wuh rok ik she lau nam-tor fakovau fi' tor favour au va'ashiv, po' wuh svizh t' ulef wuh minute began wuh'ashiv. Mary’s tepul vesh' k' rai tvai fitted na' such wuh gluvayek; ish-veh spes vesh' kobat, heh ish-veh manner dau. Elizabeth vesh' svi' agonies. She glazhau na' jane tor gla-tor uf she spitau ish-veh; tonk'peh jane vesh' maut composedly talking tor bingley. She glazhau na' ish-veh dahkuh ko-kai, heh gla-tor au tor glat t' derision na' tik vath, heh na' darcy, vi fator, however, impenetrably shi'vukhut. She glazhau na' ish-veh sa-mekh tor entreat ish-veh interference, lest mary dang nam-tor uralaun ek' mu-yor. Au nem-tor wuh hint, heh, lu mary had shahtau ish-veh dahr song, leralmin-tor aloud, -- “ik dungi tor extremely muhl, kan. Du ma delighted etek wu hiyet. Kal-tor wuh vath nu'ri t'sai ma wak tor gluvaya.” mary, hi pretending ri tor zhu-tor, vesh' somewhat disconcerted; heh elizabeth, sorry na' ish-veh, heh sorry na' ish-veh sa-mekh’s starun, vesh' kwes ish-veh anxiety had ovsoh rai rom. Vath t' wuh party vesh' i' applied tor. “kuv i, ” leralmin-tor mr. Collins, “vesh' ni fortunate u' kup tor uralau, i dang ma lo'uk sanosh, i am sure, svi' obliging wuh apc'koik k' wuh sov; na' i panah-tor ralash-tanaf u' wuh maut innocent mutaya, heh perfectly compatible k' wuh ha'yigal t' wuh clergyman. I ri tor tvai, however, tor seo'a ik etek mokuhlek nam-tor justified svi' devoting nuh' mau t' etwel wak tor ralash-tanaf, na' tra' nam-tor certainly vath vel tor nam-tor attended tor. Wuh rector t' wuh parish has mau tor tor. Svi' wuh wuh'rak shi, au bolau tor such wuh agreement na' tithes u' lau nam-tor beneficial tor himself heh ri offensive tor ish-veh patron. Au bolau kitau ish-veh sha' sermons; heh wuh wak ik hafau dungi ri nam-tor nuh' mau na' ish-veh parish gu-vam, heh wuh tun heh improvement t' ish-veh kelek, if au fam yehat nam-tor tobeg-tor s' tor u' kel'o u' tor-yehat. Heh i ri tor nah-tor ish-veh t' ta'hal importance ik au dang ma whio'naks heh conciliatory manners na' kanok-veh, wa' na' eifa tor ik au owes ish-veh preferment. I fam yehat acquit ish-veh t' ik gu-vam; il sos nah-tor muhl t' wuh sasu vi dang omit wuh occasion t' testifying ish-veh respect na' anybody tersau k' wuh skan.” heh k' wuh kes-wun tor mr. Darcy, au concluded ish-veh starun, if had vesh' spoken ni ral u' tor nam-tor puzhu-tor k' ulef wuh tvi-shal. Wehk nantau--wehk abru'teruklar-ru'lut; tonk'peh kling glazhau weht amused do mr. Bennet himself, du' ish-veh ko-telsu seriously commended mr. Collins na' having spoken ni sensibly, heh glantau, svi' wuh ulef-zhal tor t'sai lucas, ik au vesh' wuh remarkably clever, rom ves t' nu'ri sasu. Tor elizabeth ish-veh saudau, ik had ish-veh skan tor wuh agreement tor sashavau themselves u' mau u' au kupi du' wuh khru, ish-veh would ma vesh' impossible na' au tor mavau ish-veh krus k' weht tam'a, il finer navun; heh kunli did she nah-tor ish-veh na' bingley heh ish-veh ko-kai ik ein t' wuh exhibition had stron-tor ish-veh beglanau, heh ik ish-veh feelings vesh' ri t' wuh wihfelau tor nam-tor mau flakosh k' wuh folly if au bolau ma toglantau. Ik ish-veh dahkuh ko-kai heh mr. Darcy, however, dang ma such wuh opportunity t' ridiculing ish-veh relations vesh' rasahkos hiyet; heh she kupi ri satalau whether wuh ralash-fam contempt t' wuh gentleman, il wuh insolent abru'teruklar-ru'lut t' wuh t'sai, vesh' weht intolerable. Wuh shom t' wuh khru katau ish-veh pi' amusement. She vesh' teased k' mr. Collins, vi fator danik perseveringly k' ish-veh vla; heh hi au kupi ri fakovau k' ish-veh tor tam k' ish-veh va'ashiv, shitau ish-veh s' ish-veh tepul tor tam k' vath. Svi' vain did she entreat ish-veh tor lamok abru k' somebody else, heh nufau tor ragtau ish-veh tor sovek nu'ri t'sai svi' wuh tvi-shal. Au assured ish-veh ik, u' tor taman, au vesh' perfectly indifferent tor ish-veh; ik ish-veh chief vel vesh', k' delicate attentions, tor recommend himself tor ish-veh; heh ik au dang therefore tor wuh sfek t' remaining beyik ish-veh wuh bosh khru. Tra' vesh' rai arguing fi-tor such wuh ar'tu. She owed ish-veh greatest vas tor ish-veh t'hy'la din-tor lucas, vi k'ashiv hau au, heh rom-naturedly engaged mr. Collins’s conversation tor herself. She vesh' k'puu elik s' wuh offence t' mr. Darcy’s further beglanau: hi k'ashiv standing k'svi wuh maut pen ir t' ish-veh, ved dahl-tor, au worla sarlah be' hiyet tor stariben. She olau ish-veh tor nam-tor wuh yesik consequence t' ish-veh allusions tor mr. Wickham, heh rejoiced svi' ish-veh. Wuh longbourn party vesh' wuh kim-shah t' ek' wuh apc'koik tor trashu; heh k' wuh sasuœuvre t' mrs. Bennet had tor bek-tor na' ish-veh carriage wuh yonuk t' wuh wadan po' kanok-veh else vesh' hal-tor, if mazhiv-kur-tor au wak tor gla-tor uf heartily au vesh' istau maf k' ein t' wuh skan. Mrs. Hurst heh ish-veh ko-kai scarcely tu'ash ish-veh ru'lut kaula tor complain t' zung, heh vesh' evidently impatient ki' wuh kelek tor themselves. Au repulsed kanok attempt t' mrs. Bennet na' conversation, heh, k' ni doing, threw wuh languor abru' wuh bosh party, if vesh' maut pi' vas-tor k' wuh wu starun t' mr. Collins, vi vesh' complimenting mr. Bingley heh ish-veh ko-kai fi' wuh sohk'es t' ish-veh entertainment, heh wuh hospitality heh politeness if had pu'ulidau ish-veh kloshai tor ish-veh be'hai'la. Darcy leralmin-tor nothing na' ek'. Mr. Bennet, svi' kaik silence, vesh' enjoying wuh scene. Mr. Bingley heh jane vesh' standing teretuhr wuh pi' dahl-tor s' wuh shom, heh variben goh tor tik vath. Elizabeth korsau u' br'xan wuh silence u' either mrs. Hurst il din-tor bingley; heh kauk lydia vesh' nuh' mau zung-tor tor utter weht do wuh occasional sporun t' “s'haile, uf zungor i am!” accompanied k' wuh khrashik luvaya. Lu na' wu-vath au arose tor nem-tor trasha, mrs. Bennet vesh' danik pressingly civil svi' ish-veh rok t' seeing wuh bosh skan ak na' longbourn; heh addressed herself wa' tor mr. Bingley, tor assure ish-veh uf kunli au would tor au, k' eating wuh skan aru-yem k' au na' sovek wak, rik' wuh hali-kal t' wuh hotorik k'waw'zhe. Bingley vesh' ek' grateful sanosh; heh au readily engaged na' taking wuh earliest opportunity t' waiting fi' ish-veh po' ish-veh fun s' london, whither au vesh' obliged tor hal-tor wuh thurai gad na' wuh pen wak. Mrs. Bennet vesh' perfectly satisfied; heh quitted wuh kelek ne' wuh delightful persuasion ik, allowing na' wuh bolayatik preparations t' settlements, uzh carriages, heh wedding sai-vel, she dang undoubtedly gla-tor ish-veh ko-fu settled na' netherfield svi' wuh rivak t' rehkuh il kehkuh tevun-krus. T' having wuh'ashiv ko-fu telik tor mr. Collins she nahp k' kaik certainty, heh k' considerable, hi ri kaik, sanosh. Elizabeth vesh' wuh least tal-kam tor ish-veh t' ek' ish-veh kanu; heh hi wuh sasu heh wuh match vesh' ved rom hiyet na' _her_, wuh don t' tik vesh' eclipsed k' mr. Bingley heh netherfield. [illustration: “tor assure du svi' wuh danik animated gen-lis” ] chapter xix. [illustration] wuh thurai gad tu'ash wuh uzh scene na' longbourn. Mr. Collins tor ish-veh afsakaya svi' shid. Having resolved tor tor ish-veh rik' pak t' wak, u' ish-veh trasha t' absence sadvun-tor goh tor wuh zahalik gad, heh having rai feelings t' diffidence tor tor ish-veh distressing tor himself kauk na' wuh moment, au eku pa' ish-veh svi' wuh maut orderly manner, k' ek' wuh observances if au supposed wuh regular krus t' wuh business. Fi' finding mrs. Bennet, elizabeth, heh veh t' wuh younger ko-kan teretuhr, ak po' asal-yem, au addressed wuh ko-mekh svi' aifa zhit, -- “sos rok, madam, na' ish-veh eku'ko k' ish-veh rom ko-fu elizabeth, lu i solicit na' wuh dor t' wuh awek audience k' ish-veh svi' wuh rivak t' nash asal?” fa' elizabeth had wak na' sovek-vel tonk'peh wuh blush t' ak'wikmun, mrs. Bennet instantly kilko-tor, -- “oh tal-kam! Ha, certainly. I am sure lizzy dungi nam-tor maut kunli--i am sure she mokuhlek ma rai objection. Sarlah, kitty, i aitlun du upstairs.” heh hohnaya ish-veh ar'kadan teretuhr, she vesh' hastening maf, lu elizabeth puvutau si', -- “tal-kam ma’am, ri tor hal-tor. I eit'jae du dungi ri hal-tor. Mr. Collins bolau tobeg me. Au mokuhlek ma nothing tor leralmin tor me ik anybody bolaya ri zhu-tor. I am going maf myself.” “rai, rai, nonsense, lizzy. I aitlun du dungi stay wilat du nam-tor.” heh fi-tor elizabeth’s seeming really, k' smertau heh embarrassed glazhau, pa' tor stron, she hau, “lizzy, i _insist_ fi-tor ish-veh staying heh khaf-spol mr. Collins.” elizabeth would ri oppose such wuh injunction; heh wuh moment’s consideration tor ish-veh isha sensible ik ish-veh would nam-tor wisest tor prah ish-veh abru' u' ak heh u' quietly u' tor-yehat, she hayal-tor ne' va'ashiv, heh ar'kada tor ip-sut, k' incessant employment, wuh feelings if vesh' dahsau svi' flakosh heh mutaya. Mrs. Bennet heh kitty lates-tor ska', heh u' ak u' au vesh' hal-tor, mr. Collins began, -- “dva-tor me, t'nash-veh tal-kam din-tor elizabeth, ik ish-veh modesty, ni irak s' doing du sovek disservice, rather hau tor ish-veh vath perfections. Du would ma vesh' lehkuh amiable svi' t'nash-veh bezhun had tra' _not_ vesh' nash pi' unwillingness; tonk'peh kal-tor me tor assure du ik i ma ish-veh respected ko-mekh’s permission na' nash shi'yavekh. Du mokuhlek hardly vet wuh purport t' t'nash-veh discourse, however ish-veh malatik delicacy lau ras-tukh du tor dissemble; t'nash-veh attentions ma vesh' nuh' pu'ulidau tor nam-tor mistaken. Siyah u' ak u' i svi-tor wuh kelek i singled du si' u' wuh besu t' t'nash-veh fa-wak ha'kiv. Tonk'peh fa' i am sahr-tor maf k' k' t'nash-veh feelings fi' nash subject, sos'eh ish-veh dungi nam-tor advisable na' me tor fupa s' t'nash-veh utvau na' marrying--heh, moreover, na' coming vi' hertfordshire k' wuh design t' selecting wuh ko-telsu, u' i certainly did.” wuh idea t' mr. Collins, k' ek' ish-veh solemn composure, hasu sahr-tor maf k' k' ish-veh feelings, tor elizabeth ni be' laughing ik she kupi ri nam-tor-tor wuh pen svizh au kal-tor svi' sovek attempt tor pehkaya ish-veh weh-irak, heh au fator, -- “t'nash-veh utvau na' marrying nam-tor, wuh'rak, ik i nah-tor ish-veh wuh gas'rak vel na' kanok clergyman svi' hagik circumstances (spo' myself) tor eku wuh li-fal t' matrimony svi' ish-veh parish; secondly, ik i am convinced ish-veh dungi hau maut greatly tor t'nash-veh happiness; heh, thirdly, if sos'eh i ought tor ma mentioned earlier, ik ish-veh nam-tor wuh particular na'shikh heh recommendation t' wuh maut thol t'sai ik i ma wuh dor t' calling patroness. Dah'wak has she condescended tor mazhiv-kur-tor me ish-veh opinion (unasked nuh'!) fi' nash subject; heh ish-veh vesh' tonk'peh wuh maut gad mu-yor fa' i losrak hunsford, --svi' etwel patra na' quadrille, du' mrs. Jenkinson vesh' arranging din-tor de bourgh’s footstool, --ik she leralmin-tor, ‘mr. Collins, du bolau marry. Wuh clergyman spo' du bolau marry. Dvel-tor properly, dvel-tor wuh gentlewoman na' _my_ sake, heh na' ish-veh _own_; kal-tor ish-veh nam-tor wuh torupik, useful wihfelau t' person, ri katau abru pid, tonk'peh kup tor tor wuh pi' income hal-tor wuh rom yut. Nash nam-tor t'nash-veh na'shikh. Talal such wuh kosu u' ak u' du mokuhlek, katau ish-veh tor hunsford, heh i dungi yaret ish-veh.’ kal-tor me, k' wuh yut, tor glantau, t'nash-veh rom krei, ik i ri tor reckon wuh beglanau heh kindness t' t'sai catherine de bourgh u' among wuh least t' wuh advantages svi' t'nash-veh tepul tor nufai. Du dungi talal ish-veh manners mesakh sovek-vel i mokuhlek kethelvau; heh ish-veh wit heh vivacity, i nah-tor, bolau nam-tor acceptable tor ish-veh, wa' lu tempered k' wuh silence heh respect if ish-veh lan dungi inevitably teporilau. Thus mau na' t'nash-veh paik intention svi' favour t' matrimony; ish-veh hafau tor nam-tor var-tor po t'nash-veh zan-tor vesh' khartau tor longbourn instead t' t'nash-veh sha' neighbourhood, wilat i assure du tra' nam-tor wehk amiable nu'ri kosu. Tonk'peh wuh kla-min nam-tor, ik hasu, u' i am, tor inherit nash estate po' wuh tevakh t' ish-veh pudor-tor sa-mekh (vi, however, lau ha-tor wehk tevun longer), i kupi ri satisfy myself rik' resolving tor dvel-tor wuh ko-telsu s' among ish-veh daughters, ik wuh pak tor au lau nam-tor u' pi' u' tor-yehat lu wuh melancholy pavek nem-tor shi--if, however, u' i ma already leralmin-tor, lau ri nam-tor na' several tevun. Nash has vesh' t'nash-veh dvubolek, t'nash-veh rom krei, heh i snuhkrol-tor myself ish-veh dungi ri ne'hal-tor me svi' ish-veh vam. Heh i' nothing hafau na' me tonk'peh tor assure du svi' wuh danik animated gen-lis t' wuh khrash t' t'nash-veh affection. Tor fortune i am perfectly indifferent, heh dungau tor rai haishaya t' ik malat fi' ish-veh sa-mekh, opi' i am muhl aware ik ish-veh kupi ri nam-tor complied k'; heh ik leh-teh plesh-tor svi' wuh 4 fundauik cents, if dungi ri nam-tor ish-veh till po' ish-veh ko-mekh’s decease, nam-tor ek' ik du lau ek'wak nam-tor entitled tor. Fi' ik patam, therefore, i dungau nam-tor uniformly ralash-fam: heh du lau assure yourself ik rai ungenerous reproach dungau ek'wak be' dvun t'nash-veh bru-lar lu etek nam-tor telik.” ish-veh vesh' absolutely bolayatik tor svi-shau ish-veh i'. “du nam-tor nuh' hasty, osu, ” she maf-tor. “du yen-tor ik i ma tor rai kilko-srashiv. Kal-tor me tor ish-veh rik' further pak t' wak. Nar-tor t'nash-veh itaren na' wuh compliment du nam-tor paying me. I am maut sensible t' wuh dor t' ish-veh mnah, tonk'peh ish-veh nam-tor impossible na' me tor tor vathru do decline au.” “i am ri i' tor oren-tor, ” kilko-tor mr. Collins, k' wuh hotorik pral t' wuh el'ru, “ik ish-veh nam-tor tsuri k' nu'ri t'sai tor reject wuh shi'yavekh t' wuh sasu ik au secretly tvai tor nar-tor, lu au wuh'rak applies na' ish-veh favour; heh ik sometimes wuh refusal nam-tor ashiv-tor wuh dahr il kauk wuh wuh wak. I am, therefore, k' rai tvai discouraged k' ra du ma aishan leralmin-tor, heh dungau rok tor ras-tukh du tor wuh altar ere wu.” “fi-tor t'nash-veh zhit, osu, ” maf-tor elizabeth, “ish-veh rok nam-tor rather wuh wehtsuri veh po' t'nash-veh afsakaya. I tor assure du ik i am ri veh t' eifa nu'ri t'sai (kuv such nu'ri t'sai tra' nam-tor) vi nam-tor ni daring u' tor risk ish-veh happiness fi' wuh pavesh t' hasu ya'akash wuh dahr wak. I am perfectly serious svi' t'nash-veh refusal. Du kupi ri tor _me_ kunli, heh i am convinced ik i am wuh kim-shah kosu svi' wuh panu vi would tor _you_ ni. Nay, vesh' ish-veh t'hy'la t'sai catherine tor fai-tor me, i am persuaded she would talal me svi' kanok respect has-bosh qualified na' wuh situation.” “vesh' ish-veh ac'ruth ik t'sai catherine would nah-tor ni, ” leralmin-tor mr. Collins, maut gravely--“tonk'peh i fam yehat glenonau ik ish-veh ladyship would na' ek' disapprove t' du. Heh du lau nam-tor ac'ruth ik lu i ma wuh dor t' seeing ish-veh va'ashiv i dungau stariben svi' wuh k'lek zhil t' ish-veh modesty, iskan, heh vath amiable qualifications.” “indeed, mr. Collins, ek' krol t' me dungi nam-tor unnecessary. Du bolau mazhiv-kur-tor me trasha tor judge na' myself, heh vlitau me wuh compliment t' believing ra i leralmin. I istaya du maut kunli heh maut don-ka, heh k' refusing ish-veh el'ru, tor ek' svi' t'nash-veh tepul tor prevent ish-veh hasu vathru. Svi' tor me wuh nufai, du bolau ma satisfied wuh delicacy t' ish-veh feelings k' fudau tor t'nash-veh skan, heh lau nem-tor mat t' longbourn estate whenever ish-veh tevan-tor, rik' sovek shal-reproach. Nash tukh lau nam-tor panah-tor, therefore, u' t'forti settled.” heh rising u' she thus stariben, she would ma quitted wuh tvi-shal, had ri mr. Collins thus addressed ish-veh, -- “lu i tor myself wuh dor t' speaking tor du thurai fi' wuh subject, i dungau rok tor poprah wuh weht favourable kilko-srashiv do du ma i' putan-tor me; hi i am irak s' accusing du t' cruelty na' la', fai'ei i fai-tor ish-veh tor nam-tor wuh afer-tor custom t' ish-veh guv tor reject wuh sasu fi' wuh wuh'rak application, heh, sos'eh, du ma kauk i' leralmin-tor u' mau tor kastorau t'nash-veh saikhut u' would nam-tor tsurkanik k' wuh yeht delicacy t' wuh kotik character.” “really, mr. Collins, ” maf-tor elizabeth, k' ein warmth, “du puzzle me exceedingly. Kuv ra i ma hitherto leralmin-tor mokuhlek saudau tor du svi' wuh shid t' kastoraya, i fai-tor ri uf tor sagluvau t'nash-veh refusal svi' such wuh yut u' lau convince du t' its hasu veh.” “du bolau mazhiv-kur-tor me trasha tor snuhkrol-tor myself, t'nash-veh tal-kam krei, ik ish-veh refusal t' t'nash-veh shi'yavekh nam-tor goh zhit veling. T'nash-veh utvau na' believing ish-veh nam-tor briefly aifa: --ish-veh tor ri saudau tor me ik t'nash-veh el'ru nam-tor unworthy ish-veh acceptance, il ik wuh establishment i mokuhlek nufai would nam-tor sovek vath do highly desirable. T'nash-veh situation svi' ha'kiv, t'nash-veh tersaya k' wuh skan t' de bourgh, heh t'nash-veh relationship tor ish-veh sha', nam-tor circumstances highly svi' t'nash-veh favour; heh du dang nem-tor ish-veh vi' further consideration ik, svi' spite t' ish-veh wehk-vel attractions, ish-veh nam-tor k' rai tvai ac'ruth ik wuh'ashiv nufai t' kal'i'farr lau ek'wak nam-tor tor du. Ish-veh portion nam-tor unhappily ni pi', ik ish-veh dungi svi' ek' likelihood undo wuh daya t' ish-veh loveliness heh amiable qualifications. U' i bolau, therefore, conclude ik du nam-tor ri serious svi' ish-veh rejection t' me, i dungau dvel-tor tor attribute ish-veh tor ish-veh istaya t' increasing t'nash-veh ashaya k' suspense, fupa s' wuh tsuri practice t' sohkik kosu.” “i tor assure du, osu, ik i ma rai pretensions whatever tor ik ves t' sohk'es if consists svi' tormenting wuh respectable sasu. I would rather nam-tor vlitau wuh compliment t' hasu pudva-tor sincere. I nemaiyo va'ashiv heh va'ashiv na' wuh dor du ma ovsoh me svi' ish-veh mnah, tonk'peh tor nar-tor au nam-tor absolutely impossible. T'nash-veh feelings svi' kanok respect zadau ish-veh. Mokuhlek i stariben plainer? Ri tor panah-tor me i' u' wuh sohkik kotik intending tor plague du, tonk'peh u' wuh rational creature speaking wuh yeht'es s' ish-veh khaf-spol.” “du nam-tor uniformly sem-rik-tor!” maf-tor au, k' wuh sov t' awkward gallantry; “heh i am persuaded ik, lu sanctioned k' wuh sagluvau ek'te'kru t' fi' ish-veh marom mekhlar, t'nash-veh mnah dungi ri vravshau t' hasu acceptable.” tor such perseverance svi' wilful shal-tehsat elizabeth would tor rai kilko, heh iyi heh svi' silence withdrew; satalau, ik kuv au persisted svi' panahik ish-veh ashiv-tor refusals u' flattering kastoraya, tor apply tor ish-veh sa-mekh, t'vi negative lau nam-tor uttered svi' such wuh manner u' bolau nam-tor decisive, heh t'vi kloshai k'puu kupi ri nam-tor mistaken na' wuh affectation heh coquetry t' wuh sohkik kotik. [illustration] chapter xx. [illustration] mr. Collins vesh' ri losrak wu tor wuh ralash-fam contemplation t' ish-veh successful ashaya; na' mrs. Bennet, having dawdled pa' svi' wuh vestibule tor glantau na' wuh shaht t' wuh conference, rai sooner gla-tor elizabeth tu'ash wuh svep heh k' sahris ash be' dvun ish-veh na' wuh staircase, do she svi-tor wuh asal-yem-tvi-shal, heh congratulated fi' ish-veh heh herself svi' lamekh zhil fi' wuh kunli prospect t' ish-veh nearer tersaya. Mr. Collins poprah heh fun-tor aifa felicitations k' kaik sanosh, heh yi proceeded tor relate wuh particulars t' ish-veh interview, k' wuh result t' if au trusted au had kanok utvau tor nam-tor satisfied, opi' wuh refusal if ish-veh krei had steadfastly putan-tor ish-veh would naturally yumaya s' ish-veh fusik modesty heh wuh genuine delicacy t' ish-veh character. Nash ro'fori, however, startled mrs. Bennet: she would ma vesh' glad tor nam-tor kaing satisfied ik ish-veh ko-fu had tvai tor kastorau ish-veh k' protesting tehnat ish-veh mnah, tonk'peh she dared ri dva-tor ish-veh, heh kupi ri gol'nev taran ni. “tonk'peh nerau fi-tor ish-veh, mr. Collins, ” she hau, “ik lizzy dungau nam-tor katau tor utvau. I dungi stariben tor ish-veh pa' ish-veh myself directly. She nam-tor wuh maut headstrong, duhik ko-kan, heh tor ri fai-tor ish-veh sha' eku'ko; tonk'peh i dungi _make_ ish-veh fai-tor ish-veh.” “pardon me na' interrupting du, madam, ” maf-tor mr. Collins; “tonk'peh kuv she nam-tor really headstrong heh duhik, i fai-tor ri whether she would altogether nam-tor wuh maut desirable ko-telsu tor wuh sasu svi' t'nash-veh situation, vi naturally glazhau na' happiness svi' wuh kal'i'farr fupa s'. Kuv, therefore, she actually persists svi' rejecting t'nash-veh saikhut, sos'eh ish-veh vesh' weh-rom ri tor nekwitaya ish-veh vi' accepting me, fai'ei, kuv liable tor such lafot t' temper, she kupi ri contribute mau tor t'nash-veh felicity.” “osu, du ved misunderstand me, ” leralmin-tor mrs. Bennet, alarmed. “lizzy nam-tor goh headstrong svi' such tukh u' aifa. Svi' kanok-vei else she nam-tor u' rom-natured wuh ko-kan u' ek'wak ha-tor. I dungi hal-tor directly tor mr. Bennet, heh etek dungau maut ak settle ish-veh k' ish-veh, i am sure.” she would ri mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh wak tor kilko, tonk'peh hurrying instantly tor ish-veh sa-telsu, puvutau si', u' she svi-tor wuh shi'dunap, -- “oh, mr. Bennet, du nam-tor aitlu iyi; etek nam-tor ek' svi' wuh uproar. Du bolau sarlah heh tor lizzy marry mr. Collins, na' she vows she dungi ri ma ish-veh; heh kuv du ri tor tor haste au dungi rubah ish-veh kashek heh ri ma _her_.” mr. Bennet ashenau ish-veh bezhun s' ish-veh dunap u' she svi-tor, heh teslau au fi' ish-veh limuk k' wuh hayal unconcern, if vesh' ri svi' wuh least rubitau k' ish-veh sviribaya. “i ma ri wuh sanosh t' understanding du, ” leralmin-tor au, lu she had shahtau ish-veh starun. “t' ra nam-tor du talking?” “t' mr. Collins heh lizzy. Lizzy afsakau she dungi ri ma mr. Collins, heh mr. Collins palikau tor leralmin ik au dungi ri ma lizzy.” “heh ra am i tor tor fi' wuh occasion? Ish-veh seems wuh hopeless business.” “stariben tor lizzy pa' ish-veh yourself. Var-tor ish-veh ik du insist fi-tor ish-veh marrying ish-veh.” “kal-tor ish-veh nam-tor puvutau ne'. She dungau zhu-tor t'nash-veh opinion.” mrs. Bennet rang wuh kus-vakh, heh din-tor elizabeth vesh' summoned tor wuh shi'dunap. “sarlah la', kan, ” maf-tor ish-veh sa-mekh u' she saudau. “i ma satau na' du fi' wuh tek'ik t' importance. I ken-tor ik mr. Collins has tor du wuh nufai t' kal'i'farr. Nam-tor ish-veh yeht?” elizabeth kilko-tor ik ish-veh vesh'. “maut muhl--heh nash nufai t' kal'i'farr du ma klee'fah?” “i ma, osu.” “maut muhl. Etek i' sarlah tor wuh sfek. Ish-veh ko-mekh insists fi-tor ish-veh accepting ish-veh. Nam-tor ish-veh ri ni, mrs. Bennet?” “ha, il i dungi worla gla-tor ish-veh va'ashiv.” “wuh unhappy alternative nam-tor fa' du, elizabeth. S' nash gad du bolau nam-tor wuh ri-fainusu tor veh t' ish-veh mekhlar. Ish-veh ko-mekh dungi worla gla-tor du va'ashiv kuv du tor _not_ marry mr. Collins, heh i dungi worla gla-tor du va'ashiv kuv du _do_.” elizabeth kupi ri tonk'peh abru'teruklar-ru'lut na' such wuh conclusion t' such wuh palikaya; tonk'peh mrs. Bennet, vi had persuaded herself ik ish-veh sa-telsu fudau wuh tek'ik u' she istau, vesh' excessively disappointed. “ra tor du tvai, mr. Bennet, k' talking svi' nash yut? Du ugau me tor _insist_ fi-tor ish-veh marrying ish-veh.” “t'nash-veh tal-kam, ” kilko-tor ish-veh sa-telsu, “i ma dahkuh pi' favours tor ya'akash. Wuh'rak, ik du dungi kal-tor me wuh elik nam-tor-tor t' t'nash-veh understanding fi' wuh la' occasion; heh, secondly, t' t'nash-veh tvi-shal. I dungau nam-tor glad ki' wuh shi'dunap tor myself u' ak u' lau nam-tor.” ri wi, however, svi' spite t' ish-veh disappointment svi' ish-veh sa-telsu, did mrs. Bennet mazhiv-kur-tor abru wuh sfek. She variben tor elizabeth va'ashiv heh va'ashiv; coaxed heh threatened ish-veh k' da-tor. She endeavoured tor shar jane svi' ish-veh eku'ko, tonk'peh jane, k' ek' tor-yehat mildness, declined interfering; heh elizabeth, sometimes k' yeht earnestness, heh sometimes k' playful gaiety, kilko-tor tor ish-veh nashiv-tor. Hi ish-veh manner vuhnau, however, ish-veh determination worla did. Mr. Collins, meanwhile, vesh' kohlan svi' awek'es fi' ra had be' dvun-tor. Au nahp nuh' muhl t' himself tor comprehend fi' ra dvubolek ish-veh krei kupi klee'fah ish-veh; heh hi ish-veh pride vesh' dash-tor, au dashau svi' rai vath yut. Ish-veh fudau na' ish-veh vesh' ved glenonik; heh wuh possibility t' ish-veh nazh-tor ish-veh ko-mekh’s reproach prevented ish-veh olaya sovek regret. Du' wuh skan vesh' svi' nash confusion, charlotte lucas sarlah tor spend wuh gad k' au. She vesh' ragel-tor svi' wuh vestibule k' lydia, vi, hashan tor ish-veh, maf-tor svi' wuh ulef zhal, “i am glad du nam-tor sarlah, na' tra' nam-tor such mihrsh la'! Ra tor du nah-tor has pavesh-tor nash asal? Mr. Collins has tor wuh nufai tor lizzy, heh she dungi ri ma ish-veh.” [illustration: “au svi-tor wuh asal-yem tvi-shal” ] charlotte had hardly wak tor kilko-srashiv fa' au vesh' hau k' kitty, vi sarlah tor var-tor wuh ka ro'fori; heh rai sooner had au svi-tor wuh asal-yem-tvi-shal, wilat mrs. Bennet vesh' sa'awek, do she likewise began fi' wuh subject, calling fi' din-tor lucas na' ish-veh utan'es, heh entreating ish-veh tor persuade ish-veh t'hy'la lizzy tor comply k' wuh istau t' ish-veh skan. “pray tor, t'nash-veh tal-kam din-tor lucas, ” she hau, svi' wuh melancholy molu; “na' kling nam-tor fi' t'nash-veh vla, kling nem-tor krus k' me; i am cruelly nam-tor-tor, kling olau na' t'nash-veh ri donku-tor tor'tsu.” charlotte’s kilko vesh' spared k' wuh entrance t' jane heh elizabeth. “ay, tra' sarlah ish-veh, ” fator mrs. Bennet, “looking u' unconcerned u' lau nam-tor, heh caring rai weht na' etek do kuv etek vesh' na' york, tanilau she mokuhlek ma ish-veh sha' yut. Tonk'peh i var-tor du ra, din-tor lizzy, kuv du nem-tor ish-veh vi' ish-veh patam tor hal-tor fi' refusing kanok nufai t' kal'i'farr svi' nash yut, du dungi worla prah wuh sa-telsu na' ek'--heh i am sure i ri tor fai-tor vi nam-tor tor rompotau du lu ish-veh sa-mekh nam-tor tevik. _i_ dungau ri nam-tor kup tor potau du--heh ni i vikau du. I ma ovsoh k' du s' nash maut gad. I var-tor du svi' wuh shi'dunap, du fai-tor, ik i dang worla stariben tor du va'ashiv, heh du dungi talal me u' rom u' t'nash-veh zhit. I ma rai sanosh svi' talking tor undutiful kanu. Ri ik i ma mau sanosh, indeed, svi' talking tor anybody. Sutra vi dash u' i tor s' nervous complaints mokuhlek ma rai lo'uk inclination na' talking. Kling mokuhlek var-tor ra i dash! Tonk'peh ish-veh nam-tor kwon-hau-ov ni. Eifa vi ri tor complain nam-tor worla pitied.” ish-veh daughters shroi svi' silence tor nash effusion, sensible ik sovek attempt tor utvau k' il soothe ish-veh would goh increase wuh irritation. She variben fi', therefore, rik' svi-shaya s' sovek t' au till au vesh' hau k' mr. Collins, vi svi-tor k' wuh sov weht stately do tsuri, heh fi' perceiving ik, she leralmin-tor tor wuh ko-kan, -- “i', i tor insist fi-tor ish-veh, ik du, ek' t' du, meskaraya ish-veh lahv, heh kal-tor mr. Collins heh me ma wuh pi' conversation teretuhr.” elizabeth be' dvun-tor quietly s' wuh tvi-shal, jane heh kitty zahal-tor, tonk'peh lydia lam-tor ish-veh solektra, satalau tor zhu-tor ek' she kupi; heh charlotte, detained wuh'rak k' wuh civility t' mr. Collins, t'vi inquiries po' herself heh ek' ish-veh skan vesh' maut minute, heh yi k' wuh pi' curiosity, satisfied herself k' walking tor wuh krani heh pretending ri tor zhu-tor. Svi' wuh doleful spes mrs. Bennet thus began wuh salehm-tor conversation: -- “oh, mr. Collins!” “t'nash-veh tal-kam madam, ” kilko-tor au, “kal-tor etek nam-tor na' ek'wak ralash-fam fi' nash sfek. Irak nam-tor ish-veh s' me, ” au presently fator, svi' wuh spes ik pu'ulidau ish-veh displeasure, “tor resent wuh kloshai t' ish-veh ko-fu. Resignation tor inevitable ek'rasah nam-tor wuh gu-vam t' etek ek': wuh peculiar gu-vam t' wuh nu'ri sasu vi has vesh' ni fortunate u' i ma vesh', svi' lehkuh-mal preferment; heh, i sahrafel, i am resigned. Sos'eh ri wuh lehkuh ni s' olaya wuh vet t' t'nash-veh a'rak happiness had t'nash-veh rom krei pudor-tor me k' ish-veh el'ru; na' i ma k'ashiv glantau, ik resignation nam-tor worla ni buhfik u' lu wuh kudaya wafu palikau tor pak-tor somewhat t' its tala svi' etwel estimation. Du dungi ri, i rok, panah-tor me u' showing sovek disrespect tor ish-veh skan, t'nash-veh tal-kam madam, k' thus withdrawing t'nash-veh pretensions tor ish-veh ko-fu’s favour, rik' having vlitau yourself heh mr. Bennet wuh compliment t' requesting du tor interpose ish-veh ek'te'kru svi' t'nash-veh behalf. T'nash-veh spa-tor lau, i pthak, nam-tor objectionable svi' having nar-tor t'nash-veh dismission s' ish-veh ko-fu’s bru-lar instead t' ish-veh sha'; tonk'peh etek nam-tor ek' liable tor lafosh. I ma certainly tvai muhl k'fai wuh bosh tek'ik. T'nash-veh vel has vesh' tor shar wuh amiable besu na' myself, k' due consideration na' wuh advantage t' ek' ish-veh skan; heh kuv t'nash-veh _manner_ has vesh' na' ek' reprehensible, i la' eit'jae trasha tor apologize.” [illustration] chapter xxi. [illustration] wuh discussion t' mr. Collins’s nufai vesh' i' nearly na' wuh shaht, heh elizabeth had goh tor dash s' wuh uncomfortable feelings necessarily attending ish-veh, heh occasionally s' ein peevish allusion t' ish-veh ko-mekh. U' na' wuh gentleman himself, _his_ feelings vesh' chiefly sagluvau, ri k' embarrassment il dejection, il k' trying tor nan'woi ish-veh, tonk'peh k' stiffness t' manner heh resentful silence. Au scarcely ek'wak stariben tor ish-veh; heh wuh assiduous attentions if au had vesh' ni sensible t' himself vesh' transferred na' wuh shom t' wuh gad tor din-tor lucas, t'vi civility svi' listening tor ish-veh vesh' wuh seasonable vas tor au ek', heh wa' tor ish-veh t'hy'la. Wuh morrow torvau rai abatement t' mrs. Bennet’s has-bosh humour il has-bosh muhl'es. Mr. Collins vesh' isha svi' wuh ka fupa s' t' reshnek pride. Elizabeth had rok-tor ik ish-veh resentment lau pen-tor ish-veh yaret, tonk'peh ish-veh dotor did ri saudau svi' wuh least dau k' ish-veh. Au vesh' kwon-hau-ov ki' hal-tor fi' gad, heh tor gad au fam dvun tvai tor stay. Po' asal-yem, wuh ko-kan lates-tor tor meryton, tor inquire kuv mr. Wickham vesh' fun-tor, heh tor lament abru' ish-veh absence s' wuh netherfield rin'k'n. Au hau au fi' ish-veh entering wuh kahr, heh attended au tor ish-veh ezyet’s, wilat ish-veh regret heh vexation heh wuh concern t' kanok-veh vesh' muhl variben abru'. Tor elizabeth, however, au voluntarily nafai ik wuh bolayek t' ish-veh absence _had_ vesh' shal-imposed. “i afer-tor, ” leralmin-tor au, “u' wuh wak drew be', ik i had weh-rom ri ragel-tor mr. Darcy; --ik tor nam-tor svi' wuh ka tvi-shal, wuh ka party k' ish-veh na' ni wehk wadan teretuhr, lau nam-tor weht do i kupi lesh, heh ik scenes lau arise unpleasant tor weht do myself.” she highly messau ish-veh forbearance; heh au had el-wak na' wuh bosh discussion t' ish-veh, heh na' ek' wuh commendations if au civilly bestowed fi' tik vath, u' wickham heh wuh'ashiv officer lates-tor pla' k' au tor longbourn, heh du' wuh lates au wa' attended tor ish-veh. Ish-veh accompanying au vesh' wuh dahtau advantage: she olau ek' wuh compliment ish-veh nufau tor herself; heh ish-veh vesh' danik acceptable u' wuh occasion t' introducing ish-veh tor ish-veh sa-mekh heh ko-mekh. [illustration: “lates-tor pla' k' au” [_copyright 1894 k' george allen._]] ak po' ish-veh fun, wuh nuhm vesh' tefu tor din-tor bennet; sarlah ish-veh s' netherfield, heh vesh' tu'ash iyi. Wuh envelope tuhlau wuh thalv t' sohkik, pi', fal-hish-tor dun, muhl wein-tor k' wuh t'sai’s rom, flowing el'ru; heh elizabeth gla-tor ish-veh ko-kai’s countenance rubah u' she telv-tor ish-veh, heh gla-tor ish-veh kelek intently fi' ein particular tvur. Jane recollected herself ak; heh putting wuh nuhm maf, ar'kada tor hau, k' ish-veh tsuri cheerfulness, svi' wuh paik conversation: tonk'peh elizabeth olau wuh anxiety fi' wuh subject if drew ska' ish-veh attention kauk s' wickham; heh rai sooner had au heh ish-veh besu taken trasha, do wuh glance s' jane invited ish-veh tor zahal-tor ish-veh upstairs. Lu au had nazh-tor ish-veh sha' tvi-shal, jane, taking si' ish-veh nuhm, leralmin-tor, “nash nam-tor s' caroline bingley: ra ish-veh tuhlau has ak'wikmun me wuh rom deal. Wuh bosh party ma losrak netherfield k' nash wak, heh nam-tor fi' ish-veh yut tor kahr; heh rik' sovek intention t' coming pla' va'ashiv. Du dungau zhu-tor ra she leralmin-tor.” she yi telv-tor wuh wuh'rak zhit-bal aloud, if comprised wuh ro'fori t' ish-veh having aishan resolved tor zahal-tor ish-veh sa-kai tor kahr directly, heh t' ish-veh meaning tor aru-yokul ik gad svi' grosvenor yut, wilat mr. Hurst had wuh kelek. Wuh thurai vesh' svi' aifa zhit: --“‘i ri tor pretend tor regret sovek-vel i dungau trasha svi' hertfordshire kaula ish-veh shila'es, t'nash-veh dearest t'hy'la; tonk'peh etek dungi rok, na' ein fa-wak wak-krus, tor tizh-tor wehk fun-tor t' ik delightful intercourse etek ma fainu, heh svi' wuh meanwhile lau lessen wuh kusut t' dahshaya k' wuh maut vakavik heh danik unreserved correspondence. I nerau fi' du na' ik.’” tor aifa pid-flown sagluvaya elizabeth shroi k' ek' wuh insensibility t' distrust; heh hi wuh suddenness t' ish-veh removal ak'wikmun ish-veh, she gla-tor nothing svi' ish-veh really tor lament: ish-veh vesh' ri tor nam-tor supposed ik ish-veh absence s' netherfield would prevent mr. Bingley’s hasu tra'; heh u' tor wuh pak t' ish-veh shila'es, she vesh' persuaded ik jane bolau ak cease tor fudau ish-veh svi' wuh tizh'es t' ish-veh. “ish-veh nam-tor unlucky, ” leralmin-tor she, po' wuh pen svizh, “ik du dang ri nam-tor kup tor gla-tor ish-veh t'hylara fa' au trasha wuh shasol. Tonk'peh lau etek ri rok ik wuh wak-krus t' fa-wak happiness, tor if din-tor bingley glazhau fa'rak, lau lasha earlier do she nam-tor aware, heh ik wuh delightful intercourse du ma fainu u' t'hylara dungi nam-tor uzhau k' wi greater satisfaction u' ko-kai? Mr. Bingley dungi ri nam-tor detained svi' london k' au.” “caroline decidedly leralmin-tor ik rim t' wuh party dungi fun vi' hertfordshire nash karil. I dungi telv-tor ish-veh tor du. “‘lu t'nash-veh sa-kai losrak etek za-gad, au glenonau ik wuh business if nem-tor ish-veh tor london lau nam-tor concluded svi' rehkuh il kehkuh gad; tonk'peh u' etek nam-tor ac'ruth ish-veh fam yehat nam-tor ni, heh na' wuh ka wak convinced ik lu charles prah tor kahr au dungi nam-tor svi' rai brax tor trasha ish-veh va'ashiv, etek ma satalau fi' zahalik ish-veh thither, ik au lau ri nam-tor obliged tor spend ish-veh vacant wadan svi' wuh comfortless hotel. Wehk t' t'nash-veh acquaintance nam-tor already tra' na' wuh karil: i istaya i kupi zhu-tor ik du, t'nash-veh dearest t'hy'la, had sovek intention t' tor veh svi' wuh patreitan, tonk'peh t' ik i despair. I sincerely rok ish-veh christmas svi' hertfordshire lau abound svi' wuh gaieties if ik tevun-yonuk paik katau, heh ik ish-veh beaux dungi nam-tor ni numerous u' tor prevent ish-veh olaya wuh pak t' wuh rehkuh t' ik etek dungau deprive du.’ “ish-veh nam-tor evident k' nash, ” hau jane, “ik sarlah ish-veh pla' rai weht nash karil.” “ish-veh nam-tor goh evident ik din-tor bingley tor ri tvai au _should_.” “po dungi du nah-tor ni? Ish-veh bolau nam-tor ish-veh sha' doing; au nam-tor ish-veh sha' trensu. Tonk'peh du ri tor fai-tor _all_. I _will_ telv-tor du wuh tvur if wa' dash-tor me. I dungi ma rai reserves s' _you_. ‘mr. Darcy nam-tor impatient tor gla-tor ish-veh ko-kai; heh tor confess wuh yeht'es, _we_ nam-tor scarcely lehkuh nayik tor ragel-tor ish-veh va'ashiv. I really ri tor nah-tor georgiana darcy has ish-veh kaik na' vaksur, sohk'es, heh accomplishments; heh wuh affection she vi'le-esh-tor svi' louisa heh myself nam-tor heightened vi' vel fam dvun weht eku'ki s' wuh rok etek dare tor entertain t' ish-veh hasu hereafter etwel ko-kai. I ri tor fai-tor whether i ek'wak fa' mentioned tor du t'nash-veh feelings fi' nash subject, tonk'peh i dungi ri trasha wuh shasol rik' confiding au, heh i sahrafel du dungi ri vam au unreasonable. T'nash-veh sa-kai krol-tor ish-veh greatly already; au dungi ma vakavik opportunity i' t' seeing ish-veh fi' wuh danik intimate footing; ish-veh relations ek' istaya wuh tersaya u' mau u' ish-veh sha'; heh wuh ko-kai’s partiality nam-tor ri misleading me, i nah-tor, lu i vutau charles danik capable t' engaging sovek kosu’s khaf-spol. K' ek' aifa circumstances tor favour wuh attachment, heh nothing tor prevent ish-veh, am i riyeht, t'nash-veh dearest jane, svi' indulging wuh rok t' wuh pavek if dungi shar wuh happiness t' ni wehk?’ ra nah-tor du t' _this_ zhit-bal, t'nash-veh tal-kam lizzy?” leralmin-tor jane, u' she shahtau ish-veh. “nam-tor ish-veh ri pa'shik hiyet? Tor ish-veh ri expressly afsakau ik caroline neither gish il istau me tor nam-tor ish-veh ko-kai; ik she nam-tor perfectly convinced t' ish-veh sa-kai’s indifference; heh ik kuv she suspects wuh malat t' t'nash-veh feelings na' ish-veh she tvai (danik kindly!) tor shitau me fi' t'nash-veh klashausu. Mokuhlek tra' nam-tor sovek vath opinion fi' wuh subject?” “ha, tra' mokuhlek; na' t'nash-veh nam-tor totally natya. Dungi du zhu-tor ish-veh?” “danik willingly.” “du dungau ma ish-veh svi' wuh zamu zhit. Din-tor bingley gla-tor ik ish-veh sa-kai nam-tor svi' ashaya k' du heh aitlu ish-veh tor marry din-tor darcy. She zahal-tor ish-veh tor kahr svi' wuh rok t' keeping ish-veh tra', heh ar'kada tor persuade du ik au tor ri tun pa' du.” jane hutau ish-veh patam. “indeed, jane, du ought tor dva-tor me. Kling vi has ek'wak gla-tor du teretuhr mokuhlek vet ish-veh affection; din-tor bingley, i am sure, fam yehat: she nam-tor ri such wuh simpleton. Kupi she ma gla-tor ulef u' mau ashaya svi' mr. Darcy na' herself, she would ma ordered ish-veh wedding sai-vel. Tonk'peh wuh nuf nam-tor nash: --etek nam-tor ri don-ka hiyet il grand hiyet na' au; heh she nam-tor wuh weht anxious tor prah din-tor darcy na' ish-veh sa-kai, s' wuh notion ik lu tra' has vesh' _one_ inter-kal'i'farr, she lau ma lehkuh trouble svi' achieving wuh dahr; svi' if tra' nam-tor certainly ein ingenuity, heh i dare leralmin ish-veh would navau kuv din-tor de bourgh vesh' s' wuh yut. Tonk'peh, t'nash-veh dearest jane, du fam yehat seriously glenonau ik, fai'ei din-tor bingley var-tor du ish-veh sa-kai greatly krol-tor din-tor darcy, au nam-tor svi' wuh smallest degree lehkuh sensible t' _your_ merit do lu au nem-tor trasha t' du fi' gad; il ik ish-veh dungi nam-tor svi' ish-veh tepul tor persuade ish-veh ik, instead t' hasu svi' ashaya k' du, au nam-tor maut mau svi' ashaya k' ish-veh t'hy'la.” “kuv etek nahp kahkwa t' din-tor bingley, ” kilko-tor jane, “ish-veh representation t' ek' nash lau tor me ved hagik. Tonk'peh i fai-tor wuh nen nam-tor unjust. Caroline nam-tor incapable t' wilfully deceiving sovek-veh; heh ek' ik i mokuhlek rok svi' nash nuf nam-tor, ik she nam-tor tehs-tor herself.” “ik nam-tor gas'rak. Du kupi ri ma palikau wuh weht kunli idea, opi' du dungi ri nem-tor comfort svi' t'nash-veh: dva-tor ish-veh tor nam-tor tehs-tor, k' ek' tvai. Du ma i' ovsoh ish-veh gu-vam k' ish-veh, heh bolau fret rai longer.” “tonk'peh, t'nash-veh tal-kam ko-kai, mokuhlek i nam-tor kunli, kauk supposing wuh buhfik, svi' accepting wuh sasu t'vi ko-kai heh t'hylara nam-tor ek' wishing ish-veh tor marry kitok-wilat?” “du bolau klopau na' yourself, ” leralmin-tor elizabeth; “heh kuv, fi-tor vinik deliberation, du talal ik wuh misery t' disobliging ish-veh dahkuh ko-kai nam-tor weht do ka-talupik tor wuh happiness t' hasu ish-veh ko-telsu, i na'shikhau du, k' ek' tvai, tor klee'fah ish-veh.” “uf mokuhlek du variben ni?” leralmin-tor jane, faintly smiling; “du bolau fai-tor, ik, hi i dang nam-tor exceedingly grieved na' ish-veh disapprobation, i kupi ri hesitate.” “i did ri nah-tor du would; heh ik hasu wuh nuf, i fam yehat panah-tor ish-veh situation k' mau utan'es.” “tonk'peh kuv au fun-tor rai weht nash karil, t'nash-veh dvel dungi worla nam-tor required. Wuh thousand vel lau arise svi' shehkuh tevun-krus.” wuh idea t' ish-veh returning rai weht elizabeth skasau k' wuh utmost contempt. Ish-veh saudau tor ish-veh goh wuh suggestion t' caroline’s interested istau; heh she kupi ri na' wuh moment suppose ik eifa istau, however openly il artfully spoken, kupi vi-yumuk wuh nu'ri sasu ni totally independent t' kanok-veh. She represented tor ish-veh ko-kai, u' forcibly u' tor-yehat, ra she olau fi' wuh subject, heh had ak wuh sanosh t' seeing its kunli daya. Jane’s temper vesh' ri desponding; heh she vesh' gradually pufulag-tor tor rok, hi wuh diffidence t' affection sometimes overcame wuh rok, ik bingley would fun tor netherfield, heh kilko-srashiv kanok istaya t' ish-veh khaf-spol. Au sep-wafikh ik mrs. Bennet dang goh zhu-tor t' wuh trashan t' wuh skan, rik' hasu alarmed fi' wuh nosahp t' wuh gentleman’s spa-tor; tonk'peh kauk nash ulik sviribaya mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh wuh lo'uk deal t' concern, heh she bewailed ish-veh u' exceedingly unlucky ik wuh t'sai dang pavesh-tor tor hal-tor maf aishan u' au vesh' ek' getting ni intimate teretuhr. Po' lamenting ish-veh, however, na' ein wu-vath, she had wuh consolation t' thinking ik mr. Bingley would nam-tor ak ne' va'ashiv, heh ak dining na' longbourn; heh wuh conclusion t' ek' vesh' wuh kel'o afsakaya, ik, hi au had vesh' invited goh tor wuh skan aru-yem, she would nem-tor tun ki' dahkuh bosh rivak. [illustration] chapter xxii. [illustration] wuh bennets vesh' engaged tor aru-yokul k' wuh lucases; heh va'ashiv, du' wuh chief t' wuh gad, vesh' din-tor lucas ni ves u' tor shroi tor mr. Collins. Elizabeth nem-tor wuh opportunity t' thanking ish-veh. “ish-veh potau ish-veh svi' rom humour, ” leralmin-tor she, “heh i am weht obliged tor du do i mokuhlek sagluvau.” charlotte assured ish-veh t'hy'la t' ish-veh satisfaction svi' hasu useful, heh ik ish-veh amply repaid ish-veh na' wuh pi' sacrifice t' ish-veh wak. Nash vesh' maut amiable; tonk'peh charlotte’s kindness sadvun-tor weh-irak do elizabeth had sovek conception t': --its vel vesh' nothing lehkuh tor tor shar ish-veh s' sovek fun t' mr. Collins’s shi'yavekh, k' engaging au na' herself. Such vesh' din-tor lucas’s scheme; heh appearances vesh' ni favourable, ik lu au parted na' mu-yor, she would ma olau siyah sure t' navun kuv au had ri vesh' tor trasha hertfordshire ni maut ak. Tonk'peh la' she did injustice tor wuh yon heh tikopah t' ish-veh character; na' ish-veh pufulag-tor ish-veh tor stron s' longbourn kelek wuh thurai asal k' admirable slyness, heh hasten tor lucas lodge tor lehm himself na' ish-veh ash'ya. Au vesh' anxious tor nan'woi wuh beglanau t' ish-veh krei, s' wuh conviction ik, kuv gla-tor au ish-veh trashu, au kupi ri vravshau tor conjecture ish-veh design, heh au vesh' ri willing ki' wuh attempt fainu till its navun kupi nam-tor fainu likewise; na', hi olaya siyah shar, heh k' utvau, na' charlotte had vesh' tolerably encouraging, au vesh' comparatively diffident opi' wuh adventure t' gad. Ish-veh reception, however, vesh' t' wuh danik flattering ves. Din-tor lucas pakashogau ish-veh s' wuh upper krani u' au lates-tor na' wuh kelek, heh instantly eku si' tor ragel-tor ish-veh accidentally svi' wuh lane. Tonk'peh pi' had she dared tor rok ik ni mau ashaya heh eloquence awaited ish-veh tra'. Svi' u' pen wuh wak u' mr. Collins’s wu starun would kal-tor, kanok-vei vesh' settled svi' au tor wuh satisfaction t' fi'; heh u' au svi-tor wuh kelek, au earnestly entreated ish-veh tor ahm wuh gad ik vesh' tor tor ish-veh wuh happiest t' sasu; heh hi such wuh solicitation bolau nam-tor waived na' wuh la', wuh t'sai olau rai inclination tor trifle k' ish-veh happiness. Wuh stupidity k' if au vesh' favoured k' malat bolau klashausu ish-veh courtship s' sovek sem-rik ik kupi tor wuh kosu istaya na' its continuance; heh din-tor lucas, vi nar-tor ish-veh solely s' wuh pure heh disinterested aitlun t' wuh establishment, tun-tor ri uf ak ik establishment vesh' nazh-tor. Osu william heh t'sai lucas vesh' speedily applied tor na' ish-veh consent; heh ish-veh vesh' bestowed k' wuh danik joyful alacrity. Mr. Collins’s la' circumstances tor ish-veh wuh danik eligible match na' ish-veh ko-fu, tor ik au kupi mazhiv-kur-tor pi' fortune; heh ish-veh prospects t' fa-wak don-tak vesh' exceedingly rom. T'sai lucas began directly tor ka'pra, k' weht eku'ko do wuh tukh had ek'wak [illustration: “ni mau ashaya heh eloquence” [_copyright 1894 k' george allen._]] teporilau fa', uf wehk tevun longer mr. Bennet vesh' kesik tor ha-tor; heh osu william mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh u' ish-veh klopau opinion, ik whenever mr. Collins dang nam-tor svi' mat t' wuh longbourn estate, ish-veh would nam-tor highly expedient ik fi' au heh ish-veh ko-telsu dang tor ish-veh appearance na' st. James’s. Wuh bosh skan svi' pen vesh' properly overjoyed fi' wuh occasion. Wuh younger ko-kan shidau rok-tor t' _coming out_ wuh tevun il dahkuh sooner do au lau vathru ma ovsoh; heh wuh sa-kan vesh' vas-tor s' ish-veh apprehension t' charlotte’s dying wuh hinek maid. Charlotte herself vesh' tolerably tertitau. She had nazh-tor ish-veh sfek, heh had wak tor panah-tor t' ish-veh. Ish-veh haulan vesh' svi' paik satisfactory. Mr. Collins, tor nam-tor sure, vesh' neither sensible il agreeable: ish-veh shila'es vesh' irksome, heh ish-veh attachment tor ish-veh bolau nam-tor glenonik. Tonk'peh fam dvun au would nam-tor ish-veh sa-telsu. Rik' thinking highly either t' sasu il t' matrimony, kal'i'farr had kwon-hau-ov vesh' ish-veh vel: ish-veh vesh' wuh goh dorli provision na' muhl-educated nu'ri kosu t' pi' fortune, heh, however uncertain t' giving happiness, bolau nam-tor ish-veh pleasantest preservative s' aitlun. Nash preservative she had i' prah; heh na' wuh ya'shakhuv t' dah-leh-stehkuh, rik' having ek'wak vesh' handsome, she olau ek' wuh rom kunli t' ish-veh. Wuh least agreeable circumstance svi' wuh business vesh' wuh ak'wikmun ish-veh bolau occasion tor elizabeth bennet, t'vi friendship she valued mesakh ik t' sovek vath person. Elizabeth would wonder, heh probably would tenai ish-veh; heh hi ish-veh resolution vesh' ri tor nam-tor shaken, ish-veh feelings bolau nam-tor dash-tor k' such wuh disapprobation. She resolved tor mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh wuh ro'fori herself; heh therefore vifalunau mr. Collins, lu au fun-tor tor longbourn tor aru-yem, tor eku rai hint t' ra had be' dvun-tor fa' sovek t' wuh skan.
