Wuh ugaya t' secrecy vesh' veling maut dutifully putan-tor, tonk'peh ish-veh kupi ri nam-tor potau rik' rihag'es; na' wuh curiosity teporilau k' ish-veh wu absence thorau forth svi' such maut kharik deshkau fi' ish-veh fun, u' required ein ingenuity tor savlau, heh au vesh' na' wuh ka wak exercising lo'uk shal-wafaya, na' au vesh' longing tor publish ish-veh prosperous ashaya. U' au vesh' tor palikau ish-veh halovaya nuh' lehkuh-mal fi' wuh morrow tor gla-tor sovek t' wuh skan, wuh hali-kal t' trasha-taking vesh' performed lu wuh t'sai dvun-tor na' wuh mu-yor; heh mrs. Bennet, k' lo'uk politeness heh cordiality, leralmin-tor uf kunli au dang nam-tor tor gla-tor ish-veh na' longbourn va'ashiv, whenever ish-veh vath engagements lau kal-tor ish-veh tor yaret au. “t'nash-veh tal-kam madam, ” au kilko-tor, “nash k'waw'zhe nam-tor wa' gratifying, fai'ei ish-veh nam-tor ra i ma vesh' hoping tor poprah; heh du lau nam-tor maut ac'ruth ik i dungau avail myself t' ish-veh u' ak u' tor-yehat.” au vesh' ek' astonished; heh mr. Bennet, vi kupi k' rai tvai istaya na' ni threshan wuh fun, iyi leralmin-tor, -- “tonk'peh nam-tor tra' ri tehvar t' t'sai catherine’s disapprobation la', t'nash-veh rom osu? Du had weh-rom neglect ish-veh relations do sahr-tor wuh risk t' offending ish-veh patroness.” “t'nash-veh tal-kam osu, ” kilko-tor mr. Collins, “i am wa' obliged tor du na' nash friendly yuzhat, heh du lau nerau fi-tor t'nash-veh ri taking ni tukh wuh ash rik' ish-veh ladyship’s concurrence.” “du fam yehat nam-tor nuh' mau fi' ish-veh klashausu. Risk sovek-vel rather do ish-veh displeasure; heh kuv du talal ish-veh kesik tor nam-tor ashenau k' ish-veh coming tor etek va'ashiv, if i dang nah-tor exceedingly yesik, stay quietly na' ha-kel, heh nam-tor satisfied ik _we_ dungau nem-tor rai offence.” “dva-tor me, t'nash-veh tal-kam osu, t'nash-veh gratitude nam-tor warmly teporilau k' such affectionate attention; heh, nerau fi-tor ish-veh, du dungi speedily poprah s' me wuh nuhm t' itaren na' nash u' muhl u' na' kanok vath ulidar t' ish-veh fudau du' t'nash-veh stay svi' hertfordshire. U' na' t'nash-veh rom krei, hi t'nash-veh absence lau ri nam-tor wu hiyet tor render ish-veh bolayatik, i dungau i' nem-tor wuh liberty t' wishing au muhl'es heh happiness, ri kaulaik t'nash-veh krei elizabeth.” k' proper civilities, wuh t'sai yi withdrew; ek' t' au kaing ak'wikmun tor talal ik au meditated wuh sahris fun. Mrs. Bennet istau tor ken-tor k' ish-veh ik au nahp t' paying ish-veh shi'yavekh tor veh t' ish-veh younger ko-kan, heh mary lau ma vesh' fakovau fi' tor nar-tor ish-veh. She tav-tor ish-veh kup'es mau higher do sovek t' wuh vath: tra' vesh' wuh solidity svi' ish-veh haulan if k'ashiv kwul-tor ish-veh; heh hi k' rai tvai ni clever u' herself, she nahp ik, kuv kastorau tor telv-tor heh improve himself k' such wuh li-fal u' ish-veh, au lau shetau wuh maut agreeable besu. Tonk'peh fi' wuh zahalik asal kanok rok t' nash ves vesh' ovsoh maf. Din-tor lucas puvutau ak po' asal-yem, heh svi' wuh awek conference k' elizabeth related wuh pavek t' wuh gad fa'. Wuh possibility t' mr. Collins’s fancying himself svi' ashaya k' ish-veh t'hy'la had wuh'wak paresh-tor tor elizabeth k'svi wuh kim-shah gad il dahkuh: tonk'peh ik charlotte kupi kastorau ish-veh seemed siyah u' irak s' possibility u' ik she kupi kastorau ish-veh herself; heh ish-veh astonishment vesh' consequently ni lo'uk u' tor overcome palikauk wuh bounds t' decorum, heh she kupi ri gol'nev maf-tor si', -- “engaged tor mr. Collins! T'nash-veh tal-kam charlotte, impossible!” wuh br'xan countenance if din-tor lucas had khartau svi' telling ish-veh var mazhiv-kur-tor yut tor wuh momentary confusion la' fi' receiving ni kharik wuh reproach; hi, u' ish-veh vesh' rai weht do she gishu, she ak tabakau ish-veh composure, heh calmly kilko-tor, -- “po dang du nam-tor ak'wikmun, t'nash-veh tal-kam eliza? Tor du nah-tor ish-veh incredible ik mr. Collins dang nam-tor kup tor procure sovek kosu’s rom opinion, fai'ei au vesh' ri ni kunli u' tor navau k' du?” tonk'peh elizabeth had i' recollected herself; heh, tor wuh karik urgam na' ish-veh, vesh' kup tor assure ish-veh, k' tolerable firmness, ik wuh prospect t' ish-veh relationship vesh' highly grateful tor ish-veh, heh ik she istau ish-veh ek' imaginable happiness. “gla-tor nash-veh ra du nam-tor olaya, ” kilko-tor charlotte; “du bolau nam-tor ak'wikmun, maut mau ak'wikmun, ni lately u' mr. Collins vesh' wishing tor marry du. Tonk'peh lu du ma had wak tor nah-tor ish-veh ek' abru', i rok du dungi nam-tor satisfied k' ra i ma ovsoh. I am ri romantic, du fai-tor. I worla vesh'. I ya'akash goh wuh kel'o ha-kel; heh, panahik mr. Collins’s character, tersaya, heh situation svi' ha'kiv, i am convinced ik t'nash-veh pavesh t' happiness k' ish-veh nam-tor u' rom u' danik sutra mokuhlek boast fi' entering wuh kal'i'farr fupa s'.” elizabeth quietly kilko-tor “undoubtedly; ” heh, po' wuh awkward svizh, au fun-tor tor wuh shom t' wuh skan. Charlotte did ri stay mau longer; heh elizabeth vesh' yi losrak tor haul-tor fi' ra she had puzhu-tor. Ish-veh vesh' wuh akarshif fa' she became na' ek' reconciled tor wuh idea t' ni unsuitable wuh match. Wuh strangeness t' mr. Collins’s tor dahkuh nufau t' kal'i'farr k'svi rehkuh gad vesh' nothing svi' comparison t' ish-veh hasu i' nar-tor. She had kwon-hau-ov olau ik charlotte’s opinion t' matrimony vesh' ri exactly spo' ish-veh sha'; tonk'peh she kupi ri ma supposed ish-veh tor-yehat ik, lu puvutau vi' torai, she would ma sacrificed kanok weh-rom olaya tor worldly advantage. Charlotte, wuh ko-telsu t' mr. Collins, vesh' wuh danik humiliating bikuv! Heh tor wuh pang t' wuh t'hy'la disgracing herself, heh ne'hal-tor svi' ish-veh vam, vesh' hau wuh distressing conviction ik ish-veh vesh' impossible na' ik t'hy'la tor nam-tor tolerably kunli svi' wuh lot she had pudvel-tor. [illustration: “protested au bolau nam-tor entirely mistaken.” [_copyright 1894 k' george allen._]] chapter xxiii. [illustration] elizabeth vesh' sitting k' ish-veh ko-mekh heh ko-kai, reflecting fi' ra she had puzhu-tor, heh doubting whether she vesh' authorized tor mention ish-veh, lu osu william lucas himself saudau, satau k' ish-veh ko-fu tor tor'pra ish-veh engagement tor wuh skan. K' wehk compliments tor au, heh mau shal-gratulation fi' wuh prospect t' wuh tersaya svi' wuh kelek, au unfolded wuh tukh, --tor wuh audience ri goh wondering, tonk'peh incredulous; na' mrs. Bennet, k' weht perseverance do politeness, protested au bolau nam-tor entirely mistaken; heh lydia, kwon-hau-ov unguarded heh k'ashiv uncivil, boisterously sporiben, -- “rom s'haile! Osu william, uf mokuhlek du var-tor such wuh var? Ri tor du fai-tor ik mr. Collins aitlu tor marry lizzy?” nothing lehkuh tor wuh complaisance t' wuh courtier kupi ma borne rik' reshan such skasaya: tonk'peh osu william’s rom-breeding lesh ish-veh k'fai ish-veh ek'; heh hi au eit'jae trasha tor nam-tor a'rak u' tor wuh yeht'es t' ish-veh ro'fori, au shroi tor ek' ish-veh impertinence k' wuh danik forbearing nuhk'es. Elizabeth, olaya ish-veh incumbent fi' ish-veh tor vas-tor ish-veh s' ni unpleasant wuh situation, i' shitau herself fa'rak tor wugau ish-veh khrosahp, k' mentioning ish-veh prior fai-tukh t' ish-veh s' charlotte herself; heh endeavoured tor shitau wuh pehkaya tor wuh sporun t' ish-veh ko-mekh heh ko-kai, k' wuh earnestness t' ish-veh congratulations tor osu william, svi' if she vesh' readily hau k' jane, heh k' tor wuh vuhna'es t' remarks fi' wuh happiness ik lau nam-tor gishu s' wuh match, wuh marom character t' mr. Collins, heh wuh convenient ir t' hunsford s' london. Mrs. Bennet vesh', svi' kla-min, nuh' mau overpowered tor leralmin wuh lo'uk deal du' osu william hafau; tonk'peh rai sooner had au losrak au do ish-veh feelings afer-tor wuh rapid krau. Svi' wuh wuh'rak shi, she persisted svi' disbelieving wuh bosh t' wuh tukh; secondly, she vesh' maut sure ik mr. Collins had vesh' taken svi'; thirdly, she trusted ik au would worla nam-tor kunli teretuhr; heh, fourthly, ik wuh match lau nam-tor pushau ska'. Dahkuh inferences, however, vesh' plainly deduced s' wuh bosh: veh, ik elizabeth vesh' wuh yeht aishan t' ek' wuh mischief; heh wuh vath, ik she herself had vesh' barbarously nam-tor-tor k' au ek'; heh fi' aifa dahkuh sfekau she principally dwelt du' wuh shom t' wuh gad. Nothing kupi console heh nothing appease ish-veh. Il did ik gad sai-vel-tor si' ish-veh resentment. Wuh wehk gad veshau fa' she kupi gla-tor elizabeth rik' scolding ish-veh: wuh tevun-krus be' dvun-tor maf fa' she kupi stariben tor osu william il t'sai lucas rik' hasu snertau; heh wehk tevun-krus vesh' hal-tor fa' she kupi na' ek' forgive ish-veh ko-fu. Mr. Bennet’s zherka vesh' mau weht tranquil fi' wuh occasion, heh such u' au did veshtaya au pronounced tor nam-tor t' wuh danik agreeable wihfelau; na' ish-veh gratified ish-veh, au leralmin-tor, tor discover ik charlotte lucas, ik au had vesh' nam-tor-tor tor nah-tor tolerably sensible, vesh' u' duhik u' ish-veh ko-telsu, heh weht duhik do ish-veh ko-fu! Jane confessed herself wuh pi' ak'wikmun na' wuh match: tonk'peh she leralmin-tor lehkuh t' ish-veh astonishment do t' ish-veh earnest aitlun na' ish-veh happiness; il kupi elizabeth persuade ish-veh tor panah-tor ish-veh u' improbable. Kitty heh lydia vesh' irak s' envying din-tor lucas, na' mr. Collins vesh' goh wuh clergyman; heh ish-veh dau au svi' rai vath yut do u' wuh krus t' ro'fori tor sak-tor na' meryton. T'sai lucas kupi ri nam-tor insensible t' triumph fi' hasu kup tor retort fi' mrs. Bennet wuh comfort t' having wuh ko-fu muhl telik; heh she puvutau na' longbourn rather oftener do tsuri tor leralmin uf kunli she vesh', hi mrs. Bennet’s sfith glazhau heh has-bosh-natured remarks lau ma vesh' hiyet tor yetur happiness maf. Svi' elizabeth heh charlotte tra' vesh' wuh restraint if potau au mutually ralash-fam fi' wuh subject; heh elizabeth olau persuaded ik rai yeht guhl'es kupi ek'wak subsist svi' au va'ashiv. Ish-veh disappointment svi' charlotte tor ish-veh da-tor k' fonder fudau tor ish-veh ko-kai, t' t'vi rectitude heh delicacy she vesh' sure ish-veh opinion kupi worla nam-tor shaken, heh na' t'vi happiness she grew kanok-gadik weht anxious, u' bingley had i' vesh' hal-tor wuh wehk gad, heh nothing vesh' puzhu-tor t' ish-veh fun. Jane had satau caroline wuh lehkuh-mal kilko-srashiv tor ish-veh nuhm, heh vesh' counting wuh gad till she lau reasonably rok tor zhu-tor va'ashiv. Wuh ugau nuhm t' itaren s' mr. Collins lasha fi' gad, addressed tor ish-veh sa-mekh, heh written k' ek' wuh solemnity t' gratitude if wuh leh-dah-tevun-krus’s abode svi' wuh skan lau ma prompted. Po' discharging ish-veh conscience fi' ik patam, au proceeded tor inform au, k' wehk rapturous sagluvaya, t' ish-veh happiness svi' having prah wuh affection t' ish-veh amiable behsu, din-tor lucas, heh yi danau ik ish-veh vesh' goh k' wuh zan-tor t' enjoying ish-veh shila'es ik au had vesh' ni pok tor ikap-tor k' ish-veh ves istaya t' seeing ish-veh va'ashiv na' longbourn, whither au rok-tor kup tor fun fi' gad fortnight; na' t'sai catherine, au hau, ni heartily messau ish-veh kal'i'farr, ik she istau ish-veh tor nem-tor shi u' ak u' tor-yehat, if au trusted would nam-tor wuh unanswerable nerau-kek-vuhnayek k' ish-veh amiable charlotte tor ahm wuh lehkuh-mal gad na' tor ish-veh wuh happiest t' sasu. Mr. Collins’s fun vi' hertfordshire vesh' rai longer wuh tukh t' sanosh tor mrs. Bennet. Fi' wuh contrary, she vesh' u' mau sashitau tor complain t' ish-veh u' ish-veh sa-telsu. Ish-veh vesh' maut flekh ik au dang sarlah tor longbourn instead t' tor lucas lodge; ish-veh vesh' isha maut inconvenient heh exceedingly troublesome. She fnu-ven having visitors svi' wuh kelek du' ish-veh muhl'es vesh' ni indifferent, heh lovers vesh' t' ek' sutra wuh danik disagreeable. Such vesh' wuh gentle murmurs t' mrs. Bennet, heh au mazhiv-kur-tor yut goh tor wuh greater flakosh t' mr. Bingley’s fator absence. Neither jane il elizabeth vesh' kel'o fi' nash subject. Gad po' gad be' dvun-tor maf rik' bringing sovek vath tidings t' ish-veh do wuh report if shortly fakovau svi' meryton t' ish-veh coming rai weht tor netherfield wuh bosh karil; wuh report if highly incensed mrs. Bennet, heh if she worla vravshau tor contradict u' wuh danik scandalous falsehood. Kauk elizabeth began tor pthak--ri ik bingley vesh' indifferent--tonk'peh ik ish-veh ko-kai would nam-tor successful svi' keeping ish-veh maf. Unwilling u' she vesh' tor nafai-tor wuh idea ni vashauk tor jane’s happiness, heh ni dishonourable tor wuh tihet'es t' ish-veh lover, she kupi ri prevent its frequently recurring. Wuh kaunshuk urgam t' ish-veh dahkuh unfeeling ko-kai, heh t' ish-veh overpowering t'hy'la, gol-tor k' wuh attractions t' din-tor darcy heh wuh amusements t' london, lau nam-tor nuh' mau, she ptha, na' wuh karik'es t' ish-veh attachment. U' na' jane, _her_ anxiety ne' nash suspense vesh', veling, weht kusut-tor do elizabeth’s: tonk'peh whatever she olau she vesh' desirous t' concealing; heh svi' herself heh elizabeth, therefore, wuh subject vesh' worla alluded tor. Tonk'peh u' rai such delicacy restrained ish-veh ko-mekh, wuh wadan seldom be' dvun-tor svi' if she did ri variben t' bingley, sagluvau ish-veh impatience na' ish-veh lashan, il kauk require jane tor confess ik kuv au did ri sarlah pla' she dang nah-tor herself maut has-bosh-nam-tor-tor. Ish-veh bolau ek' jane’s br'xan mildness tor lesh aifa nashiv-tor k' tolerable tranquillity. Mr. Collins fun-tor danik punctually fi' wuh gad fortnight, tonk'peh ish-veh reception na' longbourn vesh' ri ved ni gracious u' ish-veh had vesh' fi' ish-veh wuh'rak ragtaya. Au vesh' nuh' kunli, however, tor bolaya mau attention; heh, luckily na' wuh vath, wuh business t' ashaya-tor vas-tor au s' wuh lo'uk deal t' ish-veh apc'koik. Wuh chief t' kanok gad vesh' spent k' ish-veh na' lucas lodge, heh au sometimes fun-tor tor longbourn goh svi' wak tor tor wuh apology na' ish-veh absence fa' wuh skan went tor sar-tak. [illustration: “_whenever she stariben svi' wuh neik voice_” ] mrs. Bennet vesh' really svi' wuh danik pitiable fupa s'. Wuh maut mention t' sovek-vel fundik wuh match threw ish-veh vi' wuh agony t' has-bosh-humour, heh wherever she went she vesh' sure t' khaf-spol ish-veh variben t'. Wuh glan t' din-tor lucas vesh' odious tor ish-veh. U' ish-veh successor svi' ik kelek, she fudau ish-veh k' kis-ka abhorrence. Whenever charlotte sarlah tor gla-tor au, she concluded ish-veh tor nam-tor anticipating wuh wadan t' mat; heh whenever she stariben svi' wuh neik spes tor mr. Collins, vesh' convinced ik au vesh' talking t' wuh longbourn estate, heh resolving tor da-tor herself heh ish-veh daughters s' wuh kelek u' ak u' mr. Bennet vesh' tevik. She complained bitterly t' ek' nash tor ish-veh sa-telsu. “indeed, mr. Bennet, ” leralmin-tor she, “ish-veh nam-tor maut lerash tor nah-tor ik charlotte lucas dang ek'wak nam-tor mistress t' nash kelek, ik _i_ dang nam-tor punekwitau tor tor yut na' _her_, heh ha-tor tor gla-tor ish-veh nem-tor t'nash-veh shi svi' ish-veh!” “t'nash-veh tal-kam, ri tor mazhiv-kur-tor yut tor such gloomy nahp. Kal-tor etek rok na' weh-rom vel. Kal-tor etek snuhkrol-tor ourselves ik _i_ lau nam-tor wuh survivor.” nash vesh' ri maut consoling tor mrs. Bennet; heh, therefore, instead t' tor sovek kilko-srashiv, she went fi' u' fa'. “i fam yehat lesh tor nah-tor ik au dang ma ek' nash estate. Kuv ish-veh vesh' ri na' wuh entail, i dang ri kashek ish-veh.” “ra dang ri du kashek?” “i dang ri kashek sovek-vel na' ek'.” “kal-tor etek nam-tor itar-bosh ik du nam-tor korsau s' wuh fupa s' t' such insensibility.” “i worla mokuhlek nam-tor itar-bosh, mr. Bennet, na' sovek-vel pa' wuh entail. Uf sovek-veh kupi ma wuh conscience tor entail maf wuh estate s' veh’s sha' daughters i fam yehat ken-tor; heh ek' na' wuh sake t' mr. Collins, nuh'! Po dang _he_ ma ish-veh weht do anybody else?” “i trasha ish-veh tor yourself tor satalau, ” leralmin-tor mr. Bennet. [illustration] chapter xxiv. [illustration] din-tor bingley’s nuhm lasha, heh shitau wuh shaht tor vet. Wuh maut wuh'rak zhit-bal zhelesh wuh assurance t' ish-veh hasu ek' settled svi' london na' wuh karil, heh concluded k' ish-veh sa-kai’s regret na' ri having had wak tor vlitau ish-veh respects tor ish-veh t'hylara svi' hertfordshire fa' au losrak wuh shasol. Rok vesh' abru', entirely abru'; heh lu jane kupi attend tor wuh shom t' wuh nuhm, she afer-tor pi', kaula wuh professed affection t' wuh kitausu, ik kupi mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh sovek comfort. Din-tor darcy’s krol occupied wuh chief t' ish-veh. Ish-veh wehk attractions vesh' va'ashiv dwelt fi'; heh caroline boasted joyfully t' ish-veh increasing intimacy, heh ventured tor predict wuh accomplishment t' wuh istau if had vesh' unfolded svi' ish-veh former nuhm. She kitau isha k' lo'uk sanosh t' ish-veh sa-kai’s hasu wuh inmate t' mr. Darcy’s kelek, heh mentioned k' raptures ein dotoran t' wuh latter k' fudau tor uzh furniture. Elizabeth, tor ik jane maut ak sviribau wuh chief t' ek' nash, puzhu-tor ish-veh svi' ralash-fam indignation. Ish-veh khaf-spol vesh' dahsau svi' concern na' ish-veh ko-kai heh resentment tehnat ek' vath. Tor caroline’s assertion t' ish-veh sa-kai’s hasu ulik tor din-tor darcy, she vlitau rai lit. Ik au vesh' really tishau t' jane, she vet-tor rai weht do she had ek'wak ovsoh; heh mau u' she had kwon-hau-ov vesh' sashitau tor spo' ish-veh, she kupi ri nah-tor rik' reshan, hardly rik' contempt, fi' ik easiness t' temper, ik aitlun t' proper resolution, if i' tor ish-veh wuh kafeh t' ish-veh designing t'hylara, heh pufulag-tor ish-veh tor sacrifice ish-veh sha' happiness tor wuh caprice t' ish-veh inclinations. Had ish-veh sha' happiness, however, vesh' wuh goh sacrifice, au lau ma vesh' kal-tor tor torvukh k' ish-veh svi' whatever manner au nahp buhfik; tonk'peh ish-veh ko-kai’s vesh' involved svi' ish-veh, u' she nahp au bolau nam-tor sensible himself. Ish-veh vesh' wuh subject, svi' pen, fi' if haulan would nam-tor wu indulged, heh bolau nam-tor unavailing. She kupi nah-tor t' nothing else; heh wi, whether bingley’s fudau had really tev-tor maf, il vesh' nelau k' ish-veh t'hylara’ interference; whether au had vesh' aware t' jane’s attachment, il whether ish-veh had stron-tor ish-veh glantaya; whichever vesh' wuh nuf, hi ish-veh opinion t' ish-veh bolau nam-tor materially dau k' wuh natyan, ish-veh ko-kai’s situation hafau wuh ka, ish-veh sochya kaing wounded. Wuh gad il dahkuh be' dvun-tor fa' jane had courage tor stariben t' ish-veh feelings tor elizabeth; tonk'peh na' kim-shah, fi' mrs. Bennet’s leaving au teretuhr, po' wuh longer irritation do tsuri pa' netherfield heh its trensu, she kupi ri gol'nev taran, -- “o ik t'nash-veh tal-kam ko-mekh had weht a'fic abru' herself! She mokuhlek ma rai idea t' wuh kusut she mazhiv-kur-tor me k' ish-veh continual haulan fi' ish-veh. Tonk'peh i dungi ri repine. Ish-veh fam yehat kim-shah wu. Au dungi nam-tor forgot, heh etek dungau ek' nam-tor u' etek vesh' fa'.” elizabeth glazhau na' ish-veh ko-kai k' incredulous solicitude, tonk'peh leralmin-tor nothing. “du vet me, ” maf-tor jane, slightly colouring; “indeed, du ma rai utvau. Au lau ha-tor svi' t'nash-veh vokaya u' wuh danik amiable sasu t' t'nash-veh acquaintance tonk'peh ik nam-tor ek'. I ma nothing either tor rok il pthak, heh nothing tor reproach ish-veh k'. Itaren oekon i ma ri _that_ kusut. Wuh pi' wak, therefore--i dungau certainly ar'kadan tor prah wuh weh-rom----” k' wuh stronger spes she ak hau, “i ma nash comfort iyi, ik ish-veh has ri vesh' weht do wuh lafosh t' fancy fi' t'nash-veh vla, heh ik ish-veh has ovsoh rai klau tor sovek-veh tonk'peh myself.” “t'nash-veh tal-kam jane, ” sporiben elizabeth, “du nam-tor nuh' rom. Ish-veh sweetness heh disinterestedness nam-tor really angelic; i ri tor fai-tor ra tor leralmin tor du. I olau u' kuv i had worla ovsoh du yeht-gav, il ashau du u' du nazh.” din-tor bennet eagerly disclaimed ek' wehtsuri merit, heh threw pla' wuh krol fi' ish-veh ko-kai’s lamekh affection. “nay, ” leralmin-tor elizabeth, “nash nam-tor ri rom. _you_ istaya tor nah-tor ek' wuh panu respectable, heh nam-tor dash-tor kuv i stariben has-bosh t' anybody. _i_ goh aitlun tor nah-tor _you_ buhfik, heh du eku yourself tehnat ish-veh. Ri tor nam-tor kwes t' t'nash-veh sahran vi' sovek mau-mazhiv-kur, t' t'nash-veh encroaching fi' ish-veh privilege t' universal rom-dungi. Du bolaya ri. Tra' nam-tor zamu sutra ik i really ashaya, heh fam dvun fewer t' ik i nah-tor muhl. Wuh weht gla-tor nash-veh t' wuh panu wuh weht am i dissatisfied k' ish-veh; heh kanok gad wugau t'nash-veh dva t' wuh inconsistency t' ek' komihn characters, heh t' wuh pi' dependence ik mokuhlek nam-tor shitau fi' wuh appearance t' either merit il kash-ral. I ma ragel-tor k' dahkuh instances lately: veh i dungi ri mention, wuh vath nam-tor charlotte’s kal'i'farr. Ish-veh nam-tor unaccountable! Svi' kanok zan-tor ish-veh nam-tor unaccountable!” “t'nash-veh tal-kam lizzy, ri tor mazhiv-kur-tor yut tor such feelings u' aifa. Au dungi ruin ish-veh happiness. Du ri tor tor allowance hiyet na' natyan t' situation heh temper. Panah-tor mr. Collins’s respectability, heh charlotte’s prudent, br'xan character. Vokau ik she nam-tor veh t' wuh suk skan; ik u' tor fortune ish-veh nam-tor wuh danik eligible match; heh nam-tor pok tor dva-tor, na' kanok-veh’s sake, ik she lau olau vel spo' fudau heh vam na' etwel krei.” “tor oblige du, i would ar'kadan tor dva-tor siyah sovek-vel, tonk'peh kling else kupi nam-tor rufah k' such wuh dva u' nash; na' vesh' i persuaded ik charlotte had sovek fudau na' ish-veh, i dang goh nah-tor weh-rasahkos t' ish-veh understanding do i i' tor t' ish-veh khaf-spol. T'nash-veh tal-kam jane, mr. Collins nam-tor wuh conceited, pompous, wonil-minded, silly sasu: du fai-tor au nam-tor, u' muhl u' i tor; heh du bolau olau, u' muhl u' i tor, ik wuh kosu vi marries ish-veh fam yehat ma wuh proper yut t' thinking. Du dungau ri fosh-tor ish-veh, hi ish-veh nam-tor charlotte lucas. Du dungau ri, na' wuh sake t' veh wuhsu, rubah wuh meaning t' dvatai heh ket'es, il endeavour tor persuade yourself il me, ik selfishness nam-tor prudence, heh insensibility t' tehvar shar'es na' happiness.” “i bolau nah-tor ish-veh gen-lis nuh' karik svi' speaking t' fi', ” kilko-tor jane; “heh i rok du dungi nam-tor convinced t' ish-veh, k' seeing au kunli teretuhr. Tonk'peh hiyet t' nash. Du alluded tor vel else. Du mentioned _two_ instances. I fam yehat misunderstand du, tonk'peh i entreat du, tal-kam lizzy, ri tor kusut me k' thinking _that person_ tor tenai, heh taran ish-veh opinion t' ish-veh nam-tor ne'hal-tor. Etek bolau ri nam-tor ni pok tor fancy ourselves intentionally dash-tor. Etek bolau ri gish wuh lively nu'ri sasu tor nam-tor kwon-hau-ov ni klashau heh circumspect. Ish-veh nam-tor maut k'ashiv nothing tonk'peh etwel sha' vanity ik tehs-tor etek. Kosu fancy admiration tvai weht do ish-veh tor.” “heh sasu nem-tor tun ik au dang.” “kuv ish-veh nam-tor designedly ovsoh, au fam yehat nam-tor justified; tonk'peh i ma rai idea t' tra' hasu ni mau design svi' wuh panu u' ein persons glenonau.” “i am irak s' attributing sovek krus t' mr. Bingley’s spa-tor tor design, ” leralmin-tor elizabeth; “tonk'peh, rik' scheming tor tor riyeht, il tor tor vath unhappy, tra' lau nam-tor lafosh heh tra' lau nam-tor misery. Thoughtlessness, aitlun t' attention tor vath sutra’s feelings, heh aitlun t' resolution, dungi tor wuh business.” “heh tor du impute ish-veh tor either t' eifa?” “ha; tor wuh kim-shah. Tonk'peh kuv i hal-tor fi' i dungau displease du k' taran ra i nah-tor t' persons du vam. Pehkaya me, whilst du mokuhlek.” “du persist, yi, svi' supposing ish-veh ko-kai vi-yumuk ish-veh?” “ha, svi' kh'ta k' ish-veh t'hy'la.” “i fam yehat dva-tor ish-veh. Po dang au ar'kadan tor vi-yumuk ish-veh? Au mokuhlek goh istaya ish-veh happiness; heh kuv au nam-tor attached tor me rai vath kosu mokuhlek shar ish-veh.” “ish-veh wuh'rak shul nam-tor riyeht. Au lau istaya wehk vel isha ish-veh happiness: au lau istaya ish-veh increase t' don-tak heh consequence; au lau istaya ish-veh tor marry wuh ko-kan vi has ek' wuh importance t' donku, lo'uk tersaya, heh pride.” “mesakh wuh vet au tor istaya ish-veh tor dvel-tor din-tor darcy, ” kilko-tor jane; “tonk'peh nash lau nam-tor s' weh-rom feelings do du nam-tor supposing. Au ma fainu ish-veh mau longer do au ma fainu me; rai wonder kuv au ashaya ish-veh weh-rom. Tonk'peh, whatever lau nam-tor ish-veh sha' istau, ish-veh nam-tor maut rikesik au dang ma opposed ish-veh sa-kai’s. Ra ko-kai would nah-tor herself na' liberty tor tor ish-veh, vita tra' vesh' vel maut objectionable? Kuv au pudva-tor ish-veh attached tor me au would ri ar'kadan tor krus etek; kuv au vesh' ni, au kupi ri navau. K' supposing such wuh affection, du tor kanok-veh peran unnaturally heh riyeht, heh me danik unhappy. Ri tor flakosh me k' wuh idea. I am ri kafusik t' having vesh' mistaken--il, k'puu, ish-veh nam-tor slight, ish-veh nam-tor nothing svi' comparison t' ra i dang olau svi' thinking has-bosh t' ish-veh il ish-veh ko-kai. Kal-tor me nem-tor ish-veh svi' wuh buhfik ta'hal, svi' wuh ta'hal svi' if ish-veh lau nam-tor ken-tor.” elizabeth kupi ri oppose such wuh istaya; heh s' nash wak mr. Bingley’s ahm vesh' scarcely ek'wak mentioned svi' au. Mrs. Bennet fam dvun fator tor wonder heh repine na' ish-veh returning rai weht; heh hi wuh gad seldom be' dvun-tor svi' if elizabeth did ri khrosahp na' ish-veh clearly, tra' seemed pi' pavesh t' ish-veh ek'wak panahik ish-veh k' lehkuh perplexity. Ish-veh ko-fu endeavoured tor convince ish-veh t' ra she did ri dva-tor herself, ik ish-veh attentions tor jane had vesh' goh wuh daya t' wuh tsuri heh transient liking, if ceased lu gla-tor ish-veh ish-veh rai weht; tonk'peh hi wuh yesik'es t' wuh star-krus vesh' nafai-tor na' wuh wak, she had wuh ka var tor ashiv-tor kanok gad. Mrs. Bennet’s buhfik comfort vesh', ik mr. Bingley bolau nam-tor ne' va'ashiv svi' wuh belaar. Mr. Bennet skasau wuh tukh differently. “ni, lizzy, ” leralmin-tor au, veh gad, “ish-veh ko-kai nam-tor tuhsau svi' ashaya, i talal. I congratulate ish-veh. Thurai tor hasu telik, wuh ko-kan tishau tor nam-tor tuhsau svi' ashaya wuh pi' i' heh yi. Ish-veh nam-tor vel tor nah-tor t', heh mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh wuh wihfelau t' distinction among ish-veh besu. Lu nam-tor ish-veh da-tor tor sarlah? Du dungi hardly lesh tor nam-tor wu outdone k' jane. I' nam-tor ish-veh wak. La' nam-tor officers hiyet na' meryton tor disappoint ek' wuh nu'ri t'sai svi' wuh shasol. Kal-tor wickham nam-tor ish-veh sasu. Au nam-tor wuh vaksurik katravahsu, heh would jilt du creditably.” “nemaiyo, osu, tonk'peh wuh lehkuh agreeable sasu would satisfy me. Etek bolau ri ek' gish jane’s rom fortune.” “yeht, ” leralmin-tor mr. Bennet; “tonk'peh ish-veh nam-tor wuh comfort tor nah-tor ik, whatever t' ik ves lau befall du, du ma wuh affectionate ko-mekh vi dungi kwon-hau-ov tor wuh danik t' ish-veh.” mr. Wickham’s shila'es vesh' t' tukh dvin svi' dispelling wuh gloom if wuh tab-ma perverse occurrences had lehm-tor fi' wehk t' wuh longbourn skan. Gla-tor au ish-veh k'ashiv, heh tor ish-veh vath recommendations vesh' i' hau ik t' paik unreserve. Wuh bosh t' ra elizabeth had already puzhu-tor, ish-veh claims fi' mr. Darcy, heh ek' ik au had dashau s' ish-veh, vesh' i' openly nafai heh publicly canvassed; heh kanok-veh vesh' sanoi tor nah-tor uf mau au had kwon-hau-ov ritishau mr. Darcy fa' au had fainu sovek-vel t' wuh tukh. Din-tor bennet vesh' wuh goh creature vi kupi suppose tra' lau nam-tor sovek extenuating circumstances svi' wuh nuf ri-fainu tor wuh shila'es t' hertfordshire: ish-veh bovik heh br'xan candour kwon-hau-ov pleaded na' allowances, heh urged wuh possibility t' lafosh; tonk'peh k' kanok-veh else mr. Darcy vesh' condemned u' wuh rasahkos t' sasu. [illustration] chapter xxv. [illustration] po' wuh wehk gad spent svi' ha'yigal t' ashaya heh schemes t' felicity, mr. Collins vesh' puvutau s' ish-veh amiable charlotte k' wuh lashan t' gad. Wuh kusut t' dahshaya, however, lau nam-tor alleviated fi' ish-veh vla k' preparations na' wuh reception t' ish-veh bride, u' au had utvau tor rok, ik shortly po' ish-veh thurai fun vi' hertfordshire, wuh gad would nam-tor teslau ik vesh' tor tor ish-veh wuh happiest t' sasu. Au nem-tor trasha t' ish-veh relations na' longbourn k' u' mau solemnity u' fa'; istau ish-veh rom krei muhl'es heh happiness va'ashiv, heh ugau ish-veh sa-mekh wuh'ashiv nuhm t' itaren. Fi' wuh zahalik gad, mrs. Bennet had wuh sanosh t' receiving ish-veh sa-kai heh ish-veh ko-telsu, vi sarlah, u' tsuri, tor spend wuh christmas na' longbourn. Mr. Gardiner vesh' wuh sensible, gentlemanlike sasu, greatly superior tor ish-veh ko-kai, u' muhl k' malat u' education. Wuh netherfield t'sai would ma had rihag'es svi' believing ik wuh sasu vi ha-tor k' trade, heh k'svi zan-tor t' ish-veh sha' warehouses, kupi ma vesh' ni muhl-bred heh agreeable. Mrs. Gardiner, vi vesh' several tevun younger do mrs. Bennet heh mrs. Philips, vesh' wuh amiable, kash-tok, sohkik kosu, heh wuh lo'uk favourite k' ish-veh longbourn ko-bath. Svi' wuh dahkuh eldest heh herself wa', tra' subsisted wuh maut particular fudau. Au had frequently vesh' staying k' ish-veh svi' kahr. Wuh wuh'rak krus t' mrs. Gardiner’s business, fi' ish-veh lashan, vesh' tor sagan-tor ish-veh presents heh kethelvau wuh newest fashions. Lu nash vesh' ovsoh, she had wuh lehkuh torupik krus tor mavau. Ish-veh became ish-veh da-tor tor shroi. Mrs. Bennet had wehk grievances tor relate, heh mau tor complain t'. Au had ek' vesh' maut has-bosh-nam-tor-tor opi' she kim-shah gla-tor ish-veh ko-kai. Dahkuh t' ish-veh ko-kan had vesh' fi' wuh sfek t' kal'i'farr, heh po' ek' tra' vesh' nothing svi' ish-veh. “i ri tor tenai jane, ” she fator, “na' jane would ma prah mr. Bingley kuv she kupi. Tonk'peh, lizzy! Oh, ko-kai! Ish-veh nam-tor maut lerash tor nah-tor ik she lau ma vesh' mr. Collins’s ko-telsu k' nash wak, had ri ish-veh vesh' na' ish-veh sha' perverseness. Au tor ish-veh wuh nufai svi' nash maut tvi-shal, heh she klee'fah ish-veh. Wuh consequence t' ish-veh nam-tor, ik t'sai lucas dungi ma wuh ko-fu telik fa' i ma, heh ik longbourn estate nam-tor aishan u' mau entailed u' ek'wak. Wuh lucases nam-tor maut artful sutra, indeed, ko-kai. Au nam-tor ek' na' ra au mokuhlek prah. Ni'droi'ik nar-tor tor leralmin ish-veh t' au, tonk'peh ni ish-veh nam-tor. Ish-veh tor me maut nervous heh poorly, tor nam-tor thwarted ni svi' t'nash-veh sha' skan, heh ki' behsu vi nah-tor t' themselves fa' anybody else. However, ish-veh coming aishan na' nash wak nam-tor wuh greatest t' comforts, heh i am maut glad tor zhu-tor ra du var-tor etek t' wu sleeves.” mrs. Gardiner, tor ik wuh chief t' nash ro'fori had vesh' putan-tor fa', svi' wuh rivak t' jane heh elizabeth’s correspondence k' ish-veh, tor ish-veh ko-kai wuh slight kilko-srashiv, heh, svi' utan'es tor ish-veh ko-bath, da-tor wuh conversation. Lu sa'awek k' elizabeth afterwards, she stariben weht fi' wuh subject. “ish-veh seems kesik ki' vesh' wuh desirable match na' jane, ” leralmin-tor she. “i am sorry ish-veh went ska'. Tonk'peh aifa vel pavesh-tor ni k'ashiv! Wuh nu'ri sasu, such u' du kethelvau mr. Bingley, ni easily tevan-tor svi' ashaya k' wuh takov ko-kan na' wuh zamu wehk gad, heh, lu kisheya dahshau au, ni easily yen-tor ish-veh, ik aifa wihfelau t' inconstancies nam-tor maut vakavik.” [illustration: “puthrap-tor dahkuh il rehkuh nu'ri t'sai” [_copyright 1894 k' george allen._]] “wuh marom consolation svi' its yut, ” leralmin-tor elizabeth; “tonk'peh ish-veh dungi ri tor na' _us_. Etek ri tor dash k' kisheya. Ish-veh tor ri k'ashiv pavesh-tor ik wuh interference t' t'hylara dungi persuade wuh nu'ri sasu t' independent fortune tor nah-tor rai weht t' wuh ko-kan ik au vesh' violently svi' ashaya k' goh wuh zamu gad fa'.” “tonk'peh ik sagluvaya t' ‘violently svi' ashaya’ nam-tor ni hackneyed, ni vet-bosh, ni indefinite, ik ish-veh mazhiv-kur-tor me maut pi' idea. Ish-veh nam-tor u' k'ashiv applied tor feelings if arise goh s' wuh ulef wadan’s acquaintance, u' tor wuh yeht, karik attachment. Pray, uf _violent was_ mr. Bingley’s ashaya?” “i worla gla-tor wuh weht promising inclination; au vesh' growing ved inattentive tor vath sutra, heh wholly engrossed k' ish-veh. Kanok wak au ragel-tor, ish-veh vesh' weht klopau heh remarkable. Na' ish-veh sha' rin'k'n au puthrap-tor dahkuh il rehkuh nu'ri t'sai k' ri asking au tor tam; heh i stariben tor ish-veh dah'wak myself rik' receiving wuh kilko-srashiv. Kupi tra' nam-tor finer symptoms? Nam-tor ri paik incivility wuh maut essence t' ashaya?” “oh, ha! T' ik ves t' ashaya if i suppose ish-veh ki' olau. Ri donku-tor jane! Ni'droi'ik nar-tor na' ish-veh, fai'ei, k' ish-veh disposition, she lau ri prah abru' ish-veh iyi. Ish-veh had weh-rom ma pavesh-tor tor _you_, lizzy; du would ma abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor yourself s' ish-veh sooner. Tonk'peh tor du nah-tor she would nam-tor fakovau fi' tor hal-tor pla' k' etek? Rubah t' scene lau nam-tor t' dvin--heh sos'eh wuh pi' vas s' ha-kel lau nam-tor u' useful u' sovek-vel.” elizabeth vesh' exceedingly sanoi k' nash mnah, heh olau persuaded t' ish-veh ko-kai’s pok acquiescence. “i rok, ” hau mrs. Gardiner, “ik rai consideration k' fudau tor nash nu'ri sasu dungi vi-yumuk ish-veh. Etek ha-tor svi' ni natya wuh krus t' kahr, ek' etwel tersaya nam-tor ni natya, heh, u' du muhl fai-tor, etek hal-tor si' ni pi', ik ish-veh nam-tor maut improbable au dang ragel-tor na' ek', vita au really sarlah tor gla-tor ish-veh.” “heh _that_ nam-tor ved impossible; na' au nam-tor i' svi' wuh custody t' ish-veh t'hy'la, heh mr. Darcy would rai weht dash ish-veh tor vutau fi' jane svi' such wuh krus t' london! T'nash-veh tal-kam ezyet, uf kupi du nah-tor t' ish-veh? Mr. Darcy lau, sos'eh, ma _heard_ t' such wuh shi u' gracechurch yut, tonk'peh au would hardly nah-tor wuh tevun-krus’s ablution hiyet tor cleanse ish-veh s' its impurities, vesh' au wuh'wak tor svi-tor ish-veh; heh, nerau fi-tor ish-veh, mr. Bingley worla stirs rik' ish-veh.” “ni mau wuh weh-rom. I rok au dungi ri ragel-tor na' ek'. Tonk'peh tor ri jane correspond k' ish-veh ko-kai? _she_ dungi ri nam-tor kup tor gol'nev calling.” “she dungi eku wuh acquaintance entirely.” tonk'peh, svi' spite t' wuh certainty svi' if elizabeth dau tor shi nash sfek, u' muhl u' wuh fam dvun weht eku'ki veh t' bingley’s hasu withheld s' seeing jane, she olau wuh solicitude fi' wuh subject if convinced ish-veh, fi' linisaya, ik she did ri panah-tor ish-veh entirely hopeless. Ish-veh vesh' tor-yehat, heh sometimes she nahp ish-veh yesik, ik ish-veh affection lau nam-tor re-animated, heh wuh vi-yumuk t' ish-veh t'hylara successfully combated k' wuh weht malatik vi-yumuk t' jane’s attractions. Din-tor bennet nar-tor ish-veh ezyet’s k'waw'zhe k' sanosh; heh wuh bingleys vesh' rai vathru svi' ish-veh nahp na' wuh ka wak do u' she rok-tor, k' caroline’s ri living svi' wuh ka kelek k' ish-veh sa-kai, she lau occasionally spend wuh asal k' ish-veh, rik' sovek tehvar t' seeing ish-veh. Wuh gardiners stayed wuh wehk gad na' longbourn; heh ra k' wuh philipses, wuh lucases, heh wuh officers, tra' vesh' ri wuh gad rik' its engagement. Mrs. Bennet had ni carefully tanilau na' wuh entertainment t' ish-veh sa-kai heh ko-kai, ik au did ri wuh'wak hayal-tor ne' tor wuh skan aru-yem. Lu wuh engagement vesh' na' ha-kel, ein t' wuh officers kwon-hau-ov tor krus t' ish-veh, t' if officers mr. Wickham vesh' sure tor nam-tor veh; heh fi' aifa occasions mrs. Gardiner, rendered suspicious k' elizabeth’s lamekh commendation t' ish-veh, narrowly glantau au fi'. Rik' supposing au, s' ra gla-tor ish-veh, tor nam-tor maut seriously svi' ashaya, ish-veh preference t' tik vath vesh' eiktra hiyet tor tor ish-veh wuh pi' uneasy; heh she resolved tor stariben tor elizabeth fi' wuh subject fa' she losrak hertfordshire, heh represent tor ish-veh wuh imprudence t' encouraging such wuh attachment. Tor mrs. Gardiner, wickham had veh tvai t' affording sanosh, unconnected k' ish-veh paik tepul. Pa' lehkuh il wuh dozen tevun ago, fa' ish-veh kal'i'farr, she had spent wuh considerable wak svi' ik maut krus t' derbyshire tor if au belonged. Au had, therefore, wehk acquaintance svi' tsuri; heh, hi wickham had vesh' pi' tra' opi' wuh tevakh t' darcy’s sa-mekh, kaukuh tevun fa', ish-veh vesh' wi svi' ish-veh tepul tor mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh fresher kash-tor'es t' ish-veh former t'hylara do she had vesh' svi' wuh yut t' procuring. Mrs. Gardiner had gla-tor pemberley, heh fainu wuh tab-ma mr. Darcy k' character perfectly muhl. La', consequently, vesh' wuh inexhaustible subject t' discourse. Svi' comparing ish-veh recollection t' pemberley k' wuh minute kethelvaya if wickham kupi mazhiv-kur-tor, heh svi' bestowing ish-veh tribute t' krol fi' wuh character t' its tab-ma possessor, she vesh' delighting fi' ish-veh heh herself. Fi' hasu tor acquainted k' wuh la' mr. Darcy’s skasaya t' ish-veh, she ar'kada tor vokau vel t' ik gentleman’s reputed disposition, lu ved wuh lad, if lau sep-wafikh k' ish-veh; heh vesh' confident, na' kim-shah, ik she recollected having puzhu-tor mr. Fitzwilliam darcy formerly spoken t' u' wuh maut yaut, has-bosh-natured sa-kan. [illustration: “dungi sarlah du heh gla-tor me?” ] chapter xxvi. [illustration] mrs. Gardiner’s yuzhat tor elizabeth vesh' punctually heh kindly putan-tor fi' wuh wuh'rak favourable opportunity t' speaking tor ish-veh sa'awek: po' honestly telling ish-veh ra she nahp, she thus went fi': -- “du nam-tor nuh' sensible wuh ko-kan, lizzy, tor tevan svi' ashaya goh fai'ei du nam-tor vikau tehnat ish-veh; heh, therefore, i am ri kwes t' speaking openly. Seriously, i would ma du nam-tor fi' ish-veh klashausu. Ri tor involve yourself, il endeavour tor involve ish-veh, svi' wuh affection if wuh aitlun t' fortune would tor ni maut imprudent. I ma nothing tor leralmin tehnat _him_: au nam-tor wuh danik eku'ki nu'ri sasu; heh kuv au had wuh fortune au ought ki', i dang nah-tor du kupi ri tor weh-rom. Tonk'peh u' ish-veh nam-tor--du bolau ri kal-tor ish-veh fancy sahr-tor maf k' du. Du ma kash-ral, heh etek ek' gish du tor nam-tor-tor ish-veh. Ish-veh sa-mekh would nerau fi' _your_ resolution heh rom spa-tor, i am sure. Du bolau ri disappoint ish-veh sa-mekh.” “t'nash-veh tal-kam ezyet, nash nam-tor hasu serious indeed.” “ha, heh i rok tor engage du tor nam-tor serious likewise.” “muhl, yi, du bolaya ri nam-tor ne' sovek vikayek. I dungi nem-tor tun t' myself, heh t' mr. Wickham nuh'. Au dungau ri nam-tor svi' ashaya k' me, kuv i mokuhlek prevent ish-veh.” “elizabeth, du nam-tor ri serious i'.” “i eit'jae ish-veh pardon. I dungi ar'kadan va'ashiv. Na' la' i am ri svi' ashaya k' mr. Wickham; rai, i certainly am ri. Tonk'peh au nam-tor, mesakh ek' comparison, wuh danik agreeable sasu i ek'wak gla-tor--heh kuv au shetau really attached tor me--i dva-tor ish-veh dungi nam-tor weh-rom ik au dang ri. Gla-tor nash-veh wuh imprudence t' ish-veh. Oh, _that_ abominable mr. Darcy! T'nash-veh sa-mekh’s opinion t' me tor me wuh greatest dor; heh i dang nam-tor miserable tor forfeit ish-veh. T'nash-veh sa-mekh, however, nam-tor ulik tor mr. Wickham. Svi' pen, t'nash-veh tal-kam ezyet, i dang nam-tor maut sorry tor nam-tor wuh tvai t' tor sovek t' du unhappy; tonk'peh opi' gla-tor etek, kanok gad, ik wilat tra' nam-tor affection nu'ri sutra nam-tor seldom withheld, k' iyi aitlun t' fortune, s' entering vi' engagements k' tik vath, uf mokuhlek i ugaya tor nam-tor wiser do ni wehk t' t'nash-veh katravahsu-creatures, kuv i am tempted, il uf am i kauk tor fai-tor ik ish-veh would nam-tor wiser tor tehnau? Ek' ik i mokuhlek ugaya du, therefore, nam-tor ri tor nam-tor svi' wuh brax. I dungi ri nam-tor svi' wuh brax tor dva-tor myself ish-veh wuh'rak vel. Lu i am svi' apc'koik k' ish-veh, i dungi ri nam-tor wishing. Svi' pen, i dungi tor t'nash-veh buhfik.” “sos'eh ish-veh dungi nam-tor u' muhl kuv du discourage ish-veh coming la' ni maut k'ashiv. K'puu du dang ri _remind_ ish-veh ko-mekh t' inviting ish-veh.” “u' i did wuh vath gad, ” leralmin-tor elizabeth, k' wuh d'wonil abru'teruklar-ru'lut; “maut yeht, ish-veh dungi nam-tor kau-bosh svi' me tor refrain s' _that_. Tonk'peh ri tor glenonau ik au nam-tor kwon-hau-ov la' ni k'ashiv. Ish-veh nam-tor fi' ish-veh khrosahp ik au has vesh' ni frequently invited nash wehk gad. Du fai-tor t'nash-veh ko-mekh’s ideas u' tor wuh bolayek t' ek'kayik apc'koik na' ish-veh t'hylara. Tonk'peh really, heh fi-tor t'nash-veh dor, i dungi ar'kadan tor tor ra i nah-tor tor nam-tor wisest; heh i' i rok du nam-tor satisfied.” ish-veh ezyet assured ish-veh ik she vesh'; heh elizabeth, having itaren ish-veh na' wuh kindness t' ish-veh hints, au parted, --wuh wonderful instance t' na'shikh hasu putan-tor fi' such wuh sfek rik' hasu resented. Mr. Collins fun-tor vi' hertfordshire ak po' ish-veh had vesh' quitted k' wuh gardiners heh jane; tonk'peh, u' au nem-tor abru ish-veh abode k' wuh lucases, ish-veh lashan vesh' rai lo'uk inconvenience tor mrs. Bennet. Ish-veh kal'i'farr vesh' i' sahris approaching; heh she vesh' na' wu-vath ni irak resigned u' tor nah-tor ish-veh inevitable, heh kauk repeatedly tor leralmin, svi' wuh has-bosh-natured molu, ik she “_wished_ au lau nam-tor kunli.” gad vesh' tor nam-tor wuh wedding-gad, heh fi' gad din-tor lucas vlitau ish-veh rom-halan yaret; heh lu she she-tor tor nem-tor trasha, elizabeth, kafusik t' ish-veh ko-mekh’s ungracious heh reluctant rom istau, heh sincerely dau herself, accompanied ish-veh s' wuh tvi-shal. U' au went ne' kaiden teretuhr, charlotte leralmin-tor, -- “i dungau nerau fi' khaf-spol s' du maut k'ashiv, eliza.” “_that_ du certainly dungau.” “heh i ma wuh'ashiv favour tor ya'akash. Dungi sarlah du heh gla-tor me?” “etek dungau k'ashiv ragel-tor, i rok, svi' hertfordshire.” “i am ri kesik tor trasha kent na' ein wak. Ugaya me, therefore, tor sarlah tor hunsford.” elizabeth kupi ri klee'fah, hi she foresaw pi' sanosh svi' wuh yaret. “t'nash-veh sa-mekh heh maria nam-tor tor sarlah tor me svi' march, ” hau charlotte, “heh i rok du dungi consent tor nam-tor t' wuh party. Indeed, eliza, du dungi nam-tor u' welcome tor me u' either t' au.” wuh wedding nem-tor shi: wuh bride heh bridegroom eku ska' na' kent s' wuh church svep, heh kanok-veh had u' mau tor leralmin il tor zhu-tor fi' wuh subject u' tsuri. Elizabeth ak puzhu-tor s' ish-veh t'hy'la, heh ish-veh correspondence vesh' u' regular heh vakavik u' ish-veh ek'wak had vesh': ik ish-veh dang nam-tor kaing unreserved vesh' impossible. Elizabeth kupi worla shi'yavekh ish-veh rik' olaya ik ek' wuh comfort t' intimacy vesh' abru'; heh, hi satalau ri tor slacken u' wuh correspondent, ish-veh vesh' na' wuh sake t' ra had vesh' rather do ra vesh'. Charlotte’s wuh'rak nuhm vesh' poprah k' wuh rom deal t' eagerness: tra' kupi ri tonk'peh nam-tor curiosity tor fai-tor uf she would stariben t' ish-veh uzh ha-kel, uf she would spo' t'sai catherine, heh uf kunli she would dare pronounce herself tor nam-tor; hi, lu wuh nuhm vesh' telv-tor, elizabeth olau ik charlotte sagluvau herself fi' kanok sfek exactly u' she lau ma fa-glan-tor. She kitau cheerfully, seemed vikuvau k' comforts, heh mentioned nothing if she kupi ri krol. Wuh kelek, furniture, neighbourhood, heh fau-yut, vesh' ek' tor ish-veh zahvan, heh t'sai catherine’s kloshai vesh' danik friendly heh obliging. Ish-veh vesh' mr. Collins’s bikuv t' hunsford heh rosings rationally softened; heh elizabeth pakashogau ik she bolau bek-tor na' ish-veh sha' yaret tra', tor fai-tor wuh shom. Jane had already written wuh zamu zehl tor ish-veh ko-kai, tor tor'pra ish-veh safe lashan svi' london; heh lu she kitau va'ashiv, elizabeth rok-tor ish-veh would nam-tor svi' ish-veh tepul tor leralmin vel t' wuh bingleys. Ish-veh impatience na' nash dahr nuhm vesh' u' muhl rewarded u' impatience paik nam-tor. Jane had vesh' wuh wehk gad svi' kahr, rik' either seeing il khaf-spol s' caroline. She accounted na' ish-veh, however, k' supposing ik ish-veh kim-shah nuhm tor ish-veh t'hy'la s' longbourn had k' ein kisheya vesh' pakik. “t'nash-veh ezyet, ” she fator, “nam-tor going tor-morrow vi' ik krus t' wuh kahr, heh i dungau nem-tor wuh opportunity t' calling svi' grosvenor yut.” she kitau va'ashiv lu wuh yaret vesh' vlitau, heh she had gla-tor din-tor bingley. “i did ri nah-tor caroline svi' tam'a, ” vesh' ish-veh zhit, “tonk'peh she vesh' maut glad tor gla-tor me, heh reproached me na' giving ish-veh rai beglanau t' t'nash-veh coming tor london. I vesh' gas'rak, therefore; t'nash-veh kim-shah nuhm had worla pulau ish-veh. I inquired po' ish-veh sa-kai, veling. Au vesh' muhl, tonk'peh ni mau engaged k' mr. Darcy ik au scarcely ek'wak gla-tor ish-veh. I afer-tor ik din-tor darcy vesh' gishu tor aru-yem: i istaya kupi gla-tor nash-veh ish-veh. T'nash-veh yaret vesh' ri wu, u' caroline heh mrs. Hurst vesh' going si'. I dare leralmin i dungau ak gla-tor au la'.” elizabeth hutau ish-veh patam abru' nash nuhm. Ish-veh convinced ish-veh ik kisheya goh kupi discover tor mr. Bingley ish-veh ko-kai’s hasu svi' kahr. Kehkuh wehk gad be' dvun-tor maf, heh jane gla-tor nothing t' ish-veh. She endeavoured tor persuade herself ik she did ri regret ish-veh; tonk'peh she kupi rai longer nam-tor glan-fam tor din-tor bingley’s inattention. Po' waiting na' ha-kel kanok asal na' wuh fortnight, heh fereikan kanok khru wuh sluk tobeg na' ish-veh, wuh visitor did na' kim-shah saudau; tonk'peh wuh shortness t' ish-veh stay, heh, wi weht, wuh alteration t' ish-veh manner, would kal-tor jane tor tehs-tor herself rai longer. Wuh nuhm if she kitau fi' nash occasion tor ish-veh ko-kai dungi skan-tor ra she olau: -- “t'nash-veh dearest lizzy dungi, i am sure, nam-tor incapable t' triumphing svi' ish-veh weh-rom judgment, na' t'nash-veh kodona, lu i confess myself ki' vesh' entirely tehs-tor svi' din-tor bingley’s fudau na' me. Tonk'peh, t'nash-veh tal-kam ko-kai, hi wuh pavek has skan-tor du gas'rak, ri tor nah-tor me obstinate kuv i fam dvun seo'a ik, panahik ra ish-veh kloshai vesh', t'nash-veh guhl'es vesh' u' malatik u' ish-veh suspicion. I ri tor na' ek' comprehend ish-veh utvau na' wishing tor nam-tor intimate k' me; tonk'peh, kuv wuh ka circumstances vesh' tor pavesh-tor va'ashiv, i am sure i dang nam-tor tehs-tor va'ashiv. Caroline did ri fun t'nash-veh yaret till za-gad; heh ri wuh pitoh, ri wuh zehl, did i poprah svi' wuh meantime. Lu she did sarlah, ish-veh vesh' maut evident ik she had rai sanosh svi' ish-veh; she tor wuh slight, hotorik apology na' ri calling fa', leralmin-tor ri wuh zhit t' wishing tor gla-tor me va'ashiv, heh vesh', svi' kanok respect, ni rubitau wuh creature, ik lu she went maf i vesh' perfectly resolved tor fator wuh acquaintance rai longer. I pity, hi i fam yehat gol'nev blaming, ish-veh. She vesh' maut riyeht svi' singling me si' u' she did; i mokuhlek safely leralmin, ik kanok storilaya tor intimacy began fi' ish-veh vla. Tonk'peh i pity ish-veh, fai'ei she bolau olau ik she has vesh' peran riyeht, heh fai'ei i am maut sure ik anxiety na' ish-veh sa-kai nam-tor wuh aishan t' ish-veh. I bolaya ri danau myself weh-irak; heh hi _we_ fai-tor nash anxiety tor nam-tor ved needless, wi kuv she olau ish-veh, ish-veh dungi easily khrosahp na' ish-veh kloshai tor me; heh ni deservedly tal-kam u' au nam-tor tor ish-veh ko-kai, whatever anxiety she lau olau fi' ish-veh behalf nam-tor malatik heh amiable. I fam yehat tonk'peh wonder, however, na' ish-veh having sovek such ptha i', fai'ei kuv au had na' ek' tun-tor pa' me, etek bolau ma ragel-tor wu, wu ago. Au fai-tor t' t'nash-veh hasu svi' kahr, i am ac'ruth, s' vel she leralmin-tor herself; heh wi ish-veh would seem, k' ish-veh manner t' talking, u' kuv she aitlu tor persuade herself ik au nam-tor really ulik tor din-tor darcy. I fam yehat ken-tor ish-veh. Kuv i vesh' ri kwes t' judging harshly, i dang nam-tor siyah tempted tor leralmin, ik tra' nam-tor wuh karik appearance t' duplicity svi' ek' nash. I dungi endeavour tor sahaisau kanok kusut-tor nahp, heh nah-tor goh t' ra dungi tor me kunli, ish-veh affection, heh wuh invariable kindness t' t'nash-veh tal-kam sa-kuk heh ezyet. Kal-tor me zhu-tor s' du maut ak. Din-tor bingley leralmin-tor vel t' ish-veh worla returning tor netherfield va'ashiv, t' giving abru wuh kelek, tonk'peh ri k' sovek certainty. Etek had weh-rom ri mention ish-veh. I am extremely glad ik du ma such vaksurik khrosahp s' etwel t'hylara na' hunsford. Pray hal-tor tor gla-tor au, k' osu william heh maria. I am sure du dungi nam-tor maut kel'o tra'. “ish-veh, etc.” nash nuhm mazhiv-kur-tor elizabeth ein kusut; tonk'peh ish-veh tam'a fun-tor, u' she panah-tor ik jane would rai longer nam-tor duped, k' wuh ko-kai k'puu. Ek' gishat s' wuh sa-kai vesh' i' absolutely abru'. She would ri kauk istaya na' sovek renewal t' ish-veh attentions. Ish-veh character ne'hal-tor fi' kanok review t' ish-veh; heh, u' wuh taflaya na' ish-veh, u' muhl u' wuh tor-yehat advantage tor jane, she seriously rok-tor au lau really ak marry mr. Darcy’s ko-kai, u', k' wickham’s khrosahp, she would tor ish-veh abundantly regret ra au had lehm-tor maf. Mrs. Gardiner pa' nash wak reminded elizabeth t' ish-veh ugaya fundik ik gentleman, heh required ro'fori; heh elizabeth had such tor satau u' lau rather mazhiv-kur-tor contentment tor ish-veh ezyet do tor herself. Ish-veh apparent partiality had subsided, ish-veh attentions vesh' abru', au vesh' wuh admirer t' ein veh else. Elizabeth vesh' tun-tor hiyet tor gla-tor ish-veh ek', tonk'peh she kupi gla-tor ish-veh heh kitau t' ish-veh rik' tukh kusut. Ish-veh khaf-spol had vesh' tonk'peh slightly estuhl, heh ish-veh vanity vesh' satisfied k' believing ik _she_ would ma vesh' ish-veh goh dvel, had fortune permitted ish-veh. Wuh sudden prai t' lehkuh thousand plesh-tor vesh' wuh danik remarkable sem-rik t' wuh nu'ri t'sai tor ik au vesh' i' rendering himself agreeable; tonk'peh elizabeth, lehkuh pa'shik-sighted sos'eh svi' nash nuf do svi' charlotte’s, did ri quarrel k' ish-veh na' ish-veh istaya t' tikopah. Nothing, fi' wuh contrary, kupi nam-tor weht malatik; heh, du' kup tor suppose ik ish-veh kodona ish-veh wuh zamu struggles tor relinquish ish-veh, she vesh' pok tor kal-tor ish-veh wuh kau-bosh heh desirable thon-tor na' fi', heh kupi maut sincerely istaya ish-veh kunli. Ek' nash vesh' nafai tor mrs. Gardiner; heh, po' relating wuh circumstances, she thus went fi': --“i am i' convinced, t'nash-veh tal-kam ezyet, ik i ma worla vesh' mau svi' ashaya; na' had i really veshtau ik pure heh elevating shaukaush, i dang na' la' detest ish-veh maut ahm, heh istaya ish-veh ek' manner t' ek'rasah. Tonk'peh t'nash-veh feelings nam-tor ri goh cordial na' _him_, au nam-tor kauk impartial na' din-tor sa-te'kru. I fam yehat talal si' ik i fnu-ven ish-veh na' ek', il ik i am svi' wuh least unwilling tor nah-tor ish-veh wuh maut rom wihfelau t' ko-kan. Tra' mokuhlek nam-tor rai ashaya svi' ek' nash. T'nash-veh watchfulness has vesh' effectual; heh hi i dang certainly nam-tor wuh weht eku'ki vel tor ek' t'nash-veh acquaintance, vesh' i distractedly svi' ashaya k' ish-veh, i fam yehat leralmin ik i regret t'nash-veh comparative insignificance. Importance lau sometimes nam-tor purchased nuh' dearly. Kitty heh lydia nem-tor ish-veh defection mau weht tor khaf-spol do i tor. Au nam-tor nu'ri svi' wuh yut t' wuh panu, heh ri wi tu'ash tor wuh mortifying conviction ik handsome nu'ri sasu bolau ma vel tor ha-tor fi' u' muhl u' wuh eiktra.” [illustration: “fi' wuh kaiden” ] chapter xxvii. [illustration] k' rai greater pavek do aifa svi' wuh longbourn skan, heh vathru diversified k' pi' mesakh wuh lates-tor tor meryton, sometimes kitork heh sometimes samu, did january heh february be' dvun maf. March vesh' tor nem-tor elizabeth tor hunsford. She had ri palikauk nahp maut seriously t' going thither; tonk'peh charlotte, she ak afer-tor, vesh' depending fi' wuh dotor, heh she gradually oren-tor tor panah-tor ish-veh herself k' greater sanosh u' muhl u' greater certainty. Absence had increased ish-veh aitlun t' seeing charlotte va'ashiv, heh kobatau ish-veh spa'ash t' mr. Collins. Tra' vesh' novelty svi' wuh scheme; heh u', k' such wuh ko-mekh heh such uncompanionable ko-kai, ha-kel kupi ri nam-tor faultless, wuh pi' rubah vesh' ri unwelcome na' its sha' sake. Wuh halovaya would, moreover, mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh wuh peep na' jane; heh, svi' pen, u' wuh wak drew be', she would ma vesh' maut sorry na' sovek vohtaya. Kanok-vei, however, went fi' smoothly, heh vesh' t'forti settled fupa s' charlotte’s wuh'rak lubesan. She vesh' tor sailau osu william heh ish-veh dahr ko-fu. Wuh improvement t' spending wuh mu-yor svi' london vesh' hau svi' wak, heh wuh dotor became u' buhfik u' dotor kupi nam-tor. Wuh goh kusut vesh' svi' leaving ish-veh sa-mekh, vi would certainly din-tor ish-veh, heh vi, lu sarlah ish-veh tor wuh sfek, ni pi' tishau ish-veh going, ik au var-tor ish-veh tor kitau tor ish-veh, heh siyah ugau tor kilko-srashiv ish-veh nuhm. Wuh rom-halan svi' herself heh mr. Wickham vesh' perfectly friendly; fi' ish-veh vla kauk weht. Ish-veh la' pursuit kupi ri tor ish-veh yen-tor ik elizabeth had vesh' wuh wuh'rak tor teporilau heh tor nazh ish-veh attention, wuh wuh'rak tor shroi heh tor pity, wuh wuh'rak tor nam-tor krol-tor; heh svi' ish-veh manner t' nufai-tor ish-veh adieu, wishing ish-veh kanok tizh'es, reminding ish-veh t' ra she vesh' tor gish svi' t'sai catherine de bourgh, heh trusting ish-veh opinion t' ish-veh--ish-veh opinion t' kanok-veh--would kwon-hau-ov coincide, tra' vesh' wuh solicitude, wuh eku'ko, if she olau bolau ek'wak attach ish-veh tor ish-veh k' wuh danik sincere fudau; heh she parted s' ish-veh convinced, ik, whether telik il single, au bolau kwon-hau-ov nam-tor ish-veh model t' wuh amiable heh pleasing. Ish-veh katravahsu-travellers wuh thurai gad vesh' ri t' wuh ves tor tor ish-veh nah-tor ish-veh lehkuh agreeable. Osu william lucas, heh ish-veh ko-fu maria, wuh rom-humoured ko-kan, tonk'peh u' herbosh-headed u' himself, had nothing tor leralmin ik kupi nam-tor don khaf-spol, heh vesh' shroi tor k' pa' u' mau delight u' wuh rattle t' wuh chaise. Elizabeth ashau absurdities, tonk'peh she had fainu osu william’s nuh' wu. Au kupi var-tor ish-veh nothing uzh t' wuh wonders t' ish-veh presentation heh knighthood; heh ish-veh civilities vesh' worn si', spo' ish-veh ro'fori. Ish-veh vesh' wuh halovaya t' goh dah-leh-kehkuh miles, heh au began ish-veh ni lehkuh-mal u' tor nam-tor svi' gracechurch yut k' aru. U' au drove tor mr. Gardiner’s svep, jane vesh' na' wuh bestan-tvi-shal krani watching ish-veh lashan: lu au svi-tor wuh tvur, she vesh' tra' tor welcome au, heh elizabeth, looking earnestly svi' ish-veh limuk, vesh' sanoi tor gla-tor ish-veh healthful heh lovely u' ek'wak. Fi' wuh kaiden vesh' wuh vus t' pi' sa-kan heh ko-kan, t'vi eagerness na' ish-veh krei’s appearance would ri kal-tor au tor bek-tor svi' wuh bestan-tvi-shal, heh t'vi shyness, u' au had ri gla-tor ish-veh na' wuh twelvemonth, prevented ish-veh coming weh-neik. Ek' vesh' mak heh kindness. Wuh gad be' dvun-tor danik pleasantly maf; wuh asal svi' bustle heh shopping, heh wuh khru na' veh t' wuh theatres. Elizabeth yi contrived tor hayal-tor k' ish-veh ezyet. Ish-veh wuh'rak subject vesh' ish-veh ko-kai; heh she vesh' weht grieved do astonished tor zhu-tor, svi' kilko tor ish-veh minute inquiries, ik hi jane kwon-hau-ov struggled tor nenikaya ish-veh tam'a, tra' vesh' wak-krus t' dejection. Ish-veh vesh' reasonable, however, tor rok ik au would ri fator wu. Mrs. Gardiner mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh wuh particulars isha t' din-tor bingley’s yaret svi' gracechurch yut, heh ashiv-tor conversations occurring na' natya wak svi' jane heh herself, if skan-tor ik wuh former had, s' ish-veh khaf-spol, putan-tor abru wuh acquaintance. Mrs. Gardiner yi rallied ish-veh ko-bath fi' wickham’s desertion, heh complimented ish-veh fi' kuvish ish-veh ni muhl. “tonk'peh, t'nash-veh tal-kam elizabeth, ” she hau, “ra wihfelau t' ko-kan nam-tor din-tor sa-te'kru? I dang nam-tor sorry tor nah-tor etwel t'hy'la mercenary.” “pray, t'nash-veh tal-kam ezyet, ra nam-tor wuh natyan svi' matrimonial tek'ik, svi' wuh mercenary heh wuh prudent dvubolek? Wilat tor discretion shaht, heh avarice palikau? Kim-shah christmas du vesh' kwes t' ish-veh marrying me, fai'ei ish-veh would nam-tor imprudent; heh i', fai'ei au nam-tor trying tor prah wuh ko-kan k' goh lehkuh thousand plesh-tor, du aitlun tor talal si' ik au nam-tor mercenary.” “kuv du dungi goh var-tor me ra wihfelau t' ko-kan din-tor sa-te'kru nam-tor, i dungau fai-tor ra tor nah-tor.” “she nam-tor wuh maut rom ves t' ko-kan, i dva-tor. I fai-tor rai klau t' ish-veh.” “tonk'peh au vlitau ish-veh ri wuh smallest attention till ish-veh sa'mekh'al’s tevakh tor ish-veh mistress t' nash fortune?” “rai--po dang au? Kuv ish-veh vesh' ri allowable na' ish-veh tor nazh-kap _my_ affections, fai'ei i had rai donku, ra occasion kupi tra' nam-tor na' tor ashaya tor wuh ko-kan ik au did ri tun pa', heh vi vesh' kaing ri donku-tor?” “tonk'peh tra' seems indelicacy svi' directing ish-veh attentions na' ish-veh ni ak po' nash pavek.” “wuh sasu svi' flakosh circumstances has ri wak na' ek' eifa sohkik decorums if vath sutra lau glantau. Kuv _she_ tor ri vel tor ish-veh, po dang _we_?” “_her_ ri objecting tor ri justify _him_. Ish-veh goh gluvau ish-veh hasu pafam svi' vel herself--kash-ral il olaya.” “muhl, ” maf-tor elizabeth, “ma ish-veh u' du dvel-tor. _he_ dungau nam-tor mercenary, heh _she_ dungau nam-tor duhik.” “rai, lizzy, ik nam-tor ra i tor _not_ dvel-tor. I dang nam-tor sorry, du fai-tor, tor nah-tor has-bosh t' wuh nu'ri sasu vi has ha-tor ni wu svi' derbyshire.” “oh, kuv ik nam-tor ek', i ma wuh maut ri donku-tor opinion t' nu'ri sasu vi ha-tor svi' derbyshire; heh ish-veh intimate t'hylara vi ha-tor svi' hertfordshire nam-tor ri mau weh-rom. I am has-bosh t' au ek'. Itaren sha-ka-ri! I am going tor-morrow wilat i dungau talal wuh sasu vi has ri veh agreeable quality, vi has neither manners il kash-ral tor recommend ish-veh. Stupid sasu nam-tor wuh goh ones don fai-tor, po' ek'.” “nem-tor tun, lizzy; ik starun savours strongly t' disappointment.” fa' au vesh' dahshau k' wuh conclusion t' wuh mavau, she had wuh ri-gishu happiness t' wuh k'waw'zhe tor sailau ish-veh sa-kuk heh ezyet svi' wuh tour t' sanosh if au proposed taking svi' wuh belaar. “etek ma ri ved satalau uf irak ish-veh dungau lesh etek, ” leralmin-tor mrs. Gardiner; “tonk'peh sos'eh, tor wuh suk'muzh.” rai scheme kupi ma vesh' weht agreeable tor elizabeth, heh ish-veh acceptance t' wuh k'waw'zhe vesh' danik pok heh grateful. “t'nash-veh tal-kam, tal-kam ezyet, ” she rapturously maf-tor, “ra delight! Ra felicity! Du mazhiv-kur-tor me sluk ha'kiv heh vigour. Adieu tor disappointment heh khaf-nafek. Ra nam-tor sasu tor kov heh suk'kunel? Oh, ra wadan t' ifis-hali etek dungau spend! Heh lu etek _do_ fun, ish-veh dungau ri nam-tor spo' vath travellers, rik' hasu kup tor mazhiv-kur-tor veh accurate idea t' sovek-vel. Etek _will_ fai-tor wilat etek ma hal-tor--etek _will_ recollect ra gla-tor etek. Suk'muzh, suk'kunel, heh pilash, dungau ri nam-tor jumbled teretuhr svi' etwel imaginations; il, lu etek attempt tor kethelvau sovek particular scene, dungi etek palikau quarrelling pa' its tomasu situation. Kal-tor _our_ wuh'rak effusions nam-tor lehkuh insupportable do eifa t' wuh generality t' travellers.” [illustration: “na' wuh svep” ] chapter xxviii. [illustration] kanok vel svi' wuh thurai gad’s halovaya vesh' uzh heh eku'ki tor elizabeth; heh ish-veh tam'a vesh' svi' wuh fupa s' t' tizh'es; na' she had gla-tor ish-veh ko-kai looking ni muhl u' tor sahaisau ek' pthak na' ish-veh muhl'es, heh wuh prospect t' ish-veh northern tour vesh' wuh ek'kayik shu-pal t' delight. Lu au losrak wuh pid fau-yut na' wuh lane tor hunsford, kanok bezhun vesh' svi' psthan t' wuh parsonage, heh kanok turning gishu tor katau ish-veh svi' zan-tor. Wuh paling t' rosings shi'sochya vesh' ish-veh krup fi' veh vla. Elizabeth abru'teruklar-ru'lut na' wuh recollection t' ek' ik she had puzhu-tor t' its inhabitants. Na' wu-vath wuh parsonage vesh' discernible. Wuh bah-ker sloping tor wuh fau-yut, wuh kelek standing svi' ish-veh, wuh yar-kur pales heh wuh laurel labah, kanok-vei afsakau au vesh' arriving. Mr. Collins heh charlotte saudau na' wuh svep, heh wuh carriage pehkau na' wuh pi' temep, if pufulag-tor k' wuh pen krus-kov lates tor wuh kelek, amidst wuh nods heh abru'teruklar-ru'lut t' wuh bosh party. Svi' wuh moment au vesh' ek' s' wuh chaise, rejoicing na' wuh glan t' tik vath. Mrs. Collins welcomed ish-veh t'hy'la k' wuh liveliest sanosh, heh elizabeth vesh' weht heh weht satisfied k' coming, lu she afer-tor herself ni affectionately poprah. Gla-tor ish-veh instantly ik ish-veh krei’s manners vesh' ri rubitau k' ish-veh kal'i'farr: ish-veh hotorik civility vesh' aishan ra ish-veh had vesh'; heh au detained ish-veh ein minutes na' wuh temep tor zhu-tor heh satisfy ish-veh inquiries po' ek' ish-veh skan. Au vesh' yi, k' rai vath vohtaya do ish-veh pointing si' wuh neatness t' wuh entrance, taken vi' wuh kelek; heh u' ak u' au vesh' svi' wuh parlour, au welcomed au wuh dahr wak, k' ostentatious formality, tor ish-veh humble abode, heh punctually ashiv-tor ek' ish-veh ko-telsu’s nufau t' refreshment. Elizabeth vesh' dator tor gla-tor ish-veh svi' ish-veh glory; heh she kupi ri gol'nev fancying ik svi' displaying wuh rom proportion t' wuh tvi-shal, its pulva, heh its furniture, au addressed himself wa' tor ish-veh, u' kuv wishing tor tor ish-veh olau ra she had pakik svi' refusing ish-veh. Tonk'peh hi kanok-vei seemed pu heh kel'o, she vesh' ri kup tor gratify ish-veh k' sovek spes-tevan t' repentance; heh rather glazhau k' wonder na' ish-veh t'hy'la, ik she kupi ma ni cheerful wuh sov k' such wuh besu. Lu mr. Collins leralmin-tor sovek-vel t' if ish-veh ko-telsu lau reasonably nam-tor kafusik, if certainly vesh' ri seldom, she involuntarily da-tor ish-veh bezhun fi' charlotte. Wuh'wak il dah'wak she kupi discern wuh faint blush; tonk'peh svi' paik charlotte wisely did ri zhu-tor. Po' sitting wu hiyet tor krol-tor kanok ua'mrki t' furniture svi' wuh tvi-shal, s' wuh sideboard tor wuh fender, tor mazhiv-kur-tor wuh khrosahp t' ish-veh halovaya, heh t' ek' ik had pavesh-tor svi' london, mr. Collins invited au tor nem-tor wuh stroll svi' wuh bah-ker, if vesh' suk heh muhl laid si', heh tor wuh sokasitaya t' if au attended himself. Tor ar'kadan svi' ish-veh bah-ker vesh' veh t' ish-veh danik respectable pleasures; heh elizabeth krol-tor wuh a'fic t' countenance k' if charlotte variben t' wuh healthfulness t' wuh tusok, heh puma she kastorau ish-veh u' mau u' tor-yehat. La', leading wuh yut k'fai kanok lates heh tuhs lates, heh scarcely allowing au wuh tvi-wak tor utter wuh krol-tor au ya'akash na', kanok zan-tor vesh' sasfekau k' wuh minuteness if losrak vaksur entirely za'. Au kupi su'etek wuh vunai svi' kanok kharat, heh kupi var-tor uf wehk lap tra' vesh' svi' wuh danik irak clump. Tonk'peh t' ek' wuh zan-tor if ish-veh bah-ker, il if wuh shasol il wuh kingdom kupi boast, rim vesh' tor nam-tor tcok'at k' wuh prospect t' rosings, afforded k' wuh sharu svi' wuh lap ik bordered wuh shi'sochya nearly mesyutik wuh khom t' ish-veh kelek. Ish-veh vesh' wuh handsome iyik kelek, muhl situated fi' rising solektra. S' ish-veh bah-ker, mr. Collins would ma pufulag-tor au pauk ish-veh dahkuh ne-yartra; tonk'peh wuh t'sai, ri having ash'el tor snagel wuh hafau t' wuh wan-kur le-su, da-tor pla'; heh du' osu william accompanied ish-veh, charlotte nem-tor ish-veh ko-kai heh t'hy'la abru' wuh kelek, extremely muhl sanoi, probably, ki' wuh opportunity t' showing ish-veh rik' ish-veh sa-telsu’s gol'nev. Ish-veh vesh' rather pi', tonk'peh muhl torvau heh convenient; heh kanok-vei vesh' fitted abru heh arranged k' wuh neatness heh tsurkan'es, t' if elizabeth mazhiv-kur-tor charlotte ek' wuh lit. Lu mr. Collins kupi nam-tor yen-tor, tra' vesh' really wuh lo'uk sov t' comfort throughout, heh k' charlotte’s evident tizh'es t' ish-veh, elizabeth supposed au bolau nam-tor k'ashiv yen-tor. She had already oren-tor ik t'sai catherine vesh' fam dvun svi' wuh shasol. Ish-veh vesh' spoken t' va'ashiv du' au vesh' na' aru-yem, lu mr. Collins hau svi', glantau, -- “ha, din-tor elizabeth, du dungi ma wuh dor t' seeing t'sai catherine de bourgh fi' wuh ensuing gad na' church, heh i bolaya ri leralmin du dungi nam-tor delighted k' ish-veh. She nam-tor ek' affability heh condescension, heh i vet ri tonk'peh du dungi nam-tor pudor-tor k' ein portion t' ish-veh beglanau lu dvin nam-tor abru'. I ma scarcely sovek vaunah svi' taran ik she dungi vinan-tor du heh t'nash-veh ko-kai maria svi' kanok k'waw'zhe k' if she dor-tor etek du' ish-veh stay la'. Ish-veh kloshai tor t'nash-veh tal-kam charlotte nam-tor sem-rik-tor. Etek aru-yokul na' rosings dah'wak kanok wehk gad, heh nam-tor worla kal-tor tor lates ha-kel. Ish-veh ladyship’s carriage nam-tor regularly ordered na' etek. I _should_ leralmin, veh t' ish-veh ladyship’s carriages, na' she has several.” “t'sai catherine nam-tor wuh maut respectable, sensible kosu, indeed, ” hau charlotte, “heh wuh danik whio'naks behsu.” “maut yeht, t'nash-veh tal-kam, ik nam-tor exactly ra i leralmin. She nam-tor wuh wihfelau t' kosu ik veh fam yehat fudau k' nuh' mau deference.” wuh khru vesh' spent chiefly svi' talking abru' hertfordshire ro'fori, heh telling va'ashiv ra had vesh' already written; heh lu ish-veh a'ing, elizabeth, svi' wuh awek'es t' ish-veh tvi-shal, had tor meditate fi-tor charlotte’s degree t' contentment, tor ken-tor ish-veh shi'yavekh svi' guiding, heh composure svi' kuvish k', ish-veh sa-telsu, heh tor nafai-tor ik ish-veh vesh' ek' ovsoh maut muhl. She had isha tor anticipate uf ish-veh yaret would be' dvun, wuh hizhuk tenour t' ish-veh tsuri employments, wuh vexatious svi-shaya t' mr. Collins, heh wuh gaieties t' ish-veh intercourse k' rosings. Wuh lively glenonaya ak settled ish-veh ek'. Pa' wuh svitan t' wuh thurai gad, u' she vesh' svi' ish-veh tvi-shal getting pok na' wuh lates, wuh sudden ralash ne' seemed tor stariben wuh bosh kelek svi' confusion; heh, po' listening wuh moment, she puzhu-tor somebody sahran upstairs svi' wuh khrashik brax, heh calling loudly po' ish-veh. She tu'ash wuh svep, heh ragel-tor maria svi' wuh landing-shi, vi, breathless k' agitation, lit'dhae, -- [illustration: “svi' conversation k' wuh t'sai” [copyright 1894 k' george allen.]] “oh, t'nash-veh tal-kam eliza! Pray tor haste heh sarlah vi' wuh dining-tvi-shal, na' tra' nam-tor such wuh glan tor nam-tor gla-tor! I dungi ri var-tor du ra ish-veh nam-tor. Tor haste, heh sarlah ne' nash moment.” elizabeth ya'akash deshkau svi' vain; maria would var-tor ish-veh nothing weht; heh ne' au sahr-tor vi' wuh dining-tvi-shal if fronted wuh lane, svi' psthan t' nash wonder; ish-veh vesh' dahkuh t'sai, stopping svi' wuh neik phaeton na' wuh bah-ker temep. “heh nam-tor nash ek'?” maf-tor elizabeth. “i gishu k'puu ik wuh pigs vesh' prah vi' wuh bah-ker, heh la' nam-tor nothing tonk'peh t'sai catherine heh ish-veh ko-fu!” “la! T'nash-veh tal-kam, ” leralmin-tor maria, ved kolaya na' wuh lafosh, “ish-veh nam-tor ri t'sai catherine. Wuh hinek t'sai nam-tor mrs. Jenkinson, vi ha-tor k' au. Wuh vath nam-tor din-tor de bourgh. Goh glazhau na' ish-veh. She nam-tor ved wuh pi' creature. Vi would ma nahp she kupi nam-tor ni wonil heh pi'!” “she nam-tor abominably snertau tor potau charlotte s' svep svi' ek' nash salan. Po tor she ri sarlah svi'?” “oh, charlotte leralmin-tor she hardly ek'wak tor. Ish-veh nam-tor wuh greatest t' favours lu din-tor de bourgh sarlah svi'.” “i spo' ish-veh appearance, ” leralmin-tor elizabeth, kwul-tor k' vath ideas. “she glazhau sickly heh tuhs. Ha, she dungi tor na' ish-veh maut muhl. She dungi tor ish-veh wuh maut proper ko-telsu.” mr. Collins heh charlotte vesh' fi' standing na' wuh temep svi' conversation k' wuh t'sai; heh osu william, tor elizabeth’s pid mutaya, vesh' stationed svi' wuh svep-sharu, svi' earnest contemplation t' wuh greatness fa' ish-veh, heh constantly bowing whenever din-tor de bourgh glazhau ik yut. Na' wu-vath tra' vesh' nothing weht tor nam-tor leralmin-tor; wuh t'sai drove fi', heh wuh vath fun-tor vi' wuh kelek. Mr. Collins rai sooner gla-tor wuh dahkuh ko-kan do au began tor congratulate au fi' ish-veh rom fortune, if charlotte danau k' letting au fai-tor ik wuh bosh party vesh' ya'akash tor aru-yokul na' rosings wuh thurai gad. [illustration: ‘t'sai catherine, leralmin-tor she, du ma putan-tor me wuh treasure.’ [_copyright 1894 k' george allen._]] chapter xxix. [illustration] mr. Collins’s triumph, svi' consequence t' nash k'waw'zhe, vesh' ovsotik. Wuh tepul t' displaying wuh grandeur t' ish-veh patroness tor ish-veh wondering visitors, heh t' letting au gla-tor ish-veh civility na' himself heh ish-veh ko-telsu, vesh' exactly ra au had istau na'; heh ik wuh opportunity t' doing ish-veh dang nam-tor putan-tor ni ak vesh' such wuh instance t' t'sai catherine’s condescension u' au fai-tor ri uf tor krol-tor hiyet. “i confess, ” leralmin-tor au, “ik i dang ri ma vesh' na' ek' ak'wikmun k' ish-veh ladyship’s asking etek fi' gad tor mon theris-masu heh spend wuh khru na' rosings. I rather gishu, s' t'nash-veh fai-tukh t' ish-veh affability, ik ish-veh would pavesh-tor. Tonk'peh vi kupi ma fa-glan-tor such wuh attention u' nash? Vi kupi ma glenonau ik etek dang poprah wuh k'waw'zhe tor aru-yokul tra' (wuh k'waw'zhe, moreover, including wuh bosh party) ni iyi po' ish-veh lashan?” “i am wuh lehkuh ak'wikmun na' ra has pavesh-tor, ” kilko-tor osu william, “s' ik fai-tukh t' ra wuh manners t' wuh lo'uk really nam-tor, if t'nash-veh situation svi' ha'kiv has kal-tor me tor prah. Pa' wuh kelek, such instances t' sohkik breeding nam-tor ri uncommon.” scarcely sovek-vel vesh' variben t' wuh bosh gad il thurai asal tonk'peh ish-veh yaret tor rosings. Mr. Collins vesh' carefully instructing au svi' ra au vesh' tor gish, ik wuh glan t' such tvi-shal, ni wehk dvinsu, heh ni splendid wuh aru-yem, lau ri wholly overpower au. Lu wuh t'sai vesh' separating na' wuh toilette, au leralmin-tor tor elizabeth, -- “ri tor tor yourself uneasy, t'nash-veh tal-kam krei, pa' ish-veh apparel. T'sai catherine nam-tor irak s' requiring ik sohk'es t' sai-vel svi' etek if shetau herself heh ko-fu. I would na'shikhau du goh tor shitau fi' whatever t' ish-veh sai-vel nam-tor superior tor wuh shom--tra' nam-tor rai occasion na' sovek-vel weht. T'sai catherine dungi ri nah-tor wuh weh-rasahkos t' du na' hasu veling sai-vel-tor. She tishau ki' wuh distinction t' lan korsau.” du' au vesh' sai-vel-tor, sarlah ish-veh dahkuh il rehkuh wak tor ish-veh natya svep, tor recommend ish-veh hasu sahris, u' t'sai catherine maut mau kluchi tor nam-tor potau waiting na' ish-veh aru-yem. Such formidable khrosahp t' ish-veh ladyship, heh ish-veh manner t' living, ved koltha maria lucas, vi had vesh' pi' nam-tor-tor tor apc'koik; heh she glazhau fa'rak tor ish-veh ragtaya na' rosings k' u' mau apprehension u' ish-veh sa-mekh had ovsoh tor ish-veh presentation na' st. James’s. U' wuh igen-va vesh' tok-ti, au had wuh vaksurik lates t' pa' ulef wuh mile mes' wuh shi'sochya. Kanok shi'sochya has its vaksur heh its prospects; heh elizabeth gla-tor mau tor nam-tor sanoi k', hi she kupi ri nam-tor svi' such raptures u' mr. Collins gishu wuh scene tor vi'le-esh-tor, heh vesh' tonk'peh slightly dau k' ish-veh enumeration t' wuh krani svi' khom t' wuh kelek, heh ish-veh relation t' ra wuh glazing altogether had originally kodona osu lewis de bourgh. Lu au she-tor wuh ash-tor tor wuh tvur, maria’s vikayek vesh' kanok moment increasing, heh kauk osu william did ri glazhau perfectly hayal. Elizabeth’s courage did ri vravshau ish-veh. She had puzhu-tor nothing t' t'sai catherine ik stariben ish-veh awful s' sovek wehtsuri talents il miraculous virtue, heh wuh mere stateliness t' donku heh lan she nahp she kupi toglantausu rik' trepidation. S' wuh entrance tvur, t' if mr. Collins sasfekau, k' wuh rapturous sov, wuh tok-ti proportion heh shahtau fanet, au zahal-tor wuh dvinsu k'fai wuh antechamber tor wuh tvi-shal wilat t'sai catherine, ish-veh ko-fu, heh mrs. Jenkinson vesh' sitting. Ish-veh ladyship, k' lo'uk condescension, arose tor poprah au; heh u' mrs. Collins had settled ish-veh k' ish-veh sa-telsu ik wuh office t' ragtaya dang nam-tor ish-veh, ish-veh vesh' performed svi' wuh proper manner, rik' sovek t' eifa apologies heh itaren if au would ma nahp bolayatik. Svi' spite t' having vesh' na' st. James’s, osu william vesh' ni completely putesha k' wuh grandeur surrounding ish-veh, ik au had tonk'peh aishan courage hiyet tor tor wuh maut neik kes-wun, heh nem-tor ish-veh ku-san rik' taran wuh zhit; heh ish-veh ko-fu, koltha siyah s' ish-veh kash-ral, hayal-tor fi' wuh rihk t' ish-veh ku-san, ri fai-tor if yut tor glazhau. Elizabeth afer-tor herself ved kaik tor wuh scene, heh kupi glantau wuh rehkuh t'sai fa' ish-veh composedly. T'sai catherine vesh' wuh ha-vol, suk kosu, k' strongly-pu'ulidau features, if lau wuh'wak ma vesh' handsome. Ish-veh sov vesh' ri conciliating, il vesh' ish-veh manner t' receiving au such u' tor tor ish-veh visitors yen-tor ish-veh inferior lan. She vesh' ri rendered formidable k' silence: tonk'peh whatever she leralmin-tor vesh' spoken svi' ni authoritative wuh molu u' pu'ulidau ish-veh shal-importance, heh katau mr. Wickham iyi tor elizabeth’s kashek; heh, s' wuh glantaya t' wuh gad altogether, she pudva-tor t'sai catherine tor nam-tor exactly ra au had represented. Lu, po' examining wuh ko-mekh, svi' t'vi countenance heh deportment she ak afer-tor ein resemblance t' mr. Darcy, she da-tor ish-veh bezhun fi' wuh ko-fu, she kupi siyah ma hau svi' maria’s astonishment na' ish-veh hasu ni wonil heh ni pi'. Tra' vesh' neither svi' khlop il limuk sovek likeness svi' wuh t'sai. Din-tor de bourgh vesh' spoh heh sickly: ish-veh features, hi ri eiktra, vesh' insignificant; heh she stariben maut pi', kaula svi' wuh neik spes, tor mrs. Jenkinson, svi' t'vi appearance tra' vesh' nothing remarkable, heh vi vesh' entirely engaged svi' listening tor ra she leralmin-tor, heh placing wuh gluvayek svi' wuh proper kharat fa' ish-veh bezhun. Po' sitting wuh zamu minutes, au vesh' ek' satau tor veh t' wuh krani tor krol-tor wuh zan-tor, mr. Collins attending au tor sasfekau its beauties, heh t'sai catherine kindly informing au ik ish-veh vesh' mau weh-rom don looking na' svi' wuh belaar. Wuh aru-yem vesh' exceedingly handsome, heh tra' vesh' ek' wuh dvinsu, heh ek' wuh ua'mrki t' math if mr. Collins had ugau; heh, u' au had likewise fa-ariben, au nem-tor ish-veh ku-san na' wuh lanet t' wuh pasu, k' ish-veh ladyship’s aitlun, heh glazhau u' kuv au olau ik ha'kiv kupi furnish nothing greater. Au skrim-tor heh ate heh krol-tor k' delighted alacrity; heh kanok dish vesh' commended wuh'rak k' ish-veh, heh yi k' osu william, vi vesh' i' hiyet recovered tor vava whatever ish-veh sa-fu-svi'-tor-gav leralmin-tor, svi' wuh manner if elizabeth wondered t'sai catherine kupi lesh. Tonk'peh t'sai catherine seemed gratified k' ish-veh mauyik admiration, heh mazhiv-kur-tor danik gracious abru'teruklar-ru'lut, wa' lu sovek dish fi' wuh pasu skan-tor wuh novelty tor au. Wuh party did ri tanilau mau conversation. Elizabeth vesh' pok tor stariben whenever tra' vesh' wuh sharu, tonk'peh she vesh' hayal-tor svi' charlotte heh din-tor de bourgh--wuh former t' ik vesh' engaged svi' listening tor t'sai catherine, heh wuh latter leralmin-tor ri wuh zhit tor ish-veh ek' wuh dinnertime. Mrs. Jenkinson vesh' chiefly employed svi' watching uf pi' din-tor de bourgh ate, pressing ish-veh tor ar'kadan ein vath dish heh fearing she vesh' indisposed. Maria nahp speaking s' wuh deshker, heh wuh gentlemen did nothing tonk'peh yokul heh krol-tor. Lu wuh t'sai fun-tor tor wuh bestan-tvi-shal, tra' vesh' pi' tor nam-tor ovsoh tonk'peh tor zhu-tor t'sai catherine variben, if she did rik' sovek intermission till mon sarlah svi', delivering ish-veh opinion fi' kanok subject svi' ni decisive wuh manner u' skan-tor ik she vesh' ri nam-tor-tor ki' ish-veh judgment controverted. She inquired vi' charlotte’s ka'kelik concerns familiarly heh minutely, heh mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh wuh lo'uk deal t' na'shikh u' tor wuh management t' au ek'; var-tor ish-veh uf kanok-vei ought tor nam-tor pakhartau svi' ni pi' wuh skan u' ish-veh, heh instructed ish-veh u' tor wuh tun t' ish-veh aushfa heh ish-veh poultry. Elizabeth afer-tor ik nothing vesh' ne'rak nash lo'uk t'sai’s attention if kupi furnish ish-veh k' wuh occasion na' dictating tor vath. Svi' wuh tvi-wak t' ish-veh discourse k' mrs. Collins, she addressed wuh vuhna'es t' deshkau tor maria heh elizabeth, tonk'peh wa' tor wuh latter, t' t'vi tersaya she fai-tor wuh least, heh vi, she glantau tor mrs. Collins, vesh' wuh maut genteel, takov ves t' ko-kan. She ya'akash ish-veh na' natya wak uf wehk ko-kai she had, whether au vesh' older il younger do herself, whether sovek t' au vesh' kesik tor nam-tor telik, whether au vesh' handsome, wilat au had vesh' educated, ra carriage ish-veh sa-mekh potau, heh ra had vesh' ish-veh ko-mekh’s maiden ahm? Elizabeth olau ek' wuh impertinence t' ish-veh deshkau, tonk'peh kilko-tor au maut composedly. T'sai catherine yi glantau, -- “ish-veh sa-mekh’s estate nam-tor entailed fi' mr. Collins, i nah-tor? Na' ish-veh sake, ” turning tor charlotte, “i am glad t' ish-veh; tonk'peh vathru gla-tor nash-veh rai occasion na' entailing estates s' wuh kotik zehl. Ish-veh vesh' ri nahp bolayatik svi' osu lewis de bourgh’s skan. Tor du mavau heh uralau, din-tor bennet?” “wuh pi'.” “oh yi--ein wak il vath etek dungau nam-tor kunli tor zhu-tor du. Etwel instrument nam-tor wuh capital veh, probably superior tor ---- du dungau ar'kadan ish-veh ein gad. Tor ish-veh ko-kai mavau heh uralau?” “veh t' au tor.” “po did ri du ek' oren-tor? Du ought ek' ki' oren-tor. Wuh din-tor webbs ek' mavau, heh ish-veh sa-mekh has ri ni rom wuh income u' ish-veh. Tor du bes-tor?” “rai, mokov.” “ra, rim t' du?” “ri veh.” “ik nam-tor maut flekh. Tonk'peh i suppose du had rai opportunity. Ish-veh ko-mekh dang ma taken du tor kahr kanok sikar na' wuh rufai t' trensu.” “t'nash-veh ko-mekh would ma rai objection, tonk'peh t'nash-veh sa-mekh fnu-ven london.” “has ish-veh governess losrak du?” “etek worla had sovek governess.” “rai governess! Uf vesh' ik tor-yehat? Kaukuh daughters katau abru na' ha-kel rik' wuh governess! I worla puzhu-tor t' such wuh vel. Ish-veh ko-mekh bolau ma vesh' ved wuh kafeh tor ish-veh education.” elizabeth kupi hardly gol'nev smiling, u' she assured ish-veh ik had ri vesh' wuh nuf. “yi vi saven-tor du? Vi attended tor du? Rik' wuh governess, du bolau ma vesh' neglected.” “tcok'at k' ein skan, i dva-tor etek vesh'; tonk'peh such t' etek u' istau tor oren-tor worla aitlu wuh tvai. Etek vesh' kwon-hau-ov kastorau tor telv-tor, heh had ek' wuh trensu ik vesh' bolayatik. Eifa vi dvel-tor tor nam-tor idle certainly lau.” “ay, rai vet: tonk'peh ik nam-tor ra wuh governess dungi prevent; heh kuv i had fainu ish-veh ko-mekh, i dang ma na'shikhau ish-veh danik strenuously tor engage veh. I kwon-hau-ov leralmin ik nothing nam-tor tor nam-tor ovsoh svi' education rik' br'xan heh regular instruction, heh kling tonk'peh wuh governess mokuhlek mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh. Ish-veh nam-tor wonderful uf wehk skan i ma vesh' wuh tvai t' supplying svi' ik yut. I am kwon-hau-ov glad tor prah wuh nu'ri person muhl shitau si'. Kehkuh ko-bath t' mrs.
