Jenkinson nam-tor danik delightfully situated k'fai t'nash-veh tvai; heh ish-veh vesh' tonk'peh wuh vath gad ik i recommended wuh'ashiv nu'ri person, vi vesh' goh accidentally mentioned tor me, heh wuh skan nam-tor ved delighted k' ish-veh. Mrs. Collins, did i var-tor du t' t'sai metcalfe’s calling za-gad tor itaren me? She tal-tor din-tor pope wuh treasure. ‘t'sai catherine, ’ leralmin-tor she, ‘du ma putan-tor me wuh treasure.’ nam-tor sovek t' ish-veh younger ko-kai si', din-tor bennet?” “ha, ma’am, ek'.” “ek'! Ra, ek' kaukuh si' na' wuh'wak? Maut shaik! Heh du goh wuh dahr. Wuh younger ones si' fa' wuh tela'at nam-tor telik! Ish-veh younger ko-kai bolau nam-tor maut nu'ri?” “ha, t'nash-veh youngest nam-tor ri leh-sheh. Sos'eh _she_ nam-tor bosh nu'ri tor nam-tor mau svi' apc'koik. Tonk'peh really, ma’am, i nah-tor ish-veh would nam-tor maut lerash fi-tor younger ko-kai ik au dang ri ma ish-veh thresh t' shila'es heh amusement, fai'ei wuh tela'at lau ri ma wuh tvai il inclination tor marry lehkuh-mal. Wuh kim-shah pukeshta has u' rom wuh gas'rak tor wuh pleasures t' youth u' wuh wuh'rak. Heh tor nam-tor potau pla' fi' _such_ wuh dvubolek! I nah-tor ish-veh would ri nam-tor maut kesik tor promote sisterly affection il delicacy t' kashek.” “fi-tor t'nash-veh zhit, ” leralmin-tor ish-veh ladyship, “du mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh opinion maut decidedly na' ni nu'ri wuh person. Pray, ra nam-tor ish-veh ya'shakhuv?” “k' rehkuh younger ko-kai grown abru, ” kilko-tor elizabeth, smiling, “ish-veh ladyship mokuhlek hardly gish me tor sha' ish-veh.” t'sai catherine seemed ved astonished na' ri receiving wuh kharik kilko-srashiv; heh elizabeth suspected herself tor nam-tor wuh wuh'rak creature vi had ek'wak dared tor trifle k' ni mau dignified impertinence. “du fam yehat nam-tor weht do dah-leh, i am sure, --therefore du bolaya ri ip-sut ish-veh ya'shakhuv.” “i am ri veh-heh-dah-leh.” lu wuh gentlemen had hau au, heh theris-masu vesh' abru', wuh nop pasu vesh' shitau. T'sai catherine, osu william, heh mr. Heh mrs. Collins hayal-tor ne' tor quadrille; heh u' din-tor de bourgh dvel-tor tor mavau na' cassino, wuh dahkuh ko-kan had wuh dor t' assisting mrs. Jenkinson tor tor abru ish-veh party. Ish-veh pasu vesh' superlatively stupid. Scarcely wuh zhit-shaya vesh' uttered ik did ri relate tor wuh zhagra, kaula lu mrs. Jenkinson sagluvau ish-veh ptha t' din-tor de bourgh’s hasu nuh' fal il nuh' samu, il having nuh' mau il nuh' pi' ta'hal. Wuh lo'uk deal weht be' dvun-tor na' wuh vath pasu. T'sai catherine vesh' paik speaking--fupa s' wuh lafosh t' wuh rehkuh vath, il relating ein anecdote t' herself. Mr. Collins vesh' employed svi' agreeing tor kanok-vei ish-veh ladyship leralmin-tor, thanking ish-veh na' kanok aluk au skil-tor, heh apologizing kuv au nahp au skil-tor nuh' wehk. Osu william did ri leralmin mau. Au vesh' storing ish-veh vokaya k' anecdotes heh thol ahm. Lu t'sai catherine heh ish-veh ko-fu had mavau u' wu u' au dvel-tor, wuh pasu vesh' pushau abru, wuh carriage vesh' nufau tor mrs. Collins, gratefully nar-tor, heh iyi ordered. Wuh party yi hoknau pauk wuh yon tor zhu-tor t'sai catherine satalau ra igen-va au vesh' ki' fi' wuh morrow. S' aifa instructions au vesh' summoned k' wuh lashan t' wuh coach; heh k' wehk starun t' thankfulness fi' mr. Collins’s vla, heh u' wehk ovalau fi' osu william’s, au trashu. U' ak u' au had driven s' wuh svep, elizabeth vesh' puvutau fi' k' ish-veh krei tor mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh opinion t' ek' ik she had gla-tor na' rosings, if, na' charlotte’s sake, she tor weht favourable do ish-veh really vesh'. Tonk'peh ish-veh commendation, hi costing ish-veh ein trouble, kupi k' rai tvai satisfy mr. Collins, heh au vesh' maut ak obliged tor nem-tor ish-veh ladyship’s krol vi' ish-veh sha' el'ru. [illustration] chapter xxx. [illustration] osu william stayed goh wuh wehk gad na' hunsford; tonk'peh ish-veh yaret vesh' wu hiyet tor convince ish-veh t' ish-veh ko-fu’s hasu danik comfortably settled, heh t' ish-veh possessing such wuh sa-telsu heh such wuh behsu u' vesh' ri k'ashiv ragel-tor k'. Du' osu william vesh' k' au, mr. Collins vaikau ish-veh asal tor driving ish-veh si' svi' ish-veh gig, heh showing ish-veh wuh shasol: tonk'peh lu au went maf, wuh bosh skan fun-tor tor ish-veh tsuri employments, heh elizabeth vesh' itar-bosh tor talal ik au did ri gla-tor weht t' ish-veh krei k' wuh alteration; na' wuh chief t' wuh wak svi' asal-yem heh aru-yem vesh' i' be' dvun-tor k' ish-veh either na' ar'kadan svi' wuh bah-ker, il svi' telvan heh kitaun, heh looking s' krani svi' ish-veh sha' dunap tvi-shal, if fronted wuh fau-yut. Wuh tvi-shal svi' if wuh t'sai hayal-tor vesh' pla'rak. Elizabeth palikauk had rather wondered ik charlotte dang ri prefer wuh dining parlour na' tsuri nam-tor-tor; ish-veh vesh' wuh weh-rom sized tvi-shal, heh had wuh pleasanter pulva: tonk'peh she ak gla-tor ik ish-veh t'hy'la had wuh marom utvau na' ra she did, na' mr. Collins would undoubtedly ma vesh' mau lehkuh svi' ish-veh sha' ha-shal had au hayal-tor svi' veh kaing lively; heh she mazhiv-kur-tor charlotte lit na' wuh arrangement. S' wuh bestan-tvi-shal au kupi distinguish nothing svi' wuh lane, heh vesh' indebted tor mr. Collins na' wuh fai-tukh t' ra carriages went bi', heh uf k'ashiv wa' din-tor de bourgh drove k' svi' ish-veh phaeton, if au worla vravshau coming tor inform au t', hi ish-veh pavesh-tor siyah kanok gad. She ri unfrequently pehkau na' wuh parsonage, heh had wuh zamu minutes’ conversation k' charlotte, tonk'peh vesh' scarcely ek'wak fakovau fi' tor prah si'. Maut zamu gad be' dvun-tor svi' if mr. Collins did ri lates tor rosings, heh ri wehk svi' if ish-veh ko-telsu did ri nah-tor ish-veh bolayatik tor hal-tor likewise; heh till elizabeth recollected ik tra' lau nam-tor vath skan livings tor nam-tor sashitau t', she kupi ri ken-tor wuh sacrifice t' ni wehk wadan. I' heh yi au vesh' pudor-tor k' wuh vutau s' ish-veh ladyship, heh nothing stron-tor ish-veh glantaya ik vesh' be' dvun-tor svi' wuh tvi-shal du' aifa yaretau. She linisau vi' ish-veh employments, glazhau na' ish-veh ar'kadan, heh na'shikhau au tor tor ish-veh differently; afer-tor lafot k' wuh arrangement t' wuh furniture, il patal-tor wuh housemaid svi' negligence; heh kuv she nar-tor sovek refreshment, seemed tor tor ish-veh goh na' wuh sake t' finding si' ik mrs. Collins’s joints t' kahm vesh' nuh' suk na' ish-veh skan. Elizabeth ak pakashogau, ik hi nash lo'uk t'sai vesh' ri svi' wuh kadvin t' wuh sochya na' wuh county, she vesh' wuh danik torupik magistrate svi' ish-veh sha' parish, wuh minutest concerns t' if vesh' lesh tor ish-veh k' mr. Collins; heh whenever sovek t' wuh cottagers vesh' sashitau tor nam-tor quarrelsome, discontented, il nuh' ri donku-tor, she sallied forth vi' wuh pi'kahr tor settle ish-veh natyan, silence ish-veh complaints, heh scold au vi' kril'es heh plenty. [illustration: “au worla vravshau tor inform au” ] wuh entertainment t' dining na' rosings vesh' ashiv-tor pa' dah'wak wuh wehk gad; heh, allowing na' wuh pak t' osu william, heh tra' hasu goh veh nop-pasu svi' wuh khru, kanok such entertainment vesh' wuh counterpart t' wuh wuh'rak. Ish-veh vath engagements vesh' zamu, u' wuh style t' living t' wuh neighbourhood svi' paik vesh' mesakh wuh collinses’ pulau. Nash, however, vesh' rai ek'rasah tor elizabeth, heh fi-tor wuh bosh she spent ish-veh wak comfortably hiyet: tra' vesh' ulef wadan t' vaksurik conversation k' charlotte, heh wuh igen-va vesh' ni tok-ti na' wuh wak t' tevun, ik she had k'ashiv lo'uk tizh'es s' svep. Ish-veh favourite lates, heh wilat she frequently went du' wuh vath vesh' calling fi' t'sai catherine, vesh' bi' wuh tu'ash pi'laptra if rihkau ik vla t' wuh shi'sochya, wilat tra' vesh' wuh nice rau-tor yut, if kling seemed tor tala tonk'peh herself, heh wilat she olau mesakh wuh pulau t' t'sai catherine’s curiosity. Svi' nash hizhuk yut wuh wuh'rak fortnight t' ish-veh yaret ak be' dvun-tor maf. Easter vesh' approaching, heh wuh wehk gad preceding ish-veh vesh' tor katau wuh haya tor wuh skan na' rosings, if svi' ni pi' wuh da-kuv bolau nam-tor yauluhk. Elizabeth had puzhu-tor, ak po' ish-veh lashan, ik mr. Darcy vesh' gishu tra' svi' wuh rivak t' wuh zamu wehk gad; heh hi tra' vesh' ri wehk t' ish-veh acquaintance ik she did ri prefer, ish-veh coming would furnish veh comparatively uzh tor glazhau na' svi' ish-veh rosings parties, heh she lau nam-tor amused svi' seeing uf hopeless din-tor bingley’s designs fi' ish-veh vesh', k' ish-veh kloshai tor ish-veh krei, na' ik au vesh' evidently destined k' t'sai catherine, vi variben t' ish-veh coming k' wuh greatest satisfaction, stariben t' ish-veh svi' zhil t' wuh k'lek admiration, heh seemed siyah reshnek tor talal ik au had already vesh' frequently gla-tor k' din-tor lucas heh herself. Ish-veh lashan vesh' ak fainu na' wuh parsonage; na' mr. Collins vesh' walking wuh bosh asal k'svi zan-tor t' wuh lodges sharu vi' hunsford lane, svi' zek ki' [illustration: “wuh gentlemen accompanied ish-veh.” [_copyright 1894 k' george allen._]] wuh earliest assurance t' ish-veh; heh, po' tor ish-veh kes-wun u' wuh carriage da-tor vi' wuh shi'sochya, hurried ha-kel k' wuh lo'uk kash-tor'es. Fi' wuh zahalik asal au hastened tor rosings tor vlitau ish-veh respects. Tra' vesh' dahkuh sa-bath t' t'sai catherine tor require au, na' mr. Darcy had katau k' ish-veh wuh shal-lan fitzwilliam, wuh younger sa-fu t' ish-veh sa-kuk, s'haile ----; heh, tor wuh lo'uk ak'wikmun t' ek' wuh party, lu mr. Collins fun-tor, wuh gentlemen accompanied ish-veh. Charlotte had gla-tor au s' ish-veh sa-telsu’s tvi-shal, mes wuh fau-yut, heh iyi sahran vi' wuh vath, var-tor wuh ko-kan ra wuh dor au lau gish, hau, -- “i lau nemaiyo, eliza, na' nash krus t' civility. Mr. Darcy would worla ma sarlah ni ak tor bek-tor fi-tor me.” elizabeth had scarcely wak tor disclaim ek' gas'rak tor wuh compliment fa' ish-veh betaya vesh' tor'pra k' wuh svep-kus-vakh, heh shortly afterwards wuh rehkuh gentlemen svi-tor wuh tvi-shal. Shal-lan fitzwilliam, vi pufulag-tor wuh yut, vesh' pa' reh-leh, ri handsome, tonk'peh svi' person heh shi'yavekh danik truly wuh gentleman. Mr. Darcy glazhau aishan u' au had vesh' nam-tor-tor tor glazhau svi' hertfordshire, vlitau ish-veh compliments, k' ish-veh tsuri reserve, tor mrs. Collins; heh whatever lau nam-tor ish-veh feelings na' ish-veh t'hy'la, ragel-tor ish-veh k' kanok appearance t' composure. Elizabeth goh courtesied tor ish-veh, rik' taran wuh zhit. Shal-lan fitzwilliam svi-tor vi' conversation directly, k' wuh readiness heh ease t' wuh muhl-bred sasu, heh variben maut pleasantly; tonk'peh ish-veh krei, po' having addressed wuh slight glantaya fi' wuh kelek heh bah-ker tor mrs. Collins, hayal-tor na' ein wak rik' speaking tor anybody. Na' wu-vath, however, ish-veh civility vesh' ni irak awakened u' tor inquire t' elizabeth po' wuh muhl'es t' ish-veh skan. She kilko-tor ish-veh svi' wuh tsuri yut; heh, po' wuh moment’s svizh, hau, -- “t'nash-veh eldest ko-kai has vesh' svi' kahr aifa rehkuh tevun-krus. Ma du worla pavesh-tor tor gla-tor ish-veh tra'?” she vesh' perfectly sensible ik au worla had: tonk'peh she istau tor gla-tor whether au would svik-tor sovek hokni'es t' ra had be' dvun-tor svi' wuh bingleys heh jane; heh she nahp au glazhau wuh pi' confused u' au kilko-tor ik au had worla vesh' ni fortunate u' tor ragel-tor din-tor bennet. Wuh subject vesh' pursued rai further, heh wuh gentlemen ak afterwards went maf. [illustration: “na' church” ] chapter xxxi. [illustration] shal-lan fitzwilliam’s manners vesh' maut mau krol-tor na' wuh parsonage, heh wuh t'sai ek' olau ik au bolau hau considerably tor wuh sanosh t' ish-veh engagements na' rosings. Ish-veh vesh' ein gad, however, fa' au poprah sovek k'waw'zhe thither, na' du' tra' vesh' visitors svi' wuh kelek au kupi ri nam-tor bolayatik; heh ish-veh vesh' ri till easter-gad, siyah wuh wehk gad po' wuh gentlemen’s lashan, ik au vesh' pudor-tor k' such wuh attention, heh yi au vesh' goh ya'akash fi' leaving church tor sarlah tra' svi' wuh khru. Na' wuh kim-shah wehk gad au had gla-tor maut pi' t' either t'sai catherine il ish-veh ko-fu. Shal-lan fitzwilliam had puvutau na' wuh parsonage weht do wuh'wak du' wuh wak, tonk'peh mr. Darcy au had goh gla-tor na' church. Wuh k'waw'zhe vesh' nar-tor, veling, heh na' wuh proper wadan au hau wuh party svi' t'sai catherine’s bestan-tvi-shal. Ish-veh ladyship poprah au civilly, tonk'peh ish-veh vesh' eiktra ik ish-veh apc'koik vesh' k' rai tvai ni acceptable u' lu she kupi prah kling else; heh she vesh', svi' kla-min, siyah engrossed k' ish-veh sa-bath, speaking tor au, wa' tor darcy, mau weht do tor sovek vath person svi' wuh tvi-shal. Shal-lan fitzwilliam seemed really glad tor gla-tor au: sovek-vel vesh' wuh welcome vas tor ish-veh na' rosings; heh mrs. Collins’s takov t'hy'la had, moreover, kum-tor ish-veh fancy maut mau. Au i' hayal-tor himself k' ish-veh, heh variben ni agreeably t' kent heh hertfordshire, t' travelling heh staying na' ha-kel, t' uzh dunap heh ralash-tanaf, ik elizabeth had worla vesh' ulef ni muhl entertained svi' ik tvi-shal fa'; heh au conversed k' ni mau tam'a heh yumaya u' tor bes-tor wuh attention t' t'sai catherine herself, u' muhl u' t' mr. Darcy. _his_ bezhun had vesh' ak heh repeatedly da-tor na' au k' wuh glazhau t' curiosity; heh ik ish-veh ladyship, po' wuh du', thresh-tor wuh olaya, vesh' weht openly nafai, na' she did ri scruple tor vutau si', -- “ra nam-tor ik du nam-tor taran, fitzwilliam? Ra nam-tor ish-veh du nam-tor talking t'? Ra nam-tor du telling din-tor bennet? Kal-tor me zhu-tor ra ish-veh nam-tor.” “etek vesh' talking t' ralash-tanaf, madam, ” leralmin-tor au, lu rai longer kup tor nan'woi wuh kilko. “t' ralash-tanaf! Yi pray stariben aloud. Ish-veh nam-tor t' ek' subjects t'nash-veh delight. I bolau ma t'nash-veh thresh svi' wuh conversation, kuv du nam-tor speaking t' ralash-tanaf. Tra' nam-tor zamu sutra svi' england, i suppose, vi ma weht yeht tizh'es t' ralash-tanaf do myself, il wuh weh-rom malatik zahvan. Kuv i had ek'wak oren-tor, i dang ma vesh' wuh lo'uk proficient. Heh ni would anne, kuv ish-veh muhl'es had kal-tor ish-veh tor apply. I am confident ik she would ma performed delightfully. Uf tor georgiana prah fi', darcy?” mr. Darcy stariben k' affectionate krol t' ish-veh ko-kai’s proficiency. “i am maut glad tor zhu-tor such wuh rom khrosahp t' ish-veh, ” leralmin-tor t'sai catherine; “heh pray var-tor ish-veh s' me, ik she fam yehat gish tor marom-tor, kuv she tor ri practise wuh lo'uk deal.” “i assure du, madam, ” au kilko-tor, “ik she tor ri bolaya such na'shikh. She practises maut constantly.” “ni mau wuh weh-rom. Ish-veh fam yehat nam-tor ovsoh nuh' mau; heh lu i thurai kitau tor ish-veh, i dungau falun ish-veh ri tor neglect ish-veh fi' sovek khrosahp. I k'ashiv var-tor nu'ri t'sai, ik rai marom'es svi' ralash-tanaf nam-tor tor nam-tor acquired rik' ek'kayik practice. I ma var-tor din-tor bennet several wak, ik she dungi worla mavau really muhl, vita she practises weht; heh hi mrs. Collins has rai instrument, she nam-tor maut welcome, u' i ma k'ashiv var-tor ish-veh, tor sarlah tor rosings kanok gad, heh mavau fi' wuh pianoforte svi' mrs. Jenkinson’s tvi-shal. She would nam-tor svi' kling’s yut, du fai-tor, svi' ik krus t' wuh kelek.” mr. Darcy glazhau wuh pi' kafusik t' ish-veh ezyet’s has-bosh-breeding, heh tor rai kilko-srashiv. Lu mon vesh' abru', shal-lan fitzwilliam reminded elizabeth t' having ugau tor mavau tor ish-veh; heh she hayal-tor ne' directly tor wuh instrument. Au drew wuh ku-san be' ish-veh. T'sai catherine shroi tor ulef wuh song, heh yi variben, u' fa', tor ish-veh vath sa-bath; till wuh latter lates-tor maf s' ish-veh, heh dvun-tor k' ish-veh tsuri deliberation na' wuh pianoforte, stationed himself ni u' tor a'fic wuh bosh zan-tor t' wuh rom performer’s countenance. Elizabeth gla-tor ra au vesh' doing, heh na' wuh wuh'rak convenient svizh da-tor tor ish-veh k' wuh kesek abru'teruklar-ru'lut, heh leralmin-tor, -- “du tvai tor koltha me, mr. Darcy, k' coming svi' ek' nash fupa s' tor zhu-tor me. Tonk'peh i dungi ri nam-tor alarmed, hi ish-veh ko-kai _does_ mavau ni muhl. Tra' nam-tor wuh stubbornness pa' me ik worla mokuhlek lesh tor nam-tor koltha na' wuh dungi t' vath. T'nash-veh courage kwon-hau-ov she-tor k' kanok attempt tor intimidate me.” “i dungau ri leralmin ik du nam-tor mistaken, ” au kilko-tor, “fai'ei du kupi ri really dva-tor me tor entertain sovek design t' alarming du; heh i ma had wuh sanosh t' ish-veh acquaintance wu hiyet tor fai-tor, ik du talal lo'uk tizh'es svi' occasionally professing opinions if, svi' kla-min, nam-tor ri ish-veh sha'.” elizabeth abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor heartily na' nash bikuv t' herself, heh leralmin-tor tor shal-lan fitzwilliam, “ish-veh krei dungi mazhiv-kur-tor du wuh maut takov notion t' me, heh saven-tor du ri tor dva-tor wuh zhit i leralmin. I am wa' unlucky svi' latva k' wuh person ni muhl kup tor sashavau t'nash-veh yeht character, svi' wuh krus t' wuh panu wilat i had rok-tor tor be' dvun myself ska' k' ein degree t' lit. Indeed, mr. Darcy, ish-veh nam-tor maut ungenerous svi' du tor mention ek' ik du fai-tor tor t'nash-veh disadvantage svi' hertfordshire--heh, mazhiv-kur-tor me trasha tor leralmin, maut impolitic nuh'--na' ish-veh nam-tor provoking me tor retaliate, heh such vel lau sasarlah u' dungi kolaya ish-veh relations tor zhu-tor.” “i am ri kwes t' du, ” leralmin-tor au, smilingly. “pray kal-tor me zhu-tor ra du ma tor accuse ish-veh t', ” maf-tor shal-lan fitzwilliam. “i dang spo' tor fai-tor uf au kloshah among ri-fainusu.” “du dungau zhu-tor, yi--tonk'peh dator na' vel maut dreadful. Wuh wuh'rak wak t' t'nash-veh ek'wak seeing ish-veh svi' hertfordshire, du bolau fai-tor, vesh' na' wuh rin'k'n--heh na' nash rin'k'n, ra tor du nah-tor au did? Au tam-tor goh kehkuh tam-tor! Ni'droi'ik nar-tor tor kusut du, tonk'peh ni ish-veh vesh'. Au tam-tor goh kehkuh tam-tor, hi gentlemen vesh' ritsuri; heh, tor t'nash-veh ac'ruth fai-tukh, weht do veh nu'ri t'sai vesh' sitting ne' svi' aitlun t' wuh tersu. Mr. Darcy, du fam yehat wafu wuh kla-min.” “i had ri na' ik wak wuh dor t' fai-tor sovek t'sai svi' wuh feretai mesakh t'nash-veh sha' party.” “yeht; heh kling mokuhlek ek'wak nam-tor puragtau svi' wuh rin'k'n-tvi-shal. Muhl, shal-lan fitzwilliam, ra tor i mavau thurai? T'nash-veh ozh bek-tor ish-veh zek.” “sos'eh, ” leralmin-tor darcy, “i dang ma judged weh-rom had i sought wuh ragtaya, tonk'peh i am has-bosh-qualified tor recommend myself tor ri-fainusu.” “dungau etek ya'akash ish-veh krei wuh utvau t' nash?” leralmin-tor elizabeth, fam dvun addressing shal-lan fitzwilliam. “dungau etek ya'akash ish-veh po wuh sasu t' kash-ral heh education, heh vi has ha-tor svi' wuh panu, nam-tor has-bosh-qualified tor recommend himself tor ri-fainusu?” “i mokuhlek kilko-srashiv ish-veh deshker, ” leralmin-tor fitzwilliam, “rik' applying tor ish-veh. Ish-veh nam-tor fai'ei au dungi ri mazhiv-kur-tor himself wuh trouble.” “i certainly ma ri wuh talent if ein sutra ma, ” leralmin-tor darcy, “t' conversing easily k' eifa i ma worla gla-tor fa'. I fam yehat kum ish-veh molu t' conversation, il saudau interested svi' ish-veh concerns, u' i k'ashiv gla-tor ovsoh.” “t'nash-veh ozh, ” leralmin-tor elizabeth, “ri tor dvun abru' nash instrument svi' wuh masterly manner if gla-tor nash-veh ni wehk kosu’s tor. Au ma ri wuh ka nekwitaya il rapidity, heh ri tor torvau wuh ka sagluvaya. Tonk'peh yi i ma kwon-hau-ov supposed ish-veh tor nam-tor t'nash-veh sha' lafot--fai'ei i would ri nem-tor wuh trouble t' practising. Ish-veh nam-tor ri ik i ri tor dva-tor _my_ ozh u' capable u' sovek vath kosu’s t' superior execution.” darcy abru'teruklar-ru'lut heh leralmin-tor, “du nam-tor perfectly gas'rak. Du ma employed ish-veh wak mau weh-rom. Kling nafai-tor tor wuh privilege t' khaf-spol du mokuhlek nah-tor sovek-vel wanting. Etek neither t' etek perform tor ri-fainusu.” la' au vesh' svi-shau k' t'sai catherine, vi shoret fai-tor ra au vesh' talking t'. Elizabeth iyi began mavaun va'ashiv. T'sai catherine betau, heh, po' listening na' wuh zamu minutes, leralmin-tor tor darcy, -- “din-tor bennet would ri mavau na' ek' amiss kuv she practised weht, heh kupi ma wuh advantage t' wuh london trensu. She has wuh maut rom notion t' fingering, hi ish-veh zahvan nam-tor ri kaik tor anne’s. Anne would ma vesh' wuh delightful performer, had ish-veh muhl'es kal-tor ish-veh tor oren-tor.” elizabeth glazhau na' darcy, tor gla-tor uf cordially au assented tor ish-veh krei’s krol: tonk'peh neither na' ik moment il na' sovek vath kupi she discern sovek symptom t' ashaya; heh s' wuh bosh t' ish-veh kloshai tor din-tor de bourgh she derived nash comfort na' din-tor bingley, ik au lau ma vesh' aishan u' kesik tor marry _her_, had she vesh' ish-veh relation. T'sai catherine fator ish-veh remarks fi' elizabeth’s performance, mixing k' au wehk instructions fi' execution heh zahvan. Elizabeth poprah au k' ek' wuh forbearance t' civility; heh na' wuh ya'akash t' wuh gentlemen hafau na' wuh instrument till ish-veh ladyship’s carriage vesh' pok tor nem-tor au ek' ha-kel. [illustration] chapter xxxii. [illustration] elizabeth vesh' sitting k' herself wuh thurai asal, heh kitaun tor jane, du' mrs. Collins heh maria vesh' hal-tor fi' business vi' wuh pi'kahr, lu she vesh' startled k' wuh mokov na' wuh svep, wuh ac'ruth glantokaya t' wuh visitor. U' she had puzhu-tor rai carriage, she nahp ish-veh ri rikesik tor nam-tor t'sai catherine; heh ne' ik apprehension vesh' putting maf ish-veh ulef-shahtau nuhm, ik she lau stron ek' impertinent deshkau, lu wuh svep tu'ash, heh tor ish-veh maut lo'uk ak'wikmun mr. Darcy, heh mr. Darcy goh, svi-tor wuh tvi-shal. Au seemed astonished nuh' fi' finding ish-veh sa'awek, heh apologized na' ish-veh vi-kwitaya, k' letting ish-veh fai-tor ik au had ken-tor ek' wuh t'sai tor nam-tor k'svi. Au yi hayal-tor ne', heh lu ish-veh inquiries po' rosings vesh' tor, seemed svi' tehvar t' sinking vi' ovus silence. Ish-veh vesh' absolutely bolayatik, therefore, tor nah-tor t' vel; heh svi' nash kefik recollecting _when_ she had gla-tor ish-veh kim-shah svi' hertfordshire, heh olaya curious tor fai-tor ra au would leralmin fi' wuh subject t' ish-veh hasty trashan, she glantau, -- “uf maut suddenly du ek' quitted netherfield kim-shah november, mr. Darcy! Ish-veh bolau ma vesh' wuh danik agreeable ak'wikmun tor mr. Bingley tor gla-tor du ek' po' ish-veh ni ak; na', kuv i recollect gas'rak, au went tonk'peh wuh gad fa'. Au heh ish-veh ko-kai vesh' muhl, i rok, lu du losrak london?” “perfectly ni, i nemaiyo.” she afer-tor ik she vesh' tor poprah rai vath kilko-srashiv; heh, po' wuh pen svizh, hau, -- “i nah-tor i ma ken-tor ik mr. Bingley has ri mau idea t' ek'wak returning tor netherfield va'ashiv?” “i ma worla puzhu-tor ish-veh leralmin ni; tonk'peh ish-veh nam-tor yesik ik au lau spend maut pi' t' ish-veh wak tra' svi' fa-wak. Au has wehk t'hylara, heh au nam-tor na' wuh wak t' ha'kiv lu t'hylara heh engagements nam-tor continually increasing.” “kuv au tvai tor nam-tor tonk'peh pi' na' netherfield, ish-veh would nam-tor weh-rom na' wuh neighbourhood ik au dang mazhiv-kur-tor abru wuh shi entirely, na' yi etek lau possibly prah wuh settled skan tra'. Tonk'peh, sos'eh, mr. Bingley did ri nem-tor wuh kelek ni mau na' wuh convenience t' wuh neighbourhood u' na' ish-veh sha', heh etek bolau gish ish-veh tor potau il quit ish-veh fi' wuh ka dvatai.” “i dang ri nam-tor ak'wikmun, ” leralmin-tor darcy, “kuv au vesh' tor mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh abru u' ak u' sovek eligible purchase nufau.” elizabeth tor rai kilko-srashiv. She vesh' kwes t' talking longer t' ish-veh t'hy'la; heh, having nothing else tor leralmin, vesh' i' satalau tor trasha wuh trouble t' finding wuh subject tor ish-veh. Au nem-tor wuh hint heh ak began k', “nash seems wuh maut kel'o kelek. T'sai catherine, i dva-tor, did wuh lo'uk deal tor ish-veh lu mr. Collins wuh'rak sarlah tor hunsford.” “i dva-tor she did--heh i am sure she kupi ri ma bestowed ish-veh kindness fi' wuh weht grateful vel.” “mr. Collins saudau maut fortunate svi' ish-veh dvel t' wuh ko-telsu.” “ha, indeed; ish-veh t'hylara lau muhl rejoice svi' ish-veh having ragel-tor k' veh t' wuh maut zamu sensible kosu vi would ma nar-tor ish-veh, il ma tor ish-veh kunli kuv au had. T'nash-veh t'hy'la has wuh marom understanding--hi i am ri ac'ruth ik i panah-tor ish-veh marrying mr. Collins u' wuh wisest vel she ek'wak did. She seems perfectly kunli, however; heh, svi' wuh prudential ta'hal, ish-veh nam-tor certainly wuh maut rom match na' ish-veh.” “ish-veh bolau nam-tor maut agreeable tor ish-veh tor nam-tor settled k'svi ni hagik wuh ir t' ish-veh sha' skan heh t'hylara.” “wuh hagik ir tor du vutau ish-veh? Ish-veh nam-tor nearly kau-leh miles.” “heh ra nam-tor kau-leh miles t' rom fau-yut? Pi' weht do ulef wuh gad’s halovaya. Ha, i vutau ish-veh wuh maut hagik ir.” “i dang worla ma panah-tor wuh ir u' veh t' wuh _advantages_ t' wuh match, ” maf-tor elizabeth. “i dang worla ma leralmin-tor mrs. Collins vesh' settled _near_ ish-veh skan.” “ish-veh nam-tor wuh skan t' ish-veh sha' attachment tor hertfordshire. Sovek-vel mesakh wuh maut neighbourhood t' longbourn, i suppose, would saudau irak.” u' au stariben tra' vesh' wuh wihfelau t' abru'teruklar-ru'lut, if elizabeth fancied she ken-tor; au bolau nam-tor supposing ish-veh tor nam-tor thinking t' jane heh netherfield, heh she blushed u' she kilko-tor, -- “i ri tor tvai tor leralmin ik wuh kosu lau ri nam-tor settled nuh' be' ish-veh skan. Wuh irak heh wuh be' bolau nam-tor tomasu, heh nerau fi' wehk varying circumstances. Wilat tra' nam-tor fortune tor tor wuh kodona t' travelling unimportant, ir shetau rai ek'rasah. Tonk'peh ik nam-tor ri wuh nuf _here_. Mr. Heh mrs. Collins ma wuh kel'o income, tonk'peh ri such wuh veh u' dungi kal-tor t' vakavik halovaya--heh i am persuaded t'nash-veh t'hy'la would ri vutau herself _near_ ish-veh skan ne' lehkuh tor _half_ wuh la' ir.” mr. Darcy drew ish-veh ku-san wuh pi' na' ish-veh, heh leralmin-tor, “_you_ fam yehat ma wuh gas'rak tor such maut karik local attachment. _you_ fam yehat ma vesh' kwon-hau-ov na' longbourn.” elizabeth glazhau ak'wikmun. Wuh gentleman veshtau ein rubah t' olaya; au drew pla' ish-veh ku-san, nem-tor wuh newspaper s' wuh pasu, heh, glancing abru' ish-veh, leralmin-tor, svi' wuh colder spes, -- “nam-tor du sanoi k' kent?” wuh pen dialogue fi' wuh subject t' wuh shasol ensued, fi' either vla hayal heh concise--heh ak shitau wuh shaht tor k' wuh entrance t' charlotte heh ish-veh ko-kai, aishan fun-tor s' ish-veh lates. Wuh _tête-à-tête_ ak'wikmun au. Mr. Darcy related wuh lafosh if had occasioned ish-veh intruding fi' din-tor bennet, heh, po' sitting wuh zamu minutes longer, rik' taran mau tor anybody, went maf. [illustration: “accompanied k' ish-veh ezyet” [_copyright 1894 k' george allen._]] “ra mokuhlek nam-tor wuh meaning t' nash?” leralmin-tor charlotte, u' ak u' au vesh' hal-tor. “t'nash-veh tal-kam eliza, au bolau nam-tor svi' ashaya k' du, il au would worla ma puvutau fi' etek svi' nash familiar yut.” tonk'peh lu elizabeth var-tor t' ish-veh silence, ish-veh did ri seem maut kesik, kauk tor charlotte’s istau, tor nam-tor wuh nuf; heh, po' vuhnauk conjectures, au kupi na' kim-shah goh suppose ish-veh yaret tor proceed s' wuh rihag'es t' finding sovek-vel tor tor, if vesh' wuh weht yesik s' wuh wak t' tevun. Ek' vunai torvukh vesh' abru'. K'svi svep tra' vesh' t'sai catherine, dunap, heh wuh billiard pasu, tonk'peh gentlemen fam yehat nam-tor kwon-hau-ov k'svi svep; heh svi' wuh nearness t' wuh parsonage, il wuh pleasantness t' wuh lates tor ish-veh, il t' wuh sutra vi ha-tor svi' ish-veh, wuh dahkuh krei afer-tor wuh temptation s' nash wak-krus t' walking thither siyah kanok gad. Au puvutau na' vuhnauk wak t' wuh asal, sometimes separately, sometimes teretuhr, heh i' heh yi accompanied k' ish-veh ezyet. Ish-veh vesh' eiktra tor au ek' ik shal-lan fitzwilliam sarlah fai'ei au had sanosh svi' ish-veh shila'es, wuh persuasion if veling recommended ish-veh fam dvun weht; heh elizabeth vesh' reminded k' ish-veh sha' satisfaction svi' hasu k' ish-veh, u' muhl u' k' ish-veh evident admiration, t' ish-veh former favourite, george wickham; heh hi, svi' comparing au, gla-tor ish-veh tra' vesh' lehkuh captivating softness svi' shal-lan fitzwilliam’s manners, she pudva-tor au lau ma wuh buhfik informed kashek. Tonk'peh po mr. Darcy sarlah ni k'ashiv tor wuh parsonage ish-veh vesh' weht rihagik tor ken-tor. Ish-veh kupi ri nam-tor na' shila'es, u' au frequently hayal-tor tra' lehkuh minutes teretuhr rik' sharu ish-veh bru-lar; heh lu au did stariben, ish-veh seemed wuh daya t' bolayek rather do t' dvel--wuh sacrifice tor propriety, ri wuh sanosh tor himself. Au seldom saudau really animated. Mrs. Collins fai-tor ri ra tor tor t' ish-veh. Shal-lan fitzwilliam’s occasionally laughing na' ish-veh stupidity skan-tor ik au vesh' paik natya, if ish-veh sha' fai-tukh t' ish-veh kupi ri ma var-tor ish-veh; heh u' she would ma tishau tor dva-tor nash rubah wuh daya t' ashaya, heh wuh vel t' ik ashaya ish-veh t'hy'la eliza, she eku herself seriously tor ar'kadan tor talal ish-veh si': she glantau ish-veh whenever au vesh' na' rosings, heh whenever sarlah ish-veh tor hunsford; tonk'peh rik' mau navun. Au certainly glazhau na' ish-veh t'hy'la wuh lo'uk deal, tonk'peh wuh sagluvaya t' ik glazhau vesh' disputable. Ish-veh vesh' wuh earnest, steadfast gaze, tonk'peh she k'ashiv vet-tor whether tra' vesh' mau admiration svi' ish-veh, heh sometimes ish-veh seemed nothing tonk'peh k'torr kashek. She had wuh'wak il dah'wak suggested tor elizabeth wuh possibility t' ish-veh hasu ulik tor ish-veh, tonk'peh elizabeth kwon-hau-ov abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor na' wuh idea; heh mrs. Collins did ri nah-tor ish-veh gas'rak tor hish-tor wuh subject, s' wuh tehvar t' raising gishat if lau goh shaht svi' disappointment; na' svi' ish-veh opinion ish-veh nafai-tor ri t' wuh vet, ik ek' ish-veh t'hy'la’s ritishaya would vanish, kuv she kupi suppose ish-veh tor nam-tor svi' ish-veh tepul. Svi' ish-veh ves schemes na' elizabeth, she sometimes dotoran ish-veh marrying shal-lan fitzwilliam. Au vesh', mesakh comparison, wuh pleasantest sasu: au certainly krol-tor ish-veh, heh ish-veh situation svi' ha'kiv vesh' danik eligible; tonk'peh, tor counterbalance aifa advantages, mr. Darcy had considerable patronage svi' wuh church, heh ish-veh krei kupi ma rim na' ek'. [illustration: “fi' looking abru”] chapter xxxiii. [illustration] weht do wuh'wak did elizabeth, svi' ish-veh ramble k'svi wuh shi'sochya, unexpectedly ragel-tor mr. Darcy. She olau ek' wuh perverseness t' wuh mischance ik dang katau ish-veh wilat kling else vesh' katau; heh, tor prevent its ek'wak aisha va'ashiv, nem-tor tun tor inform ish-veh, palikauk, ik ish-veh vesh' wuh favourite haunt t' ish-veh. Uf ish-veh kupi paresh-tor wuh dahr wak, therefore, vesh' maut shaik! Wi ish-veh did, heh kauk wuh wuh. Ish-veh seemed spo' wilful has-bosh-malat, il wuh toripik penance; na' fi' aifa occasions ish-veh vesh' ri goh wuh zamu hotorik inquiries heh wuh awkward svizh heh yi maf, tonk'peh au actually nahp ish-veh bolayatik tor da-tor pla' heh lates k' ish-veh. Au worla leralmin-tor wuh lo'uk deal, il did she mazhiv-kur-tor herself wuh trouble t' talking il t' listening mau; tonk'peh ish-veh kwul-tor ish-veh svi' wuh rivak t' ish-veh wuh rencounter ik au vesh' asking ein shaik unconnected deshkau--pa' ish-veh sanosh svi' hasu na' hunsford, ish-veh ashaya t' solitary lates-tor, heh ish-veh opinion t' mr. Heh mrs. Collins’s happiness; heh ik svi' speaking t' rosings, heh ish-veh ri perfectly understanding wuh kelek, au seemed tor gish ik whenever sarlah ish-veh vi' kent va'ashiv she would nam-tor staying _there_ nuh'. Ish-veh zhit seemed tor imply ish-veh. Kupi au ma shal-lan fitzwilliam svi' ish-veh nahp? She supposed, kuv au tvai sovek-vel, au bolau tvai wuh allusion tor ra lau arise svi' ik yonuk. Ish-veh flakosh ish-veh wuh pi', heh she vesh' ved glad tor talal herself na' wuh temep svi' wuh pales mesyutik wuh parsonage. She vesh' engaged veh gad, u' she lates-tor, svi' re-perusing jane’s kim-shah nuhm, heh kelek fi' ein tvur if skan-tor ik jane had ri written svi' tam'a, lu, instead t' hasu va'ashiv ak'wikmun k' mr. Darcy, gla-tor ish-veh, fi' looking abru, ik shal-lan fitzwilliam vesh' latva ish-veh. Putting maf wuh nuhm iyi, heh forcing wuh abru'teruklar-ru'lut, she leralmin-tor, -- “i did ri fai-tor fa' ik du ek'wak lates-tor nash yut.” “i ma vesh' tor wuh tour t' wuh shi'sochya, ” au kilko-tor, “u' i paik tor kanok tevun, heh intended tor ikap-tor ish-veh k' wuh vutau na' wuh parsonage. Nam-tor du going mau weh-irak?” “rai, i dang ma da-tor svi' wuh moment.” heh accordingly she did da-tor, heh au lates-tor na' wuh parsonage teretuhr. “tor du certainly trasha kent fi' gad?” leralmin-tor she. “ha--kuv darcy tor ri shitau ish-veh ska' va'ashiv. Tonk'peh i am na' ish-veh sashitaya. Au arranges wuh business aishan u' au sanoi.” “heh kuv ri kup tor sanoi himself svi' wuh arrangement, au has k'puu lo'uk sanosh svi' wuh tepul t' dvel. I ri tor fai-tor anybody vi seems weht tor tizh-tor wuh tepul t' doing ra au tishau do mr. Darcy.” “au tishau ki' ish-veh sha' yut maut muhl, ” kilko-tor shal-lan fitzwilliam. “tonk'peh ni etek ek' tor. Ish-veh nam-tor goh ik au has weh-rom tvai t' having ish-veh do wehk vath, fai'ei au nam-tor don-ka, heh wehk vath nam-tor ri donku-tor. I stariben feelingly. Wuh younger sa-fu, du fai-tor, bolau nam-tor inured tor shal-wafaya heh dependence.” “svi' t'nash-veh opinion, wuh younger sa-fu t' wuh earl mokuhlek fai-tor maut pi' t' either. I', seriously, ra ma du ek'wak fainu t' shal-wafaya heh dependence? Lu ma du vesh' prevented k' aitlun t' donku s' going wherever du dvel-tor il procuring sovek-vel du had wuh fancy na'?” “aifa nam-tor ha-kel deshkau--heh sos'eh i fam yehat leralmin ik i ma veshtau wehk hardships t' ik malat. Tonk'peh svi' tukh t' greater rasath, i lau dash s' wuh aitlun t' donku. Younger sa-fu fam yehat marry wilat au spo'.” “vita wilat au spo' kosu t' fortune, if i nah-tor au maut k'ashiv tor.” “etwel es'merka t' kodona tor etek nuh' nerik, heh tra' nam-tor ri wehk svi' t'nash-veh lan t' ha'kiv vi mokuhlek afford tor marry rik' ein attention tor donku.” “nam-tor nash, ” nahp elizabeth, “tvai na' me?” heh she kur-tor na' wuh idea; tonk'peh, recovering herself, leralmin-tor svi' wuh lively molu, “heh pray, ra nam-tor wuh tsuri price t' wuh earl’s younger sa-fu? Vita wuh tela'at sa-kai nam-tor maut sickly, i suppose du would ri ya'akash abru' kau-leh thousand plesh-tor.” au kilko-tor ish-veh svi' wuh ka style, heh wuh subject eku-tor. Tor svi-shau wuh silence if lau tor ish-veh fancy ish-veh dau k' ra had be' dvun-tor, she ak afterwards leralmin-tor, -- “i glenonau ish-veh krei katau du ne' k' ish-veh chiefly na' wuh sake t' having somebody na' ish-veh sashitaya. I wonder au tor ri marry, tor shar wuh lasting convenience t' ik ves. Tonk'peh, sos'eh, ish-veh ko-kai tor u' muhl na' wuh la'; heh, u' she nam-tor ne' ish-veh lad tun, au lau tor ra au tishau k' ish-veh.” “rai, ” leralmin-tor shal-lan fitzwilliam, “ik nam-tor wuh advantage if au bolau dahsaya k' me. I am hau k' ish-veh svi' wuh guardianship t' din-tor darcy.” “nam-tor du, indeed? Heh pray ra wihfelau t' wuh guardian tor du tor? Tor ish-veh falun mazhiv-kur-tor du mau trouble? Nu'ri t'sai t' ish-veh ya'shakhuv nam-tor sometimes wuh pi' rihagik tor khartau; heh kuv she has wuh yeht darcy tam'a, she lau spo' ki' ish-veh sha' yut.” u' she stariben, she glantau ish-veh looking na' ish-veh earnestly; heh wuh manner svi' if au iyi ya'akash ish-veh po she supposed din-tor darcy kesik tor mazhiv-kur-tor au sovek uneasiness, convinced ish-veh ik she had somehow il vath prah takov be' wuh yeht'es. She directly kilko-tor, -- “du bolaya ri nam-tor koltha. I worla puzhu-tor sovek klau t' ish-veh; heh i dare leralmin she nam-tor veh t' wuh danik tractable creatures svi' wuh panu. She nam-tor wuh maut lo'uk favourite k' ein t'sai t' t'nash-veh acquaintance, mrs. Hurst heh din-tor bingley. I nah-tor i ma puzhu-tor du leralmin ik du fai-tor au.” “i fai-tor au wuh pi'. Ish-veh sa-kai nam-tor wuh vaksurik, gentlemanlike sasu--au nam-tor wuh lo'uk t'hy'la t' darcy’s.” “oh ha, ” leralmin-tor elizabeth drily--“mr. Darcy nam-tor uncommonly ves tor mr. Bingley, heh nem-tor wuh prodigious deal t' tun t' ish-veh.” “tun t' ish-veh! Ha, i really dva-tor darcy _does_ nem-tor tun t' ish-veh svi' eifa sfekau wilat au danik aitlu tun. S' vel ik au var-tor me svi' etwel halovaya hither, i ma utvau tor nah-tor bingley maut mau indebted tor ish-veh. Tonk'peh i ought tor eit'jae ish-veh pardon, na' i ma rai gas'rak tor suppose ik bingley vesh' wuh person tvai. Ish-veh vesh' ek' conjecture.” “ra nam-tor ish-veh du tvai?” “ish-veh nam-tor wuh circumstance if darcy veling kupi ri istaya tor nam-tor paik fainu, fai'ei kuv ish-veh vesh' tor prah pauk tor wuh t'sai’s skan ish-veh would nam-tor wuh unpleasant vel.” “du lau nerau fi-tor t'nash-veh ri mentioning ish-veh.” “heh vokau ik i ma ri mau utvau na' supposing ish-veh tor nam-tor bingley. Ra au var-tor me vesh' goh nash: ik au congratulated himself fi' having lately korsau wuh t'hy'la s' wuh inconveniences t' wuh danik imprudent kal'i'farr, tonk'peh rik' mentioning ahm il sovek vath particulars; heh i goh suspected ish-veh tor nam-tor bingley s' believing ish-veh wuh ves t' nu'ri sasu tor prah vi' wuh theshau t' ik wihfelau, heh s' fai-tor au ki' vesh' teretuhr wuh bosh t' kim-shah belaar.” “did mr. Darcy mazhiv-kur-tor du ish-veh utvau na' nash interference?” “i ken-tor ik tra' vesh' ein maut karik objections tehnat wuh t'sai.” “heh ra arts did au nam-tor-tor tor dahshauk au?” “au did ri variben tor me t' ish-veh sha' arts, ” leralmin-tor fitzwilliam, smiling. “au goh var-tor me ra i ma i' var-tor du.” elizabeth tor rai kilko-srashiv, heh lates-tor fi', ish-veh khaf-spol puv k' indignation. Po' watching ish-veh wuh pi', fitzwilliam ya'akash ish-veh po she vesh' ni thoughtful. “i am thinking t' ra du ma vesh' telling me, ” leralmin-tor she. “ish-veh krei’s spa-tor tor ri saikhut t'nash-veh feelings. Po vesh' au tor nam-tor wuh judge?” “du nam-tor rather sashitau tor vutau ish-veh interference officious?” “i ri tor gla-tor ra gas'rak mr. Darcy had tor klopau fi' wuh propriety t' ish-veh t'hy'la’s inclination; il po, fi-tor ish-veh sha' judgment sa'awek, au vesh' tor satalau heh kharik svi' ra manner ik t'hy'la vesh' tor nam-tor kunli. Tonk'peh, ” she fator, recollecting herself, “u' etek fai-tor rim t' wuh particulars, ish-veh nam-tor ri rom tor condemn ish-veh. Ish-veh nam-tor ri tor nam-tor supposed ik tra' vesh' mau affection svi' wuh nuf.” “ik nam-tor ri wuh unnatural surmise, ” leralmin-tor fitzwilliam; “tonk'peh ish-veh nam-tor lessening wuh dor t' t'nash-veh krei’s triumph maut sadly.” nash vesh' spoken jestingly, tonk'peh ish-veh saudau tor ish-veh ni aishan wuh bikuv t' mr. Darcy, ik she would ri sahrafel herself k' wuh kilko-srashiv; heh, therefore, abruptly rubai wuh conversation, variben fi' indifferent tukh till au pulau wuh parsonage. Tra', ikap-tor vi' ish-veh sha' tvi-shal, u' ak u' ish-veh visitor losrak au, she kupi nah-tor rik' svi-shaya t' ek' ik she had puzhu-tor. Ish-veh vesh' ri tor nam-tor supposed ik sovek vath sutra kupi nam-tor tvai do eifa k' ik she vesh' tersau. Tra' kupi ri nam-tor svi' wuh panu _two_ sasu abru' ik mr. Darcy kupi ma such boundless vi-yumuk. Ik au had vesh' concerned svi' wuh thon-tor taken tor dahshauk mr. Bingley heh jane, she had worla vet-tor; tonk'peh she had kwon-hau-ov attributed tor din-tor bingley wuh principal design heh arrangement t' au. Kuv ish-veh sha' vanity, however, did ri mislead ish-veh, _he_ vesh' wuh aishan--ish-veh pride heh caprice vesh' wuh aishan--t' ek' ik jane had dashau, heh fam dvun fator tor dash. Au had ruined na' wuh du' kanok rok t' happiness na' wuh danik affectionate, generous khaf-spol svi' wuh panu; heh kling kupi leralmin uf lasting wuh ek'rasah au lau ma inflicted. “tra' vesh' ein maut karik objections tehnat wuh t'sai, ” vesh' shal-lan fitzwilliam’s zhit; heh aifa karik objections probably vesh', ish-veh having veh sa-kuk vi vesh' wuh shasol attorney, heh wuh'ashiv vi vesh' svi' business svi' london. “tor jane herself, ” she sporiben, “tra' kupi nam-tor rai possibility t' objection, --ek' loveliness heh goodness u' she nam-tor! Ish-veh understanding marom, ish-veh kashek improved, heh ish-veh manners captivating. Neither kupi sovek-vel nam-tor urged tehnat t'nash-veh sa-mekh, vi, hi k' ein peculiarities, has kup'es if mr. Darcy himself bolaya ri disdain, heh respectability if au dungi probably worla pulau.” lu she nahp t' ish-veh ko-mekh, indeed, ish-veh guhl'es mazhiv-kur-tor yut wuh pi'; tonk'peh she would ri kal-tor ik sovek objections _there_ had tukh rasath k' mr. Darcy, t'vi pride, she vesh' convinced, would poprah wuh deeper skek s' wuh aitlun t' importance svi' ish-veh t'hy'la’s tersaya do s' ish-veh aitlun t' kash-ral; heh she vesh' ved klopau, na' kim-shah, ik au had vesh' partly governed k' nash rasahkos ves t' pride, heh partly k' wuh istaya t' retaining mr. Bingley na' ish-veh ko-kai. Wuh agitation heh bezhun-masu if wuh subject occasioned katau fi' wuh headache; heh ish-veh grew ni mau weh-rasahkos na' wuh khru ik, hau tor ish-veh unwillingness tor gla-tor mr. Darcy, ish-veh satalau ish-veh ri tor attend ish-veh krei tor rosings, wilat au vesh' engaged tor mon theris-masu. Mrs. Collins, seeing ik she vesh' really unwell, did ri hish-tor ish-veh tor hal-tor, heh u' mau u' tor-yehat prevented ish-veh sa-telsu s' pressing ish-veh; tonk'peh mr. Collins kupi ri ip-sut ish-veh apprehension t' t'sai catherine’s hasu rather displeased k' ish-veh staying na' ha-kel. [illustration] chapter xxxiv. [illustration] lu au vesh' hal-tor, elizabeth, u' kuv intending tor exasperate herself u' mau u' tor-yehat tehnat mr. Darcy, dvel-tor na' ish-veh employment wuh linisaya t' ek' wuh nuhm if jane had written tor ish-veh opi' ish-veh hasu svi' kent. Au tuhlau rai actual complaint, il vesh' tra' sovek revival t' vesht occurrences, il sovek sviribaya t' la' suffering. Tonk'peh svi' ek', heh svi' siyah kanok zehl t' tik, tra' vesh' wuh aitlun t' ik cheerfulness if had vesh' nam-tor-tor tor characterize ish-veh style, heh if, proceeding s' wuh mol-kom t' wuh kashek na' ease k' itself, heh kindly sashitau na' kanok-veh, had vesh' scarcely ek'wak clouded. Elizabeth pubeglanau kanok zhit-bal conveying wuh idea t' uneasiness, k' wuh attention if ish-veh had hardly poprah fi' wuh wuh'rak perusal. Mr. Darcy’s shameful boast t' ra misery au had vesh' kup tor inflict mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh wuh keener kash-ral t' ish-veh ko-kai’s sufferings. Ish-veh vesh' ein consolation tor nah-tor ik ish-veh yaret tor rosings vesh' tor shaht fi' wuh gad po' wuh thurai, heh wuh fam dvun greater ik svi' lehkuh tor wuh fortnight she dang herself nam-tor k' jane va'ashiv, heh enabled tor contribute tor wuh recovery t' ish-veh tam'a, k' ek' ik affection kupi tor. She kupi ri nah-tor t' darcy’s leaving kent rik' remembering ik ish-veh krei vesh' tor hal-tor k' ish-veh; tonk'peh shal-lan fitzwilliam had tor ish-veh pa'shik ik au had rai intentions na' ek', heh, agreeable u' au vesh', she did ri tvai tor nam-tor unhappy pa' ish-veh. Du' settling nash sfek, she vesh' suddenly kastorilau k' wuh ralash t' wuh svep-kus-vakh; heh ish-veh tam'a vesh' wuh pi' nuv-tor k' wuh idea t' its hasu shal-lan fitzwilliam himself, vi had wuh'wak fa' puvutau tab-ma svi' wuh khru, heh lau i' sarlah tor inquire wa' po' ish-veh. Tonk'peh nash idea vesh' ak klee'fah'tu, heh ish-veh tam'a vesh' maut differently dau, lu, tor ish-veh utter tauraya, gla-tor ish-veh mr. Darcy lates vi' wuh tvi-shal. Svi' wuh hurried manner au iyi began wuh inquiry po' ish-veh muhl'es, imputing ish-veh yaret tor wuh istaya t' khaf-spol ik she vesh' weh-rom. She kilko-tor ish-veh k' samu civility. Au hayal-tor ne' na' wuh zamu moments, heh yi getting abru lates-tor pa' wuh tvi-shal. Elizabeth vesh' ak'wikmun, tonk'peh leralmin-tor ri wuh zhit. Po' wuh silence t' several minutes, sarlah ish-veh na' ish-veh svi' wuh pahutau manner, heh thus began: -- “svi' vain ma i struggled. Ish-veh dungi ri tor. T'nash-veh feelings dungi ri nam-tor repressed. Du bolau kal-tor me tor var-tor du uf ardently i krol-tor heh ashaya du.” elizabeth’s astonishment vesh' mesakh sagluvaya. She nantau, kur-tor, vet-tor, heh vesh' ralash-fam. Nash au panah-tor sufficient kastoraya, heh wuh avowal t' ek' ik au olau heh had wu olau na' ish-veh iyi zahal-tor. Au stariben muhl; tonk'peh tra' vesh' feelings isha eifa t' wuh khaf-spol tor nam-tor detailed, heh au vesh' ri weht eloquent fi' wuh subject t' tenderness do t' pride. Ish-veh kash-ral t' ish-veh inferiority, t' its hasu wuh degradation, t' wuh skan obstacles if judgment had kwon-hau-ov opposed tor inclination, vesh' dwelt fi' k' wuh warmth if seemed due tor wuh consequence au vesh' wounding, tonk'peh vesh' maut rikesik tor recommend ish-veh saikhut. Svi' spite t' ish-veh deeply-rooted ritishaya, she kupi ri nam-tor insensible tor wuh compliment t' such wuh sasu’s affection, heh hi ish-veh intentions did ri vuhnau na' wuh instant, she vesh' palikauk sorry na' wuh kusut au vesh' tor poprah; till kastorilau tor resentment k' ish-veh subsequent gen-lis, she pakik ek' utan'es svi' reshan. She ar'kada, however, tor tertitau herself tor kilko-srashiv ish-veh k' tranush, lu au dang ma ovsoh. Au concluded k' representing tor ish-veh wuh karik'es t' ik attachment if svi' spite t' ek' ish-veh endeavours au had afer-tor impossible tor conquer; heh k' expressing ish-veh rok ik ish-veh would i' nam-tor rewarded k' ish-veh acceptance t' ish-veh el'ru. U' au leralmin-tor nash she kupi easily gla-tor ik au had rai vet t' wuh favourable kilko-srashiv. Au _spoke_ t' apprehension heh anxiety, tonk'peh ish-veh countenance sagluvau yeht shar'es. Such wuh circumstance kupi goh exasperate weh-irak; heh lu au ceased wuh kur she-tor vi' ish-veh nak heh she leralmin-tor, -- “svi' such nuf u' nash, ish-veh nam-tor, i dva-tor, wuh afer-tor nuk tor sagluvau wuh kash-ral t' obligation na' wuh sentiments avowed, however unequally au lau nam-tor fun-tor. Ish-veh nam-tor malatik ik obligation dang nam-tor olau, heh kuv i kupi _feel_ gratitude, i would i' nemaiyo. Tonk'peh i fam yehat--i ma worla aitlu ish-veh rom opinion, heh du ma certainly bestowed ish-veh danik unwillingly. Ni'droi'ik nar-tor ki' occasioned kusut tor sovek-veh. Ish-veh has vesh' danik unconsciously ovsoh, however, heh i rok dungi nam-tor t' pen duration. Wuh feelings if du var-tor me ma wu prevented wuh acknowledgment t' ish-veh fudau mokuhlek ma pi' rihag'es svi' overcoming ish-veh po' nash danaya.” mr. Darcy, vi vesh' leaning tehnat wuh mantel-krus k' ish-veh bezhun teslau fi' ish-veh limuk, seemed tor kum ish-veh zhit k' rai lehkuh resentment do ak'wikmun. Ish-veh complexion became spoh k' reshan, heh wuh ertaya t' ish-veh kashek vesh' visible svi' kanok feature. Au vesh' struggling na' wuh appearance t' composure, heh would ri tu'ash ish-veh bru-lar till au pudva-tor himself ki' attained ish-veh. Wuh svizh vesh' tor elizabeth’s feelings dreadful. Na' wu-vath, svi' wuh spes t' punekwitau calmness, au leralmin-tor, -- “heh nash nam-tor ek' wuh kilko if i am ki' wuh dor t' expecting! I lau, sos'eh, istaya tor nam-tor informed po, k' ni pi' _endeavour_ na' civility, i am thus rejected. Tonk'peh ish-veh nam-tor t' pi' importance.” “i lau u' muhl inquire, ” kilko-tor she, “po, k' ni evident wuh design t' offending heh insulting me, du dvel-tor tor var-tor me ik du tishau me tehnat ish-veh dungi, tehnat ish-veh utvau, heh kauk tehnat ish-veh character? Vesh' ri nash ein tobeg na' incivility, kuv i _was_ uncivil? Tonk'peh i ma vath provocations. Du fai-tor i ma. Had ri t'nash-veh sha' feelings klopau tehnat du, had au vesh' indifferent, il had au kauk vesh' favourable, tor du nah-tor ik sovek consideration would tempt me tor nar-tor wuh sasu vi has vesh' wuh tvai t' ruining, sos'eh na' ek'wak, wuh happiness t' wuh danik k'diwa ko-kai?” u' she pronounced aifa zhit, mr. Darcy rubai kur; tonk'peh wuh zherka vesh' pen, heh au shroi rik' attempting tor svi-shau ish-veh du' she fator, -- “i ma kanok utvau svi' wuh panu tor nah-tor has-bosh t' du. Rai dvubolek mokuhlek tobeg wuh unjust heh ungenerous krus du bae'cok _there_. Du dare ri, du fam yehat wafu ik du ma vesh' wuh principal, kuv ri wuh goh tvai t' dividing au s' tik vath, t' exposing veh tor wuh censure t' wuh panu na' caprice heh rifihet'es, wuh vath tor its derision na' disappointed rok-tor, heh involving au fi' svi' misery t' wuh acutest ves.” she svizh-tor, heh gla-tor k' rai slight indignation ik au vesh' listening k' wuh sov if skan-tor ish-veh wholly unmoved k' sovek olaya t' remorse. Au kauk glazhau na' ish-veh k' wuh abru'teruklar-ru'lut t' dau incredulity. “mokuhlek du wafu ik du ma ovsoh ish-veh?” she ashiv-tor. K' assumed tranquillity au yi kilko-tor, “i ma rai istaya t' denying ik i did kanok-vei svi' t'nash-veh tepul tor dahshauk t'nash-veh t'hy'la s' ish-veh ko-kai, il ik i rejoice svi' t'nash-veh navun. Na' _him_ i ma vesh' kinder do na' myself.” elizabeth disdained wuh appearance t' noticing nash civil haulan, tonk'peh its meaning did ri stron, il vesh' ish-veh kesik tor conciliate ish-veh. “tonk'peh ish-veh nam-tor ri goh nash tek'ik, ” she fator, “fi' if t'nash-veh ritishaya nam-tor founded. Wu fa' ish-veh had taken shi, t'nash-veh opinion t' du vesh' klopau. Ish-veh character vesh' unfolded svi' wuh recital if i poprah wehk tevun-krus ago s' mr. Wickham. Fi' nash subject, ra mokuhlek du ma tor leralmin? Svi' ra glenonik bae'cok t' friendship mokuhlek du la' fosh-tor yourself? Il ne' ra misrepresentation mokuhlek du la' impose fi-tor vath?” “du nem-tor wuh nayik eku'ko svi' ik gentleman’s concerns, ” leralmin-tor darcy, svi' wuh lehkuh tranquil molu, heh k' wuh heightened kur. “vi ik fai-tor ra ish-veh misfortunes ma vesh' mokuhlek gol'nev olaya wuh eku'ko svi' ish-veh?” “ish-veh misfortunes!” ashiv-tor darcy, contemptuously, --“ha, ish-veh misfortunes ma vesh' lo'uk indeed.” “heh t' ish-veh infliction, ” maf-tor elizabeth, k' tepul; “du ma netakidau ish-veh tor ish-veh la' fupa s' t' poverty--comparative poverty. Du ma withheld wuh advantages if du bolau fai-tor ki' vesh' designed na' ish-veh. Du ma deprived wuh buhfik tevun t' ish-veh ha'kiv t' ik tikopah if vesh' rai lehkuh ish-veh due do ish-veh eshikh. Du ma ovsoh ek' nash! Heh wi du mokuhlek skasau wuh mention t' ish-veh misfortunes k' contempt heh ridicule.” “heh nash, ” maf-tor darcy, u' au lates-tor k' sahris ash-tor mes' wuh tvi-shal, “nam-tor ish-veh opinion t' me! Nash nam-tor wuh estimation svi' if du meskaraya me! I nemaiyo na' explaining ish-veh ni fully. T'nash-veh lafot, fupa s' nash calculation, nam-tor ras indeed! Tonk'peh, sos'eh, ” hau au, stopping svi' ish-veh lates, heh turning na' ish-veh, “aifa offences lau ma vesh' overlooked, had ri ish-veh pride vesh' dash-tor k' t'nash-veh trau confession t' wuh scruples ik had wu prevented t'nash-veh forming sovek serious design. Aifa sfith(-) accusations lau ma vesh' nelau, had i, k' greater policy, ip-sut t'nash-veh struggles, heh snuhkrol-tor du vi' wuh dva t' t'nash-veh hasu impelled k' unqualified, unalloyed inclination; k' utvau, k' haulan, k' kanok-vei. Tonk'peh pasut t' kanok wihfelau nam-tor t'nash-veh abhorrence. Il am i kafusik t' wuh feelings i related. Au vesh' malatik heh aishan. Kupi du gish me tor rejoice svi' wuh inferiority t' ish-veh tersaya?--tor congratulate myself fi' wuh rok t' relations t'vi nosh svi' ha'kiv nam-tor ni decidedly ne'rak t'nash-veh sha'?” elizabeth olau herself growing weht reshnek kanok moment; wi she ar'kada tor wuh utmost tor stariben k' composure lu she leralmin-tor, -- “du nam-tor mistaken, mr. Darcy, kuv du suppose ik wuh nuk t' ish-veh afsakaya dau me svi' sovek vath yut do u' ish-veh spared me wuh concern if i lau ma olau svi' refusing du, had du behaved svi' wuh weht gentlemanlike manner.” gla-tor ish-veh ish-veh palikaya na' nash; tonk'peh au leralmin-tor nothing, heh she fator, -- “du kupi ri ma tor me wuh nufai t' ish-veh el'ru svi' sovek tor-yehat yut ik would ma tempted me tor nar-tor ish-veh.” va'ashiv ish-veh astonishment vesh' obvious; heh au glazhau na' ish-veh k' wuh sagluvaya t' mingled incredulity heh mortification. She went fi', -- “s' wuh maut palikaya, s' wuh wuh'rak moment, i lau siyah leralmin, t' t'nash-veh acquaintance k' du, ish-veh manners impressing me k' wuh fullest dva t' ish-veh arrogance, ish-veh conceit, heh ish-veh selfish disdain t' wuh feelings t' vath, vesh' such u' tor shid ik groundwork t' disapprobation, fi' if succeeding pavek ma torvau ni immovable wuh ritishaya; heh i had ri fainu du wuh tevun-krus fa' i olau ik du vesh' wuh kim-shah sasu svi' wuh panu ik i kupi ek'wak nam-tor fakovau fi' tor marry.” “du ma leralmin-tor ved hiyet, madam. I perfectly comprehend ish-veh feelings, heh ma i' goh tor nam-tor kafusik t' ra t'nash-veh sha' ma vesh'. Forgive me na' having taken abru ni mau t' ish-veh wak, heh nar-tor t'nash-veh buhfik istau na' ish-veh muhl'es heh happiness.” heh k' aifa zhit au hastily losrak wuh tvi-shal, heh elizabeth puzhu-tor ish-veh wuh thurai moment tu'ash wuh khom svep heh quit wuh kelek. Wuh tumult t' ish-veh kashek vesh' i' painfully lo'uk. She fai-tor ri uf tor nenikaya herself, heh, s' actual kobat'es, hayal-tor ne' heh maf-tor na' ulef wuh wadan. Ish-veh astonishment, u' she haul-tor fi' ra had be' dvun-tor, vesh' increased k' kanok review t' ish-veh. Ik she dang poprah wuh nufai t' kal'i'farr s' mr. Darcy! Ik au dang ma vesh' svi' ashaya k' ish-veh na' ni wehk tevun-krus! Ni mau svi' ashaya u' tor istaya tor marry ish-veh svi' spite t' ek' wuh objections if had tor ish-veh prevent ish-veh t'hy'la’s marrying ish-veh ko-kai, heh if bolau saudau k'puu k' kaik nekwitaya svi' ish-veh sha' nuf, vesh' siyah incredible! Ish-veh vesh' gratifying ki' vi'le-esh-tor unconsciously ni karik wuh affection. Tonk'peh ish-veh pride, ish-veh abominable pride, ish-veh shameless avowal t' ra au had ovsoh k' respect tor jane, ish-veh unpardonable assurance svi' acknowledging, hi au kupi ri justify ish-veh, heh wuh unfeeling manner if au had mentioned mr. Wickham, ish-veh cruelty na' ik au had ri attempted tor wafu, ak overcame wuh pity if wuh consideration t' ish-veh attachment had na' wuh moment teporilau. She fator svi' maut agitating haulan till wuh ralash t' t'sai catherine’s carriage tor ish-veh olau uf unequal she vesh' tor snagel charlotte’s glantaya, heh hurried ish-veh maf tor ish-veh tvi-shal. [illustration: “khaf-spol herself puvutau” ] chapter xxxv. [illustration] elizabeth awoke wuh thurai asal tor wuh ka nahp heh meditations if had na' wu-vath a'ing ish-veh bezhun. She kupi ri wi recover s' wuh ak'wikmun t' ra had pavesh-tor: ish-veh vesh' impossible tor nah-tor t' sovek-vel else; heh, totally indisposed na' employment, she resolved ak po' asal-yem tor indulge herself svi' sov heh tusok. She vesh' proceeding directly tor ish-veh favourite lates, lu wuh recollection t' mr. Darcy’s sometimes coming tra' pehkau ish-veh, heh instead t' entering wuh shi'sochya, she da-tor abru wuh lane if pufulag-tor ish-veh weh-irak s' wuh turnpike fau-yut. Wuh shi'sochya paling vesh' fam dvun wuh krup fi' veh vla, heh she ak be' dvun-tor veh t' wuh temep vi' wuh solektra. Po' walking dahkuh il rehkuh wak bi' ik krus t' wuh lane, she vesh' tempted, k' wuh pleasantness t' wuh asal, tor pehkaya na' wuh temep heh glazhau vi' wuh shi'sochya. Wuh kaukuh wehk gad if she had i' be' dvun-tor svi' kent had tor wuh lo'uk natyan svi' wuh shasol, heh kanok gad vesh' hau tor wuh verdure t' wuh lehkuh-mal lap. She vesh' fi' wuh sfek t' continuing ish-veh lates, lu she kum-tor wuh glimpse t' wuh gentleman k'svi wuh wihfelau t' pi'laptra if rihkau wuh shi'sochya: au vesh' dvun-tor ik yut; heh pthak-bosh t' its hasu mr. Darcy, she vesh' directly retreating. Tonk'peh wuh person vi storilau vesh' i' be' hiyet tor gla-tor ish-veh, heh stepping fa'rak k' eagerness, pronounced ish-veh ahm. She had da-tor maf; tonk'peh fi' khaf-spol herself puvutau, hi svi' wuh spes if skan-tor ish-veh tor nam-tor mr. Darcy, she dvun-tor va'ashiv na' wuh temep. Au had k' ik wak pulau ish-veh isha; heh, holding si' wuh nuhm, if she instinctively nem-tor, leralmin-tor, k' wuh glazhau t' haughty composure, “i ma vesh' walking svi' wuh pi'laptra ein wak, svi' wuh rok t' latva du. Dungi du tor me wuh dor t' telvan ik nuhm?” heh yi, k' wuh slight kes-wun, da-tor va'ashiv vi' wuh plantation, heh vesh' ak s' glan. K' rai gishat t' sanosh, tonk'peh k' wuh strongest curiosity, elizabeth tu'ash wuh nuhm, heh tor ish-veh fam dvun increasing wonder, pakashogau wuh envelope containing dahkuh thalv t' nuhm dun, written ved k'fai, svi' wuh maut ikap-tor el'ru. Wuh envelope itself vesh' likewise bosh. Pursuing ish-veh yut bi' wuh lane, she yi began ish-veh. Ish-veh vesh' dated s' rosings, na' ohkuh o’wak-vel svi' wuh asal, heh vesh' u' zahal-tor: -- “nam-tor ri alarmed, madam, fi' receiving nash nuhm, k' wuh apprehension t' its containing sovek repetition t' eifa sentiments, il renewal t' eifa nufau, if vesh' kim-shah mu-yor ni disgusting tor du. I kitau rik' sovek intention t' paining du, il humbling myself, k' kelek fi' istau, if, na' wuh happiness t' fi', fam yehat nam-tor nuh' ak yen-tor; heh wuh urgam if wuh shidoraya heh wuh perusal t' nash nuhm bolau occasion, dang ma vesh' spared, had ri t'nash-veh character required ish-veh tor nam-tor written heh telv-tor. Du bolau, therefore, pardon wuh el'es k' if i haishaya ish-veh attention; ish-veh feelings, i fai-tor, dungi bestow ish-veh unwillingly, tonk'peh i haishaya ish-veh t' ish-veh yeht-gav. “dahkuh offences t' wuh maut natya malat, heh k' rai tvai t' kaik pul'es, du kim-shah mu-yor laid tor t'nash-veh falun. Wuh wuh'rak mentioned vesh', ik, regardless t' wuh sentiments t' either, i had dahl-tor mr. Bingley s' ish-veh ko-kai, --heh wuh vath, ik i had, svi' defiance t' vuhnauk claims, svi' defiance t' dor heh humanity, ruined wuh iyi smusma'es heh thorshau wuh prospects t' mr. Wickham. Wilfully heh wantonly ki' lehm-tor ska' wuh besu t' t'nash-veh youth, wuh nafai favourite t' t'nash-veh sa-mekh, wuh nu'ri sasu vi had scarcely sovek vath dependence do fi' etwel patronage, heh vi had vesh' katau abru tor gish its pideshan, would nam-tor wuh depravity, tor if wuh dahshaya t' dahkuh nu'ri persons t'vi affection kupi nam-tor wuh tor'ovak t' goh wuh zamu wehk gad, kupi lesh rai comparison. Tonk'peh s' wuh severity t' ik tenai if vesh' kim-shah mu-yor ni liberally bestowed, respecting tik circumstance, i dungau rok tor nam-tor svi' fa-wak shar-tor, lu wuh zahalik khrosahp t' t'nash-veh torai heh ish-veh dvubolek has vesh' telv-tor. Kuv, svi' wuh danaya t' au if nam-tor due tor myself, i am ne' wuh bolayek t' relating feelings if lau nam-tor offensive tor ish-veh, i mokuhlek goh leralmin ik ni'droi'ik nar-tor. Wuh bolayek bolau nam-tor obeyed, heh further apology would nam-tor absurd. I had ri vesh' wu svi' hertfordshire fa' vesht gla-tor nash-veh, svi' tsuri k' vath, ik bingley preferred ish-veh tela'at ko-kai tor sovek vath nu'ri kosu svi' wuh shasol. Tonk'peh ish-veh vesh' ri till wuh khru t' wuh tam na' netherfield ik i had sovek apprehension t' ish-veh olaya wuh serious attachment. I had k'ashiv gla-tor ish-veh svi' ashaya fa'. Na' ik rin'k'n, du' i had wuh dor t' taman k' du, i vesh' wuh'rak tor acquainted, k' osu william lucas’s ur'kif ro'fori, ik bingley’s attentions tor ish-veh ko-kai had putan-tor shen tor wuh paik gishat t' ish-veh kal'i'farr. Au stariben t' ish-veh u' wuh ac'ruth pavek, t' if wuh wak sa'awek kupi nam-tor undecided. S' ik moment i glantau t'nash-veh t'hy'la’s kloshai attentively; heh i kupi yi pakashogau ik ish-veh partiality na' din-tor bennet vesh' mesakh ra i had ek'wak toglantau svi' ish-veh. Ish-veh ko-kai i isha glantau. Ish-veh glazhau heh manners vesh' tu'ash, cheerful, heh engaging u' ek'wak, tonk'peh rik' sovek symptom t' peculiar fudau; heh i hafau convinced, s' wuh khru’s scrutiny, ik hi she poprah ish-veh attentions k' sanosh, she did ri invite au k' sovek participation t' sentiment. Kuv _you_ ma ri vesh' mistaken la', _i_ bolau ma vesh' svi' wuh lafosh. Ish-veh superior fai-tukh t' ish-veh ko-kai bolau tor wuh latter yesik. Kuv ish-veh nam-tor ni, kuv i ma vesh' misled k' such lafosh tor inflict kusut fi' ish-veh, ish-veh resentment has ri vesh' unreasonable. Tonk'peh i dungau ri scruple tor seo'a, ik wuh mol-kom t' ish-veh ko-kai’s countenance heh sov vesh' such u' lau ma putan-tor wuh danik zat observer wuh conviction ik, however amiable ish-veh temper, ish-veh khaf-spol vesh' ri kesik tor nam-tor easily estuhl. Ik i vesh' desirous t' believing ish-veh indifferent nam-tor ac'ruth; tonk'peh i dungi venture tor leralmin ik t'nash-veh investigations heh klopaya nam-tor ri usually vi-yumuk k' t'nash-veh rok-tor il ptha. I did ri dva-tor ish-veh tor nam-tor indifferent fai'ei i istau ish-veh; i pudva-tor ish-veh fi' impartial conviction, u' truly u' i istau ish-veh svi' utvau. T'nash-veh objections tor wuh kal'i'farr vesh' ri goh eifa if i kim-shah mu-yor nafai ki' required wuh utmost nekwitaya t' shaukaush tor shitau aside svi' t'nash-veh sha' nuf; wuh aitlun t' tersaya kupi ri nam-tor ni lo'uk wuh ek'rasah tor t'nash-veh t'hy'la u' tor me. Tonk'peh tra' vesh' vath aisha t' repugnance; aisha if, hi fam dvun existing, heh existing tor wuh kaik degree svi' fi' instances, i had myself endeavoured tor yen-tor, fai'ei au vesh' ri iyi fa' me. Aifa aisha bolau nam-tor fupa s', hi briefly. Wuh situation t' ish-veh ko-mekh’s skan, hi objectionable, vesh' nothing svi' comparison t' ik ovus aitlun t' propriety ni frequently, ni siyah uniformly pusvik-tor k' herself, k' ish-veh rehkuh younger ko-kai, heh occasionally kauk k' ish-veh sa-mekh: --pardon me, --ish-veh kusut-tor me tor thrap-tor du. Tonk'peh amidst ish-veh concern na' wuh lafot t' ish-veh nearest relations, heh ish-veh displeasure na' nash representation t' au, kal-tor ish-veh mazhiv-kur-tor du consolation tor panah-tor ik ki' conducted yourselves ni u' tor nan'woi sovek thresh t' wuh spo' censure nam-tor krol rai lehkuh paik bestowed fi' du heh ish-veh eldest ko-kai do ish-veh nam-tor dorli tor wuh kash-ral heh disposition t' fi'. I dungi goh leralmin, weh-irak, ik s' ra be' dvun-tor ik khru t'nash-veh opinion t' ek' parties vesh' wugau, heh kanok inducement heightened, if kupi ma pufulag-tor me fa' tor korsau t'nash-veh t'hy'la s' ra i vam wuh danik unhappy tersaya. Au losrak netherfield na' london fi' wuh gad zahalik, u' du, i am ac'ruth, vokau, k' wuh design t' ak returning. Wuh krus if i bae'cok nam-tor i' tor nam-tor danau. Ish-veh ko-kai’ uneasiness had vesh' kaing teporilau k' t'nash-veh sha': etwel coincidence t' olaya vesh' ak discovered; heh, kahkwa sensible ik rai wak vesh' tor nam-tor pakik svi' detaching ish-veh sa-kai, etek shortly resolved fi' hau ish-veh directly svi' london. Etek accordingly went--heh tra' i readily engaged svi' wuh office t' pointing si' tor t'nash-veh t'hy'la wuh ac'ruth ek'rasah t' such wuh dvel. I kethelvau heh togolau au earnestly. Tonk'peh however nash remonstrance lau ma staggered il vohtau ish-veh determination, i ri tor suppose ik ish-veh would ultimately ma prevented wuh kal'i'farr, had ish-veh ri vesh' seconded k' wuh assurance, if i hesitated ri svi' giving, t' ish-veh ko-kai’s indifference. Au had fa' pudva-tor ish-veh tor fun ish-veh affection k' sincere, kuv ri k' kaik, fudau. Tonk'peh bingley has lo'uk malatik modesty, k' wuh stronger dependence fi' t'nash-veh judgment do fi' ish-veh sha'. Tor convince ish-veh, therefore, ik au had tehs-tor himself vesh' rai maut rihagik sfek. Tor persuade ish-veh tehnat returning vi' hertfordshire, lu ik conviction had vesh' putan-tor, vesh' scarcely wuh ar'kadan t' wuh moment. I fam yehat tenai myself na' having ovsoh thus mau. Tra' nam-tor tonk'peh veh krus t' t'nash-veh spa-tor, svi' wuh bosh tek'ik, fi' if i ri tor haul-tor k' satisfaction; ish-veh nam-tor ik i condescended tor thanai wuh thon-tor t' tanaf ni irak u' tor ip-sut s' ish-veh ish-veh ko-kai’s hasu svi' kahr. I fai-tor ish-veh myself, u' ish-veh vesh' fainu tor din-tor bingley; tonk'peh ish-veh sa-kai nam-tor kauk wi ignorant t' ish-veh. Ik au lau ma ragel-tor rik' has-bosh consequence nam-tor, sos'eh, yesik; tonk'peh ish-veh fudau did ri saudau tor me hiyet sayonotau na' ish-veh tor gla-tor ish-veh rik' ein tehvar. Sos'eh nash concealment, nash pasut, vesh' ne'rak me. Ish-veh nam-tor ovsoh, however, heh ish-veh vesh' ovsoh na' wuh buhfik. Fi' nash subject i ma nothing weht tor leralmin, rai vath apology tor nufai. Kuv i ma wounded ish-veh ko-kai’s feelings, ish-veh vesh' unknowingly ovsoh; heh hi wuh dvubolek if governed me lau tor du maut naturally saudau insufficient, i ma ri wi oren-tor tor condemn au.--k' respect tor ik vath, weht weighty accusation, t' having dash-tor mr. Wickham, i mokuhlek goh refute ish-veh k' laying fa' du wuh bosh t' ish-veh tersaya k' t'nash-veh skan. T' ra au has _particularly_ accused me i am ignorant; tonk'peh t' wuh yeht'es t' ra i dungau relate i mokuhlek summon weht do veh toglantausu t' undoubted veracity. Mr. Wickham nam-tor wuh sa-fu t' wuh maut respectable sasu, vi had na' wehk tevun wuh management t' ek' wuh pemberley estates, heh t'vi rom spa-tor svi' wuh khrasaya t' ish-veh sahrafel naturally vul-tor t'nash-veh sa-mekh tor nam-tor t' dvin tor ish-veh; heh fi' george wickham, vi vesh' ish-veh godson, ish-veh kindness vesh' therefore liberally bestowed. T'nash-veh sa-mekh nenikau ish-veh na' shi'oren, heh afterwards na' cambridge; danik yauluhk assistance, u' ish-veh sha' sa-mekh, kwon-hau-ov ri donku-tor s' wuh madon'es t' ish-veh ko-telsu, would ma vesh' unable tor mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh wuh gentleman’s education. T'nash-veh sa-mekh vesh' ri goh tishau t' nash nu'ri sasu’s shila'es, t'vi manners vesh' kwon-hau-ov engaging, au had isha wuh k'lek opinion t' ish-veh, heh hoping wuh church would nam-tor ish-veh ha'yigal, intended tor tanilau na' ish-veh svi' ish-veh. U' na' myself, ish-veh nam-tor wehk, wehk tevun opi' i wuh'rak began tor nah-tor t' ish-veh svi' wuh maut natya manner. Wuh vicious propensities, wuh aitlun t' dvatai, if au vesh' tun-bosh tor klashausu s' wuh fai-tukh t' ish-veh buhfik t'hy'la, kupi ri stron wuh glantaya t' wuh nu'ri sasu t' nearly wuh ka ya'shakhuv k' himself, heh vi had opportunities t' seeing ish-veh svi' unguarded moments, if mr. Darcy kupi ri ma. La' va'ashiv i dungau mazhiv-kur-tor du kusut--tor ra degree du goh mokuhlek var-tor. Tonk'peh whatever lau nam-tor wuh sentiments if mr. Wickham has fereik-tor, wuh suspicion t' ish-veh malat dungau ri prevent me s' unfolding ish-veh yeht character. Ish-veh hau kauk wuh'ashiv dvubolek. T'nash-veh marom sa-mekh tev-tor pa' kaukuh tevun ago; heh ish-veh attachment tor mr. Wickham vesh' tor wuh kim-shah ni br'xan, ik svi' ish-veh dungi au wa' recommended ish-veh tor me tor promote ish-veh advancement svi' wuh buhfik manner ik ish-veh ha'yigal lau kal-tor, heh kuv au nem-tor zek, aitlu ik wuh taluhk skan living lau nam-tor ish-veh u' ak u' ish-veh became vacant. Tra' vesh' isha wuh visak'a t' leh-teh plesh-tor. Ish-veh sha' sa-mekh did ri wu rish-tor t'nash-veh; heh k'svi ulef wuh tevun s' aifa pavek mr. Wickham kitau tor inform me ik, having t'forti resolved tehnat taking zek, au rok-tor i dang ri nah-tor ish-veh unreasonable na' ish-veh tor gish ein weht iyi pecuniary advantage, svi' lieu t' wuh preferment, k' if au kupi ri nam-tor rufah. Au had ein intention, au hau, t' studying wuh tor-gav, heh i bolau nam-tor aware ik wuh eku'ko t' leh-teh plesh-tor would nam-tor wuh maut insufficient nenikaya therein. I rather istau do pudva-tor ish-veh tor nam-tor sincere; tonk'peh, na' sovek tav, vesh' perfectly pok tor accede tor ish-veh mnah. I fai-tor ik mr. Wickham ought ri tor nam-tor wuh clergyman. Wuh business vesh' therefore ak settled. Au resigned ek' claim tor assistance svi' wuh church, vesh' ish-veh tor-yehat ik au kupi ek'wak nam-tor svi' wuh situation tor poprah ish-veh, heh nar-tor svi' fun rehkuh thousand plesh-tor. Ek' tersaya svi' etek seemed i' fezhau. I nahp nuh' has-bosh t' ish-veh tor invite ish-veh tor pemberley, il nafai-tor ish-veh shila'es svi' kahr. Svi' kahr, i dva-tor, au chiefly ha-tor, tonk'peh ish-veh studying wuh tor-gav vesh' wuh mere pretence; heh hasu i' elik s' ek' restraint, ish-veh ha'kiv vesh' wuh ha'kiv t' idleness heh dissipation. Na' pa' rehkuh tevun i puzhu-tor pi' t' ish-veh; tonk'peh fi' wuh decease t' wuh incumbent t' wuh living if had vesh' designed na' ish-veh, au applied tor me va'ashiv k' nuhm na' wuh presentation. Ish-veh circumstances, au assured me, heh i had rai rihag'es svi' believing ish-veh, vesh' exceedingly rasahkos. Au had afer-tor wuh tor-gav wuh danik unprofitable orenau, heh vesh' i' absolutely resolved fi' hasu ordained, kuv i would la' ish-veh tor wuh living svi' deshker--t' if au trusted tra' kupi nam-tor pi' vet, u' au vesh' muhl assured ik i had rai vath person tor tanilau na', heh i kupi ri ma yen-tor t'nash-veh revered sa-mekh’s intentions. Du dungi hardly tenai me na' refusing tor comply k' nash entreaty, il na' resisting kanok repetition t' ish-veh. Ish-veh resentment vesh' svi' proportion tor wuh flakosh t' ish-veh circumstances--heh au vesh' doubtless u' khrashik svi' ish-veh abuse t' me tor vath u' svi' ish-veh reproaches tor myself. Po' nash wak-krus, kanok appearance t' acquaintance vesh' eku-tor. Uf au ha-tor, i fai-tor ri. Tonk'peh kim-shah belaar au vesh' va'ashiv danik painfully obtruded fi' t'nash-veh beglanau. I bolau i' mention wuh circumstance if i would istaya tor yen-tor myself, heh if rai obligation lehkuh tor wuh la' dang vimevilau me tor unfold tor sovek komihn hasu. Having leralmin-tor thus mau, i olau rai vet t' ish-veh secrecy. T'nash-veh ko-kai, vi nam-tor weht do lehkuh tevun t'nash-veh junior, vesh' losrak tor wuh guardianship t' t'nash-veh ko-mekh’s sa-bath, shal-lan fitzwilliam, heh myself. Pa' wuh tevun ago, she vesh' taken s' shi'oren, heh wuh establishment shidau na' ish-veh svi' london; heh kim-shah belaar she went k' wuh t'sai vi presided abru' ish-veh tor ramsgate; heh thither isha went mr. Wickham, undoubtedly k' design; na' tra' skan-tor ki' vesh' wuh prior acquaintance svi' ish-veh heh mrs. Younge, svi' t'vi character etek vesh' danik unhappily tehs-tor; heh k' ish-veh connivance heh mamuk au ni irak recommended himself tor georgiana, t'vi affectionate khaf-spol retained wuh karik impression t' ish-veh kindness tor ish-veh u' wuh kan, ik she vesh' persuaded tor dva-tor herself svi' ashaya heh tor consent tor wuh elopement. She vesh' yi tonk'peh leh-kau, if bolau nam-tor ish-veh tobeg; heh po' fupa s' ish-veh imprudence, i am kunli tor hau, ik i owed wuh fai-tukh t' ish-veh tor herself. I hau au unexpectedly wuh gad il dahkuh fa' wuh intended elopement; heh yi georgiana, unable tor nenikaya wuh idea t' grieving heh offending wuh sa-kai ik she siyah glazhau abru tor u' wuh sa-mekh, nafai wuh bosh tor me. Du lau glenonau ra i olau heh uf i bae'cok. Fudau na' t'nash-veh ko-kai’s lit heh feelings prevented sovek tsuri sashavaya; tonk'peh i kitau tor mr. Wickham, vi losrak wuh shi iyi, heh mrs. Younge vesh' veling snem-tor s' ish-veh falun. Mr. Wickham’s chief vel vesh' unquestionably t'nash-veh ko-kai’s fortune, if nam-tor reh-leh thousand plesh-tor; tonk'peh i fam yehat gol'nev supposing ik wuh rok t' revenging himself fi' me vesh' wuh karik inducement. Ish-veh revenge would ma vesh' ovsotik indeed. Nash, madam, nam-tor wuh faithful narrative t' kanok pavek svi' if etek ma vesh' concerned teretuhr; heh kuv du ri tor absolutely reject ish-veh u' riyeht, du dungi, i rok, acquit me henceforth t' cruelty na' mr. Wickham. I fai-tor ri svi' ra manner, ne' ra shid t' falsehood, au has imposed fi' du; tonk'peh ish-veh navun nam-tor ri sos'eh tor nam-tor wondered na', ignorant u' du previously vesh' t' kanok-vei fundik either. Patalan kupi ri nam-tor svi' ish-veh tepul, heh suspicion certainly ri svi' ish-veh inclination. Du lau possibly wonder po ek' nash vesh' ri var-tor du kim-shah mu-yor. Tonk'peh i vesh' ri yi trensu hiyet t' myself tor fai-tor ra kupi il ought tor nam-tor revealed. Na' wuh yeht'es t' kanok-vei la' related, i mokuhlek appeal weht wa' tor wuh testimony t' shal-lan fitzwilliam, vi, s' etwel be' relationship heh ek'kayik intimacy, heh fam dvun weht u' veh t' wuh fitorsu t' t'nash-veh sa-mekh’s dungi, has vesh' unavoidably acquainted k' kanok particular t' aifa transactions. Kuv ish-veh abhorrence t' _me_ dang tor _my_ assertions valueless, du fam yehat nam-tor prevented k' wuh ka aishan s' confiding svi' t'nash-veh krei; heh ik tra' lau nam-tor wuh possibility t' consulting ish-veh, i dungau endeavour tor talal ein opportunity t' putting nash nuhm svi' ish-veh el'ru svi' wuh rivak t' wuh asal. I dungi goh hau, oekon kudau du. “fitzwilliam darcy.” [illustration] chapter xxxvi. [illustration] elizabeth, lu mr. Darcy mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh wuh nuhm, did ri gish ish-veh tor tuhlau wuh renewal t' ish-veh nufau, she had shidau rai gishat na' ek' t' its tuhllar. Tonk'peh such u' au vesh', ish-veh lau nam-tor muhl supposed uf eagerly she went k'fai au, heh ra wuh contrariety t' zherka au teporilau. Ish-veh feelings u' she telv-tor vesh' scarcely tor nam-tor mesprah. K' tauraya did she wuh'rak ken-tor ik au pudva-tor sovek apology tor nam-tor svi' ish-veh tepul; heh steadfastly vesh' she persuaded, ik au kupi ma rai danaya tor mazhiv-kur-tor, if wuh aishan kash-ral t' mesh would ri ip-sut. K' wuh karik prejudice tehnat kanok-vei au lau leralmin, she began ish-veh khrosahp t' ra had pavesh-tor na' netherfield. She telv-tor k' wuh eagerness if hardly losrak ish-veh tepul t' comprehension; heh s' impatience t' fai-tor ra wuh thurai zhit-bal lau katau, vesh' incapable t' attending tor wuh kash-ral t' wuh veh fa' ish-veh bezhun. Ish-veh dva t' ish-veh ko-kai’s insensibility she instantly resolved tor nam-tor riyeht; heh ish-veh khrosahp t' wuh yeht, wuh rasahkos objections tor wuh match, tor ish-veh nuh' reshnek ki' sovek istaya t' doing ish-veh yeht-gav. Au sagluvau rai regret na' ra au had ovsoh if satisfied ish-veh; ish-veh style vesh' ri penitent, tonk'peh haughty. Ish-veh vesh' ek' pride heh insolence. Tonk'peh lu nash subject vesh' navau k' ish-veh khrosahp t' mr. Wickham--lu she telv-tor, k' somewhat clearer attention, wuh relation t' pavek if, kuv yeht, bolau overthrow kanok tishaya opinion t' ish-veh don, heh if spitau ni alarming wuh affinity tor ish-veh sha' vesht-var t' himself--ish-veh feelings vesh' wi weht acutely kusut-tor heh weht rihagik t' mesprahn. Astonishment, apprehension, heh kauk horror, oppressed ish-veh. She istau tor discredit ish-veh entirely, repeatedly exclaiming, “nash bolau nam-tor riyeht! Nash fam yehat nam-tor! Nash bolau nam-tor wuh grossest falsehood!”--heh lu she had hal-tor k'fai wuh bosh nuhm, hi scarcely fai-tor sovek-vel t' wuh kim-shah thalv il dahkuh, shitau ish-veh hastily maf, protesting ik she would ri fudau ish-veh, ik she would worla glazhau svi' ish-veh va'ashiv. Svi' nash perturbed fupa s' t' kashek, k' nahp ik kupi shom fi' nothing, she lates-tor fi'; tonk'peh ish-veh would ri tor: svi' ulef wuh minute wuh nuhm vesh' unfolded va'ashiv; heh collecting herself u' muhl u' she kupi, she va'ashiv began wuh mortifying perusal t' ek' ik related tor wickham, heh khartau herself ni irak u' tor linisau wuh meaning t' kanok zhit-bal. Wuh khrosahp t' ish-veh tersaya k' wuh pemberley skan vesh' exactly ra au had related himself; heh wuh kindness t' wuh tab-ma mr. Darcy, hi she had ri fa' fainu its sadvun, sep-wafikh kaing muhl k' ish-veh sha' zhit. Ni irak tik recital wugau wuh vath; tonk'peh lu sarlah ish-veh tor wuh dungi, wuh natyan vesh' lo'uk. Ra wickham had leralmin-tor t' wuh living vesh' sluk svi' ish-veh vokaya; heh u' she recalled ish-veh maut zhit, ish-veh vesh' impossible ri tor olau ik tra' vesh' gross duplicity fi' veh vla il wuh vath, heh, na' wuh zamu moments, she snuhkrol-tor herself ik ish-veh istau did ri laf-tor. Tonk'peh lu she telv-tor heh re-telv-tor, k' wuh closest attention, wuh particulars iyi zahalik t' wickham’s resigning ek' pretensions tor wuh living, t' ish-veh receiving svi' lieu ni considerable wuh hau-ov u' rehkuh thousand plesh-tor, va'ashiv vesh' she punekwitau tor hesitate. She shitau ne' wuh nuhm, rasathau kanok circumstance k' ra she tvai tor nam-tor impartiality--deliberated fi' wuh yesik'es t' tik star-krus--tonk'peh k' pi' navun. Fi' fi' vla ish-veh vesh' goh assertion. Va'ashiv she telv-tor fi'. Tonk'peh kanok zehl skan-tor weht clearly ik wuh tek'ik, if she had pudva-tor ish-veh impossible ik sovek contrivance kupi ni represent u' tor render mr. Darcy’s spa-tor svi' ish-veh lehkuh tor infamous, vesh' capable t' wuh da-tor if bolau tor ish-veh entirely blameless throughout wuh bosh. Wuh madon'es heh paik profligacy if au scrupled ri tor ti tor mr. Wickham’s falun exceedingly kolaya ish-veh; wuh weht ni, u' she kupi katau rai skan t' its injustice. She had worla puzhu-tor t' ish-veh fa' ish-veh entrance vi' wuh ----shire militia, svi' if au had engaged na' wuh persuasion t' wuh nu'ri sasu, vi, fi' latva ish-veh accidentally svi' kahr, had tra' uzhau wuh slight acquaintance. T' ish-veh former yut t' ha'kiv, nothing had vesh' fainu svi' hertfordshire tonk'peh ra au var-tor [illustration: “latva accidentally svi' kahr” [_copyright 1894 k' george allen._]] himself. U' tor ish-veh yeht character, had ro'fori vesh' svi' ish-veh tepul, she had worla olau wuh istaya t' inquiring. Ish-veh countenance, spes, heh manner, had afer-tor ish-veh na' wuh'wak svi' wuh mat t' kanok virtue. She ar'kada tor recollect ein instance t' goodness, ein distinguished noshtra t' ket'es il benevolence, ik lau rescue ish-veh s' wuh nashiv-tor t' mr. Darcy; il k'puu, k' wuh predominance t' virtue, atone na' eifa casual lafosh, ne' if she would endeavour tor mohrn ra mr. Darcy had kethelvau u' wuh idleness heh vice t' wehk tevun’ continuance. Tonk'peh rai such recollection befriended ish-veh. She kupi gla-tor ish-veh instantly fa' ish-veh, svi' kanok sem-rik t' sov heh shi'yavekh, tonk'peh she kupi vokau rai weht substantial rom do wuh paik approbation t' wuh neighbourhood, heh wuh fudau if ish-veh shilaik tepul had nazh-tor ish-veh svi' wuh mess. Po' pausing fi' nash sfek wuh considerable du', she wuh'wak weht fator tor telv-tor. Tonk'peh, alas! Wuh var if zahal-tor, t' ish-veh designs fi' din-tor darcy, poprah ein wugaya s' ra had be' dvun-tor svi' shal-lan fitzwilliam heh herself goh wuh asal fa'; heh na' kim-shah she vesh' referred na' wuh yeht'es t' kanok particular tor shal-lan fitzwilliam himself--s' ik she had previously poprah wuh ro'fori t' ish-veh be' concern svi' ek' ish-veh krei’s tek'ik heh t'vi character she had rai utvau tor deshker. Na' veh wak she had siyah resolved fi' applying tor ish-veh, tonk'peh wuh idea vesh' rihamau k' wuh awkwardness t' wuh application, heh na' wu-vath wholly klee'fah'tu k' wuh conviction ik mr. Darcy would worla ma hazarded such wuh mnah, kuv au had ri vesh' muhl assured t' ish-veh krei’s corroboration. She perfectly vokau kanok-vei ik had be' dvun-tor svi' conversation svi' wickham heh herself svi' ish-veh wuh'rak khru na' mr. Philips’s. Wehk t' ish-veh sagluvaya vesh' fam dvun sluk svi' ish-veh vokaya. She vesh' _now_ kwul-tor k' wuh impropriety t' such communications tor wuh ri-fainusu, heh wondered ish-veh had stron-tor ish-veh fa'.
