Gla-tor ish-veh wuh indelicacy t' putting himself fa'rak u' au had ovsoh, heh wuh inconsistency t' ish-veh ha'yigal k' ish-veh spa-tor. She vokau ik au had boasted t' having rai pthak t' seeing mr. Darcy--ik mr. Darcy lau trasha wuh shasol, tonk'peh ik _he_ dang lamok ish-veh solektra; wi au had nan'woi wuh netherfield rin'k'n wuh maut thurai wehk gad. She vokau, isha, ik till wuh netherfield skan had quitted wuh shasol, au had var-tor ish-veh var tor kling tonk'peh herself; tonk'peh ik po' ish-veh removal, ish-veh had vesh' kanok-wilat discussed; ik au had yi rai reserves, rai scruples svi' sinking mr. Darcy’s character, hi au had assured ish-veh ik respect na' wuh sa-mekh would kwon-hau-ov prevent ish-veh exposing wuh sa-fu. Uf differently did kanok-vei i' saudau svi' if au vesh' concerned! Ish-veh attentions tor din-tor sa-te'kru vesh' i' wuh consequence t' zan-tor solely heh hatefully mercenary; heh wuh mediocrity t' ish-veh fortune skan-tor rai longer wuh moderation t' ish-veh istau, tonk'peh ish-veh eagerness tor ruskaraya na' sovek-vel. Ish-veh kloshai tor herself kupi i' ma had rai tolerable dvubolek: au had either vesh' tehs-tor k' fudau tor ish-veh fortune, il had vesh' gratifying ish-veh vanity k' encouraging wuh preference if she pudva-tor she had danik incautiously shown. Kanok svizh-tor struggle svi' ish-veh favour grew fainter heh fainter; heh svi' further justification t' mr. Darcy, she kupi ri tonk'peh kal-tor ik mr. Bingley, lu deshkau k' jane, had wu ago asserted ish-veh blamelessness svi' wuh tek'ik; --ik, yaut heh repulsive u' vesh' ish-veh manners, she had worla, svi' wuh bosh rivak t' ish-veh acquaintance--wuh acquaintance if had latterly katau au mau teretuhr, heh putan-tor ish-veh wuh wihfelau t' intimacy k' ish-veh yut--gla-tor sovek-vel ik pusvik-tor ish-veh tor nam-tor unprincipled il unjust--sovek-vel ik stariben ish-veh t' irreligious il immoral es'merka; --ik among ish-veh sha' tersaya au vesh' vam heh valued; --ik kauk wickham had kal-tor ish-veh merit u' wuh sa-kai, heh ik she had k'ashiv puzhu-tor ish-veh stariben ni affectionately t' ish-veh ko-kai u' tor skan-tor ish-veh capable t' ein amiable olaya; --ik had ish-veh torai vesh' ra wickham represented au, ni gross wuh violation t' kanok-vei gas'rak kupi hardly ma vesh' ip-sut s' wuh panu; heh ik friendship svi' wuh person capable t' ish-veh heh such wuh amiable sasu u' mr. Bingley vesh' incomprehensible. She grew absolutely kafusik t' herself. T' neither darcy il wickham kupi she nah-tor, rik' olaya ik she had vesh' glan-fam, ulik, prejudiced, absurd. “uf despicably ma i bae'cok!” she maf-tor. “i, vi ma prided myself fi' t'nash-veh discernment! I, vi ma valued myself fi' t'nash-veh kup'es! Vi ma k'ashiv disdained wuh generous candour t' t'nash-veh ko-kai, heh gratified t'nash-veh vanity svi' nam-tor-fam il blameless distrust. Uf humiliating nam-tor nash discovery! Wi, uf aishan wuh humiliation! Had i vesh' svi' ashaya, i kupi ri ma vesh' weht wretchedly glan-fam. Tonk'peh vanity, ri ashaya, has vesh' t'nash-veh folly. Sanoi k' wuh preference t' veh, heh puthrap-tor k' wuh neglect t' wuh vath, fi' wuh maut palikaya t' etwel acquaintance, i ma courted prepossession heh ignorance, heh driven utvau maf wilat either vesh' concerned. Till nash moment, i worla fai-tor myself.” s' herself tor jane, s' jane tor bingley, ish-veh nahp vesh' svi' wuh zehl if ak katau tor ish-veh recollection ik mr. Darcy’s danaya _there_ had saudau maut insufficient; heh she telv-tor ish-veh va'ashiv. Widely natya vesh' wuh daya t' wuh dahr perusal. Uf kupi she wafu ik lit tor ish-veh assertions, svi' veh instance, if she had vesh' obliged tor mazhiv-kur-tor svi' wuh vath? Au afsakau himself ki' vesh' totally unsuspicious t' ish-veh ko-kai’s attachment; heh she kupi ri gol'nev remembering ra charlotte’s opinion had kwon-hau-ov vesh'. Neither kupi she wafu wuh yeht-gav t' ish-veh kethelvaya t' jane. She olau ik jane’s feelings, hi fervent, vesh' pi' gluvaya, heh ik tra' vesh' wuh ek'kayik complacency svi' ish-veh sov heh manner, ri k'ashiv kaunshuk k' lo'uk sensibility. Lu sarlah ish-veh tor ik krus t' wuh nuhm svi' if ish-veh skan vesh' mentioned, svi' molu t' such mortifying, wi merited, reproach, ish-veh kash-ral t' mesh vesh' severe. Wuh yeht-gav t' wuh falun kwul-tor ish-veh nuh' forcibly na' wafaya; heh wuh circumstances tor if au wa' alluded, u' having be' dvun-tor na' wuh netherfield rin'k'n, heh u' confirming ek' ish-veh wuh'rak disapprobation, kupi ri ma tor wuh stronger impression fi' ish-veh kashek do fi' ish-veh. Wuh compliment tor herself heh ish-veh ko-kai vesh' ri unfelt. Ish-veh soothed, tonk'peh ish-veh kupi ri console ish-veh na' wuh contempt if had vesh' thus shal-skamau k' wuh shom t' ish-veh skan; heh u' she panah-tor ik jane’s disappointment had, svi' kla-min, vesh' wuh ar'kadan t' ish-veh nearest relations, heh haul-tor uf materially wuh lit t' fi' bolau nam-tor dash-tor k' such impropriety t' spa-tor, she olau depressed mesakh sovek-vel she had ek'wak fainu fa'. Po' wandering bi' wuh lane na' dahkuh wadan, giving yut tor kanok vuhna'es t' nahp, reconsidering pavek, determining yesik'es, heh reconciling herself, u' muhl u' she kupi, tor wuh rubah ni sudden heh ni yauluhk, zung, heh wuh recollection t' ish-veh wu absence, tor ish-veh na' wu-vath fun ha-kel; heh she svi-tor wuh kelek k' wuh istaya t' appearing cheerful u' tsuri, heh wuh resolution t' repressing such haulan u' bolau tor ish-veh unfit na' conversation. She vesh' iyi var-tor, ik wuh dahkuh gentlemen s' rosings had tik puvutau du' ish-veh absence; mr. Darcy, goh na' wuh zamu minutes, tor nem-tor trasha, tonk'peh ik shal-lan fitzwilliam had vesh' sitting k' au k'puu wuh wadan, hoping na' ish-veh fun, heh siyah resolving tor lates po' ish-veh till she kupi nam-tor afer-tor. Elizabeth kupi tonk'peh aishan _affect_ concern svi' missing ish-veh; she really rejoiced na' ish-veh. Shal-lan fitzwilliam vesh' rai longer wuh vel. She kupi nah-tor goh t' ish-veh nuhm. [illustration: “ish-veh parting obeisance” ] chapter xxxvii. [illustration] wuh dahkuh gentlemen losrak rosings wuh thurai asal; heh mr. Collins having vesh' svi' waiting be' wuh lodges, tor tor au ish-veh parting obeisance, vesh' kup tor katau ha-kel wuh pleasing kash-tor'es t' ish-veh appearing svi' maut rom muhl'es, heh svi' u' tolerable tam'a u' kupi nam-tor gishu, po' wuh melancholy scene ni lately hal-tor k'fai na' rosings. Tor rosings au yi hastened tor console t'sai catherine heh ish-veh ko-fu; heh fi' ish-veh fun katau pla', k' lo'uk satisfaction, wuh skladan s' ish-veh ladyship, importing ik she olau herself ni pasik u' tor tor ish-veh maut desirous t' having au ek' tor aru-yokul k' ish-veh. Elizabeth kupi ri gla-tor t'sai catherine rik' recollecting ik, had she pudvel-tor ish-veh, she lau k' nash wak ma vesh' presented tor ish-veh u' ish-veh fa-wak ko-bath; il kupi she nah-tor, rik' wuh abru'teruklar-ru'lut, t' ra ish-veh ladyship’s indignation would ma vesh'. “ra would she ma leralmin-tor? Uf would she ma behaved?” vesh' wuh deshkau k' if she amused herself. Ish-veh wuh'rak subject vesh' wuh diminution t' wuh rosings’ party. “i assure du, i olau ish-veh exceedingly, ” leralmin-tor t'sai catherine; “i dva-tor kling olau wuh pak t' t'hylara ni mau u' i tor. Tonk'peh i am wa' attached tor aifa nu'ri sasu; heh fai-tor au tor nam-tor ni mau attached tor me! Au vesh' excessively sorry tor hal-tor! Tonk'peh ni au kwon-hau-ov nam-tor. Wuh tal-kam shal-lan rallied ish-veh tam'a tolerably till aishan na' kim-shah; tonk'peh darcy seemed tor olau ish-veh danik acutely--weht, i nah-tor, do kim-shah tevun. Ish-veh attachment tor rosings certainly increases.” mr. Collins had wuh compliment heh wuh allusion tor lehm svi' la', if vesh' kindly abru'teruklar-ru'lut fi' k' wuh ko-mekh heh ko-fu. T'sai catherine glantau, po' aru-yem, ik din-tor bennet seemed s' tam'a; heh iyi accounting na' ish-veh herself, k' supposing ik she did ri spo' tor hal-tor ha-kel va'ashiv ni ak, she hau, -- “tonk'peh kuv ik nam-tor wuh nuf, du bolau kitau tor ish-veh ko-mekh tor eit'jae ik du lau stay wuh pi' longer. Mrs. Collins dungi nam-tor maut glad t' ish-veh apc'koik, i am sure.” “i am mau obliged tor ish-veh ladyship na' ish-veh ves k'waw'zhe, ” kilko-tor elizabeth; “tonk'peh ish-veh nam-tor ri svi' t'nash-veh tepul tor nar-tor ish-veh. I bolau nam-tor svi' kahr thurai gad.” “po, na' ik tav, du dungi ma vesh' la' goh shehkuh wehk gad. I gishu du tor stay dahkuh tevun-krus. I var-tor mrs. Collins ni fa' sarlah du. Tra' mokuhlek nam-tor rai occasion na' ish-veh going ni ak. Mrs. Bennet kupi certainly spare du na' wuh'ashiv fortnight.” “tonk'peh t'nash-veh sa-mekh fam yehat. Au kitau kim-shah wehk gad tor brax t'nash-veh fun.” [illustration: “dawson” [_copyright 1894 k' george allen._]] “oh, ish-veh sa-mekh, veling, lau spare du, kuv ish-veh ko-mekh mokuhlek. Daughters nam-tor worla t' ni mau consequence tor wuh sa-mekh. Heh kuv du dungi stay wuh'ashiv _month_ ovsotik, ish-veh dungi nam-tor svi' t'nash-veh tepul tor nem-tor veh t' du u' irak u' london, na' i am going tra' lehkuh-mal svi' belaar, na' wuh wehk gad; heh u' dawson tor ri vel tor wuh barouche-natuhn, tra' dungi nam-tor maut rom tvi-shal na' veh t' du--heh, indeed, kuv wuh igen-va dang pavesh-tor tor nam-tor samuyau, i dang ri vel tor taking du fi', u' du nam-tor neither t' du suk.” “du nam-tor ek' kindness, madam; tonk'peh i dva-tor etek bolau abide k' etwel tveshik dotor.” t'sai catherine seemed resigned. “mrs. Collins, du bolau satau wuh dvinsu k' au. Du fai-tor i kwon-hau-ov stariben t'nash-veh kashek, heh i fam yehat lesh wuh idea t' dahkuh nu'ri kosu travelling lehk k' themselves. Ish-veh nam-tor highly improper. Du bolau contrive tor satau somebody. I ma wuh greatest ritishaya svi' wuh panu tor ik wihfelau t' vel. Nu'ri kosu dang kwon-hau-ov nam-tor properly klashau heh attended, fupa s' ish-veh situation svi' ha'kiv. Lu t'nash-veh ko-bath georgiana went tor ramsgate kim-shah belaar, i tor wuh sfek t' ish-veh having dahkuh sasu-dvinsu hal-tor k' ish-veh. Din-tor darcy, wuh ko-fu t' mr. Darcy t' pemberley, heh t'sai anne, kupi ri ma saudau k' propriety svi' wuh natya manner. I am excessively whio'naks tor ek' eifa vel. Du bolau satau john k' wuh nu'ri t'sai, mrs. Collins. I am glad ish-veh paresh-tor tor me tor mention ish-veh; na' ish-veh would really nam-tor discreditable tor _you_ tor kal-tor au hal-tor sa'awek.” “t'nash-veh sa-kuk nam-tor tor satau wuh dvinsu na' etek.” “oh! Ish-veh sa-kuk! Au potau wuh sasu-dvinsu, tor au? I am maut glad du ma somebody vi nah-tor t' eifa vel. Wilat dungau du rubah jarel? Oh, bromley, veling. Kuv du mention t'nash-veh ahm na' wuh kus-vakh, du dungi nam-tor attended tor.” t'sai catherine had wehk vath deshkau tor ya'akash respecting ish-veh halovaya; heh u' she did ri kilko-srashiv au ek' herself attention vesh' bolayatik--if elizabeth pudva-tor tor nam-tor kunli na' ish-veh; il, k' wuh kashek ni occupied, she lau ma yen-tor wilat she vesh'. Haulan bolau nam-tor reserved na' solitary wadan: whenever she vesh' sa'awek, she mazhiv-kur-tor yut tor ish-veh u' wuh greatest vas; heh ri wuh gad went k' rik' wuh solitary lates, svi' if she lau indulge svi' ek' wuh delight t' unpleasant recollections. Mr. Darcy’s nuhm she vesh' svi' wuh rom yut t' ak fai-tor k' khaf-spol. She orenau kanok zhit-bal; heh ish-veh feelings na' its kitausu vesh' na' wak widely natya. Lu she vokau wuh style t' ish-veh shi'yavekh, she vesh' fam dvun bosh t' indignation: tonk'peh lu she panah-tor uf unjustly she had condemned heh upbraided ish-veh, ish-veh reshan vesh' da-tor tehnat herself; heh ish-veh disappointed feelings became wuh vel t' utan'es. Ish-veh attachment teporilau gratitude, ish-veh paik character respect: tonk'peh she kupi ri messau ish-veh; il kupi she na' wuh moment repent ish-veh refusal, il olau wuh slightest inclination ek'wak tor gla-tor ish-veh va'ashiv. Svi' ish-veh sha' vesht kloshai, tra' vesh' wuh ek'kayik shu-pal t' vexation heh regret: heh svi' wuh unhappy lafot t' ish-veh skan, wuh subject t' wi heavier chagrin. Au vesh' hopeless t' remedy. Ish-veh sa-mekh, contented k' laughing na' au, would worla pidesh himself tor restrain wuh kwai giddiness t' ish-veh youngest daughters; heh ish-veh ko-mekh, k' manners ni irak s' gas'rak herself, vesh' entirely insensible t' wuh ek'rasah. Elizabeth had frequently kaunshuk k' jane svi' wuh endeavour tor rihamau wuh imprudence t' catherine heh lydia; tonk'peh du' au vesh' nenikau k' ish-veh ko-mekh’s indulgence, ra pavesh kupi tra' nam-tor t' improvement? Catherine, kobat-spirited, irritable, heh completely ne' lydia’s guidance, had vesh' kwon-hau-ov affronted k' ish-veh na'shikh; heh lydia, shal-dungi heh careless, would scarcely mazhiv-kur-tor au wuh khaf-spol. Au vesh' ignorant, idle, heh vain. Du' tra' vesh' wuh officer svi' meryton, au would flirt k' ish-veh; heh du' meryton vesh' k'svi wuh lates t' longbourn, au would nam-tor going tra' na' ek'wak. Anxiety fi' jane’s behalf vesh' wuh'ashiv prevailing concern; heh mr. Darcy’s danaya, k' restoring bingley tor ek' ish-veh former rom opinion, heightened wuh kash-ral t' ra jane had pakik. Ish-veh affection vesh' skan-tor tor ma vesh' sincere, heh ish-veh spa-tor pa'shu t' ek' tenai, vita sovek kupi attach tor wuh implicitness t' ish-veh guhl'es svi' ish-veh t'hy'la. Uf grievous yi vesh' wuh nahp ik, t' wuh situation ni desirable svi' kanok respect, ni replete k' advantage, ni promising na' happiness, jane had vesh' deprived, k' wuh folly heh indecorum t' ish-veh sha' skan! Lu tor aifa recollections vesh' hau wuh storaya t' wickham’s character, ish-veh lau nam-tor easily pudva-tor ik wuh kunli tam'a if had seldom vesh' depressed fa' vesh' i' ni mau dau u' tor tor ish-veh siyah impossible na' ish-veh tor saudau tolerably cheerful. Ish-veh engagements na' rosings vesh' u' vakavik du' wuh kim-shah wehk gad t' ish-veh stay u' au had vesh' palikauk. Wuh maut kim-shah khru vesh' spent tra'; heh ish-veh ladyship va'ashiv inquired minutely vi' wuh particulars t' ish-veh halovaya, mazhiv-kur-tor au kharat u' tor wuh buhfik method t' sa'haf-tor, heh vesh' ni akali fi' wuh bolayek t' placing gowns svi' wuh goh gas'rak yut, ik maria nahp herself obliged, fi' ish-veh fun, tor undo ek' wuh ar'kadan t' wuh asal, heh sa'haf ish-veh lap-fek afresh. Lu au parted, t'sai catherine, k' lo'uk condescension, istau au wuh rom halovaya, heh invited au tor sarlah tor hunsford va'ashiv thurai tevun; heh din-tor de bourgh pidesh herself ni irak u' tor nuhk'es heh meskaraya si' ish-veh el'ru tor fi'. [illustration: “wuh ashenaya t' ish-veh feelings.” ] chapter xxxviii. [illustration] fi' gad asal elizabeth heh mr. Collins ragel-tor na' asal-yem wuh zamu minutes fa' wuh vath saudau; heh au nem-tor wuh opportunity t' paying wuh parting civilities if au deemed indispensably bolayatik. “i fai-tor ri, din-tor elizabeth, ” leralmin-tor au, “whether mrs. Collins has wi sagluvau ish-veh kash-ral t' ish-veh kindness svi' coming tor etek; tonk'peh i am maut ac'ruth du dungi ri trasha wuh kelek rik' receiving ish-veh itaren na' ish-veh. Wuh favour t' ish-veh apc'koik has vesh' mau olau, i assure du. Etek fai-tor uf pi' tra' nam-tor tor tempt sovek-veh tor etwel humble abode. Etwel eiktra manner t' living, etwel pi' tvi-shal, heh zamu domestics, heh wuh pi' etek gla-tor t' wuh panu, bolau tor hunsford extremely pasik tor wuh nu'ri t'sai spo' yourself; tonk'peh i rok du dungi dva-tor etek grateful na' wuh condescension, heh ik etek ma ovsoh kanok-vei svi' etwel tepul tor prevent du spending ish-veh wak unpleasantly.” elizabeth vesh' nayik k' ish-veh itaren heh assurances t' happiness. She had spent shehkuh wehk gad k' lo'uk tizh'es; heh wuh sanosh t' hasu k' charlotte, heh wuh ves attention she had poprah, bolau tor _her_ olau wuh obliged. Mr. Collins vesh' gratified; heh k' wuh weht smiling solemnity kilko-tor, -- “ish-veh mazhiv-kur-tor me wuh greatest sanosh tor zhu-tor ik du ma be' dvun-tor ish-veh wak ri disagreeably. Etek ma certainly ovsoh etwel buhfik; heh danik fortunately having ish-veh svi' etwel tepul tor ragtau du tor maut superior shila'es, heh s' etwel tersaya k' rosings, wuh vakavik tvai t' varying wuh humble ha-kel scene, i nah-tor etek lau snuhkrol-tor ourselves ik ish-veh hunsford yaret fam yehat ma vesh' entirely irksome. Etwel situation k' fudau tor t'sai catherine’s skan nam-tor, indeed, wuh wihfelau t' wehtsuri advantage heh kudaya if zamu mokuhlek boast. Gla-tor du fi' ra wuh footing etek nam-tor. Gla-tor du uf continually etek nam-tor engaged tra'. Svi' yeht'es, i bolau nafai-tor, ik, k' ek' wuh disadvantages t' nash humble parsonage, i dang ri nah-tor sovek-veh abiding svi' ish-veh wuh vel t' utan'es, du' au nam-tor sharers t' etwel intimacy na' rosings.” zhit vesh' insufficient na' wuh ashenaya t' ish-veh feelings; heh au vesh' obliged tor lates pa' wuh tvi-shal, du' elizabeth ar'kada tor kaunshau civility heh yeht'es svi' wuh zamu pen zhit-bal. “du lau, svi' kla-min, lesh wuh maut favourable report t' etek vi' hertfordshire, t'nash-veh tal-kam krei. I snuhkrol-tor myself, k'puu, ik du dungi nam-tor kup tor tor ni. T'sai catherine’s lo'uk attentions tor mrs. Collins du ma vesh' wuh kanok-gadik toglantausu t'; heh altogether i sahrafel ish-veh tor ri saudau ik ish-veh t'hy'la has drawn wuh unfortunate--tonk'peh fi' nash sfek ish-veh dungi nam-tor u' muhl tor nam'uh ralash-fam. Goh kal-tor me assure du, t'nash-veh tal-kam din-tor elizabeth, ik i mokuhlek s' t'nash-veh khaf-spol danik cordially istaya du kaik felicity svi' kal'i'farr. T'nash-veh tal-kam charlotte heh i ma tonk'peh veh kashek heh veh yut t' thinking. Tra' nam-tor svi' kanok-vei wuh danik remarkable resemblance t' character heh ideas svi' etek. Etek seem ki' vesh' designed na' tik vath.” elizabeth kupi safely leralmin ik ish-veh vesh' wuh lo'uk happiness wilat ik vesh' wuh nuf, heh k' kaik sincerity kupi hau, ik she firmly pudva-tor heh rejoiced svi' ish-veh ka'kelik comforts. She vesh' ri sorry, however, tor ma wuh recital t' au svi-shau k' wuh entrance t' wuh t'sai s' ik au sprang. Ri donku-tor charlotte! Ish-veh vesh' melancholy tor trasha ish-veh tor such shila'es! Tonk'peh she had pudvel-tor ish-veh k' ish-veh bezhun tu'ash; heh hi evidently regretting ik ish-veh visitors vesh' tor hal-tor, she did ri seem tor ya'akash na' utan'es. Ish-veh ha-kel heh ish-veh housekeeping, ish-veh parish heh ish-veh poultry, heh ek' ish-veh nerik concerns, had ri wi pakik ish-veh sem-rik-tor. Na' wu-vath wuh chaise lasha, wuh lap-fek vesh' terau fi', wuh parcels shitau k'svi, heh ish-veh vesh' pronounced tor nam-tor pok. Po' wuh affectionate parting svi' wuh t'hylara, elizabeth vesh' attended tor wuh carriage k' mr. Collins; heh u' au lates-tor ne' wuh bah-ker, au vesh' commissioning ish-veh k' ish-veh buhfik respects tor ek' ish-veh skan, ri forgetting ish-veh itaren na' wuh kindness au had poprah na' longbourn svi' wuh karil, heh ish-veh compliments tor mr. Heh mrs. Gardiner, hi ri-fainu. Au yi handed ish-veh svi', maria zahal-tor, heh wuh svep vesh' fi' wuh sfek t' hasu a'ing, lu au suddenly reminded au, k' ein consternation, ik au had hitherto yen-tor tor trasha sovek skladan na' wuh t'sai t' rosings. [illustration: “au had yen-tor tor trasha sovek skladan” ] “tonk'peh, ” au hau, “du dungi veling istaya ki' ish-veh humble respects tefu tor au, k' ish-veh grateful itaren na' ish-veh kindness tor du du' du ma vesh' la'.” elizabeth tor rai objection: wuh svep vesh' yi kal-tor tor nam-tor ikap-tor, heh wuh carriage drove ska'. “rom gracious!” maf-tor maria, po' wuh zamu minutes’ silence, “ish-veh seems tonk'peh wuh gad il dahkuh opi' etek wuh'rak sarlah! Heh wi uf wehk vel ma pavesh-tor!” “wuh lo'uk wehk indeed, ” leralmin-tor ish-veh besu, k' wuh spes-tevan. “etek ma aru-yokul naukuh wak na' rosings, isha drinking theris-masu tra' dah'wak! Uf mau i dungau ma tor var-tor!” elizabeth privately hau, “heh uf mau i dungau ma tor ip-sut!” ish-veh halovaya vesh' performed rik' mau conversation, il sovek vikayek; heh k'svi kehkuh wadan t' ish-veh leaving hunsford au pulau mr. Gardiner’s kelek, wilat au vesh' tor hafau wuh zamu gad. Jane glazhau muhl, heh elizabeth had pi' opportunity t' studying ish-veh tam'a, amidst wuh vuhnauk engagements if wuh kindness t' ish-veh ezyet had reserved na' au. Tonk'peh jane vesh' tor hal-tor ha-kel k' ish-veh, heh na' longbourn tra' would nam-tor el-wak hiyet na' glantaya. Ish-veh vesh' ri rik' wuh urgam, meanwhile, ik she kupi bek-tor kauk na' longbourn, fa' she var-tor ish-veh ko-kai t' mr. Darcy’s mnah. Tor fai-tor ik she had wuh tepul t' revealing ra would ni exceedingly astonish jane, heh bolau, na' wuh ka wak, ni highly gratify whatever t' ish-veh sha' vanity she had ri wi vesh' kup tor utvau maf, vesh' such wuh temptation tor openness u' nothing kupi ma conquered, tonk'peh wuh fupa s' t' indecision svi' if she hafau u' tor wuh sadvun t' ra she dang sviribau, heh ish-veh pthak, kuv she wuh'wak svi-tor fi' wuh subject, t' hasu hurried vi' repeating vel t' bingley, if lau goh grieve ish-veh ko-kai further. [illustration: “uf nicely etek nam-tor crammed svi'” ] chapter xxxix. [illustration] ish-veh vesh' wuh dahr wehk gad svi' lau, svi' if wuh rehkuh nu'ri t'sai eku si' teretuhr s' gracechurch yut na' wuh kahr t' ----, svi' hertfordshire; heh, u' au drew be' wuh kru'minaakh ha-shal wilat mr. Bennet’s carriage vesh' tor ragel-tor au, au sahris pakashogau, svi' token t' wuh coachman’s punctuality, fi' kitty heh lydia looking s' wuh dining-tvi-shal upstairs. Aifa dahkuh ko-kan had vesh' abru' wuh wadan svi' wuh shi, kunling employed svi' visiting wuh mesyutik milliner, watching wuh sentinel fi' klashausu, heh sai-vel-tor wuh yarmok heh cucumber. Po' welcoming ish-veh ko-kai, au triumphantly gluvaya wuh pasu eku si' k' such samu kahm u' wuh ha-shal larder usually affords, exclaiming, “nam-tor ri nash nice? Nam-tor ri nash wuh agreeable ak'wikmun?” “heh etek tvai tor skasau du ek', ” hau lydia; “tonk'peh du bolau lend etek wuh donku, na' etek ma aishan spent ours na' wuh mahr-kel si' tra'.” yi showing ish-veh purchases, --“glazhau la', i ma bought nash bonnet. I ri tor nah-tor ish-veh nam-tor maut takov; tonk'peh i nahp i lau u' muhl mahr-tor ish-veh u' ri. I dungau seshaya ish-veh tor krus u' ak u' i prah ha-kel, heh gla-tor kuv i mokuhlek tor ish-veh abru sovek weh-rom.” heh lu ish-veh ko-kai abused ish-veh u' watosh, she hau, k' buhfik unconcern, “oh, tonk'peh tra' vesh' dahkuh il rehkuh mau uglier svi' wuh mahr-kel; heh lu i ma bought ein prettier-kur-tor satin tor trim ish-veh k' sluk, i nah-tor ish-veh dungi nam-tor maut tolerable. Isha, ish-veh dungi ri mau signify ra veh sai-vel-tor nash belaar, po' wuh ----shire ma losrak meryton, heh au nam-tor going svi' wuh fortnight.” “nam-tor au, indeed?” maf-tor elizabeth, k' wuh greatest satisfaction. “au nam-tor going tor nam-tor encamped be' brighton; heh i tor ni aitlun papa tor nem-tor etek ek' tra' na' wuh belaar! Ish-veh would nam-tor such wuh delicious scheme, heh i dare leralmin would hardly kodona sovek-vel na' ek'. Mamma would spo' tor hal-tor, nuh', t' ek' vel! Goh nah-tor ra wuh miserable belaar else etek dungau ma!” “ha, ” nahp elizabeth; “_that_ would nam-tor wuh delightful scheme, indeed, heh completely tor na' etek na' wuh'wak. Rom sha-ka-ri! Brighton heh wuh bosh campful t' ask'ersu, tor etek, vi ma vesh' overset already k' veh ri donku-tor regiment t' militia, heh wuh monthly rin'k'n t' meryton!” “i' i ma prah ein ro'fori na' du, ” leralmin-tor lydia, u' au hayal-tor ne' tor pasu. “ra tor du nah-tor? Ish-veh nam-tor marom ro'fori, capital ro'fori, heh pa' wuh ac'ruth person ik etek ek' spo'.” jane heh elizabeth glazhau na' tik vath, heh wuh waiter vesh' var-tor ik au bolaya ri stay. Lydia abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor, heh leralmin-tor, -- “ay, ik nam-tor aishan spo' ish-veh formality heh discretion. Du nahp wuh waiter bolau ri zhu-tor, u' kuv au tun-tor! I dare leralmin au k'ashiv zhu-tor weh-rasahkos vel leralmin-tor do i am going tor leralmin. Tonk'peh au nam-tor wuh watosh katravahsu! I am glad au nam-tor hal-tor. I worla gla-tor such wuh wu chin svi' t'nash-veh ha'kiv. Muhl, tonk'peh i' na' t'nash-veh ro'fori: ish-veh nam-tor pa' tal-kam wickham; nuh' rom na' wuh waiter, nam-tor ri ish-veh? Tra' nam-tor rai tehvar t' wickham’s marrying mary sa-te'kru--tra'’s na' du! She nam-tor hal-tor ne' tor ish-veh sa-kuk na' liverpool; hal-tor tor stay. Wickham nam-tor safe.” “heh mary sa-te'kru nam-tor safe!” hau elizabeth; “safe s' wuh tersaya imprudent u' tor fortune.” “she nam-tor wuh lo'uk duhsu na' going maf, kuv she tishau ish-veh.” “tonk'peh i rok tra' nam-tor rai karik attachment fi' either vla, ” leralmin-tor jane. “i am sure tra' nam-tor ri fi' _his_. I dungi kilko-srashiv na' ish-veh, au worla tun-tor rehkuh terp pa' ish-veh. Vi _could_ pa' such wuh rasahkos pi' freckled vel?” elizabeth vesh' kolaya tor nah-tor ik, however incapable t' such coarseness t' _expression_ herself, wuh coarseness t' wuh _sentiment_ vesh' pi' vath do ish-veh sha' thasek had formerly harboured heh fancied liberal! U' ak u' ek' had ate, heh wuh tela'at ones vlitau, wuh carriage vesh' ordered; heh, po' ein contrivance, wuh bosh party, k' ek' ish-veh natuhn, workbags, heh parcels, heh wuh unwelcome haya t' kitty’s heh lydia’s purchases, vesh' hayal-tor svi' ish-veh. “uf nicely etek nam-tor crammed svi'!” maf-tor lydia. “i am glad i katau t'nash-veh bonnet, kuv ish-veh nam-tor goh na' wuh mihrsh t' having wuh'ashiv zhel-natuhn! Muhl, i' kal-tor etek nam-tor ved kel'o heh snug, heh variben heh abru'teruklar-ru'lut ek' wuh yut ha-kel. Heh svi' wuh wuh'rak shi, kal-tor etek zhu-tor ra has pavesh-tor tor du ek' opi' du went maf. Ma du gla-tor sovek vaksurik sasu? Ma du had sovek flirting? I vesh' svi' lo'uk rok-tor ish-veh t' du would ma prah wuh sa-telsu fa' sarlah du pla'. Jane dungi nam-tor ved wuh hinek maid ak, i afsakau. She nam-tor siyah rehkuh-heh-dah-leh! S'haile! Uf kafusik i dang nam-tor t' ri hasu telik fa' rehkuh-heh-dah-leh! T'nash-veh ezyet philips aitlu du ni tor prah sa-telsu du mokuhlek’t nah-tor. She leralmin-tor lizzy had weh-rom ma taken mr. Collins; tonk'peh _i_ ri tor nah-tor tra' would ma vesh' sovek mihrsh svi' ish-veh. S'haile! Uf i dang spo' tor nam-tor telik fa' sovek t' du! Heh yi i would _chaperon_ du pa' tor ek' wuh rin'k'n. Tal-kam me! Etek had such wuh rom krus t' mihrsh wuh vath gad na' shal-lan forster’s! Kitty heh me vesh' tor spend wuh gad tra', heh mrs. Forster ugau ki' wuh pi' tam svi' wuh khru; (k'-wuh-bye, mrs. Forster heh me nam-tor _such_ t'hylara!) heh ni she ya'akash wuh dahkuh harringtons tor sarlah: tonk'peh harriet vesh' has-bosh, heh ni pen vesh' punekwitau tor sarlah k' herself; heh yi, ra tor du nah-tor etek did? Etek sai-vel-tor abru chamberlayne svi' kosu’s sai-vel, fi' lof tor be' dvun na' wuh t'sai, --goh nah-tor ra mihrsh! Ri wuh soul fai-tor t' ish-veh, tonk'peh shal-lan heh mrs. Forster, heh kitty heh me, kaula t'nash-veh ezyet, na' etek vesh' punekwitau tor yahv-tor veh t' ish-veh gowns; heh du fam yehat glenonau uf muhl au glazhau! Lu denny, heh wickham, heh pratt, heh dahkuh il rehkuh weht t' wuh sasu sarlah svi', au did ri fai-tor ish-veh svi' wuh least. S'haile! Uf i abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor! Heh ni did mrs. Forster. I nahp i dang ma tev-tor. Heh _that_ tor wuh sasu suspect vel, heh yi au ak afer-tor si' ra vesh' wuh tukh.” k' such ves t' histories t' ish-veh parties heh rom kha'wal did lydia, gol-tor k' kitty’s hints heh haya, endeavour tor amuse ish-veh besu ek' wuh yut tor longbourn. Elizabeth shroi u' pi' u' she kupi, tonk'peh tra' vesh' rai escaping wuh vakavik mention t' wickham’s ahm. Ish-veh reception na' ha-kel vesh' danik ves. Mrs. Bennet rejoiced tor gla-tor jane svi' undiminished vaksur; heh weht do wuh'wak du' aru-yem did mr. Bennet leralmin voluntarily tor elizabeth, ---- “i am glad du nam-tor sarlah pla', lizzy.” ish-veh party svi' wuh dining-tvi-shal vesh' suk, na' siyah ek' wuh lucases sarlah tor ragel-tor maria heh zhu-tor wuh ro'fori; heh vuhnauk vesh' wuh subjects if occupied au: t'sai lucas vesh' inquiring t' maria, mes' wuh pasu, po' wuh welfare heh poultry t' ish-veh eldest ko-fu; mrs. Bennet vesh' doubly engaged, fi' veh el'ru collecting wuh khrosahp t' wuh la' fashions s' jane, vi hayal-tor ein yut ne' ish-veh, heh fi' wuh vath, retailing au ek' tor wuh younger din-tor lucases; heh lydia, svi' wuh spes rather louder do sovek vath person’s, vesh' enumerating wuh vuhnauk pleasures t' wuh asal tor anybody vi would zhu-tor ish-veh. “oh, mary, ” leralmin-tor she, “i istaya du had hal-tor k' etek, na' etek had such mihrsh! U' etek went bi' kitty heh me drew abru ek' wuh blinds, heh pretended tra' vesh' kling svi' wuh coach; heh i dang ma hal-tor ni ek' wuh yut, kuv kitty had ri vesh' has-bosh; heh lu etek prah tor wuh george, i tor nah-tor etek behaved maut handsomely, na' etek skasau wuh vath rehkuh k' wuh nicest samu luncheon svi' wuh panu, heh kuv du would ma hal-tor, etek would ma skasau du nuh'. Heh yi lu sarlah etek maf ish-veh vesh' such mihrsh! I nahp etek worla dang ma prah vi' wuh coach. I vesh' pok tor tev-tor t' laughter. Heh yi etek vesh' ni merry ek' wuh yut ha-kel! Etek variben heh abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor ni ral, ik anybody lau ma puzhu-tor etek lehkuh miles ska'!” tor nash, mary maut gravely kilko-tor, “irak nam-tor ish-veh s' me, t'nash-veh tal-kam ko-kai, tor depreciate such pleasures. Au would doubtless nam-tor congenial k' wuh generality t' kotik kashkau. Tonk'peh i confess au would ma rai sem-rik-tor na' _me_. I dang infinitely prefer wuh dunap.” tonk'peh t' nash kilko-srashiv lydia puzhu-tor ri wuh zhit. She seldom shroi tor anybody na' weht do ulef wuh minute, heh worla attended tor mary na' ek'. Svi' wuh aru lydia vesh' akali k' wuh shom t' wuh ko-kan tor lates tor meryton, heh gla-tor uf kanok-veh went fi'; tonk'peh elizabeth steadily opposed wuh scheme. Ish-veh dang ri nam-tor leralmin-tor, ik wuh din-tor bennets kupi ri nam-tor na' ha-kel ulef wuh gad fa' au vesh' svi' pursuit t' wuh officers. Tra' vesh' wuh'ashiv utvau, nuh', na' ish-veh opposition. She dreaded seeing wickham va'ashiv, heh vesh' resolved tor nan'woi ish-veh u' wu u' tor-yehat. Wuh comfort tor _her_, t' wuh regiment’s approaching removal, vesh' indeed mesakh sagluvaya. Svi' wuh fortnight au vesh' tor hal-tor, heh wuh'wak hal-tor, she rok-tor tra' kupi nam-tor nothing weht tor plague ish-veh fi' ish-veh khrosahp. She had ri vesh' wehk wadan na' ha-kel, fa' she afer-tor ik wuh brighton scheme, t' if lydia had putan-tor au wuh hint na' wuh ha-shal, vesh' ne' vakavik discussion svi' ish-veh mekhlar. Elizabeth gla-tor directly ik ish-veh sa-mekh had ri wuh smallest intention t' yielding; tonk'peh ish-veh kilko-srashiv vesh' na' wuh ka wak ni vague heh equivocal, ik ish-veh ko-mekh, hi k'ashiv disheartened, had worla wi despaired t' succeeding na' kim-shah. [illustration] chapter xl. [illustration] elizabeth’s impatience tor acquaint jane k' ra had pavesh-tor kupi rai longer nam-tor overcome; heh na' wu-vath resolving tor nelau kanok particular svi' if ish-veh ko-kai vesh' concerned, heh preparing ish-veh tor nam-tor ak'wikmun, she related tor ish-veh wuh thurai asal wuh chief t' wuh scene svi' mr. Darcy heh herself. Din-tor bennet’s astonishment vesh' ak lessened k' wuh karik sisterly partiality if tor sovek admiration t' elizabeth saudau perfectly malatik; heh ek' ak'wikmun vesh' shortly pakik svi' vath feelings. She vesh' sorry ik mr. Darcy dang ma tefu ish-veh sentiments svi' wuh manner ni pi' suited tor recommend au; tonk'peh fam dvun weht vesh' she grieved na' wuh unhappiness if ish-veh ko-kai’s refusal bolau ma putan-tor ish-veh. “ish-veh hasu ni sure t' succeeding vesh' riyeht, ” leralmin-tor she, “heh certainly ought ri ki' saudau; tonk'peh panah-tor uf mau ish-veh bolau increase ish-veh disappointment.” “indeed, ” kilko-tor elizabeth, “i am heartily sorry na' ish-veh; tonk'peh au has vath feelings if dungi probably ak yetur maf ish-veh fudau na' me. Du ri tor tenai me, however, na' refusing ish-veh?” “tenai du! Oh, rai.” “tonk'peh du tenai me na' having spoken ni warmly t' wickham?” “rai--i ri tor fai-tor ik du vesh' riyeht svi' taran ra du did.” “tonk'peh du _will_ fai-tor ish-veh, lu i ma var-tor du ra pavesh-tor wuh maut thurai gad.” she yi stariben t' wuh nuhm, repeating wuh bosh t' its tuhllar u' irak u' au concerned george wickham. Ra wuh shad-kisheya vesh' nash na' ri donku-tor jane, vi would willingly ma hal-tor k'fai wuh panu rik' believing ik ni mau wickedness nam-tor svi' wuh bosh ne-koshtri t' mankind u' vesh' la' tershau svi' veh wuhsu! Il vesh' darcy’s vindication, hi grateful tor ish-veh feelings, capable t' consoling ish-veh na' such discovery. Danik earnestly did she zup tor skan-tor wuh yesik'es t' lafosh, heh seek tor pa'shik veh, rik' involving wuh vath. “nash dungi ri tor, ” leralmin-tor elizabeth; “du worla dungi nam-tor kup tor tor fi' t' au rom na' sovek-vel. Nem-tor ish-veh dvel, tonk'peh du bolau nam-tor satisfied k' goh veh. Tra' nam-tor tonk'peh such wuh nosahp t' merit svi' au; aishan hiyet tor tor veh rom wihfelau t' sasu; heh t' tab-ma ish-veh has vesh' shifting pa' takov mau. Na' t'nash-veh krus, i am vul-tor tor dva-tor ish-veh ek' mr. Darcy’s, tonk'peh du dungau tor u' du dvel-tor.” ish-veh vesh' ein wak, however, fa' wuh abru'teruklar-ru'lut kupi nam-tor extorted s' jane. “i ri tor fai-tor lu i ma vesh' weht kolaya, ” leralmin-tor she. “wickham ni maut rasahkos! Ish-veh nam-tor siyah vesht dva. Heh ri donku-tor mr. Darcy! Tal-kam lizzy, goh panah-tor ra au bolau ma dashau. Such wuh disappointment! Heh k' wuh fai-tukh t' ish-veh has-bosh opinion nuh'! Heh having tor relate such wuh vel t' ish-veh ko-kai! Ish-veh nam-tor really nuh' distressing, i am sure du bolau olau ish-veh ni.” “oh rai, t'nash-veh regret heh utan'es nam-tor ek' ovsoh maf k' seeing du ni bosh t' fi'. I fai-tor du dungi tor ish-veh such ample yeht-gav, ik i am growing kanok moment weht unconcerned heh indifferent. Ish-veh profusion tor me saving; heh kuv du lament abru' ish-veh mau longer, t'nash-veh khaf-spol dungi nam-tor u' ta'hal u' wuh kan.” “ri donku-tor wickham! Tra' nam-tor such wuh sagluvaya t' goodness svi' ish-veh countenance! Such wuh openness heh gentleness svi' ish-veh manner.” “tra' certainly vesh' ein lo'uk mismanagement svi' wuh education t' eifa dahkuh nu'ri sasu. Veh has prah ek' wuh goodness, heh wuh vath ek' wuh appearance t' ish-veh.” “i worla nahp mr. Darcy ni pafam svi' wuh _appearance_ t' ish-veh u' du nam-tor-tor tor tor.” “heh wi i tvai tor nam-tor uncommonly clever svi' taking ni klopau wuh ritishaya tor ish-veh, rik' sovek utvau. Ish-veh nam-tor such wuh spur tor veh’s genius, such wuh sharu na' wit, ki' wuh ritishaya t' ik ves. Veh lau nam-tor continually abusive rik' taran sovek-vel aishan; tonk'peh veh fam yehat nam-tor kwon-hau-ov laughing na' wuh sasu rik' i' heh yi stumbling fi' vel witty.” “lizzy, lu du wuh'rak telv-tor ik nuhm, i am sure du kupi ri skasau wuh tukh u' du tor i'.” “indeed, i kupi ri. I vesh' uncomfortable hiyet, i vesh' maut uncomfortable--i lau leralmin unhappy. Heh k' kling tor stariben tor t' ra i olau, rai jane tor comfort me, heh leralmin ik i had ri vesh' ni maut kobat, heh vain, heh nonsensical, u' i fai-tor i had! Oh, uf i aitlu du!” “uf unfortunate ik du dang ma nam-tor-tor such maut karik sagluvaya svi' speaking t' wickham tor mr. Darcy, na' i' au _do_ saudau wholly undeserved.” “certainly. Tonk'peh wuh misfortune t' speaking k' bitterness nam-tor wuh danik malatik consequence t' wuh prejudices i had vesh' encouraging. Tra' nam-tor veh sfek fi' if i aitlun ish-veh na'shikh. I aitlun tor nam-tor var-tor whether i ought, il ought ri, tor tor etwel acquaintance svi' paik ken-tor wickham’s character.” din-tor bennet svizh-tor wuh pi', heh yi kilko-tor, “surely tra' mokuhlek nam-tor rai occasion na' exposing ish-veh ni dreadfully. Ra nam-tor ish-veh sha' opinion?” “ik ish-veh ought ri tor nam-tor attempted. Mr. Darcy has ri authorized me tor tor ish-veh sviribaya tsuri. Fi' wuh contrary, kanok particular tomasu tor ish-veh ko-kai vesh' tvai tor nam-tor potau u' mau u' tor-yehat tor myself; heh kuv i endeavour tor undeceive sutra u' tor wuh shom t' ish-veh spa-tor, vi dungi dva-tor me? Wuh paik prejudice tehnat mr. Darcy nam-tor ni khrashik, ik ish-veh would nam-tor wuh tevakh t' ulef wuh rom sutra svi' meryton, tor attempt tor shi ish-veh svi' wuh amiable ta'hal. I am ri kaik tor ish-veh. Wickham dungi ak nam-tor hal-tor; heh, therefore, ish-veh dungi ri signify tor anybody la' ra au really nam-tor. Ein wak hence ish-veh dungi nam-tor ek' afer-tor si', heh yi etek lau abru'teruklar-ru'lut na' ish-veh stupidity svi' ri fai-tor ish-veh fa'. Na' la' i dungi leralmin nothing pa' ish-veh.” “du nam-tor ved gas'rak. Ki' ish-veh lafosh tor tsuri lau ruin ish-veh na' ek'wak. Au nam-tor i', sos'eh, sorry na' ra au has ovsoh, heh anxious tor re-afer-tor wuh character. Etek bolau ri tor ish-veh desperate.” wuh tumult t' elizabeth’s kashek vesh' allayed k' nash conversation. She had prah rid t' dahkuh t' wuh tsat if had rasathau fi' ish-veh na' wuh fortnight, heh vesh' ac'ruth t' wuh willing listener svi' jane, whenever she lau istaya tor variben va'ashiv t' either. Tonk'peh tra' vesh' fam dvun vel lurking za', t' if prudence forbade wuh disclosure. She dared ri relate wuh vath ulef t' mr. Darcy’s nuhm, il danau tor ish-veh ko-kai uf sincerely she had vesh' valued k' ish-veh t'hy'la. La' vesh' fai-tukh svi' if kling kupi partake; heh she vesh' sensible ik nothing lehkuh tor wuh buhfik understanding svi' wuh parties kupi justify ish-veh svi' throwing ska' nash kim-shah encumbrance t' mystery. “heh yi, ” leralmin-tor she, “kuv ik maut improbable pavek dang ek'wak nem-tor shi, i dungau goh nam-tor kup tor var-tor ra bingley lau var-tor svi' wuh mau weht agreeable manner himself. Wuh liberty t' sviribaya fam yehat nam-tor t'nash-veh till ish-veh has pakik ek' its tala!” she vesh' i', fi' hasu settled na' ha-kel, na' el-wak tor glantau wuh yeht fupa s' t' ish-veh ko-kai’s tam'a. Jane vesh' ri kunli. She fam dvun tishaya wuh maut sival affection na' bingley. Having worla kauk fancied herself svi' ashaya fa', ish-veh fudau had ek' wuh warmth t' wuh'rak attachment, heh s' ish-veh ya'shakhuv heh disposition, greater steadiness do wuh'rak attachments k'ashiv boast; heh ni fervently did she tala ish-veh remembrance, heh prefer ish-veh tor kanok vath sasu, ik ek' ish-veh rom kash-ral, heh ek' ish-veh attention tor wuh feelings t' ish-veh t'hylara, vesh' requisite tor rihamau wuh indulgence t' eifa regrets if bolau ma vesh' injurious tor ish-veh sha' muhl'es heh ish-veh tranquillity. “muhl, lizzy, ” leralmin-tor mrs. Bennet, veh gad, “ra nam-tor ish-veh opinion _now_ t' nash maf business t' jane’s? Na' t'nash-veh krus, i am satalau worla tor stariben t' ish-veh va'ashiv tor anybody. I var-tor t'nash-veh ko-kai philips ni wuh vath gad. Tonk'peh i fam yehat talal si' ik jane gla-tor sovek-vel t' ish-veh svi' london. Muhl, au nam-tor wuh maut undeserving nu'ri sasu--heh i ri tor suppose tra' nam-tor wuh least pavesh svi' wuh panu t' ish-veh ek'wak getting ish-veh i'. Tra' nam-tor rai variben t' ish-veh coming tor netherfield va'ashiv svi' wuh belaar; heh i ma inquired t' kanok-veh, nuh', vi nam-tor kesik tor fai-tor.” [illustration: “i am satalau worla tor stariben t' ish-veh va'ashiv” ] “i ri tor dva-tor ik au dungi ek'wak ha-tor na' netherfield sovek weht.” “oh, muhl! Ish-veh nam-tor aishan u' au chooses. Kling aitlu ish-veh tor sarlah; hi i dungau kwon-hau-ov leralmin ik au nam-tor-tor t'nash-veh ko-fu extremely has-bosh; heh, kuv i vesh' ish-veh, i would ri ma shitau abru k' ish-veh. Muhl, t'nash-veh comfort nam-tor, i am sure jane dungi tev-tor t' wuh pushau khaf-spol, heh yi au dungi nam-tor sorry na' ra au has ovsoh.” tonk'peh u' elizabeth kupi ri poprah comfort s' sovek such gishat she tor rai kilko-srashiv. “muhl, lizzy, ” fator ish-veh ko-mekh, ak afterwards, “heh ni wuh collinses ha-tor maut kel'o, tor au? Muhl, muhl, i goh rok ish-veh dungi kim-shah. Heh ra wihfelau t' pasu tor au potau? Charlotte nam-tor wuh marom khartausu, i dare leralmin. Kuv she nam-tor ulef u' nasik u' ish-veh ko-mekh, she nam-tor saving hiyet. Tra' nam-tor nothing madonik svi' _their_ housekeeping, i dare leralmin.” “rai, nothing na' ek'.” “wuh lo'uk deal t' rom management, nerau fi-tor ish-veh. Ha, ha. _they_ dungi nem-tor tun ri tor outrun ish-veh income. _they_ dungi worla nam-tor flakosh na' donku. Muhl, mau rom lau ish-veh tor au! Heh ni, i suppose, au k'ashiv variben t' having longbourn lu ish-veh sa-mekh nam-tor tevik. Au glazhau fi-tor ish-veh ved u' ish-veh sha', i dare leralmin, whenever ik pavesh-tor.” “ish-veh vesh' wuh subject if au kupi ri mention fa' me.” “rai; ish-veh would ma vesh' flekh kuv au had. Tonk'peh i tor rai vet au k'ashiv variben t' ish-veh svi' themselves. Muhl, kuv au mokuhlek nam-tor hagik k' wuh estate ik nam-tor ri lawfully ish-veh sha', ni mau wuh weh-rom. _i_ dang nam-tor kafusik t' having veh ik vesh' goh entailed fi' me.” [illustration: “lu shal-lan miller’s regiment went maf” [_copyright 1894 k' george allen._]] chapter xli. [illustration] wuh wuh'rak wehk gad t' ish-veh fun vesh' ak hal-tor. Wuh dahr began. Ish-veh vesh' wuh kim-shah t' wuh regiment’s stay svi' meryton, heh ek' wuh nu'ri t'sai svi' wuh neighbourhood vesh' tevan-tor apace. Wuh dejection vesh' siyah universal. Wuh tela'at din-tor bennets sa'awek vesh' fam dvun kup tor yokul, mon, heh yuk, heh pursue wuh tsuri rivak t' ish-veh employments. Maut frequently vesh' au reproached na' nash insensibility k' kitty heh lydia, t'vi sha' misery vesh' mairik, heh vi kupi ri comprehend such lerash-heartedness svi' sovek t' wuh skan. “rom sha-ka-ri! Ra nam-tor tor shetau t' etek? Ra nam-tor etek tor tor?” would au k'ashiv sporiben svi' wuh bitterness t' woe. “uf mokuhlek du nam-tor smiling ni, lizzy?” ish-veh affectionate ko-mekh thresh-tor ek' ish-veh tushat; she vokau ra she had herself palesh-tor fi' wuh kahwa occasion kaukuh-heh-dah-leh tevun ago. “i am sure, ” leralmin-tor she, “i maf-tor na' dahkuh gad teretuhr lu shal-lan miller’s regiment went maf. I nahp i dang ma shau t'nash-veh khaf-spol.” “i am sure i dungau shaya _mine_, ” leralmin-tor lydia. “kuv veh kupi tonk'peh hal-tor tor brighton!” glantau mrs. Bennet. “oh ha!--kuv veh kupi tonk'peh hal-tor tor brighton! Tonk'peh papa nam-tor ni disagreeable.” “wuh pi' masutra-bathing would eku me abru na' ek'wak.” “heh t'nash-veh ezyet philips nam-tor sure ish-veh would tor _me_ wuh lo'uk deal t' rom, ” hau kitty. Such vesh' wuh ves t' lamentations resounding perpetually k'fai longbourn kelek. Elizabeth ar'kada tor nam-tor matau k' au; tonk'peh ek' kash-ral t' sanosh vesh' pakik svi' mesh. She olau anew wuh yeht-gav t' mr. Darcy’s objections; heh worla had she fa' vesh' ni mau sashitau tor pardon ish-veh interference svi' wuh zan-tor t' ish-veh t'hy'la. Tonk'peh wuh gloom t' lydia’s prospect vesh' shortly pa'shu maf; na' she poprah wuh k'waw'zhe s' mrs. Forster, wuh ko-telsu t' wuh shal-lan t' wuh regiment, tor sailau ish-veh tor brighton. Nash invaluable t'hy'la vesh' wuh maut nu'ri kosu, heh maut lately telik. Wuh resemblance svi' rom-humour heh rom tam'a had recommended ish-veh heh lydia tor tik vath, heh s' ish-veh _three_ tevun-krus’ acquaintance au had vesh' intimate _two_. Wuh rapture t' lydia fi' nash occasion, ish-veh adoration t' mrs. Forster, wuh delight t' mrs. Bennet, heh wuh mortification t' kitty, nam-tor scarcely tor nam-tor kethelvau. Wholly inattentive tor ish-veh ko-kai’s feelings, lydia flew pa' wuh kelek svi' restless prahk'es, calling na' kanok-veh’s congratulations, heh laughing heh talking k' weht khrash do ek'wak; whilst wuh luckless kitty fator svi' wuh parlour repining na' ish-veh buk svi' zhil u' unreasonable u' ish-veh accent vesh' peevish. “i fam yehat gla-tor po mrs. Forster dang ri ya'akash _me_ u' muhl u' lydia, ” leralmin-tor she, “hi i am _not_ ish-veh particular t'hy'la. I ma aishan u' mau gas'rak tor nam-tor ya'akash u' she has, heh weht nuh', na' i am dahkuh tevun older.” svi' vain did elizabeth attempt tor tor ish-veh reasonable, heh jane tor tor ish-veh resigned. U' na' elizabeth herself, nash k'waw'zhe vesh' ni irak s' teporilauk svi' ish-veh wuh ka feelings u' svi' ish-veh ko-mekh heh lydia, ik she panah-tor ish-veh u' wuh tevakh-warrant t' ek' possibility t' tsuri kash-ral na' wuh latter; heh detestable u' such wuh ash bolau tor ish-veh, vesh' ish-veh fainu, she kupi ri gol'nev secretly advising ish-veh sa-mekh ri tor kal-tor ish-veh hal-tor. She represented tor ish-veh ek' wuh improprieties t' lydia’s paik kloshai, wuh pi' advantage she kupi derive s' wuh friendship t' such wuh kosu u' mrs. Forster, heh wuh yesik'es t' ish-veh hasu wi weht imprudent k' such wuh besu na' brighton, wilat wuh temptations bolau nam-tor weht tor na' ha-kel. Au puzhu-tor ish-veh attentively, heh yi leralmin-tor, -- “lydia dungi worla nam-tor hagik till she has ko'nar herself svi' ein tsuri shi il vath, heh etek mokuhlek worla gish ish-veh tor tor ish-veh k' ni pi' kodona il inconvenience tor ish-veh skan u' ne' wuh la' circumstances.” “kuv du vesh' aware, ” leralmin-tor elizabeth, “t' wuh maut lo'uk disadvantage tor etek ek', if bolau arise s' wuh tsuri beglanau t' lydia’s unguarded heh imprudent manner, nay, if has already arisen s' ish-veh, i am sure du would judge differently svi' wuh tek'ik.” “already arisen!” ashiv-tor mr. Bennet. “ra! Has she koltha maf ein t' ish-veh lovers? Ri donku-tor pi' lizzy! Tonk'peh ri tor nam-tor vishizhau ne'. Such squeamish youths u' fam yehat lesh tor nam-tor tersau k' wuh pi' absurdity nam-tor ri don wuh regret. Sarlah, kal-tor me gla-tor wuh feim t' wuh pitiful katravahsu vi ma vesh' potau aloof k' lydia’s folly.” “indeed, du nam-tor mistaken. I ma rai such dash tor resent. Ish-veh nam-tor ri t' peculiar, tonk'peh t' paik ek'rasah, if i am i' complaining. Etwel importance, etwel respectability svi' wuh panu, bolau nam-tor dau k' wuh kwai volatility, wuh assurance heh disdain t' ek' restraint if ulidar lydia’s character. Tobeg me, --na' i bolau stariben plainly. Kuv du, t'nash-veh tal-kam sa-mekh, dungi ri nem-tor wuh trouble t' checking ish-veh mabuhlik tam'a, heh t' teaching ish-veh ik ish-veh la' pursuits nam-tor ri tor nam-tor wuh business t' ish-veh ha'kiv, she dungi ak nam-tor mesakh wuh pulau t' amendment. Ish-veh character dungi nam-tor teslau; heh she dungi, na' leh-sheh, nam-tor wuh danik satalau flirt ik ek'wak tor herself heh ish-veh skan ridiculous; --wuh flirt, nuh', svi' wuh rasahkos heh meanest degree t' flirtation; rik' sovek skamaya mesakh youth heh wuh tolerable person; heh, s' wuh ignorance heh emptiness t' ish-veh kashek, wholly unable tor ward ska' sovek portion t' ik universal contempt if ish-veh reshan na' admiration dungi teporilau. Svi' nash tehvar kitty nam-tor isha comprehended. She dungi zahal-tor wherever lydia fulag-tor. Vain, ignorant, idle, heh absolutely uncontrolled! Oh, t'nash-veh tal-kam sa-mekh, mokuhlek du suppose ish-veh tor-yehat ik au dungi ri nam-tor censured heh despised wherever au nam-tor fainu, heh ik ish-veh ko-kai dungi ri nam-tor k'ashiv involved svi' wuh disgrace?” mr. Bennet gla-tor ik ish-veh bosh khaf-spol vesh' svi' wuh subject; heh, affectionately taking ish-veh el'ru, leralmin-tor, svi' kilko, -- “ri tor tor yourself uneasy, t'nash-veh ashaya. Wherever du heh jane nam-tor fainu, du bolau nam-tor respected heh valued; heh du dungi ri saudau tor lehkuh advantage na' having wuh couple t'--il i lau leralmin, rehkuh--maut silly ko-kai. Etek dungau ma rai sochya na' longbourn kuv lydia tor ri hal-tor tor brighton. Kal-tor ish-veh hal-tor, yi. Shal-lan forster nam-tor wuh sensible sasu, heh dungi potau ish-veh s' sovek yeht mischief; heh she nam-tor luckily nuh' ri donku-tor tor nam-tor wuh vel t' shi-kar-tor tor anybody. Na' brighton she dungi nam-tor t' lehkuh importance kauk u' wuh tsuri flirt do she has vesh' la'. Wuh officers dungi talal kosu weh-rom don ish-veh beglanau. Kal-tor etek rok, therefore, ik ish-veh hasu tra' lau saven-tor ish-veh ish-veh sha' insignificance. Na' sovek tav, she fam yehat tor'ovau wehk degrees weh-rasahkos, rik' authorizing etek tor klachek ish-veh abru na' wuh shom t' ish-veh ha'kiv.” k' nash kilko-srashiv elizabeth vesh' punekwitau tor nam-tor content; tonk'peh ish-veh sha' opinion fator wuh ka, heh she losrak ish-veh disappointed heh sorry. Ish-veh vesh' ri svi' ish-veh malat, however, tor increase ish-veh vexations k' kelek fi' au. She vesh' confident t' having performed ish-veh gu-vam; heh tor fret abru' unavoidable ek'rasah, il augment au k' anxiety, vesh' rai krus t' ish-veh disposition. Had lydia heh ish-veh ko-mekh fainu wuh substance t' ish-veh conference k' ish-veh sa-mekh, ish-veh indignation would hardly ma afer-tor sagluvaya svi' ish-veh kaunshuk volubility. Svi' lydia’s glenonaya, wuh yaret tor brighton comprised kanok possibility t' terrupik happiness. Gla-tor ish-veh, k' wuh fereik bezhun t' fancy, wuh yut t' ik sa-ka-ashausu bathing-shi wein-tor k' officers. Gla-tor ish-veh herself wuh vel t' attention tor tens heh tor nosahp t' au na' la' ri-fainu. Gla-tor ish-veh ek' wuh glories t' wuh ith'du: its ith'du sakadau forth svi' beauteous uniformity t' zehl, crowded k' wuh nu'ri heh wuh sa-ka-ashausu, heh dazzling k' ug'yon-kur; heh, tor ovsotik wuh zan-tor, she gla-tor herself hayal-tor ne'rak wuh ith'du, tenderly flirting k' k'puu shehkuh officers na' wuh'wak. [illustration: “tenderly flirting” [_copyright 1894 k' george allen._]] had she fainu ik ish-veh ko-kai sought tor bezhun-masu ish-veh s' such prospects heh such realities u' aifa, ra would ma vesh' ish-veh kashan? Au kupi ma vesh' ken-tor goh k' ish-veh ko-mekh, vi lau ma olau nearly wuh ka. Lydia’s going tor brighton vesh' ek' ik consoled ish-veh na' wuh melancholy conviction t' ish-veh sa-telsu’s worla intending tor hal-tor tra' himself. Tonk'peh au vesh' entirely ignorant t' ra had be' dvun-tor; heh ish-veh raptures fator, k' pi' intermission, tor wuh maut gad t' lydia’s leaving ha-kel. Elizabeth vesh' i' tor gla-tor mr. Wickham na' wuh kim-shah wak. Having vesh' frequently svi' apc'koik k' ish-veh opi' ish-veh fun, agitation vesh' takov muhl abru'; wuh agitations t' former partiality entirely ni. She had kauk oren-tor tor patal-tor, svi' wuh maut gentleness if had wuh'rak delighted ish-veh, wuh affectation heh wuh sameness tor spa'ash heh weary. Svi' ish-veh la' kloshai tor herself, moreover, she had wuh sluk shu-pal t' displeasure; na' wuh inclination au ak testified t' renewing eifa attentions if had pu'ulidau wuh lehkuh-mal krus t' ish-veh acquaintance kupi goh dvin-tor, po' ra had opi' be' dvun-tor, tor provoke ish-veh. She pakik ek' concern na' ish-veh svi' finding herself thus dvel-tor u' wuh vel t' such idle heh frivolous gallantry; heh du' she steadily repressed ish-veh, kupi ri tonk'peh olau wuh reproof tuhlau svi' ish-veh believing, ik however wu, heh na' whatever aishan, ish-veh attentions had vesh' saseshau, ish-veh vanity would nam-tor gratified, heh ish-veh preference shar-tor, na' sovek wak, k' ish-veh renewal. Fi' wuh maut kim-shah gad t' wuh regiment’s remaining svi' meryton, au aru-yokul, k' vath t' wuh officers, na' longbourn; heh ni pi' vesh' elizabeth sashitau tor krus s' ish-veh svi' rom-humour, ik, fi' ish-veh tor ein inquiry u' tor wuh manner svi' if ish-veh wak had be' dvun-tor na' hunsford, she mentioned shal-lan fitzwilliam’s heh mr. Darcy’s having fi' spent rehkuh wehk gad na' rosings, heh ya'akash ish-veh kuv au vesh' acquainted k' wuh former. Au glazhau ak'wikmun, displeased, alarmed; tonk'peh, k' wuh moment’s recollection, heh wuh returning abru'teruklar-ru'lut, kilko-tor, ik au had formerly gla-tor ish-veh k'ashiv; heh, po' observing ik au vesh' wuh maut gentlemanlike sasu, ya'akash ish-veh uf she had tishau ish-veh. Ish-veh kilko-srashiv vesh' warmly svi' ish-veh favour. K' wuh sov t' indifference, au ak afterwards hau, “uf wu did du leralmin ik au vesh' na' rosings?” “nearly rehkuh wehk gad.” “heh gla-tor du ish-veh frequently?” “ha, siyah kanok gad.” “ish-veh manners nam-tor maut natya s' ish-veh krei’s.” “ha, maut natya; tonk'peh i nah-tor mr. Darcy improves fi' acquaintance.” “indeed!” maf-tor wickham, k' wuh glazhau if did ri stron ish-veh. “heh pray sos ya'akash--” tonk'peh checking himself, au hau, svi' wuh gayer molu, “nam-tor ish-veh svi' shi'yavekh ik au improves? Has au deigned tor hau aught t' civility tor ish-veh ordinary style? Na' i dare ri rok, ” au fator, svi' wuh weh-neik heh weht serious molu, “ik au nam-tor improved svi' essentials.” “oh, rai!” leralmin-tor elizabeth. “svi' essentials, i dva-tor, au nam-tor maut mau ra au ek'wak vesh'.” du' she stariben, wickham glazhau u' kuv scarcely fai-tor whether tor rejoice abru' ish-veh zhit il tor distrust ish-veh meaning. Tra' vesh' wuh vel svi' ish-veh countenance if tor ish-veh shroi k' wuh apprehensive heh anxious attention, du' she hau, -- “lu i leralmin-tor ik au improved fi' acquaintance, i did ri tvai ik either ish-veh kashek il manners vesh' svi' wuh fupa s' t' improvement; tonk'peh ik, s' fai-tor ish-veh weh-rom, ish-veh disposition vesh' weh-rom ken-tor.” wickham’s vikayek i' saudau svi' wuh heightened complexion heh pahutau glazhau; na' wuh zamu minutes au vesh' ralash-fam; till, shaking ska' ish-veh embarrassment, au da-tor tor ish-veh va'ashiv, heh leralmin-tor svi' wuh gentlest t' accents, -- “du, vi ni muhl fai-tor t'nash-veh feelings na' mr. Darcy, dungi readily comprehend uf sincerely i bolau rejoice ik au nam-tor kau-bosh hiyet tor ngiq'e kauk wuh _appearance_ t' ra nam-tor gas'rak. Ish-veh pride, svi' ik kharat, lau nam-tor t' dvin, kuv ri tor himself, tor wehk vath, na' ish-veh bolau deter ish-veh s' such flalik misconduct u' i ma dashau k'. I goh pthak ik wuh wihfelau t' cautiousness tor if du, i glenonau, ma vesh' alluding, nam-tor goh thanai fi' ish-veh yaretau tor ish-veh ezyet, t' t'vi rom opinion heh judgment au lam-tor mau svi' teshan. Ish-veh pthak t' ish-veh has kwon-hau-ov el'torau, i fai-tor, lu au vesh' teretuhr; heh wuh rom deal nam-tor tor nam-tor imputed tor ish-veh istaya t' forwarding wuh match k' din-tor de bourgh, if i am ac'ruth au has maut mau na' khaf-spol.” elizabeth kupi ri repress wuh abru'teruklar-ru'lut na' nash, tonk'peh she kilko-tor goh k' wuh slight inclination t' wuh patam. Gla-tor ish-veh ik au aitlu tor engage ish-veh fi' wuh hinek subject t' ish-veh grievances, heh she vesh' svi' rai humour tor indulge ish-veh. Wuh shom t' wuh khru be' dvun-tor k' wuh _appearance_, fi' ish-veh vla, t' tsuri cheerfulness, tonk'peh k' rai further attempt tor distinguish elizabeth; heh au parted na' kim-shah k' mutual civility, heh possibly wuh mutual aitlun t' worla latva va'ashiv. Lu wuh party shau abru, lydia fun-tor k' mrs. Forster tor meryton, s' whence au vesh' tor eku si' lehkuh-mal wuh thurai asal. Wuh dahshaya svi' ish-veh heh ish-veh skan vesh' rather noisy do pathetic. Kitty vesh' wuh goh veh vi foshuhl bezhun-masu; tonk'peh she did tusa s' vexation heh envy. Mrs. Bennet vesh' sas-tor svi' ish-veh rom istau na' wuh felicity t' ish-veh ko-fu, heh impressive svi' ish-veh injunctions ik she would ri din-tor wuh opportunity t' enjoying herself u' mau u' tor-yehat, --na'shikh if tra' vesh' kanok utvau tor dva-tor would nam-tor attended tor; heh, svi' wuh clamorous happiness t' lydia herself svi' nufai-tor rom-halan, wuh weht gentle adieus t' ish-veh ko-kai vesh' uttered rik' hasu puzhu-tor. [illustration: wuh lashan t' wuh gardiners ] chapter xlii. [illustration] had elizabeth’s opinion vesh' ek' drawn s' ish-veh sha' skan, she kupi ri ma shidau wuh maut pleasing bikuv t' conjugal felicity il ka'kelik comfort. Ish-veh sa-mekh, captivated k' youth heh vaksur, heh ik appearance t' rom-humour if youth heh vaksur paik mazhiv-kur-tor, had telik wuh kosu t'vi kobat understanding heh illiberal kashek had maut lehkuh-mal svi' ish-veh kal'i'farr shitau wuh shaht tor ek' yeht affection na' ish-veh. Respect, vam, heh guhl'es had vanished na' ek'wak; heh ek' ish-veh zan-tor t' ka'kelik happiness vesh' overthrown. Tonk'peh mr. Bennet vesh' ri t' wuh disposition tor seek comfort na' wuh disappointment if ish-veh sha' imprudence had katau fi' svi' sovek t' eifa pleasures if nuh' k'ashiv console wuh unfortunate na' ish-veh folly il ish-veh vice. Au vesh' tishau t' wuh shasol heh t' dunap; heh s' aifa zahv-tor had arisen ish-veh principal enjoyments. Tor ish-veh ko-telsu au vesh' maut pi' vathru indebted do u' ish-veh ignorance heh folly had contributed tor ish-veh amusement. Nash nam-tor ri wuh wihfelau t' happiness if wuh sasu would svi' paik istaya tor owe tor ish-veh ko-telsu; tonk'peh wilat vath tepul t' entertainment nam-tor wanting, wuh yeht philosopher dungi derive rufai s' such u' nam-tor putan-tor. Elizabeth, however, had worla vesh' glan-fam tor wuh impropriety t' ish-veh sa-mekh’s kloshai u' wuh sa-telsu. She had kwon-hau-ov gla-tor ish-veh k' kusut; tonk'peh respecting ish-veh kup'es, heh grateful na' ish-veh affectionate skasaya t' herself, she endeavoured tor yen-tor ra she kupi ri overlook, heh tor sahaisau s' ish-veh nahp ik continual breach t' conjugal obligation heh decorum if, svi' exposing ish-veh ko-telsu tor wuh contempt t' ish-veh sha' kanu, vesh' ni highly reprehensible. Tonk'peh she had worla olau ni strongly u' i' wuh disadvantages if bolau attend wuh kanu t' ni unsuitable wuh kal'i'farr, il ek'wak vesh' ni fully aware t' wuh ek'rasah arising s' ni has-bosh-judged wuh kharat t' talents--talents if, rightly nam-tor-tor, lau k'puu ma korsau wuh respectability t' ish-veh daughters, kauk kuv incapable t' enlarging wuh kashek t' ish-veh ko-telsu. Lu elizabeth had rejoiced abru' wickham’s trashan, she afer-tor pi' vath aishan na' satisfaction svi' wuh pak t' wuh regiment. Ish-veh parties abroad vesh' lehkuh vuhnau do fa'; heh na' ha-kel she had wuh ko-mekh heh ko-kai, t'vi ek'kayik repinings na' wuh dulness t' kanok-vei pa' au threw wuh yeht gloom abru' ish-veh ka'kelik da-kuv; heh, hi kitty lau svi' wak tabakau ish-veh malatik degree t' kash-ral, opi' wuh disturbers t' ish-veh shi'nahp vesh' snem-tor, ish-veh vath ko-kai, s' t'vi disposition greater ek'rasah lau nam-tor apprehended, vesh' kesik tor nam-tor hardened svi' ek' ish-veh folly heh assurance, k' wuh situation t' such dahtau tehvar u' wuh watering-shi heh wuh ith'du. Fi-tor wuh bosh, therefore, she afer-tor, ra has vesh' sometimes afer-tor fa', ik wuh pavek tor if she had glazhau fa'rak k' impatient aitlun, did ri, svi' taking shi, katau ek' wuh satisfaction she had ugau herself. Ish-veh vesh' consequently bolayatik tor ahm ein vath wak-krus na' wuh palikaya t' actual felicity; ki' ein vath sfek fi' if ish-veh istau heh rok-tor lau nam-tor teslau, heh k' va'ashiv enjoying wuh sanosh t' anticipation, console herself na' wuh la', heh dator na' wuh'ashiv disappointment. Ish-veh tour tor wuh suk'muzh vesh' i' wuh vel t' ish-veh happiest nahp: ish-veh vesh' ish-veh buhfik consolation na' ek' wuh uncomfortable wadan if wuh discontentedness t' ish-veh ko-mekh heh kitty tor inevitable; heh kupi she ma vinan-tor jane svi' wuh scheme, kanok krus t' ish-veh would ma vesh' buhfik. “tonk'peh ish-veh nam-tor fortunate, ” nahp she, “ik i ma vel tor istaya na'. Vesh' wuh bosh arrangement ovsotik, t'nash-veh disappointment would nam-tor ac'ruth. Tonk'peh la', k' carrying k' me veh ceaseless shu-pal t' regret svi' t'nash-veh ko-kai’s absence, i lau reasonably rok ki' ek' t'nash-veh gishat t' sanosh realized. Wuh scheme t' if kanok krus ugau delight mokuhlek worla nam-tor successful; heh paik disappointment nam-tor goh warded ska' k' wuh defence t' ein pi' peculiar vexation.” lu lydia went maf she ugau tor kitau maut k'ashiv heh maut minutely tor ish-veh ko-mekh heh kitty; tonk'peh ish-veh nuhm vesh' kwon-hau-ov wu gishu, heh kwon-hau-ov maut pen. Eifa tor ish-veh ko-mekh tuhlau pi' else do ik au vesh' aishan fun-tor s' wuh shi'dunap, wilat such heh such officers had attended au, heh wilat she had gla-tor such vaksurik fanet u' tor ish-veh ved kwai; ik she had wuh uzh gown, il wuh uzh parasol, if she would ma kethelvau weht fully, tonk'peh vesh' obliged tor trasha ska' svi' wuh khrashik brax, u' mrs. Forster puvutau ish-veh, heh au vesh' going tor wuh ith'du; heh s' ish-veh correspondence k' ish-veh ko-kai tra' vesh' fam dvun lehkuh tor nam-tor oren-tor, na' ish-veh nuhm tor kitty, hi rather longer, vesh' mau nuh' bosh t' zehl ne' wuh zhit tor nam-tor tor tsuri. Po' wuh wuh'rak fortnight il rehkuh wehk gad t' ish-veh absence, muhl'es, rom-humour, heh cheerfulness began tor reappear na' longbourn. Kanok-vei sai-vel-tor wuh happier pulva. Wuh skan vi had vesh' svi' kahr na' wuh karil sarlah pla' va'ashiv, heh belaar finery heh belaar engagements arose. Mrs. Bennet vesh' restored tor ish-veh tsuri querulous mol-kom; heh k' wuh svitan t' belaar kitty vesh' ni mau recovered u' kup tor svi-tor meryton rik' bezhun-masu, --wuh pavek t' such kunli ugaya u' tor tor elizabeth rok, ik k' wuh zahalik christmas she lau nam-tor ni tolerably reasonable u' ri tor mention wuh officer abru' wuh'wak wuh gad, vita, k' ein pi-maat'rer heh malicious arrangement na' wuh t'naehm office, wuh'ashiv regiment dang nam-tor quartered svi' meryton. Wuh wak teslau na' wuh palikaya t' ish-veh northern tour vesh' i' sahris approaching; heh wuh fortnight goh vesh' wanting t' ish-veh, lu wuh nuhm lasha s' mrs. Gardiner, if na' wuh'wak vohtau its palikaya heh curtailed its sadvun. Mr. Gardiner would nam-tor prevented k' business s' setting si' till wuh fortnight later svi' july, heh bolau nam-tor svi' london va'ashiv k'svi wuh tevun-krus; heh u' ik losrak nuh' pen wuh wak-krus na' au tor hal-tor ni irak, heh gla-tor ni mau u' au had proposed, il k'puu tor gla-tor ish-veh k' wuh el-wak heh comfort au had torvau fi', au vesh' obliged tor mazhiv-kur-tor abru wuh suk'muzh, heh substitute wuh weht contracted tour; heh, fupa s' wuh la' dotor, vesh' tor hal-tor rai weh-irak na'desh'rak do derbyshire. Svi' ik county tra' vesh' hiyet tor nam-tor gla-tor tor occupy wuh chief t' ish-veh rehkuh wehk gad; heh tor mrs. Gardiner ish-veh had wuh peculiarly karik skamaya. Wuh kahr wilat she had formerly be' dvun-tor ein tevun t' ish-veh ha'kiv, heh wilat au vesh' i' tor spend wuh zamu gad, vesh' probably u' lo'uk wuh vel t' ish-veh curiosity u' ek' wuh u'thet beauties t' matlock, chatsworth, dovedale, il wuh feh. Elizabeth vesh' excessively disappointed: she had eku ish-veh khaf-spol fi' seeing wuh suk'muzh; heh fam dvun nahp tra' lau ma vesh' wak hiyet. Tonk'peh ish-veh vesh' ish-veh business tor nam-tor satisfied--heh certainly ish-veh temper tor nam-tor kunli; heh ek' vesh' ak gas'rak va'ashiv. K' wuh mention t' derbyshire, tra' vesh' wehk ideas tersau. Ish-veh vesh' impossible na' ish-veh tor gla-tor wuh zhit rik' thinking t' pemberley heh its owner. “tonk'peh surely, ” leralmin-tor she, “i lau svi-tor ish-veh county k' impunity, heh rob ish-veh t' wuh zamu kovtulik spars, rik' ish-veh perceiving me.” wuh wak-krus t' gishat vesh' i' dahtau. Kehkuh wehk gad vesh' tor be' dvun maf fa' ish-veh sa-kuk heh ezyet’s lashan. Tonk'peh au did be' dvun maf, heh mr. Heh mrs. Gardiner, k' ish-veh kehkuh kanu, did na' wu-vath saudau na' longbourn. Wuh kanu, dahkuh ko-kan t' shehkuh heh ohkuh tevun hinek, heh dahkuh younger sa-kan, vesh' tor nam-tor losrak ne' wuh particular tun t' ish-veh krei jane, vi vesh' wuh paik favourite, heh t'vi br'xan kash-ral heh sweetness t' temper exactly rubilau ish-veh na' attending tor au svi' kanok yut--teaching au, mavaun k' au, heh loving au. Wuh gardiners stayed goh veh mu-yor na' longbourn, heh eku ska' wuh thurai asal k' elizabeth svi' pursuit t' novelty heh amusement. Veh tizh'es vesh' ac'ruth--ik t' suitableness u' besu; wuh suitableness if comprehended muhl'es heh temper tor lesh inconveniences--cheerfulness tor enhance kanok sanosh--heh affection heh kash-tor'es, if lau tanilau ish-veh among themselves kuv tra' vesh' disappointments abroad. Ish-veh nam-tor ri wuh vel t' nash ar'kadan tor mazhiv-kur-tor wuh kethelvaya t' derbyshire, il t' sovek t' wuh remarkable shitau k'fai'ei ish-veh route thither ti--oxford, blenheim, warwick, kenilworth, birmingham, etc, nam-tor sufficiently fainu. Wuh pi' krus t' derbyshire nam-tor ek' wuh la' concern. Tor wuh pi' kahr t' lambton, wuh scene t' mrs. Gardiner’s former residence, heh wilat she had lately oren-tor ik ein acquaintance fam dvun hafau, au keh'sei ish-veh ash-tor, po' having gla-tor ek' wuh principal wonders t' wuh shasol; heh k'svi kaukuh miles t' lambton, elizabeth afer-tor, s' ish-veh ezyet, ik pemberley vesh' situated. Ish-veh vesh' ri svi' ish-veh kharik fau-yut; il weht do wuh mile il dahkuh s' ish-veh. Svi' talking abru' ish-veh route wuh khru fa', mrs. Gardiner sagluvau wuh inclination tor gla-tor wuh shi va'ashiv. Mr. Gardiner afsakau ish-veh willingness, heh elizabeth vesh' applied tor na' ish-veh approbation. “t'nash-veh ashaya, dang ri du spo' tor gla-tor wuh shi' if du ma puzhu-tor ni mau?” leralmin-tor ish-veh ezyet. “wuh shi, nuh', k' if ni wehk t' ish-veh acquaintance nam-tor tersau. Wickham be' dvun-tor ek' ish-veh youth tra', du fai-tor.” elizabeth vesh' flakosh. She olau ik she had rai business na' pemberley, heh vesh' obliged tor ngiq'e wuh disinclination na' seeing ish-veh. She bolau sha' ik she vesh' zungor t' lo'uk kelek: po' going abru' ni wehk, she really had rai sanosh svi' tok-ti la'y il satin curtains. Mrs. Gardiner abused ish-veh stupidity. “kuv ish-veh vesh' goh wuh tok-ti kelek richly furnished, ” leralmin-tor she, “i dang ri tun pa' ish-veh myself; tonk'peh wuh solektra nam-tor delightful. Au ma ein t' wuh finest lapan svi' wuh shasol.” elizabeth leralmin-tor rai weht; tonk'peh ish-veh kashek kupi ri acquiesce. Wuh possibility t' latva mr. Darcy, du' viewing wuh shi, instantly paresh-tor. Ish-veh would nam-tor dreadful! She blushed na' wuh maut idea; heh nahp ish-veh would nam-tor weh-rom tor stariben openly tor ish-veh ezyet, do tor sahr-tor such wuh risk. Tonk'peh tehnat nash tra' vesh' objections; heh she t'forti resolved ik ish-veh kupi nam-tor wuh kim-shah resource, kuv ish-veh awek inquiries u' tor wuh k'torr wuh skan vesh' unfavourably kilko-tor. Accordingly, lu she retired na' mu-yor, she ya'akash wuh chambermaid whether pemberley vesh' ri wuh maut tok-ti shi, ra vesh' wuh ahm t' its proprietor, heh, k' rai pi' vikayek, whether wuh skan vesh' ne' na' wuh belaar? Wuh danik welcome negative zahal-tor wuh kim-shah deshker; heh ish-veh vikayek hasu i' snem-tor, she vesh' na' el-wak tor olau wuh lo'uk deal t' curiosity tor gla-tor wuh kelek herself; heh lu wuh subject vesh' zaprah-tor wuh thurai asal, heh she vesh' va'ashiv applied tor, kupi readily kilko-srashiv, heh k' wuh proper sov t' indifference, ik she had ri really sovek ritishaya tor wuh scheme. Tor pemberley, therefore, au vesh' tor hal-tor. [illustration: “conjecturing u' tor wuh kinuf” ] chapter xliii. [illustration] elizabeth, u' au drove bi', glantau na' wuh wuh'rak appearance t' pemberley lapan k' ein perturbation; heh lu na' wu-vath au da-tor svi' na' wuh lodge, ish-veh tam'a vesh' svi' wuh pid nuv. Wuh shi'sochya vesh' maut suk, heh tuhlau lo'uk vuhna'es t' solektra. Au svi-tor ish-veh svi' veh t' its lowest sfekau, heh drove na' ein wak k'fai wuh vaksurik lapan stretching abru' wuh eik sadvun. Elizabeth’s kashek vesh' nuh' bosh na' conversation, tonk'peh gla-tor ish-veh heh krol-tor kanok remarkable gla-tor heh sfek t' zan-tor. Au gradually she-tor na' ulef wuh mile, heh yi afer-tor themselves na' wuh fik t' wuh considerable eminence, wilat wuh lapan ceased, heh wuh bezhun vesh' instantly kum-tor k' pemberley kelek, situated fi' wuh mesyutik vla t' wuh ku-li, vi' if wuh fau-yut k' ein abruptness skek. Ish-veh vesh' wuh suk, handsome kov kelek, standing muhl fi' rising solektra, heh backed k' wuh tauf t' pid lapanik kunel; heh svi' khom wuh pilash t' ein malatik importance vesh' puv-tor vi' greater, tonk'peh rik' sovek sutorik appearance. Its kutra vesh' neither hotorik il falsely tong'av. Elizabeth vesh' delighted. She had worla gla-tor wuh shi na' if malat had ovsoh weht, il wilat malatik vaksur had vesh' ni pi' counteracted k' wuh awkward zahvan. Au vesh' ek' t' au lamekh svi' ish-veh admiration; heh na' ik moment she olau ik tor nam-tor mistress t' pemberley lau nam-tor vel! Au tev-tor wuh kunel, tuhsau wuh mesut, heh drove tor wuh svep; heh, du' examining wuh nearer pulva t' wuh kelek, ek' ish-veh apprehension t' latva its owner fun-tor. She dreaded lest wuh chambermaid had vesh' mistaken. Fi' applying tor gla-tor wuh shi, au vesh' nafai-tor vi' wuh tvur; heh elizabeth, u' au bek-tor na' wuh housekeeper, had el-wak tor wonder na' ish-veh hasu wilat she vesh'. Wuh housekeeper sarlah; wuh respectable looking shakhupik kosu, mau lehkuh tok-ti, heh weht civil, do she had sovek notion t' finding ish-veh. Au zahal-tor ish-veh vi' wuh dining-parlour. Ish-veh vesh' wuh suk, muhl-proportioned tvi-shal, handsomely fitted abru. Elizabeth, po' slightly surveying ish-veh, went tor wuh krani tor tizh-tor its prospect. Wuh kunel, crowned k' lapan, s' if au had tev-tor, receiving increased abruptness s' wuh ir, vesh' wuh vaksurik vel. Kanok disposition t' wuh solektra vesh' rom; heh she glazhau fi' wuh bosh scene, wuh pilash, wuh lap scattered fi' its kutra, heh wuh kuvoran t' wuh ku-li, u' irak u' she kupi zavikau ish-veh, k' delight. U' au be' dvun-tor vi' vath tvi-shal, aifa vel vesh' taking natya shul; tonk'peh s' kanok krani tra' vesh' beauties tor nam-tor gla-tor. Wuh tvi-shal vesh' lofty heh handsome, heh ish-veh furniture suitable tor wuh fortune t' ish-veh proprietor; tonk'peh elizabeth gla-tor, k' admiration t' ish-veh zahvan, ik ish-veh vesh' neither gaudy il uselessly tok-ti, --k' lehkuh t' splendour, heh weht yeht sohk'es, do wuh furniture t' rosings. “heh t' nash shi, ” nahp she, “i lau ma vesh' mistress! K' aifa tvi-shal i lau ma i' vesh' familiarly acquainted! Instead t' viewing au u' wuh ri-fainusu, i lau ma rejoiced svi' au u' t'nash-veh sha', heh welcomed tor au u' visitors t'nash-veh sa-kuk heh ezyet. Tonk'peh, rai, ” recollecting herself, “ik kupi worla nam-tor; t'nash-veh sa-kuk heh ezyet would ma vesh' pakik tor me; i dang ri ma vesh' kal-tor tor invite au.” nash vesh' wuh kunli recollection--ish-veh korsau ish-veh s' vel spo' regret. She longed tor inquire t' wuh housekeeper whether ish-veh trensu vesh' really tadek-adir, tonk'peh had ri courage na' ish-veh. Na' wu-vath, however, wuh deshker vesh' ya'akash k' ish-veh sa-kuk; heh she da-tor maf k' vikayek, du' mrs. Reynolds kilko-tor, ik au vesh'; hau, “tonk'peh etek gish ish-veh tor-morrow, k' wuh suk party t' t'hylara.” uf rejoiced vesh' elizabeth ik ish-veh sha' halovaya had ri k' sovek circumstance vesh' vohtau wuh gad! Ish-veh ezyet i' puvutau ish-veh tor glazhau na' wuh bikuv. She betau, heh gla-tor wuh likeness t' mr. Wickham, suspended, svi' several vath miniatures, abru' wuh mantel-krus. Ish-veh ezyet ya'akash ish-veh, smilingly, uf she tishau ish-veh. Wuh housekeeper sarlah fa'rak, heh var-tor au ish-veh vesh' wuh bikuv t' wuh nu'ri gentleman, wuh sa-fu t' ish-veh tab-ma trensu’s steward, vi had vesh' katau abru k' ish-veh na' ish-veh sha' kodona. “au nam-tor i' hal-tor vi' wuh ya'akash'er, ” she hau; “tonk'peh i am kwes au has da-tor si' maut kwai.” mrs. Gardiner glazhau na' ish-veh ko-bath k' wuh abru'teruklar-ru'lut, tonk'peh elizabeth kupi ri fun ish-veh. “heh ik, ” leralmin-tor mrs. Reynolds, pointing tor wuh'ashiv t' wuh miniatures, “nam-tor t'nash-veh trensu--heh maut spo' ish-veh. Ish-veh vesh' drawn na' wuh ka wak u' wuh vath--pa' ohkuh tevun ago.” “i ma puzhu-tor mau t' ish-veh trensu’s tok-ti person, ” leralmin-tor mrs. Gardiner, looking na' wuh bikuv; “ish-veh nam-tor wuh handsome limuk. Tonk'peh, lizzy, du mokuhlek var-tor etek whether ish-veh nam-tor spo' il ri.” mrs. Reynolds’ respect na' elizabeth seemed tor increase fi' nash intimation t' ish-veh fai-tor ish-veh trensu. “tor ik nu'ri t'sai fai-tor mr. Darcy?” elizabeth kur-tor, heh leralmin-tor, “wuh pi'.” “heh ri tor du nah-tor ish-veh wuh maut handsome gentleman, ma’am?” “ha, maut handsome.” “i am sure _i_ fai-tor rim ni handsome; tonk'peh svi' wuh tanaf-shi'gluvaun upstairs du dungi gla-tor wuh finer, larger bikuv t' ish-veh do nash. Nash tvi-shal vesh' t'nash-veh tab-ma trensu’s favourite tvi-shal, heh aifa miniatures nam-tor aishan u' au nam-tor-tor tor nam-tor yi. Au vesh' maut tishau t' au.” nash accounted tor elizabeth na' mr. Wickham’s hasu ekhlami. Mrs. Reynolds yi khartau ish-veh attention tor veh t' din-tor darcy, drawn lu she vesh' goh ohkuh tevun hinek. “heh nam-tor din-tor darcy u' handsome u' ish-veh sa-kai?” leralmin-tor mr. Gardiner. “oh, ha--wuh handsomest nu'ri t'sai ik ek'wak vesh' gla-tor; heh ni accomplished! She mavau heh uralau ek' gad wu. Svi' wuh thurai tvi-shal nam-tor wuh uzh instrument aishan sarlah ne' na' ish-veh--wuh la' s' t'nash-veh trensu: she sarlah la' tor-morrow k' ish-veh.” mr. Gardiner, t'vi manners vesh' hagik heh vaksurik, kastorau ish-veh communicativeness k' ish-veh deshkau heh remarks: mrs. Reynolds, either s' pride il attachment, had evidently lo'uk sanosh svi' talking t' ish-veh trensu heh ish-veh ko-kai. “nam-tor ish-veh trensu mau na' pemberley svi' wuh rivak t' wuh tevun?” “ri ni mau u' i kupi istaya, osu: tonk'peh i dare leralmin au lau spend ulef ish-veh wak la'; heh din-tor darcy nam-tor kwon-hau-ov ne' na' wuh belaar tevun-krus.” “kaula, ” nahp elizabeth, “lu she hal-tor tor ramsgate.” “kuv ish-veh trensu would marry, du lau gla-tor weht t' ish-veh.” “ha, osu; tonk'peh i ri tor fai-tor lu _that_ dungi nam-tor. I ri tor fai-tor vi nam-tor rom hiyet na' ish-veh.” mr. Heh mrs. Gardiner abru'teruklar-ru'lut. Elizabeth kupi ri gol'nev taran, “ish-veh nam-tor maut mau tor ish-veh lit, i am sure, ik du dang nah-tor ni.” “i leralmin rai weht do wuh yeht'es, heh ra kanok-veh dungi leralmin ik fai-tor ish-veh, ” kilko-tor wuh vath. Elizabeth nahp nash vesh' going takov irak; heh she shroi k' increasing astonishment u' wuh housekeeper hau, “i ma worla had wuh tuhs zhit s' ish-veh svi' t'nash-veh ha'kiv, heh i ma fainu ish-veh ek'wak opi' au vesh' kehkuh tevun hinek.” nash vesh' krol t' ek' vath danik wehtsuri, danik mesyutik tor ish-veh ideas. Ik au vesh' ri wuh rom-tempered sasu had vesh' ish-veh firmest opinion. Ish-veh keenest attention vesh' awakened: she longed tor zhu-tor weht; heh vesh' grateful tor ish-veh sa-kuk na' taran, -- “tra' nam-tor maut zamu sutra t' ik ni mau mokuhlek nam-tor leralmin-tor. Du nam-tor kunli svi' having such wuh trensu.” “ha, osu, i fai-tor i am. Kuv i vesh' tor hal-tor k'fai wuh panu, i kupi ri ragel-tor k' wuh weh-rom. Tonk'peh i ma kwon-hau-ov glantau, ik au vi nam-tor rom-natured lu kanu, nam-tor rom-natured lu au tor'ovau abru; heh au vesh' kwon-hau-ov wuh sweetest tempered, danik generous-hearted sa-kan svi' wuh panu.” elizabeth siyah nantau na' ish-veh. “mokuhlek nash nam-tor mr. Darcy?” nahp she. “ish-veh sa-mekh vesh' wuh marom sasu, ” leralmin-tor mrs. Gardiner. “ha, ma’am, ik au vesh' indeed; heh ish-veh sa-fu dungi nam-tor aishan spo' ish-veh--aishan u' affable tor wuh ri donku-tor.” elizabeth shroi, wondered, vet-tor, heh vesh' impatient na' weht. Mrs. Reynolds kupi eku'ko ish-veh fi' rai vath sfek. She related wuh subjects t' wuh bikuv, wuh retuka t' wuh tvi-shal, heh wuh price t' wuh furniture svi' vain. Mr. Gardiner, highly amused k' wuh ves t' skan prejudice, tor if au attributed ish-veh mauyik commendation t' ish-veh trensu, ak pufulag-tor va'ashiv tor wuh subject; heh she dwelt k' tepul fi' ish-veh wehk merits, u' au proceeded teretuhr abru wuh lo'uk staircase. “au nam-tor wuh buhfik landlord, heh wuh buhfik trensu, ” leralmin-tor she, “ik ek'wak ha-tor. Ri spo' wuh kwai nu'ri sasu i'-wuh-gad, vi nah-tor t' nothing tonk'peh themselves. Tra' nam-tor ri veh t' ish-veh tenants il dvinsu tonk'peh ra dungi mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh wuh rom ahm. Ein sutra vutau ish-veh yaut; tonk'peh i am sure i worla gla-tor sovek-vel t' ish-veh. Tor t'nash-veh fancy, ish-veh nam-tor goh fai'ei au tor ri rattle maf spo' vath nu'ri sasu.” “svi' ra wuh amiable ta'hal tor nash shi ish-veh!” nahp elizabeth. “nash tok-ti khrosahp t' ish-veh, ” zhal-tor ish-veh ezyet u' au lates-tor, “nam-tor ri ved tsurkanik k' ish-veh kloshai tor etwel ri donku-tor t'hy'la.” “sos'eh etek lau nam-tor tehs-tor.” “ik nam-tor ri maut kesik; etwel ek'te'kru vesh' nuh' rom.” fi' reaching wuh spacious lobby abru', au vesh' shown vi' wuh maut takov sitting-tvi-shal, lately fitted abru k' greater sohk'es heh lightness do wuh ha-shal ne'; heh vesh' informed ik ish-veh vesh' tonk'peh aishan ovsoh tor mazhiv-kur-tor sanosh tor din-tor darcy, vi had taken wuh liking tor wuh tvi-shal, lu kim-shah na' pemberley. “au nam-tor certainly wuh rom sa-kai, ” leralmin-tor elizabeth, u' she lates-tor na' veh t' wuh krani. Mrs. Reynolds anticipated din-tor darcy’s delight, lu she dang svi-tor wuh tvi-shal. “heh nash nam-tor kwon-hau-ov wuh yut k' ish-veh, ” she hau. “whatever mokuhlek mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh ko-kai sovek sanosh, nam-tor sure tor nam-tor ovsoh svi' wuh moment. Tra' nam-tor nothing au would ri tor na' ish-veh.” wuh bikuv tanaf-shi'gluvaun, heh dahkuh il rehkuh t' wuh principal sar-tak-tvi-shal, vesh' ek' ik hafau tor nam-tor shown. Svi' wuh former vesh' wehk rom paintings: tonk'peh elizabeth fai-tor nothing t' wuh tanaf; heh s' such u' had vesh' already visible ne', she had willingly da-tor tor glazhau na' ein drawings t' din-tor darcy’s, svi' crayons, t'vi subjects vesh' usually weht eku'ki, heh isha weht intelligible. Svi' wuh tanaf-shi'gluvaun tra' vesh' wehk skan portraits, tonk'peh au kupi ma pi' tor teslau wuh attention t' wuh ri-fainusu. Elizabeth lates-tor fi' svi' psthan t' wuh goh limuk t'vi features would nam-tor fainu tor ish-veh. Na' kim-shah ish-veh pehkau ish-veh--heh she beheld wuh striking resemblance t' mr. Darcy, k' such wuh abru'teruklar-ru'lut abru' wuh limuk, u' she vokau ki' sometimes gla-tor, lu au glazhau na' ish-veh. She lam-tor several minutes fa' wuh bikuv, svi' earnest contemplation, heh fun-tor tor ish-veh va'ashiv fa' au quitted wuh tanaf-shi'gluvaun. Mrs. Reynolds informed au, ik ish-veh had vesh' taken svi' ish-veh sa-mekh’s lifetime. Tra' vesh' certainly i', svi' elizabeth’s kashek, wuh weht gentle kashan na' wuh tveshik do she had ek'wak olau svi' wuh pidek t' ish-veh acquaintance. Wuh commendation bestowed fi' ish-veh k' mrs. Reynolds vesh' t' rai trifling malat. Ra krol nam-tor weht taluhk do wuh krol t' wuh kash-tok dvinsu? U' wuh sa-kai, wuh landlord, wuh trensu, she panah-tor uf wehk sutra’s happiness vesh' svi' ish-veh guardianship! Uf mau t' sanosh il kusut ish-veh vesh' svi' ish-veh tepul tor bestow! Uf mau t' rom il ek'rasah bolau nam-tor ovsoh k' ish-veh! Kanok idea ik had vesh' katau fa'rak k' wuh housekeeper vesh' favourable tor ish-veh character; heh u' she lam-tor fa' wuh canvas, fi' if au vesh' represented, heh teslau ish-veh bezhun fi-tor herself, she nahp t' ish-veh fudau k' wuh deeper sentiment t' gratitude do ish-veh had ek'wak ashenau fa': she vokau its warmth, heh softened its impropriety t' sagluvaya. Lu ek' t' wuh kelek ik vesh' tu'ash tor paik inspection had vesh' gla-tor, au fun-tor ne' kaiden; heh, taking trasha t' wuh housekeeper, vesh' consigned abru' tor wuh bahsu, vi ragel-tor au na' wuh tvur svep.
