U' au lates-tor mes' wuh yartra na' wuh pilash, elizabeth da-tor pla' tor glazhau va'ashiv; ish-veh sa-kuk heh ezyet pehkau isha; heh du' wuh former vesh' conjecturing u' tor wuh kinuf t' wuh kelek, wuh owner t' ish-veh himself suddenly sarlah fa'rak s' wuh fau-yut if pufulag-tor za' ish-veh tor wuh stables. Au vesh' k'svi dah-leh ker t' tik vath; heh ni abrupt vesh' ish-veh appearance, ik ish-veh vesh' impossible tor nan'woi ish-veh glan. Ish-veh bezhun instantly ragel-tor, heh wuh nak t' tik vesh' overspread k' wuh deepest blush. Au absolutely palikau, heh na' wuh moment seemed immovable s' ak'wikmun; tonk'peh shortly recovering himself, storilau na' wuh party, heh stariben tor elizabeth, kuv ri svi' zhil t' buhfik composure, k'puu t' buhfik civility. She had instinctively da-tor maf; tonk'peh stopping fi' ish-veh betaya, poprah ish-veh compliments k' wuh embarrassment impossible tor nam-tor overcome. Had ish-veh wuh'rak appearance, il ish-veh resemblance tor wuh bikuv au had aishan vesh' examining, vesh' insufficient tor assure wuh vath dahkuh ik au i' gla-tor mr. Darcy, wuh bahsu’s sagluvaya t' ak'wikmun, fi' beholding ish-veh trensu, bolau iyi ma var-tor ish-veh. Au lam-tor wuh pi' aloof du' au vesh' talking tor ish-veh ko-bath, vi, astonished heh confused, scarcely dared abertau ish-veh bezhun tor ish-veh limuk, heh fai-tor ri ra kilko-srashiv she fun-tor tor ish-veh civil inquiries po' ish-veh skan. Putaurau na' wuh alteration t' ish-veh manner opi' au kim-shah parted, kanok zhit-bal ik au uttered vesh' increasing ish-veh embarrassment; heh kanok idea t' wuh impropriety t' ish-veh hasu afer-tor tra' recurring tor ish-veh kashek, wuh zamu minutes svi' if au fator teretuhr vesh' ein t' wuh danik uncomfortable t' ish-veh ha'kiv. Il did au seem mau weht na' ease; lu au stariben, ish-veh accent had rim t' its tsuri sedateness; heh au ashiv-tor ish-veh inquiries u' tor wuh wak t' ish-veh having losrak longbourn, heh t' ish-veh stay svi' derbyshire, ni k'ashiv, heh svi' ni hurried wuh yut, u' plainly stariben wuh saglakolaya t' ish-veh nahp. Na' wu-vath, kanok idea seemed tor vravshau ish-veh; heh po' standing wuh zamu moments rik' taran wuh zhit, au suddenly recollected himself, heh nem-tor trasha. Wuh vath yi hau ish-veh, heh sagluvau ish-veh admiration t' ish-veh khlop; tonk'peh elizabeth puzhu-tor ri wuh zhit, heh, wholly engrossed k' ish-veh sha' feelings, zahal-tor au svi' silence. She vesh' overpowered k' mesh heh vexation. Ish-veh coming tra' vesh' wuh danik unfortunate, wuh danik has-bosh-judged vel svi' wuh panu! Uf flekh bolau ish-veh saudau tor ish-veh! Svi' ra wuh disgraceful ta'hal lau ish-veh ri kwul ni vain wuh sasu! Ish-veh lau seem u' kuv she had purposely lehm-tor herself svi' ish-veh yut va'ashiv! Oh! Po did she sarlah? Il, po did au thus sarlah wuh gad fa' au vesh' gishu? Had au vesh' goh lehkuh minutes sooner, au dang ma vesh' mesakh wuh pulau t' ish-veh sakathilaya; na' ish-veh vesh' eiktra ik au vesh' ik moment lasha, ik moment alighted s' ish-veh jarel il ish-veh carriage. She blushed va'ashiv heh va'ashiv abru' wuh perverseness t' wuh latva. Heh ish-veh kloshai, ni strikingly rubitau, --ra kupi ish-veh tvai? Ik au dang kauk stariben tor ish-veh vesh' taurauk!--tonk'peh tor stariben k' such civility, tor inquire po' ish-veh skan! Worla svi' ish-veh ha'kiv had she gla-tor ish-veh manners ni pi' dignified, worla had au spoken k' such gentleness u' fi' nash ri-gishu latva. Ra wuh contrast did ish-veh nufai tor ish-veh kim-shah shi'yavekh svi' rosings shi'sochya, lu au shitau ish-veh nuhm vi' ish-veh el'ru! She fai-tor ri ra tor nah-tor, il uf tor khrosahp na' ish-veh. Au had i' svi-tor wuh vaksurik lates k' wuh vla t' wuh masu, heh kanok ash vesh' bringing fa'rak wuh nobler tevan t' solektra, il wuh finer pulau t' wuh lapan tor if au vesh' approaching: tonk'peh ish-veh vesh' ein wak fa' elizabeth vesh' sensible t' sovek t' ish-veh; heh, hi she kilko-tor mechanically tor wuh ashiv-tor appeals t' ish-veh sa-kuk heh ezyet, heh seemed tor kharik ish-veh bezhun tor such vel u' au sasfekau, she distinguished rai krus t' wuh scene. Ish-veh nahp vesh' ek' teslau fi' ik veh gla-tor t' pemberley kelek, whichever ish-veh lau nam-tor, wilat mr. Darcy yi vesh'. She longed tor fai-tor ra na' ik moment vesh' be' dvun-tor svi' ish-veh kashek; svi' ra manner au nahp t' ish-veh, heh whether, svi' defiance t' kanok-vei, she vesh' fam dvun tal-kam tor ish-veh. Sos'eh au had vesh' civil goh fai'ei au olau himself na' ease; wi tra' had vesh' _that_ svi' ish-veh spes, if vesh' ri spo' ease. Whether au had olau weht t' kusut il t' sanosh svi' seeing ish-veh, she kupi ri var-tor, tonk'peh au certainly had ri gla-tor ish-veh k' composure. Na' wu-vath, however, wuh remarks t' ish-veh besu fi' ish-veh k'torr kashek kastorilau ish-veh, heh she olau wuh bolayek t' appearing weht spo' herself. Au svi-tor wuh lapan, heh, nufai-tor adieu tor wuh pilash na' wuh du', she-tor ein t' wuh higher solektra; whence, svi' gla-tor wilat wuh sharu t' wuh lap mazhiv-kur-tor wuh bezhun tepul tor czar, vesh' wehk sem-rik-tor zan-tor t' wuh ku-li, wuh mesyutik kunel, k' wuh wu eik'es t' lapan overspreading wehk, heh occasionally krus t' wuh pilash. Mr. Gardiner sagluvau wuh istaya t' going pauk wuh bosh shi'sochya, tonk'peh ptha ish-veh lau nam-tor mesakh wuh lates. K' wuh triumphant abru'teruklar-ru'lut, au vesh' var-tor, ik ish-veh vesh' lehkuh miles pauk. Ish-veh settled wuh tukh; heh au pursued wuh accustomed raf-kuv; if katau au va'ashiv, po' ein wak, svi' wuh tevan among hanging lapan, tor wuh rihk t' wuh masu, heh veh t' its narrowest krus. Au tuhsau ish-veh k' wuh velik mesut, svi' character k' wuh paik sov t' wuh scene: ish-veh vesh' wuh gla-tor lehkuh tong'av do sovek au had wi yaretau; heh wuh ku-li, la' contracted vi' wuh glen, kal-tor tvi-shal goh na' wuh pilash, heh wuh wonil lates amidst wuh rough coppice-lapan if bordered ish-veh. Elizabeth longed tor explore its windings; tonk'peh lu au had tuhsau wuh mesut, heh pakashogau ish-veh ir s' wuh kelek, mrs. Gardiner, vi vesh' ri wuh lo'uk walker, kupi hal-tor rai weh-irak, heh nahp goh t' returning tor wuh carriage u' sahris u' tor-yehat. Ish-veh ko-bath vesh', therefore, obliged tor nekhau, heh au nem-tor ish-veh yut na' wuh kelek fi' wuh mesyutik vla t' wuh pilash, svi' wuh nearest kharat; tonk'peh ish-veh progress vesh' vohris, na' mr. Gardiner, hi seldom kup tor indulge wuh zahvan, vesh' maut tishau t' fishing, heh vesh' ni mau engaged svi' watching wuh occasional appearance t' ein trout svi' wuh masu, heh talking tor wuh sasu pa' au, ik au storilau tonk'peh pi'. Whilst wandering fi' svi' nash vohris manner, au vesh' va'ashiv ak'wikmun, heh elizabeth’s astonishment vesh' ved kaik tor ra ish-veh had vesh' palikauk, k' wuh glan t' mr. Darcy approaching au, heh na' rai lo'uk ir. Wuh lates hasu la' lehkuh rau-tor do fi' wuh vath vla, kal-tor au tor gla-tor ish-veh fa' au ragel-tor. Elizabeth, however astonished, vesh' k'puu weht dator na' wuh interview do fa', heh resolved tor saudau heh tor stariben k' calmness, kuv au really intended tor ragel-tor au. Na' wuh zamu moments, indeed, she olau ik au would probably kwul vi' ein vath yut. Wuh idea palesh-tor du' wuh turning svi' wuh lates ip-sut ish-veh s' ish-veh zan-tor; wuh turning vesht, au vesh' iyi fa' au. K' wuh glance gla-tor ish-veh ik au had pakik rim t' ish-veh recent civility; heh, tor va'amau ish-veh politeness, she began u' au ragel-tor tor krol-tor wuh vaksur t' wuh shi; tonk'peh she had ri prah mesakh wuh zhit “delightful, ” heh “sem-rik-tor, ” lu ein unlucky recollections obtruded, heh she fancied ik krol t' pemberley s' ish-veh lau nam-tor mischievously construed. Ish-veh kur rubai, heh she leralmin-tor rai weht. Mrs. Gardiner vesh' standing wuh pi' za'; heh fi' ish-veh pausing, au ya'akash ish-veh kuv she would tor ish-veh wuh dor t' introducing ish-veh tor ish-veh t'hylara. Nash vesh' wuh shad-kisheya t' civility na' if she vesh' ved unprepared; heh she kupi hardly nelau wuh abru'teruklar-ru'lut na' ish-veh hasu i' seeking wuh acquaintance t' ein t' eifa maut sutra, tehnat ik ish-veh pride had revolted, svi' ish-veh nufai tor herself. “ra dungi nam-tor ish-veh ak'wikmun, ” nahp she, “lu au fai-tor vi au nam-tor! Au nem-tor au i' na' sutra t' fashion.” wuh ragtaya, however, vesh' iyi tor; heh u' she ahmau ish-veh relationship tor herself, she vazgau wuh sly glazhau na' ish-veh, tor gla-tor uf au spitau ish-veh; heh vesh' ri rik' wuh gishat t' ish-veh decamping u' sahris u' au kupi s' such disgraceful besu. Ik au vesh' _surprised_ k' wuh tersaya vesh' evident: au potun-tor ish-veh, however, k' fortitude: heh, ni irak s' going maf, da-tor pla' k' au, heh svi-tor vi' conversation k' mr. Gardiner. Elizabeth kupi ri tonk'peh nam-tor sanoi, kupi ri tonk'peh triumph. Ish-veh vesh' consoling ik au dang fai-tor she had ein relations na' ik tra' vesh' rai bolaya tor blush. She shroi danik attentively tor ek' ik be' dvun-tor svi' au, heh gloried svi' kanok sagluvaya, kanok zhit-bal t' ish-veh sa-kuk, if pu'ulidau ish-veh kash-tor'es, ish-veh zahvan, il ish-veh rom manners. Wuh conversation ak da-tor fi-tor fishing; heh she puzhu-tor mr. Darcy invite ish-veh, k' wuh greatest civility, tor aluk tra' u' k'ashiv u' au dvel-tor, du' au fator svi' wuh neighbourhood, nufaya na' wuh ka wak tor tanilau ish-veh k' fishing tackle, heh pointing si' eifa krus t' wuh pilash wilat tra' vesh' usually danik torvukh. Mrs. Gardiner, vi vesh' walking kar svi' kar k' elizabeth, mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh wuh glazhau expressive t' ish-veh wonder. Elizabeth leralmin-tor nothing, tonk'peh ish-veh gratified ish-veh exceedingly; wuh compliment bolau nam-tor ek' na' herself. Ish-veh astonishment, however, vesh' mairik; heh continually vesh' she repeating, “po nam-tor au ni rubitau? S' ra mokuhlek ish-veh proceed? Ish-veh fam yehat nam-tor na' _me_, ish-veh fam yehat nam-tor na' _my_ sake ik ish-veh manners nam-tor thus softened. T'nash-veh reproofs na' hunsford kupi ri ar'kadan such wuh rubah u' nash. Ish-veh nam-tor impossible ik au dang fam dvun ashaya me.” po' walking ein wak svi' nash yut, wuh dahkuh t'sai svi' khom, wuh dahkuh gentlemen za', fi' resuming ish-veh shitau, po' descending tor wuh rihk t' wuh pilash na' wuh weh-rom inspection t' ein curious masu-kastik, tra' chanced tor nam-tor wuh pi' alteration. Ish-veh tveshulau svi' mrs. Gardiner, vi, zung-tor k' wuh tusok t' wuh asal, afer-tor elizabeth’s kar inadequate tor ish-veh nenikaya, heh consequently preferred ish-veh sa-telsu’s. Mr. Darcy nem-tor ish-veh shi k' ish-veh ko-bath, heh au lates-tor fi' teretuhr. Po' wuh pen silence wuh t'sai wuh'rak stariben. She istau ish-veh tor fai-tor ik she had vesh' assured t' ish-veh absence fa' sarlah ish-veh tor wuh shi, heh accordingly began k' observing, ik ish-veh lashan had vesh' maut ri-gishu--“na' ish-veh housekeeper, ” she hau, “informed etek ik du would certainly ri nam-tor la' till tor-morrow; heh, indeed, fa' etek losrak bakewell, etek ken-tor ik du vesh' ri iyi gishu svi' wuh shasol.” au nafai wuh yeht'es t' ish-veh ek'; heh leralmin-tor ik business k' ish-veh steward had occasioned ish-veh coming fa'rak wuh zamu wadan fa' wuh shom t' wuh party k' ik au had vesh' travelling. “au dungi hau me lehkuh-mal tor-morrow, ” au fator, “heh ekhlami nam-tor ein vi dungi claim wuh acquaintance k' du, --mr. Bingley heh ish-veh ko-kai.” elizabeth kilko-tor goh k' wuh slight kes-wun. Ish-veh nahp vesh' instantly driven pla' tor wuh wak lu mr. Bingley’s ahm had vesh' kim-shah mentioned svi' au; heh kuv she lau judge s' ish-veh complexion, _his_ kashek vesh' ri maut differently engaged. “tra' nam-tor isha veh vath person svi' wuh party, ” au fator po' wuh svizh, “vi weht wa' istau tor nam-tor fainu tor du. Dungi du kal-tor me, il tor i ya'akash nuh' mau, tor ragtau t'nash-veh ko-kai tor ish-veh acquaintance du' ish-veh stay na' lambton?” wuh ak'wikmun t' such wuh application vesh' lo'uk indeed; ish-veh vesh' nuh' lo'uk na' ish-veh tor fai-tor svi' ra manner she acceded tor ish-veh. She iyi olau ik whatever aitlun din-tor darcy lau ma t' hasu acquainted k' ish-veh, bolau nam-tor wuh ar'kadan t' ish-veh sa-kai, heh rik' looking weh-irak, ish-veh vesh' satisfactory; ish-veh vesh' gratifying tor fai-tor ik ish-veh resentment had ri tor ish-veh nah-tor really has-bosh t' ish-veh. Au i' lates-tor fi' svi' silence; tik t' au glu svi' nahp. Elizabeth vesh' ri kel'o; ik vesh' impossible; tonk'peh she vesh' snuhkrol-tor heh sanoi. Ish-veh istaya t' introducing ish-veh ko-kai tor ish-veh vesh' wuh compliment t' wuh k'lek ves. Au ak outstripped wuh vath; heh lu au had pulau wuh carriage, mr. Heh mrs. Gardiner vesh' ulef wuh yonuk t' wuh mile za'. Au yi ya'akash ish-veh tor lates vi' wuh kelek--tonk'peh she afsakau herself ri zungor, heh au lam-tor teretuhr fi' wuh yartra. Na' such wuh wak mau lau ma vesh' leralmin-tor, heh silence vesh' maut awkward. She aitlu tor variben, tonk'peh tra' seemed wuh embargo fi' kanok subject. Na' kim-shah she recollected ik she had vesh' travelling, heh au variben t' matlock heh dovedale k' lo'uk perseverance. Wi wak heh ish-veh ezyet dvun-tor slowly--heh ish-veh tranush heh ish-veh ideas vesh' nearly worn si' fa' wuh _tête-à-tête_ vesh' abru'. Fi' mr. Heh mrs. Gardiner’s coming abru au vesh' ek' hish-tor tor hal-tor vi' wuh kelek heh nem-tor ein refreshment; tonk'peh nash vesh' declined, heh au parted fi' tik vla k' wuh utmost politeness. Mr. Darcy handed wuh t'sai vi' wuh carriage; heh lu ish-veh drove ska', elizabeth gla-tor ish-veh walking slowly na' wuh kelek. Wuh glantaya t' ish-veh sa-kuk heh ezyet i' began; heh tik t' au pronounced ish-veh tor nam-tor infinitely superior tor sovek-vel au had gishu. “au nam-tor perfectly muhl-behaved, polite, heh unassuming, ” leralmin-tor ish-veh sa-kuk. “tra' _is_ vel wuh pi' stately svi' ish-veh, tor nam-tor sure, ” kilko-tor ish-veh ezyet; “tonk'peh ish-veh nam-tor confined tor ish-veh sov, heh nam-tor ri unbecoming. I mokuhlek i' leralmin k' wuh housekeeper, ik hi ein sutra lau vutau ish-veh yaut, _i_ ma gla-tor nothing t' ish-veh.” “i vesh' worla weht ak'wikmun do k' ish-veh kloshai tor etek. Ish-veh vesh' weht do civil; ish-veh vesh' really whio'naks; heh tra' vesh' rai bolayek na' such attention. Ish-veh acquaintance k' elizabeth vesh' maut trifling.” “tor nam-tor sure, lizzy, ” leralmin-tor ish-veh ezyet, “au nam-tor ri ni handsome u' wickham; il rather au has ri wickham’s countenance, na' ish-veh features nam-tor perfectly rom. Tonk'peh uf sarlah du tor var-tor etek ik au vesh' ni disagreeable?” elizabeth tobeg-tor herself u' muhl u' she kupi: leralmin-tor ik she had tishau ish-veh weh-rom lu au ragel-tor svi' kent do fa', heh ik she had worla gla-tor ish-veh ni vaksurik u' nash asal. “tonk'peh sos'eh au lau nam-tor wuh pi' whimsical svi' ish-veh civilities, ” kilko-tor ish-veh sa-kuk. “ish-veh lo'uk sasu k'ashiv nam-tor; heh therefore i dungau ri nem-tor ish-veh na' ish-veh zhit pa' fishing, u' au lau rubah ish-veh kashek wuh'ashiv gad, heh vikau me ska' ish-veh solektra.” elizabeth olau ik au had entirely mistaken ish-veh character, tonk'peh leralmin-tor nothing. “s' ra gla-tor etek t' ish-veh, ” fator mrs. Gardiner, “i really dang ri ma nahp ik au kupi ma behaved svi' ni pi-maat'rer wuh yut k' anybody u' au has ovsoh k' ri donku-tor wickham. Au has ri wuh has-bosh-natured glazhau. Fi' wuh contrary, tra' nam-tor vel pleasing pa' ish-veh ru'lut lu au stariben. Heh tra' nam-tor vel t' dignity svi' ish-veh countenance, ik would ri mazhiv-kur-tor veh wuh unfavourable idea t' ish-veh khaf-spol. Tonk'peh, tor nam-tor sure, wuh rom t'sai vi gluvau etek wuh kelek did mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh wuh danik flaming character! I kupi hardly gol'nev laughing aloud sometimes. Tonk'peh au nam-tor wuh liberal trensu, i suppose, heh _that_, svi' wuh bezhun t' wuh dvinsu, comprehends kanok virtue.” elizabeth la' olau herself puvutau fi' tor leralmin vel svi' vindication t' ish-veh kloshai tor wickham; heh, therefore, mazhiv-kur-tor au tor ken-tor, svi' u' klashau wuh manner u' she kupi, ik k' ra she had puzhu-tor s' ish-veh relations svi' kent, ish-veh torai vesh' capable t' wuh maut natya torvaya; heh ik ish-veh character vesh' k' rai tvai ni lafotik, il wickham’s ni amiable, u' au had vesh' panah-tor svi' hertfordshire. Svi' wugaya t' nash, she related wuh particulars t' ek' wuh pecuniary transactions svi' if au had vesh' tersau, rik' actually naming ish-veh ek'te'kru, tonk'peh fupa s' ish-veh tor nam-tor such u' lau nam-tor relied fi'. Mrs. Gardiner vesh' ak'wikmun heh concerned: tonk'peh u' au vesh' i' approaching wuh scene t' ish-veh former pleasures, kanok idea mazhiv-kur-tor yut tor wuh sem-rik t' recollection; heh she vesh' nuh' mau engaged svi' pointing si' tor ish-veh sa-telsu ek' wuh eku'ki gla-tor svi' its environs, tor nah-tor t' sovek-kitok. Zung-tor u' she had vesh' k' wuh asal’s lates, au had rai sooner aru-yokul do she eku ska' va'ashiv svi' psthan t' ish-veh former acquaintance, heh wuh khru vesh' spent svi' wuh satisfactions t' wuh intercourse uzhau po' wehk tevun’ discontinuance. Wuh occurrences t' wuh gad vesh' nuh' bosh t' eku'ko tor trasha elizabeth mau attention na' sovek t' aifa uzh t'hylara; heh she kupi tor nothing tonk'peh nah-tor, heh nah-tor k' wonder, t' mr. Darcy’s civility, heh, abru' ek', t' ish-veh wishing ish-veh tor nam-tor acquainted k' ish-veh ko-kai. [illustration] chapter xliv. [illustration] elizabeth had settled ish-veh ik mr. Darcy would katau ish-veh ko-kai tor yaret ish-veh wuh maut gad po' ish-veh reaching pemberley; heh vesh', consequently, resolved ri tor nam-tor s' glan t' wuh ha-shal wuh bosh t' ik asal. Tonk'peh ish-veh conclusion vesh' riyeht; na' fi' wuh maut asal po' ish-veh sha' lashan na' lambton aifa visitors sarlah. Au had vesh' walking pa' wuh shi k' ein t' ish-veh uzh t'hylara, heh vesh' aishan fun-tor tor wuh ha-shal sai-vel-tor themselves na' dining k' wuh ka skan, lu wuh ralash t' wuh carriage drew au tor wuh krani, heh gla-tor au wuh gentleman heh t'sai svi' wuh curricle driving abru wuh yut. Elizabeth, iyi recognizing wuh livery, guessed ra ish-veh tvai, heh imparted rai pi' degree t' ak'wikmun tor ish-veh relations, k' acquainting au k' wuh dor if she gishu. Ish-veh sa-kuk heh ezyet vesh' ek' tauraya; heh wuh embarrassment t' ish-veh manner u' she stariben, hau tor wuh circumstance itself, heh wehk t' wuh circumstances t' wuh preceding gad, tu'ash tor au wuh uzh idea fi' wuh business. Nothing had ek'wak suggested ish-veh fa', tonk'peh au i' olau ik tra' vesh' rai vath yut t' accounting na' such attentions s' such wuh yonuk do k' supposing wuh partiality na' ish-veh ko-bath. Du' aifa newly-pukeshta notions vesh' be' dvun-tor svi' ish-veh patam, wuh perturbation t' elizabeth’s feelings vesh' kanok moment increasing. She vesh' ved putaurau na' ish-veh sha' discomposure; tonk'peh, svi' vath aisha t' disquiet, she dreaded lest wuh partiality t' wuh sa-kai dang ma leralmin-tor nuh' mau svi' ish-veh favour; heh, weht do commonly anxious tor sanoi, she naturally suspected ik kanok tepul t' pleasing would vravshau ish-veh. She retreated s' wuh krani, pthak-bosh t' hasu gla-tor; heh u' she lates-tor abru heh ne' wuh tvi-shal, endeavouring tor tertitau herself, gla-tor such glazhau t' inquiring ak'wikmun svi' ish-veh sa-kuk heh ezyet u' tor kanok-vei weh-rasahkos. Din-tor darcy heh ish-veh sa-kai saudau, heh nash formidable ragtaya nem-tor shi. K' astonishment did elizabeth gla-tor ik ish-veh uzh acquaintance vesh' k'puu u' mau embarrassed u' herself. Opi' ish-veh hasu na' lambton, she had puzhu-tor ik din-tor darcy vesh' exceedingly yaut; tonk'peh wuh glantaya t' wuh maut zamu minutes convinced ish-veh ik she vesh' goh exceedingly fusik. She afer-tor ish-veh rihagik tor prah kauk wuh zhit s' ish-veh mesakh wuh monosyllable. Din-tor darcy vesh' ha-vol, heh fi' wuh larger wef do elizabeth; heh, hi pi' weht do leh-sheh, ish-veh khlop vesh' shidau, heh ish-veh appearance womanly heh graceful. She vesh' lehkuh handsome do ish-veh sa-kai, tonk'peh tra' vesh' kash-ral heh rom-humour svi' ish-veh limuk, heh ish-veh manners vesh' perfectly unassuming heh gentle. Elizabeth, vi had gishu tor talal svi' ish-veh u' zat heh unembarrassed wuh observer u' ek'wak mr. Darcy had vesh', vesh' mau vas-tor k' discerning such natya feelings. Au had ri vesh' wu teretuhr fa' darcy var-tor ish-veh ik bingley vesh' isha coming tor bek-tor fi' ish-veh; heh she had barely wak tor sagluvau ish-veh satisfaction, heh dator na' such wuh visitor, lu bingley’s sahris ash vesh' puzhu-tor fi' wuh kaiden, heh svi' wuh moment au svi-tor wuh tvi-shal. Ek' elizabeth’s reshan tehnat ish-veh had vesh' wu ovsoh maf; tonk'peh had she fam dvun olau sovek, ish-veh kupi hardly ma lam-tor its solektra tehnat wuh unaffected cordiality k' if au sagluvau himself fi' seeing ish-veh va'ashiv. Au inquired svi' wuh friendly, hi paik, yut, po' ish-veh skan, heh glazhau heh stariben k' wuh ka rom-humoured ease ik au had ek'wak ovsoh. Tor mr. Heh mrs. Gardiner au vesh' scarcely wuh lehkuh eku'ki personage do tor herself. Au had wu istau tor gla-tor ish-veh. Wuh bosh party fa' au, indeed, teporilau wuh lively attention. Wuh suspicions if had aishan arisen t' mr. Darcy heh ish-veh ko-bath, khartau ish-veh glantaya na' tik k' wuh earnest, hi klashau, inquiry; heh au ak drew s' eifa inquiries wuh bosh conviction ish-veh t' au k'puu fai-tor ra ish-veh vesh' tor ashaya. T' wuh t'sai’s kashan au hafau wuh pi' svi' vet; tonk'peh ik wuh gentleman vesh' overflowing k' admiration vesh' evident hiyet. Elizabeth, fi' ish-veh vla, had mau tor tor. She aitlu tor ascertain wuh feelings t' tik t' ish-veh visitors, she aitlu tor tertitau ish-veh sha', heh tor tor herself agreeable tor ek'; heh svi' wuh latter vel, wilat she ptha danik tor vravshau, she vesh' danik sure t' navun, na' eifa tor ik she endeavoured tor mazhiv-kur-tor sanosh vesh' pre-ma svi' ish-veh favour. Bingley vesh' pok, georgiana vesh' nayik, heh darcy satalau, tor nam-tor sanoi. [illustration: “tor tor herself agreeable tor ek'” [_copyright 1894 k' george allen._]] svi' seeing bingley, ish-veh nahp naturally flew tor ish-veh ko-kai; heh oh! Uf ardently did she wu tor fai-tor whether sovek t' ish-veh vesh' khartau svi' wuh spo' manner. Sometimes she kupi fancy ik au variben lehkuh tor fi' former occasions, heh wuh'wak il dah'wak sanoi herself k' wuh notion ik, u' au glazhau na' ish-veh, au vesh' trying tor zavikau wuh resemblance. Tonk'peh, hi nash lau nam-tor glenonik, she kupi ri nam-tor tehs-tor u' tor ish-veh kloshai tor din-tor darcy, vi had vesh' eku abru u' wuh rival tor jane. Rai glazhau saudau fi' either vla ik stariben particular fudau. Nothing paresh-tor svi' au ik kupi justify wuh rok-tor t' ish-veh ko-kai. Fi' nash sfek she vesh' ak satisfied; heh dahkuh il rehkuh pi' circumstances paresh-tor ere au parted, if, svi' ish-veh anxious interpretation, denoted wuh recollection t' jane, ri untinctured k' tenderness, heh wuh istaya t' taran weht ik lau ras-tukh tor wuh mention t' ish-veh, had au dared. Au glantau tor ish-veh, na' wuh moment lu wuh vath vesh' talking teretuhr, heh svi' wuh molu if had vel t' yeht regret, ik ish-veh “vesh' wuh maut wu wak opi' au had had wuh sanosh t' seeing ish-veh; ” heh, fa' she kupi kilko, au hau, “ish-veh nam-tor abru' ohkuh tevun-krus. Etek ma ri ragel-tor opi' wuh 26th t' november, lu etek vesh' ek' taman teretuhr na' netherfield.” elizabeth vesh' sanoi tor talal ish-veh vokaya ni faikaik; heh au afterwards nem-tor occasion tor ya'akash ish-veh, lu unattended tor k' sovek t' wuh shom, whether _all_ ish-veh ko-kai vesh' na' longbourn. Tra' vesh' ri mau svi' wuh deshker, il svi' wuh preceding remark; tonk'peh tra' vesh' wuh glazhau heh wuh manner if mazhiv-kur-tor au meaning. Ish-veh vesh' ri k'ashiv ik she kupi da-tor ish-veh bezhun fi' mr. Darcy himself; tonk'peh whenever she did kum wuh glimpse gla-tor ish-veh wuh sagluvaya t' paik complaisance, heh svi' ek' ik au leralmin-tor, she puzhu-tor wuh accent ni irak snem-tor s' _hauteur_ il disdain t' ish-veh besu, u' convinced ish-veh ik wuh improvement t' manners if she had za-gad toglantau, however rikwonik its nam lau skan-tor, had k'puu outlived veh gad. Lu gla-tor ish-veh ish-veh thus seeking wuh acquaintance, heh courting wuh rom opinion t' sutra k' ik sovek intercourse wuh zamu tevun-krus ago would ma vesh' wuh disgrace; lu gla-tor ish-veh ish-veh thus civil, ri goh tor herself, tonk'peh tor wuh maut relations ik au had openly disdained, heh recollected ish-veh kim-shah lively scene svi' hunsford parsonage, wuh natyan, wuh rubah vesh' ni lo'uk, heh kwul-tor ni forcibly fi' ish-veh kashek, ik she kupi hardly restrain ish-veh astonishment s' hasu visible. Worla, kauk svi' wuh apc'koik t' ish-veh tal-kam t'hylara na' netherfield, il ish-veh dignified relations na' rosings, had she gla-tor ish-veh ni desirous tor sanoi, ni elik s' shal-consequence il unbending reserve, u' i', lu rai importance kupi result s' wuh navun t' ish-veh endeavours, heh lu kauk wuh acquaintance t' eifa tor ik ish-veh attentions vesh' addressed, would bes-tor ne' wuh ridicule heh censure t' wuh t'sai fi' t' netherfield heh rosings. Ish-veh visitors stayed k' au abru' ulef wuh wadan; heh lu au arose tor trashu, mr. Darcy puvutau fi' ish-veh ko-kai tor hau ish-veh svi' expressing ish-veh istaya t' seeing mr. Heh mrs. Gardiner, heh din-tor bennet, tor aru-yem na' pemberley, fa' au losrak wuh shasol. Din-tor darcy, hi k' wuh diffidence if pu'ulidau ish-veh pi' svi' wuh es'merka t' giving k'waw'zhe, readily obeyed. Mrs. Gardiner glazhau na' ish-veh ko-bath, desirous t' fai-tor uf _she_, ik wuh k'waw'zhe danik concerned, olau sashitau u' tor its acceptance, tonk'peh elizabeth had da-tor maf ish-veh patam. Presuming, however, ik nash orenau avoidance stariben rather wuh momentary embarrassment do sovek ritishaya t' wuh mnah, heh seeing svi' ish-veh sa-telsu, vi vesh' tishau t' shila'es, wuh buhfik willingness tor nar-tor ish-veh, she ventured tor engage na' ish-veh attendance, heh wuh gad po' wuh thurai vesh' teslau fi'. Bingley sagluvau lo'uk sanosh svi' wuh certainty t' seeing elizabeth va'ashiv, having fam dvun wuh lo'uk deal tor leralmin tor ish-veh, heh wehk inquiries tor tor po' ek' ish-veh hertfordshire t'hylara. Elizabeth, construing ek' nash vi' wuh istaya t' khaf-spol ish-veh stariben t' ish-veh ko-kai, vesh' sanoi; heh fi' nash khrosahp, u' muhl u' ein vath, afer-tor herself, lu ish-veh visitors losrak au, capable t' panahik wuh kim-shah ulef wadan k' ein satisfaction, hi du' ish-veh vesh' be' dvun-tor wuh tizh'es t' ish-veh had vesh' pi'. Nayik tor nam-tor sa'awek, heh pthak-bosh t' inquiries il hints s' ish-veh sa-kuk heh ezyet, she stayed k' au goh wu hiyet tor zhu-tor ish-veh favourable opinion t' bingley, heh yi hurried maf sai-vel-tor. Tonk'peh she had rai utvau tor pthak mr. Heh mrs. Gardiner’s curiosity; ish-veh vesh' ri ish-veh istaya tor nekwitaya ish-veh sviribaya. Ish-veh vesh' evident ik she vesh' mau weh-rom acquainted k' mr. Darcy do au had fa' sovek idea t'; ish-veh vesh' evident ik au vesh' maut mau svi' ashaya k' ish-veh. Gla-tor au mau tor eku'ko, tonk'peh nothing tor justify inquiry. T' mr. Darcy ish-veh vesh' i' wuh tukh t' anxiety tor nah-tor muhl; heh, u' irak u' ish-veh acquaintance pulau, tra' vesh' rai lafot tor talal. Au kupi ri nam-tor untouched k' ish-veh politeness; heh had au drawn ish-veh character s' ish-veh sha' feelings heh ish-veh dvinsu’s report, rik' sovek dzhinaya tor sovek vath khrosahp, wuh da-kuv svi' hertfordshire tor if au vesh' fainu would ri ma recognized ish-veh na' mr. Darcy. Tra' vesh' i' wuh eku'ko, however, svi' believing wuh housekeeper; heh au ak became sensible ik wuh ek'te'kru t' wuh dvinsu, vi had fainu ish-veh opi' au vesh' kehkuh tevun hinek, heh t'vi sha' manners indicated respectability, vesh' ri tor nam-tor hastily rejected. Neither had sovek-vel paresh-tor svi' wuh kash-tor'es t' ish-veh lambton t'hylara ik kupi materially lessen its rasath. Au had nothing tor accuse ish-veh t' tonk'peh pride; pride au probably had, heh kuv ri, ish-veh would certainly nam-tor imputed k' wuh inhabitants t' wuh pi' mahr-kel kahr wilat wuh skan did ri yaret. Ish-veh vesh' nafai, however, ik au vesh' wuh liberal sasu, heh did mau rom among wuh ri donku-tor. K' respect tor wickham, wuh travellers ak afer-tor ik au vesh' ri meskarau tra' svi' mau estimation; na' hi wuh chief t' ish-veh concerns k' wuh sa-fu t' ish-veh patron vesh' imperfectly ken-tor, ish-veh vesh' wi wuh muhl-fainu kla-min ik, fi' ish-veh quitting derbyshire, au had losrak wehk sa'akh za' ish-veh, if mr. Darcy afterwards khrasau. U' na' elizabeth, ish-veh nahp vesh' na' pemberley nash khru weht do wuh kim-shah; heh wuh khru, hi u' ish-veh be' dvun-tor ish-veh seemed wu, vesh' ri wu hiyet tor satalau ish-veh feelings na' _one_ svi' ik mansion; heh she ti kum'i dahkuh bosh wadan, endeavouring tor tor au si'. She certainly did ri fnu-ven ish-veh. Rai; hatred had vanished wu ago, heh she had siyah u' wu vesh' kafusik t' ek'wak olaya wuh ritishaya tehnat ish-veh, ik kupi nam-tor ni puvutau. Wuh respect fereik-tor k' wuh conviction t' ish-veh taluhk qualities, hi palikauk unwillingly nafai-tor, had na' ein wak ceased tor nam-tor repugnant tor ish-veh feelings; heh ish-veh vesh' i' heightened vi' somewhat t' wuh friendlier malat k' wuh testimony ni highly svi' ish-veh favour, heh bringing fa'rak ish-veh disposition svi' ni amiable wuh ta'hal, if za-gad had torvau. Tonk'peh abru' ek', abru' respect heh vam, tra' vesh' wuh dvubolek k'svi ish-veh t' rom-dungi if kupi ri nam-tor overlooked. Ish-veh vesh' gratitude; --gratitude, ri goh na' having wuh'wak ashau ish-veh, tonk'peh na' loving ish-veh fam dvun muhl hiyet tor forgive ek' wuh petulance heh acrimony t' ish-veh manner svi' rejecting ish-veh, heh ek' wuh unjust accusations accompanying ish-veh rejection. Au vi, she had vesh' persuaded, would nan'woi ish-veh u' ish-veh greatest nemut, seemed, fi' nash ur'kif latva, danik nayik tor korsau wuh acquaintance; heh rik' sovek indelicate gluvayek t' fudau, il sovek peculiarity t' manner, wilat ish-veh dahkuh selves goh vesh' concerned, vesh' soliciting wuh rom opinion t' ish-veh t'hylara, heh keh'sei fi' tor ish-veh fainu tor ish-veh ko-kai. Such wuh rubah svi' wuh sasu t' ni mau pride teporilau ri goh astonishment tonk'peh gratitude--na' tor ashaya, ardent ashaya, ish-veh bolau nam-tor attributed; heh, u' such, its impression fi' ish-veh vesh' t' wuh wihfelau tor nam-tor kastorau, u' k' rai tvai unpleasing, hi ish-veh kupi ri nam-tor exactly mesprah. She respected, she vam, she vesh' grateful tor ish-veh, she olau wuh yeht eku'ko svi' ish-veh welfare; heh she goh aitlu tor fai-tor uf irak she istau ik welfare tor nerau fi-tor herself, heh uf irak ish-veh would nam-tor na' wuh happiness t' fi' ik she dang employ wuh tepul, if ish-veh fancy var-tor ish-veh she fam dvun ma, t' bringing fi' wuh renewal t' ish-veh shi'yavekh. Ish-veh had vesh' settled svi' wuh khru, svi' wuh ezyet heh ko-bath, ik such wuh striking civility u' din-tor darcy’s, svi' coming tor au fi' wuh maut gad t' ish-veh lashan na' pemberley--na' she had pulau ish-veh goh tor wuh tab-ma asal-yem--ought tor nam-tor va'amau, hi ish-veh kupi ri nam-tor equalled, k' ein pideshan t' politeness fi' ish-veh vla; heh, consequently, ik ish-veh would nam-tor highly expedient tor bek-tor fi' ish-veh na' pemberley wuh zahalik asal. Au vesh', therefore, tor hal-tor. Elizabeth vesh' sanoi; hi lu she ya'akash herself wuh utvau, she had maut pi' tor leralmin svi' kilko. Mr. Gardiner losrak au ak po' asal-yem. Wuh fishing scheme had vesh' uzhau wuh gad fa', heh wuh a'rak engagement tor t' ish-veh latva ein t' wuh gentlemen na' pemberley k' aru. [illustration: “engaged k' wuh pilash” ] chapter xlv. [illustration] convinced u' elizabeth i' vesh' ik din-tor bingley’s ritishaya t' ish-veh had tveshulau svi' jealousy, she kupi ri gol'nev olaya uf maut unwelcome ish-veh appearance na' pemberley bolau nam-tor tor ish-veh, heh vesh' curious tor fai-tor k' uf mau civility fi' ik t'sai’s vla wuh acquaintance would i' nam-tor uzhau. Fi' reaching wuh kelek, au vesh' shown k'fai wuh tvur vi' wuh saloon, t'vi northern pulva rendered ish-veh delightful na' belaar. Its krani, sharu tor wuh solektra, nafai-tor wuh danik refreshing zan-tor t' wuh pid lapanik kunel za' wuh kelek, heh t' wuh vaksurik oaks heh spanish chestnuts if vesh' scattered abru' wuh intermediate yartra. Svi' nash tvi-shal au vesh' poprah k' din-tor darcy, vi vesh' sitting tra' k' mrs. Hurst heh din-tor bingley, heh wuh t'sai k' ik she ha-tor svi' london. Georgiana’s reception t' au vesh' maut civil, tonk'peh attended k' ek' ik embarrassment if, hi proceeding s' shyness heh wuh pthak t' doing riyeht, would easily mazhiv-kur-tor tor eifa vi olau themselves inferior wuh dva t' ish-veh hasu yaut heh reserved. Mrs. Gardiner heh ish-veh ko-bath, however, did ish-veh yeht-gav, heh pitied ish-veh. K' mrs. Hurst heh din-tor bingley au vesh' pubeglanau goh k' wuh nuhk'es; heh fi' ish-veh hasu hayal-tor, wuh svizh, awkward u' such svizh-tor bolau kwon-hau-ov nam-tor, navau na' wuh zamu moments. Ish-veh vesh' wuh'rak pushau k' mrs. Annesley, wuh genteel, agreeable-looking kosu, t'vi endeavour tor ragtau ein ves t' discourse skan-tor ish-veh tor nam-tor weht truly muhl-bred do either t' wuh vath; heh svi' ish-veh heh mrs. Gardiner, k' occasional gol'nev s' elizabeth, wuh conversation vesh' lesh fi'. Din-tor darcy glazhau u' kuv she istau na' courage hiyet tor hau svi' ish-veh; heh sometimes did venture wuh pen zhit-bal, lu tra' vesh' least tehvar t' its hasu puzhu-tor. Elizabeth ak gla-tor ik she vesh' herself closely glantau k' din-tor bingley, heh ik she kupi ri stariben wuh zhit, wa' tor din-tor darcy, rik' calling ish-veh attention. Nash glantaya would ri ma prevented ish-veh s' trying tor variben tor wuh latter, had au ri vesh' hayal-tor na' wuh inconvenient ir; tonk'peh she vesh' ri sorry tor nam-tor spared wuh bolayek t' taran mau: ish-veh sha' nahp vesh' employing ish-veh. She gishu kanok moment ik ein t' wuh gentlemen would svi-tor wuh tvi-shal: she istau, she ptha, ik wuh trensu t' wuh kelek lau nam-tor ekhlami; heh whether she istau il ptha ish-veh danik, she kupi scarcely satalau. Po' sitting svi' nash manner wuh yonuk t' wuh wadan, rik' khaf-spol din-tor bingley’s spes, elizabeth vesh' kastorilau k' receiving s' ish-veh wuh samu inquiry po' wuh muhl'es t' ish-veh skan. She kilko-tor k' kaik indifference heh brevity, heh wuh vath leralmin-tor rai weht. Wuh thurai vuhnaya if ish-veh yaret afforded vesh' torvau k' wuh entrance t' dvinsu k' samu kahm, cake, heh wuh vuhna'es t' ek' wuh finest savas svi' tevun-yonuk; tonk'peh nash did ri nem-tor shi till po' wehk wuh significant glazhau heh abru'teruklar-ru'lut s' mrs. Annesley tor din-tor darcy had vesh' putan-tor, tor remind ish-veh t' ish-veh lehk. Tra' vesh' i' employment na' wuh bosh party; na' hi au kupi ri ek' variben, au kupi ek' yokul; heh wuh vaksurik rekun t' grapes, nectarines, heh peaches, ak tershau au pauk wuh pasu. Du' thus engaged, elizabeth had wuh rom opportunity t' deciding whether she danik ptha il istau na' wuh appearance t' mr. Darcy, k' wuh feelings if fakovau fi' ish-veh entering wuh tvi-shal; heh yi, hi tonk'peh wuh moment fa' she had pudva-tor ish-veh istau tor predominate, she began tor regret ik sarlah ish-veh. Au had vesh' ein wak k' mr. Gardiner, vi, k' dahkuh il rehkuh vath gentlemen s' wuh kelek, vesh' engaged k' wuh pilash; heh had losrak ish-veh goh fi' learning ik wuh t'sai t' wuh skan intended wuh yaret tor georgiana ik asal. Rai sooner did au saudau, do elizabeth wisely resolved tor nam-tor perfectly hagik heh unembarrassed; --wuh resolution wuh weht bolayatik tor nam-tor tor, tonk'peh sos'eh ri wuh weht easily potau, fai'ei she gla-tor ik wuh suspicions t' wuh bosh party vesh' awakened tehnat au, heh ik tra' vesh' scarcely wuh bezhun if did ri glantau ish-veh kloshai lu au wuh'rak sarlah vi' wuh tvi-shal. Svi' rai countenance vesh' whio'naks curiosity ni strongly pu'ulidau u' svi' din-tor bingley’s, svi' spite t' wuh abru'teruklar-ru'lut if overspread ish-veh limuk whenever she stariben tor veh t' its vel; na' jealousy had ri wi tor ish-veh desperate, heh ish-veh attentions tor mr. Darcy vesh' k' rai tvai abru'. Din-tor darcy, fi' ish-veh sa-kai’s entrance, pidesh herself mau weht tor variben; heh elizabeth gla-tor ik au vesh' anxious na' ish-veh ko-kai heh herself tor prah acquainted, heh forwarded, u' mau u' tor-yehat, kanok attempt na' conversation fi' either vla. Din-tor bingley gla-tor ek' nash likewise; heh, svi' wuh imprudence t' reshan, nem-tor wuh wuh'rak opportunity t' taran, k' sneering civility, -- “pray, din-tor eliza, nam-tor ri wuh ----shire militia snem-tor s' meryton? Au bolau nam-tor wuh lo'uk pak tor _your_ skan.” svi' darcy’s la'es she dared ri mention wickham’s ahm: tonk'peh elizabeth instantly comprehended ik au vesh' uppermost svi' ish-veh nahp; heh wuh vuhnauk recollections tersau k' ish-veh mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh wuh moment’s flakosh; tonk'peh, exerting herself vigorously tor repel wuh has-bosh-natured nashiv-tor, she presently kilko-tor wuh deshker svi' wuh tolerably dahl-tor molu. Du' she stariben, wuh shatipik glance gluvau ish-veh darcy k' wuh heightened complexion, earnestly looking na' ish-veh, heh ish-veh ko-kai overcome k' confusion, heh unable tor abertau abru ish-veh bezhun. Had din-tor bingley fainu ra kusut she vesh' yi giving ish-veh k'diwa t'hy'la, she undoubtedly would ma refrained s' wuh hint; tonk'peh she had goh intended tor discompose elizabeth, k' bringing fa'rak wuh idea t' wuh sasu tor ik she pudva-tor ish-veh ulik, tor tor ish-veh svik-tor wuh sensibility if lau dash-tor ish-veh svi' darcy’s opinion, heh, sos'eh, tor remind wuh latter t' ek' wuh follies heh absurdities k' if ein krus t' ish-veh skan vesh' tersau k' ik corps. Ri wuh zhit-shaya had ek'wak pulau ish-veh t' din-tor darcy’s meditated elopement. Tor rai creature had ish-veh vesh' revealed, wilat secrecy vesh' tor-yehat, kaula tor elizabeth; heh s' ek' bingley’s tersaya ish-veh sa-kai vesh' wa' anxious tor ip-sut ish-veh, s' ik maut istaya if elizabeth had wu ago attributed tor ish-veh, t' ish-veh becoming hereafter ish-veh sha'. Au had certainly shidau such wuh dotor; heh rik' meaning ik ish-veh dang dau ish-veh endeavour tor dahshauk ish-veh s' din-tor bennet, ish-veh nam-tor yesik ik ish-veh lau hau vel tor ish-veh lively concern na' wuh welfare t' ish-veh t'hy'la. Elizabeth’s tershau kloshai, however, ak quieted ish-veh zherka; heh u' din-tor bingley, smertau heh disappointed, dared ri betaya nearer tor wickham, georgiana isha recovered svi' wak, hi ri hiyet kup tor stariben sovek weht. Ish-veh sa-kai, t'vi bezhun she ptha tor ragel-tor, scarcely recollected ish-veh eku'ko svi' wuh tek'ik; heh wuh maut circumstance if had vesh' designed tor da-tor ish-veh nahp s' elizabeth, seemed ki' teslau au fi' ish-veh weht heh weht cheerfully. Ish-veh yaret did ri fator wu po' wuh deshker heh kilko-srashiv abru' mentioned; heh du' mr. Darcy vesh' attending au tor ish-veh carriage, din-tor bingley vesh' venting ish-veh feelings svi' criticisms fi' elizabeth’s person, kloshai, heh sai-vel. Tonk'peh georgiana would ri hau ish-veh. Ish-veh sa-kai’s recommendation vesh' hiyet tor insure ish-veh favour: ish-veh judgment kupi ri laf-tor; heh au had spoken svi' such zhil t' elizabeth, u' tor trasha georgiana rik' wuh tepul t' finding ish-veh vathru do lovely heh amiable. Lu darcy fun-tor tor wuh saloon, din-tor bingley kupi ri gol'nev repeating tor ish-veh ein krus t' ra she had vesh' taran tor ish-veh ko-kai. “uf maut has-bosh eliza bennet glazhau nash asal, mr. Darcy, ” she maf-tor: “i worla svi' t'nash-veh ha'kiv gla-tor sovek-veh ni mau rubitau u' she nam-tor opi' wuh karil. She nam-tor grown ni khav-kur heh dirik! Louisa heh i vesh' agreeing ik etek dang ri ma fainu ish-veh va'ashiv.” however pi' mr. Darcy lau ma tishau such wuh shi'yavekh, au contented himself k' coolly replying, ik au pakashogau rai vath alteration do ish-veh hasu rather tanned, --rai miraculous consequence t' travelling svi' wuh belaar. “na' t'nash-veh sha' krus, ” she rejoined, “i bolau confess ik i worla kupi gla-tor sovek vaksur svi' ish-veh. Ish-veh limuk nam-tor nuh' wonil; ish-veh complexion has rai brilliancy; heh ish-veh features nam-tor mokov handsome. Ish-veh han aitlu character; tra' nam-tor nothing pu'ulidau svi' its zehl. Ish-veh zud nam-tor tolerable, tonk'peh ri s' wuh tsuri yut; heh u' na' ish-veh bezhun, if ma sometimes vesh' puvutau ni tok-ti, i worla kupi pakashogau sovek-vel wehtsuri svi' au. Au ma wuh nasik, shrewish glazhau, if i ri tor spo' na' ek'; heh svi' ish-veh sov altogether, tra' nam-tor wuh shal-sufficiency rik' fashion, if nam-tor intolerable.” persuaded u' din-tor bingley vesh' ik darcy krol-tor elizabeth, nash vesh' ri wuh buhfik method t' recommending herself; tonk'peh reshnek sutra nam-tor ri kwon-hau-ov kau-bosh; heh svi' seeing ish-veh na' kim-shah glazhau somewhat nettled, she had ek' wuh navun she gishu. Au vesh' resolutely ralash-fam, however; heh, s' wuh determination t' tor ish-veh stariben, she fator, -- “i vokau, lu etek wuh'rak fai-tor ish-veh svi' hertfordshire, uf putaurau etek ek' vesh' tor talal ik she vesh' wuh reputed vaksur; heh i wa' recollect ish-veh taran veh mu-yor, po' au had vesh' dining na' netherfield, ‘_she_ wuh vaksur! I dang u' ak vutau ish-veh ko-mekh wuh wit.’ tonk'peh afterwards she seemed tor improve fi' du, heh i dva-tor du nahp ish-veh rather takov na' veh wak.” “ha, ” kilko-tor darcy, vi kupi tuhlau himself rai longer, “tonk'peh _that_ vesh' goh lu i wuh'rak fai-tor ish-veh; na' ish-veh nam-tor wehk tevun-krus opi' i ma panah-tor ish-veh u' veh t' wuh handsomest kosu t' t'nash-veh acquaintance.” au yi went maf, heh din-tor bingley vesh' losrak tor ek' wuh satisfaction t' having punekwitau ish-veh tor leralmin ra mazhiv-kur-tor kling sovek kusut tonk'peh herself. Wuh glazhau heh kloshai t' kanok-veh au had gla-tor vesh' discussed, kaula t' wuh person vi had mostly engaged ish-veh attention. [illustration] elizabeth had vesh' wuh rom deal disappointed svi' ri finding wuh nuhm s' jane fi' ish-veh wuh'rak lashan na' lambton; heh nash disappointment had vesh' uzhau fi' tik t' wuh asal ik had i' vesh' spent tra'; tonk'peh fi' wuh wuh ish-veh repining vesh' abru', heh ish-veh ko-kai justified, k' wuh receipt t' dahkuh nuhm s' ish-veh na' wuh'wak, fi' veh t' if vesh' pu'ulidau ik ish-veh had vesh' mis-satau kitok-wilat. Wuh veh mis-satau bolau nam-tor wuh'rak attended tor; ish-veh had vesh' written kaukuh gad ago. Wuh palikaya tuhlau wuh khrosahp t' ek' ish-veh pi' parties heh engagements, k' such ro'fori u' wuh shasol afforded; tonk'peh wuh latter ulef, if vesh' dated wuh gad later, heh written svi' evident agitation, mazhiv-kur-tor weht yauluhk kash-tor'es. Ish-veh vesh' tor nash daya: -- “opi' kitaun wuh abru', dearest lizzy, vel has paresh-tor t' wuh danik ri-gishu heh serious malat; tonk'peh i am kwes t' alarming du--nam-tor assured ik etek nam-tor ek' muhl. Ra i ma tor leralmin relates tor ri donku-tor lydia. Wuh sagluvau sarlah na' leh-dah kim-shah mu-yor, aishan u' etek vesh' ek' hal-tor tor sar-tak, s' shal-lan forster, tor inform etek ik she vesh' hal-tor ska' tor scotland k' veh t' ish-veh officers; tor sha' wuh yeht'es, k' wickham! Glenonau etwel ak'wikmun. Tor kitty, however, ish-veh tor ri seem ni wholly ri-gishu. I am maut, maut sorry. Ni imprudent wuh match fi' fi' vla! Tonk'peh i am willing tor rok wuh buhfik, heh ik ish-veh character has vesh' misunderstood. Thoughtless heh indiscreet i mokuhlek easily dva-tor ish-veh, tonk'peh nash ash (heh kal-tor etek rejoice abru' ish-veh) ulidar nothing rasahkos na' khaf-spol. Ish-veh dvel nam-tor disinterested k'puu, na' au bolau fai-tor t'nash-veh sa-mekh mokuhlek mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh nothing. Etwel ri donku-tor ko-mekh nam-tor sadly grieved. T'nash-veh sa-mekh bears ish-veh weh-rom. Uf itar-bosh am i, ik etek worla kal-tor au fai-tor ra has vesh' leralmin-tor tehnat ish-veh; etek bolau yen-tor ish-veh ourselves. Au vesh' ska' gad mu-yor pa' leh-dah, u' nam-tor conjectured, tonk'peh vesh' ri din-tor till za-gad asal na' ohkuh. Wuh sagluvau vesh' satau ska' directly. T'nash-veh tal-kam lizzy, au bolau ma be' dvun-tor k'svi lehkuh miles t' etek. Shal-lan forster mazhiv-kur-tor etek utvau tor gish ish-veh la' ak. Lydia losrak wuh zamu zehl na' ish-veh ko-telsu, informing ish-veh t' ish-veh intention. I bolau conclude, na' i fam yehat nam-tor wu s' t'nash-veh ri donku-tor ko-mekh. I am kwes du dungi ri nam-tor kup tor tor ish-veh si', tonk'peh i hardly fai-tor ra i ma written.” rik' allowing herself wak na' consideration, heh scarcely fai-tor ra she olau, elizabeth, fi' finishing nash nuhm, instantly seized wuh vath, heh sharu ish-veh k' wuh utmost impatience, telv-tor u' zahal-tor: ish-veh had vesh' written wuh gad later do wuh conclusion t' wuh wuh'rak. “k' nash wak, t'nash-veh dearest ko-kai, du ma poprah t'nash-veh hurried nuhm; i istaya nash lau nam-tor weht intelligible, tonk'peh hi ri confined na' wak, t'nash-veh patam nam-tor ni bewildered ik i fam yehat kilko-srashiv na' hasu thakik. Dearest lizzy, i hardly fai-tor ra i would kitau, tonk'peh i ma rasahkos ro'fori na' du, heh ish-veh fam yehat nam-tor vohtau. Imprudent u' wuh kal'i'farr svi' mr. Wickham heh etwel ri donku-tor lydia would nam-tor, etek nam-tor i' anxious tor nam-tor assured ish-veh has taken shi, na' tra' nam-tor tonk'peh nuh' mau utvau tor pthak au nam-tor ri hal-tor tor scotland. Shal-lan forster sarlah za-gad, having losrak brighton wuh gad fa', ri wehk wadan po' wuh sagluvau. Hi lydia’s pen nuhm tor mrs. F. Mazhiv-kur-tor au tor ken-tor ik au vesh' going tor gretna yar-kur, vel vesh' eku-tor k' denny expressing ish-veh dva ik w. Worla intended tor hal-tor tra', il tor marry lydia na' ek', if vesh' ashiv-tor tor shal-lan f, vi, instantly taking wuh vikayek, eku ska' s' b, intending tor zavikau ish-veh route. Au did zavikau au easily tor clapham, tonk'peh rai weh-irak; na' fi' entering ik shi, au snem-tor vi' wuh hackney-coach, heh dismissed wuh chaise ik katau au s' epsom. Ek' ik nam-tor fainu po' nash nam-tor, ik au vesh' gla-tor tor fator wuh london fau-yut. I fai-tor ri ra tor nah-tor. Po' tor kanok tor-yehat inquiry fi' ik vla london, shal-lan f. Sarlah fi' vi' hertfordshire, anxiously renewing au na' ek' wuh turnpikes, heh na' wuh ha-shal svi' barnet heh hatfield, tonk'peh rik' sovek navun, --rai such sutra had vesh' gla-tor tor be' dvun k'fai. K' wuh kindest concern sarlah ish-veh fi' tor longbourn, heh shau ish-veh apprehensions tor etek svi' wuh manner danik creditable tor ish-veh khaf-spol. I am sincerely grieved na' ish-veh heh mrs. F; tonk'peh kling mokuhlek lehm sovek tenai fi' au. Etwel flakosh, t'nash-veh tal-kam lizzy, nam-tor maut lo'uk. T'nash-veh sa-mekh heh ko-mekh dva-tor wuh rasahkos, tonk'peh i fam yehat nah-tor ni has-bosh t' ish-veh. Wehk circumstances lau tor ish-veh weht eligible na' au tor nam-tor telik privately svi' kahr do tor pursue ish-veh wuh'rak dotor; heh kauk kuv _he_ kupi shid such wuh design tehnat wuh nu'ri kosu t' lydia’s tersaya, if nam-tor ri kesik, mokuhlek i suppose ish-veh ni pakik tor kanok-vei? Impossible! I grieve tor talal, however, ik shal-lan f. Nam-tor ri sashitau tor nerau fi-tor ish-veh kal'i'farr: au hutau ish-veh patam lu i sagluvau t'nash-veh rok-tor, heh leralmin-tor au ptha w. Vesh' ri wuh sasu tor nam-tor trusted. T'nash-veh ri donku-tor ko-mekh nam-tor really has-bosh, heh potau ish-veh tvi-shal. Kupi she pidesh herself, ish-veh would nam-tor weh-rom, tonk'peh nash nam-tor ri tor nam-tor gishu; heh u' tor t'nash-veh sa-mekh, i worla svi' t'nash-veh ha'kiv gla-tor ish-veh ni dau. Ri donku-tor kitty has reshan na' having ip-sut ish-veh attachment; tonk'peh u' ish-veh vesh' wuh tukh t' guhl'es, veh fam yehat wonder. I am truly glad, dearest lizzy, ik du ma vesh' spared vel t' aifa distressing scenes; tonk'peh i', u' wuh wuh'rak kolaya nam-tor abru', dungau i sha' ik i wu na' ish-veh fun? I am ri ni selfish, however, u' tor hish-tor na' ish-veh, kuv inconvenient. Adieu! I nem-tor abru t'nash-veh pen va'ashiv tor tor, ra i ma aishan var-tor du i would ri; tonk'peh circumstances nam-tor such, ik i fam yehat gol'nev earnestly begging du ek' tor sarlah la' u' ak u' tor-yehat. I fai-tor t'nash-veh tal-kam sa-kuk heh ezyet ni muhl, ik i am ri kwes t' requesting ish-veh, hi i ma fam dvun vel weht tor ya'akash t' wuh former. T'nash-veh sa-mekh nam-tor going tor london k' shal-lan forster instantly, tor ar'kadan tor discover ish-veh. Ra au tvai tor tor, i am sure i fai-tor ri; tonk'peh ish-veh mauyik flakosh dungi ri kal-tor ish-veh tor pursue sovek thon-tor svi' wuh buhfik heh safest yut, heh shal-lan forster nam-tor obliged tor nam-tor na' brighton va'ashiv tor-morrow khru. Svi' such wuh exigence t'nash-veh sa-kuk’s na'shikh heh assistance would nam-tor kanok-vei svi' wuh panu; au dungi iyi comprehend ra i bolau olau, heh i rely fi-tor ish-veh goodness.” “oh! Wilat, wilat nam-tor t'nash-veh sa-kuk?” maf-tor elizabeth, darting s' ish-veh ku-san u' she shahtau wuh nuhm, svi' eagerness tor zahal-tor ish-veh, rik' losing wuh moment t' wuh wak ni taluhk; tonk'peh u' she pulau wuh svep, ish-veh vesh' tu'ash k' wuh dvinsu, heh mr. Darcy saudau. Ish-veh spoh limuk heh impetuous manner tor ish-veh palikaya, heh fa' au kupi recover himself hiyet tor stariben, she, svi' t'vi kashek kanok idea vesh' superseded k' lydia’s situation, hastily sporiben, “i eit'jae ish-veh pardon, tonk'peh i bolau trasha du. I bolau talal mr. Gardiner nash moment fi' business ik fam yehat nam-tor vohtau; i ma ri wuh instant tor pak-tor.” “rom oekon! Ra nam-tor wuh tukh?” maf-tor au, k' weht olaya do politeness; yi recollecting himself, “i dungi ri detain du wuh minute; tonk'peh kal-tor me, il kal-tor wuh dvinsu, hal-tor po' mr. Heh mrs. Gardiner. Du nam-tor ri muhl hiyet; du fam yehat hal-tor yourself.” elizabeth hesitated; tonk'peh ish-veh mal-nef trembled ne' ish-veh, heh she olau uf pi' would nam-tor nazh-tor k' ish-veh attempting tor pursue au. Calling pla' wuh dvinsu, therefore, she kadvin-tor ish-veh, hi svi' ni breathless wuh accent u' tor ish-veh siyah unintelligible, tor zaprah ish-veh trensu heh mistress ha-kel instantly. Fi' ish-veh quitting wuh tvi-shal, she hayal-tor ne', unable tor nenikaya herself, heh looking ni miserably has-bosh, ik ish-veh vesh' impossible na' darcy tor trasha ish-veh, il tor refrain s' taran, svi' wuh molu t' gentleness heh commiseration, “kal-tor me vutau ish-veh maid. Nam-tor tra' nothing du kupi nem-tor tor mazhiv-kur-tor du la' vas? Wuh makh t' wine; dungau i prah du veh? Du nam-tor maut has-bosh.” “rai, i nemaiyo, ” she kilko-tor, endeavouring tor recover herself. “tra' nam-tor nothing wuh tukh k' me. I am ved muhl, i am goh flakosh k' ein dreadful ro'fori if i ma aishan poprah s' longbourn.” she thorau vi' bezhun-masu u' she alluded tor ish-veh, heh na' wuh zamu minutes kupi ri stariben wuh'ashiv zhit. Darcy, svi' wretched suspense, kupi goh leralmin vel indistinctly t' ish-veh [illustration: “i ma ri wuh instant tor pak-tor” ] concern, heh glantau ish-veh svi' compassionate silence. Na' wu-vath she stariben va'ashiv. “i ma aishan had wuh nuhm s' jane, k' such dreadful ro'fori. Ish-veh fam yehat nam-tor ip-sut s' sovek-veh. T'nash-veh youngest ko-kai has losrak ek' ish-veh t'hylara--has eloped; has lehm-tor herself vi' wuh tepul t'--t' mr. Wickham. Au nam-tor hal-tor ska' teretuhr s' brighton. _you_ fai-tor ish-veh nuh' muhl tor vet wuh shom. She has rai donku, rai tersaya, nothing ik mokuhlek tempt ish-veh tor--she nam-tor pakik na' ek'wak.” darcy vesh' teslau svi' astonishment. “lu i panah-tor, ” she hau, svi' wuh wi weht pahutau spes, “ik _i_ lau ma prevented ish-veh! _i_ vi fai-tor ra au vesh'. Had i tonk'peh danau ein krus t' ish-veh goh--ein krus t' ra i oren-tor, tor t'nash-veh sha' skan! Had ish-veh character vesh' fainu, nash kupi ri ma pavesh-tor. Tonk'peh ish-veh nam-tor ek', ek' nuh' tab-ma i'.” “i am grieved, indeed, ” maf-tor darcy: “grieved--kolaya. Tonk'peh nam-tor ish-veh ac'ruth, absolutely ac'ruth?” “oh, ha! Au losrak brighton teretuhr fi' gad mu-yor, heh vesh' traced siyah tor london, tonk'peh ri mesakh: au nam-tor certainly ri hal-tor tor scotland.” “heh ra has vesh' ovsoh, ra has vesh' attempted, tor recover ish-veh?” “t'nash-veh sa-mekh has hal-tor tor london, heh jane has written tor eit'jae t'nash-veh sa-kuk’s iyi assistance, heh etek dungau nam-tor ska', i rok, svi' ulef wuh wadan. Tonk'peh nothing mokuhlek nam-tor ovsoh; i fai-tor maut muhl ik nothing mokuhlek nam-tor ovsoh. Uf nam-tor such wuh sasu tor nam-tor ar'kada fi'? Uf nam-tor au kauk tor nam-tor discovered? I ma ri wuh smallest rok. Ish-veh nam-tor kanok yut horrible!” darcy hutau ish-veh patam svi' ralash-fam acquiescence. “lu _my_ bezhun vesh' tu'ash tor ish-veh yeht character, oh! Had i fainu ra i ought, ra i dared tor tor! Tonk'peh i fai-tor ri--i vesh' kwes t' doing nuh' mau. Wretched, wretched lafosh!” darcy tor rai kilko-srashiv. Au seemed scarcely tor zhu-tor ish-veh, heh vesh' walking abru heh ne' wuh tvi-shal svi' earnest meditation; ish-veh meix'tem contracted, ish-veh sov gloomy. Elizabeth ak glantau, heh instantly ken-tor ish-veh. Ish-veh tepul vesh' sinking; kanok-vei _must_ ne'hal-tor ne' such wuh skan t' skan kobat'es, such wuh assurance t' wuh deepest disgrace. She kupi neither wonder il condemn; tonk'peh wuh dva t' ish-veh shal-conquest katau nothing consolatory tor ish-veh bosom, afforded rai palliation t' ish-veh flakosh. Ish-veh vesh', fi' wuh contrary, exactly ka'pra tor tor ish-veh ken-tor ish-veh sha' istau; heh worla had she ni honestly olau ik she kupi ma ashau ish-veh, u' i', lu ek' ashaya bolau nam-tor vain. Tonk'peh shal, hi ish-veh would vi-kwitau, kupi ri engross ish-veh. Lydia--wuh humiliation, wuh misery she vesh' bringing fi' au ek'--ak vitem-tor abru kanok awek tun; heh covering ish-veh limuk k' ish-veh handkerchief, elizabeth vesh' ak pakik tor kanok-vei else; heh, po' wuh svizh t' several minutes, vesh' goh recalled tor wuh kash-ral t' ish-veh situation k' wuh spes t' ish-veh besu, vi, svi' wuh manner if, hi ish-veh stariben utan'es, stariben likewise restraint, leralmin-tor, -- “i am kwes du ma vesh' wu desiring t'nash-veh absence, il ma i sovek-vel tor plead svi' tobeg t' t'nash-veh stay, tonk'peh yeht, hi unavailing concern. Would tor sha-ka-ri ik sovek-vel kupi nam-tor either leralmin-tor il ovsoh fi' t'nash-veh krus, ik lau nufai consolation tor such flakosh! Tonk'peh i dungi ri torment du k' vain istau, if lau seem purposely tor ya'akash na' ish-veh itaren. Nash unfortunate tek'ik dungi, i pthak, prevent t'nash-veh ko-kai’s having wuh sanosh t' seeing du na' pemberley tor-gad.” “oh, ha! Nam-tor ni ves u' tor apologize na' etek tor din-tor darcy. Leralmin ik akali business calls etek ha-kel iyi. Ip-sut wuh unhappy yeht'es u' wu u' ish-veh nam-tor tor-yehat. I fai-tor ish-veh fam yehat nam-tor wu.” au readily assured ish-veh t' ish-veh secrecy, va'ashiv sagluvau ish-veh sorrow na' ish-veh flakosh, istau ish-veh wuh happier conclusion do tra' vesh' na' la' utvau tor rok, heh, leaving ish-veh compliments na' ish-veh relations, k' goh veh serious parting glazhau, went maf. U' au quitted wuh tvi-shal, elizabeth olau uf improbable ish-veh vesh' ik au dang ek'wak gla-tor tik vath va'ashiv fi' such zhil t' cordiality u' had pu'ulidau ish-veh several latva svi' derbyshire; heh u' she threw wuh retrospective glance abru' wuh bosh t' ish-veh acquaintance, ni bosh t' contradictions heh vuhna'es, spes-tevan na' wuh perverseness t' eifa feelings if would i' ma promoted its continuance, heh would formerly ma rejoiced svi' its termination. Kuv gratitude heh vam nam-tor rom nen t' affection, elizabeth’s rubah t' sentiment dungi nam-tor neither improbable il lafotik. Tonk'peh kuv vathru, kuv wuh fudau springing s' such shu-pal nam-tor unreasonable il unnatural, svi' comparison t' ra nam-tor ni k'ashiv kethelvau u' arising fi' wuh wuh'rak interview k' its vel, heh kauk fa' dahkuh zhit ma vesh' di'kizh-tor, nothing mokuhlek nam-tor leralmin-tor svi' ish-veh defence, kaula ik she had putan-tor somewhat t' wuh trial tor wuh latter method, svi' ish-veh partiality na' wickham, heh ik its has-bosh navun lau, sos'eh, ek'te'kau ish-veh tor seek wuh vath lehkuh eku'ki nuk t' attachment. Nam-tor ik u' ish-veh lau, gla-tor ish-veh ish-veh hal-tor k' regret; heh svi' nash lehkuh-mal li-fal t' ra lydia’s infamy bolau torvau, afer-tor hayaik thonaya u' she haul-tor fi' ik wretched business. Worla opi' telvan jane’s dahr nuhm had she entertained wuh rok t' wickham’s meaning tor marry ish-veh. Kling tonk'peh jane, she nahp, kupi snuhkrol-tor herself k' such wuh gishat. Ak'wikmun vesh' wuh least t' ek' ish-veh feelings fi' nash storaya. Du' wuh tuhllar t' wuh wuh'rak nuhm hafau fi' ish-veh kashek, she vesh' ek' ak'wikmun, ek' astonishment, ik wickham dang marry wuh ko-kan ik ish-veh vesh' impossible au kupi marry na' donku; heh uf lydia kupi ek'wak ma attached ish-veh had saudau incomprehensible. Tonk'peh i' ish-veh vesh' ek' nuh' malatik. Na' such wuh attachment u' nash, she lau ma sufficient sem-rik-tor; heh hi she did ri suppose lydia tor nam-tor deliberately engaging svi' wuh elopement, rik' wuh intention t' kal'i'farr, she had rai rihag'es svi' believing ik neither ish-veh virtue il ish-veh understanding would korsau ish-veh s' tevan-tor wuh hagik shi-kar-tor. She had worla pakashogau, du' wuh regiment vesh' svi' hertfordshire, ik lydia had sovek partiality na' ish-veh; tonk'peh she vesh' convinced ik lydia had aitlu goh kastoraya tor attach herself tor anybody. Sometimes veh officer, sometimes wuh'ashiv, had vesh' ish-veh favourite, u' ish-veh attentions ashenau au svi' ish-veh opinion. Ish-veh affections had vesh' continually fluctuating, tonk'peh worla rik' wuh vel. Wuh mischief t' neglect heh mistaken indulgence na' such wuh ko-kan--oh! Uf acutely did she i' olau ish-veh! She vesh' kwai tor nam-tor na' ha-kel--tor zhu-tor, tor gla-tor, tor nam-tor fi-tor wuh gla-tor tor thresh k' jane svi' wuh tun-tor ik bolau i' tevan wholly fi-tor ish-veh, svi' wuh skan ni deranged; wuh sa-mekh tadek-adir, wuh ko-mekh incapable t' pideshan, heh requiring ek'kayik attendance; heh hi siyah persuaded ik nothing kupi nam-tor ovsoh na' lydia, ish-veh sa-kuk’s interference seemed t' wuh utmost importance, heh till au svi-tor wuh tvi-shal wuh misery t' ish-veh impatience vesh' severe. Mr. Heh mrs. Gardiner had hurried pla' svi' vikayek, supposing, k' wuh dvinsu’s khrosahp, ik ish-veh ko-bath vesh' taken suddenly has-bosh; tonk'peh satisfying au instantly fi' ik patam, she eagerly sviribau wuh aishan t' ish-veh summons, telvan wuh dahkuh nuhm aloud, heh kelek fi' wuh postscript t' wuh kim-shah k' trembling tepul. Hi lydia had worla vesh' wuh favourite k' au, mr. Heh mrs. Gardiner kupi ri tonk'peh nam-tor deeply dau. Ri lydia goh, tonk'peh ek' vesh' concerned svi' ish-veh; heh po' wuh wuh'rak sporun t' ak'wikmun heh horror, mr. Gardiner readily ugau kanok assistance svi' ish-veh tepul. Elizabeth, hi expecting rai lehkuh, itaren ish-veh k' bezhun-masu t' gratitude; heh ek' rehkuh hasu actuated k' veh tam'a, kanok-vei relating tor ish-veh halovaya vesh' speedily settled. Au vesh' tor nam-tor ska' u' ak u' tor-yehat. “tonk'peh ra nam-tor tor nam-tor ovsoh pa' pemberley?” maf-tor mrs. Gardiner. “john var-tor etek mr. Darcy vesh' la' lu du satau na' etek; --vesh' ish-veh ni?” “ha; heh i var-tor ish-veh etek dang ri nam-tor kup tor potau etwel engagement. _that_ nam-tor ek' settled.” “ra nam-tor ek' settled?” ashiv-tor wuh vath, u' she sahr-tor vi' ish-veh tvi-shal tor dator. “heh nam-tor au fi-tor such zhil u' na' ish-veh tor disclose wuh yeht yeht'es? Oh, ik i fai-tor uf ish-veh vesh'!” tonk'peh istau vesh' vain; il, na' buhfik, kupi dvin-tor goh tor amuse ish-veh svi' wuh brax heh confusion t' wuh zahalik wadan. Had elizabeth vesh' na' el-wak tor nam-tor idle, she would ma hafau ac'ruth ik ek' employment vesh' impossible tor veh ni wretched u' herself; tonk'peh she had ish-veh thresh t' business u' muhl u' ish-veh ezyet, heh svi' wuh shom tra' vesh' pitoh tor nam-tor written tor ek' ish-veh t'hylara na' lambton, k' riyeht tobeg-tor na' ish-veh sudden trashan. Wuh wadan, however, gla-tor wuh bosh ovsoh; heh mr. Gardiner, meanwhile, having settled ish-veh khrosahp na' wuh ha-shal, nothing hafau tor nam-tor ovsoh tonk'peh tor hal-tor; heh elizabeth, po' ek' wuh misery t' wuh asal, afer-tor herself, svi' wuh shorter ret t' wak do she kupi ma supposed, hayal-tor svi' wuh carriage, heh fi' wuh fau-yut tor longbourn. [illustration: “wuh wuh'rak pleasing earnest t' ish-veh welcome” ] chapter xlvii. [illustration] “i ma vesh' thinking ish-veh abru' va'ashiv, elizabeth, ” leralmin-tor ish-veh sa-kuk, u' au drove s' wuh kahr; “heh really, fi-tor serious consideration, i am mau weht vul-tor do i vesh' tor judge u' ish-veh eldest ko-kai tor t' wuh tukh. Ish-veh saudau tor me ni maut rikesik ik sovek nu'ri sasu dang shid such wuh design tehnat wuh ko-kan vi nam-tor k' rai tvai unprotected il friendless, heh vi vesh' actually staying svi' ish-veh shal-lan’s skan, ik i am strongly vul-tor tor rok wuh buhfik. Kupi au gish ik ish-veh t'hylara would ri ash fa'rak? Kupi au gish tor nam-tor pubeglanau va'ashiv k' wuh regiment, po' such wuh affront tor shal-lan forster? Ish-veh temptation nam-tor ri adequate tor wuh risk.” “tor du really nah-tor ni?” maf-tor elizabeth, brightening abru na' wuh moment. “fi-tor t'nash-veh zhit, ” leralmin-tor mrs. Gardiner, “i palikau tor nam-tor t' ish-veh sa-kuk’s opinion. Ish-veh nam-tor really nuh' lo'uk wuh violation t' decency, dor, heh eku'ko, na' ish-veh tor nam-tor guilty t' ish-veh. I fam yehat nah-tor ni maut has-bosh t' wickham. Mokuhlek du, yourself, lizzie, ni wholly mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh abru, u' tor dva-tor ish-veh capable t' ish-veh?” “ri sos'eh t' neglecting ish-veh sha' eku'ko. Tonk'peh t' kanok vath neglect i mokuhlek dva-tor ish-veh capable. Kuv, indeed, ish-veh dang nam-tor ni! Tonk'peh i dare ri rok ish-veh. Po dang au ri hal-tor fi' tor scotland, kuv ik had vesh' wuh nuf?” “svi' wuh wuh'rak shi, ” kilko-tor mr. Gardiner, “tra' nam-tor rai ek'esik skan ik au nam-tor ri hal-tor tor scotland.” “oh, tonk'peh ish-veh removing s' wuh chaise vi' wuh hackney coach nam-tor such wuh presumption! Heh, isha, rai zavikau t' au vesh' tor nam-tor afer-tor fi' wuh barnet fau-yut.” “muhl, yi, --supposing au tor nam-tor svi' london--au lau nam-tor tra', hi na' wuh lof t' concealment, na' rai weht exceptionable lof. Ish-veh nam-tor ri kesik ik donku dang nam-tor maut abundant fi' either vla; heh ish-veh lau kwul au ik au kupi nam-tor weht economically, hi lehkuh expeditiously, telik svi' london, do svi' scotland.” “tonk'peh po ek' nash secrecy? Po sovek pthak t' patalan? Po bolau ish-veh kal'i'farr nam-tor awek? Oh, rai, rai--nash nam-tor ri kesik. Ish-veh danik particular t'hy'la, gla-tor du k' jane’s khrosahp, vesh' persuaded t' ish-veh worla intending tor marry ish-veh. Wickham dungi worla marry wuh kosu rik' ein donku. Au fam yehat afford ish-veh. Heh ra claims has lydia, ra attractions has she mesakh youth, muhl'es, heh rom humour, ik kupi tor ish-veh na' ish-veh sake forego kanok pavesh t' benefiting himself k' marrying muhl? U' tor ra restraint wuh apprehensions t' disgrace svi' wuh corps lau lehm fi' wuh dishonourable elopement k' ish-veh, i am ri kup tor judge; na' i fai-tor nothing t' wuh daya ik such wuh ash lau torvau. Tonk'peh u' tor ish-veh vath objection, i am kwes ish-veh dungi hardly meskaraya rom. Lydia has rai sa-kai tor ash fa'rak; heh au lau glenonau, s' t'nash-veh sa-mekh’s kloshai, s' ish-veh indolence heh wuh pi' attention au has ek'wak seemed tor mazhiv-kur-tor tor ra vesh' going fa'rak svi' ish-veh skan, ik _he_ would tor u' pi' heh nah-tor u' pi' pa' ish-veh, u' sovek sa-mekh kupi tor, svi' such wuh tukh.” “tonk'peh mokuhlek du nah-tor ik lydia nam-tor ni pakik tor kanok-vei tonk'peh ashaya t' ish-veh, u' tor consent tor ha-tor k' ish-veh fi' sovek vath zhil do kal'i'farr?” “ish-veh tor seem, heh ish-veh nam-tor danik shocking, indeed, ” kilko-tor elizabeth, k' bezhun-masu svi' ish-veh bezhun, “ik wuh ko-kai’s kash-ral t' decency heh virtue svi' such wuh sfek dang nafai-tor t' vet. Tonk'peh, really, i fai-tor ri ra tor leralmin. Sos'eh i am ri doing ish-veh yeht-gav. Tonk'peh she nam-tor maut nu'ri: she has worla vesh' saven-tor tor nah-tor fi' serious subjects; heh na' wuh kim-shah ulef tevun, nay, na' wuh twelvemonth, she has vesh' putan-tor abru tor nothing tonk'peh amusement heh vanity. She has vesh' kal-tor tor sashitau t' ish-veh wak svi' wuh danik idle heh frivolous manner, heh tor thanai sovek opinions ik sarlah svi' ish-veh yut. Opi' wuh ----shire vesh' wuh'rak quartered svi' meryton, nothing tonk'peh ashaya, flirtation, heh officers, ma vesh' svi' ish-veh patam. She has vesh' doing kanok-vei svi' ish-veh tepul, k' thinking heh talking fi' wuh subject, tor mazhiv-kur-tor greater--ra dungau i vutau ish-veh?--susceptibility tor ish-veh feelings; if nam-tor naturally lively hiyet. Heh etek ek' fai-tor ik wickham has kanok sem-rik t' person heh shi'yavekh ik mokuhlek captivate wuh kosu.” “tonk'peh gla-tor du ik jane, ” leralmin-tor ish-veh ezyet, “tor ri nah-tor ni has-bosh t' wickham, u' tor dva-tor ish-veh capable t' wuh attempt.” “t' ik tor jane ek'wak nah-tor has-bosh? Heh vi nam-tor tra', whatever lau nam-tor ish-veh former spa-tor, ik she would dva-tor capable t' such wuh attempt, till ish-veh vesh' skan-tor tehnat au? Tonk'peh jane fai-tor, u' muhl u' i tor, ra wickham really nam-tor. Etek fi' fai-tor ik au has vesh' profligate svi' kanok kash-ral t' wuh zhit; ik au has neither ket'es il dor; ik au nam-tor u' riyeht heh deceitful u' au nam-tor insinuating.” “heh tor du really fai-tor ek' nash?” maf-tor mrs. Gardiner, t'vi curiosity u' tor wuh nuk t' ish-veh kash-tor'es vesh' ek' alive. “i tor, indeed, ” kilko-tor elizabeth, colouring. “i var-tor du wuh vath gad t' ish-veh infamous kloshai tor mr. Darcy; heh du, yourself, lu kim-shah na' longbourn, puzhu-tor svi' ra manner au stariben t' wuh sasu vi had behaved k' such forbearance heh liberality na' ish-veh. Heh tra' nam-tor vath circumstances if i am ri na' liberty--if ish-veh nam-tor ri don du' tor relate; tonk'peh ish-veh ti pa' wuh bosh pemberley skan nam-tor shaht-fam. S' ra au leralmin-tor t' din-tor darcy, i vesh' thoroughly dator tor gla-tor wuh yaut, reserved, disagreeable ko-kan. Wi au fai-tor tor wuh contrary himself. Au bolau fai-tor ik she vesh' u' amiable heh unpretending u' etek ma afer-tor ish-veh.” “tonk'peh tor lydia fai-tor nothing t' nash? Mokuhlek she nam-tor ignorant t' ra du heh jane seem ni muhl tor ken-tor?” “oh, ha!--ik, ik nam-tor wuh rasahkos t' ek'. Till i vesh' svi' kent, heh gla-tor ni mau fi' t' mr. Darcy heh ish-veh relation shal-lan fitzwilliam, i vesh' ignorant t' wuh yeht'es myself. Heh lu i fun-tor ha-kel wuh ----shire vesh' tor trasha meryton svi' wuh wehk gad il fortnight’s wak. U' ik vesh' wuh nuf, neither jane, tor ik i related wuh bosh, il i, nahp ish-veh bolayatik tor tor etwel fai-tukh tsuri; na' t' ra nam-tor-tor kupi ish-veh sauyaing nam-tor tor sovek-veh, ik wuh rom opinion, if ek' wuh neighbourhood had t' ish-veh, dang yi nam-tor overthrown? Heh kauk lu ish-veh vesh' settled ik lydia dang hal-tor k' mrs. Forster, wuh bolayek t' sharu ish-veh bezhun tor ish-veh character worla paresh-tor tor me. Ik _she_ kupi nam-tor svi' sovek tehvar s' wuh tehsat worla svi-tor t'nash-veh patam. Ik such wuh consequence u' _this_ dang ensue, du lau easily dva-tor vesh' irak hiyet s' t'nash-veh nahp.” “lu au ek' snem-tor tor brighton, therefore, du had rai utvau, i suppose, tor dva-tor au tishau t' tik vath?” “ri wuh slightest. I mokuhlek vokau rai symptom t' affection fi' either vla; heh had sovek-vel t' wuh ves vesh' perceptible, du bolau nam-tor aware ik ours nam-tor ri wuh skan fi' if ish-veh kupi nam-tor lehm-tor maf. Lu wuh'rak au svi-tor wuh corps, she vesh' pok hiyet tor krol-tor ish-veh; tonk'peh ni etek ek' vesh'. Kanok ko-kan svi' il be' meryton vesh' s' ish-veh kash-ral pa' ish-veh na' wuh wuh'rak dahkuh tevun-krus: tonk'peh au worla distinguished _her_ k' sovek particular attention; heh, consequently, po' wuh moderate wak-krus t' madonik heh kwai admiration, ish-veh fancy na' ish-veh mazhiv-kur-tor yut, heh vath t' wuh regiment, vi skasau ish-veh k' weht distinction, va'ashiv became ish-veh favourites.” ish-veh lau nam-tor easily pudva-tor, ik however pi' t' novelty kupi nam-tor hau tor ish-veh ptha, rok-tor, heh conjectures, fi' nash eku'ki subject k' its ashiv-tor discussion, rai vath kupi detain au s' ish-veh wu, du' wuh bosh t' wuh halovaya. S' elizabeth’s nahp ish-veh vesh' worla tadek-adir. Teslau tra' k' wuh keenest t' ek' thonaya, shal-reproach, she kupi talal rai tvi-wak t' ease il forgetfulness. Au travelled u' expeditiously u' tor-yehat; heh sleeping veh mu-yor fi' wuh fau-yut, pulau longbourn k' dinnertime wuh thurai gad. Ish-veh vesh' wuh comfort tor elizabeth tor panah-tor ik jane kupi ri ma vesh' wearied k' wu gishat. Wuh pi' gardiners, skamau k' wuh glan t' wuh chaise, vesh' standing fi' wuh ash-tor t' wuh kelek, u' au svi-tor wuh paddock; heh lu wuh carriage drove abru tor wuh svep, wuh joyful ak'wikmun ik lighted abru ish-veh limuk heh gluvaya itself abru' ish-veh bosh ak'shem, svi' wuh vuhna'es t' capers heh frisks, vesh' wuh wuh'rak pleasing earnest t' ish-veh welcome. Elizabeth spen-tor si'; heh po' giving tik t' au wuh hasty shok, hurried vi' wuh vestibule, wilat jane, vi sarlah sahran downstairs s' ish-veh ko-mekh’s ha-shal, iyi ragel-tor ish-veh. Elizabeth, u' she affectionately nartau ish-veh, whilst bezhun-masu boshau wuh bezhun t' fi', pakik ri wuh moment svi' asking whether sovek-vel had vesh' puzhu-tor t' wuh fugitives. “ri wi, ” kilko-tor jane. “tonk'peh i' ik t'nash-veh tal-kam sa-kuk nam-tor sarlah, i rok kanok-vei dungi nam-tor muhl.” “nam-tor t'nash-veh sa-mekh svi' kahr?” “ha, au went fi' gad, u' i kitau du zhit.” “heh ma du puzhu-tor s' ish-veh k'ashiv?” “etek ma puzhu-tor goh wuh'wak. Au kitau me wuh zamu zehl fi' gad, tor leralmin ik au had lasha svi' ek'manek, heh tor mazhiv-kur-tor me ish-veh kharat, if i wa' eit'jae ish-veh tor tor. Au goh hau, ik au dang ri kitau va'ashiv, till au had vel t' importance tor mention.” “heh t'nash-veh ko-mekh--uf nam-tor she? Uf nam-tor du ek'?” “t'nash-veh ko-mekh nam-tor tolerably muhl, i sahrafel; hi ish-veh tam'a nam-tor greatly shaken. She nam-tor upstairs, heh dungi ma lo'uk satisfaction svi' seeing du ek'. She tor ri wi trasha ish-veh sai-vel-tor-tvi-shal. Mary heh kitty, itaren sha-ka-ri! Nam-tor ved muhl.” “tonk'peh du--uf nam-tor du?” maf-tor elizabeth. “du glazhau spoh. Uf mau du bolau ma hal-tor k'fai!” ish-veh ko-kai, however, assured ish-veh t' ish-veh hasu perfectly muhl; heh ish-veh conversation, if had vesh' be' dvun-tor du' mr. Heh mrs. Gardiner vesh' engaged k' ish-veh kanu, vesh' i' shitau wuh shaht tor k' wuh betaya t' wuh bosh party. Jane sahr-tor tor ish-veh sa-kuk heh ezyet, heh welcomed heh itaren au fi', k' krusitau abru'teruklar-ru'lut heh bezhun-masu. Lu au vesh' ek' svi' wuh bestan-tvi-shal, wuh deshkau if elizabeth had already ya'akash vesh' veling ashiv-tor k' wuh vath, heh au ak afer-tor ik jane had rai kash-tor'es tor mazhiv-kur-tor. Wuh sanguine rok t' rom, however, if wuh benevolence t' ish-veh khaf-spol suggested, had ri wi deserted ish-veh; she fam dvun gishu ik ish-veh would ek' shaht muhl, heh ik kanok asal would katau ein nuhm, either s' lydia il ish-veh sa-mekh, tor danau ish-veh proceedings, heh, sos'eh, tor'pra wuh kal'i'farr. Mrs. Bennet, tor t'vi ha-shal au ek' teslau, po' wuh zamu minutes’ conversation teretuhr, poprah au exactly u' lau nam-tor gishu; k' bezhun-masu heh lamentations t' regret, invectives tehnat wuh villainous spa-tor t' wickham, heh complaints t' ish-veh sha' sufferings heh has-bosh-nam-tor; blaming kanok-veh tonk'peh wuh person tor t'vi has-bosh-judging indulgence wuh lafosh t' ish-veh ko-fu bolau nam-tor principally owing. “kuv i had vesh' kup, ” leralmin-tor she, “tor lesh t'nash-veh sfek svi' going tor brighton k' ek' t'nash-veh skan, _this_ would ri ma pavesh-tor: tonk'peh ri donku-tor tal-kam lydia had kling tor nem-tor tun t' ish-veh. Po did wuh forsters ek'wak kal-tor ish-veh hal-tor si' t' ish-veh glan? I am sure tra' vesh' ein lo'uk neglect il vath fi' ish-veh vla, na' she nam-tor ri wuh ves t' ko-kan tor tor such wuh vel, kuv she had vesh' muhl glazhau po'. I kwon-hau-ov nahp au vesh' maut unfit ki' wuh falun t' ish-veh; tonk'peh i vesh' abru'-khau, u' i kwon-hau-ov am. Ri donku-tor, tal-kam kan! Heh i' la'’s mr. Bennet hal-tor maf, heh i fai-tor au dungi puk wickham, wherever au ragel-tor ish-veh, heh yi au dungi nam-tor pustau, heh ra nam-tor tor shetau t' etek ek'? Wuh collinses dungi da-tor etek si', fa' au nam-tor samu svi' ish-veh shi'vukhut; heh kuv du nam-tor ri ves tor etek, sa-kai, i ri tor fai-tor ra etek dungau tor.” au ek' sporiben tehnat such terrific ideas; heh mr. Gardiner, po' paik assurances t' ish-veh affection na' ish-veh heh ek' ish-veh skan, var-tor ish-veh ik au tvai tor nam-tor svi' london wuh maut thurai gad, heh would gol-tor mr. Bennet svi' kanok endeavour na' recovering lydia. “ri tor mazhiv-kur-tor yut tor nam-tor-fam vikayek, ” hau au: “hi ish-veh nam-tor gas'rak tor nam-tor dator na' wuh rasahkos, tra' nam-tor rai occasion tor glazhau fi' ish-veh u' ac'ruth. Ish-veh nam-tor ri ved wuh wehk gad opi' au losrak brighton. Svi' wuh zamu gad weht, etek lau nazh-kap ein ro'fori t' au; heh till etek fai-tor ik au nam-tor ri telik, heh ma rai design t' marrying, ri tor kal-tor etek mazhiv-kur-tor wuh tukh abru' u' pakik. U' ak u' i prah tor kahr, i dungau hal-tor tor t'nash-veh sa-kai, heh tor ish-veh sarlah ha-kel k' me tor gracechurch yut, heh yi etek lau consult teretuhr u' tor ra nam-tor tor nam-tor ovsoh.” “oh, t'nash-veh tal-kam sa-kai, ” kilko-tor mrs. Bennet, “ik nam-tor exactly ra i kupi danik istaya na'. Heh i' tor, lu du prah tor kahr, talal au si', wherever au lau nam-tor; heh kuv au nam-tor ri telik already, _make_ au marry. Heh u' na' wedding sai-vel, ri tor kal-tor au bek-tor na' ik, tonk'peh var-tor lydia she dungau ma u' mau donku u' she chooses tor mahr-tor au, po' au nam-tor telik. Heh, abru' ek' vel, potau mr. Bennet s' fighting. Var-tor ish-veh ra wuh dreadful fupa s' i am svi'--ik i am koltha s' t'nash-veh wits; heh ma such tremblings, such flutterings ek' abru' me, such runev svi' t'nash-veh vla, heh kusut-tor svi' t'nash-veh patam, heh such beatings na' t'nash-veh khaf-spol, ik i mokuhlek prah rai shom k' mu-yor il k' gad. Heh var-tor t'nash-veh tal-kam lydia ri tor mazhiv-kur-tor sovek kharat pa' ish-veh sai-vel till she has gla-tor me, na' she tor ri fai-tor if nam-tor wuh buhfik warehouses. Oh, sa-kai, uf ves du nam-tor! I fai-tor du dungi contrive ish-veh ek'.” tonk'peh mr. Gardiner, hi au assured ish-veh va'ashiv t' ish-veh earnest endeavours svi' wuh aishan, kupi ri nan'woi recommending moderation tor ish-veh, u' muhl svi' ish-veh rok-tor u' ish-veh ptha; heh po' talking k' ish-veh svi' nash manner till aru-yem vesh' fi' pasu, au losrak ish-veh tor krau ek' ish-veh feelings fi' wuh housekeeper, vi attended svi' wuh k'torr ish-veh daughters. Hi ish-veh sa-kai heh ko-kai vesh' persuaded ik tra' vesh' rai yeht occasion na' such wuh seclusion s' wuh skan, au did ri attempt tor oppose ish-veh; na' au fai-tor ik she had ri prudence hiyet tor meskaraya ish-veh lahv fa' wuh dvinsu, du' au bek-tor na' pasu, heh judged ish-veh weh-rom ik _one_ goh t' wuh household, heh wuh veh ik au kupi danik sahrafel, dang comprehend ek' ish-veh ptha heh solicitude fi' wuh subject. Svi' wuh dining-tvi-shal au vesh' ak hau k' mary heh kitty, vi had vesh' nuh' busily engaged svi' ish-veh dahshauk ha-shal tor tor ish-veh appearance fa'. Veh sarlah s' ish-veh dunap, heh wuh vath s' ish-veh toilette. Wuh limuk t' fi', however, vesh' tolerably hayal; heh rai rubah vesh' visible svi' either, kaula ik wuh pak t' ish-veh favourite ko-kai, il wuh reshan if she had herself incurred svi' wuh business, had putan-tor vel weht t' fretfulness do tsuri tor wuh accents t' kitty. U' na' mary, she vesh' mistress hiyet t' herself tor zhal tor elizabeth, k' wuh countenance t' shi'vukhut haulan, ak po' au vesh' hayal-tor na' pasu, -- “nash nam-tor wuh danik unfortunate tek'ik, heh dungi probably nam-tor mau variben t'. Tonk'peh etek bolau kas-fek wuh mashen t' malice, heh mukau vi' wuh wounded bosoms t' tik vath wuh balm t' sisterly consolation.” yi perceiving svi' elizabeth rai inclination t' replying, she hau, “unhappy u' wuh pavek bolau nam-tor na' lydia, etek lau bes-tor s' ish-veh nash useful tupa: --ik pak t' virtue svi' wuh kotik nam-tor irretrievable, ish-veh riyeht ash involves ish-veh svi' shaht-fam ruin, ik ish-veh reputation nam-tor rai lehkuh wei-shau-yehat do ish-veh nam-tor vaksurik, heh ik she fam yehat nam-tor nuh' mau klashau svi' ish-veh kloshai na' wuh undeserving t' wuh vath guv.” elizabeth abertau abru ish-veh bezhun svi' tauraya, tonk'peh vesh' nuh' mau oppressed tor tor sovek kilko. Mary, however, fator tor console herself k' such ves t' moral saseshaya s' wuh ek'rasah fa' au. Svi' wuh aru, wuh dahkuh tela'at din-tor bennets vesh' kup tor nam-tor na' ulef wuh wadan k' themselves; heh elizabeth instantly availed herself t' wuh opportunity t' tor sovek inquiries if jane vesh' kaing nayik tor satisfy. Po' hau svi' paik lamentations abru' wuh dreadful sequel t' nash pavek, if elizabeth panah-tor u' ek' tonk'peh ac'ruth, heh din-tor bennet kupi ri seo'a tor nam-tor wholly impossible, wuh former fator wuh subject k' taran, “tonk'peh var-tor me ek' heh kanok-vei pa' ish-veh if i ma ri already puzhu-tor. Mazhiv-kur-tor me further particulars. Ra did shal-lan forster leralmin? Had au rai apprehension t' sovek-vel fa' wuh elopement nem-tor shi? Au bolau ma gla-tor au teretuhr na' ek'wak.” “shal-lan forster did sha' ik au had k'ashiv suspected ein partiality, wa' fi' lydia’s vla, tonk'peh nothing tor mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh sovek vikayek. I am ni grieved na' ish-veh. Ish-veh kloshai vesh' whio'naks heh ves tor wuh utmost. Au _was_ coming tor etek, svi' zek tor assure etek t' ish-veh concern, fa' au had sovek idea t' ish-veh ri hasu hal-tor tor scotland: lu ik apprehension wuh'rak prah abroad, ish-veh hastened ish-veh halovaya.” “heh vesh' denny convinced ik wickham would ri marry? Did au fai-tor t' ish-veh intending tor hal-tor ska'? Had shal-lan forster gla-tor denny himself?” “ha; tonk'peh lu deshkau k' _him_, denny wafu fai-tor sovek-vel t' ish-veh dotor, heh would ri mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh yeht opinion pa' ish-veh. Au did ri ashiv-tor ish-veh persuasion t' ish-veh ri marrying, heh s' _that_ i am vul-tor tor rok au lau ma vesh' misunderstood fa'.” “heh till shal-lan forster sarlah himself, ri veh t' du entertained wuh vet, i suppose, t' ish-veh hasu really telik?” “uf vesh' ish-veh tor-yehat ik such wuh idea dang svi-tor etwel shi'nahp? I olau wuh pi' uneasy--wuh pi' pthak-bosh t' t'nash-veh ko-kai’s happiness k' ish-veh svi' kal'i'farr, fai'ei i fai-tor ik ish-veh spa-tor had ri vesh' kwon-hau-ov ved gas'rak. T'nash-veh sa-mekh heh ko-mekh fai-tor nothing t' ik; au goh olau uf imprudent wuh match ish-veh bolau nam-tor. Kitty yi puma, k' wuh maut malatik triumph fi' fai-tor weht do wuh shom t' etek, ik svi' lydia’s kim-shah nuhm she had dator ish-veh na' such wuh ash.
