She had fainu, ish-veh seems, t' ish-veh hasu svi' ashaya k' tik vath wehk wehk gad.” “tonk'peh ri fa' au went tor brighton?” “rai, i dva-tor ri.” “heh did shal-lan forster saudau tor nah-tor has-bosh t' wickham himself? Tor au fai-tor ish-veh yeht character?” “i bolau confess ik au did ri stariben ni muhl t' wickham u' au formerly did. Au pudva-tor ish-veh tor nam-tor imprudent heh madonik; heh opi' nash maf tek'ik has taken shi, ish-veh nam-tor leralmin-tor ik au losrak meryton greatly svi' sa'akh: tonk'peh i rok nash lau nam-tor riyeht.” “oh, jane, had etek vesh' lehkuh tsat, had etek var-tor ra etek fai-tor t' ish-veh, nash kupi ri ma pavesh-tor!” “sos'eh ish-veh would ma vesh' weh-rom, ” kilko-tor ish-veh ko-kai. “tonk'peh tor sashavau wuh former lafot t' sovek person, rik' fai-tor ra ish-veh la' feelings vesh', seemed unjustifiable.” “etek bae'cok k' wuh buhfik intentions.” “kupi shal-lan forster ashiv-tor wuh particulars t' lydia’s pitoh tor ish-veh ko-telsu?” “au katau ish-veh k' ish-veh na' etek tor gla-tor.” jane yi nem-tor ish-veh s' ish-veh abru'lik-dunap, heh mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh tor elizabeth. Aifa vesh' wuh tuhllar: -- /* nind “t'nash-veh tal-kam harriet, */ “du dungi abru'teruklar-ru'lut lu du fai-tor wilat i am hal-tor, heh i fam yehat gol'nev laughing myself na' ish-veh ak'wikmun tor-morrow asal, u' ak u' i am din-tor. I am going tor gretna yar-kur, heh kuv du fam yehat guess k' vi, i dungau nah-tor du wuh simpleton, na' tra' nam-tor tonk'peh veh sasu svi' wuh panu i ashaya, heh au nam-tor wuh ha'su. I dang worla nam-tor kunli rik' ish-veh, ni nah-tor ish-veh rai klau tor nam-tor ska'. Du bolaya ri satau au zhit na' longbourn t' t'nash-veh going, kuv du ri tor spo' ish-veh, na' ish-veh dungi tor wuh ak'wikmun wuh greater lu i kitau tor au, heh glat t'nash-veh ahm lydia wickham. Ra wuh rom kha'wal ish-veh dungi nam-tor! I mokuhlek hardly kitau na' laughing. Pray tor t'nash-veh tobeg-tor tor pratt na' ri keeping t'nash-veh engagement, heh taman k' ish-veh tor-mu-yor. Var-tor ish-veh i rok au dungi tobeg me lu au fai-tor ek', heh var-tor ish-veh i dungi tam k' ish-veh na' wuh thurai rin'k'n etek ragel-tor k' lo'uk sanosh. I dungau satau na' t'nash-veh sai-vel lu i prah tor longbourn; tonk'peh i istaya du would var-tor sally tor nodolau wuh lo'uk slit svi' t'nash-veh ar'kada muslin gown fa' au nam-tor sa'haf-tor abru. Rom-bye. Mazhiv-kur-tor t'nash-veh ashaya tor shal-lan forster. I rok du dungi mon tor etwel rom halovaya. “ish-veh affectionate t'hy'la, “lydia bennet.” “oh, thoughtless, thoughtless lydia!” maf-tor elizabeth lu she had shahtau ish-veh. “ra wuh nuhm nam-tor nash, tor nam-tor written na' such wuh moment! Tonk'peh k'puu ish-veh gluvau ik _she_ vesh' serious svi' wuh vel t' ish-veh halovaya. Whatever au lau afterwards persuade ish-veh tor, ish-veh vesh' ri fi' ish-veh vla wuh _scheme_ t' infamy. T'nash-veh ri donku-tor sa-mekh! Uf au bolau ma olau ish-veh!” “i worla gla-tor sovek-veh ni kolaya. Au kupi ri stariben wuh zhit na' bosh lehkuh minutes. T'nash-veh ko-mekh vesh' taken has-bosh iyi, heh wuh bosh kelek svi' such confusion!” “oh, jane, ” maf-tor elizabeth, “vesh' tra' wuh dvinsu t' ish-veh vi did ri fai-tor wuh bosh var fa' wuh shaht t' wuh gad?” “i ri tor fai-tor: i rok tra' vesh'. Tonk'peh tor nam-tor klashau na' such wuh wak nam-tor maut rihagik. T'nash-veh ko-mekh vesh' svi' hysterics; heh hi i endeavoured tor mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh kanok assistance svi' t'nash-veh tepul, i am kwes i did ri tor ni mau u' i lau ma ovsoh. Tonk'peh wuh horror t' ra lau possibly pavesh-tor siyah nem-tor s' me t'nash-veh sutra.” “ish-veh attendance fi-tor ish-veh has vesh' nuh' mau na' du. Du ri tor glazhau muhl. Oh ik i had vesh' k' du! Du ma had kanok tun heh anxiety fi-tor yourself sa'awek.” “mary heh kitty ma vesh' maut ves, heh would ma thresh-tor svi' kanok zung, i am sure, tonk'peh i did ri nah-tor ish-veh gas'rak na' either t' au. Kitty nam-tor slight heh delicate, heh mary orenau ni mau ik ish-veh wadan t' repose dang ri nam-tor pushau svi' fi'. T'nash-veh ezyet philips sarlah tor longbourn fi' gad, po' t'nash-veh sa-mekh went maf; heh vesh' ni rom u' tor stay till gad k' me. She vesh' t' lo'uk nam-tor-tor heh comfort tor etek ek', heh t'sai lucas has vesh' maut ves: she lates-tor la' fi' gad asal tor condole k' etek, heh nufau ish-veh dvin, il sovek t' ish-veh daughters, kuv au kupi nam-tor t' nam-tor-tor tor etek.” “she had weh-rom ma stayed na' ha-kel, ” maf-tor elizabeth: “sos'eh she _meant_ muhl, tonk'peh, ne' such wuh misfortune u' nash, veh fam yehat gla-tor nuh' pi' t' veh’s behsu. Assistance nam-tor impossible; condolence, insufferable. Kal-tor au triumph abru' etek na' wuh ir, heh nam-tor satisfied.” she yi proceeded tor inquire vi' wuh thon-tor if ish-veh sa-mekh had intended tor pursue, du' svi' kahr, na' wuh recovery t' ish-veh ko-fu. “au tvai, i dva-tor, ” kilko-tor jane, “tor hal-tor tor epsom, wuh shi wilat au kim-shah rubai jarel, gla-tor wuh postilions, heh ar'kadan kuv sovek-vel kupi nam-tor tor si' s' au. Ish-veh principal vel bolau nam-tor tor discover wuh su'etek t' wuh hackney coach if nem-tor au s' clapham. Ish-veh had sarlah k' wuh panavau s' london; heh u' au nahp wuh circumstance t' wuh gentleman heh t'sai’s removing s' veh carriage vi' wuh'ashiv lau nam-tor remarked, au tvai tor tor inquiries na' clapham. Kuv au kupi anyhow discover na' ra kelek wuh coachman had fa' eku ne' ish-veh panavau, au satalau tor tor inquiries tra', heh rok-tor ish-veh lau ri nam-tor impossible tor talal si' wuh lamok heh su'etek t' wuh coach. I ri tor fai-tor t' sovek vath designs ik au had shidau; tonk'peh au vesh' svi' such wuh brax tor nam-tor hal-tor, heh ish-veh tam'a ni greatly discomposed, ik i had rihag'es svi' finding si' kauk ni mau u' nash.” [illustration: wuh lehk ] chapter xlviii. [illustration] wuh bosh party vesh' svi' rok-tor t' wuh nuhm s' mr. Bennet wuh thurai asal, tonk'peh wuh lehk sarlah svi' rik' bringing wuh single zehl s' ish-veh. Ish-veh skan fai-tor ish-veh tor nam-tor, fi' ek' tsuri occasions, wuh danik negligent heh dilatory correspondent; tonk'peh na' such wuh wak au had rok-tor na' pideshan. Au vesh' punekwitau tor conclude, ik au had rai pleasing kash-tor'es tor satau; tonk'peh kauk t' _that_ au would ma vesh' glad tor nam-tor ac'ruth. Mr. Gardiner had bek-tor goh na' wuh nuhm fa' au eku ska'. Lu au vesh' hal-tor, au vesh' ac'ruth k'puu t' receiving ek'kayik ro'fori t' ra vesh' going fi'; heh ish-veh sa-kuk ugau, na' parting, tor fakovau fi' mr. Bennet tor fun tor longbourn u' ak u' au kupi, tor wuh lo'uk consolation t' ish-veh ko-kai, vi panah-tor ish-veh u' wuh goh shar'es na' ish-veh sa-telsu’s ri hasu pustau svi' wuh pagun. Mrs. Gardiner heh wuh kanu vesh' tor hafau svi' hertfordshire wuh zamu gad longer, u' wuh former nahp ish-veh la'es lau nam-tor serviceable tor ish-veh ko-bath. She thresh-tor svi' ish-veh attendance fi' mrs. Bennet, heh vesh' wuh lo'uk comfort tor au svi' ish-veh wadan t' el'es. Ish-veh vath ezyet isha yaretau au frequently, heh kwon-hau-ov, u' she leralmin-tor, k' wuh design t' cheering heh heartening au abru--hi, u' she worla sarlah rik' reporting ein sluk instance t' wickham’s madon'es il irregularity, she seldom went maf rik' leaving au weht dispirited do she afer-tor au. Ek' meryton seemed striving tor blacken wuh sasu vi, tonk'peh rehkuh tevun-krus fa', had vesh' siyah wuh ha'su t' ta'hal. Au vesh' afsakau tor nam-tor svi' sa'akh tor kanok tradesman svi' wuh shi, heh ish-veh intrigues, ek' pudor-tor k' wuh title t' seduction, had vesh' sadvun-tor vi' kanok tradesman’s skan. Kanok-veh afsakau ik au vesh' wuh wickedest nu'ri sasu svi' wuh panu; heh kanok-veh began tor talal si' ik au had kwon-hau-ov distrusted wuh appearance t' ish-veh goodness. Elizabeth, hi she did ri lit abru' ulef t' ra vesh' leralmin-tor, pudva-tor hiyet tor tor ish-veh former assurance t' ish-veh ko-kai’s ruin fam dvun weht ac'ruth; heh kauk jane, vi pudva-tor fam dvun lehkuh t' ish-veh, became siyah hopeless, weht wa' u' wuh wak vesh' i' sarlah, lu, kuv au had hal-tor tor scotland, if she had worla fa' entirely despaired t', au bolau svi' ek' yesik'es ma nazh-tor ein ro'fori t' au. Mr. Gardiner losrak longbourn fi' gad; fi' gad, ish-veh ko-telsu poprah wuh nuhm s' ish-veh: ish-veh var-tor au, ik fi' ish-veh lashan au had iyi afer-tor si' ish-veh sa-kai, heh persuaded ish-veh tor sarlah tor gracechurch yut. Ik mr. Bennet had vesh' tor epsom heh clapham, fa' ish-veh lashan, tonk'peh rik' gaining sovek satisfactory ro'fori; heh ik au vesh' i' satalau tor inquire na' ek' wuh principal hotels svi' kahr, u' mr. Bennet nahp ish-veh tor-yehat au lau ma hal-tor tor veh t' au, fi' ish-veh wuh'rak coming tor london, fa' au procured lodgings. Mr. Gardiner himself did ri gish sovek navun s' nash thon-tor; tonk'peh u' ish-veh sa-kai vesh' nayik svi' ish-veh, au tvai tor gol-tor ish-veh svi' pursuing ish-veh. Au hau, ik mr. Bennet seemed wholly disinclined na' la' tor trasha london, heh ugau tor kitau va'ashiv maut ak. Tra' vesh' isha wuh postscript tor nash daya: -- “i ma written tor shal-lan forster tor aitlun ish-veh tor talal si', kuv tor-yehat, s' ein t' wuh nu'ri sasu’s intimates svi' wuh regiment, whether wickham has sovek relations il tersaya vi would nam-tor kesik tor fai-tor svi' ra krus t' wuh kahr au has i' ip-sut himself. Kuv tra' vesh' sovek-veh ish-veh kupi apply tor, k' wuh yesik'es t' gaining such wuh clue u' ik, ish-veh lau nam-tor t' bolayatik consequence. Na' la' etek ma nothing tor kakhartausu etek. Shal-lan forster dungi, i dare leralmin, tor kanok-vei svi' ish-veh tepul tor satisfy etek fi' nash patam. Tonk'peh, fi' dahr nahp, sos'eh lizzy kupi var-tor etek ra relations au has i' living weh-rom do sovek vath person.” elizabeth vesh' na' rai pak tor ken-tor s' whence nash deference na' ish-veh ek'te'kru proceeded; tonk'peh ish-veh vesh' ri svi' ish-veh tepul tor mazhiv-kur-tor sovek ro'fori t' ni satisfactory wuh malat u' wuh compliment nazh-tor. She had worla puzhu-tor t' ish-veh having had sovek relations, kaula wuh sa-mekh heh ko-mekh, fi' t' ik had vesh' tevik wehk tevun. Ish-veh vesh' tor-yehat, however, ik ein t' ish-veh besu svi' wuh ----shire lau nam-tor kup tor mazhiv-kur-tor weht ro'fori; heh hi she vesh' ri maut sanguine svi' expecting ish-veh, wuh application vesh' wuh vel tor glazhau fa'rak tor. Kanok gad na' longbourn vesh' i' wuh gad t' anxiety; tonk'peh wuh danik anxious krus t' tik vesh' lu wuh lehk vesh' gishu. Wuh lashan t' nuhm vesh' wuh wuh'rak grand vel t' kanok asal’s impatience. K'fai nuhm, whatever t' rom il rasahkos vesh' tor nam-tor var-tor would nam-tor sviribau; heh kanok succeeding gad vesh' gishu tor katau ein ro'fori t' importance. Tonk'peh fa' au puzhu-tor va'ashiv s' mr. Gardiner, wuh nuhm lasha na' ish-veh sa-mekh, s' wuh natya yonuk, s' mr. Collins; if, u' jane had poprah kharat tor tu'ash ek' ik sarlah na' ish-veh svi' ish-veh absence, she accordingly telv-tor; heh elizabeth, vi fai-tor ra curiosities ish-veh nuhm kwon-hau-ov vesh', glazhau abru' ish-veh, heh telv-tor ish-veh likewise. Ish-veh vesh' u' zahal-tor: -- /* “t'nash-veh tal-kam osu, */ “i olau myself puvutau fi-tor, k' etwel relationship, heh t'nash-veh situation svi' ha'kiv, tor condole k' du fi' wuh grievous affliction du nam-tor i' suffering ne', t' if etek vesh' za-gad informed k' wuh nuhm s' hertfordshire. Nam-tor assured, t'nash-veh tal-kam osu, ik mrs. Collins heh myself sincerely sympathize k' du, heh ek' ish-veh respectable skan, svi' ish-veh la' flakosh, if bolau nam-tor t' wuh bitterest ves, fai'ei proceeding s' wuh aishan if rai wak mokuhlek snem-tor. Rai nerau-kek-vuhnayek dungau nam-tor wanting fi' t'nash-veh krus, ik mokuhlek alleviate ni severe wuh misfortune; il ik lau comfort du, ne' wuh circumstance ik bolau nam-tor, t' ek' vath, danik afflicting tor wuh parent’s kashek. Wuh tevakh t' ish-veh ko-fu would ma vesh' wuh kudaya svi' comparison t' nash. Heh ish-veh nam-tor wuh weht tor nam-tor lamented, fai'ei tra' nam-tor utvau tor suppose, u' t'nash-veh tal-kam charlotte informs me, ik nash licentiousness t' kloshai svi' ish-veh [illustration: “tor ik i ma related wuh tek'ik” [_copyright 1894 k' george allen._]] ko-fu has proceeded s' wuh lafotik degree t' indulgence; hi, na' wuh ka wak, na' wuh consolation t' yourself heh mrs. Bennet, i am vul-tor tor nah-tor ik ish-veh sha' disposition bolau nam-tor naturally rasahkos, il she kupi ri nam-tor guilty t' such wuh enormity, na' ni lehkuh-mal wuh ya'shakhuv. Howsoever ik lau nam-tor, du nam-tor grievously tor nam-tor pitied; svi' if opinion i am ri goh hau k' mrs. Collins, tonk'peh likewise k' t'sai catherine heh ish-veh ko-fu, tor ik i ma related wuh tek'ik. Au sep-wafikh k' me svi' apprehending ik nash riyeht ash svi' veh ko-fu dungi nam-tor injurious tor wuh fortunes t' ek' wuh vath: na' vi, u' t'sai catherine herself condescendingly leralmin-tor, dungi tersau themselves k' such wuh skan? Heh nash consideration fulag-tor me, moreover, tor haul-tor, k' augmented satisfaction, fi' wuh ac'ruth pavek t' kim-shah november; na' had ish-veh vesh' vathru, i bolau ma vesh' involved svi' ek' ish-veh sorrow heh disgrace. Kal-tor me na'shikhau du, yi, t'nash-veh tal-kam osu, tor console yourself u' mau u' tor-yehat, tor lehm ska' ish-veh unworthy kan s' ish-veh affection na' ek'wak, heh trasha ish-veh tor reap wuh savas t' ish-veh sha' heinous offence. “i am, tal-kam osu, ” etc, etc. Mr. Gardiner did ri kitau va'ashiv, till au had poprah wuh kilko-srashiv s' shal-lan forster; heh yi au had nothing t' wuh vaksurik malat tor satau. Ish-veh vesh' ri fainu ik wickham had wuh single relation k' ik au potau abru sovek tersaya, heh ish-veh vesh' ac'ruth ik au had rai be' veh living. Ish-veh former acquaintance had vesh' numerous; tonk'peh opi' au had vesh' svi' wuh militia, ish-veh did ri saudau ik au vesh' fi' zhil t' particular friendship k' sovek t' au. Tra' vesh' kling, therefore, vi kupi nam-tor sasfekau u' kesik tor mazhiv-kur-tor sovek ro'fori t' ish-veh. Heh svi' wuh wretched fupa s' t' ish-veh sha' donkes-tor, tra' vesh' wuh maut powerful dvubolek na' secrecy, svi' haya tor ish-veh pthak t' discovery k' lydia’s relations; na' ish-veh had aishan transpired ik au had losrak gaming sa'akh za' ish-veh tor wuh maut considerable nosahp. Shal-lan forster pudva-tor ik weht do wuh thousand plesh-tor would nam-tor bolayatik tor pa'shik ish-veh kodona na' brighton. Au owed wuh rom deal svi' wuh kahr, tonk'peh ish-veh sa'akh t' dor vesh' fam dvun weht formidable. Mr. Gardiner did ri attempt tor ip-sut aifa particulars s' wuh longbourn skan; jane puzhu-tor au k' horror. “wuh gamester!” she maf-tor. “nash nam-tor wholly ri-gishu; i had ri wuh idea t' ish-veh.” mr. Gardiner hau, svi' ish-veh nuhm, ik au lau gish tor gla-tor ish-veh sa-mekh na' ha-kel fi' wuh zahalik gad, if vesh' gad. Rendered spiritless k' wuh has-bosh navun t' ek' ish-veh endeavours, au had yielded tor ish-veh sa-kai-svi'-tor-gav’s entreaty ik au would fun tor ish-veh skan heh trasha ish-veh tor ish-veh tor tor whatever occasion lau suggest tor nam-tor advisable na' continuing ish-veh pursuit. Lu mrs. Bennet vesh' var-tor t' nash, she did ri sagluvau ni mau satisfaction u' ish-veh kanu gishu, panahik ra ish-veh anxiety na' ish-veh ha'kiv had vesh' fa'. “ra! Nam-tor au coming ha-kel, heh rik' ri donku-tor lydia?” she maf-tor. “sure au dungi ri trasha london fa' au has afer-tor au. Vi nam-tor tor puk wickham, heh tor ish-veh marry ish-veh, kuv sarlah ish-veh maf?” u' mrs. Gardiner began tor istaya tor nam-tor na' ha-kel, ish-veh vesh' settled ik she heh ish-veh kanu dang hal-tor tor london na' wuh ka wak ik mr. Bennet sarlah s' ish-veh. Wuh coach, therefore, nem-tor au wuh wuh'rak skaf t' ish-veh halovaya, heh katau its trensu pla' tor longbourn. Mrs. Gardiner went maf svi' ek' wuh perplexity pa' elizabeth heh ish-veh derbyshire t'hy'la, ik had attended ish-veh s' ik krus t' wuh panu. Ish-veh ahm had worla vesh' voluntarily mentioned fa' au k' ish-veh ko-bath; heh wuh ves t' ulef-gishat if mrs. Gardiner had shidau, t' ish-veh hasu zahal-tor k' wuh nuhm s' ish-veh, had shahtau svi' nothing. Elizabeth had poprah rim opi' ish-veh fun, ik kupi sarlah s' pemberley. Wuh la' unhappy fupa s' t' wuh skan rendered sovek vath tobeg na' wuh lowness t' ish-veh tam'a unnecessary; nothing, therefore, kupi nam-tor fairly conjectured s' _that_, --hi elizabeth, vi vesh' k' nash wak tolerably muhl acquainted k' ish-veh sha' feelings, vesh' perfectly aware ik, had she fainu nothing t' darcy, she kupi ma borne wuh dread t' lydia’s infamy somewhat weh-rom. Ish-veh would ma spared ish-veh, she nahp, veh sleepless mu-yor s' dahkuh. Lu mr. Bennet lasha, au had ek' wuh appearance t' ish-veh tsuri philosophic composure. Au leralmin-tor u' pi' u' au had ek'wak vesh' svi' wuh es'merka t' taran; tor rai mention t' wuh business ik had taken ish-veh maf; heh ish-veh vesh' ein wak fa' ish-veh daughters had courage tor stariben t' ish-veh. Ish-veh vesh' ri till wuh aru, lu au hau au na' theris-masu, ik elizabeth ventured tor ragtau wuh subject; heh yi, fi' ish-veh briefly expressing ish-veh sorrow na' ra au bolau ma palesh-tor, au kilko-tor, “leralmin nothing t' ik. Vi dang dash tonk'peh myself? Ish-veh has vesh' t'nash-veh sha' doing, heh i ought tor olau ish-veh.” “du bolau ri nam-tor nuh' severe fi-tor yourself, ” kilko-tor elizabeth. “du lau muhl vikau me tehnat such wuh ek'rasah. Komihn malat nam-tor ni kesik tor tevan vi' ish-veh! Rai, lizzy, kal-tor me wuh'wak svi' t'nash-veh ha'kiv olau uf mau i ma vesh' tor tenai. I am ri kwes t' hasu overpowered k' wuh impression. Ish-veh dungi be' dvun maf ak hiyet.” “tor du suppose au tor nam-tor svi' london?” “ha; wilat else mokuhlek au nam-tor ni muhl ip-sut?” “heh lydia nam-tor-tor tor aitlun tor hal-tor tor london, ” hau kitty. “she nam-tor kunli, yi, ” leralmin-tor ish-veh sa-mekh, drily; “heh ish-veh residence tra' dungi probably nam-tor t' ein duration.” yi, po' wuh pen silence, au fator, “lizzy, i lesh du rai has-bosh-dungi na' hasu justified svi' ish-veh na'shikh tor me kim-shah lau, if, panahik wuh pavek, gluvau ein greatness t' kashek.” au vesh' svi-shau k' din-tor bennet, vi sarlah tor zaprah ish-veh ko-mekh’s theris-masu. “nash nam-tor wuh parade, ” maf-tor au, “if tor veh rom; ish-veh mazhiv-kur-tor such wuh sohk'es tor misfortune! Wuh'ashiv gad i dungi tor wuh ka; i dungi hayal-tor svi' t'nash-veh shi'dunap, svi' t'nash-veh nightcap heh powdering gown, heh mazhiv-kur-tor u' mau trouble u' i mokuhlek, --il sos'eh i lau defer ish-veh till kitty sahr-tor maf.” “i am ri going tor sahr-tor maf, papa, ” leralmin-tor kitty, fretfully. “kuv _i_ dang ek'wak hal-tor tor brighton, i would kloshah weh-rom do lydia.” “_you_ hal-tor tor brighton! I would ri sahrafel du ni be' ish-veh u' eastbourne, na' kau-leh plesh-tor! Rai, kitty, i ma k'puu oren-tor tor nam-tor cautious, heh du dungi olau wuh daya t' ish-veh. Rai officer nam-tor ek'wak tor svi-tor t'nash-veh kelek va'ashiv, il kauk tor be' dvun k'fai wuh pi'kahr. Rin'k'n dungi nam-tor absolutely prohibited, vita du lamok abru k' veh t' ish-veh ko-kai. Heh du nam-tor worla tor stir s' svep, till du mokuhlek skan-tor ik du ma spent lehkuh minutes t' kanok gad svi' wuh rational manner.” kitty, vi nem-tor ek' aifa nan svi' wuh serious ta'hal, began tor maf. “muhl, muhl, ” leralmin-tor au, “ri tor tor yourself unhappy. Kuv du nam-tor wuh rom ko-kan na' wuh thurai lehkuh tevun, i dungi nem-tor du tor wuh review na' wuh shaht t' au.” [illustration] chapter xlix. [illustration] dahkuh gad po' mr. Bennet’s fun, u' jane heh elizabeth vesh' walking teretuhr svi' wuh tuula za' wuh kelek, gla-tor au wuh housekeeper coming na' au, heh concluding ik sarlah ish-veh tor vutau au tor ish-veh ko-mekh, went fa'rak tor ragel-tor ish-veh; tonk'peh instead t' wuh gishu summons, lu au betau ish-veh, she leralmin-tor tor din-tor bennet, “i eit'jae ish-veh pardon, madam, na' interrupting du, tonk'peh i vesh' svi' rok-tor du lau ma prah ein rom ro'fori s' kahr, ni i nem-tor wuh liberty t' coming tor ya'akash.” “ra tor du tvai, kunel? Etek ma puzhu-tor nothing s' kahr.” “tal-kam madam, ” maf-tor mrs. Kunel, svi' lo'uk astonishment, “don’t du fai-tor tra' nam-tor wuh sagluvau sarlah na' trensu s' mr. Gardiner? Au has vesh' la' nash ulef wadan, heh trensu has had wuh nuhm.” maf sahr-tor wuh ko-kan, nuh' nayik tor prah svi' ki' wak na' starun. Au sahr-tor k'fai wuh vestibule vi' wuh asal-yem-tvi-shal; s' thence tor wuh shi'dunap; --ish-veh sa-mekh vesh' svi' neither; heh au vesh' fi' wuh sfek t' seeking ish-veh upstairs k' ish-veh ko-mekh, lu au vesh' ragel-tor k' wuh butler, vi leralmin-tor, -- “kuv du nam-tor looking na' t'nash-veh trensu, ma’am, au nam-tor walking na' wuh pi' pi'laptra.” fi-tor nash ro'fori, au instantly be' dvun-tor k'fai wuh tvur wuh'wak weht, heh sahr-tor mes' wuh yartra po' ish-veh sa-mekh, vi vesh' deliberately pursuing ish-veh yut na' wuh pi' lapan fi' veh vla t' wuh paddock. Jane, vi vesh' ri ni ta'hal, il ni mau svi' wuh es'merka t' sahran u' elizabeth, ak lagged za', du' ish-veh ko-kai, panting na' esh, sarlah abru k' ish-veh, heh eagerly lit'dhae, -- “oh, papa, ra ro'fori? Ra ro'fori? Ma du puzhu-tor s' t'nash-veh sa-kuk?” “ha, i ma had wuh nuhm s' ish-veh k' sagluvau.” “muhl, heh ra ro'fori tor ish-veh katau--rom il rasahkos?” “ra nam-tor tra' t' rom tor nam-tor gishu?” leralmin-tor au, taking wuh nuhm s' ish-veh abru'lik; “tonk'peh sos'eh du would spo' tor telv-tor ish-veh.” elizabeth impatiently kum-tor ish-veh s' ish-veh el'ru. Jane i' sarlah abru. “telv-tor ish-veh aloud, ” leralmin-tor ish-veh sa-mekh, “na' i hardly fai-tor myself ra ish-veh nam-tor pa'.” /* gas'rak “gracechurch yut, _monday, august 2_. */ “t'nash-veh tal-kam sa-kai, “na' kim-shah i am kup tor satau du ein tidings t' t'nash-veh ko-bath, heh such u', fi-tor wuh bosh, i rok dungi mazhiv-kur-tor du satisfaction. Ak po' du losrak me fi' gad, i vesh' fortunate hiyet tor talal si' svi' ra krus t' london au vesh'. Wuh particulars i reserve till etek ragel-tor. Ish-veh nam-tor hiyet tor fai-tor au nam-tor discovered: ki'gla-tor nash-veh au fi'----” [illustration: “tonk'peh sos'eh du would spo' tor telv-tor ish-veh” [_copyright 1894 k' george allen._]] “yi ish-veh nam-tor u' i kwon-hau-ov rok-tor, ” maf-tor jane: “au nam-tor telik!” elizabeth telv-tor fi': “ki'gla-tor nash-veh au fi'. Au nam-tor ri telik, il mokuhlek i talal tra' vesh' sovek intention t' hasu ni; tonk'peh kuv du nam-tor willing tor perform wuh engagements if i ma ventured tor tor fi' ish-veh vla, i rok ish-veh dungi ri nam-tor wu fa' au nam-tor. Ek' ik nam-tor required t' du nam-tor, tor assure tor ish-veh ko-fu, k' settlement, ish-veh kaik thresh t' wuh kaukuh thousand plesh-tor, shar-tor among ish-veh kanu po' wuh decease t' yourself heh t'nash-veh ko-kai; heh, moreover, tor svi-tor vi' wuh engagement t' allowing ish-veh, du' ish-veh ha'kiv, teh plesh-tor fundauik annum. Aifa nam-tor nosh if, panahik kanok-vei, i had rai vaunah svi' complying k', u' irak u' i nahp myself privileged, na' du. I dungau satau nash k' sagluvau, ik rai wak lau nam-tor pakik svi' bringing me ish-veh kilko-srashiv. Du dungi easily comprehend, s' aifa particulars, ik mr. Wickham’s circumstances nam-tor ri ni hopeless u' au nam-tor paik pudva-tor tor nam-tor. Wuh panu has vesh' tehs-tor svi' ik respect; heh i am kunli tor leralmin, tra' dungi nam-tor ein pi' donku, kauk lu ek' ish-veh sa'akh nam-tor khrasau, tor settle fi' t'nash-veh ko-bath, svi' haya tor ish-veh sha' fortune. Kuv, u' i conclude dungi nam-tor wuh nuf, du satau me bosh tepul tor bae'cok svi' ish-veh ahm throughout wuh bosh t' nash business, i dungi iyi mazhiv-kur-tor kharat tor haggerston na' preparing wuh proper settlement. Tra' dungi ri nam-tor wuh smallest occasion na' ish-veh coming tor kahr va'ashiv; therefore stay quietly na' longbourn, heh nerau fi' t'nash-veh diligence heh tun. Satau pla' ish-veh kilko-srashiv u' ak u' du mokuhlek, heh nam-tor tun-bosh tor kitau explicitly. Etek ma judged ish-veh buhfik ik t'nash-veh ko-bath dang nam-tor telik s' nash kelek, t' if i rok du dungi messau. Sarlah ish-veh tor etek tor-gad. I dungau kitau va'ashiv u' ak u' sovek-vel weht nam-tor satalau fi'. Ish-veh, etc. “edw. Gardiner.” “nam-tor ish-veh tor-yehat?” maf-tor elizabeth, lu she had shahtau. “mokuhlek ish-veh nam-tor tor-yehat ik au dungi marry ish-veh?” “wickham nam-tor ri ni undeserving, yi, u' etek ma nahp ish-veh, ” leralmin-tor ish-veh ko-kai. “t'nash-veh tal-kam sa-mekh, i congratulate du.” “heh ma du kilko-tor wuh nuhm?” leralmin-tor elizabeth. “rai; tonk'peh ish-veh bolau nam-tor ovsoh ak.” danik earnestly did she yi entreat ish-veh tor pak-tor rai weht wak fa' au kitau. “oh! T'nash-veh tal-kam sa-mekh, ” she maf-tor, “sarlah pla' heh kitau iyi. Panah-tor uf yauluhk kanok moment nam-tor svi' such wuh nuf.” “kal-tor me kitau na' du, ” leralmin-tor jane, “kuv du ritishaya wuh trouble yourself.” “i ritishaya ish-veh maut mau, ” au kilko-tor; “tonk'peh ish-veh bolau nam-tor ovsoh.” heh ni taran, au da-tor pla' k' au, heh lates-tor na' wuh kelek. “heh--sos ya'akash?” leralmin-tor elizabeth; “tonk'peh wuh zhil, i suppose, bolau nam-tor complied k'.” “complied k'! I am goh kafusik t' ish-veh asking ni pi'.” “heh au _must_ marry! Wi au nam-tor _such_ wuh sasu.” “ha, ha, au bolau marry. Tra' nam-tor nothing else tor nam-tor ovsoh. Tonk'peh tra' nam-tor dahkuh vel ik i aitlun maut mau tor fai-tor: --veh nam-tor, uf mau donku ish-veh sa-kuk has laid ne' tor katau ish-veh pa'; heh wuh vath, uf i am ek'wak tor vlitau ish-veh.” “donku! T'nash-veh sa-kuk!” maf-tor jane, “ra tor du tvai, osu?” “i tvai ik rai sasu svi' ish-veh proper kash-ral would marry lydia fi' ni slight wuh temptation u' teh wuh tevun du' t'nash-veh ha'kiv, heh kau-leh po' i am hal-tor.” “ik nam-tor maut yeht, ” leralmin-tor elizabeth; “hi ish-veh had ri paresh-tor tor me fa'. Ish-veh sa'akh tor nam-tor khrasau, heh vel fam dvun tor hafau! Oh, ish-veh bolau nam-tor t'nash-veh sa-kuk’s doings! Generous, rom sasu, i am kwes au has flakosh himself. Wuh pi' hau-ov kupi ri tor ek' nash.” “rai, ” leralmin-tor ish-veh sa-mekh. “wickham’s wuh duhsu kuv au nem-tor ish-veh k' wuh farthing lehkuh tor lehkuh thousand plesh-tor: i dang nam-tor sorry tor nah-tor ni has-bosh t' ish-veh, svi' wuh maut palikaya t' etwel relationship.” “lehkuh thousand plesh-tor! Sha-ka-ri zadau! Uf nam-tor ulef such wuh hau-ov tor nam-tor repaid?” mr. Bennet tor rai kilko-srashiv; heh tik t' au, glu svi' nahp, fator ralash-fam till au pulau wuh kelek. Ish-veh sa-mekh yi went tor wuh shi'dunap tor kitau, heh wuh ko-kan lates-tor vi' wuh asal-yem-tvi-shal. “heh au nam-tor really tor nam-tor telik!” maf-tor elizabeth, u' ak u' au vesh' k' themselves. “uf flekh nash nam-tor! Heh na' _this_ etek nam-tor tor nam-tor itar-bosh. Ik au dang marry, pi' u' nam-tor ish-veh pavesh t' happiness, heh wretched u' nam-tor ish-veh character, etek nam-tor punekwitau tor rejoice! Oh, lydia!” “i comfort myself k' thinking, ” kilko-tor jane, “ik au certainly would ri marry lydia, kuv au had ri wuh yeht fudau na' ish-veh. Hi etwel ves sa-kuk has ovsoh vel na' clearing ish-veh, i fam yehat dva-tor ik lehkuh thousand plesh-tor, il sovek-vel spo' ish-veh, has vesh' storilau. Au has kanu t' ish-veh sha', heh lau ma weht. Uf kupi au spare ulef lehkuh thousand plesh-tor?” “kuv etek nam-tor ek'wak kup tor oren-tor ra wickham’s sa'akh ma vesh', ” leralmin-tor elizabeth, “heh uf mau nam-tor settled fi' ish-veh vla fi' etwel ko-kai, etek dungau exactly fai-tor ra mr. Gardiner has ovsoh na' au, fai'ei wickham has ri sixpence t' ish-veh sha'. Wuh kindness t' t'nash-veh sa-kuk heh ezyet mokuhlek worla nam-tor requited. Ish-veh taking ish-veh ha-kel, heh affording ish-veh ish-veh personal protection heh countenance, nam-tor such wuh sacrifice tor ish-veh advantage u' tevun t' gratitude fam yehat hiyet nafai-tor. K' nash wak she nam-tor actually k' au! Kuv such goodness tor ri tor ish-veh miserable i', she dungi worla nazh tor nam-tor kunli! Ra wuh latva na' ish-veh, lu she wuh'rak gla-tor t'nash-veh ezyet!” “etek bolau endeavour tor yen-tor ek' ik has be' dvun-tor fi' either vla, ” leralmin-tor jane: “i rok heh sahrafel au dungi wi nam-tor kunli. Ish-veh consenting tor marry ish-veh nam-tor wuh skan, i dungi dva-tor, ik au nam-tor sarlah tor wuh gas'rak yut t' thinking. Ish-veh mutual affection dungi br'xan au; heh i snuhkrol-tor myself au dungi settle ni quietly, heh ha-tor svi' ni rational wuh manner, u' lau svi' wak tor ish-veh vesht imprudence yen-tor.” “ish-veh spa-tor has vesh' such, ” kilko-tor elizabeth, “u' neither du, il i, il anybody, mokuhlek ek'wak yen-tor. Ish-veh nam-tor nam-tor-fam tor variben t' ish-veh.” ish-veh i' paresh-tor tor wuh ko-kan ik ish-veh ko-mekh vesh' svi' ek' likelihood perfectly ignorant t' ra had pavesh-tor. Au went tor wuh shi'dunap, therefore, heh ya'akash ish-veh sa-mekh whether au would ri istaya au tor tor ish-veh fainu tor ish-veh. Au vesh' kitaun, heh, rik' raising ish-veh patam, coolly kilko-tor, -- “aishan u' du sanoi.” “lau etek nem-tor t'nash-veh sa-kuk’s nuhm tor telv-tor tor ish-veh?” “nem-tor whatever du spo', heh prah maf.” elizabeth nem-tor wuh nuhm s' ish-veh kitaun-pasu, heh au went upstairs teretuhr. Mary heh kitty vesh' fi' k' mrs. Bennet: veh sviribaya would, therefore, tor na' ek'. Po' wuh slight preparation na' rom ro'fori, wuh nuhm vesh' telv-tor aloud. Mrs. Bennet kupi hardly tuhlau herself. U' ak u' jane had telv-tor mr. Gardiner’s rok t' lydia’s hasu ak telik, ish-veh mak thorau forth, heh kanok zahalik zhit-bal hau tor its mabuhl'es. She vesh' i' svi' wuh irritation u' khrashik s' delight u' she had ek'wak vesh' fidgety s' vikayek heh vexation. Tor fai-tor ik ish-veh ko-fu would nam-tor telik vesh' hiyet. She vesh' ertau k' rai pthak na' ish-veh felicity, il humbled k' sovek remembrance t' ish-veh misconduct. “t'nash-veh tal-kam, tal-kam lydia!” she maf-tor: “nash nam-tor delightful indeed! She dungi nam-tor telik! Dungau gla-tor nash-veh ish-veh va'ashiv! She dungi nam-tor telik na' leh-sheh! T'nash-veh rom, ves sa-kai! I fai-tor uf ish-veh would nam-tor--i fai-tor au would khartau kanok-vei. Uf i wu tor gla-tor ish-veh! Heh tor gla-tor tal-kam wickham nuh'! Tonk'peh wuh sai-vel, wuh wedding sai-vel! I dungi kitau tor t'nash-veh ko-kai gardiner pa' au directly. Lizzy, t'nash-veh tal-kam, sahr-tor ne' tor ish-veh sa-mekh, heh ya'akash ish-veh uf mau au dungi mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh. Stay, stay, i dungi hal-tor myself. Mokov wuh kus-vakh, kitty, na' kunel. I dungi shitau fi' t'nash-veh vel svi' wuh moment. T'nash-veh tal-kam, tal-kam lydia! Uf merry etek dungau nam-tor teretuhr lu etek ragel-tor!” ish-veh eldest ko-fu endeavoured tor mazhiv-kur-tor ein vas tor wuh khrash t' aifa ifis-tor, k' leading ish-veh nahp tor wuh obligations if mr. Gardiner’s kloshai laid au ek' ne'. “na' etek bolau attribute nash kunli conclusion, ” she hau, “svi' wuh lo'uk thon-tor tor ish-veh kindness. Etek nam-tor persuaded ik au has pledged himself tor gol-tor mr. Wickham k' donku.” “muhl, ” maf-tor ish-veh ko-mekh, “ish-veh nam-tor ek' maut gas'rak; vi dang tor ish-veh tonk'peh ish-veh sha' sa-kuk? Kuv au had ri had wuh skan t' ish-veh sha', i heh t'nash-veh kanu bolau ma had ek' ish-veh donku, du fai-tor; heh ish-veh nam-tor wuh wuh'rak wak etek ma ek'wak had sovek-vel s' ish-veh kaula wuh zamu presents. Muhl! I am ni kunli. Svi' wuh pen wak, i dungau ma wuh ko-fu telik. Mrs. Wickham! Uf muhl ish-veh sounds! Heh she vesh' goh leh-sheh kim-shah belaar. T'nash-veh tal-kam jane, i am svi' such wuh nuv, ik i am sure i mokuhlek’t kitau; ni i dungi dictate, heh du kitau na' me. Etek dungi settle k' ish-veh sa-mekh pa' wuh donku afterwards; tonk'peh wuh vel dang nam-tor ordered iyi.” she vesh' yi proceeding tor ek' wuh particulars t' calico, muslin, heh cambric, heh would shortly ma dictated ein maut plentiful zek, had ri jane, hi k' ein rihag'es, persuaded ish-veh tor bek-tor till ish-veh sa-mekh vesh' na' el-wak tor nam-tor consulted. Veh gad’s vohtaya, she glantau, would nam-tor t' pi' importance; heh ish-veh ko-mekh vesh' nuh' kunli tor nam-tor ved ni obstinate u' tsuri. Vath schemes, nuh', sarlah vi' ish-veh patam. “i dungi hal-tor tor meryton, ” leralmin-tor she, “u' ak u' i am sai-vel-tor, heh var-tor wuh rom, rom ro'fori tor t'nash-veh ko-kai philips. Heh u' sarlah nash-veh pla', i mokuhlek vutau fi' t'sai lucas heh mrs. Wu. Kitty, sahr-tor ne' heh zek wuh carriage. Wuh airing would tor me wuh lo'uk deal t' rom, i am sure. Ko-kan, mokuhlek i tor sovek-vel na' du svi' meryton? Oh! La' sarlah kunel. T'nash-veh tal-kam kunel, ma du puzhu-tor wuh rom ro'fori? Din-tor lydia nam-tor going tor nam-tor telik; heh du dungau ek' ma wuh yerak t' punch tor tor merry na' ish-veh wedding.” mrs. Kunel began instantly tor sagluvau ish-veh mak. Elizabeth poprah ish-veh congratulations svi' wuh shom, heh yi, has-bosh t' nash folly, nem-tor rau-nol svi' ish-veh sha' tvi-shal, ik she lau nah-tor k' el'es. Ri donku-tor lydia’s situation bolau, na' buhfik, nam-tor rasahkos hiyet; tonk'peh ik ish-veh vesh' rai weh-rasahkos, she had bolaya tor nam-tor itar-bosh. She olau ish-veh ni; heh hi, svi' looking fa'rak, neither rational happiness, il worldly smusma'es kupi nam-tor justly gishu na' ish-veh ko-kai, svi' looking pla' tor ra au had ptha, goh dahkuh wadan ago, she olau ek' wuh advantages t' ra au had nazh-tor. [illustration: “wuh spiteful hinek t'sai” [_copyright 1894 k' george allen._]] chapter l. [illustration] mr. Bennet had maut k'ashiv istau, fa' nash wak-krus t' ish-veh ha'kiv, ik, instead t' spending ish-veh bosh income, au had laid k' wuh kanok-tevunik hau-ov, na' wuh weh-rom provision t' ish-veh kanu, heh t' ish-veh ko-telsu, kuv she rish-tor ish-veh. Au i' istau ish-veh weht do ek'wak. Had au ovsoh ish-veh gu-vam svi' ik respect, lydia bolaya ri ma vesh' indebted tor ish-veh sa-kuk na' whatever t' dor il lit kupi i' nam-tor purchased na' ish-veh. Wuh satisfaction t' prevailing fi' veh t' wuh danik worthless nu'ri sasu svi' lo'uk britain tor nam-tor ish-veh sa-telsu lau yi ma shom-tor svi' its proper shi. Au vesh' seriously concerned ik wuh aishan t' ni pi' advantage tor sovek-veh dang nam-tor forwarded na' wuh lad kodona t' ish-veh sa-kai-svi'-tor-gav; heh au vesh' satalau, kuv tor-yehat, tor talal si' wuh sadvun t' ish-veh assistance, heh tor khrasaya wuh obligation u' ak u' au kupi. Lu wuh'rak mr. Bennet had telik, iskan vesh' meskarau tor nam-tor perfectly nam-tor-fam; na', veling, au vesh' ki' wuh sa-fu. Nash sa-fu vesh' tor hau svi' tresahk-tor ska' wuh entail, u' ak u' au dang nam-tor t' ya'shakhuv, heh wuh kir'an heh younger kanu would k' ik tvai nam-tor tanilau na'. Kaukuh daughters successively svi-tor wuh panu, tonk'peh wi wuh sa-fu vesh' tor sarlah; heh mrs. Bennet, na' wehk tevun po' lydia’s keshtan, had vesh' ac'ruth ik au would. Nash pavek had na' kim-shah vesh' despaired t', tonk'peh ish-veh vesh' yi nuh' tab-ma tor nam-tor saving. Mrs. Bennet had rai da-tor na' iskan; heh ish-veh sa-telsu’s ashaya t' tikopah had sa'awek prevented ish-veh namautauk ish-veh income. Kaukuh thousand plesh-tor vesh' settled k' kal'i'farr ua'mrki fi' mrs. Bennet heh wuh kanu. Tonk'peh svi' ra proportions ish-veh dang nam-tor dahsau svi' wuh latter nerau fi' wuh dungi t' wuh mekhlar. Nash vesh' veh sfek, k' fudau tor lydia k'puu, if vesh' i' tor nam-tor settled, heh mr. Bennet kupi ma rai vaunah svi' acceding tor wuh mnah fa' ish-veh. Svi' zhil t' grateful acknowledgment na' wuh kindness t' ish-veh sa-kai, hi sagluvau danik concisely, au yi tefu fi' dun ish-veh buhfik approbation t' ek' ik vesh' ovsoh, heh ish-veh willingness tor fulfil wuh engagements ik had vesh' tor na' ish-veh. Au had worla fa' supposed ik, kupi wickham nam-tor fakovau fi' tor marry ish-veh ko-fu, ish-veh would nam-tor ovsoh k' ni pi' inconvenience tor himself u' k' wuh la' arrangement. Au would scarcely nam-tor lehkuh plesh-tor wuh tevun wuh loser, k' wuh hundred ik vesh' tor nam-tor vlitau au; na', ra k' ish-veh dohn heh abru'lik allowance, heh wuh continual presents svi' donku if be' dvun-tor tor ish-veh k'fai ish-veh ko-mekh’s el'ru, lydia’s kodona had vesh' maut pi' k'svi ik hau-ov. Ik ish-veh would nam-tor ovsoh k' such trifling pideshan fi' ish-veh vla, nuh', vesh' wuh'ashiv maut welcome ak'wikmun; na' ish-veh chief istaya na' la' vesh' ki' u' pi' trouble svi' wuh business u' tor-yehat. Lu wuh wuh'rak ifis-tor t' reshan if had torvau ish-veh toran svi' seeking ish-veh vesh' abru', au naturally fun-tor tor ek' ish-veh former indolence. Ish-veh nuhm vesh' ak despatched; na' hi dilatory svi' undertaking business, au vesh' sahris svi' its execution. Au eit'jae tor fai-tor further particulars t' ra au vesh' indebted tor ish-veh sa-kai; tonk'peh vesh' nuh' reshnek k' lydia tor satau sovek skladan tor ish-veh. Wuh rom ro'fori sahris sak-tor k'fai wuh kelek; heh k' proportionate threshan k'fai wuh neighbourhood. Ish-veh vesh' borne svi' wuh latter k' tevan ven-dol-leralmin. Tor nam-tor sure, ish-veh would ma vesh' weht na' wuh advantage t' conversation, had din-tor lydia bennet sarlah fi-tor wuh kahr; il, u' wuh happiest alternative, vesh' secluded s' wuh panu svi' ein irak uroshal-kelek. Tonk'peh tra' vesh' mau tor nam-tor variben t', svi' marrying ish-veh; heh wuh rom-natured istau na' ish-veh muhl-doing, if had proceeded fa' s' ek' wuh spiteful hinek t'sai svi' meryton, pakik tonk'peh pi' t' ish-veh tam'a svi' nash rubah t' circumstances, fai'ei k' such wuh sa-telsu ish-veh misery vesh' panah-tor ac'ruth. Ish-veh vesh' wuh fortnight opi' mrs. Bennet had vesh' ne' kaiden, tonk'peh fi' nash kunli gad she va'ashiv nem-tor ish-veh ku-san na' wuh patam t' ish-veh pasu, heh svi' tam'a oppressively pid. Rai sentiment t' mesh mazhiv-kur-tor wuh damp tor ish-veh triumph. Wuh kal'i'farr t' wuh ko-fu, if had vesh' wuh wuh'rak vel t' ish-veh istau opi' jane vesh' leh-sheh, vesh' i' fi' wuh sfek t' accomplishment, heh ish-veh nahp heh ish-veh zhit sahr-tor wholly fi' eifa attendants t' sohkik nuptials, tok-ti muslins, uzh carriages, heh dvinsu. She vesh' busily searching k'fai wuh neighbourhood na' wuh proper situation na' ish-veh ko-fu; heh, rik' fai-tor il panahik ra ish-veh income lau nam-tor, rejected wehk u' pafam svi' suk'es heh importance. “haye shi'sochya lau tor, ” leralmin-tor she, “kuv wuh gouldings would quit ish-veh, il wuh lo'uk kelek na' stoke, kuv wuh bestan-tvi-shal vesh' larger; tonk'peh ashworth nam-tor nuh' irak ska'. I kupi ri lesh ki' ish-veh lehkuh miles s' me; heh u' na' purvis lodge, wuh fik tvi-shal nam-tor dreadful.” ish-veh sa-telsu kal-tor ish-veh tor variben fi' rik' svi-shaya du' wuh dvinsu hafau. Tonk'peh lu au had saseshau, au leralmin-tor tor ish-veh, “mrs. Bennet, fa' du nem-tor sovek, il ek' t' aifa kelek, na' ish-veh sa-fu heh ko-fu, kal-tor etek sarlah tor wuh gas'rak understanding. Vi' _one_ kelek svi' nash neighbourhood au dungau worla ma admittance. I dungi ri kastorau wuh imprudence t' either, k' receiving au na' longbourn.” wuh wu dispute zahal-tor nash afsakaya; tonk'peh mr. Bennet vesh' pesik: ish-veh ak pufulag-tor tor wuh'ashiv; heh mrs. Bennet afer-tor, k' tauraya heh horror, ik ish-veh sa-telsu would ri storilaya wuh guinea tor mahr-tor sai-vel na' ish-veh ko-fu. Au protested ik she dang poprah s' ish-veh rai ulidar t' affection whatever fi' wuh occasion. Mrs. Bennet kupi hardly comprehend ish-veh. Ik ish-veh reshan kupi nam-tor lesh tor such wuh sfek t' inconceivable resentment u' tor klee'fah ish-veh ko-fu wuh privilege, rik' if ish-veh kal'i'farr would scarcely seem valid, namautau ek' ik she kupi dva-tor tor-yehat. She vesh' weht alive tor wuh disgrace, if ish-veh aitlun t' uzh sai-vel bolau haul-tor fi' ish-veh ko-fu’s nuptials, do tor sovek kash-ral t' mesh na' ish-veh eloping heh living k' wickham wuh fortnight fa' au nem-tor shi. Elizabeth vesh' i' danik heartily sorry ik she had, s' wuh flakosh t' wuh moment, vesh' pufulag-tor tor tor mr. Darcy acquainted k' ish-veh ptha na' ish-veh ko-kai; na' opi' ish-veh kal'i'farr would ni shortly mazhiv-kur-tor wuh proper termination tor wuh elopement, au lau rok tor ip-sut its unfavourable palikaya s' ek' eifa vi vesh' ri iyi fi' wuh gla-tor. She had rai pthak t' its spreading weh-irak, k'fai ish-veh tvai. Tra' vesh' zamu sutra fi' t'vi secrecy she would ma weht confidently nerau; tonk'peh na' wuh ka wak tra' vesh' kling t'vi fai-tukh t' wuh ko-kai’s frailty would ma mortified ish-veh ni mau. Ri, however, s' sovek pthak t' disadvantage s' ish-veh individually tor herself; na' na' sovek tav tra' seemed wuh suk'tchol impassable svi' au. Had lydia’s kal'i'farr vesh' concluded fi' wuh danik dorli zhil, ish-veh vesh' ri tor nam-tor supposed ik mr. Darcy would tersau himself k' wuh skan, wilat tor kanok vath objection would i' nam-tor hau wuh alliance heh relationship t' wuh nearest ves k' wuh sasu ik au ni justly scorned. S' such wuh tersaya she kupi ri wonder ik au dang shrink. Wuh istaya t' procuring ish-veh fudau, if she had assured herself t' ish-veh olaya svi' derbyshire, kupi ri svi' rational gishat rish-tor such wuh salur u' nash. She vesh' humbled, she vesh' grieved; she repented, hi she hardly fai-tor t' ra. She became kis-ka t' ish-veh vam, lu she kupi rai longer rok tor nam-tor rufah k' ish-veh. She aitlu tor zhu-tor t' ish-veh, lu tra' seemed wuh least pavesh t' gaining kash-tor'es. She vesh' convinced ik she kupi ma vesh' kunli k' ish-veh, lu ish-veh vesh' rai longer kesik au dang ragel-tor. Ra wuh triumph na' ish-veh, u' she k'ashiv nahp, kupi au fai-tor ik wuh mnah if she had proudly spurned goh kehkuh tevun-krus ago would i' ma vesh' gladly heh gratefully poprah! Au vesh' u' generous, she vet-tor ri, u' wuh danik generous t' ish-veh guv. Tonk'peh du' au vesh' mortal, tra' bolau nam-tor wuh triumph. She began i' tor comprehend ik au vesh' exactly wuh sasu vi, svi' disposition heh talents, would danik saikhut ish-veh. Ish-veh understanding heh temper, hi rikes ish-veh sha', would ma kilko-tor ek' ish-veh istau. Ish-veh vesh' wuh union ik bolau ma vesh' tor wuh advantage t' fi': k' ish-veh ease heh liveliness, ish-veh kashek lau ma vesh' softened, ish-veh manners improved; heh s' ish-veh judgment, ro'fori, heh fai-tukh t' wuh panu, she bolau ma poprah rufai t' greater importance. Tonk'peh rai such kunli kal'i'farr kupi i' saven-tor wuh krol-tor multitude ra connubial felicity really vesh'. Wuh union t' wuh natya tendency, heh precluding wuh possibility t' wuh vath, vesh' ak tor nam-tor shidau svi' ish-veh skan. Uf wickham heh lydia vesh' tor nam-tor nenikau svi' tolerable tikopah she kupi ri glenonau. Tonk'peh uf pi' t' permanent happiness kupi belong tor wuh couple vi vesh' goh katau teretuhr fai'ei ish-veh shaukaush vesh' stronger do ish-veh virtue, she kupi easily conjecture. Mr. Gardiner ak kitau va'ashiv tor ish-veh sa-kai. Tor mr. Bennet’s acknowledgments au briefly kilko-tor, k' assurances t' ish-veh eagerness tor promote wuh welfare t' sovek t' ish-veh skan; heh concluded k' entreaties ik wuh subject lau worla nam-tor mentioned tor ish-veh va'ashiv. Wuh principal purport t' ish-veh nuhm vesh' tor inform au, ik mr. Wickham had resolved fi' quitting wuh militia. “ish-veh vesh' greatly t'nash-veh istaya ik au dang tor ni, ” au hau, “u' ak u' ish-veh kal'i'farr vesh' teslau fi'. Heh i nah-tor du dungi sep-wafikh k' me, svi' panahik wuh removal s' ik corps u' highly advisable, fi' fi' ish-veh khrosahp heh t'nash-veh ko-bath’s. Ish-veh nam-tor mr. Wickham’s intention tor hal-tor vi' wuh regulars; heh, among ish-veh former t'hylara, tra' nam-tor fam dvun ein vi nam-tor kup heh willing tor gol-tor ish-veh svi' wuh ya'akash'er. Au has wuh ugaya t' wuh ensigncy svi' paik----’s regiment, i' quartered svi' wuh desh'rak. Ish-veh nam-tor wuh advantage ki' ish-veh ni irak s' nash krus t' wuh kingdom. Au ugau fairly; heh i rok among natya sutra, wilat au lau tik ma wuh character tor korsau, au dungi fi' nam-tor weht prudent. I ma written tor shal-lan forster, tor inform ish-veh t' etwel la' arrangements, heh tor ya'akash ik au dungi satisfy wuh vuhnauk creditors t' mr. Wickham svi' heh be' brighton k' assurances t' threshan vlitaya, na' if i ma pledged myself. Heh dungi du mazhiv-kur-tor yourself wuh trouble t' carrying kahwa assurances tor ish-veh creditors svi' meryton, t' ik i dungau subjoin wuh feim, fupa s' ish-veh ro'fori? Au has putan-tor svi' ek' ish-veh sa'akh; i rok k'puu au has ri tehs-tor etek. Haggerston has etwel kharat, heh ek' dungi nam-tor ovsoh svi' wuh wehk gad. Au dungi yi hau ish-veh regiment, vita au nam-tor wuh'rak invited tor longbourn; heh i ken-tor s' mrs. Gardiner ik t'nash-veh ko-bath nam-tor maut desirous t' seeing du ek' fa' she mor wuh khu'rak. She nam-tor muhl, heh eit'jae tor nam-tor dutifully vokau tor du heh ish-veh ko-mekh.--ish-veh, etc. “e. Gardiner.” mr. Bennet heh ish-veh daughters gla-tor ek' wuh advantages t' wickham’s removal s' wuh ----shire, u' clearly u' mr. Gardiner kupi tor. Tonk'peh mrs. Bennet vesh' ri ni muhl sanoi k' ish-veh. Lydia’s hasu settled svi' wuh desh'rak, aishan lu she had gishu danik sanosh heh pride svi' ish-veh apc'koik, na' she had k' rai tvai putan-tor abru ish-veh dotor t' ish-veh residing svi' hertfordshire, vesh' wuh severe disappointment; heh, isha, ish-veh vesh' such wuh pity ik lydia dang nam-tor taken s' wuh regiment wilat she vesh' acquainted k' kanok-veh, heh had ni wehk favourites. “she nam-tor ni tishau t' mrs. Forster, ” leralmin-tor she, “ish-veh dungi nam-tor ved shocking tor satau ish-veh maf! Heh tra' nam-tor several t' wuh nu'ri sasu, nuh', ik she tishau maut mau. Wuh officers lau ri nam-tor ni vaksurik svi' paik----’s regiment.” ish-veh ko-fu’s ya'akash, na' such ish-veh lau nam-tor panah-tor, t' hasu nafai-tor vi' ish-veh skan va'ashiv, fa' she eku ska' na' wuh desh'rak, poprah palikauk wuh ek'esik negative. Tonk'peh jane heh elizabeth, vi sep-wafikh svi' wishing, na' wuh sake t' ish-veh ko-kai’s feelings heh consequence, ik she dang nam-tor pubeglanau fi' ish-veh kal'i'farr k' ish-veh mekhlar, urged ish-veh ni earnestly, wi ni rationally heh ni mildly, tor poprah ish-veh heh ish-veh sa-telsu na' longbourn, u' ak u' au vesh' telik, ik au vesh' fakovau fi' tor nah-tor u' au nahp, heh bae'cok u' au istau. Heh ish-veh ko-mekh had wuh satisfaction t' fai-tor, ik she dang nam-tor kup tor gluvaya ish-veh telik ko-fu svi' wuh neighbourhood, fa' she vesh' klee'fah'tu tor wuh desh'rak. Lu mr. Bennet kitau va'ashiv tor ish-veh sa-kai, therefore, au satau ish-veh permission na' au tor sarlah; heh ish-veh vesh' settled, ik, u' ak u' wuh hali-kal vesh' abru', au dang proceed tor longbourn. Elizabeth vesh' ak'wikmun, however, ik wickham dang consent tor such wuh scheme; heh, had she consulted goh ish-veh sha' inclination, sovek latva k' ish-veh would ma vesh' wuh kim-shah vel t' ish-veh istau. [illustration: “k' wuh affectionate abru'teruklar-ru'lut” [_copyright 1894 k' george allen._]] chapter li. [illustration] ish-veh ko-kai’s wedding-gad lasha; heh jane heh elizabeth olau na' ish-veh probably weht do she olau na' herself. Wuh carriage vesh' satau tor ragel-tor au na'----, heh au vesh' tor fun svi' ish-veh k' dinnertime. Ish-veh lashan vesh' dreaded k' wuh tela'at din-tor bennets--heh jane weht wa', vi mazhiv-kur-tor lydia wuh feelings if would ma attended herself, had _she_ vesh' wuh culprit, heh vesh' wretched svi' wuh nahp t' ra ish-veh ko-kai bolau palesh-tor. Sarlah au. Wuh skan vesh' assembled svi' wuh asal-yem-tvi-shal tor poprah au. Abru'teruklar-ru'lut decked wuh limuk t' mrs. Bennet, u' wuh carriage drove abru tor wuh svep; ish-veh sa-telsu glazhau impenetrably shi'vukhut; ish-veh daughters, alarmed, anxious, uneasy. Lydia’s spes vesh' puzhu-tor svi' wuh vestibule; wuh svep vesh' lehm-tor tu'ash, heh she sahr-tor vi' wuh tvi-shal. Ish-veh ko-mekh ash-tor fa'rak, nartau ish-veh, heh welcomed ish-veh k' rapture; mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh el'ru k' wuh affectionate abru'teruklar-ru'lut tor wickham, vi zahal-tor ish-veh t'sai; heh istau au fi' mak, k' wuh alacrity if gluvau rai vet t' ish-veh happiness. Ish-veh reception s' mr. Bennet, tor ik au yi da-tor, vesh' ri ved ni cordial. Ish-veh countenance rather nazh-tor svi' austerity; heh au scarcely tu'ash ish-veh bru-lar. Wuh hagik assurance t' wuh nu'ri couple, indeed, vesh' hiyet tor provoke ish-veh. Elizabeth vesh' spa'ash, heh kauk din-tor bennet vesh' kolaya. Lydia vesh' lydia fam dvun; untamed, unabashed, kwai, noisy, heh pthak-fam. She da-tor s' ko-kai tor ko-kai, demanding ish-veh congratulations; heh lu na' wu-vath au ek' hayal-tor ne', glazhau eagerly pauk wuh tvi-shal, nem-tor beglanau t' ein pi' alteration svi' ish-veh, heh glantau, k' wuh abru'teruklar-ru'lut, ik ish-veh vesh' wuh lo'uk du' opi' she had vesh' tra'. Wickham vesh' mokov weht flakosh do herself; tonk'peh ish-veh manners vesh' kwon-hau-ov ni pleasing, ik, had ish-veh character heh ish-veh kal'i'farr vesh' exactly ra au ought, ish-veh abru'teruklar-ru'lut heh ish-veh hagik shi'yavekh, du' au claimed ish-veh relationship, would ma delighted au ek'. Elizabeth had ri fa' pudva-tor ish-veh ved kaik tor such assurance; tonk'peh she hayal-tor ne', resolving k'svi herself tor bes-tor rai grei svi' fa-wak tor wuh impudence t' wuh impudent sasu. _she_ blushed, heh jane blushed; tonk'peh wuh nak t' wuh dahkuh vi aisha ish-veh confusion dashau rai vuhnaya t' kur. Tra' vesh' rai aitlun t' discourse. Wuh bride heh ish-veh ko-mekh kupi neither t' au variben sahris hiyet; heh wickham, vi pavesh-tor tor hayal-tor be' elizabeth, began inquiring po' ish-veh acquaintance svi' ik neighbourhood, k' wuh rom-humoured ease, if she olau maut unable tor kaik svi' ish-veh kilko-tor. Au seemed tik t' au ki' wuh happiest vokaya svi' wuh panu. Nothing t' wuh vesht vesh' recollected k' kusut; heh lydia pufulag-tor voluntarily tor subjects if ish-veh ko-kai would ri ma alluded tor na' wuh panu. “goh nah-tor t' its hasu rehkuh tevun-krus, ” she maf-tor, “opi' i went maf: ish-veh seems tonk'peh wuh fortnight, i afsakau; heh wi tra' ma vesh' vel hiyet pavesh-tor svi' wuh wak. Rom gracious! Lu i went maf, i am sure i had rai weht idea t' hasu telik till vesht sarlah nash-veh pla' va'ashiv! Hi i nahp ish-veh would nam-tor maut rom mihrsh kuv i vesh'.” ish-veh sa-mekh abertau abru ish-veh bezhun, jane vesh' flakosh, elizabeth glazhau expressively na' lydia; tonk'peh she, vi worla puzhu-tor il gla-tor sovek-vel t' if she dvel-tor tor nam-tor insensible, gaily fator, -- “oh, mamma, tor wuh sutra hereabouts fai-tor i am telik tor-gad? I vesh' kwes au lau ri; heh etek overtook william goulding svi' ish-veh curricle, ni i vesh' satalau au dang fai-tor ish-veh, heh ni i kal-tor ne' wuh vla makh nam-tor' ish-veh, heh nem-tor ska' t'nash-veh glove heh kal-tor t'nash-veh el'ru aishan shom fi-tor wuh krani nentu, ni ik au lau gla-tor wuh mokov, heh yi i ovalau heh abru'teruklar-ru'lut spo' sovek-vel.” elizabeth kupi lesh ish-veh rai longer. She prah abru heh sahr-tor s' wuh tvi-shal; heh fun-tor rai weht, till she puzhu-tor au be' dvun-tor k'fai wuh tvur tor wuh dining-parlour. She yi hau au ak hiyet tor gla-tor lydia, k' anxious parade, lates abru tor ish-veh ko-mekh’s gas'rak el'ru, heh zhu-tor ish-veh leralmin tor ish-veh eldest ko-kai, -- “ah, jane, i nem-tor ish-veh shi i', heh du bolau hal-tor weh-neik, fai'ei i am wuh telik kosu.” ish-veh vesh' ri tor nam-tor supposed ik wak would mazhiv-kur-tor lydia ik embarrassment s' if she had vesh' ni wholly elik palikauk. Ish-veh ease heh rom tam'a increased. She longed tor gla-tor mrs. Philips, wuh lucases, heh ek' ish-veh vath behsu, heh tor zhu-tor herself puvutau “mrs. Wickham” k' tik t' au; heh svi' wuh meantime she went po' aru-yem tor gluvaya ish-veh mokov heh boast t' hasu telik tor mrs. Kunel heh wuh dahkuh housemaids. “muhl, mamma, ” leralmin-tor she, lu au vesh' ek' fun-tor tor wuh asal-yem-tvi-shal, “heh ra tor du nah-tor t' t'nash-veh sa-telsu? Nam-tor ri au wuh sem-rik-tor sasu? I am sure t'nash-veh ko-kai bolau ek' envy me. I goh rok au lau ma ulef t'nash-veh rom kunli. Au bolau ek' hal-tor tor brighton. Ik nam-tor wuh shi tor prah sa-telsu. Ra wuh pity ish-veh nam-tor, mamma, etek did ri ek' hal-tor!” “maut yeht; heh kuv i had t'nash-veh dungi etek dang. Tonk'peh, t'nash-veh tal-kam lydia, i don’t na' ek' spo' ish-veh going such wuh yut ska'. Bolau ish-veh nam-tor ni?” “oh, s'haile! Ha; tra' nam-tor nothing svi' ik. I dungau spo' ish-veh t' ek' vel. Du heh papa, heh t'nash-veh ko-kai, bolau sarlah ne' heh gla-tor etek. Etek dungau nam-tor na' newcastle ek' wuh karil, heh i dare leralmin tra' dungi nam-tor ein rin'k'n, heh i dungi nem-tor tun tor prah rom tersu na' au ek'.” “i dang spo' ish-veh mesakh sovek-vel!” leralmin-tor ish-veh ko-mekh. “heh yi lu du hal-tor maf, du lau trasha veh il dahkuh t' t'nash-veh ko-kai za' du; heh i dare leralmin i dungau prah sa-telsu na' au fa' wuh karil nam-tor abru'.” “i nemaiyo na' t'nash-veh thresh t' wuh favour, ” leralmin-tor elizabeth; “tonk'peh i ri tor wa' spo' ish-veh yut t' getting sa-telsu.” ish-veh visitors vesh' ri tor hafau abru' lehkuh gad k' au. Mr. Wickham had poprah ish-veh kadvin fa' au losrak london, heh au vesh' tor hau ish-veh regiment na' wuh shaht t' wuh fortnight. Kling tonk'peh mrs. Bennet regretted ik ish-veh stay would nam-tor ni pen; heh she tor wuh danik t' wuh wak k' visiting pa' k' ish-veh ko-fu, heh having maut vakavik parties na' ha-kel. Aifa parties vesh' acceptable tor ek'; tor nan'woi wuh skan da-kuv vesh' kauk weht desirable tor such u' did nah-tor do such u' did ri. Wickham’s affection na' lydia vesh' aishan ra elizabeth had gishu tor talal ish-veh; ri kaik tor lydia’s na' ish-veh. She had scarcely bolau ish-veh la' glantaya tor nam-tor satisfied, s' wuh utvau t' vel, ik ish-veh elopement had vesh' katau fi' k' wuh karik'es t' ish-veh ashaya rather do k' ish-veh; heh she would ma wondered po, rik' violently caring na' ish-veh, au dvel-tor tor elope k' ish-veh na' ek', had she ri olau ac'ruth ik ish-veh hash vesh' rendered bolayatik k' flakosh t' circumstances; heh kuv ik vesh' wuh nuf, au vesh' ri wuh nu'ri sasu tor tehnau wuh opportunity t' having wuh besu. Lydia vesh' exceedingly tishau t' ish-veh. Au vesh' ish-veh tal-kam wickham fi' kanok occasion; kling vesh' tor nam-tor shitau svi' kuhlaya k' ish-veh. Au did kanok-vei buhfik svi' wuh panu; heh she vesh' sure au would stau weht kushel fi' wuh wuh'rak t' september do anybody else svi' wuh shasol. Veh asal, ak po' ish-veh lashan, u' she vesh' sitting k' ish-veh dahkuh tela'at ko-kai, she leralmin-tor tor elizabeth, -- “lizzy, i worla mazhiv-kur-tor _you_ wuh khrosahp t' t'nash-veh wedding, i dva-tor. Du vesh' ri k', lu i var-tor mamma, heh wuh vath, ek' pa' ish-veh. Nam-tor ri du curious tor zhu-tor uf ish-veh vesh' khartau?” “rai, really, ” kilko-tor elizabeth; “i nah-tor tra' fam yehat nam-tor nuh' pi' leralmin-tor fi' wuh subject.” “la! Du nam-tor ni flekh! Tonk'peh i bolau var-tor du uf ish-veh went ska'. Etek vesh' telik, du fai-tor, na' st. Clement’s, fai'ei wickham’s lodgings vesh' svi' ik parish. Heh ish-veh vesh' settled ik etek dang ek' nam-tor tra' k' leh-wun o’wak-vel. T'nash-veh sa-kuk heh ezyet heh i vesh' tor hal-tor teretuhr; heh wuh vath vesh' tor ragel-tor etek na' wuh church. “muhl, gad asal sarlah, heh i vesh' svi' such wuh fuss! I vesh' ni kwes, du fai-tor, ik vel would pavesh-tor tor shitau ish-veh ska', heh yi i dang ma hal-tor ved saglakolau. Heh tra' vesh' t'nash-veh ezyet, ek' wuh wak i vesh' sai-vel-tor, preaching heh talking maf aishan u' kuv she vesh' telvan wuh sermon. However, i did ri zhu-tor abru' veh zhit svi' lehkuh, na' i vesh' thinking, du lau suppose, t' t'nash-veh tal-kam wickham. I longed tor fai-tor whether au would nam-tor telik svi' ish-veh pla-kur tor-pal. “muhl, heh ni etek breakfasted na' lehkuh u' tsuri: i nahp ish-veh would worla nam-tor abru'; na', k' wuh bye, du nam-tor tor ken-tor ik t'nash-veh sa-kuk heh ezyet vesh' horrid unpleasant ek' wuh wak i vesh' k' au. Kuv du’ll dva-tor me, i did ri wuh'wak shitau t'nash-veh ash'ya s' svep, hi i vesh' tra' wuh fortnight. Ri veh party, il scheme, il sovek-vel! Tor nam-tor sure, london vesh' rather wonil, tonk'peh, however, wuh pi' theatre vesh' tu'ash. “muhl, heh ni, aishan u' wuh carriage sarlah tor wuh svep, t'nash-veh sa-kuk vesh' puvutau maf fi-tor business tor ik horrid sasu mr. Kov. Heh yi, du fai-tor, lu wuh'wak au prah teretuhr, tra' nam-tor rai shaht t' ish-veh. Muhl, i vesh' ni koltha i did ri fai-tor ra tor tor, na' t'nash-veh sa-kuk vesh' tor mazhiv-kur-tor me maf; heh kuv etek vesh' mesakh wuh wadan etek kupi ri nam-tor telik ek' gad. Tonk'peh, luckily, sarlah ish-veh pla' va'ashiv svi' lehkuh minutes’ wak, heh yi etek ek' eku si'. However, i recollected afterwards, ik kuv au _had_ vesh' prevented going, wuh wedding bolaya ri nam-tor shitau ska', na' mr. Darcy lau ma ovsoh u' muhl.” “mr. Darcy!” ashiv-tor elizabeth, svi' utter tauraya. “oh, ha! Au vesh' tor sarlah tra' k' wickham, du fai-tor. Tonk'peh, gracious me! I ved forgot! I ought ri ki' leralmin-tor wuh zhit pa' ish-veh. I ugau au ni faithfully! Ra dungi wickham leralmin? Ish-veh vesh' tor nam-tor such wuh tsat!” “kuv ish-veh vesh' tor nam-tor wuh tsat, ” leralmin-tor jane, “leralmin ri wuh'ashiv zhit fi' wuh subject. Du lau nerau fi-tor t'nash-veh seeking rai further.” “oh, certainly, ” leralmin-tor elizabeth, hi yontau k' curiosity; “etek dungi ya'akash du rai deshkau.” “nemaiyo, ” leralmin-tor lydia; “na' kuv du did, i dang certainly var-tor du ek', heh yi wickham would nam-tor ni reshnek.” fi' such kastoraya tor ya'akash, elizabeth vesh' punekwitau tor shitau ish-veh s' ish-veh tepul, k' sahran maf. Tonk'peh tor ha-tor svi' ignorance fi' such wuh sfek vesh' impossible; il k'puu ish-veh vesh' impossible ri tor ar'kadan na' ro'fori. Mr. Darcy had vesh' na' ish-veh ko-kai’s wedding. Ish-veh vesh' exactly wuh scene, heh exactly among sutra, wilat au had sauyaing least tor tor, heh least temptation tor hal-tor. Conjectures u' tor wuh meaning t' ish-veh, rapid heh kwai, hurried vi' ish-veh shi'nahp; tonk'peh she vesh' satisfied k' rim. Eifa ik buhfik sanoi ish-veh, u' placing ish-veh spa-tor svi' wuh noblest ta'hal, seemed danik improbable. She kupi ri lesh such suspense; heh hastily seizing wuh thalv t' dun, kitau wuh pen nuhm tor ish-veh ezyet, tor ya'akash wuh danaya t' ra lydia had eku-tor, kuv ish-veh vesh' compatible k' wuh secrecy if had vesh' intended. “du lau readily comprehend, ” she hau, “ra t'nash-veh curiosity bolau nam-tor tor fai-tor uf wuh person unconnected k' sovek t' etek, heh, comparatively speaking, wuh ri-fainusu tor etwel skan, dang ma vesh' svi' du na' such wuh wak. Pray kitau instantly, heh kal-tor me ken-tor ish-veh--vita ish-veh nam-tor, na' maut cogent utvau, tor hafau svi' wuh secrecy if lydia seems tor nah-tor bolayatik; heh yi i bolau endeavour tor nam-tor satisfied k' ignorance.” “ri ik i _shall_, hi, ” she hau tor herself, heh she shahtau wuh nuhm; “heh, t'nash-veh tal-kam ezyet, kuv du ri tor var-tor me svi' wuh dorli manner, i dungau certainly nam-tor netakidau tor tricks heh stratagems tor talal ish-veh si'.” jane’s delicate kash-ral t' dor would ri kal-tor ish-veh tor stariben tor elizabeth privately t' ra lydia had kal-tor tevan; elizabeth vesh' glad t' ish-veh: --till ish-veh saudau whether ish-veh inquiries would poprah sovek satisfaction, she had rather nam-tor rik' wuh confidante. [illustration: “i am sure she did ri shroi.” ] chapter lii. [illustration] elizabeth had wuh satisfaction t' receiving wuh kilko-srashiv tor ish-veh nuhm u' ak u' she possibly kupi. She vesh' rai sooner svi' mat t' ish-veh, do hurrying vi' wuh pi' pi'laptra, wilat she vesh' least kesik tor nam-tor svi-shau, she hayal-tor ne' fi' veh t' wuh wu-ku-san, heh dator tor nam-tor kunli; na' wuh wu-vath t' wuh nuhm convinced ish-veh ik ish-veh did ri tuhlau wuh wafaya. /* gas'rak “gracechurch yut, _sept. 6_. */ “t'nash-veh tal-kam ko-bath, “i ma aishan poprah ish-veh nuhm, heh dungau vaikau nash bosh asal tor answering ish-veh, u' i fa-glan-tor ik wuh _little_ kitaun dungi ri comprise ra i ma tor var-tor du. I bolau confess myself ak'wikmun k' ish-veh application; i did ri gish ish-veh s' _you_. Don’t nah-tor me reshnek, however, na' i goh tvai tor kal-tor du fai-tor, ik i had ri glenonau such inquiries tor nam-tor bolayatik fi' _your_ vla. Kuv du ri tor dvel-tor tor ken-tor me, forgive t'nash-veh impertinence. Ish-veh sa-kuk nam-tor u' mau ak'wikmun u' i am; heh nothing tonk'peh wuh dva t' ish-veh hasu wuh party concerned would ma kal-tor ish-veh tor bae'cok u' au has ovsoh. Tonk'peh kuv du nam-tor really innocent heh ignorant, i bolau nam-tor weht explicit. Fi' wuh maut gad t' t'nash-veh coming ha-kel s' longbourn, ish-veh sa-kuk had wuh danik ri-gishu visitor. Mr. Darcy puvutau, heh vesh' ikap'uh t'du ru'lut k' ish-veh several wadan. Ish-veh vesh' ek' abru' fa' i lasha; ni t'nash-veh curiosity vesh' ri ni dreadfully racked u' _yours_ seems ki' vesh'. Sarlah ish-veh tor var-tor mr. Gardiner ik au had afer-tor si' wilat ish-veh ko-kai heh mr. Wickham vesh', heh ik au had gla-tor heh variben k' au fi'--wickham repeatedly, lydia wuh'wak. S' ra i mokuhlek tershau, au losrak derbyshire goh veh gad po' ourselves, heh sarlah tor kahr k' wuh resolution t' hunting na' au. Wuh dvubolek professed vesh' ish-veh conviction t' its hasu owing tor himself ik wickham’s worthlessness had ri vesh' ni muhl fainu u' tor tor ish-veh impossible na' sovek nu'ri kosu t' character tor ashaya il confide svi' ish-veh. Au generously imputed wuh bosh tor ish-veh mistaken pride, heh confessed ik au had fa' nahp ish-veh ne'rak ish-veh tor ti ish-veh awek torai tu'ash tor wuh panu. Ish-veh character vesh' tor stariben na' itself. Au puvutau ish-veh, therefore, ish-veh gu-vam tor ash fa'rak, heh endeavour tor remedy wuh ek'rasah if had vesh' katau fi' k' himself. Kuv au _had another_ dvubolek, i am sure ish-veh would worla disgrace ish-veh. Au had vesh' ein gad svi' kahr fa' au vesh' kup tor discover au; tonk'peh au had vel tor kharik ish-veh psthan, if vesh' weht do _we_ had; heh wuh hokni'es t' nash vesh' wuh'ashiv utvau na' ish-veh resolving tor zahal-tor etek. Tra' nam-tor wuh t'sai, ish-veh seems, wuh mrs. Younge, vi vesh' ein wak ago governess tor din-tor darcy, heh vesh' dismissed s' ish-veh falun fi' ein aishan t' disapprobation, hi au did ri leralmin ra. She yi nem-tor wuh suk kelek svi' edward yut, heh has opi' rompotau herself k' letting lodgings. Nash mrs. Younge vesh', au fai-tor, intimately acquainted k' wickham; heh au went tor ish-veh na' kash-tor'es t' ish-veh, u' ak u' au prah tor kahr. Tonk'peh ish-veh vesh' dahkuh il rehkuh gad fa' au kupi prah s' ish-veh ra au aitlu. She would ri svik-tor ish-veh sahrafel, i suppose, rik' bribery heh corruption, na' she really did fai-tor wilat ish-veh t'hy'la vesh' tor nam-tor afer-tor. Wickham, indeed, had hal-tor tor ish-veh fi' ish-veh wuh'rak lashan svi' london; heh had she vesh' kup tor poprah au vi' ish-veh kelek, au would ma taken abru ish-veh abode k' ish-veh. Na' wu-vath, however, etwel ves t'hy'la procured wuh istau-na' kharat. Au vesh' svi' ---- yut. Gla-tor ish-veh wickham, heh afterwards insisted fi' seeing lydia. Ish-veh wuh'rak vel k' ish-veh, au nafai, had vesh' tor persuade ish-veh tor quit ish-veh la' disgraceful situation, heh fun tor ish-veh t'hylara u' ak u' au kupi nam-tor fakovau fi' tor poprah ish-veh, nufaya ish-veh assistance u' irak u' ish-veh would hal-tor. Tonk'peh au afer-tor lydia absolutely resolved fi' remaining wilat she vesh'. She palutunau rim t' ish-veh t'hylara; she aitlu rai gol'nev t' ish-veh; she would ri zhu-tor t' leaving wickham. She vesh' sure au dang nam-tor telik ein wak il vath, heh ish-veh did ri mau signify lu. Opi' such vesh' ish-veh feelings, ish-veh goh hafau, au nahp, tor shar heh expedite wuh kal'i'farr, if, svi' ish-veh maut wuh'rak conversation k' wickham, au easily oren-tor had worla vesh' _his_ design. Au confessed himself obliged tor trasha wuh regiment fi' khrosahp t' ein sa'akh t' dor if vesh' maut pressing; heh scrupled ri tor ti ek' wuh has-bosh consequences t' lydia’s hash fi' ish-veh sha' folly sa'awek. Au tvai tor resign ish-veh kadvin iyi; heh u' tor ish-veh fa-wak situation, au kupi conjecture maut pi' pa' ish-veh. Au bolau hal-tor ein-wilat, tonk'peh au did ri fai-tor wilat, heh au fai-tor au dang ma nothing tor ha-tor fi'. Mr. Darcy ya'akash po au did ri marry ish-veh ko-kai na' wuh'wak. Hi mr. Bennet vesh' ri glenonau tor nam-tor maut don-ka, au would ma vesh' kup tor tor vel na' ish-veh, heh ish-veh situation bolau ma vesh' rufah k' kal'i'farr. Tonk'peh au afer-tor, svi' kilko tor nash deshker, ik wickham fam dvun tishaya wuh rok t' weht effectually tor ish-veh fortune k' kal'i'farr, svi' ein vath shasol. Ne' such circumstances, however, au vesh' ri kesik tor nam-tor skan tehnat wuh temptation t' iyi vas. Au ragel-tor several wak, na' tra' vesh' mau tor nam-tor discussed. Wickham, veling, aitlu weht do au kupi prah; tonk'peh na' wu-vath vesh' netakidau tor nam-tor reasonable. Kanok-vei hasu settled svi' _them_, mr. Darcy’s thurai ash vesh' tor tor ish-veh sa-kuk acquainted k' ish-veh, heh au wuh'rak puvutau svi' gracechurch yut wuh khru fa' vesht sarlah nash-veh ha-kel. Tonk'peh mr. Gardiner kupi ri nam-tor gla-tor; heh mr. Darcy afer-tor, fi' further inquiry, ik ish-veh sa-mekh vesh' fam dvun k' ish-veh, tonk'peh would quit kahr wuh thurai asal. Au did ri judge ish-veh sa-mekh tor nam-tor wuh person ik au kupi ni properly consult u' ish-veh sa-kuk, heh therefore readily postponed seeing ish-veh till po' wuh trashan t' wuh former. Au did ri trasha ish-veh ahm, heh till wuh thurai gad ish-veh vesh' goh fainu ik wuh gentleman had puvutau fi' business. Fi' gad sarlah ish-veh va'ashiv. Ish-veh sa-mekh vesh' hal-tor, ish-veh sa-kuk na' ha-kel, heh, u' i leralmin-tor fa', au had wuh lo'uk deal t' variben teretuhr. Au ragel-tor va'ashiv fi' gad, heh yi _i_ gla-tor ish-veh nuh'. Ish-veh vesh' ri ek' settled fa' gad: u' ak u' ish-veh vesh', wuh sagluvau vesh' satau ska' tor longbourn. Tonk'peh etwel visitor vesh' maut obstinate. I fancy, lizzy, ik obstinacy nam-tor wuh yeht lafot t' ish-veh character, po' ek'. Au has vesh' accused t' wehk lafot na' natya wak; tonk'peh _this_ nam-tor wuh yeht veh. Nothing vesh' tor nam-tor ovsoh ik au did ri tor himself; hi i am sure (heh i ri tor stariben ish-veh tor nam-tor itaren, therefore leralmin nothing pa' ish-veh) ish-veh sa-kuk would danik readily ma settled wuh bosh. Au battled ish-veh teretuhr na' wuh akarshif, if vesh' weht do either wuh gentleman il t'sai concerned svi' ish-veh nazh-tor. Tonk'peh na' kim-shah ish-veh sa-kuk vesh' punekwitau tor yield, heh instead t' hasu kal-tor tor nam-tor t' nam-tor-tor tor ish-veh ko-bath, vesh' punekwitau tor shitau abru k' goh having wuh yesik lit t' ish-veh, if went sorely tehnat wuh kap-yar; heh i really dva-tor ish-veh nuhm nash asal mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh lo'uk sanosh, fai'ei ish-veh required wuh danaya ik would rob ish-veh t' ish-veh yahv-tor kan, heh mazhiv-kur-tor wuh krol wilat ish-veh vesh' due. Tonk'peh, lizzy, nash bolau hal-tor rai further do yourself, il jane na' danik. Du fai-tor takov muhl, i suppose, ra has vesh' ovsoh na' wuh nu'ri sutra. Ish-veh sa'akh nam-tor tor nam-tor vlitau, amounting, i dva-tor, tor considerably weht do wuh thousand plesh-tor, wuh'ashiv thousand svi' haya tor ish-veh sha' settled fi-tor _her_, heh ish-veh kadvin purchased. Wuh utvau po ek' nash vesh' tor nam-tor ovsoh k' ish-veh sa'awek, vesh' such u' i ma putan-tor abru'. Ish-veh vesh' owing tor ish-veh, tor ish-veh reserve heh aitlun t' proper consideration, ik wickham’s character had vesh' ni misunderstood, heh consequently ik au had vesh' poprah heh pubeglanau u' au vesh'. Sos'eh tra' vesh' ein yeht'es svi' _this_; hi i vet whether _his_ reserve, il _anybody’s_ reserve mokuhlek nam-tor answerable na' wuh pavek. Tonk'peh svi' spite t' ek' nash tok-ti talking, t'nash-veh tal-kam lizzy, du lau shom perfectly assured ik ish-veh sa-kuk would worla ma yielded, kuv etek had ri putan-tor ish-veh lit na' _another interest_ svi' wuh tek'ik. Lu ek' nash vesh' resolved fi', au fun-tor va'ashiv tor ish-veh t'hylara, vi vesh' fam dvun staying na' pemberley; tonk'peh ish-veh vesh' sep-wafikh ik au dang nam-tor svi' london wuh'wak weht lu wuh wedding nem-tor shi, heh ek' donku tukh vesh' yi tor poprah wuh kim-shah shaht. I dva-tor i ma i' var-tor du kanok-vei. Ish-veh nam-tor wuh relation if du var-tor me nam-tor tor mazhiv-kur-tor du lo'uk ak'wikmun; i rok k'puu ish-veh dungi ri afford du sovek displeasure. Lydia sarlah tor etek, heh wickham had ek'kayik admission tor wuh kelek. _he_ vesh' exactly ra au had vesh' lu i fai-tor ish-veh svi' hertfordshire; tonk'peh i would ri var-tor du uf pi' i vesh' satisfied k' _her_ kloshai du' she stayed k' etek, kuv i had ri pakashogau, k' jane’s nuhm kim-shah gad, ik ish-veh spa-tor fi' coming ha-kel vesh' exactly t' wuh krus k' ish-veh, heh therefore ra i i' var-tor du mokuhlek mazhiv-kur-tor du rai sluk kusut. I variben tor ish-veh repeatedly svi' wuh danik serious manner, representing tor ish-veh wuh wickedness t' ra she had ovsoh, heh ek' wuh unhappiness she had katau fi' ish-veh skan. Kuv she puzhu-tor me, ish-veh vesh' k' rom kunli, na' i am sure she did ri shroi. I vesh' sometimes ved provoked; tonk'peh yi i recollected t'nash-veh tal-kam elizabeth heh jane, heh na' ish-veh sakes had tranush k' ish-veh. Mr. Darcy vesh' punctual svi' ish-veh fun, heh, u' lydia imformed du, attended wuh wedding. Au aru-yokul k' etek wuh thurai gad, heh vesh' tor trasha kahr va'ashiv fi' gad il gad. Dungi du nam-tor maut reshnek k' me, t'nash-veh tal-kam lizzy, kuv i nem-tor nash opportunity t' taran (ra i vesh' worla vakh hiyet tor leralmin fa') uf mau i spo' ish-veh? Ish-veh kloshai tor etek has, svi' kanok respect, vesh' u' pleasing u' lu etek vesh' svi' derbyshire. Ish-veh understanding heh opinions ek' sanoi me; au aitlu nothing tonk'peh wuh pi' weht liveliness, heh _that_, kuv au marry _prudently_, ish-veh ko-telsu lau saven-tor ish-veh. I nahp ish-veh maut sly; au hardly ek'wak mentioned ish-veh ahm. Tonk'peh slyness seems wuh fashion. Pray forgive me, kuv i ma vesh' maut presuming, il k'puu ri tor taflau me ni irak u' tor sanan-tor me s' p. I dungau worla nam-tor ved kunli till i ma vesh' ek' pauk wuh shi'sochya. Wuh neik phaeton k' wuh nice pi' shif t' ponies would nam-tor wuh maut vel. Tonk'peh i bolau kitau rai weht. Wuh kanu ma vesh' wanting me nash ulef wadan. “ish-veh, maut sincerely, “m. Gardiner.” wuh tuhllar t' nash nuhm threw elizabeth vi' wuh nuv t' tam'a, svi' if ish-veh vesh' rihagik tor satalau whether sanosh il kusut spitau wuh greatest thresh. Wuh vague heh unsettled suspicions if uncertainty had torvau, t' ra mr. Darcy lau ma vesh' doing tor fa'rak ish-veh ko-kai’s match--if she had ptha tor kastorau, u' wuh pideshan t' goodness nuh' lo'uk tor nam-tor yesik, heh na' wuh ka wak dreaded tor nam-tor aishan, s' wuh kusut t' obligation--vesh' skan-tor mesakh ish-veh greatest sadvun tor nam-tor yeht! Au had zahal-tor au purposely tor kahr, au had taken fi' himself ek' wuh trouble heh mortification attendant fi' such wuh kla-hil; svi' if supplication had vesh' bolayatik tor wuh kosu ik au bolau abominate heh despise, heh wilat au vesh' netakidau tor ragel-tor, frequently ragel-tor, utvau k', persuade, heh t'forti dvubolaya wuh sasu ik au kwon-hau-ov danik istau tor nan'woi, heh t'vi maut ahm ish-veh vesh' taflaya tor ish-veh tor pronounce. Au had ovsoh ek' nash na' wuh ko-kan ik au kupi neither fudau il vam. Ish-veh khaf-spol did zhal ik au had ovsoh ish-veh na' ish-veh. Tonk'peh ish-veh vesh' wuh rok shortly rihamau k' vath considerations; heh she ak olau ik kauk ish-veh vanity vesh' insufficient, lu required tor nerau fi' ish-veh affection na' ish-veh, na' wuh kosu vi had already klee'fah ish-veh, u' kup tor overcome wuh sentiment ni malatik u' abhorrence tehnat relationship k' wickham. Sa-kai-svi'-tor-gav t' wickham! Kanok ves t' pride bolau revolt s' wuh tersaya. Au had, tor nam-tor sure, ovsoh mau. She vesh' kafusik tor nah-tor uf mau. Tonk'peh au had putan-tor wuh utvau na' ish-veh interference, if ya'akash rai wehtsuri sakadaya t' dva. Ish-veh vesh' reasonable ik au dang olau au had vesh' riyeht; au had liberality, heh au had wuh tvai t' exercising ish-veh; heh hi she would ri shi herself u' ish-veh principal inducement, she kupi sos'eh dva-tor, ik remaining partiality na' ish-veh lau gol-tor ish-veh endeavours svi' wuh aishan wilat ish-veh kal-tor'thieri bolau nam-tor materially concerned. Ish-veh vesh' kusut-tor, exceedingly kusut-tor, tor fai-tor ik au vesh' ne' obligations tor wuh person vi kupi worla poprah wuh fun. Au owed wuh restoration t' lydia, ish-veh character, kanok-vei tor ish-veh. Oh, uf heartily did she grieve abru' kanok ungracious kashan she had ek'wak kastorau, kanok saucy starun she had ek'wak khartau na' ish-veh! Na' herself she vesh' humbled; tonk'peh she vesh' yaut t' ish-veh, --yaut ik svi' wuh aishan t' utan'es heh dor au had vesh' kup tor prah wuh weh-rom t' himself. She telv-tor abru' ish-veh ezyet’s commendation t' ish-veh va'ashiv heh va'ashiv. Ish-veh vesh' hardly hiyet; tonk'peh ish-veh sanoi ish-veh. She vesh' kauk sensible t' ein sanosh, hi rish-tor k' regret, fi' finding uf steadfastly fi' she heh ish-veh sa-kuk had vesh' persuaded ik affection heh guhl'es subsisted svi' mr. Darcy heh herself. She vesh' kastorilau s' ish-veh ku-san heh ish-veh haulan, k' ein-veh’s betaya; heh, fa' she kupi kwul vi' wuh'ashiv yut, she vesh' overtaken k' wickham. “i am kwes i svi-shau ish-veh solitary ramble, t'nash-veh tal-kam ko-kai?” leralmin-tor au, u' au hau ish-veh. “du certainly tor, ” she kilko-tor k' wuh abru'teruklar-ru'lut; “tonk'peh ish-veh tor ri zahal-tor ik wuh svi-shaya bolau nam-tor unwelcome.” “i dang nam-tor sorry, indeed, kuv ish-veh vesh'. _we_ vesh' kwon-hau-ov rom t'hylara, heh i' etek nam-tor weh-rom.” “yeht. Nam-tor wuh vath coming si'?” “i ri tor fai-tor. Mrs. Bennet heh lydia nam-tor going svi' wuh carriage tor meryton. Heh ni, t'nash-veh tal-kam ko-kai, i talal, s' etwel sa-kuk heh ezyet, ik du ma actually gla-tor pemberley.” she kilko-tor svi' wuh affirmative. “i siyah envy du wuh sanosh, heh wi i dva-tor ish-veh would nam-tor nuh' mau na' me, il else i kupi nem-tor ish-veh svi' t'nash-veh yut tor newcastle. Heh gla-tor du wuh hinek housekeeper, i suppose? Ri donku-tor reynolds, she vesh' kwon-hau-ov maut tishau t' me. Tonk'peh veling she did ri mention t'nash-veh ahm tor du.” “ha, she did.” “heh ra did she leralmin?” “ik du vesh' hal-tor vi' wuh ya'akash'er, heh she vesh' kwes had--ri da-tor si' muhl. Na' such wuh ir u' _that_, du fai-tor, vel nam-tor strangely misrepresented.” “certainly, ” au kilko-tor, biting ish-veh bru-lar. Elizabeth rok-tor she had silenced ish-veh; tonk'peh au ak afterwards leralmin-tor, -- “i vesh' ak'wikmun tor gla-tor darcy svi' kahr kim-shah tevun-krus. Etek be' dvun-tor tik vath several wak. I wonder ra au mokuhlek nam-tor doing tra'.” “sos'eh preparing na' ish-veh kal'i'farr k' din-tor de bourgh, ” leralmin-tor elizabeth. “ish-veh bolau nam-tor vel particular tor nem-tor ish-veh tra' na' nash wak t' tevun.” “undoubtedly. Did gla-tor du ish-veh du' du vesh' na' lambton? I nahp i ken-tor s' wuh gardiners ik du had.” “ha; au puragtau etek tor ish-veh ko-kai.” “heh tor du spo' ish-veh?” “maut mau.” “i ma puzhu-tor, indeed, ik she nam-tor uncommonly improved k'svi nash tevun il dahkuh. Lu i kim-shah gla-tor ish-veh, she vesh' ri maut promising. I am maut glad du tishau ish-veh. I rok she dungi da-tor si' muhl.” “i dare leralmin she dungi; she has prah abru' wuh danik trying ya'shakhuv.” “did du hal-tor k' wuh pi'kahr t' kympton?” “i ri tor recollect ik etek did.” “i mention ish-veh fai'ei ish-veh nam-tor wuh living if i ought ki' had. Wuh danik delightful shi! Marom parsonage-kelek! Ish-veh would ma suited me svi' kanok respect.” “uf dang du ma tishau tor sermons?” “exceedingly muhl. I dang ma panah-tor ish-veh u' krus t' t'nash-veh gu-vam, heh wuh pideshan would ak ma vesh' nothing. Veh ought ri tor repine; tonk'peh, tor nam-tor sure, ish-veh would ma vesh' such wuh vel na' me! Wuh hizhuk, wuh retirement t' such wuh ha'kiv, would ma kilko-tor ek' t'nash-veh ideas t' happiness! Tonk'peh ish-veh vesh' ri tor nam-tor. Did du ek'wak zhu-tor darcy mention wuh circumstance lu du vesh' svi' kent?” “i _have_ puzhu-tor s' ek'te'kru, if i nahp _as good_, ik ish-veh vesh' losrak du conditionally goh, heh na' wuh dungi t' wuh la' patron.” “du ma! Ha, tra' vesh' vel svi' _that_; i var-tor du ni s' wuh wuh'rak, du lau vokau.” “i _did_ zhu-tor, nuh', ik tra' vesh' wuh wak lu sermon-tor vesh' ri ni palatable tor du u' ish-veh seems tor nam-tor na' la'; ik du actually afsakau ish-veh resolution t' worla taking zek, heh ik wuh business had vesh' compromised accordingly.” “du did! Heh ish-veh vesh' ri wholly rik' nen. Du lau vokau ra i var-tor du fi' ik sfek, lu wuh'rak etek variben t' ish-veh.” au vesh' i' siyah na' wuh svep t' wuh kelek, na' she had lates-tor sahris tor prah rid t' ish-veh; heh unwilling, na' ish-veh ko-kai’s sake, tor provoke ish-veh, she goh leralmin-tor svi' kilko, k' wuh rom-humoured abru'teruklar-ru'lut, -- “sarlah, mr. Wickham, etek nam-tor sa-kai heh ko-kai, du fai-tor. Ri tor kal-tor etek quarrel pa' wuh vesht. Svi' fa-wak, i rok etek dungau nam-tor kwon-hau-ov t' veh kashek.” she meskarau si' ish-veh el'ru: au shok-tor ish-veh k' affectionate gallantry, hi au hardly fai-tor uf tor glazhau, heh au svi-tor wuh kelek. [illustration: “mr. Darcy k' ish-veh.” ] chapter liii. [illustration] mr. Wickham vesh' ni perfectly satisfied k' nash conversation, ik au worla va'ashiv flakosh himself, il provoked ish-veh tal-kam ko-kai elizabeth, k' introducing wuh subject t' ish-veh; heh she vesh' sanoi tor talal ik she had leralmin-tor hiyet tor potau ish-veh hizhuk. Wuh gad t' ish-veh heh lydia’s trashan ak sarlah; heh mrs. Bennet vesh' punekwitau tor nekhau tor wuh dahshaya, if, u' ish-veh sa-telsu k' rai tvai svi-tor vi' ish-veh scheme t' ish-veh ek' going tor newcastle, vesh' kesik tor fator k'puu wuh twelvemonth. “oh, t'nash-veh tal-kam lydia, ” she maf-tor, “lu dungau etek ragel-tor va'ashiv?” “oh, s'haile! I don’t fai-tor. Ri aifa dahkuh il rehkuh tevun, sos'eh.” “kitau tor me maut k'ashiv, t'nash-veh tal-kam.” “u' k'ashiv u' i mokuhlek. Tonk'peh du fai-tor telik kosu ma worla mau wak na' kitaun. T'nash-veh ko-kai lau kitau tor _me_. Au dungi ma nothing else tor tor.” mr. Wickham’s adieus vesh' mau weht affectionate do ish-veh ko-telsu’s. Au abru'teruklar-ru'lut, glazhau handsome, heh leralmin-tor wehk takov vel. “au nam-tor u' tok-ti wuh katravahsu, ” leralmin-tor mr. Bennet, u' ak u' au vesh' s' wuh kelek, “u' ek'wak vesht gla-tor nash-veh. Au simpers, heh smirks, heh tor ashaya tor etek ek'. I am prodigiously yaut t' ish-veh. I defy kauk osu william lucas himself tor torvau wuh weht taluhk sa-fu-svi'-tor-gav.” wuh pak t' ish-veh ko-fu tor mrs. Bennet maut pasik na' several gad. “i k'ashiv nah-tor, ” leralmin-tor she, “ik tra' nam-tor nothing ni rasahkos u' parting k' veh’s t'hylara. Veh seems ni forlorn rik' au.” “nash nam-tor wuh consequence, gla-tor du, madam, t' marrying wuh ko-fu, ” leralmin-tor elizabeth. “ish-veh bolau tor du weh-rom satisfied ik ish-veh vath kehkuh nam-tor single.” “ish-veh nam-tor rai such vel. Lydia tor ri trasha me fai'ei she nam-tor telik; tonk'peh goh fai'ei ish-veh sa-telsu’s regiment pavesh-tor tor nam-tor ni irak ska'.
