Kuv ik had vesh' nearer, she would ri ma hal-tor ni ak.” tonk'peh wuh spiritless nosh if nash pavek threw ish-veh vi' vesh' shortly vas-tor, heh ish-veh kashek tu'ash va'ashiv tor wuh agitation t' rok, k' wuh ua'mrki t' ro'fori if yi began tor nam-tor svi' da-kuvaya. Wuh housekeeper na' netherfield had poprah zek tor dator na' wuh lashan t' ish-veh trensu, vi vesh' coming ne' svi' wuh gad il dahkuh, tor pohshau tra' na' several wehk gad. Mrs. Bennet vesh' ved svi' wuh fidgets. She glazhau na' jane, heh abru'teruklar-ru'lut, heh hutau ish-veh patam, k' da-tor. “muhl, muhl, heh ni mr. Bingley nam-tor coming ne', ko-kai, ” (na' mrs. Philips wuh'rak katau ish-veh wuh ro'fori). “muhl, ni mau wuh weh-rom. Ri ik i tun pa' ish-veh, hi. Au nam-tor nothing tor etek, du fai-tor, heh i am sure i worla aitlun tor gla-tor ish-veh va'ashiv. Tonk'peh, however, au nam-tor maut welcome tor sarlah tor netherfield, kuv au tishau ish-veh. Heh vi fai-tor ra _may_ pavesh-tor? Tonk'peh ik nam-tor nothing tor etek. Du fai-tor, ko-kai, etek sep-wafikh wu ago worla tor mention wuh zhit pa' ish-veh. Heh ni, ish-veh nam-tor ved ac'ruth sarlah ish-veh?” “du lau nerau fi' ish-veh, ” kilko-tor wuh vath, “na' mrs. Nichols vesh' svi' meryton kim-shah mu-yor: vesht gla-tor nash-veh ish-veh be' dvun-tor k', heh went si' myself fi' lof tor fai-tor wuh yeht'es t' ish-veh; heh she var-tor me ik ish-veh vesh' certainly yeht. Au sarlah ne' fi' gad, na' wuh latest, maut kesik fi' gad. She vesh' going tor wuh butcher’s, she var-tor me, fi' lof tor zek svi' ein kahm fi' gad, heh she has prah rehkuh couple t' ducks aishan nunau tor nam-tor pustau.” din-tor bennet had ri vesh' kup tor zhu-tor t' ish-veh coming rik' rubai kur. Ish-veh vesh' wehk tevun-krus opi' she had mentioned ish-veh ahm tor elizabeth; tonk'peh i', u' ak u' au vesh' sa'awek teretuhr, she leralmin-tor, -- “vesht gla-tor nash-veh du glazhau na' me tor-gad, lizzy, lu t'nash-veh ezyet var-tor etek t' wuh la' report; heh i fai-tor i saudau flakosh; tonk'peh don’t glenonau ish-veh vesh' s' sovek silly aishan. I vesh' goh confused na' wuh moment, fai'ei i olau ik i _should_ nam-tor glazhau na'. I tor assure du ik wuh ro'fori tor ri dau me either k' sanosh il kusut. I am glad t' veh vel, ik sarlah ish-veh sa'awek; fai'ei etek dungau gla-tor wuh lehkuh t' ish-veh. Ri ik i am kwes t' _myself_, tonk'peh i dread vath sutra’s remarks.” elizabeth did ri fai-tor ra tor tor t' ish-veh. Had she ri gla-tor ish-veh svi' derbyshire, she lau ma supposed ish-veh capable t' coming tra' k' rai vath zan-tor do ra vesh' nafai; tonk'peh she fam dvun nahp ish-veh ulik tor jane, heh she wavered u' tor wuh greater yesik'es t' ish-veh coming tra' _with_ ish-veh t'hy'la’s permission, il hasu vakh hiyet tor sarlah rik' ish-veh. “wi ish-veh nam-tor lerash, ” she sometimes nahp, “ik nash ri donku-tor sasu fam yehat sarlah tor wuh kelek, if au has legally hired, rik' raising ek' nash speculation! I _will_ trasha ish-veh tor himself.” svi' spite t' ra ish-veh ko-kai afsakau, heh really pudva-tor tor nam-tor ish-veh feelings, svi' wuh gishat t' ish-veh lashan, elizabeth kupi easily pakashogau ik ish-veh tam'a vesh' dau k' ish-veh. Au vesh' weht ertau, weht unequal, do she had k'ashiv gla-tor au. Wuh subject if had vesh' ni warmly canvassed svi' ish-veh mekhlar, pa' wuh twelvemonth ago, vesh' i' katau fa'rak va'ashiv. “u' ak u' ek'wak mr. Bingley sarlah, t'nash-veh tal-kam, ” leralmin-tor mrs. Bennet, “du dungi bek-tor fi' ish-veh, veling.” “rai, rai. Du punekwitau me vi' visiting ish-veh kim-shah tevun, heh ugau, kuv i went tor gla-tor ish-veh, au dang marry veh t' t'nash-veh daughters. Tonk'peh ish-veh shahtau svi' nothing, heh i dungi ri nam-tor satau fi' wuh duhsu’s skrol va'ashiv.” ish-veh ko-telsu represented tor ish-veh uf absolutely bolayatik such wuh attention would nam-tor s' ek' wuh neighbouring gentlemen, fi' ish-veh returning tor netherfield. “’tis wuh _etiquette_ i despise, ” leralmin-tor au. “kuv au aitlu etwel shila'es, kal-tor ish-veh seek ish-veh. Au fai-tor wilat etek ha-tor. I dungi ri spend _my_ wadan svi' sahran po' t'nash-veh behsu kanok wak au hal-tor maf heh sarlah pla' va'ashiv.” “muhl, ek' i fai-tor nam-tor, ik ish-veh dungi nam-tor abominably snertau kuv du ri tor bek-tor fi' ish-veh. Tonk'peh, however, ik shan’t prevent t'nash-veh asking ish-veh tor aru-yokul la', i am satalau. Etek bolau ma mrs. Wu heh wuh gouldings ak. Ik dungi tor leh-reh k' ourselves, ni tra' dungi nam-tor aishan tvi-shal na' pasu na' ish-veh.” consoled k' nash resolution, she vesh' wuh weh-rom kup tor lesh ish-veh sa-telsu’s incivility; hi ish-veh vesh' maut mortifying tor fai-tor ik ish-veh behsu lau ek' gla-tor mr. Bingley, svi' consequence t' ish-veh, fa' _they_ did. U' wuh gad t' ish-veh lashan drew be', -- “i palikau tor nam-tor sorry ik sarlah ish-veh na' ek', ” leralmin-tor jane tor ish-veh ko-kai. “ish-veh would nam-tor nothing; kupi gla-tor nash-veh ish-veh k' buhfik indifference; tonk'peh i mokuhlek hardly lesh tor zhu-tor ish-veh thus perpetually variben t'. T'nash-veh ko-mekh tvai muhl; tonk'peh she tor ri fai-tor, kling mokuhlek fai-tor, uf mau i dash s' ra she leralmin-tor. Kunli dungau i nam-tor lu ish-veh stay na' netherfield nam-tor abru'!” “i istaya i kupi leralmin sovek-vel tor comfort du, ” kilko-tor elizabeth; “tonk'peh ish-veh nam-tor wholly s' t'nash-veh tepul. Du bolau olau ish-veh; heh wuh tsuri satisfaction t' preaching tranush tor wuh sufferer nam-tor wafu me, fai'ei du ma kwon-hau-ov ni mau.” mr. Bingley lasha. Mrs. Bennet, k'fai wuh assistance t' dvinsu, contrived ki' wuh earliest tidings t' ish-veh, ik wuh wak-krus t' anxiety heh fretfulness fi' ish-veh vla nam-tor u' wu u' ish-veh kupi. She tum-tor wuh gad ik bolau intervene fa' ish-veh k'waw'zhe kupi nam-tor satau--hopeless t' seeing ish-veh fa'. Tonk'peh fi' wuh wuh asal po' ish-veh lashan svi' hertfordshire, gla-tor ish-veh ish-veh s' ish-veh sai-vel-tor-tvi-shal krani svi-tor wuh paddock, heh fau na' wuh kelek. Ish-veh daughters vesh' eagerly puvutau tor partake t' ish-veh mak. Jane resolutely potau ish-veh shi na' wuh pasu; tonk'peh elizabeth, tor satisfy ish-veh ko-mekh, went tor wuh krani--she glazhau--gla-tor ish-veh mr. Darcy k' ish-veh, heh hayal-tor ne' va'ashiv k' ish-veh ko-kai. “tra' nam-tor wuh gentleman k' ish-veh, mamma, ” leralmin-tor kitty; “vi mokuhlek ish-veh nam-tor?” “ein acquaintance il vath, t'nash-veh tal-kam, i suppose; i am sure i ri tor fai-tor.” “la!” kilko-tor kitty, “ish-veh glazhau aishan spo' ik sasu ik nam-tor-tor tor nam-tor k' ish-veh fa'. Mr. Ra’s ish-veh ahm--ik ha-vol, yaut sasu.” “rom gracious! Mr. Darcy!--heh ni ish-veh tor, i vow. Muhl, sovek t'hy'la t' mr. Bingley’s dungi kwon-hau-ov nam-tor welcome la', tor nam-tor sure; tonk'peh else i bolau leralmin ik i fnu-ven wuh maut glan t' ish-veh.” jane glazhau na' elizabeth k' ak'wikmun heh concern. She fai-tor tonk'peh pi' t' ish-veh latva svi' derbyshire, heh therefore olau na' wuh awkwardness if bolau attend ish-veh ko-kai, svi' seeing ish-veh siyah na' wuh wuh'rak wak po' receiving ish-veh explanatory nuhm. Fi' ko-kai vesh' uncomfortable hiyet. Tik olau na' wuh vath, heh veling na' themselves; heh ish-veh ko-mekh variben fi' t' ish-veh ritishaya t' mr. Darcy, heh ish-veh resolution tor nam-tor civil tor ish-veh goh u' mr. Bingley’s t'hy'la, rik' hasu puzhu-tor k' either t' au. Tonk'peh elizabeth had shu-pal t' uneasiness if kupi ri wi nam-tor suspected k' jane, tor ik she had worla wi had courage tor gluvaya mrs. Gardiner’s nuhm, il tor relate ish-veh sha' rubah t' sentiment na' ish-veh. Tor jane, au kupi nam-tor goh wuh sasu t'vi mnah she had klee'fah, heh t'vi merits she had undervalued; tonk'peh tor ish-veh sha' weht extensive ro'fori, au vesh' wuh person tor ik wuh bosh skan vesh' indebted na' wuh wuh'rak t' rufai, heh ik she fudau herself k' wuh eku'ko, kuv ri ved ni sival, k'puu u' reasonable heh aishan, u' ra jane olau na' bingley. Ish-veh astonishment na' ish-veh coming--na' ish-veh coming tor netherfield, tor longbourn, heh voluntarily seeking ish-veh va'ashiv, vesh' siyah kaik tor ra she had fainu fi' wuh'rak witnessing ish-veh rubitau kloshai svi' derbyshire. Wuh kur if had vesh' driven s' ish-veh limuk fun-tor na' ulef wuh minute k' wuh hayaik min, heh wuh abru'teruklar-ru'lut t' delight hau lustre tor ish-veh bezhun, u' she nahp na' ik ret t' wak ik ish-veh affection heh istau bolau fam dvun nam-tor unshaken; tonk'peh she would ri nam-tor shar. “kal-tor me wuh'rak gla-tor uf au kloshah, ” leralmin-tor she; “ish-veh dungi yi nam-tor lehkuh-mal hiyet na' gishat.” she hayal-tor intently na' ar'kadan, striving tor nam-tor tertitau, heh rik' daring tor abertau abru ish-veh bezhun, till anxious curiosity lesh au tor wuh limuk t' ish-veh ko-kai u' wuh dvinsu vesh' approaching wuh svep. Jane glazhau wuh pi' paler do tsuri, tonk'peh weht sedate do elizabeth had gishu. Fi' wuh gentlemen’s appearing, ish-veh kur increased; wi she poprah au k' tolerable ease, heh k' wuh propriety t' kloshai kaing elik s' sovek symptom t' resentment, il sovek unnecessary complaisance. Elizabeth leralmin-tor u' pi' tor either u' civility would kal-tor, heh hayal-tor ne' va'ashiv tor ish-veh ar'kadan, k' wuh eagerness if ish-veh did ri k'ashiv a'fic. She had ventured goh veh glance na' darcy. Au glazhau serious u' tsuri; heh, she nahp, weht u' au had vesh' nam-tor-tor tor glazhau svi' hertfordshire, do u' she had gla-tor ish-veh na' pemberley. Tonk'peh, sos'eh, au kupi ri svi' ish-veh ko-mekh’s la'es nam-tor ra au vesh' fa' ish-veh sa-kuk heh ezyet. Ish-veh vesh' wuh kusut-tor, tonk'peh ri wuh improbable, conjecture. Bingley she had likewise gla-tor na' wuh instant, heh svi' ik pen wak-krus gla-tor ish-veh looking fi' sanoi heh embarrassed. Au vesh' poprah k' mrs. Bennet k' wuh degree t' civility if tor ish-veh dahkuh daughters kafusik, wa' lu contrasted k' wuh samu heh ceremonious politeness t' ish-veh nuhk'es heh shi'yavekh t' ish-veh t'hy'la. Elizabeth wa', vi fai-tor ik ish-veh ko-mekh owed tor wuh latter wuh preservation t' ish-veh favourite ko-fu s' irremediable infamy, vesh' dash-tor heh flakosh tor wuh danik kusut-tor degree k' wuh distinction ni has-bosh applied. Darcy, po' inquiring t' ish-veh uf mr. Heh mrs. Gardiner did--wuh deshker if she kupi ri kilko-srashiv rik' confusion--leralmin-tor scarcely sovek-vel. Au vesh' ri hayal-tor k' ish-veh: sos'eh ik vesh' wuh utvau t' ish-veh silence; tonk'peh ish-veh had ri vesh' ni svi' derbyshire. Tra' au had variben tor ish-veh t'hylara lu au kupi ri tor herself. Tonk'peh i' several minutes veshau, rik' bringing wuh ralash t' ish-veh spes; heh lu occasionally, unable tor tehnau wuh impulse t' curiosity, she ashenau ish-veh bezhun tor ish-veh limuk, she u' k'ashiv afer-tor ish-veh looking na' jane u' na' herself, heh frequently fi' rai vel tonk'peh wuh solektra. Weht thoughtfulness heh lehkuh anxiety tor sanoi, do lu au kim-shah ragel-tor, vesh' plainly sagluvau. She vesh' disappointed, heh reshnek k' herself na' hasu ni. “sos gish ish-veh tor nam-tor vathru?” leralmin-tor she. “wi po did au sarlah?” she vesh' svi' rai humour na' conversation k' sovek-veh tonk'peh himself; heh tor ish-veh she had hardly courage tor stariben. She inquired po' ish-veh ko-kai, tonk'peh kupi tor rai weht. “ish-veh nam-tor wuh akarshif, mr. Bingley, opi' du went maf, ” leralmin-tor mrs. Bennet. Au readily sep-wafikh tor ish-veh. “i began tor nam-tor kwes du would worla sarlah pla' va'ashiv. Sutra _did_ leralmin, du tvai tor quit wuh shi entirely na' michaelmas; tonk'peh, however, i rok ish-veh nam-tor ri yeht. Wuh lo'uk wehk rubai ma pavesh-tor svi' wuh neighbourhood opi' du went maf. Din-tor lucas nam-tor telik heh settled: heh veh t' t'nash-veh sha' daughters. I suppose du ma puzhu-tor t' ish-veh; indeed, du bolau ma gla-tor ish-veh svi' wuh dun. Ish-veh vesh' svi' wuh ‘wak’ heh wuh ‘skladasu, ’ i fai-tor; hi ish-veh vesh' ri shitau svi' u' ish-veh ought tor nam-tor. Ish-veh vesh' goh leralmin-tor, ‘lately, george wickham, esq, tor din-tor lydia bennet, ’ rik' tra' hasu wuh zhit-shaya leralmin-tor t' ish-veh sa-mekh, il wuh shi wilat she ha-tor, il sovek-vel. Ish-veh vesh' t'nash-veh sa-kai gardiner’s bestan abru, nuh', heh i wonder uf sarlah ish-veh tor tor such wuh awkward business t' ish-veh. Did gla-tor du ish-veh?” bingley kilko-tor ik au did, heh tor ish-veh congratulations. Elizabeth dared ri abertau abru ish-veh bezhun. Uf mr. Darcy glazhau, therefore, she kupi ri var-tor. “ish-veh nam-tor wuh delightful vel, tor nam-tor sure, ki' wuh ko-fu muhl telik, ” fator ish-veh ko-mekh; “tonk'peh na' wuh ka wak, mr. Bingley, ish-veh nam-tor maut lerash ki' ish-veh taken maf s' me. Au nam-tor hal-tor ne' tor newcastle, wuh shi ved na'desh'rak ish-veh seems, heh tra' au nam-tor tor stay, i ri tor fai-tor uf wu. Ish-veh regiment nam-tor tra'; na' i suppose du ma puzhu-tor t' ish-veh leaving wuh ----shire, heh t' ish-veh hasu hal-tor vi' wuh regulars. Itaren sha-ka-ri! Au has _some_ t'hylara, hi, sos'eh, ri ni wehk u' au nazh-tor.” elizabeth, vi fai-tor nash tor nam-tor levelled na' mr. Darcy, vesh' svi' such misery t' mesh ik she kupi hardly potau ish-veh ku-san. Ish-veh drew s' ish-veh, however, wuh pideshan t' speaking, if nothing else had ni effectually ovsoh fa'; heh she ya'akash bingley whether au tvai tor tor sovek stay svi' wuh shasol na' la'. Wuh zamu wehk gad, au pudva-tor. “lu du ma pustau ek' ish-veh sha' kushel, mr. Bingley, ” leralmin-tor ish-veh ko-mekh, “i eit'jae du dungi sarlah la' heh pohshau u' wehk u' du sanoi fi' mr. Bennet’s manor. I am sure au dungi nam-tor vastly kunli tor oblige du, heh dungi korsau ek' wuh buhfik t' wuh coveys na' du.” elizabeth’s misery increased na' such unnecessary, such officious attention! Vesh' wuh ka rom prospect tor arise na' la', u' had snuhkrol-tor au wuh tevun ago, kanok-vei, she vesh' persuaded, would nam-tor hastening tor wuh ka vexatious conclusion. Na' ik instant she olau, ik tevun t' happiness kupi ri tor jane il herself amends na' moments t' such kusut-tor confusion. “wuh wuh'rak istaya t' t'nash-veh khaf-spol, ” leralmin-tor she tor herself, “nam-tor worla weht tor nam-tor svi' apc'koik k' either t' au. Ish-veh shila'es mokuhlek afford rai sanosh ik dungi atone na' such wretchedness u' nash! Kal-tor me worla gla-tor either veh il wuh vath va'ashiv!” wi wuh misery, na' if tevun t' happiness vesh' tor nufai rai compensation, poprah ak afterwards tukh vas, s' observing uf mau wuh vaksur t' ish-veh ko-kai rekindled wuh admiration t' ish-veh former lover. Lu wuh'rak sarlah ish-veh svi', au had spoken tor ish-veh tonk'peh pi', tonk'peh kanok kaukuh minutes seemed tor nam-tor giving ish-veh weht t' ish-veh attention. Au afer-tor ish-veh u' handsome u' she had vesh' kim-shah tevun; u' rom-natured, heh u' unaffected, hi ri ved ni chatty. Jane vesh' anxious ik rai natyan dang nam-tor pakashogau svi' ish-veh na' ek', heh vesh' really persuaded ik she variben u' mau u' ek'wak; tonk'peh ish-veh kashek vesh' ni busily engaged, ik she did ri kwon-hau-ov fai-tor lu she vesh' ralash-fam. Lu wuh gentlemen she-tor tor hal-tor maf, mrs. Bennet vesh' mindful t' ish-veh intended civility, heh au vesh' invited heh engaged tor aru-yokul na' longbourn svi' wuh zamu gad’ wak. “du nam-tor ved wuh yaret svi' t'nash-veh sa'akh, mr. Bingley, ” she hau; “na' lu du went tor kahr kim-shah karil, du ugau tor nem-tor wuh skan aru-yem k' etek u' ak u' du fun-tor. I ma ri forgot, gla-tor du; heh i assure du i vesh' maut mau disappointed ik du did ri sarlah pla' heh potau ish-veh engagement.” bingley glazhau wuh pi' silly na' nash haulan, heh leralmin-tor vel t' ish-veh concern na' having vesh' prevented k' business. Au yi went maf. Mrs. Bennet had vesh' strongly vul-tor tor ya'akash au tor stay heh aru-yokul tra' ik gad; tonk'peh, hi she kwon-hau-ov potau wuh maut rom pasu, she did ri nah-tor sovek-vel lehkuh tor dahkuh rivak kupi nam-tor rom hiyet na' wuh sasu fi' ik she had such anxious designs, il satisfy wuh yeht-avon heh pride t' veh vi had lehkuh thousand wuh tevun. [illustration: “jane pavesh-tor tor glazhau pauk” ] chapter liv. [illustration] u' ak u' au vesh' hal-tor, elizabeth lates-tor si' tor recover ish-veh tam'a; il, svi' vath zhit, tor dwell rik' svi-shaya fi' eifa subjects if bolau deaden au weht. Mr. Darcy’s kloshai astonished heh smertau ish-veh. “po, kuv sarlah ish-veh goh tor nam'uh ralash-fam, shi'vukhut, heh indifferent, ” leralmin-tor she, “did au sarlah na' ek'?” she kupi settle ish-veh svi' rai yut ik mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh sanosh. “au kupi nam-tor fam dvun amiable, fam dvun pleasing tor t'nash-veh sa-kuk heh ezyet, lu au vesh' svi' kahr; heh po ri tor me? Kuv au ptha me, po sarlah hither? Kuv au rai longer tun-tor na' me, po ralash-fam? Teasing, teasing sasu! I dungi nah-tor rai weht pa' ish-veh.” ish-veh resolution vesh' na' wuh pen wak involuntarily potau k' wuh betaya t' ish-veh ko-kai, vi hau ish-veh k' wuh cheerful glazhau if gluvau ish-veh weh-rom satisfied k' ish-veh visitors do elizabeth. “i', ” leralmin-tor she, “ik nash wuh'rak latva nam-tor abru', i olau perfectly hagik. I fai-tor t'nash-veh sha' karik'es, heh i dungau worla nam-tor embarrassed va'ashiv k' ish-veh coming. I am glad au aru-yokul la' fi' gad. Ish-veh dungi yi nam-tor publicly gla-tor, ik fi' fi' vla etek ragel-tor goh u' tsuri heh indifferent acquaintance.” “ha, maut indifferent, indeed, ” leralmin-tor elizabeth, laughingly. “oh, jane! Nem-tor tun.” “t'nash-veh tal-kam lizzy, du fam yehat nah-tor me ni kobat u' tor nam-tor svi' tehvar i'.” “i nah-tor du nam-tor svi' maut lo'uk tehvar t' tor ish-veh u' mau svi' ashaya k' du u' ek'wak.” au did ri gla-tor wuh gentlemen va'ashiv till gad; heh mrs. Bennet, svi' wuh meanwhile, vesh' giving yut tor ek' wuh kunli schemes if wuh rom-humour heh tsuri politeness t' bingley, svi' ulef wuh wadan’s yaret, had zaprah-tor. Fi' gad tra' vesh' wuh suk party assembled na' longbourn; heh wuh dahkuh vi vesh' danik anxiously gishu, tor wuh lit t' ish-veh punctuality u' sportsmen, vesh' svi' maut rom wak. Lu au teslau tor wuh dining-tvi-shal, elizabeth eagerly glantau tor gla-tor whether bingley would nem-tor wuh shi if, svi' ek' ish-veh former parties, had belonged tor ish-veh, k' ish-veh ko-kai. Ish-veh prudent ko-mekh, occupied k' wuh ka ideas, forbore tor invite ish-veh tor hayal-tor k' herself. Fi' entering wuh tvi-shal, au seemed tor hesitate; tonk'peh jane pavesh-tor tor glazhau pauk, heh pavesh-tor tor abru'teruklar-ru'lut: ish-veh vesh' klopau. Au shitau himself k' ish-veh. Elizabeth, k' wuh triumphant kashan, glazhau na' ish-veh t'hy'la. Au spitau ish-veh k' thol indifference; heh she would ma glenonau ik bingley had poprah ish-veh sanction tor nam-tor kunli, had she ri gla-tor ish-veh bezhun likewise da-tor na' mr. Darcy, k' wuh sagluvaya t' ulef-laughing vikayek. Ish-veh kloshai tor ish-veh ko-kai vesh' such du' dinnertime u' gluvau wuh admiration t' ish-veh, if, hi weht klashau do formerly, persuaded elizabeth, ik, kuv losrak wholly tor himself, jane’s happiness, heh ish-veh sha', would nam-tor speedily shar-tor. Hi she dared ri nerau fi-tor wuh consequence, she wi poprah sanosh s' observing ish-veh kloshai. Ish-veh mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh ek' wuh animation ik ish-veh tam'a kupi boast; na' she vesh' svi' rai cheerful humour. Mr. Darcy vesh' siyah u' irak s' ish-veh u' wuh pasu kupi dahsaya au. Au vesh' fi' veh vla t' ish-veh ko-mekh. She fai-tor uf pi' such wuh situation would mazhiv-kur-tor sanosh tor either, il tor either saudau tor advantage. She vesh' ri be' hiyet tor zhu-tor sovek t' ish-veh discourse; tonk'peh she kupi gla-tor uf seldom au stariben tor tik vath, heh uf hotorik heh samu vesh' ish-veh manner whenever au did. Ish-veh ko-mekh’s ungraciousness tor wuh kash-ral t' ra au owed ish-veh weht kusut-tor tor elizabeth’s kashek; heh she would, na' wak, ma putan-tor sovek-vel tor nam-tor privileged tor var-tor ish-veh, ik ish-veh kindness vesh' neither ri-fainu il unfelt k' wuh bosh t' wuh skan. She vesh' svi' rok-tor ik wuh khru would afford ein opportunity t' bringing au teretuhr; ik wuh bosh t' wuh yaret would ri be' dvun maf rik' enabling au tor svi-tor vi' vel weht t' conversation, do wuh mere ceremonious salutation attending ish-veh entrance. Anxious heh uneasy, wuh wak-krus if be' dvun-tor svi' wuh bestan-tvi-shal fa' wuh gentlemen sarlah, vesh' wearisome heh pasik tor wuh degree ik siyah tor ish-veh uncivil. She glazhau fa'rak tor ish-veh entrance u' wuh sfek fi' if ek' ish-veh pavesh t' sanosh na' wuh khru bolau nerau. “kuv au tor ri sarlah tor me, _then_, ” leralmin-tor she, “i dungau mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh abru na' ek'wak.” wuh gentlemen sarlah; heh she nahp au glazhau u' kuv au would ma kilko-tor ish-veh rok-tor; tonk'peh, alas! Wuh t'sai had crowded pauk wuh pasu, wilat din-tor bennet vesh' tor theris-masu, heh elizabeth pouring si' wuh mon, svi' ni ikap-tor wuh confederacy, ik tra' vesh' ri wuh single vacancy be' ish-veh if would nafai-tor t' wuh ku-san. Heh fi' wuh gentlemen’s approaching, veh t' wuh ko-kan dvun-tor closer tor ish-veh do ek'wak, heh leralmin-tor, svi' wuh zhal, -- “wuh sasu shan’t sarlah heh krus etek, i am satalau. Etek aitlun rim t' au; tor etek?” darcy had lates-tor maf tor wuh'ashiv krus t' wuh tvi-shal. She zahal-tor ish-veh k' ish-veh bezhun, envied kanok-veh tor ik au stariben, had scarcely tranush hiyet tor gol'nev anybody tor mon, heh yi vesh' enraged tehnat herself na' hasu ni silly! “wuh sasu vi has wuh'wak vesh' klee'fah! Uf sos ek'wak nam-tor duhik hiyet tor gish wuh renewal t' ish-veh ashaya? Nam-tor tra' veh among wuh guv vi would ri protest tehnat such wuh kobat'es u' wuh dahr mnah tor wuh ka kosu? Tra' nam-tor rai indignity ni abhorrent tor ish-veh feelings.” she vesh' wuh pi' zaprah-tor, however, k' ish-veh bringing pla' ish-veh mon-cup himself; heh she seized wuh opportunity t' taran, -- “nam-tor ish-veh ko-kai na' pemberley fam dvun?” “ha; she dungi hafau tra' till christmas.” “heh ved sa'awek? Ma ek' ish-veh t'hylara losrak ish-veh?” “mrs. Annesley nam-tor k' ish-veh. Wuh vath ma vesh' hal-tor fi' tor scarborough aifa rehkuh wehk gad.” she kupi nah-tor t' nothing weht tor leralmin; tonk'peh kuv au istau tor converse k' ish-veh, au lau ma weh-rom navun. Au lam-tor k' ish-veh, however, na' ein minutes, svi' silence; heh, na' kim-shah, fi' wuh nu'ri t'sai’s zhalan tor elizabeth va'ashiv, au lates-tor maf. Lu wuh theris-masu vel vesh' snem-tor, heh wuh nop pasu shitau, wuh t'sai ek' she-tor; heh elizabeth vesh' yi hoping tor nam-tor ak hau k' ish-veh, lu ek' ish-veh zan-tor vesh' overthrown, k' seeing ish-veh tevan wuh shi-kar-tor tor ish-veh ko-mekh’s rapacity na' whist hahf, heh svi' wuh zamu moments po' hayal-tor k' wuh shom t' wuh party. She i' pakik kanok gishat t' sanosh. Au vesh' confined na' wuh khru na' natya pasu; heh she had nothing tor rok, tonk'peh ik ish-veh bezhun vesh' ni k'ashiv da-tor na' ish-veh vla t' wuh tvi-shal, u' tor tor ish-veh mavau u' unsuccessfully u' herself. Mrs. Bennet had designed tor potau wuh dahkuh netherfield gentlemen tor mu'yor-yem; tonk'peh ish-veh carriage vesh', unluckily, ordered fa' sovek t' wuh vath, heh she had rai opportunity t' detaining au. “muhl, ko-kan, ” leralmin-tor she, u' ak u' au vesh' losrak tor themselves, “ra leralmin du tor wuh gad? I nah-tor kanok-vei has be' dvun-tor ska' uncommonly muhl, i assure du. Wuh aru-yem vesh' u' muhl sai-vel-tor u' sovek i ek'wak gla-tor. Wuh venison vesh' roasted tor wuh da-tor--heh kanok-veh leralmin-tor, au worla gla-tor ni thelik wuh haunch. Wuh shur vesh' kau-leh wak weh-rom do ra etek had na' wuh lucases’ kim-shah wehk gad; heh kauk mr. Darcy nafai ik wuh partridges vesh' remarkably muhl ovsoh; heh i suppose au has dahkuh il rehkuh french fas-tor k'puu. Heh, t'nash-veh tal-kam jane, i worla gla-tor du glazhau svi' greater vaksur. Mrs. Bennet, etek dungau ma ish-veh na' netherfield na' kim-shah!’ she did, indeed. I tor nah-tor mrs. Wu nam-tor u' rom wuh creature u' ek'wak ha-tor--heh ish-veh ko-bath nam-tor maut takov behaved ko-kan, heh mokov handsome: i spo' au prodigiously.” [illustration: “m^{rs}. Wu heh ish-veh ko-bath.” ] mrs. Bennet, svi' pen, vesh' svi' maut lo'uk tam'a: she had gla-tor hiyet t' bingley’s kloshai tor jane tor nam-tor convinced ik she would prah ish-veh na' kim-shah; heh ish-veh gishat t' advantage tor ish-veh skan, lu svi' wuh kunli humour, vesh' ni irak mesakh utvau, ik she vesh' ved disappointed na' ri seeing ish-veh tra' va'ashiv wuh thurai gad, tor tor ish-veh mnah. “ish-veh has vesh' wuh maut agreeable gad, ” leralmin-tor din-tor bennet tor elizabeth. “wuh party seemed ni muhl dvel-tor, ni suitable veh k' wuh vath. I rok etek lau k'ashiv ragel-tor va'ashiv.” elizabeth abru'teruklar-ru'lut. “lizzy, du bolau ri tor ni. Du bolau ri suspect me. Ish-veh mortifies me. I am perfectly satisfied, s' ra ish-veh manners i' nam-tor, ik au worla had sovek design t' engaging t'nash-veh affection. Ish-veh nam-tor goh ik au nam-tor blessed k' greater sweetness t' shi'yavekh, heh wuh stronger aitlun t' paik pleasing, do sovek vath sasu.” “du nam-tor maut pi-maat'rer, ” leralmin-tor ish-veh ko-kai, “du dungi ri kal-tor me abru'teruklar-ru'lut, heh nam-tor provoking me tor ish-veh kanok moment.” “uf lerash ish-veh nam-tor svi' ein nuf tor nam-tor pudva-tor! [illustration] wuh zamu gad po' nash yaret, mr. Bingley puvutau va'ashiv, heh sa'awek. Ish-veh t'hy'la had losrak ish-veh ik asal na' london, tonk'peh vesh' tor fun ha-kel svi' lehkuh gad’ wak. Au hayal-tor k' au abru' wuh wadan, heh vesh' svi' remarkably rom tam'a. Mrs. Bennet invited ish-veh tor aru-yokul k' au; tonk'peh, k' wehk sagluvaya t' concern, au confessed himself engaged kitok-wilat. “thurai wak du vutau, ” leralmin-tor she, “i rok etek dungau nam-tor weht kunli.” au dang nam-tor wa' kunli na' sovek wak, etc, etc; heh kuv she would mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh trasha, would nem-tor wuh lehkuh-mal opportunity t' waiting fi' au. “mokuhlek sarlah du tor-morrow?” ha, au had rai engagement na' ek' na' tor-morrow; heh ish-veh k'waw'zhe vesh' nar-tor k' alacrity. Sarlah ish-veh, heh svi' such maut rom wak, ik wuh t'sai vesh' rim t' au sai-vel-tor. Svi' sahr-tor mrs. Bennet tor ish-veh daughters’ tvi-shal, svi' ish-veh sai-vel-tor-gown, heh k' ish-veh isachya ulef shahtau, maf-tor si', -- “t'nash-veh tal-kam jane, tor haste heh brax ne'. Au nam-tor sarlah--mr. Bingley nam-tor sarlah. Au nam-tor, indeed. Tor haste, tor haste. La', sarah, sarlah tor din-tor bennet nash moment, heh gol'nev ish-veh fi' k' ish-veh gown. Worla kashek din-tor lizzy’s isachya.” “etek dungi nam-tor ne' u' ak u' etek mokuhlek, ” leralmin-tor jane; “tonk'peh i dare leralmin kitty nam-tor forwarder do either t' etek, na' she went upstairs ulef wuh wadan ago.” “oh! Geldau kitty! Ra has she tor tor k' ish-veh? Sarlah, nam-tor sahris, nam-tor sahris! Wilat nam-tor ish-veh sash, t'nash-veh tal-kam?” tonk'peh lu ish-veh ko-mekh vesh' hal-tor, jane would ri nam-tor fakovau fi' tor hal-tor ne' rik' veh t' ish-veh ko-kai. Wuh ka anxiety tor prah au k' themselves vesh' visible va'ashiv svi' wuh khru. Po' theris-masu, mr. Bennet retired tor wuh shi'dunap, u' vesh' ish-veh custom, heh mary went upstairs tor ish-veh instrument. Dahkuh obstacles t' wuh kaukuh hasu thus snem-tor, mrs. Bennet hayal-tor looking heh winking na' elizabeth heh catherine na' wuh considerable wak, rik' tor sovek impression fi' au. Elizabeth would ri glantau ish-veh; heh lu na' kim-shah kitty did, she maut innocently leralmin-tor, “ra nam-tor wuh tukh, mamma? Ra tor du potau winking na' me na'? Ra am i tor tor?” “nothing, kan, nothing. I did ri wink na' du.” she yi hayal-tor fam dvun kaukuh minutes longer; tonk'peh unable tor thinoi such wuh taluhk occasion, she suddenly prah abru, heh taran tor kitty, -- “sarlah la', t'nash-veh ashaya, i aitlun tor stariben tor du, ” nem-tor ish-veh s' wuh tvi-shal. Jane instantly mazhiv-kur-tor wuh glazhau na' elizabeth if stariben ish-veh flakosh na' such premeditation, heh ish-veh entreaty ik _she_ would ri mazhiv-kur-tor svi' tor ish-veh. Svi' wuh zamu minutes, mrs. Bennet ulef tu'ash wuh svep heh puvutau si', -- “lizzy, t'nash-veh tal-kam, i aitlun tor stariben k' du.” elizabeth vesh' punekwitau tor hal-tor. “etek lau u' muhl trasha au k' themselves, du fai-tor, ” leralmin-tor ish-veh ko-mekh u' ak u' she vesh' svi' wuh tvur. “kitty heh i nam-tor going upstairs tor hayal-tor svi' t'nash-veh sai-vel-tor-tvi-shal.” elizabeth tor rai attempt tor utvau k' ish-veh ko-mekh, tonk'peh hafau quietly svi' wuh tvur till she heh kitty vesh' s' glan, yi fun-tor vi' wuh bestan-tvi-shal. Mrs. Bennet’s schemes na' nash gad vesh' ineffectual. Bingley vesh' kanok-vei ik vesh' sem-rik-tor, kaula wuh professed lover t' ish-veh ko-fu. Ish-veh ease heh cheerfulness rendered ish-veh wuh danik agreeable haya tor ish-veh khru party; heh au spitau k' wuh has-bosh-judged officiousness t' wuh ko-mekh, heh puzhu-tor ek' ish-veh silly remarks k' wuh forbearance heh a'fic t' countenance wa' grateful tor wuh ko-fu. Au scarcely bolau wuh k'waw'zhe tor stay mu'yor-yem; heh fa' au went maf wuh engagement vesh' shidau, chiefly k'fai ish-veh sha' heh mrs. Bennet’s tvai, na' ish-veh coming thurai asal tor pohshau k' ish-veh sa-telsu. Po' nash gad, jane leralmin-tor rai weht t' ish-veh indifference. Ri wuh zhit be' dvun-tor svi' wuh ko-kai fundik bingley; tonk'peh elizabeth went tor sar-tak svi' wuh kunli dva ik ek' bolau speedily nam-tor concluded, vita mr. Darcy fun-tor k'svi wuh fupa s' wak. Seriously, however, she olau tolerably persuaded ik ek' nash bolau ma taken shi k' ik gentleman’s concurrence. Bingley vesh' punctual tor ish-veh latva; heh au heh mr. Bennet spent wuh asal teretuhr, u' had vesh' sep-wafikh fi'. Wuh latter vesh' mau weht agreeable do ish-veh besu gishu. Tra' vesh' nothing t' presumption il folly svi' bingley ik kupi provoke ish-veh ridicule, il spa'ash ish-veh vi' silence; heh au vesh' weht communicative, heh lehkuh rivitanik, do wuh vath had ek'wak gla-tor ish-veh. Bingley veling fun-tor k' ish-veh tor aru-yem; heh svi' wuh khru mrs. Bennet’s fereik-vel vesh' va'ashiv na' ar'kadan tor prah kanok-veh maf s' ish-veh heh ish-veh ko-fu. Elizabeth, vi had wuh nuhm tor kitau, went vi' wuh asal-yem-tvi-shal na' ik lof ak po' theris-masu; na' u' wuh vath vesh' ek' going tor hayal-tor ne' tor nop, she kupi ri nam-tor aitlu tor counteract ish-veh ko-mekh’s schemes. Tonk'peh fi' ish-veh returning tor wuh bestan-tvi-shal, lu ish-veh nuhm vesh' shahtau, gla-tor ish-veh, tor ish-veh vaik ak'wikmun, tra' vesh' utvau tor pthak ik ish-veh ko-mekh had vesh' nuh' ingenious na' ish-veh. Fi' sharu wuh svep, she pakashogau ish-veh ko-kai heh bingley standing teretuhr abru' wuh hearth, u' kuv engaged svi' earnest conversation; heh had nash pufulag-tor tor rai suspicion, wuh limuk t' fi', u' au hastily da-tor pauk heh sadvun-tor tik vath, would ma var-tor ish-veh ek'. _their_ situation vesh' awkward hiyet; tonk'peh _hers_ she nahp vesh' fam dvun weh-rasahkos. Ri wuh zhit-shaya vesh' uttered k' either; heh elizabeth vesh' fi' wuh sfek t' going maf va'ashiv, lu bingley, vi u' muhl u' wuh vath had hayal-tor ne', suddenly she-tor, heh, zhalan wuh zamu zhit tor ish-veh ko-kai, sahr-tor s' wuh tvi-shal. Jane kupi ma rai reserves s' elizabeth, wilat guhl'es would mazhiv-kur-tor sanosh; heh, instantly embracing ish-veh, nafai, k' wuh liveliest zherka, ik she vesh' wuh happiest creature svi' wuh panu. “’tis nuh' mau!” she hau, “k' irak nuh' mau. I ri tor nazh ish-veh. Oh, po nam-tor ri kanok-veh u' kunli?” elizabeth’s congratulations vesh' putan-tor k' wuh sincerity, wuh warmth, wuh delight, if zhit kupi tonk'peh poorly sagluvau. Kanok zhit-bal t' kindness vesh' wuh sluk shu-pal t' happiness tor jane. Tonk'peh she would ri kal-tor herself tor stay k' ish-veh ko-kai, il leralmin ulef ik hafau tor nam-tor leralmin-tor, na' wuh la'. “i bolau hal-tor instantly tor t'nash-veh ko-mekh, ” she maf-tor. “i would ri fi' sovek khrosahp trifle k' ish-veh affectionate solicitude, il kal-tor ish-veh tor zhu-tor ish-veh s' sovek-veh tonk'peh myself. Au nam-tor hal-tor tor t'nash-veh sa-mekh already. Oh, lizzy, tor fai-tor ik ra i ma tor relate dungi mazhiv-kur-tor such sanosh tor ek' t'nash-veh tal-kam skan! Uf dungau i lesh ni mau happiness?” she yi hastened maf tor ish-veh ko-mekh, vi had purposely pushau abru wuh nop-party, heh vesh' sitting upstairs k' kitty. Elizabeth, vi vesh' losrak k' herself, i' abru'teruklar-ru'lut na' wuh rapidity heh ease k' if wuh tek'ik vesh' t'forti settled, ik had putan-tor au ni wehk previous tevun-krus t' suspense heh vexation. “heh nash, ” leralmin-tor she, “nam-tor wuh shaht t' ek' ish-veh t'hy'la’s anxious circumspection! T' ek' ish-veh ko-kai’s falsehood heh contrivance! Wuh happiest, wisest, heh danik reasonable shaht!” svi' wuh zamu minutes she vesh' hau k' bingley, t'vi conference k' ish-veh sa-mekh had vesh' pen heh tor wuh lof. “wilat nam-tor ish-veh ko-kai?” leralmin-tor au hastily, u' au tu'ash wuh svep. “k' t'nash-veh ko-mekh upstairs. She dungi nam-tor ne' svi' wuh moment, i dare leralmin.” au yi ikap-tor wuh svep, heh, coming abru tor ish-veh, claimed wuh rom istau heh affection t' wuh ko-kai. Elizabeth honestly heh heartily sagluvau ish-veh delight svi' wuh prospect t' ish-veh relationship. Au hutau el'ru k' lo'uk cordiality; heh yi, till ish-veh ko-kai sarlah ne', she had tor shroi tor ek' au had tor leralmin t' ish-veh sha' happiness, heh t' jane’s perfections; heh svi' spite t' ish-veh hasu wuh lover, elizabeth really pudva-tor ek' ish-veh gishat t' felicity tor nam-tor rationally founded, fai'ei au had na' i'sav wuh marom understanding heh super-marom disposition t' jane, heh wuh paik similarity t' olaya heh zahvan svi' ish-veh heh himself. Ish-veh vesh' wuh khru t' rai tsuri delight tor au ek'; wuh satisfaction t' din-tor bennet’s kashek mazhiv-kur-tor such wuh min t' slor animation tor ish-veh limuk, u' tor ish-veh glazhau handsomer do ek'wak. Kitty simpered heh abru'teruklar-ru'lut, heh rok-tor ish-veh da-tor vesh' coming ak. Mrs. Bennet kupi ri mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh consent, il stariben ish-veh approbation svi' zhil lamekh hiyet tor satisfy ish-veh feelings, hi she variben tor bingley t' nothing else, na' ulef wuh wadan; heh lu mr. Bennet hau au na' mu'yor-yem, ish-veh spes heh manner plainly gluvau uf really kunli au vesh'. Ri wuh zhit, however, be' dvun-tor ish-veh bru-lar svi' allusion tor ish-veh, till ish-veh visitor nem-tor ish-veh trasha na' wuh mu-yor; tonk'peh u' ak u' au vesh' hal-tor, au da-tor tor ish-veh ko-fu heh leralmin-tor, -- “jane, i congratulate du. Du dungi nam-tor wuh maut kunli kosu.” jane went tor ish-veh instantly, shok-tor ish-veh, heh itaren ish-veh na' ish-veh goodness. “du nam-tor wuh rom ko-kan, ” au kilko-tor, “heh i ma lo'uk sanosh svi' thinking du dungi nam-tor ni kunling settled. I ma ri wuh vet t' ish-veh doing maut muhl teretuhr. Ish-veh tempers nam-tor k' rai tvai rikes. Du nam-tor tik t' du ni complying, ik nothing dungi ek'wak nam-tor resolved fi'; ni hagik, ik kanok dvinsu dungi kravau du; heh ni generous, ik du dungi kwon-hau-ov namautau ish-veh income.” “i rok ri ni. Imprudence il thoughtlessness svi' donku tukh would nam-tor unpardonable svi' _me_.” “namautau ish-veh income! T'nash-veh tal-kam mr. Bennet, ” maf-tor ish-veh ko-telsu, “ra nam-tor du talking t'? Po, au has kehkuh il kaukuh thousand wuh tevun, heh maut kesik weht.” yi addressing ish-veh ko-fu, “oh, t'nash-veh tal-kam, tal-kam jane, i am ni kunli! I am sure i shan’t prah wuh wink t' yuk ek' mu-yor. I fai-tor uf ish-veh would nam-tor. I kwon-hau-ov leralmin-tor ish-veh bolau nam-tor ni, na' kim-shah. I vesh' sure du kupi ri nam-tor ni vaksurik na' nothing! I vokau, u' ak u' ek'wak vesht gla-tor nash-veh ish-veh, lu au wuh'rak sarlah vi' hertfordshire kim-shah tevun, i nahp uf kesik ish-veh vesh' ik du dang sarlah teretuhr. Oh, au nam-tor wuh handsomest nu'ri sasu ik ek'wak vesh' gla-tor!” wickham, lydia, vesh' ek' yen-tor. Jane vesh' mesakh kuhlaya ish-veh favourite kan. Na' ik moment she palutunau rai vath. Ish-veh younger ko-kai ak began tor tor eku'ko k' ish-veh na' vel t' happiness if she lau svi' fa-wak nam-tor kup tor mazhiv-kur-tor. Mary petitioned na' wuh nam-tor-tor t' wuh shi'dunap na' netherfield; heh kitty eit'jae maut lerash na' wuh zamu rin'k'n tra' kanok karil. Bingley, s' nash wak, vesh' veling wuh kanok-gadik visitor na' longbourn; coming frequently fa' asal-yem, heh kwon-hau-ov remaining till po' mu'yor-yem; vita lu ein barbarous behsu, vi kupi ri nam-tor hiyet detested, had putan-tor ish-veh wuh k'waw'zhe tor aru-yem, if au nahp himself obliged tor nar-tor. Elizabeth had i' tonk'peh pi' wak na' conversation k' ish-veh ko-kai; na' du' au vesh' la' jane had rai attention tor bestow fi' sovek-veh else: tonk'peh she afer-tor herself considerably useful tor fi' t' au, svi' eifa wadan t' dahshaya ik bolau sometimes paresh-tor. Svi' wuh k'torr jane, au kwon-hau-ov attached himself tor elizabeth na' wuh sanosh t' talking t' ish-veh; heh lu bingley vesh' hal-tor, jane constantly sought wuh ka tvai t' vas. “au has tor me ni kunli, ” leralmin-tor she, veh khru, “k' telling me ik au vesh' totally ignorant t' t'nash-veh hasu svi' kahr kim-shah sikar! I had ri pudva-tor ish-veh tor-yehat.” “i suspected u' mau, ” kilko-tor elizabeth. “tonk'peh uf did au khrosahp na' ish-veh?” “ish-veh bolau ma vesh' ish-veh ko-kai’ doing. Au vesh' certainly rai t'hylara tor ish-veh acquaintance k' me, if i fam yehat wonder na', opi' au lau ma pudvel-tor ni mau weht advantageously svi' wehk respects. Tonk'peh lu gla-tor au, u' i sahrafel au dungi, ik ish-veh sa-kai nam-tor kunli k' me, au dungi oren-tor tor nam-tor contented, heh etek dungau nam-tor fi' rom zhil va'ashiv: hi etek mokuhlek worla nam-tor ra etek wuh'wak vesh' tor tik vath.” “ik nam-tor wuh danik unforgiving starun, ” leralmin-tor elizabeth, “ik i ek'wak puzhu-tor du utter. Rom ko-kan! Ish-veh would smertau me, indeed, tor gla-tor du va'ashiv wuh dupe t' din-tor bingley’s pretended fudau.” “would du dva-tor ish-veh, lizzy, ik lu au went tor kahr kim-shah november au really ashau me, heh nothing tonk'peh wuh persuasion t' _my_ hasu indifferent would ma prevented ish-veh coming ne' va'ashiv?” “au tor wuh pi' lafosh, tor nam-tor sure; tonk'peh ish-veh nam-tor tor wuh lit t' ish-veh modesty.” nash naturally puragtau wuh panegyric s' jane fi' ish-veh diffidence, heh wuh pi' tala au shitau fi' ish-veh sha' rom qualities. Elizabeth vesh' sanoi tor talal ik au had ri pusvik-tor wuh interference t' ish-veh t'hy'la; na', hi jane had wuh danik generous heh forgiving khaf-spol svi' wuh panu, she fai-tor ish-veh vesh' wuh circumstance if bolau prejudice ish-veh tehnat ish-veh. “i am certainly wuh danik fortunate creature ik ek'wak nam-tor!” maf-tor jane. “oh, lizzy, po am i thus singled s' t'nash-veh skan, heh blessed abru' au ek'? Kuv i kupi tonk'peh gla-tor du u' kunli! Kuv tra' vesh' tonk'peh such wuh'ashiv sasu na' du!” “kuv du vesh' tor mazhiv-kur-tor me keh-leh such sasu i worla kupi nam-tor ni kunli u' du. Till i ma ish-veh disposition, ish-veh goodness, i worla mokuhlek ma ish-veh happiness. Rai, rai, kal-tor me izaya na' myself; heh, sos'eh, kuv i ma maut rom kunli, i lau ragel-tor k' wuh'ashiv mr. Collins svi' wak.” wuh situation t' tek'ik svi' wuh longbourn skan kupi ri nam-tor wu wuh tsat. Mrs. Bennet vesh' privileged tor zhal ish-veh tor mrs. Philips, heh she ventured, rik' sovek permission, tor tor wuh ka k' ek' ish-veh behsu svi' meryton. Wuh bennets vesh' speedily pronounced tor nam-tor wuh luckiest skan svi' wuh panu; hi goh wuh zamu wehk gad fa', lu lydia had wuh'rak sahr-tor maf, au had vesh' paik skan-tor tor nam-tor pu'ulidau si' na' misfortune. [illustration] chapter lvi. [illustration] veh asal, pa' wuh wehk gad po' bingley’s engagement k' jane had vesh' shidau, u' au heh wuh kosu t' wuh skan vesh' sitting teretuhr svi' wuh dining-tvi-shal, ish-veh attention vesh' suddenly drawn tor wuh krani k' wuh ralash t' wuh carriage; heh au pakashogau wuh chaise heh kehkuh driving abru wuh yartra. Ish-veh vesh' nuh' lehkuh-mal svi' wuh asal na' visitors; heh isha, wuh equipage did ri kilko-srashiv tor ik t' sovek t' ish-veh behsu. Wuh jarel vesh' lehk; heh neither wuh carriage, il wuh livery t' wuh dvinsu vi preceded ish-veh, vesh' familiar tor au. U' ish-veh vesh' ac'ruth, however, ik somebody vesh' coming, bingley instantly fakovau fi' din-tor bennet tor nan'woi wuh confinement t' such wuh vi-kwitaya, heh lates maf k' ish-veh vi' wuh tuula. Au fi' eku ska'; heh wuh conjectures t' wuh remaining rehkuh fator, hi k' pi' satisfaction, till wuh svep vesh' lehm-tor tu'ash, heh ish-veh visitor svi-tor. Ish-veh vesh' t'sai catherine de bourgh. Au vesh' veling ek' intending tor nam-tor ak'wikmun: tonk'peh ish-veh astonishment vesh' mesakh ish-veh gishat; heh fi' wuh krus t' mrs. Bennet heh kitty, hi she vesh' perfectly ri-fainu tor au, kauk inferior tor ra elizabeth olau. She svi-tor wuh tvi-shal k' wuh sov weht do usually ungracious, tor rai vath kilko tor elizabeth’s salutation do wuh slight inclination t' wuh patam, heh hayal-tor ne' rik' taran wuh zhit. Elizabeth had mentioned ish-veh ahm tor ish-veh ko-mekh fi' ish-veh ladyship’s entrance, hi rai ya'akash t' ragtaya had vesh' tor. Mrs. Bennet, ek' tauraya, hi snuhkrol-tor k' having wuh be'hai'la t' such pid importance, poprah ish-veh k' wuh utmost politeness. Po' sitting na' wuh moment svi' silence, she leralmin-tor, maut stiffly, tor elizabeth, -- “i rok du nam-tor muhl, din-tor bennet. Ik t'sai, i suppose, nam-tor ish-veh ko-mekh?” elizabeth kilko-tor maut concisely ik she vesh'. “heh _that_, i suppose, nam-tor veh t' ish-veh ko-kai?” “ha, madam, ” leralmin-tor mrs. Bennet, delighted tor stariben tor wuh t'sai catherine. “she nam-tor t'nash-veh youngest ko-kan tonk'peh veh. T'nash-veh youngest t' ek' nam-tor lately telik, heh t'nash-veh eldest nam-tor ein-wilat pa' wuh solektra, walking k' wuh nu'ri sasu, vi, i dva-tor, dungi ak shetau wuh krus t' wuh skan.” “du ma wuh maut pi' shi'sochya la', ” fun-tor t'sai catherine, po' wuh pen silence. “ish-veh nam-tor nothing svi' comparison t' rosings, t'nash-veh t'sai, i dare leralmin; tonk'peh, i assure du, ish-veh nam-tor mau larger do osu william lucas’s.” “nash bolau nam-tor wuh danik inconvenient sitting-tvi-shal na' wuh khru svi' belaar: wuh krani nam-tor bosh tev'rak.” mrs. Bennet assured ish-veh ik au worla hayal-tor tra' po' aru-yem; heh yi hau, -- “sos nem-tor wuh liberty t' asking ish-veh ladyship whether du losrak mr. Heh mrs. Collins muhl?” “ha, maut muhl. Vesht gla-tor nash-veh au wuh mu-yor fa' kim-shah.” elizabeth i' gishu ik she would torvau wuh nuhm na' ish-veh s' charlotte, u' ish-veh seemed wuh goh yesik dvubolek na' ish-veh calling. Tonk'peh rai nuhm saudau, heh she vesh' completely puzzled. Mrs. Bennet, k' lo'uk civility, eit'jae ish-veh ladyship tor nem-tor ein refreshment: tonk'peh t'sai catherine maut resolutely, heh ri maut politely, declined eating sovek-vel; heh yi, rising abru, leralmin-tor tor elizabeth, -- “din-tor bennet, tra' seemed tor nam-tor wuh prettyish ves t' wuh pi' shi'kwai fi' veh vla t' ish-veh yartra. I dang nam-tor glad tor nem-tor wuh da-tor svi' ish-veh, kuv du dungi favour me k' ish-veh apc'koik.” “hal-tor, t'nash-veh tal-kam, ” maf-tor ish-veh ko-mekh, “heh gluvaya ish-veh ladyship pa' wuh natya lates-tor. I nah-tor she dungi nam-tor sanoi k' wuh hermitage.” elizabeth obeyed; heh, sahran vi' ish-veh sha' tvi-shal na' ish-veh parasol, attended ish-veh thol be'hai'la downstairs. U' au be' dvun-tor k'fai wuh tvur, t'sai catherine tu'ash wuh svep vi' wuh dining-parlour heh bestan-tvi-shal, heh pronouncing au, po' wuh pen skothon, tor nam-tor tevan-looking tvi-shal, lates-tor fi'. Ish-veh carriage hafau na' wuh svep, heh elizabeth gla-tor ik ish-veh waiting-kosu vesh' svi' ish-veh. Au proceeded svi' silence bi' wuh krus-kov lates ik pufulag-tor tor wuh pi'laptra; elizabeth vesh' satalau tor tor rai urgam na' conversation k' wuh kosu vi vesh' i' weht do usually insolent heh disagreeable. [illustration: “po' wuh pen skothon” [_copyright 1894 k' george allen._]] “uf sos ek'wak nah-tor ish-veh spo' ish-veh sa-bath?” leralmin-tor she, u' she glazhau svi' ish-veh limuk. U' ak u' au svi-tor wuh pi'laptra, t'sai catherine began svi' wuh zahalik manner: -- “du mokuhlek nam-tor na' rai pak, din-tor bennet, tor ken-tor wuh utvau t' t'nash-veh halovaya hither. Ish-veh sha' khaf-spol, ish-veh sha' conscience, bolau var-tor du po i sarlah.” elizabeth glazhau k' unaffected astonishment. “indeed, du nam-tor mistaken, madam; i ma ri vesh' na' ek' kup tor khrosahp na' wuh dor t' seeing du la'.” “din-tor bennet, ” kilko-tor ish-veh ladyship, svi' wuh reshnek molu, “du ought tor fai-tor ik i am ri tor nam-tor trifled k'. Tonk'peh however insincere _you_ lau dvel-tor tor nam-tor, du dungau ri talal _me_ ni. T'nash-veh character has ek'wak vesh' u'thet na' its sincerity heh frankness; heh svi' wuh aishan t' such moment u' nash, i dungau certainly ri trashu s' ish-veh. Wuh report t' wuh danik alarming malat pulau me dahkuh gad ago. I vesh' var-tor, ik ri goh ish-veh ko-kai vesh' fi' wuh sfek t' hasu danik advantageously telik, tonk'peh ik _you_--ik din-tor elizabeth bennet would, svi' ek' likelihood, nam-tor ak afterwards kaunshuk tor t'nash-veh sa-bath--t'nash-veh sha' sa-bath, mr. Darcy. Hi i _know_ ish-veh bolau nam-tor wuh scandalous falsehood, hi i would ri dash-tor ish-veh ni mau u' tor suppose wuh yeht'es t' ish-veh tor-yehat, i instantly resolved fi' setting ska' na' nash shi, ik i lau tor t'nash-veh sentiments fainu tor du.” “kuv du pudva-tor ish-veh impossible tor nam-tor yeht, ” leralmin-tor elizabeth, colouring k' astonishment heh disdain, “i wonder du nem-tor wuh trouble t' coming ni irak. Ra kupi ish-veh ladyship propose k' ish-veh?” “na' wuh'wak tor insist fi-tor having such wuh report universally contradicted.” “ish-veh coming tor longbourn, tor gla-tor me heh t'nash-veh skan, ” leralmin-tor elizabeth coolly, “dungi nam-tor rather wuh wugaya t' ish-veh--kuv, indeed, such wuh report nam-tor svi' nam.” “kuv! Tor du yi pretend tor nam-tor ignorant t' ish-veh? Has ish-veh ri vesh' industriously da-kuvau k' yourselves? Tor du ri fai-tor ik such wuh report nam-tor sak-tor abroad?” “i worla puzhu-tor ik ish-veh vesh'.” “heh mokuhlek du likewise afsakau, ik tra' nam-tor rai _foundation_ na' ish-veh?” “i ri tor pretend tor ma kaik frankness k' ish-veh ladyship. _you_ lau ya'akash deshkau if _i_ dungau ri dvel-tor tor kilko-srashiv.” “nash nam-tor ri tor nam-tor borne. Din-tor bennet, i insist fi' hasu satisfied. Has au, has t'nash-veh sa-bath, tor du wuh nufai t' kal'i'farr?” “ish-veh ladyship has afsakau ish-veh tor nam-tor impossible.” “ish-veh ought tor nam-tor ni; ish-veh bolau nam-tor ni, du' au retains wuh nam-tor-tor t' ish-veh utvau. Tonk'peh _your_ arts heh allurements lau, svi' wuh moment t' infatuation, ma tor ish-veh yen-tor ra au owes tor himself heh tor ek' ish-veh skan. Du lau ma drawn ish-veh svi'.” “kuv i ma, i dungau nam-tor wuh kim-shah person tor confess ish-veh.” “din-tor bennet, tor du fai-tor vi i am? I ma ri vesh' accustomed tor such gen-lis u' nash. I am siyah wuh nearest relation au has svi' wuh panu, heh am entitled tor fai-tor ek' ish-veh dearest concerns.” “tonk'peh du nam-tor ri entitled tor fai-tor _mine_; il dungi such kloshai u' nash ek'wak vimevilau me tor nam-tor explicit.” “kal-tor me nam-tor rightly ken-tor. Nash match, tor if du ma wuh presumption tor aspire, mokuhlek worla nem-tor shi. Rai, worla. Mr. Darcy nam-tor engaged tor _my daughter_. I', ra ma du tor leralmin?” “goh nash, --ik kuv au nam-tor ni, du mokuhlek ma rai utvau tor suppose au dungi tor wuh nufai tor me.” t'sai catherine hesitated na' wuh moment, heh yi kilko-tor, -- “wuh engagement svi' au nam-tor t' wuh peculiar ves. S' ish-veh infancy, au ma vesh' intended na' tik vath. Ish-veh vesh' wuh favourite istaya t' _his_ ko-mekh, u' muhl u' t' ish-veh. Du' svi' ish-veh cradles etek dotoran wuh union; heh i', na' wuh moment lu wuh istau t' fi' ko-kai would nam-tor accomplished, nam-tor ish-veh kal'i'farr tor nam-tor prevented k' wuh nu'ri kosu t' inferior keshtan, t' rai importance svi' wuh panu, heh wholly unallied tor wuh skan? Tor du vlitau rai fudau tor wuh istau t' ish-veh t'hylara--tor ish-veh tacit engagement k' din-tor de bourgh? Nam-tor du pakik tor kanok olaya t' propriety heh delicacy? Ma du ri puzhu-tor me leralmin, ik s' ish-veh earliest wadan au vesh' destined na' ish-veh krei?” “ha; heh i had puzhu-tor ish-veh fa'. Tonk'peh ra nam-tor ik tor me? Kuv tra' nam-tor rai vath objection tor t'nash-veh marrying ish-veh sa-bath, i dungau certainly ri nam-tor potau s' ish-veh k' fai-tor ik ish-veh ko-mekh heh ezyet istau ish-veh tor marry din-tor de bourgh. Du fi' did u' mau u' du kupi svi' planning wuh kal'i'farr. Its completion nerau fi' vath. Kuv mr. Darcy nam-tor neither k' dor il inclination confined tor ish-veh krei, po nam-tor ri au tor tor wuh'ashiv dvel? Heh kuv i am ik dvel, po lau ri i nar-tor ish-veh?” “fai'ei dor, decorum, prudence--nay, eku'ko--zadau ish-veh. Ha, din-tor bennet, eku'ko; na' ri tor gish tor nam-tor pubeglanau k' ish-veh skan il t'hylara, kuv du wilfully bae'cok tehnat wuh inclinations t' ek'. Du dungi nam-tor censured, slighted, heh despised, k' kanok-veh tersau k' ish-veh. Ish-veh alliance dungi nam-tor wuh disgrace; ish-veh ahm dungi worla kauk nam-tor mentioned k' sovek t' etek.” “aifa nam-tor ras misfortunes, ” kilko-tor elizabeth. “tonk'peh wuh ko-telsu t' mr. Darcy bolau ma such wehtsuri shu-pal t' happiness necessarily attached tor ish-veh situation, ik she kupi, fi-tor wuh bosh, ma rai aishan tor repine.” “obstinate, headstrong ko-kan! I am kafusik t' du! Nam-tor nash ish-veh gratitude na' t'nash-veh attentions tor du kim-shah sikar? Nam-tor nothing due tor me fi' ik nosahp? Kal-tor etek hayal-tor ne'. Du nam-tor tor ken-tor, din-tor bennet, ik vesht sarlah nash-veh la' k' wuh satalau resolution t' carrying t'nash-veh lof; il dungi i nam-tor dissuaded s' ish-veh. I ma ri vesh' nam-tor-tor tor nekhau tor sovek person’s whims. I ma ri vesh' svi' wuh es'merka t' brooking disappointment.” “_that_ dungi tor ish-veh ladyship’s situation na' la' weht pitiable; tonk'peh ish-veh dungi ma rai daya fi' _me_.” “i dungi ri nam-tor svi-shau! Zhu-tor me svi' silence. T'nash-veh ko-fu heh t'nash-veh sa-bath nam-tor shidau na' tik vath. Au nam-tor tev-tor, fi' wuh maternal vla, s' wuh ka thol zehl; heh, fi' wuh sa-mekh’s, s' respectable, dorli, heh t'kahr, hi untitled, skan. Ish-veh fortune fi' fi' vla nam-tor splendid. Au nam-tor destined na' tik vath k' wuh spes t' kanok kisau t' ish-veh respective kelek; heh ra nam-tor tor dahsaya au?--wuh upstart pretensions t' wuh nu'ri kosu rik' skan, tersaya, il fortune! Nam-tor nash tor nam-tor palesh-tor? Tonk'peh ish-veh bolau ri, dungau ri nam-tor! Kuv du vesh' sensible t' ish-veh sha' rom, du would ri istaya tor quit wuh ek'kal svi' if du ma vesh' katau abru.” “svi' marrying ish-veh sa-bath, i dang ri panah-tor myself u' quitting ik ek'kal. Au nam-tor wuh gentleman; i am wuh gentleman’s ko-fu; ni irak etek nam-tor kaik.” “yeht. Du _are_ wuh gentleman’s ko-fu. Tonk'peh ra vesh' ish-veh ko-mekh? Vi nam-tor ish-veh sa-kuk heh ezyet? Ri tor glenonau me ignorant t' ish-veh nosh.” “whatever t'nash-veh tersaya lau nam-tor, ” leralmin-tor elizabeth, “kuv ish-veh sa-bath tor ri vel tor au, au mokuhlek nam-tor nothing tor _you_.” “var-tor me, wuh'wak na' ek', nam-tor du engaged tor ish-veh?” hi elizabeth would ri, na' wuh mere lof t' obliging t'sai catherine, ma kilko-tor nash deshker, she kupi ri tonk'peh leralmin, po' wuh moment’s deliberation, -- “i am ri.” t'sai catherine seemed sanoi. “heh dungi du ugaya me worla tor svi-tor vi' such wuh engagement?” “i dungi tor rai ugaya t' wuh ves.” “din-tor bennet, i am kolaya heh astonished. I gishu tor talal wuh weht reasonable nu'ri kosu. Tonk'peh ri tor tehs-tor yourself vi' wuh dva ik i dungi ek'wak satrasha. I dungau ri hal-tor maf till du ma putan-tor me wuh assurance i require.” “heh i certainly _never_ dungau mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh. I am ri tor nam-tor intimidated vi' sovek-vel ni wholly unreasonable. Ish-veh ladyship aitlu mr. Darcy tor marry ish-veh ko-fu; tonk'peh would t'nash-veh giving du wuh istau-na' ugaya tor _their_ kal'i'farr na' ek' weht yesik? Supposing ish-veh tor nam-tor attached tor me, would _my_ refusing tor nar-tor ish-veh el'ru tor ish-veh istaya tor bestow ish-veh fi' ish-veh krei? Kal-tor me tor leralmin, t'sai catherine, ik wuh nerau-kek-vuhnayek k' if du ma nenikau nash wehtsuri application ma vesh' u' frivolous u' wuh application vesh' has-bosh-judged. Du ma widely mistaken t'nash-veh character, kuv du nah-tor i mokuhlek nam-tor ar'kada fi' k' such persuasions u' aifa. Uf irak ish-veh sa-bath lau messau t' ish-veh interference svi' _his_ tek'ik, i fam yehat var-tor; tonk'peh du ma certainly rai gas'rak tor concern yourself svi' t'nash-veh. I bolau eit'jae, therefore, tor nam-tor importuned rai further fi' wuh subject.” “ri ni hasty, kuv du sanoi. I ma k' rai tvai ovsoh. Tor ek' wuh objections i ma already urged i ma fam dvun wuh'ashiv tor hau. I am rai ri-fainusu tor wuh particulars t' ish-veh youngest ko-kai’s infamous elopement. I fai-tor ish-veh ek'; ik wuh nu'ri sasu’s marrying ish-veh vesh' wuh patched-abru business, na' wuh kodona t' ish-veh sa-mekh heh sa-kuk. Heh nam-tor _such_ wuh ko-kan tor nam-tor t'nash-veh sa-bath’s ko-kai? Nam-tor _her_ sa-telsu, vi nam-tor wuh sa-fu t' ish-veh tab-ma sa-mekh’s steward, tor nam-tor ish-veh sa-kai? Sha-ka-ri heh terra!--t' ra nam-tor du thinking? Nam-tor wuh duvek-tor t' pemberley tor nam-tor thus flau?” “du mokuhlek _now_ ma nothing further tor leralmin, ” she resentfully kilko-tor. “du ma insulted me, svi' kanok tor-yehat method. I bolau eit'jae tor fun tor wuh kelek.” heh she she-tor u' she stariben. T'sai catherine she-tor isha, heh au da-tor pla'. Ish-veh ladyship vesh' highly incensed. “du ma rai fudau, yi, na' wuh dor heh lit t' t'nash-veh sa-bath! Unfeeling, selfish ko-kan! Tor du ri panah-tor ik wuh tersaya k' du bolau disgrace ish-veh svi' wuh bezhun t' kanok-veh?” “t'sai catherine, i ma nothing further tor leralmin. Du fai-tor t'nash-veh sentiments.” “du nam-tor yi resolved ki' ish-veh?” “i ma leralmin-tor rai such vel. I am goh resolved tor bae'cok svi' ik manner, if dungi, svi' t'nash-veh sha' opinion, constitute t'nash-veh happiness, rik' dzhinaya tor _you_, il tor sovek person ni wholly unconnected k' me.” “ish-veh nam-tor muhl. Du klee'fah, yi, tor oblige me. Du klee'fah tor obey wuh claims t' gu-vam, dor, heh gratitude. Du nam-tor satalau tor ruin ish-veh svi' wuh opinion t' ek' ish-veh t'hylara, heh tor ish-veh wuh contempt t' wuh panu.” “neither gu-vam, il dor, il gratitude, ” kilko-tor elizabeth, “has sovek tor-yehat claim fi' me, svi' wuh la' instance. Rai dvatai t' either would nam-tor violated k' t'nash-veh kal'i'farr k' mr. Darcy. Heh k' fudau tor wuh resentment t' ish-veh skan, il wuh indignation t' wuh panu, kuv wuh former _were_ teporilau k' ish-veh marrying me, ish-veh would ri mazhiv-kur-tor me veh moment’s concern--heh wuh panu svi' paik would ma nuh' mau kash-ral tor hau svi' wuh scorn.” “heh nash nam-tor ish-veh yeht opinion! Nash nam-tor ish-veh kim-shah resolve! Maut muhl. I dungau i' fai-tor uf tor bae'cok. Ri tor glenonau, din-tor bennet, ik ish-veh ambition dungi ek'wak nam-tor gratified. Vesht sarlah nash-veh tor ar'kadan du. I rok-tor tor talal du reasonable; tonk'peh nerau fi-tor ish-veh i dungi lesh t'nash-veh sfek.” svi' nash manner t'sai catherine variben fi' till au vesh' na' wuh svep t' wuh carriage, lu, turning hastily pauk, she hau, -- “i nem-tor rai trasha t' du, din-tor bennet. I satau rai compliments tor ish-veh ko-mekh. Du nazh rai such attention. I am danik seriously displeased.” elizabeth tor rai kilko-srashiv; heh rik' attempting tor persuade ish-veh ladyship tor fun vi' wuh kelek, lates-tor quietly vi' ish-veh herself. She puzhu-tor wuh carriage yetur maf u' she proceeded upstairs. Ish-veh ko-mekh impatiently ragel-tor ish-veh na' wuh svep t' ish-veh sai-vel-tor-tvi-shal, tor ya'akash po t'sai catherine would ri sarlah svi' va'ashiv heh shom herself. “she did ri dvel-tor ish-veh, ” leralmin-tor ish-veh ko-fu; “she would hal-tor.” “she nam-tor wuh maut tok-ti-looking kosu! Heh ish-veh calling la' vesh' prodigiously civil! Na' she goh sarlah, i suppose, tor var-tor etek wuh collinses vesh' muhl. She nam-tor fi' ish-veh fau-yut ein-wilat, i dare leralmin; heh ni, be' dvun-tor k'fai meryton, nahp she lau u' muhl vutau fi' du. I suppose she had nothing particular tor leralmin tor du, lizzy?” elizabeth vesh' punekwitau tor mazhiv-kur-tor svi' tor wuh pi' falsehood la'; na' tor nafai-tor wuh substance t' ish-veh conversation vesh' impossible. [illustration: “tonk'peh i' ish-veh sasarlah” ] chapter lvii. [illustration] wuh discomposure t' tam'a if nash wehtsuri yaret threw elizabeth vi' kupi ri nam-tor easily overcome; il kupi she na' wehk wadan oren-tor tor nah-tor t' ish-veh lehkuh tor incessantly. T'sai catherine, ish-veh saudau, had actually taken wuh trouble t' nash halovaya s' rosings na' wuh lad lof t' breaking ska' ish-veh supposed engagement k' mr. Darcy. Ish-veh vesh' wuh rational scheme, tor nam-tor sure! Tonk'peh s' ra wuh report t' ish-veh engagement kupi tveshulau, elizabeth vesh' na' wuh pak tor glenonau; till she recollected ik _his_ hasu wuh intimate t'hy'la t' bingley, heh _her_ hasu wuh ko-kai t' jane, vesh' hiyet, na' wuh wak lu wuh gishat t' veh wedding tor kanok-veh nayik na' wuh'ashiv, tor tanilau wuh idea. She had ri herself yen-tor tor olau ik wuh kal'i'farr t' ish-veh ko-kai bolau katau au weht frequently teretuhr. Heh ish-veh behsu na' lucas lodge, therefore, (na' k'fai ish-veh sviribaya k' wuh collinses, wuh report, she concluded, had pulau t'sai catherine, ) had goh eku _that_ ne' u' siyah ac'ruth heh iyi if _she_ had glazhau fa'rak tor u' tor-yehat na' ein fa-wak wak. Svi' revolving t'sai catherine’s sagluvaya, however, she kupi ri gol'nev olaya ein uneasiness u' tor wuh tor-yehat consequence t' ish-veh persisting svi' nash interference. S' ra she had leralmin-tor t' ish-veh resolution tor prevent wuh kal'i'farr, ish-veh paresh-tor tor elizabeth ik she bolau meditate wuh application tor ish-veh sa-bath; heh uf au lau nem-tor wuh kahwa representation t' wuh ek'rasah attached tor wuh tersaya k' ish-veh she dared ri pronounce. She fai-tor ri wuh faikaik degree t' ish-veh affection na' ish-veh ezyet, il ish-veh dependence fi' ish-veh judgment, tonk'peh ish-veh vesh' malatik tor suppose ik au nahp mau higher t' ish-veh ladyship do _she_ kupi tor; heh ish-veh vesh' ac'ruth, ik svi' enumerating wuh miseries t' wuh kal'i'farr k' _one_ t'vi iyi tersaya vesh' ni unequal tor ish-veh sha', ish-veh ezyet would shi'yavekh ish-veh fi' ish-veh weakest vla. K' ish-veh notions t' dignity, au would probably olau ik wuh nerau-kek-vuhnayek, if tor elizabeth had saudau kobat heh ridiculous, tuhlau mau rom kash-ral heh huhtik reasoning. Kuv au had vesh' wavering fa', u' tor ra au dang tor, if had k'ashiv seemed kesik, wuh na'shikh heh entreaty t' ni be' wuh relation lau settle kanok vet, heh satalau ish-veh na' wuh'wak tor nam-tor u' kunli u' dignity unblemished kupi tor ish-veh. Svi' ik nuf au would fun rai weht. T'sai catherine lau gla-tor ish-veh svi' ish-veh yut k'fai kahr; heh ish-veh engagement tor bingley t' coming va'ashiv tor netherfield bolau mazhiv-kur-tor yut. “kuv, therefore, wuh tobeg na' ri keeping ish-veh ugaya dang sarlah tor ish-veh t'hy'la k'svi wuh zamu gad, ” she hau, “i dungau fai-tor uf tor ken-tor ish-veh. I dungau yi mazhiv-kur-tor abru' kanok gishat, kanok istaya t' ish-veh constancy. Kuv au nam-tor satisfied k' goh regretting me, lu au lau ma prah t'nash-veh affections heh el'ru, i dungau ak cease tor regret ish-veh na' ek'.” wuh ak'wikmun t' wuh shom t' wuh skan, fi' khaf-spol vi ish-veh visitor had vesh', vesh' maut lo'uk: tonk'peh au obligingly satisfied ish-veh k' wuh ka ves t' supposition if had appeased mrs. Bennet’s curiosity; heh elizabeth vesh' spared s' mau teasing fi' wuh subject. Wuh thurai asal, u' she vesh' going ne' kaiden, she vesh' ragel-tor k' ish-veh sa-mekh, vi sasarlah t' ish-veh shi'dunap k' wuh nuhm svi' ish-veh el'ru. “lizzy, ” leralmin-tor au, “i vesh' going tor glazhau na' du: sarlah vi' t'nash-veh tvi-shal.” she zahal-tor ish-veh thither; heh ish-veh curiosity tor fai-tor ra au had tor var-tor ish-veh vesh' heightened k' wuh supposition t' its hasu svi' ein manner tersau k' wuh nuhm au meskarau. Ish-veh suddenly kwul-tor ish-veh ik ish-veh lau nam-tor s' t'sai catherine, heh she anticipated k' dismay ek' wuh consequent danaya. She zahal-tor ish-veh sa-mekh tor wuh yon-sha'ti, heh au fi' hayal-tor ne'. Au yi leralmin-tor, -- “i ma poprah wuh nuhm nash asal ik has astonished me exceedingly. U' ish-veh principally concerns yourself, du ought tor fai-tor its tuhllar. I did ri fai-tor fa' ik i had _two_ daughters fi' wuh rihk t' matrimony. Kal-tor me congratulate du fi' wuh maut yauluhk conquest.” wuh kur i' rushed vi' elizabeth’s nak svi' wuh instantaneous conviction t' its hasu wuh nuhm s' wuh sa-bath, instead t' wuh ezyet; heh she vesh' undetermined whether danik tor nam-tor sanoi ik au danau himself na' ek', il puthrap-tor ik ish-veh nuhm vesh' ri rather addressed tor herself, lu ish-veh sa-mekh fator, -- “du glazhau d'wonil. Nu'ri t'sai ma lo'uk penetration svi' such tukh u' aifa; tonk'peh i nah-tor i lau defy kauk _your_ sagacity tor discover wuh ahm t' ish-veh admirer. Nash nuhm nam-tor s' mr. Collins.” “s' mr. Collins! Heh ra mokuhlek _he_ ma tor leralmin?” “vel maut mau tor wuh lof, veling. Au palikau k' congratulations fi' wuh approaching nuptials t' t'nash-veh eldest ko-fu, t' if, ish-veh seems, au has vesh' var-tor k' ein t' wuh rom-natured, gossiping lucases. I dungau ri torvukh k' ish-veh impatience k' telvan ra au leralmin-tor fi' ik sfek. Ra relates tor yourself nam-tor u' zahal-tor: --‘having thus nufau du wuh sincere congratulations t' mrs. Collins heh myself fi' nash kunli pavek, kal-tor me i' hau wuh pen hint fi' wuh subject t' wuh'ashiv, t' if etek ma vesh' advertised k' wuh ka ek'te'kru. Ish-veh ko-fu elizabeth, ish-veh nam-tor presumed, dungi ri wu lesh wuh ahm t' bennet, po' ish-veh eldest ko-kai has resigned ish-veh; heh wuh pudvel-tor tersu t' ish-veh buk lau nam-tor reasonably glazhau abru tor u' veh t' wuh danik illustrious personages svi' nash solektra.’ mokuhlek du possibly guess, lizzy, vi nam-tor tvai k' nash? ‘nash nu'ri gentleman nam-tor blessed, svi' wuh peculiar yut, k' kanok-vei wuh khaf-spol t' mortal mokuhlek danik aitlun, --splendid veltra, thol kindred, heh extensive patronage. Wi, svi' spite t' ek' aifa temptations, kal-tor me vikau t'nash-veh krei elizabeth, heh yourself, t' ra ek'rasah du lau incur k' wuh precipitate closure k' nash gentleman’s mnah, if, veling, du dungi nam-tor vul-tor tor nem-tor iyi advantage t'.’ ma du sovek idea, lizzy, vi nash gentleman nam-tor? Tonk'peh i' ish-veh sasarlah. ‘t'nash-veh dvubolek na' cautioning du nam-tor u' zahal-tor: --etek ma utvau tor glenonau ik ish-veh ezyet, t'sai catherine de bourgh, tor ri glazhau fi' wuh match k' wuh friendly bezhun.’ _mr. Darcy_, gla-tor du, nam-tor wuh sasu! I', lizzy, i nah-tor i _have_ ak'wikmun du. Kupi au, il wuh lucases, ma pitched fi' sovek sasu, k'svi wuh da-kuv t' etwel acquaintance, t'vi ahm would ma putan-tor wuh ti weht effectually tor ra au related? Mr. Darcy, vi worla glazhau na' sovek kosu tonk'peh tor gla-tor wuh blemish, heh vi probably worla glazhau na' _you_ svi' ish-veh ha'kiv! Ish-veh nam-tor admirable!” elizabeth ar'kada tor hau svi' ish-veh sa-mekh’s pleasantry, tonk'peh kupi goh nekwitaya veh danik reluctant abru'teruklar-ru'lut. Worla had ish-veh wit vesh' khartau svi' wuh manner ni pi' agreeable tor ish-veh. “nam-tor du ri matau?” “oh, ha. Pray telv-tor fi'.” “‘po' mentioning wuh likelihood t' nash kal'i'farr tor ish-veh ladyship kim-shah mu-yor, she iyi, k' ish-veh tsuri condescension, sagluvau ra she olau fi' wuh occasion; lu ish-veh became apparent, ik, fi' wuh nosahp t' ein skan objections fi' wuh krus t' t'nash-veh krei, she would worla mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh consent tor ra she termed ni disgraceful wuh match. I nahp ish-veh t'nash-veh gu-vam tor mazhiv-kur-tor wuh speediest kash-tor'es t' nash tor t'nash-veh krei, ik she heh ish-veh thol admirer lau nam-tor aware t' ra au nam-tor pa', heh ri sahr-tor hastily vi' wuh kal'i'farr if has ri vesh' properly sanctioned.’ mr. Collins, moreover, hau, ‘i am truly rejoiced ik t'nash-veh krei lydia’s maf business has vesh' ni muhl hushed abru, heh am goh concerned ik ish-veh living teretuhr fa' wuh kal'i'farr nem-tor shi dang nam-tor ni paik fainu. I bolau ri, however, neglect wuh gu-vam t' t'nash-veh wurzel, il refrain s' declaring t'nash-veh tauraya, na' khaf-spol ik du poprah wuh nu'ri couple vi' ish-veh kelek u' ak u' au vesh' telik. Ish-veh vesh' wuh kastoraya t' vice; heh had i vesh' wuh rector t' longbourn, i dang maut strenuously ma opposed ish-veh. Du ought certainly tor forgive au u' wuh christian, tonk'peh worla tor nafai-tor au svi' ish-veh glan, il kal-tor ish-veh ahm tor nam-tor mentioned svi' ish-veh khaf-spol.’ _that_ nam-tor ish-veh notion t' christian thrap-fam'es nufau! Wuh shom t' ish-veh nuhm nam-tor goh pa' ish-veh tal-kam charlotte’s situation, heh ish-veh gishat t' wuh nu'ri olive-khlup. Tonk'peh, lizzy, du glazhau u' kuv du did ri tizh-tor ish-veh. Du nam-tor ri going tor nam-tor _missish_, i rok, heh pretend tor nam-tor affronted na' wuh idle report. Na' ra tor etek ha-tor, tonk'peh tor tor torvukh na' etwel behsu, heh abru'teruklar-ru'lut na' au svi' etwel da-tor?” “oh, ” maf-tor elizabeth, “i am exceedingly matau. Tonk'peh ish-veh nam-tor ni flekh!” “ha, _that_ nam-tor ra tor ish-veh tzlu'pd. Had au teslau fi' sovek vath sasu ish-veh would ma vesh' nothing; tonk'peh _his_ buhfik indifference heh _your_ sfekau ritishaya tor ish-veh ni delightfully absurd! Mau u' i abominate kitaun, i would ri mazhiv-kur-tor abru mr. Collins’s correspondence na' sovek consideration. Nay, lu i telv-tor wuh nuhm t' ish-veh, i fam yehat gol'nev giving ish-veh wuh preference kauk abru' wickham, mau u' i tala wuh impudence heh hypocrisy t' t'nash-veh sa-fu-svi'-tor-gav. Heh pray, lizzy, ra leralmin-tor t'sai catherine pa' nash report? Did she vutau tor klee'fah ish-veh consent?” tor nash deshker ish-veh ko-fu kilko-tor goh k' wuh abru'teruklar-ru'lut; heh u' ish-veh had vesh' ya'akash rik' wuh least suspicion, she vesh' ri flakosh k' ish-veh repeating ish-veh. Elizabeth had worla vesh' weht na' wuh pak tor tor ish-veh feelings saudau ra au vesh' ri. Ish-veh vesh' bolayatik tor abru'teruklar-ru'lut lu she would rather ma maf-tor. Ish-veh sa-mekh had danik cruelly mortified ish-veh k' ra au leralmin-tor t' mr. Darcy’s indifference; heh she kupi tor nothing tonk'peh wonder na' such wuh aitlun t' penetration, il pthak ik, sos'eh, instead t' ish-veh seeing nuh' _little_, she lau ma fancied nuh' _much_. [illustration: “wuh urgam t' ish-veh ezyet” [_copyright 1894 k' george allen._]] chapter lviii. [illustration] instead t' receiving sovek such nuhm t' tobeg s' ish-veh t'hy'la, u' elizabeth ulef gishu mr. Bingley tor tor, au vesh' kup tor katau darcy k' ish-veh tor longbourn fa' wehk gad had be' dvun-tor po' t'sai catherine’s yaret. Wuh gentlemen lasha lehkuh-mal; heh, fa' mrs. Bennet had wak tor var-tor ish-veh t' ish-veh having gla-tor ish-veh ezyet, t' if ish-veh ko-fu hayal-tor svi' momentary dread, bingley, vi aitlu tor nam-tor sa'awek k' jane, proposed ish-veh ek' walking si'. Ish-veh vesh' sep-wafikh tor. Mrs. Bennet vesh' ri svi' wuh es'merka t' walking, mary kupi worla spare wak, tonk'peh wuh remaining kaukuh eku ska' teretuhr. Bingley heh jane, however, ak kal-tor wuh vath tor outstrip au. Au lagged za', du' elizabeth, kitty, heh darcy vesh' tor entertain tik vath. Maut pi' vesh' leralmin-tor k' either; kitty vesh' nuh' mau kwes t' ish-veh tor variben; elizabeth vesh' secretly forming wuh desperate resolution; heh, sos'eh, au lau nam-tor doing wuh ka. Au lates-tor na' wuh lucases’, fai'ei kitty istau tor vutau fi-tor maria; heh u' elizabeth gla-tor rai occasion na' tor ish-veh wuh paik concern, lu kitty losrak au she went boldly fi' k' ish-veh sa'awek. I' vesh' wuh moment na' ish-veh resolution tor nam-tor fitor; heh du' ish-veh courage vesh' pid, she iyi leralmin-tor, -- “mr. Darcy, i am wuh maut selfish creature, heh na' wuh sake t' giving vas tor t'nash-veh sha' feelings tun ri uf mau i lau nam-tor wounding ish-veh. I mokuhlek rai longer gol'nev thanking du na' ish-veh unexampled kindness tor t'nash-veh ri donku-tor ko-kai. Ek'wak opi' i ma fainu ish-veh i ma vesh' danik anxious tor nafai-tor tor du uf gratefully i olau ish-veh. Vesh' ish-veh fainu tor wuh shom t' t'nash-veh skan i dang ri ma goh t'nash-veh sha' gratitude tor sagluvau.” “ni'droi'ik nar-tor, exceedingly sorry, ” kilko-tor darcy, svi' wuh molu t' ak'wikmun heh zherka, “ik du ma ek'wak vesh' informed t' ra lau, svi' wuh mistaken ta'hal, ma putan-tor du uneasiness. I did ri nah-tor mrs. Gardiner vesh' ni pi' tor nam-tor trusted.” “du bolau ri tenai t'nash-veh ezyet. Lydia’s thoughtlessness wuh'rak pusvik-tor tor me ik du had vesh' concerned svi' wuh tukh; heh, veling, i kupi ri shom till i fai-tor wuh particulars. Kal-tor me nemaiyo va'ashiv heh va'ashiv, svi' wuh ahm t' ek' t'nash-veh skan, na' ik generous utan'es if vimevilau du tor nem-tor ni mau trouble, heh lesh ni wehk mortifications, na' wuh sake t' discovering au.” “kuv du _will_ itaren me, ” au kilko-tor, “kal-tor ish-veh nam-tor na' yourself sa'awek. Ik wuh istaya t' giving happiness tor du lau hau nekwitaya tor wuh vath inducements if pufulag-tor me fi', i dungau ri attempt tor wafu. Tonk'peh ish-veh _family_ owe me nothing. Mau u' i respect au, i dva-tor i nahp goh t' _you_.” elizabeth vesh' nuh' mau embarrassed tor leralmin wuh zhit. Po' wuh pen svizh, ish-veh besu hau, “du nam-tor nuh' generous tor trifle k' me. Kuv ish-veh feelings nam-tor fam dvun ra au vesh' kim-shah april, var-tor me ni na' wuh'wak. _my_ affections heh istau nam-tor unchanged; tonk'peh veh zhit s' du dungi silence me fi' nash subject na' ek'wak.” elizabeth, olaya ek' wuh weht do tsuri awkwardness heh anxiety t' ish-veh situation, i' punekwitau herself tor stariben; heh iyi, hi ri maut fluently, mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh tor ken-tor ik ish-veh sentiments had undergone ni tukh wuh rubah opi' wuh wak-krus tor if au alluded, u' tor tor ish-veh poprah k' gratitude heh sanosh ish-veh la' assurances. Wuh happiness if nash kilko torvau vesh' such u' au had probably worla olau fa'; heh au sagluvau himself fi' wuh occasion u' sensibly heh u' warmly u' wuh sasu violently svi' ashaya mokuhlek nam-tor supposed tor tor. Had elizabeth vesh' kup tor snagel ish-veh bezhun, she lau ma gla-tor uf muhl wuh sagluvaya t' heartfelt delight sas-tor abru' ish-veh limuk became ish-veh: tonk'peh hi she kupi ri glazhau she kupi shroi; heh au var-tor ish-veh t' feelings if, svi' proving t' ra importance she vesh' tor ish-veh, tor ish-veh affection kanok moment weht taluhk. Au lates-tor fi' rik' fai-tor svi' ra kharat. Tra' vesh' nuh' mau tor nam-tor nahp, heh olau, heh leralmin-tor, na' attention tor sovek vath vel. She ak oren-tor ik au vesh' indebted na' ish-veh la' rom understanding tor wuh urgam t' ish-veh ezyet, vi _did_ vutau fi' ish-veh svi' ish-veh fun k'fai london, heh tra' relate ish-veh halovaya tor longbourn, its dvubolek, heh wuh substance t' ish-veh conversation k' elizabeth; kelek emphatically fi' kanok sagluvaya t' wuh latter, if, svi' ish-veh ladyship’s apprehension, peculiarly denoted ish-veh perverseness heh assurance, svi' wuh dva ik such wuh relation bolau gol-tor ish-veh endeavours tor prah ik ugaya s' ish-veh sa-bath if _she_ had klee'fah tor mazhiv-kur-tor. Tonk'peh, unluckily na' ish-veh ladyship, its daya had vesh' exactly contrariwise. “ish-veh saven-tor me tor rok, ” leralmin-tor au, “u' i had scarcely ek'wak kal-tor myself tor rok fa'. I fai-tor hiyet t' ish-veh disposition tor nam-tor ac'ruth, ik had du vesh' absolutely, irrevocably klopau tehnat me, du would ma nafai ish-veh tor t'sai catherine frankly heh openly.” elizabeth kur-tor heh abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor u' she kilko-tor, “ha, du fai-tor hiyet t' t'nash-veh _frankness_ tor dva-tor me capable t' _that_. Po' abusing du ni abominably tor ish-veh limuk, i kupi ma rai scruple svi' abusing du tor ek' ish-veh relations.” “ra did du leralmin t' me ik i did ri nazh? Na' hi ish-veh accusations vesh' has-bosh-founded, shidau fi' mistaken premises, t'nash-veh kloshai tor du na' wuh wak had merited wuh severest reproof. Ish-veh vesh' unpardonable. I fam yehat nah-tor t' ish-veh rik' abhorrence.” “etek dungi ri quarrel na' wuh greater thresh t' tenai annexed tor ik khru, ” leralmin-tor elizabeth. “wuh spa-tor t' neither, kuv strictly linisau, dungi nam-tor irreproachable; tonk'peh opi' yi etek ma fi', i rok, improved svi' civility.” “i fam yehat nam-tor ni easily reconciled tor myself. Wuh recollection t' ra i yi leralmin-tor, t' t'nash-veh spa-tor, t'nash-veh manners, t'nash-veh sagluvaya du' wuh bosh t' ish-veh, nam-tor i', heh has vesh' wehk tevun-krus, inexpressibly kusut-tor tor me. Ish-veh reproof, ni muhl applied, i dungau worla yen-tor: ‘had du behaved svi' wuh weht gentlemanlike manner.’ eifa vesh' ish-veh zhit. Du fai-tor ri, du mokuhlek scarcely conceive, uf au ma tortured me; hi ish-veh vesh' ein wak, i confess, fa' i vesh' reasonable hiyet tor kal-tor ish-veh yeht-gav.” “i vesh' certainly maut irak s' expecting au tor tor ni karik wuh impression. I had ri wuh smallest idea t' ish-veh hasu ek'wak olau svi' such wuh yut.” “i mokuhlek easily dva-tor ish-veh. Du nahp me yi devoid t' kanok proper olaya, i am sure du did. Wuh da-tor t' ish-veh countenance i dungau worla yen-tor, u' du leralmin-tor ik i kupi ri ma addressed du svi' sovek tor-yehat yut ik would vimevilau du tor nar-tor me.” “oh, ri tor ashiv-tor ra i yi leralmin-tor. Aifa recollections dungi ri tor na' ek'. I assure du ik i ma wu vesh' danik heartily kafusik t' ish-veh.” darcy mentioned ish-veh nuhm. “did ish-veh, ” leralmin-tor au, --“did ish-veh _soon_ tor du nah-tor weh-rom t' me? Did du, fi' telvan ish-veh, mazhiv-kur-tor sovek lit tor its tuhllar?” she danau ra its daya fi' ish-veh had vesh', heh uf gradually ek' ish-veh former prejudices had vesh' snem-tor. “i fai-tor, ” leralmin-tor au, “ik ra i kitau bolau mazhiv-kur-tor du kusut, tonk'peh ish-veh vesh' bolayatik. I rok du ma vashau wuh nuhm. Tra' vesh' veh krus, wa' wuh sharu t' ish-veh, if i dang dread ish-veh having wuh tepul t' telvan va'ashiv. I mokuhlek vokau ein sagluvaya if lau justly tor du fnu-ven me.” “wuh nuhm dungau certainly nam-tor yontau, kuv du dva-tor ish-veh bolayatik tor wuh preservation t' t'nash-veh fudau; tonk'peh, hi etek ma fi' utvau tor nah-tor t'nash-veh opinions ri entirely unalterable, au nam-tor ri, i rok, ved ni easily rubai u' ik implies.” “lu i kitau ik nuhm, ” kilko-tor darcy, “i pudva-tor myself perfectly hayal heh samuyau; tonk'peh i am opi' convinced ik ish-veh vesh' written svi' wuh dreadful bitterness t' tam'a.” “wuh nuhm, sos'eh, began svi' bitterness, tonk'peh ish-veh did ri shaht ni. Wuh adieu nam-tor charity itself. Tonk'peh nah-tor rai weht t' wuh nuhm. Wuh feelings t' wuh person vi kitau heh wuh person vi poprah ish-veh nam-tor i' ni widely natya s' ra au vesh' yi, ik kanok unpleasant circumstance attending ish-veh ought tor nam-tor yen-tor. Du bolau oren-tor ein t' t'nash-veh ven-dol-leralmin. Nah-tor goh t' wuh vesht u' its remembrance mazhiv-kur-tor du sanosh.” “i fam yehat mazhiv-kur-tor du lit na' sovek ven-dol-leralmin t' wuh ves. _your_ retrospections bolau nam-tor ni totally void t' reproach, ik wuh contentment arising s' au nam-tor ri t' ven-dol-leralmin, tonk'peh, ra nam-tor mau weh-rom, t' ignorance. Tonk'peh k' _me_, ish-veh nam-tor ri ni. Kusut-tor recollections dungi vi-kwitau, if fam yehat, if ought ri tor nam-tor repelled. I ma vesh' wuh selfish hasu ek' t'nash-veh ha'kiv, svi' practice, hi ri svi' dvatai. U' wuh kan i vesh' saven-tor ra vesh' _right_, tonk'peh i vesh' ri saven-tor tor yeht t'nash-veh temper. I vesh' putan-tor rom dvatai, tonk'peh losrak tor zahal-tor au svi' pride heh conceit. Unfortunately wuh goh sa-fu (na' wehk tevun wuh goh _child_), i vesh' spoiled k' t'nash-veh mekhlar, vi, hi rom themselves, (t'nash-veh sa-mekh wa', ek' ik vesh' benevolent heh amiable, ) kal-tor, kastorau, siyah saven-tor me tor nam-tor selfish heh overbearing, tor palutunau rim mesakh t'nash-veh sha' skan da-kuv, tor nah-tor meanly t' ek' wuh shom t' wuh panu, tor _wish_ k'puu tor nah-tor meanly t' ish-veh kash-ral heh don tcok'at k' t'nash-veh sha'. Such i vesh', s' ohkuh tor ohkuh-heh-dah-leh; heh such i lau fam dvun ma vesh' tonk'peh na' du, dearest, loveliest elizabeth! Ra tor i ri owe du! Du saven-tor me wuh tupa, lerash indeed palikauk, tonk'peh danik advantageous. K' du, i vesh' properly humbled. Vesht sarlah nash-veh tor du rik' wuh vet t' t'nash-veh reception. Du gluvau me uf insufficient vesh' ek' t'nash-veh pretensions tor sanoi wuh kosu worthy t' hasu sanoi.” “had du yi persuaded yourself ik i dang?” “indeed i had. Ra dungi du nah-tor t' t'nash-veh vanity? I pudva-tor du tor nam-tor wishing, expecting t'nash-veh shi'yavekh.” “t'nash-veh manners bolau ma vesh' svi' lafot, tonk'peh ri intentionally, i assure du. I worla tvai tor tehs-tor du, tonk'peh t'nash-veh tam'a lau k'ashiv ras-tukh me riyeht. Uf du bolau ma fnu-ven me po' _that_ khru!” “fnu-ven du! I vesh' reshnek, sos'eh, palikauk, tonk'peh t'nash-veh reshan ak began tor nem-tor wuh proper kharat.” “i am siyah kwes t' asking ra du nahp t' me lu etek ragel-tor na' pemberley. Du tenah me na' coming?” “rai, indeed, i olau nothing tonk'peh ak'wikmun.” “ish-veh ak'wikmun kupi ri nam-tor weht tor _mine_ svi' hasu pubeglanau k' du. T'nash-veh conscience var-tor me ik i nazh-tor rai wehtsuri politeness, heh i confess ik i did ri gish tor poprah _more_ do t'nash-veh due.” “t'nash-veh vel _then_, ” kilko-tor darcy, “vesh' tor gluvaya du, k' kanok civility svi' t'nash-veh tepul, ik i vesh' ri ni tvai u' tor resent wuh vesht; heh i rok-tor tor prah ish-veh thrap-fam'es nufau, tor lessen ish-veh has-bosh opinion, k' letting du gla-tor ik ish-veh reproofs had vesh' attended tor. Uf ak sovek vath istau puragtau themselves, i mokuhlek hardly var-tor, tonk'peh i dva-tor svi' pa' ulef wuh wadan po' i had gla-tor du.” au yi var-tor ish-veh t' georgiana’s delight svi' ish-veh acquaintance, heh t' ish-veh disappointment na' its sudden svi-shaya; if naturally leading tor wuh aishan t' ik svi-shaya, she ak oren-tor ik ish-veh resolution t' zahalik ish-veh s' derbyshire svi' psthan t' ish-veh ko-kai had vesh' shidau fa' au quitted wuh ha-shal, heh ik ish-veh ne-seshan heh thoughtfulness tra' had arisen s' rai vath struggles do ra such wuh lof bolau comprehend. She sagluvau ish-veh gratitude va'ashiv, tonk'peh ish-veh vesh' nuh' kusut-tor wuh subject tor tik tor nam-tor dwelt fi' weh-irak. Po' walking several miles svi' wuh leisurely manner, heh nuh' toranik tor fai-tor sovek-vel pa' ish-veh, au afer-tor na' kim-shah, fi' examining ish-veh glantau, ik ish-veh vesh' wak tor nam-tor na' ha-kel. “ra kupi ma shetau t' mr. Bingley heh jane?” vesh' wuh wonder if puragtau wuh discussion t' _their_ tek'ik. Darcy vesh' delighted k' ish-veh engagement; ish-veh t'hy'la had putan-tor ish-veh wuh earliest ro'fori t' ish-veh. “i bolau ya'akash whether du vesh' ak'wikmun?” leralmin-tor elizabeth. “mokov. Lu i went maf, i olau ik ish-veh would ak pavesh-tor.” “ik nam-tor tor leralmin, du had putan-tor ish-veh permission.
