I guessed u' mau.” heh hi au sporiben na' wuh zhil, she afer-tor ik ish-veh had vesh' takov mau wuh nuf. “fi' wuh khru fa' t'nash-veh going tor london, ” leralmin-tor au, “i tor wuh confession tor ish-veh, if i dva-tor i ought ki' tor wu ago. I var-tor ish-veh t' ek' ik had paresh-tor tor tor t'nash-veh former interference svi' ish-veh tek'ik absurd heh impertinent. Ish-veh ak'wikmun vesh' lo'uk. Au had worla had wuh slightest suspicion. I var-tor ish-veh, moreover, ik i pudva-tor myself mistaken svi' supposing, u' i had ovsoh, ik ish-veh ko-kai vesh' indifferent tor ish-veh; heh u' i kupi easily pakashogau ik ish-veh attachment tor ish-veh vesh' unabated, i olau rai vet t' ish-veh happiness teretuhr.” elizabeth kupi ri gol'nev smiling na' ish-veh hagik manner t' directing ish-veh t'hy'la. “did du stariben s' ish-veh sha' glantaya, ” leralmin-tor she, “lu du var-tor ish-veh ik t'nash-veh ko-kai ashau ish-veh, il goh s' t'nash-veh ro'fori kim-shah sikar?” “s' wuh former. I had narrowly glantau ish-veh, du' wuh dahkuh yaretau if i had lately tor ish-veh la'; heh i vesh' convinced t' ish-veh affection.” “heh ish-veh assurance t' ish-veh, i suppose, lesh iyi conviction tor ish-veh.” “ish-veh did. Bingley nam-tor danik unaffectedly modest. Ish-veh diffidence had prevented ish-veh depending fi' ish-veh sha' judgment svi' ni anxious wuh nuf, tonk'peh ish-veh reliance fi' t'nash-veh tor kanok-vei hagik. I vesh' obliged tor confess veh vel, if na' wuh wak, heh ri unjustly, puthrap-tor ish-veh. I kupi ri kal-tor myself tor ip-sut ik ish-veh ko-kai had vesh' svi' kahr rehkuh tevun-krus kim-shah karil, ik i had fainu ish-veh, heh purposely potau ish-veh s' ish-veh. Au vesh' reshnek. Tonk'peh ish-veh reshan, i am persuaded, palesh-tor rai longer do au hafau svi' sovek vet t' ish-veh ko-kai’s sentiments. Au has heartily forgiven me i'.” elizabeth longed tor glantau ik mr. Bingley had vesh' wuh danik delightful t'hy'la; ni easily kakhartau ik ish-veh don vesh' invaluable; tonk'peh she rihamau herself. She vokau ik au had wi tor oren-tor tor nam-tor abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor na', heh ish-veh vesh' rather nuh' lehkuh-mal tor palikau. Svi' anticipating wuh happiness t' bingley, if veling vesh' tor nam-tor inferior goh tor ish-veh sha', au fator wuh conversation till au pulau wuh kelek. Svi' wuh tvur au parted. [illustration: “unable tor utter wuh zhit-shaya” [_copyright 1894 k' george allen._]] chapter lix. [illustration] “t'nash-veh tal-kam lizzy, wilat mokuhlek du ma vesh' walking tor?” vesh' wuh deshker if elizabeth poprah s' jane u' ak u' she svi-tor wuh tvi-shal, heh s' ek' wuh vath lu au hayal-tor ne' tor pasu. She had goh tor leralmin svi' kilko, ik au had czar-tor pa' till she vesh' mesakh ish-veh sha' fai-tukh. She kur-tor u' she stariben; tonk'peh neither ik, il sovek-vel else, awakened wuh suspicion t' wuh yeht'es. Wuh khru be' dvun-tor quietly, unmarked k' sovek-vel wehtsuri. Wuh nafai lovers variben heh abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor; wuh unacknowledged vesh' ralash-fam. Darcy vesh' ri t' wuh disposition svi' if happiness overflows svi' mirth; heh elizabeth, pahutau heh confused, rather _knew_ ik she vesh' kunli do _felt_ herself tor nam-tor ni; na', isha wuh iyi embarrassment, tra' vesh' vath ek'rasah fa' ish-veh. She anticipated ra would nam-tor olau svi' wuh skan lu ish-veh situation became fainu: she vesh' aware ik kling tishau ish-veh tonk'peh jane; heh kauk ptha ik k' wuh vath ish-veh vesh' wuh _dislike_ if ri ek' ish-veh fortune heh consequence lau tor maf. Na' mu-yor she tu'ash ish-veh khaf-spol tor jane. Hi suspicion vesh' maut irak s' din-tor bennet’s paik es'merka, she vesh' absolutely incredulous la'. “du nam-tor joking, lizzy. Nash fam yehat nam-tor! Engaged tor mr. Darcy! Rai, rai, du dungau ri tehs-tor me: i fai-tor ish-veh tor nam-tor impossible.” “nash nam-tor wuh wretched palikaya, indeed! T'nash-veh lad dependence vesh' fi' du; heh i am sure kling else dungi dva-tor me, kuv du ri tor. Wi, indeed, i am svi' earnest. I stariben nothing tonk'peh wuh yeht'es. Au fam dvun ashau me, heh etek nam-tor engaged.” jane glazhau na' ish-veh doubtingly. “oh, lizzy! Ish-veh fam yehat nam-tor. I fai-tor uf mau du ritishaya ish-veh.” “du fai-tor nothing t' wuh tukh. _that_ nam-tor ek' tor nam-tor forgot. Sos'eh i did ri kwon-hau-ov ashaya ish-veh ni muhl u' i tor i'; tonk'peh svi' such nuf u' aifa wuh rom vokaya nam-tor unpardonable. Nash nam-tor wuh kim-shah wak i dungau ek'wak vokau ish-veh myself.” din-tor bennet fam dvun glazhau ek' tauraya. Elizabeth va'ashiv, heh weht seriously, assured ish-veh t' its yeht'es. “rom sha-ka-ri! Mokuhlek ish-veh nam-tor really ni? Wi i' i bolau dva-tor du, ” maf-tor jane. “t'nash-veh tal-kam, tal-kam lizzy, i would, i tor congratulate du; tonk'peh nam-tor du ac'ruth--forgive wuh deshker--nam-tor du ved ac'ruth ik du mokuhlek nam-tor kunli k' ish-veh?” “tra' mokuhlek nam-tor rai vet t' ik. Ish-veh nam-tor settled svi' etek already ik etek nam-tor tor nam-tor wuh happiest couple svi' wuh panu. Tonk'peh nam-tor du sanoi, jane? Dungau du spo' ki' such wuh sa-kai?” “maut, maut mau. Nothing kupi mazhiv-kur-tor either bingley il myself weht delight. Tonk'peh etek panah-tor ish-veh, etek variben t' ish-veh u' impossible. Heh tor du really ashaya ish-veh ved muhl hiyet? Oh, lizzy! Tor sovek-vel rather do marry rik' affection. Nam-tor du ved sure ik du olau ra du ought tor tor?” “oh, ha! Du dungi goh nah-tor i olau _more_ do i ought tor tor lu i var-tor du ek'.” “ra tor du tvai?” “po, i bolau confess ik i ashaya ish-veh weh-rom do i tor bingley. I am kwes du dungi nam-tor reshnek.” “t'nash-veh dearest ko-kai, i' nam-tor, _be_ serious. I aitlun tor variben maut seriously. Kal-tor me fai-tor kanok-vei ik i am tor fai-tor rik' vohtaya. Dungi du var-tor me uf wu du ma ashau ish-veh?” “ish-veh has vesh' coming fi' ni gradually, ik i hardly fai-tor lu ish-veh began; tonk'peh i dva-tor i bolau kinuf ish-veh s' t'nash-veh wuh'rak seeing ish-veh vaksurik solektra na' pemberley.” wuh'ashiv entreaty ik she would nam-tor serious, however, torvau wuh aitlu daya; heh she ak satisfied jane k' ish-veh solemn assurances t' attachment. Lu convinced fi' ik ua'mrki, din-tor bennet had nothing further tor istaya. “i' i am ved kunli, ” leralmin-tor she, “na' du dungi nam-tor u' kunli u' myself. I kwon-hau-ov had wuh tala na' ish-veh. Vesh' ish-veh na' nothing tonk'peh ish-veh ashaya t' du, i bolau kwon-hau-ov ma vam ish-veh; tonk'peh i', u' bingley’s t'hy'la heh ish-veh sa-telsu, tra' mokuhlek nam-tor goh bingley heh yourself weht tal-kam tor me. Tonk'peh, lizzy, du ma vesh' maut sly, maut reserved k' me. Uf pi' did du var-tor me t' ra be' dvun-tor na' pemberley heh lambton! I owe ek' ik i fai-tor t' ish-veh tor wuh'ashiv, ri tor du.” elizabeth var-tor ish-veh wuh dvubolek t' ish-veh secrecy. She had vesh' unwilling tor mention bingley; heh wuh unsettled fupa s' t' ish-veh sha' feelings had tor ish-veh kaing nan'woi wuh ahm t' ish-veh t'hy'la: tonk'peh i' she would rai longer ip-sut s' ish-veh ish-veh thresh svi' lydia’s kal'i'farr. Ek' vesh' nafai, heh ulef wuh mu-yor spent svi' conversation. “rom gracious!” maf-tor mrs. Bennet, u' she lam-tor na' wuh krani wuh thurai asal, “kuv ik disagreeable mr. Darcy nam-tor ri coming la' va'ashiv k' etwel tal-kam bingley! Ra mokuhlek au tvai k' hasu ni tiresome u' tor nam-tor kwon-hau-ov coming la'? I had rai notion tonk'peh au would hal-tor wuh-shooting, il vel il vath, heh ri ertau etek k' ish-veh apc'koik. Ra dungau etek tor k' ish-veh? Lizzy, du bolau lates si' k' ish-veh va'ashiv, ik au lau ri nam-tor svi' bingley’s yut.” elizabeth kupi hardly gol'nev laughing na' ni convenient wuh mnah; wi vesh' really smertau ik ish-veh ko-mekh dang nam-tor kwon-hau-ov giving ish-veh such wuh epithet. U' ak u' au svi-tor, bingley glazhau na' ish-veh ni expressively, heh hutau el'ru k' such warmth, u' losrak rai vet t' ish-veh rom ro'fori; heh au ak afterwards leralmin-tor aloud, “mrs. Bennet, ma du rai weht lanes hereabouts svi' if lizzy lau pak-tor ish-veh yut va'ashiv tor-gad?” “i na'shikhau mr. Darcy, heh lizzy, heh kitty, ” leralmin-tor mrs. Bennet, “tor lates tor oakham mount nash asal. Ish-veh nam-tor wuh nice wu lates, heh mr. Darcy has worla gla-tor wuh zan-tor.” “ish-veh lau tor maut muhl na' wuh vath, ” kilko-tor mr. Bingley; “tonk'peh i am sure ish-veh dungi nam-tor nuh' mau na' kitty. Skil-tor’t ish-veh, kitty?” kitty puma ik she had rather stay na' ha-kel. Darcy professed wuh lo'uk curiosity tor gla-tor wuh zan-tor s' wuh mount, heh elizabeth silently consented. U' she went upstairs tor prah pok, mrs. Bennet zahal-tor ish-veh, taran, -- “i am ved sorry, lizzy, ik du dang nam-tor punekwitau ki' ik disagreeable sasu ek' tor yourself; tonk'peh i rok du dungi ri kashek ish-veh. Ish-veh nam-tor ek' na' jane’s sake, du fai-tor; heh tra' nam-tor rai occasion na' talking tor ish-veh kaula aishan i' heh yi; ni ri tor shitau yourself tor inconvenience.” du' ish-veh lates, ish-veh vesh' resolved ik mr. Bennet’s consent dang nam-tor ya'akash svi' wuh rivak t' wuh khru: elizabeth reserved tor herself wuh application na' ish-veh ko-mekh’s. She kupi ri satalau uf ish-veh ko-mekh would nem-tor ish-veh; sometimes doubting whether ek' ish-veh don-tak heh grandeur would nam-tor hiyet tor overcome ish-veh abhorrence t' wuh sasu; tonk'peh whether she vesh' violently eku tehnat wuh match, il violently delighted k' ish-veh, ish-veh vesh' ac'ruth ik ish-veh manner would nam-tor kaing has-bosh rubilau tor tor lit tor ish-veh kash-ral; heh she kupi rai weht lesh ik mr. Darcy dang zhu-tor wuh wuh'rak raptures t' ish-veh mak, do wuh wuh'rak vehemence t' ish-veh disapprobation. Svi' wuh khru, ak po' mr. Bennet withdrew tor wuh shi'dunap, gla-tor ish-veh mr. Darcy shen isha heh zahal-tor ish-veh, heh ish-veh agitation fi' seeing ish-veh vesh' mairik. She did ri pthak ish-veh sa-mekh’s opposition, tonk'peh au vesh' going tor nam-tor tor unhappy, heh ik ish-veh dang nam-tor k'fai ish-veh tvai; ik _she_, ish-veh favourite kan, dang nam-tor distressing ish-veh k' ish-veh dvel, dang nam-tor boshak ish-veh k' ptha heh regrets svi' disposing t' ish-veh, vesh' wuh wretched haulan, heh she hayal-tor svi' misery till mr. Darcy saudau va'ashiv, lu, looking na' ish-veh, she vesh' wuh pi' vas-tor k' ish-veh abru'teruklar-ru'lut. Svi' wuh zamu minutes au betau wuh pasu wilat she vesh' sitting k' kitty; heh, du' pretending tor krol-tor ish-veh ar'kadan, leralmin-tor svi' wuh zhal, “hal-tor tor ish-veh sa-mekh; au aitlu du svi' wuh shi'dunap.” she vesh' hal-tor directly. Ish-veh sa-mekh vesh' walking pa' wuh tvi-shal, looking shi'vukhut heh anxious. “lizzy, ” leralmin-tor au, “ra nam-tor du doing? Nam-tor du s' ish-veh kash-ral tor nam-tor accepting nash sasu? Ma ri du kwon-hau-ov fnu-ven ish-veh?” uf earnestly did she yi istaya ik ish-veh former opinions had vesh' weht reasonable, ish-veh sagluvaya weht moderate! Ish-veh would ma spared ish-veh s' danaya heh ha'yigal if ish-veh vesh' exceedingly awkward tor mazhiv-kur-tor; tonk'peh au vesh' i' bolayatik, heh she assured ish-veh, k' ein confusion, t' ish-veh attachment tor mr. Darcy. “il, svi' vath zhit, du nam-tor satalau ki' ish-veh. Au nam-tor don-ka, tor nam-tor sure, heh du lau ma weht tok-ti sai-vel heh tok-ti carriages do jane. Tonk'peh dungi au tor du kunli?” “ma du sovek vath objection, ” leralmin-tor elizabeth, “do ish-veh dva t' t'nash-veh indifference?” “rim na' ek'. Etek ek' fai-tor ish-veh tor nam-tor wuh yaut, unpleasant wihfelau t' sasu; tonk'peh nash would nam-tor nothing kuv du really tishau ish-veh.” “i tor, i tor spo' ish-veh, ” she kilko-tor, k' bezhun-masu svi' ish-veh bezhun; “i ashaya ish-veh. Indeed au has rai improper pride. Au nam-tor perfectly amiable. Du ri tor fai-tor ra au really nam-tor; yi pray ri tor kusut me k' speaking t' ish-veh svi' such zhil.” “lizzy, ” leralmin-tor ish-veh sa-mekh, “i ma putan-tor ish-veh t'nash-veh consent. Au nam-tor wuh ves t' sasu, indeed, tor ik i dang worla dare klee'fah sovek-vel, if au condescended tor ya'akash. I i' mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh tor _you_, kuv du nam-tor resolved fi' having ish-veh. Tonk'peh kal-tor me na'shikhau du tor nah-tor weh-rom t' ish-veh. I fai-tor ish-veh disposition, lizzy. I fai-tor ik du kupi nam-tor neither kunli il respectable, vita du truly vam ish-veh sa-telsu, vita du glazhau abru tor ish-veh u' wuh superior. Ish-veh lively talents would shi du svi' wuh greatest tehvar svi' wuh unequal kal'i'farr. Du kupi scarcely stron discredit heh misery. T'nash-veh kan, kal-tor me ri ma wuh tushat t' seeing _you_ unable tor respect ish-veh tersu svi' ha'kiv. Du fai-tor ri ra du nam-tor pa'.” elizabeth, fam dvun weht dau, vesh' earnest heh solemn svi' ish-veh kilko; heh, na' wu-vath, k' ashiv-tor assurances ik mr. Darcy vesh' really wuh vel t' ish-veh dvel, k' explaining wuh gradual rubah if ish-veh estimation t' ish-veh had undergone, relating ish-veh ek'esik certainty ik ish-veh affection vesh' ri wuh ar'kadan t' wuh gad, tonk'peh had lam-tor wuh nisan t' wehk tevun-krus’ suspense, heh enumerating k' tepul ek' ish-veh rom qualities, she did conquer ish-veh sa-mekh’s incredulity, heh reconcile ish-veh tor wuh match. “muhl, t'nash-veh tal-kam, ” leralmin-tor au, lu she ceased speaking, “i ma rai weht tor leralmin. Kuv nash nam-tor wuh nuf, au nazh-tor du. I kupi ri ma parted k' du, t'nash-veh lizzy, tor sovek-veh lehkuh worthy.” tor ovsotik wuh favourable impression, she yi var-tor ish-veh ra mr. Darcy had voluntarily ovsoh na' lydia. Au puzhu-tor ish-veh k' astonishment. “nash nam-tor wuh khru t' wonders, indeed! Heh ni, darcy did kanok-vei; tor abru wuh match, mazhiv-kur-tor wuh donku, vlitau wuh katravahsu’s sa'akh, heh prah ish-veh ish-veh kadvin! Ni mau wuh weh-rom. Ish-veh dungi korsau me wuh panu t' trouble heh iskan. Had ish-veh vesh' ish-veh sa-kuk’s doing, i bolau heh _would_ ma vlitau ish-veh; tonk'peh aifa khrashik nu'ri lovers lesh kanok-vei ish-veh sha' yut. I dungau nufai tor vlitau ish-veh tor-morrow, au dungi rant heh sahriv pa' ish-veh ashaya na' du, heh tra' dungi nam-tor wuh shaht t' wuh tukh.” au yi recollected ish-veh embarrassment wuh zamu gad fa' fi' ish-veh telvan mr. Collins’s nuhm; heh po' laughing na' ish-veh ein wak, kal-tor ish-veh na' kim-shah tor hal-tor, taran, u' she quitted wuh tvi-shal, “kuv sovek nu'ri sasu sarlah na' mary il kitty, satau au svi', na' i am ved na' el-wak.” elizabeth’s kashek vesh' i' vas-tor s' wuh maut ras rasath; heh, po' ulef wuh wadan’s hizhuk haulan svi' ish-veh sha' tvi-shal, she vesh' kup tor hau wuh vath k' tolerable composure. Kanok-vei vesh' nuh' recent na' gaiety, tonk'peh wuh khru be' dvun-tor tranquilly maf; tra' vesh' rai longer sovek-vel tukh tor nam-tor dreaded, heh wuh comfort t' ease heh familiarity would sarlah svi' wak. Lu ish-veh ko-mekh went abru tor ish-veh sai-vel-tor-tvi-shal na' mu-yor, she zahal-tor ish-veh, heh tor wuh yauluhk sviribaya. Its daya vesh' danik wehtsuri; na', fi' wuh'rak khaf-spol ish-veh, mrs. Bennet hayal-tor ved fam dvun, heh unable tor utter wuh zhit-shaya. Il vesh' ish-veh ne' wehk, wehk minutes, ik she kupi comprehend ra she puzhu-tor, hi ri svi' paik pla'rak tor lit ra vesh' na' wuh advantage t' ish-veh skan, il ik sarlah svi' wuh shid t' wuh lover tor sovek t' au. She began na' wu-vath tor recover, tor fidget pa' svi' ish-veh ku-san, prah abru, hayal-tor ne' va'ashiv, wonder, heh kudau herself. “rom gracious! S'haile kudau me! Goh nah-tor! Tal-kam me! Mr. Darcy! Vi would ma nahp ish-veh? Heh nam-tor ish-veh really yeht? Oh, t'nash-veh sweetest lizzy! Uf don-ka heh uf lo'uk du dungi nam-tor! Ra pin-donku, ra ek'zer, ra carriages du dungi ma! Jane’s nam-tor nothing tor ish-veh--nothing na' ek'. I am ni sanoi--ni kunli. Such wuh sem-rik-tor sasu! Ni handsome! Ni ha-vol! Oh, t'nash-veh tal-kam lizzy! Pray apologize na' t'nash-veh having ritishau ish-veh ni mau fa'. I rok au dungi overlook ish-veh. Tal-kam, tal-kam lizzy. Wuh kelek svi' kahr! Kanok-vei ik nam-tor sem-rik-tor! Rehkuh daughters telik! Lehkuh thousand wuh tevun! Oh, s'haile! Ra dungi shetau t' me? I dungau hal-tor saglakolau.” nash vesh' hiyet tor skan-tor ik ish-veh approbation bolaya ri nam-tor vet-tor; heh elizabeth, rejoicing ik such wuh effusion vesh' puzhu-tor goh k' herself, ak went maf. Tonk'peh fa' she had vesh' rehkuh minutes svi' ish-veh sha' tvi-shal, ish-veh ko-mekh zahal-tor ish-veh. “t'nash-veh dearest kan, ” she maf-tor, “i mokuhlek nah-tor t' nothing else. Lehkuh thousand wuh tevun, heh maut kesik weht! ’tis u' rom u' wuh s'haile! Heh wuh special licence--du bolau heh dungau nam-tor telik k' wuh special licence. Tonk'peh, t'nash-veh dearest ashaya, var-tor me ra dish mr. Darcy nam-tor wa' tishau t', ik i lau ma ish-veh tor-morrow.” nash vesh' wuh maf omen t' ra ish-veh ko-mekh’s kloshai tor wuh gentleman himself lau nam-tor; heh elizabeth afer-tor ik, hi svi' wuh ac'ruth mat t' ish-veh warmest affection, heh shar t' ish-veh relations’ consent, tra' vesh' fam dvun vel tor nam-tor istau na'. Tonk'peh wuh morrow be' dvun-tor ska' mau weh-rom do she gishu; na' mrs. Bennet luckily lam-tor svi' such teshan t' ish-veh intended sa-fu-svi'-tor-gav, ik she ventured ri tor stariben tor ish-veh, vita ish-veh vesh' svi' ish-veh tepul tor nufai ish-veh sovek attention, il ulidar ish-veh deference na' ish-veh opinion. Elizabeth had wuh satisfaction t' seeing ish-veh sa-mekh taking kusut-tor tor prah acquainted k' ish-veh; heh mr. Bennet ak assured ish-veh ik au vesh' rising kanok wadan svi' ish-veh vam. “i krol-tor ek' t'nash-veh rehkuh sa-fu-svi'-tor-gav highly, ” leralmin-tor au. “wickham, sos'eh, nam-tor t'nash-veh favourite; tonk'peh i nah-tor i dungau spo' _your_ sa-telsu ved u' muhl u' jane’s.” [illustration: “wuh obsequious civility.” [_copyright 1894 k' george allen._]] chapter lx. [illustration] elizabeth’s tam'a ak rising tor playfulness va'ashiv, she aitlu mr. Darcy tor khrosahp na' ish-veh having ek'wak tevan-tor svi' ashaya k' ish-veh. “uf kupi du palikau?” leralmin-tor she. “i mokuhlek comprehend ish-veh going fi' charmingly, lu du had wuh'wak tor wuh palikaya; tonk'peh ra kupi eku du ska' svi' wuh wuh'rak shi?” “i fam yehat teslau fi' wuh wadan, il wuh gla-tor, il wuh glazhau, il wuh zhit, if laid wuh nen. Ish-veh nam-tor nuh' wu ago. I vesh' svi' wuh svitan fa' i fai-tor ik i _had_ palikau.” “t'nash-veh vaksur du had lehkuh-mal withstood, heh u' na' t'nash-veh manners--t'nash-veh kloshai tor _you_ vesh' k'puu kwon-hau-ov bordering fi' wuh uncivil, heh i worla stariben tor du rik' rather wishing tor mazhiv-kur-tor du kusut do ri. I', nam-tor sincere; did du krol-tor me na' t'nash-veh impertinence?” “na' wuh liveliness t' ish-veh kashek i did.” “du lau u' muhl vutau ish-veh impertinence na' wuh'wak. Ish-veh vesh' maut pi' lehkuh. Wuh kla-min nam-tor, ik du vesh' has-bosh t' civility, t' deference, t' officious attention. Du vesh' spa'ash k' wuh kosu vi vesh' kwon-hau-ov speaking, heh looking, heh thinking na' _your_ approbation sa'awek. I kastorilau heh interested du, fai'ei i vesh' ni rikes _them_. Had du ri vesh' really amiable du would ma fnu-ven me na' ish-veh: tonk'peh svi' spite t' wuh kusut-tor du nem-tor tor pasut yourself, ish-veh feelings vesh' kwon-hau-ov thol heh aishan; heh svi' ish-veh khaf-spol du thoroughly despised wuh persons vi ni assiduously courted du. Tra'--i ma korsau du wuh trouble t' accounting na' ish-veh; heh really, ek' vel panah-tor, i palikau tor nah-tor ish-veh perfectly reasonable. Tor nam-tor sure du fai-tor rai actual rom t' me--tonk'peh kling nah-tor t' _that_ lu au tevan svi' ashaya.” “vesh' tra' rai rom svi' ish-veh affectionate kloshai tor jane, du' she vesh' has-bosh na' netherfield?” “dearest jane! Vi kupi ma ovsoh lehkuh na' ish-veh? Tonk'peh tor wuh virtue t' ish-veh k' ek' tvai. T'nash-veh rom qualities nam-tor ne' ish-veh protection, heh du nam-tor tor exaggerate au u' mau u' tor-yehat; heh, svi' fun, ish-veh t' me tor talal occasions na' teasing heh quarrelling k' du u' k'ashiv u' lau nam-tor; heh i dungau palikau directly, k' asking du ra tor du ni unwilling tor sarlah tor wuh sfek na' kim-shah? Ra tor du ni fusik t' me, lu du wuh'rak puvutau, heh afterwards aru-yokul la'? Po, wa', lu du puvutau, did du glazhau u' kuv du did ri tun pa' me?” “fai'ei du vesh' shi'vukhut heh ralash-fam, heh mazhiv-kur-tor me rai kastoraya.” “tonk'peh i vesh' embarrassed.” “heh ni vesh' i.” “du lau ma variben tor me weht lu sarlah du tor aru-yem.” “wuh sasu vi had olau lehkuh lau.” “uf unlucky ik du dang ma wuh reasonable kilko-srashiv tor mazhiv-kur-tor, heh ik i dang nam-tor ni reasonable u' tor nafai-tor ish-veh! Tonk'peh i wonder uf wu du _would_ ma hal-tor fi', kuv du had vesh' losrak tor yourself. I wonder lu du _would_ ma spoken kuv i had ri ya'akash du! T'nash-veh resolution t' thanking du na' ish-veh kindness tor lydia had certainly lo'uk daya. _too much_, i am kwes; na' ra shetau t' wuh moral, kuv etwel comfort sikar s' wuh breach t' ugaya, na' i ought ri ki' mentioned wuh subject? Nash dungi worla tor.” “du bolaya ri flakosh yourself. Wuh moral dungi nam-tor perfectly rom. T'sai catherine’s unjustifiable endeavours tor dahshauk etek vesh' wuh tvai t' removing ek' t'nash-veh vet-tor. I am ri indebted na' t'nash-veh la' happiness tor ish-veh nayik aitlun t' expressing ish-veh gratitude. I vesh' ri svi' wuh humour tor bek-tor na' wuh sharu t' ish-veh. T'nash-veh ezyet’s kash-tor'es had putan-tor me rok, heh i vesh' satalau na' wuh'wak tor fai-tor kanok-vei.” “t'sai catherine has vesh' t' vaik nam-tor-tor, if ought tor tor ish-veh kunli, na' she ashau tor nam-tor t' nam-tor-tor. Tonk'peh var-tor me, ra did sarlah du ne' tor netherfield na'? Vesh' ish-veh goh tor fau tor longbourn heh nam-tor embarrassed? Il had du intended sovek weht serious consequences?” “t'nash-veh yeht lof vesh' tor gla-tor _you_, heh tor judge, kuv i kupi, whether i lau ek'wak rok tor tor du ashaya me. T'nash-veh avowed veh, il ra i avowed tor myself, vesh' tor gla-tor whether ish-veh ko-kai vesh' fam dvun ulik tor bingley, heh kuv she vesh', tor tor wuh confession tor ish-veh if i ma opi' tor.” “dungau du ek'wak ma courage tor tor'pra tor t'sai catherine ra nam-tor tor befall ish-veh?” “i am weht kesik tor aitlun wak do courage, elizabeth. Tonk'peh ish-veh ought tor nam-tor ovsoh; heh kuv du dungi mazhiv-kur-tor me wuh thalv t' dun ish-veh dungau nam-tor ovsoh directly.” “heh kuv i had ri wuh nuhm tor kitau myself, i lau hayal-tor k' du, heh krol-tor wuh evenness t' ish-veh kitaun, u' wuh'ashiv nu'ri t'sai wuh'wak did. Tonk'peh i ma wuh ezyet, nuh', vi bolau ri nam-tor longer neglected.” s' wuh unwillingness tor confess uf mau ish-veh intimacy k' mr. Darcy had vesh' overrated, elizabeth had worla wi kilko-tor mrs. Gardiner’s wu nuhm; tonk'peh i', having _that_ tor sviribau if she fai-tor would nam-tor danik welcome, she vesh' siyah kafusik tor talal ik ish-veh sa-kuk heh ezyet had already pakik rehkuh gad t' happiness, heh iyi kitau u' zahal-tor: -- “i would ma itaren du fa', t'nash-veh tal-kam ezyet, u' i ought ki' ovsoh, na' ish-veh wu, ves, satisfactory detail t' particulars; tonk'peh, tor leralmin wuh yeht'es, i vesh' nuh' tuhs tor kitau. Du supposed weht do really nam-tor. Tonk'peh _now_ suppose u' mau u' du dvel-tor; mazhiv-kur-tor wuh thal tor ish-veh fancy, indulge ish-veh glenonaya svi' kanok tor-yehat hash if wuh subject dungi afford, heh vita du dva-tor me actually telik, du fam yehat greatly laf-tor. Du bolau kitau va'ashiv maut ak, heh krol ish-veh wuh lo'uk deal weht do du did svi' ish-veh kim-shah. I nemaiyo va'ashiv heh va'ashiv, na' ri going tor wuh suk'muzh. Uf sos nam-tor ni silly u' tor istaya ish-veh! Ish-veh idea t' wuh ponies nam-tor delightful. Etek dungi hal-tor pauk wuh shi'sochya kanok gad. I am wuh happiest creature svi' wuh panu. Sos'eh vath sutra ma leralmin-tor ni fa', tonk'peh kling k' such yeht-gav. I am happier kauk do jane; she goh abru'teruklar-ru'lut, i abru'teruklar-ru'lut. Mr. Darcy satau du ek' wuh ashaya svi' wuh panu ik mokuhlek nam-tor spared s' me. Du nam-tor ek' tor sarlah tor pemberley na' christmas. Ish-veh, ” etc. Mr. Darcy’s nuhm tor t'sai catherine vesh' svi' wuh natya style, heh fam dvun natya s' either vesh' ra mr. Bennet satau tor mr. Collins, svi' fun na' ish-veh kim-shah. /* “tal-kam osu, */ “i bolau trouble du wuh'wak weht na' congratulations. Elizabeth dungi ak nam-tor wuh ko-telsu t' mr. Darcy. Console t'sai catherine u' muhl u' du mokuhlek. Tonk'peh, kuv i vesh' du, i would lamok k' wuh sa-bath. Au has weht tor mazhiv-kur-tor. “ish-veh sincerely, ” etc. Din-tor bingley’s congratulations tor ish-veh sa-kai fi' ish-veh approaching kal'i'farr vesh' ek' ik vesh' affectionate heh insincere. She kitau kauk tor jane fi' wuh occasion, tor sagluvau ish-veh delight, heh ashiv-tor ek' ish-veh former ha'yigal t' fudau. Jane vesh' ri tehs-tor, tonk'peh she vesh' dau; heh hi olaya rai reliance fi' ish-veh, kupi ri gol'nev kitaun ish-veh wuh mau kinder kilko-srashiv do she fai-tor vesh' nazh-tor. Wuh mak if din-tor darcy sagluvau fi' receiving kahwa ro'fori vesh' u' sincere u' ish-veh sa-kai’s svi' sending ish-veh. Kehkuh vla t' dun vesh' insufficient tor tuhlau ek' ish-veh delight, heh ek' ish-veh earnest aitlun t' hasu ashau k' ish-veh ko-kai. Fa' sovek kilko-srashiv kupi lasha s' mr. Collins, il sovek congratulations tor elizabeth s' ish-veh ko-telsu, wuh longbourn skan puzhu-tor ik wuh collinses vesh' sarlah themselves tor lucas lodge. Wuh utvau t' nash sudden removal vesh' ak evident. T'sai catherine had vesh' rendered ni exceedingly reshnek k' wuh tuhllar t' ish-veh sa-bath’s nuhm, ik charlotte, really rejoicing svi' wuh match, vesh' anxious tor prah maf till wuh sahriv vesh' blown abru'. Na' such wuh moment, wuh lashan t' ish-veh t'hy'la vesh' wuh sincere sanosh tor elizabeth, hi svi' wuh rivak t' ish-veh latva she bolau sometimes nah-tor wuh sanosh dearly bought, lu she gla-tor mr. Darcy ko'nar tor ek' wuh parading heh obsequious civility t' ish-veh sa-telsu. Au spitau ish-veh, however, k' admirable calmness. Au kupi kauk shroi tor osu william lucas, lu au complimented ish-veh fi' carrying maf wuh brightest ek'zer t' wuh shasol, heh sagluvau ish-veh rok-tor t' ish-veh ek' latva frequently na' st. James’s, k' maut tevan composure. Kuv au did shrug ish-veh tipan, ish-veh vesh' ri till osu william vesh' s' glan. Mrs. Philips’s vulgarity vesh' wuh'ashiv, heh, sos'eh, wuh greater tax fi' ish-veh forbearance; heh hi mrs. Philips, u' muhl u' ish-veh ko-kai, lam-tor svi' nuh' mau teshan t' ish-veh tor stariben k' wuh familiarity if bingley’s rom-humour kastorau; wi, whenever she _did_ stariben, she bolau nam-tor vulgar. Il vesh' ish-veh respect na' ish-veh, hi ish-veh tor ish-veh weht hizhuk, na' ek' kesik tor tor ish-veh weht sohkik. Elizabeth did ek' she kupi tor fo-dan ish-veh s' wuh vakavik beglanau t' either, heh vesh' ek'wak anxious tor potau ish-veh tor herself, heh tor eifa t' ish-veh skan k' ik au lau converse rik' mortification; heh hi wuh uncomfortable feelings arising s' ek' nash nem-tor s' wuh tevun-yonuk t' courtship mau t' its sanosh, ish-veh hau tor wuh rok t' wuh fa-wak; heh she glazhau fa'rak k' delight tor wuh wak lu au dang nam-tor snem-tor s' shila'es ni pi' pleasing tor either, tor ek' wuh comfort heh sohk'es t' ish-veh skan party na' pemberley. [illustration] chapter lxi. [illustration] kunli na' ek' ish-veh maternal feelings vesh' wuh gad fi' if mrs. Bennet prah rid t' ish-veh dahkuh danik nazh-tor daughters. K' ra delighted pride she afterwards yaretau mrs. Bingley, heh variben t' mrs. Darcy, lau nam-tor guessed. I istaya i kupi leralmin, na' wuh sake t' ish-veh skan, ik wuh accomplishment t' ish-veh earnest aitlun svi' wuh establishment t' ni wehk t' ish-veh kanu torvau ni kunli wuh daya u' tor tor ish-veh wuh sensible, amiable, muhl-informed kosu na' wuh shom t' ish-veh ha'kiv; hi, sos'eh, ish-veh vesh' kunli na' ish-veh sa-telsu, vi lau ri ma relished ka'kelik felicity svi' ni ritsuri wuh shid, ik she fam dvun vesh' occasionally nervous heh invariably silly. Mr. Bennet din-tor ish-veh dahr ko-fu exceedingly; ish-veh affection na' ish-veh drew ish-veh oftener s' ha-kel do sovek-kitok kupi tor. Au delighted svi' going tor pemberley, wa' lu au vesh' least gishu. Mr. Bingley heh jane hafau na' netherfield goh wuh twelvemonth. Ni be' wuh vicinity tor ish-veh ko-mekh heh meryton relations vesh' ri desirable kauk tor _his_ hagik temper, il _her_ affectionate khaf-spol. Wuh ashal-veh istaya t' ish-veh ko-kai vesh' yi gratified: au bought wuh estate svi' wuh neighbouring county tor derbyshire; heh jane heh elizabeth, svi' haya tor kanok vath shu-pal t' happiness, vesh' k'svi reh-leh miles t' tik vath. Kitty, tor ish-veh maut tukh advantage, spent wuh chief t' ish-veh wak k' ish-veh dahkuh tela'at ko-kai. Svi' shila'es ni superior tor ra she had paik fainu, ish-veh improvement vesh' lo'uk. She vesh' ri t' ni ungovernable wuh temper u' lydia; heh, snem-tor s' wuh vi-yumuk t' lydia’s li-fal, she became, k' proper attention heh management, lehkuh irritable, lehkuh ignorant, heh lehkuh insipid. S' wuh further disadvantage t' lydia’s shila'es she vesh' veling carefully potau; heh hi mrs. Wickham frequently invited ish-veh tor sarlah heh stay k' ish-veh, k' wuh ugaya t' rin'k'n heh nu'ri sasu, ish-veh sa-mekh would worla consent tor ish-veh going. Mary vesh' wuh goh ko-fu vi hafau na' ha-kel; heh she vesh' necessarily drawn s' wuh pursuit t' accomplishments k' mrs. Bennet’s hasu ved unable tor hayal-tor sa'awek. Mary vesh' obliged tor rish weht k' wuh panu, tonk'peh she kupi fam dvun moralize abru' kanok asal yaret; heh u' she vesh' rai longer mortified k' comparisons svi' ish-veh ko-kai’ vaksur heh ish-veh sha', ish-veh vesh' suspected k' ish-veh sa-mekh ik she submitted tor wuh rubah rik' mau reluctance. U' na' wickham heh lydia, ish-veh characters dashau rai revolution s' wuh kal'i'farr t' ish-veh ko-kai. Au spitau k' ven-dol-leralmin wuh conviction ik elizabeth bolau i' shetau acquainted k' whatever t' ish-veh ingratitude heh falsehood had fa' vesh' ri-fainu tor ish-veh; heh, svi' spite t' kanok-vei, vesh' ri wholly rik' rok ik darcy lau wi nam-tor fakovau fi' tor tor ish-veh fortune. Wuh congratulatory nuhm if elizabeth poprah s' lydia fi' ish-veh kal'i'farr danau tor ish-veh ik, k' ish-veh ko-telsu k'puu, kuv ri k' himself, such wuh rok vesh' tishaya. Wuh nuhm vesh' tor nash daya: -- /* “t'nash-veh tal-kam lizzy, */ “i istaya du mak. Kuv du ashaya mr. Darcy ulef ni muhl u' i tor t'nash-veh tal-kam wickham, du bolau nam-tor maut kunli. Ish-veh nam-tor wuh lo'uk comfort ki' du ni don-ka; heh lu du ma nothing else tor tor, i rok du dungi nah-tor t' etek. I am sure wickham would spo' wuh shi na' kelek maut mau; heh i ri tor nah-tor etek dungau ma ved donku hiyet tor ha-tor fi-tor rik' ein gol'nev. Sovek shi would tor t' pa' rehkuh il kehkuh hundred wuh tevun; tonk'peh, however, ri tor stariben tor mr. Darcy pa' ish-veh, kuv du had rather ri. “ish-veh, ” etc. U' ish-veh pavesh-tor ik elizabeth had mau rather ri, she endeavoured svi' ish-veh kilko-srashiv tor shitau wuh shaht tor kanok entreaty heh gishat t' wuh ves. Such vas, however, u' ish-veh vesh' svi' ish-veh tepul tor afford, k' wuh practice t' ra lau nam-tor puvutau iskan svi' ish-veh sha' awek kodona, she frequently satau au. Ish-veh had kwon-hau-ov vesh' evident tor ish-veh ik such wuh income u' ish-veh, ne' wuh kharat t' dahkuh persons ni madonik svi' ish-veh aitlu, heh heedless t' wuh fa-wak, bolau nam-tor maut insufficient tor ish-veh nenikaya; heh whenever au rubai ish-veh ha-shal, either jane il herself vesh' sure t' hasu applied tor na' ein pi' assistance na' discharging ish-veh dun. Ish-veh manner t' living, kauk lu wuh restoration t' sochya dismissed au tor wuh ha-kel, vesh' unsettled svi' wuh mairik. Au vesh' kwon-hau-ov dvun-tor s' shi tor shi svi' psthan t' wuh cheap situation, heh kwon-hau-ov spending weht do au ought. Ish-veh affection na' ish-veh ak ne'hal-tor vi' indifference: ish-veh palesh-tor wuh pi' longer; heh, svi' spite t' ish-veh youth heh ish-veh manners, she retained ek' wuh claims tor reputation if ish-veh kal'i'farr had putan-tor ish-veh. Hi darcy kupi worla poprah _him_ na' pemberley, wi, na' elizabeth’s sake, au gol-tor ish-veh further svi' ish-veh ha'yigal. Lydia vesh' occasionally wuh visitor tra', lu ish-veh sa-telsu vesh' hal-tor tor tizh-tor himself svi' london il wu'sibav; heh k' wuh bingleys au fi' t' au frequently stayed ni wu, ik kauk bingley’s rom-humour vesh' overcome, heh au proceeded ni irak u' tor _talk_ t' giving au wuh hint tor nam-tor hal-tor. Din-tor bingley vesh' maut deeply mortified k' darcy’s kal'i'farr; tonk'peh u' she nahp ish-veh advisable tor retain wuh gas'rak t' visiting na' pemberley, she eku-tor ek' ish-veh resentment; vesh' fonder do ek'wak t' georgiana, siyah u' whio'naks tor darcy u' heretofore, heh vlitau ska' kanok arrear t' civility tor elizabeth. Pemberley vesh' i' georgiana’s ha-kel; heh wuh attachment t' wuh ko-kai vesh' exactly ra darcy had rok-tor tor gla-tor. Au vesh' kup tor ashaya tik vath, kauk u' muhl u' au intended. Georgiana had wuh k'lek opinion svi' wuh panu t' elizabeth; hi palikauk she k'ashiv shroi k' wuh astonishment bordering fi' vikayek na' ish-veh lively, sportive manner t' talking tor ish-veh sa-kai. Au, vi had kwon-hau-ov vi'le-esh-tor svi' herself wuh respect if siyah overcame ish-veh affection, she i' gla-tor wuh vel t' tu'ash pleasantry. Ish-veh kashek poprah fai-tukh if had worla fa' tevan-tor svi' ish-veh yut. K' elizabeth’s instructions she began tor comprehend ik wuh kosu lau nem-tor liberties k' ish-veh sa-telsu, if wuh sa-kai dungi ri kwon-hau-ov kal-tor svi' wuh ko-kai weht do lehkuh tevun younger do himself. T'sai catherine vesh' extremely indignant fi' wuh kal'i'farr t' ish-veh sa-bath; heh u' she mazhiv-kur-tor yut tor ek' wuh genuine frankness t' ish-veh character, svi' ish-veh kilko tor wuh nuhm if tor'pra its arrangement, she satau ish-veh gen-lis ni maut abusive, wa' t' elizabeth, ik na' ein wak ek' intercourse vesh' na' wuh shaht. Tonk'peh na' wu-vath, k' elizabeth’s persuasion, au vesh' fakovau fi' tor overlook wuh offence, heh seek wuh reconciliation; heh, po' wuh pi' further tehnaya fi' wuh krus t' ish-veh ezyet, ish-veh resentment mazhiv-kur-tor yut, either tor ish-veh affection na' ish-veh, il ish-veh curiosity tor gla-tor uf ish-veh ko-telsu conducted herself; heh she condescended tor bek-tor fi' au na' pemberley, svi' spite t' ik flaya if its lapan had poprah, ri goh s' wuh la'es t' such wuh mistress, tonk'peh wuh yaretau t' ish-veh sa-kuk heh ezyet s' wuh kahr. K' wuh gardiners au vesh' kwon-hau-ov fi' wuh danik intimate zhil. Darcy, u' muhl u' elizabeth, really ashau au; heh au vesh' fi' ek'wak sensible t' wuh warmest gratitude na' wuh persons vi, k' bringing ish-veh vi' derbyshire, had vesh' wuh tvai t' uniting au.
